An preost wes on leoden Laȝamon wes ihoten
he wes Leouenaþes sone liþe him beo Drihten
He wonede at Ernleȝe at æþelen are chirechen
vppen Seuarne staþe sel þar him þuhte
onfest Radestone þer he bock radde
Hit com him on mode and on his mern þonke
þet he wolde of Engle þa æþelæn tellen
wat heo ihoten weoren and wonene heo comen
þa Englene londe ærest ahten
æfter þan flode þe from Drihtene com
þe al her aquelde quic þat he funde
buten Noe and Sem Iaphet and Cham
 and heore four wiues þe mid heom weren on archen
Laȝamon gon liþen wide ȝond þas leode
 and biwon þa æþela boc þa he to bisne nom
He nom þa Englisca boc þa makede Seint Beda
Anoþer he nom on Latin þe makede Seinte Albin
 and þe feire Austin þe fulluht broute hider in
Boc he nom þe þridde leide þer amidden
þa makede a Frenchis clerc
Wace wes ihoten þe wel couþe writen
 and he hoe ȝef þare æþelen Ælienor
þe wes Henries quene þes heȝes kinges
Laȝamon leide þeos boc and þa leaf wende
he heom leofliche biheold liþe him beo Drihten
Feþeren he nom mid fingren and fiede on bocfelle
 and þa soþere word sette togadere
 and þa þre boc þrumde to are
Nu biddeþ Laȝamon alcne æþele mon
for þene almiten Godd
þet þeos boc rede and leornia þeos runan
þat he þeos soþfeste word segge tosumne 
for his fader saule þa hine forþ brouhte
 and for his moder saule þa hine to monne iber
 and for his awene saule þat hire þe selre beo Amen
Nv seiþ mid loftsonge þe wes on leoden preost
al swa þe boc spekeþ þe he to bisne inom
þa Grickes hefden Troye mid teone biwonen
 and þat lond iwest and þa leoden ofslawen
 and for þe wrakedome of Menelaus quene
Elene was ihoten alþeodisc wif
þa Paris Alixandre mid pretwrenche biwon
for hire weoren on ane daȝe hund þousunt deade
Vt of þan fehte þe was feondliche stor
Eneas þe duc mid ermþen atwond
Nefede he boten anne sune þe was mid him isund
Asscanius was ihoten nefede he bern no ma
 and þes duc mid his drihte to þare sæ him droh
of kunne and of folke þe fulede þan duke
of monne and of ahte þe he to þare sæ brouhte
 and tuenti gode scipen he guþliche fulde
 and þa scipen foren wide ȝeon þare wintrede sæ
mid wolcnen and mid wedere heo þoleden wensiþes
ant mid muchelure care heo to londe bicomen
On Italiȝe heo comen to londe þar Rome nou on stondeþ
fele ȝer under sunnan nas ȝet Rome biwonnen
 and heuede Eneas þe duc mid his drihtfolcke
widen iwalken ȝend þat wide water
moni lond umberowen redes him trokeden
On Italiȝe he com on lond þat him was iqueme
A þon londe he fund mete and he hine mid monscipe biwon
 and mid golde and mid gersume and he griþliche spac
I þere Tyure he eode alond þer þa sea wasceþ þat sond
ful neh þan ilke stude þar Rome nou stondeþ
Þe king was ihoten Latin þe on þan londe wes
hey wes and riche and he wes redesful
mid wintre he wes biweaued swo hit wolde Godd
Þar com Eneas and grette þen alde king
 and he hine feire onfeng mid allen his folke
Muche lond he him ȝef and mare him biheyte
anlong þare sea siden and widen
Þare quene hit ofþouhte noþeles heo hit þolede 
Þe king heuede ane douter þe him was swiþe deore
Eneam he heo biheyte to habben to wife
 and after his daye al his drihliche lond
for he nefde nenne sune þe sarure was his heorte
Þat maiden wes ihoten Lauine seþen heo wes leodena quene
feier wes þe wimmon and wunsum hire monnen
Ah Turnus was ihoten þat wes of Tuskanne duc
þet lufede þet maiden and hire monscipe bed
þat he heo wolde habben to heiȝen are quene
Þa com þat word to him þat was widene cuþ
þat þe king Latin ȝef Lauine his douter
Eneam to are brude for heo wes his deore bearn
Þa wes Turnus sari and soruful on his mode
for he heo heuede swiþe ilofed and lufþing hire biheite
Weorre makede Turnus mid teonen he wes idrefed
wiþ Eneam he nom an feiht þat wes feondliche strong
hond wiþ honde fuhten þa heȝe men
Teone wes on compe þar Turnus feol
mid mechen toheawen his monscipe wes þe lasse
Eneas nom Lauine leofliche to wife
he wes king and heo quen and kinelond heo welden
inne griþe and inne friþe and freoliche loueden
Seoþen Eneas Lauine heuede inomen and þa leodene biwnnen
he makede enne stronge castel mid starke ston walle
Lauine hehte his leuemon þene castel he clepede Lauinion
þat wes for hire worþscipe wel þat he hire uþe
Feour winter he heuede þat wif mid wrþscipe to welden
after þa feourþe ȝere he was dead his freonden hit ofþuhten
Heuede Lauine þa quene kinebearn on wombe
þa quen þerefter sone ænne sune hefde to froure 
Siluius Eneas for æþelen he wes ihoten
Ascanius his broþer þe mid his fader com from Troie
mid muchele worscipe þis kinebearn biwiste
Asscanius wes þes childes broþer ah heo nefden noht ane moder
His moder wes ihoten Creusa Priames kinges dohter
þe Eneas his fader in Troie forleas
inne þane fehte his feon heo him binomen
Asscanius heold þis drihliche lond daiȝes and ȝeres
 and he makede ane heȝe burh Albe Lingoe wes ihaten
Þa burh wes wel iȝarwed binnen lut ȝearen
he ȝef heo his stepmoder for þon lofe of his broþer
 and Lauinion þene castel and muchel lond þarto
þe his fader hefde imaked þe wile þe he on liue wes
þis lond he hire lende þat come hir lifes ende
Ah heo nom þene mahum þe heo tolden for godd
þe Eneas mid his ferde brohte from Troie
In Albe Lingue he hine sette ah sone he þonene iuatte
forþ aȝein mid þan winde þe Feond hine ferede
Asscanius þe kene þe wes i kinges stude
four and þritti winter he heold þat lond
 and þa leoden mid blissen
Þa com his lifes ende laþ þah him were
Siluium his broþer þe wes Lauine sune
he bitahte al þat lond þat Eneas heore fader hefde on hond
Ænne sune heuede Asscanius þe wes ihaten Siluius
þis child hefde his eames nome ah lut ȝer he leouede
for his ahne sune seoþen hine sceat to deaþe
Þa þis child was feir muche þa luuede he a maide
þeo was Lauine mawe mid darnscipe he heo luuede
Hit iwerþ þere swa hit deþ wel iwere
þat þeos ȝunge wiman iwerd hire mid childe
þe ȝet leouede Asscanius þe on þan londe was duc
Vnderȝetene weren þe þinges þat þeo wimon was mid childe
Þa sende Asscanius þe wes lauerd and dux
after heom ȝend þat lond þe cuþen dweomerlakes song
witen he wolde þurh þa wiþercraftes
wat þing hit were þat þeo wimon hefde on wombe
Heo wrpen heore leoten þe Scucke wes bitweonen
heo funden on þen crefte carefule leoþes 
þet þeo wimon was mid ane sune þat wes a selcuþ bearn
þat boa sculde fallen fader and his moder
þorh him heo sculden deiȝen and þene deaþ þolien
 and þurh his ealdren deþ idreuen out of londe
 and umben longne first mid wrþscipe comen liþen
Þo leoten weren iworpen and swa hit al iwearþ
Þa þe time com þat þe cnaue wes iboren
in þere burhe þa brude dead iwearþ
þe child wes iboren isund to baluen his moder
Þat child was ihaten Brutus þat bearn nas nowit feie
Þis child leuede and wel iþei and þeweas hit luuede
He was fiftene ȝer ald þa he to wode ferde
 and his fader mid him and feiesiþ makede
Heo funden ane heorde of heorte swiþe greate
þe fader heo bieode to his aȝre unneode
To his sune he heo draf himseolfue to balewe
Brutus sette on his flo
he wende to sceoten þat hea der and ihitte his aȝene fader
þurhut þere broste wao wes Brutus þerfore
Wa wes him on liue þa þe fader wes on deaþe
Þa þat iherde his kun þe he of icumen wes
þat he þe flo heuede idrawen and his fader ofslawen
heo hine flemden out of þane londe
 and he iwende sorhful ouer seastreames
into Griclonde þer he his cun funde
of þan folck of Troye þe mid teonen wes todrefed
þere quene cun Heleineþes kinges sune Priame
 and muchel folc of his þeoden ah al heo weren þeowe
 and of his aȝne kunne moni kineborene mon
Moni ȝer was agan seoþþen his cun hider com
þa wepmen weren iwexan þa wimen wel iþowene
 and heore nutene neotsume weren
Nes Brutus i þon londe bute lutel ane wile
þat alle monnen he wes leof and muchele monscipe biwon
for cniht he was swiþe god þan folke to queme
he was metecusti þat is monscipe steor
Alle monnen he was leof þe him lokeden on
heo him ȝeuen gersume and feire hine gretten
heo seiden him mid rede and mid stilliche runen
ȝif he were swa þriste and he hit don durste
þat he heom wolde leaden out of þane leoden 
out of þeowedome freo þat heo weoren
heo hine wolden maken duc and deme ofer his folke
We habbeþ seoue þusund of gode cnihten
wiþouten wifmen þe noht ne cunnen of wepnen
children and hinen þa ure nete sculen ȝemen
For muchel we wlleþ driȝen and habben care of ure life
ær we nulleþ mid frescipe faren from ure feonden
Alle þe weren at þisse reade biluuede þeos runen
Inne Griclonde was a ȝung mon of þriti ȝeren
Assaracus ihaten of swiþe heie kunne
His fader wes a Gric ikoren ah his moder wes of Troien iboren
 and heo wes a cheuese hire cheap wes þe wrse
Noþelas hit ilomp inne lut ȝere
þat þe fader wes dead his duȝeþe he bilefde
He ȝef Assaracum his sune sele þreo castles
 and al þat ligginde lond þe þerabuten lei
Assaracus heuede enne broþer þe wes under wedlac iboren
after þen heþene tidende þe wes in þan londe
Þes cniht hefde his fader lond and loþ him wes his broþer
for he heold þe stronge castles þurh staþele his fader ȝefe
His broþer heo him wolde binimen ah he ne mihte speden
þar aros wale and win and wiþerheppes feola
Assaracus wes god cniht wiþ Grickes he heold moni fiht
ah he hefde muchele strengþe of meren his cunne
of þan Troyscen monnen þe weren his moder isib
for þare sibelaȝe luue hem wes bitweonen
Assaracus hit redde mid diȝenliche runen
þat þat Troynisce folc mid his fulle fultume
nomen þene cniht Brutun and makeden hine to duke
 and he heora monredne mid monscipe onfeng
He sende his sonde wide ȝend þane londe
he heihte his folc sumunen and cumen to himseoluen
wapmen and wifmen þa weoleȝen and þa weaþlen
alle he heom sumunde and to wode sende
bote seoue þusend kempen þa he into þane castlen dude
Þa lette he riden vnirimed folc
biȝeoten wepnen and mete muchel wes þa neode 
 and al þat smale monkun he dude ȝeond þea muntes
 and himself mid his ferde biforen and bihinden
Seoþen he nom to rede and to somrunen
þat he an wriht makede al mid wisdome
Pandrasum þene king he grette mid greiþlicre speche
 and þat wriht he him sende and þeos word seaide
For þan weorldes scome and for þan muchele grome
þat Dardanisc kun þe we beoþ of icomene
woneþ in þisse londe leode to sconde
inne þeowedome þrelwerkes doþ
heo beoþ togadere icumene kuþies mæȝes
al swa þat ilke folc þe freoscipe wole biwinne
Heo habbeþ idemed þat ich am duc ofer heom
Ich abbe i min castlen seoue þusend kempen
ich habbe in þane munten monie þusund
Leouere heom his to libben bi þan woderoten
al swa þat wilde swin þat wroteþ ȝeond þan grouen
þane heo þine þeowedomes lengre iþolien
Ȝif heo wlleþ frescipe biwinnen ne wndre þou nawiht þerfore
heo biddeþ þe mid freonscipe þat þu heom ifreoie
Þes word he sendeþ al swa þe wriht þe seiþ
þat heo moten wonien werswa heo wolleþ
inne griþe and in friþe and heo wlleþ þe freonscipe don
Ȝif þou þis nult iþolien þe scal beon þa wrse
Þe king nom þat writ on hond and he hit wrodliche biheold
seolcuþ him þuhte swulcere speche
Þa he alles spac mid þræte he spilede
To wroþer heore hele habbeþ heo such werc idon
Mine þralles i mire þeode me suluen þretiaþ
Wide he sende ȝeond þat lond for he wes leoden king
þat come to hirede riche men and weþlen
al þat wapmoncun þa mihte beren wæpen
vppen lif and uppen leomen al þes londes folc
an horsen and an foten forþ heo ifusten
Þe king þræted Brutun swa he dude Assaracun
þat he heom wolde biliggen mid laþen heora feonden
Ȝif he heom mihte biwinnen mid his woredstrencþe
alle heo sculden hongien on heȝe treowen 
Brutus iherde seggen al swa hit soþ wæs
þat Pandrasus þe king him towardes com
mid muchelere ferde ah heo weren summe faie
Brutus nom to reade þat him best was
He nom his kene men þa to compe weren gode
he ferde to þan wode to þan wilderne
to þan ilke weie þe he ful ȝeare wuste
þat þe king mid his ferde forþ sculde iwenden
Brutus hefede gode cnihtes to neode
þre þusund mid him ilead to þære þruppe
Þe king him com riden mid riche his folke
Brutus heom smat on mid his grime smite
isowte he þe Grickes mid his grim ræsen
Þa Grickes neoren noht warre of heore wensiþe
wenden him þeo rugges flowen haȝe men
Achalon heihte an flum þe nes noht feor from heom
þider in iwenden moni þusunde
Brutus heom com æfter and æfer he heom leide on
mid sweord and mid spere al he todrof þes kinges here
a londe and a watere he heom adun leaide
 and þe king himself fleh he iseih his frend fallen
Muchel folc þer was ofsclawen on moniare wisen
Þe king hefde ænne broþer neafde he nenne oþer
Antigonus wes ihoaten inne Griclonde he wes heh
Iseih his broþer ferden hu heo iuaren weren
a wætere and a londe swa heom læþest wes
Antigonus mid his weapnen and mid his wælkempen
iwenden toward Brutun to his balesiþe
Heo comen togadere mid greatere heorte
Þar he mihte bihalden þe bihalues were
moni wensiþes wiþerhappes feole
moni heaued moni hond fallen to foten
monie þar fuhten monie flæm makeden
monie þar feollen þurh heora feonþewæs
Þa Troysse men sloȝen al þa Grickes þea heo neih comen
Þer Brutus nom Antigonun þes kinges broþer Pandrasum
mid him he hine lædde for leof he him wes to habben
He hine leatte wel witen mid wnder stronge benden
 and alswa his iferen þe mid him ifunden weren 
Þat iherde þe king Pandrasus hit neas him noht iqueme
þat Antigonus his broþer wes in armliche benden
Þe king sende swa wide swa ileste his riche
 and heihte eulne mon þe mihte riden oþer gan
þat heo comen mid him to þane castle of Sparatin
Nes castel nan swa strong i þon londe of Griclond
He wende hit to soþe soþ þeh hit neore
þat Brutus hefde þa men þe he mid fihte biwon
idon into þan castle and þear heom quic heolde
 and himseolf þer forþ mide for þære muchele biȝæte
Ah Brutus dude betere read and him þa beth ilomp
In þon castle he dude hende six hundred of his cnihten
himself mid his fenge he to wode ferde
Þe king to þan castle forþ mid his ferde
þer he lei abuten þarinne weren his laþe feond
His ferde he sette on ælchere siden
ofte heo ræsden and ræmden togadere
mid stelene orde and mid starka biten
mid stocken and mid stanen stalfiht heo makeden
mid Grickisce fure feollen þæ fæie
þar was muchel blodgute baluwe þer wes riue
Þa cnihtes of þan castle quicliche heom wiþstoden
þaet ne mihte þes kinges folc of heom fael makien
ah þe king of his monnen monie þusund læs
Þe king wes on mode sar þat wes for his monne lure
He tæh hine aȝein ane þrowe and þreateþ þene castel
 and þat folc þerinne þenne he hit hefde biwnnen
þat he heom wolde quellen oþer quic al forbrennen
He lette makien enne dic þe wes wnderliche deop
abouten his ferde and feiede heo mid þornen
 and leai þerabuten and abat his balesiþes
Þe king wes swiþe wraþ and swar muchelne oaþ
þat nolde he þonne faren ar his feonden feie weore
I þon castle weoren monie men and muchel mete þer bihofede
þe mete forþ iwat for þer fengen feole to
Heo nomen ænne ærendrake þe æþele wes to neode
heo sende to heore læuerde þa leof heom wes on heorten
Heo hine gretten mid godene heore worden
heo beden hine come to helpe mid allen his strengþe 
þe wile þe heo weren isunde þe weren his sele men
Brutus hine biþohte of swlchere neode
 and þas word seide mid soþere heorte
He deþ himselua freoma þa helpeþ his freondene
swa ich wlle mine bi mine quicke liue
Þa wes þere a welibore mon Anacletus wes ihaten
mid þes kinges broþer he was itaken and þer læi inne benden
Brutus him ræmde to mid grimmen his rasen
bi þone toppe he hine nom alswa he hine walde ofslean
 and his nakede sweord leide on his necke
 and þas word saide Brutus þe sele
Niþing þou ært al dead buten þou do mine read
 and þi læuerd alswa bote þu min lare do
ah ȝif þu wlt þu miht wel helpen inc seluen
Lauerd quaþ Anacletus don ic wille þine lare
help mine lauerd and me mid alle mire mihten
Do swa quad Brutus and þe scal beon þe bet
ȝe sculen habben lif and leomen and beon mine leofe freond
Brutus him swar an æþ breken þat he hit nælde
Þus seide Brutus þe wes cniht mid þane beste
Anacletus leofe freond toniht þu scalt faren
a þeon time biþ best þonne men gaþ to bedde
þu scalt forþ wenden to þas kinges ferde
Wonne þu comest to þon cnihten þat þene king biwiteþ
þær þu findest seouen houndred þa hæleþes beoþ kene
 and þu heom clepe to and cuþliche wiþ heom spec
Ich am Anacletus ich am mid ærmþen abroken
vt of þon benden þe Brutus me heuede on idon
 and ȝet ich ou sigge on oþer ibrout ich habbe þes kinges broþer
vt of þon quarcerne of þan qualehuse
þær Brutus hin hefde idon for tomarewene he hine wolde anhon
 and ich hine habbe idon i þisse wude derne
Cnihtes fuseþ me mid leteþ slæpen þene king
 and fare we on sele riht al swo stille
stelen swa we wolden
 and ich eou wlle leden forþ to mine lauerde
i þon woderime þer he vnder rise liþ
Ȝif ȝe hine mawen bringen biforen ure kinge
wel biþ him þere bringe oeu biþ þe beþ þerfore
 and for he is his broþer for nafþ he nenne oþer 
Cuþ he wes þen cnihten and heo hine icneowen
heo wenden þat his sawen soþe weren
ah alle heo weren lease for he wes his leodene swike
Nis nawer nan so wis mon þat me ne mai biswiken
Anacletus ferde biforen þe cnihtes him fuleden
ferde æfter ane bache alswa Brutus him hefde itaiht
Brutus hæfde his folc biforen and bihinden
Wes þe wei holh and long þa clude weren stronge
Brutus heom ræsde to mid richere strengþe
alle togadere he heom nom nane he ne lafde
summe he sloh summe he bond þa beste quike he atheold
 and alle he heom biwuste swa him best þuhte
Brutus nom his ferde on feowre he heo todælde
 and he hehte alle his men monscipe biwinnen
þa ȝunge and þa alde æþela iwurþen
wihte walkempen on heora wiþerwinnan
 and an hihinga faren to þan kinge
 and ich forbeode heolde mine þeinen
vppe þere muchele lufe þe us bitueiȝen
þat nan ne beo so wilde nan swa unwitti
þat word talie ne talkie mid speche
ær he ihere minne horn mid græte hiue blowen
For miself ich wlle teo toforen to telde þas kinges
anan swa ich lihte of blonken swa ich wlle blawen
anan swa ȝe hit ihereþ hende mine kempen
ohtliche heom slæþ on and weccheþ heom of slepa
leteþ þa Grickisca gliden to grunde
fallen þa feie for heo beþ vre fulle fan
Duden alle þa cnihtes swa Brutus heom taute
 and he himseolf teih biforen to telde þæs kinges
Of his horse he þreou his horn he vastliche bleu
Iherden hit Troynisce and tuhten to þon Gricken
heo heom aweihten mid heora wæles igrure
Þar fluwen haueden on felde fæiþe þer feollen
moni hond moni fot þe hæp wæs þe wrse
Moni þusend þer flowen þærmes heo droȝen
 and Brutus mid his cnihten þene king ifeng
al ihal and al isund heihliche he cleopede
Ich habbe þisses folkes king fælleþ his leoden
Ne lete ȝe nenne quick quecchen to holte 
 and ich wlle þesne king læden mid me seolfan
Þar Brutus bifeng al þat him biforen wes
Sparatin he aredde heh an his castel
Amarewen þa hit dai wes and þa niht todælde
Brutus sumunde his folc heo weren his fulle freonde
he heihte for his lufe al his leodeferde
þat heo nomen þat wæl and wel hit biburiede
inne deope seaþen setten þa deade
 and hit wes sone idon for monie þusend þerto fengen
Al þa biȝetene æhte he delde his cnihten
 and alle his leoue men he mid monscipe grette
Þa al þis wes idon þa dude he on oþer
he lette an heh climben and lude clepian
þat on þane daȝe amarwen come his drihtliche folc
 and alle his heȝe men comen to hustinge
 and heo swa duden blisse wes on daie
Þat folc com togadere guþliche cnihtes
 and heora lauerd spac and þus heom wiþ spelede
Lusteþ mine cnihtes lusteþ mine leofe men
Suggeþ me to runun ræd þat eou þunche
Ich habbe þesne leodking ileid in mine benden
 and his broþer alswa hit is þe bet mid us
 and his leoden ofslawen ihc am him þa laþere
 and alle his ahte iȝeuen mine æþelinge
Ȝif ȝe hit rædeþ ȝe beoþ mine riche men
ich wulle mid swerde his heued of swippen
 and ȝif ȝe hit willeþ ich hine wlle spillen
 and ȝif ȝe me readeþ ich hine wille freoien
ȝif he me ȝefeþ gersume gold and seoluer
alle his maþmas wiþ þon þa he mote libben
Þa ansuereden æþela cnihtes
Summen hit weora iqueme þat heo hine sculden quellen
himseolf habben þat lond and beon þere leodene king
Summe queþen ælles and þus þa quides eoden
Ȝeue us þe king and al his gold and þa maþmes of his lond
ȝef us peal ȝeue us hors ȝeue us haihe scrud
ȝeue us ænne ende of his kinelonde
ȝeue us ȝislæs þerto and þis mei beon wel idon
Þer wes moni riche mon þe cuþe lutel reden 
weþer heom weore wnsumre to faren þe to wonien
Þa wile þe heo tweoneden þus clepede Membricius
þet wes a riche mon þe wes swiþe wel idon
wys and witful wel he hit cudde
Wet speke ȝe cnihtes wet speke ȝe kempen
Vnder eou alle nis þar nan swa god
þa ȝet habbe isæid þat us is selest to don
Ȝif ȝe hit lusten wlle Brutus mi lauard
 and ȝe alle biluuien gode mine lare
ich eou wlle seggen selast ræden
 and þa ansuerede al þat folc Faihn we wllen hit iheren
Þa quaþ Membricius ludere stefne
Ȝirne we to þane kinge ȝeuen suiþe gode
þat is alreforwarde þat he us ifreoie
Sone þarafter ȝurne we his dohter
þat he heo ȝeue ure lauerde Brutun to his bedde
of his corne he us ȝeue swa muchel þat we beon iquemed
gold and garsume and his gode hors
 and al his beste mætecun þe his men habbeþ
 and alle þa liþinde scipen þe on his londe beoþ
 and alle þat bihoueþ þa scipen to driuen
of monnen and of wapnen þat we mawen wel faren
fare uorþ ouer sæ sel þat we wrþen
 and liþen swa longe þat we to londe comen
varen wide ȝeond þat lond and fondia þeo leoden
wer us beo iqueme king þat we makien
of Brute ure lauerde þe is best of us
and Ignoien to quen þe is þis kinges dohter
For ȝif we hit ȝeorneþ to wonien her mid Gricken
heo beoþ ure fulle feond for we beoþ ifead wiþ heom
for heora kun we habbet islaȝen in eorþe heo sleopeþ
we beoþ heom loaþe for heora muchele lure
heo wlleþ us biwiȝelien þurh heora wiþerecraftes
a swa heom beoþ iwrþ swa us wrse biþ
for mid ure wepnen heora kun we aqueald habbeþ
mid ure honden monie þusunde
Ȝif we sceoteþ to heora mæþe þat biþ ure imone deaþ
ȝif we heom ilefeþ þat biþ ure muchele lure
ȝif heo wel wexit heo wlleþ wonien us
Wel ich hit mai suggen to soþe ich hit wene 
nis þar nan swa heih nis þar nan swa laih
þat we nabbet his freond ifelled to grunde
For þon ȝif hit eow biloueþ þe wise beoþ on þonke
fare we from þisse londe þa leodene us beoþ laþe
Al heora god we sculen nimen and lutel hem læuen
wonien heo sculen unbalde for hora muchela bursten
 and we mæwen faren riche ȝif we ræd luuieþ
for al þat god of þisse londe we sculen leden mid us
 and heo bilæuen wrecches and wælde heom scal fulien
for þe riche haueþ muchel rum to ræsen biforen þan wrecchan
Þas word weoren iqueþene þeo quides weoren leoue
Þa he mihte ihere þe bihalues were
muchel dom muchel dune muchel folkes dream
 and alle heo clepeden þus Soþ seiþ Membricius
 and alle hit biluueden gode weren his lære
Þa letten bringen þene king vt of quarcerne
 and his broþer mid him beine togadere
mid yrene benden biforen Brutone
Heo him to clepeden and laþ spel him cudden
heo seiden þat he sculde beon anhongen an one heȝe treowe
oþer mid horsen todrawen mid droflicen vitan
buten heo heom lette freo ta faren of his londe
ȝeue heom al his aȝte þe he biȝeten mahte
 and alle his scipen gode þa floten bi sæflode
 and his dohter Ignogen heore duc to quene
Þe king hine biþoute wat he don mahte
Sari he was on liue þæs tiþende him weren læþe
Of deaþ he hefde care drof he wes on mode
Pandrasus answerede mid seorhfulle worden
Ȝe biddeþ mine dohter swa hende and haldeþ me inne bende
 and Antigonun mine broþer mid ærmliche witen
 and mine men ȝe habbeþ isclawen and ȝeorneþ mine maþmas
 and mine leoue dohter to swa laþe mannes bihoue
Ah heo mot nede beien þe mon þe ibunden biþ
Eouer axe ich eow leue laþ þeh hit me were
 and ȝif ȝe bilæuen wolden inne mire þeoden
al þridden dale mi lond ich wolde setten Brutan on hond
 and freoien al his folc and freonscipe makien
 and Ignogen mine dohter ȝeuen eowre duke
 and swa we sculden bileauen leoue mæȝes 
vre lif læden liþen tosumne
Þa ænswerede Brutus þe wes borene duke
Nulle we noht þis onfon ah we faren wlleþ
 and þu swiþe hiendliche scild þe wiþ dæþe
Ȝef us þat we wilniaþ ȝif þou libben wlt
Þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al Griclonde
þat me hit him to brohte alle his aihte
 and greiþede his scipen gode bi þan sæflode
 and al þat þærto bihouede hahliche ifunden
alswa heo wolden heora lauerd from loþen alesen
Al his men duden swa þe king hehte
Þa scipen weoren igreþede mid gode grundfulled
Þe king ȝef Brutun his dohter þe wes his bearn deora
 and al þat forward wes ilest Þa fusden þa ferde
wenden riht to þare sæ sela þa þeines
Muchel wæs þa blisse þa Brutus hafde mid him
Brutus nom Ignogen and into scipe lædde
Heo rihten heora rapes heo rærden heora mastes
heo wunden up seiles wind stod an willen
Sixtene siþe tuenti scipen tuhten from hauene
 and feower scipen greate þe weren grundladene
mid þat beste wepnen þa Brutus hauede
Heo fusden from stronde vt of Griclonde
heo wenden vt i wide sæ þa wilde wurþen itemede
Tweiȝe dawes and tua niht inne sæ weren
þen oþer dai heo comen liþen on æuen to londe
Logice hatte þat eitlond leode nere þar nane
ne wapmen ne wifmen buten westiȝe pæþes
Vtlaȝen hefden iræued þat lond and alle þa leoden ofslaȝen
 and swa hit wes al west and wnnen biræued
Ah swa monie þar waren wilde deor þat wnder heom þuhte
 and þa Troinisce men tuhten to þon deoren
 and duden of þan wilden al heora iwilla
to þan scipen lædden swa muche swa heo wælden
Heo funden i þon eitlonde ane burh swiþe stronge
Tohælde weoren þe walles weste weren hallen
Temple heo funden þar ane imaked of marme stæne
muchel and mære þe Wrse hit hafde to welden
Þerinne was an onlicnesse a wifmonnes liche 
feier hit wes and swiþe heih an are hæitnesse nome
Diana wes ihaten þe Deouel heo luuede
Heo dude wnder craftes þe Scucke hire fulste
Heo wes quen of alle wodes þe weoxen on eorþen
a þon heþene lawen me heold heo for hehne godd
To hire weoren iwoned þa wndercreftie men
of þa þingen þa weren to kumen heo heom wolde cuþen
mid tacnen and mid swefnen þonne heo weren on slæpe
Þe wile þeo on þan eitlonde wes folc woniende
heo wurþeden þat anlicnes þe Scucke hit onfeng
Brutus hit herde siggen þurh his sæmonnen
þe ær weoren on þan londe and þa lawen wusten
Brutus nam twelf witiȝen þe weren his wiseste men
 and enne preost of his lawen þa weren on þan heþen dawen
Gerion hehte þe preost he was an hirede hæh
he ferde to þere stowe þar Diane inne stod
Brutus ferde into þere temple and þa twelfe mid him
 and lette al his folc bilæuen þervte
Ana scale he bear an honde al of reade golde
milc wes i þere scale and win sume dale
þa milc wæs of are wite hinde þe Brutus sceat mid his honde
He makede bi þon weofede a swiþe wunsum fur
Niȝen siþen he bieode þat weofed for his neode
He clepede to þere leuedi heo wes him on heorten leof
mid milden his worden he ȝirnde hire mihten
Ofte he custe þat weofed mid wnsume lates
he halde þa milc in þat fur mid milden his worden
Leafdi Diana leoue Diana heȝe Diana help me to neode
Wise me and wite me þurh þine wihtful craft
whuder ich mæi liþan and ledan mine leoden
to ane wnsume londe þer ich mihte wunien
 and ȝif ich þat lond mai biȝeten and mi folc hit þurhgengen
makian ich wlle on þine nome mæren ane stowe
 and ich þe wulle huren mid wrhscipe hæȝan
Þus spec Brutus
Seoþþen he nam þe hude þa wæs of þare hinde
Biforen þan wefede he heo spradde swlc he leie on bedde
He cnelede þarufenan and seoþþen he adun læi
Swa he gon slomnen and þeræfter to slepen
Þa þuhte him on his swefne þar he on slepe læi 
þat his lauedi Diana hine leofliche biheolde
mid wnsume leahtren wel heo him bihihte
 and hendiliche hire hond on his heued leide
 and þus him to seide þer he on slepe lai
Biȝende France i þet west þu scalt finden a wunsum lond
þat lond is biurnan mid þære sæ þaron þu scalt wrþan sæl
Þar is fuȝel þar is fisc þer wuniaþ feire deor
þar is wode þar is water þar is wilderne muchel
þet lond is swiþe wunsum weallen þer beoþ feire
wuniaþ in þon londe eotantes swiþe stronge
Albion hatte þat lond ah leode ne beoþ þar nane
Þerto þu scalt teman and ane neowe Troye þar makian
þer scal of þine cunne kinebearn arisen
 and scal þin mære kun wælden þas londes
ȝeond þa weorld beon ihæȝed and þu beo hæl and isund
Þæ awoc Brutus wel wes him on life
He þoute of his swefne and hou þe læfdi him sæide
mid muchelere lufe he seide hit his leoden
hu him imette and þa læfdi hine igrette
He þonkede hire ȝeorne mid liþfulle worden
he biheite hire biheste and he hit wel laste
þat to hire he wolde teman and wrchen hire ane temple
 and on licnesse of ræde golde whenne he come to londe
 and æ to his liue hire willen idriȝen
At hire heo nomen læue and to scipe liþden
Heo hefden wind heo hefden water þe heom wel ferede
þritti dawes and þritti niht heo ferden efer forþriht
Bifore Affrike heo ferden forþ and eeuer heo drowen west and norþ
ouer þen lac of Siluius and ouer þen lac of Philisteus
bi Ruscikadan heo nomen þa sæ and bi þe montaine of Azare
In þære sæ heo funden vtlawen þa kenneste þa weoren o þon dawen
fifti scipen fulle þer weore feondes to feole
Wiþ Bruten heo fuhten and fealden of his monnen
ah Brutus hefde þa ouere hond þa fæie he sloh þe quike he bond
þar biwon Brutus feole kunnan wunnan
muchel garsum and mete his monscipe wes þa mære
Nefde Brutus nenne swa wreche man þat gold and pal ne dude him on
Þeonene he ferden forþ wel feole dawen ȝong
ouer Maluan æne flum suiþe long i Mauritane heo comen a lond
Heo liþden ȝeond þat ilke lond and þa leoden heo slowen 
þene drinc and þene mete þe heo þar funden
to heora scipe heo hit fusden feirest þat heom þohte
heo nomen of þan londe al þat heo wolden
Þa ferden heo forþ heora færþ wes on sæle
muchel ahte heo hæfden biwunnen Þa comen heo to þan bunnen
þa Hercules makede mid muchelen his strengþe
þat weoren postes longe of marmon stane stronge
Þat taken makede Hærcules þat lond þe þerabuten wes
swiþe brod and swiþe long al hit stod an his hond
Þer heo funden þe merminnen þat beoþ deor of muchele ginnen
wifmen hit þunchet fuliwis bineoþe þon gurdle hit þuncheþ fisc
Þeos habbeþ swa murie song ne beo þa dai na swa long
ne biþ na man weri heora songes to heræn
Hit is half mon and half fisc hit hafþ þes wurse taken fuliwis
for his werkes beoþ swa swete þat feolan men heo ne maȝen forleten
Brutus iherde siggen þurh his sæmonnen
of þan ufele ginnen þe cuþen þa mereminnen
He hihte hondlien kablen teon seiles to toppa
leten laden þene wind liþen mid þan uþen
Þa mereminnen heom to svommen on alchare sidan
swiþa heo heom lætten mid luþere heora craften
Neþelas Brutus atbræc al buten burstan
 and ferde riht on his wei his scipen runden swiþe
A steoresman ham talde wilspel þat he Spaine isæih
Heo drowen toward hauene haleþes weoren bliþe
To þan londe heo ferden þer heo leof folc funden
fouwer þrum ferden þer weoren feola þusend
gode knihtes þa gode weoren to fihten
Þeos weoren heora sibbemen hit wes þa beth mid heom
Þeos feower ferden from Troye weoren iflemed
Atenor heom ledde þe wes leode ælder
 and he mid þan folke fleh ut of Troye
þa Grickes hit biwnnan mid heora wælslahte
Corineus wes heora duc seþþen Atenor was dead
Corineus wes a strong mon and he heuede muchele ban
he wes swa kene he wes swa strong swilc hit weore an eotand
Þa tiþind com to Corineum þat Brutus wes þider icomen
wel wes him on liue nes he neuer ær swa bliþe 
Heo comen togadere and ofte heo custen
Brutus him seide tiþinde þat an lond he ferde sechinde
þer he mihte þurhwunian mid his wnfolke
Corineus him answerede and ich þe wulle mid fare
mid mine drihtfolke and habben dale mid þe
 and halden þe for herre and here þe for lauerd
Þis feoreward was imaked heo ferden tosomne
Heo ferden from Spaine riht toward Brutaine
Armoriche heihte þat lond þer Brutaines noma nu on stond
Peytou heo letten on riht hond swa heo comen a þet lond
in are swiþe feire æ þer Læire falleþ i þa sæ
Seoue niht and enne dæi Brutus i þare hauene læi
 and he sende ȝeond þat lond and scawede þa leoden
Goffar þan king of Peyters nes hit noht iqueme
þat he iseh swlche sonden faren ȝeond his londe
Þe king heihte his wise men þe wel cuþen a speche
þat heo to þare sæ ferden þar þa ferde læi
 and iwusten at þon cnihten wet heo þer sohten
wheþer heo walden hælden griþ and greten þes londes king
þe heo wolden mid wiþere þan kinge wiþstonden
Numbert hehte þe aldermon þe sculde þas ernde don
Corineus wes ifaren to wode and draf þer þa wilde deor
mid hornen and mid hunden and mid fif hundred cnihten
Imetten heo faren Numbert þes kinges sonde of þat eard
Numbert heom to clepede mid ludere stefne
Whonene beo ȝe cnihtes Ȝe fareþ mid unrihte
Ȝe huntieþ i þes kinges friþe þerfore ȝe sculen beon fæie
Ȝe doþ þan kinge muchel scome þerfore ȝe sculen han grome
Forboden he haueþ his deorfriþ þerfore ȝe sculen liggen stif
Corineus iwerþ him wroþ and wende him toȝeines
 and saide þas ilke word mid muchelure wreþþe
Cniht þu ært muchel sot þat þu swa motest
Ȝif þe king hit haueþ forboden ne scal him neuer beo þa bet
ne nawit for his forbode nulle ich hit bileuen
to nimen his heortes and his hindes and al þa deor þat ich finde
Þa iwreþþede Numbert þa kinges stiward of þat eard
he leadde an his honde enne bowe stronge
 and he þene streng up braid balu com on ueste 
On he sette ane fla and he feondliche droh
 and þa fla lette gliden bi Corineus siden
Corineus bleinte and þene scute biberh
 and towardes Numbert he leop swilc hit an leon weora
 and þene bowe igreap mid muchele strengþe
He smot Numbert mid þon bowe þat his hæfdbon tobrec
þat his blod and his brain ba weoren todascte
Fluȝen his iferen feondliche swiþe
to þon kinge Goffar and saiden hine tiþende sære
þet islawen wes Numbert þe wes his awene stiward
Þe king wes swiþe særi and seorhful on mode
 and sende his sonde ȝeond his kinelonde
gaderede his ferde þer weoren men fæie
Þa ferde wes isumned and heo forþ fusden
toward sele Brutun þer he bi sæ wonede
Brutus wes swiþe war for wisdome him fulede
haures he sende to hirede þes kinges
to witen of his farcost wher he wolde feihten
Þa hawres ferden and sone aȝein comen
 and comen to heora læuarda þer he lai bi hauene
 and þeos word him seiden al swa hit soþ iwarþ
Hal beo þu Brutus Þu ert þe hexste of us
Nu hafþ Goffar þe king igadered his ferde
muchel ferd and riche and heȝe word he spekeþ
þat alle heo wullet quellen quic þat heo findeþ
 and þa scipen todraȝen and þa wif drenchen
Nulleþ heo leaue nenne of ous aliue
Brutus nom al his ȝunge folc and hem to scipe fusede
 and alle his æhte his folc bitahte
 and to heom seide Brutus þe sele
Ȝe beoþ mine leofe men Hercniaþ mine lare
Ne cume ȝe neauer wiþvten scipes bord ær ich ou sende sutelword
wheþer ich maȝe þe ufere hond habben of þan kinge
Brutus nom his cnihtes and iwende forþrihtes
to þon ilke weie þer him iwised wes
þer þe king walde forþ mid muchelere his ferde
Togadere heo comen hardliche heo onsloȝen
þer wes swiþe strong feht feollen þe feie
þer wes moni steap mon mid stele toswngen 
Longe a dai leste þat feht þer feol moni god cniht
Corineus com quecchen and to himseolfe queþ
Awæi Corineus Nere þu icoren kempa
Cuþ nu þine strengþa and þina stepa main
 and þisse Peytisce folc fal to þe grunde
Corineus heom rasde to swa þe rimie wulf
þane he wule on scheapen scaþewerc wrchen
Breid he mid swiþeren hond a sweord muchel and swiþe strong
al þat he þermid hitte al hit adun healde
Neora þa bearn nea swa strong þah he hefde brunie on
ȝif he hine mid sweorde atran nea ras he neuermare
Þa he hefde twa hundred mid sweorde tohewen
þa brac þat sweord in his hond riht be þere hilte
Þa wes wroþ Corineus and þas word cleopede
Wa wrþe auer þene smiþ þa þe mid honden smeoþþede
Corineus abuten biheold for þe bearn was abolȝen
 and igrap of onnes monnes honde ana wiæx swiþe stronge
al þat he neh com þermid he hit aquelde
Þe king sette to fleonne and al þa ferde eafter
 and Corineus heom eafter com kenliche swiþe
 and heom to clepede þe unimete kempa
Goffar mid þire ferde wi wolt þu fleam makian
Ne miht þu nawiht so fleon ȝif þu us wlt heonne fleman
þu most swiþer fehten er we heonne iwenden
Ne ganninde ne ridinde ne durste him nan abiden
Þe king hefde enne þein swiþe heard he was ihaten Suard
he biheold Corineum þe heom after com
Suard hefde to iferen þreo hundred ridearen
he wende onȝean sone and he ohtliche feaht
Nes hit noht longe þat Suard mihte stonde
for Corineus him geinde to mid his guþstrencþe
he gurde Suard on þat hæfd þat he grund sohte
 and he hine forsmat amidden a twa riht bi þon ribben
Nes þer nan swa stæþeli þat lengore mihte stonden
Corineus heom tobrutte ban and heora ribbes
 and ȝeond þat lond he heom todraf moni þusend þar abad
Þat folc þat flei Corineum þat com to Brutun
 and alle heo slowen þat heo neih comen
Þe king Goffar iseih his burst and unæþe himseolf atbreac 
he fleih ut of his londe and bilæfde his leode
Into France he ferde þer he freond funde
to þon kaisere and to his tueolf iferen
and tolde heom of þan balwe þe Brutus him hefde idon
Inne Franse weren italde twelfe iferan
þa Freinsce heo cleopeden dusze pers þa weren drihtliche men
kinges heo weoren icleopede þat heo ofte cuþden
Heo bihæihten Goffaren þen kinge þat heo hine wreken wolden
wreken hine of his unwines þat him þe eþere weorra
Heo senden ȝeond al France and buden heora ferda

 and Brutus ladde his ferde in Armorichen earde
 and he wes swiþe bliþe for his muchele biȝate
Ȝeond þat lond he gon ernen and þa tunes forbearnen
 and herȝede þat lond and tæh hit to his aȝre hond
Al þat lond he wiste and al he hit awalde
Swa he ferde mid his here þat he on ænne hul bicom
He wes feir and heih and he hine swiþe biheold
He nom ræd æt his monnen þat he wolde þar castel makian
Þa þe castel vp stod he wes strong and swiþe god
Nes hit buten lutel wile þat Goffar king com him liþen
mid vnimete ferde of Frenchisce folke
 and of alle þon londen þa leȝen into France
Þa Goffar þe king þene castel kennede
swa swiþe wa him was þat al his wit he forlæs
Swiþe he fusde þiderward kene his ferde
heo todælden heom atweolfa and tuȝen on alchere halue
 and þa Troynisce men heom comen aȝein
 and anan leiden to þan grunden of þane Freinsce þreo þusende
Þa Freinsce weoren isturmede and noþelas heo stal makeden
 and heo bi niþinges beard driuen heom onȝeinwærd
Brutun and his kempan heo driuen into þan castle
 and in þera ilke uore heo fælden of his iueren
 and æl dai heo ræmden and resden to þan castle
þat com to þere nihte þat lengre heo ne mihten
I þon castle wes muchel dred a þa midniht heo nomen read

mid alle þon folke þat he hefde on his ferde
 and ferden vt swa stille swa heo stelen wolden
into ane þicke wode þa þer on uest wes 
Brutus wes i þon castle and hine wel wuste
Amarwen þo hit dawede and dai com to folke
Brutus wes onbolȝen swa biþ þa wilde bær
wenne hundes hine bistondeþ i þon wodelonde
Brutus hehte his beornes don on heora burnan
 and heora wæpne gode for heo to feht sculden
Vp heo duden heora castles ȝæten and cofliche vt wenden
fusden to þan Freinscan and heo hem toȝan fengen
Þær wes feiht swiþe strong on alche halue hit wes stor
þer wes monies kunnes folc and moni cniht feie
Þer hefde Brutus enne mæi haihte Turnus
swa wod he was to fehte þat he feie iwerþ
He feolde þa Frensca on feole kunne wisen
mid his aȝene honden he falde monie hundred
ah he ferde to feor ut from his iueren
 and heo him to liþden on elchere siden
mid wepnen hine wundeden and seoþþen hine slowen

 and þerinne biburiȝede bi ane stan walle
Þuru þan ilka Turnus Turs wes ihaten

 and feht unimete fæie þer feollen
Þat feht wes wnder strong þa Corineus of wode com

Nes næuer þa mon iboren ne swa wis mon icoren

hu monie þusende þer weoren ileid to grunde
Þa bleou Brutus and bonnede his ferde
 and speken togadere of feole wisdomes

Heo letten lude clepian and cuþen ȝeond þat ferde

wind stod on willen þloȝede þe wilde fisc
þet water wes swiþe god gumen weoren bliþe
Liþden þa leoden þat heo on londe comen
æt Dertemuþe i Totenes wel wes Brutus þes

 and heora stelane flon fusden to þon feonden

 and i þon wilderne an hudlese wuneden
Hit ilomp on ane daȝe þat Brutus and his duȝeþe
makeden halinesse mid wrscipen heȝen

Þa comen þære twenti teon of þan munten

Þa heo best wende to fleonne þa weoren heo faie

 and he quic wes ibroht biforen Brutone
Brutus hine lette witen wel mid þan beste

Forþ com Corineus and fusde hine sulfne

laþliche læches heo leiteden mid eȝan
Al was heora gristbatinge al swa wilde bares eȝe

 and þus þe hæȝe scaþe ferde to helle
Nu and æuermare haueþ þat clif þare

 and mid swilce ræde þas eotentes weoren deade
Nu wes al þis lond iahned a Brutus hond 
Þa hæfde þa Troinisce men ouercomen heora teonen
þa weoren heo bliþe on heora breostþonke
þa makeden heo hus and hæleþes sikere
Heo makeden tunes heo tileden on eorþen

al heo tileden ase heo to þohten
for al hit wes heora aȝen þat heo ouer seȝen
Þis lond was ihaten Albion þa Brutus cum heron

ah scupte him nome æfter himseluan
He wes ihaten Brutus þis lond he clepede Brutaine
 and þa Troinisce men þa temden hine to hærre
æfter Brutone Brutuns heom cleopede
 and ȝed þe nome læsteþ and a summe stude cleouieþ faste

ana dala of his londa and sette hit him an honda
Þe lauerd hehte Corineus and þat lond Corinee

Heora aȝene speke Troinisce and seoþþen heo hit cleopeden Brutunisc
ah Englisce men hit habbeþ awend seoþþen Gurmund com in þis lond

Brutaine hefde Brutus and Cornwaile Corineus
Brutus nom alle his freond þe comen in his ferde
neh him he heom lænde for heo him leofe weoren

alle he heom lænde þer heom wes alre leofest
Weox þet folk and wel iþaih for ælc hefde his iwillen
Inne lut ȝeren firste wes þat folc swa muchel
þat þer nas nan ende of folke swiþe hende
Brutus hine biþohte and þis folc biheold

biheold he þa fisches biheold he þa fuȝeles

Þa biþohte he on Troyȝen þer his cun teone þoleden
and he liþde ȝeond þis lond and scæwede þea leoden
He funde wunsum ane stude vppen ane watere
þær he gon aræren riche ane burhe
mid bouren and mid hallen mid hæȝe stan walle
Þa þe burh wes imaked þa wes he swiþe mare
þa burh wes swiþe wel idon and he hire sette name on
he ȝef hire to hire tirfulne name Troye þe Newe
to munien his ikunde whone he icomen weore
Soþþen þa leodene longe þerafter
leiden adun þene noma and Trinouant heo nemneden
Binnen feola wintre hit iwerþ seoþþen
þat aræs of Brutus kunne þat was an heh king
Lud wes ihaten þas burh he luuede swiþe
Þe king i þere burh wonede swiþe feola wintre
he lette heo lude clepian ȝond his leodfolke
hehte heo nemnen Kaerlud æfter þone kinge
Seoþþen com oþer tir and neowe tidinde
þat men heo clepeden Lundin ouer al þas leode
Seoþþen comen Englisce men and cleopeden heo Lundene
Seþþen comen þa Frensca þa mid fehte heo biwonnen
mid heora leodþeawe and Lundres heo hehten
Þus is þas burh iuaren seþþen heo ærest wes areræd
þus is þis eitlond igon from honde to hond
þet alle þa burhȝes þe Brutus iwrohte
 and heora noma gode þa on Brutus dæi stode
beoþ swiþe afelled þurh warf of þon folke
Þa Brutus hefde imaked þa hehȝe burh þa Neowe Troie was ihaten
 and he lette fusen þarto muchel of his folke
He heom bitahte þa burh and iȝearwed mid þan beste
 and he heom onleide þat weoren lawen gode
He hehte þat luue scolde liþen heom bitweonen
ælc halden oþren riht ba bi daie and bi nith 
 and weaswa nolde he sculde beon iwite
 and swa vfele he mihte don þat he sculde beon ihon
For swulchen eiȝe gode heo hefden muchele drede
 and bicomen rihtwise men and rædes heo luueden
Hæfde Brutus þis lond fower and twenti winter on his hond
 and of Ignogen his quene he hefde þreo sunen scene
Þa heora fader wes dead alle heo nomen enne read
 and hine biburien in Newe Troye þere burhȝe
þat heora fader hefde imaked mid muchelure blisse
Seþþen þa þreo broþeren hi togadere comen
æl mid seahte and al mid luue þas leode todælden
Þe ældeste broþer Locrin wes ihaten
þe wes þe wiseste þe wes þe warreste
þe wes þe strengeste stif he wes on þonke
He hæfde to dæle þat suþ lond þat æfter him Locres wes icleped
 and Cambert hehte þe oþer þat wes þe midleste broþer
him þat lond to dale com þat Cambrie wes ihaten
þat is þat wilde lond þat Welsce men luuieþ
Seþþen hit is icleped Wales for þere quen Galoes
 and for þan duke Gualun Wælsce men me heom hateþ
Þe þridde broþer hehte Albanac seoþþen Humber hine biswac
Albanac nom his lond i þon norþ ende
þat nu ure leodene Scotlond clepiaþ
ah Albanac on his daȝe Albanie hit clepede
Locrines mær eode suþ and east forþ Albanac hefde al þat norþ
Camber hefde al himsulf bi westen Sæuarne
Þo þa þre breþeren hefden þis lond þa luueden heom þeos leoden
mid sibben and mid sahten seouentene winter
Æfter seouentene ȝere sone þeræfter
cum liþen to londe þat wes an leodisc king
Humber was ihaten king of Hunuze
vuele weoren his þewes his þeines weoren kene
He hefde moni lond awest and leodene biswikene
 and moni hundred eitlonde þa weoren bi sæstronde
mestendal alle heonne to Alamaine
Humber king and al his fleote and his muchele scipferde
comen on Albanackes londe and fuhten wiþ his leodene
mid fure and mid here mid feole kunne hærme

Al Albanakes folc folden iseohten
buten whilc þat þer atwond þurh wode burȝe

he ferde ouer Scotte water mid alle his wælkempan

 and himseolf mid wæne ferde into ane watere
Þerinne he adronc and mid him muchel folc
For Humber kinges deaþe Humbre was ihaten
Humber wiþ swiþe mucle an here in Alemaine hefde iherȝed
 and hefde þat lond swiþe awest and þat folc swiþe awemmed
He nom of þan monkunne þreo swiþe feire mæidene
Þeo an wes ihaten Astrild anes hahȝes kinges dohter
þa alre feireste wifmon þe þa wunede on folke

þe wuste Humberes fæi þe whilen he wende to fehten
Þa Humber was dead in Humbre adrunken
Locrin and Camber to þon scipen comen
for to habben al þa æhte þe Humber king aute
Imong þon scipmonnen i funden þa þreo maidenes

 and he heo mid armen inom eþ him wes on heorten
 and he hire to seide Sel þe scal iwurþen
wifmon þu eart hende and ic þe wlle habben 
mid wurþscipen hæȝe to richen are quene
þa while þe ic libbe oþer nulle ic habben
for þe ic am swa bliþe swa næs I næuer ær on liue
Þa ȝet leouede Corineus þe in Cornwaile wes dux
nefde he bute æne dohter ah heo wes him swiþe deore

ah for Æstrilde luue he heo wolde bilæuen
Þis iherde Corineus þe wes in Cornwaile dux
þet his leoue dohter wes Locrin atlaþed
Corineus wes uneþe and wa on his mode
He ferde to þisse londe þat he com to Locrine
He lædde on his exle ane muchele wieax
He stod biforen Locrine and laþelich him lokede on
 and þas word him iqueþ Corineus þe kempa
Seie me Locrin saie me læþe mon
saie me þu ebare sot seorwe þe beoþ ȝeueþe
ne scal þe nan man scilden wiþ scondliche deaþe
Þu hauest mine dohter þat is mi bearn deore
 and me seolfan iscend þerfore þu scalt scrinkin
Ic liþde mid þine fader and ledde his ferde
moni swinc moni swæt monine seorhfulne pleiȝe
moni grimne reas moni greatne dunt
moni ane wnde moni wnderlich feht
þolede ich on folde biforen Brutone
þe wes mi deore wine mi drihliche lauerd
Þerfore þu scalt beon feie for nes he neuer þi fader
for ȝif þu were Brutus sune ne deodest þu me nane sceome
For his luue moni eotend ic leide dead a þene grund
an þu mi muchele swinc mid sare forȝeldest
bileafest feier and sceone mine dohter Guendoleine
for alþeodisc meiden Æstrild ihate
Þu nast of whulche londe heo com heder liþen
ne whulc king is hire fader ne whulc quen hire moder
Ah þu scalt habben for hire luue þat þe is alre laþest
þat al þu scalt toscæne mid scearpe mire eaxe
Corineus up ahof and his eax adun sloh
and smat in enne muchele stane þer Locrin stod vuenan
Þe stan al tosceande and Locrin atsturte
Alle heo hiȝeden to an elcher halfe 
 and todeleden heom atwa teona wes on hirde
þer wes moni hah word
 and þa alre seleste eoden tosumne
hulden muchel husting þa hehste of þan hirde
þat heo nolden iþolian for alþeodene gold
þat þeos laþþe weore bituxe Corineo and Locrine
Ah we wlleþ ræden and we wlleþ runan
þat weo nimen Wændoleine Locrine to are quene
 and halden alle vre aþes bitwux Corineo and Locrine
 and halden hiredes luue mid soþfasten huiȝe
 and senden Æstrilde vt of þissen londe
 and Locrin þis biluuede for hit wes his leodene read
He nom Guendoleine and hefde heo to wiue
 and he hit seide soþ þeih hit nere
þat he wolde Æstrilde senden vt of londe
Ah ne dude he nawiht swo for swiken he þohte
ah he nom his enne hiredmon þe he wel trowede on
 and hehte hine swiþe stille steolen vt of hirede
 and hehte hine faren to þon tune þe Trinouant wes ihaten
þe wes on vre leoden Lundene ihaten
 and þar an hiȝinge þurhut alle þinges
makian an eorþhus eadi and feier
þe walles of stone þe duren of whales bone
 and þat inne swiþe feire stude from socne þes folkes
 and dude þerinne muchel col and claþes inowe
pælles and purpras and guldene ponewæs
muchel win muchel wex muchel wunsum þing
 and seoþþen forþrihtes wende al bi nihte
 and mid stilliche ginne brohte Æstrild þerinne
Þus dude þes riche mon swa Locrin hine hefde ihaten
for euerulc god mon ah his lauerdes heste to don
Seouen ȝer wes Astrild i þissen eorþhuse
þat neuer ne ferde heo wiþuten dore ne na mon heo þer nuste
buten þe king Locrin and his iueren mid him
Þonne he to Trinouant wende þenne seide he to Wendoleine
þat he wolde beon seoueniht þære and his godd hure
inne diȝelnesse and elles he ne durste
þat ei mon wuste whet he þer sohte
Guendoleine him ilefede luþere weren his craftes
Þus ferde Locrin þe wilde þat Astrild wes mid childe
 and Guendoleine alswa mid childe heo weren ba twa 
Ane dohter hefde Æstrild inne þon eorþhuse
þe king heo lette fulwen æfter þon lawen þe stoden a þon ilke dawen
heo wes ihaten Abren nes feirure child nan
 and Guendoleine hefde enne sune an heorte hire wes þa bet
Madan he was ihaten heh sune þes kinges
Þis child weox and wel iþei and al folk hit wes leof
Þa he cuþe gan and speken wiþ folke
þe king Locrin hine nom his feire sune Madan
 and to Corinee hine sende into his londe
þat he hine sculde wel iteon and tuhlen him teachen
 and swa he dude mid mæine þa while þe he mihte
Þa com þe time gliden þa ælc monne abideþ
þat Corineus þe stronge makede his liues ende
Þet iherde þe king hit wes him swiþe queme
Þa he wuste to soþe þat Corineus was dead
he nom of his hirde tweolf hende men
 and Guendoleine he sende into hire fader londe
into Cornwaile into hire cuþþe
Þa wæs Guendoleine at hame and hire sune Madan
 and swiþe heo hit mænde to alle monnen
þe hire fader wolde þe while he wes on liue
Heo gæderede tosumne alle hire sibbe freond
 and alle þa knites þe heo biȝeten mihte
 and alle þat cuþe folk þat hire freond weoren
 and alle þa vncuþe to hire comen
of wel feola londe for seoluere and for golde
 and heo rumliche hit ȝef gode þon kempan
 and bæd heom for heora wurþscipe wreken hire teonan
Hæfde Locrin þe king inomen to him Æstrild
heo wes him iqueme and he heo hæfde to quene
Vnder þissere blisse þer comen muchele burstes
Me cudde Locrine þe wes þisse leodene king
þat Guendoleine mid ferde fusde to þisse londe
to wreken hire teona of þon kinge and of þer quene
Þe king mid his folke fusde hire toȝeines
 and heo togadere comen vppen ane watere
þat water hatte Stoure þat feiht was swiþe sturne
inne Deorsete Locrin deaþ þolede
on arwe him com to heorte þat he adun halde
þer he wes feie and muchel of his ferde 
 and þa quike men atflowen and muchel fleam makeden
Guendoleine hæfde þa vfere hond and iahnede hire al þis lond
 and heo ferde to þan castle þer Æstrild wes inne
heo nom Æstrild and Abren and lette heom ibinden
 and lette heom worpen in ane deope watere
þer heo adronken and þer heo deaþ þoleden
Þa wes Guendoleine leodene læfdi
Þa hehte heo ane heste mid haiȝere witte
þat me sculde þat ilke water þer Abren wes adrunken
clepian hit Auren for þane mæidene Abren
 and for Locrines lufe þe wes hire kinelouerd
þe streonede Abren vppen Astrild
Þa hefde heo isclawen þene king and þa neowe quene and heora child
 and Auren hatte ȝet þas æ at Cristeschirche heo falleþ i þare sæ
Guendoleine wes swiþe strong for al Brutenne wes on hire hond
 and heo was swa swiþe wel biþouht þat ælche monne heo dude riht
Ælch mon mihte faren ȝend hire lond þaih he bere ræd gold
Ten ȝer heo wes mid Locrine often heo hæfde seorwe and pine
Fiftene ȝer and niȝen dawæs seoþþen Locrin wes dead
al Brutaine heo wuste wel mid þon beste
inne griþe and in friþe wun wes on folke
Seoþþen heo ȝef Madan an hond al his fader kinelond
To Cornwaile he ferde aȝein þe hire fader ahte
 and þer heo wonede in þon londe þa leoden weoren þe bliþre
Madan hire sune nom a wif þe wes swiþe hende
Bi hire he hæfde twein sunen ah beine heo weoren unseli
Menbriz haihte þe aldre Malin þe ȝungre
Ah fourti wintre heore fader Madan mid mensca heold his riche
 and þa his liues ende com he wende swiþe wel to don
his tuæin sunan he sette on hond al his riche kinelond
Ah þa heora fader wes dæd þe sunen duden vuelne ræd
Bitweonen heom aræs wale and win wiþer heo weoren beien
sleȝht and muchel seorwa al for heora uniselþe
Ah Menbriz dude vnwreste he wes swike mid þan meste
wiþ Malin his broþer he nom griþ and bihahte to halden friþ
 and swa he nom enne dai þat come heore drihtliche folc
to makian saht and some bituxen him and his broþer
A þon daie þat wes iset þa comen heo tosumne
Membriz hefde inomen þat griþ ah sone he makede unfriþ 
he dude þer serwe inoh for þer he his broþer ofsloh
 and þus he iwon al þis lond þat hit stod on his awene hond
Membriz hatede al his cun for non nes him iqueme
þa riche he makede wrecchas þa hæne hine awarieden
Ȝif þar was swa hah mon þat he ne durste fordon
mid attere he hine adrengte þat he sone dæd wes
A wif he nom swiþe hende enne sune on hire he streonede
Ebrauc he wes icleped ȝeond al he wes cuþ
Menbriz dude an vuel weorc and him ec þa wrse ilomp
vuel þing him wes iqueme he forheowede al his quene
His hiredmen he nom to bedde and wifmen he al bilafde
Twenti ȝer he heold þis lond þa leoden al to hærme
 and seoþþen him a time com mid teonen he wes ifunden
þat he to wode wende to wundre himseoluan
to huntien after deoren werfore he deþ þolede
In þon wode he funde feier ane hinde
þa hunten wenden æfter mid muchelen heora lude
Swa swiþe heo liþþeden forþ þat þe king heom forleas
þat nefde he næfer enne of alle his monnen
He bicom in a bæch þer he bale funde
vppen ane weorede of wlfan awedde
Heo him to lupen on alchere halue
 and toluken þene king and his leomen todrowen
 and his hors alswa þat deade heo weoren bo twa
 and þus ferde Membriz þe his broþer biswac Malin
Enne sune he hafde bi seoluan his quene
þe was ihaten Ebrauc æþelest alre kingen
þe æuer sculde halden lond oþer biwiten leode
Al his cun he wurþede richen and wrecchen
þa richen he lette beon stille þa wrecchen hefden heore wille
þat lond heo lette tilien him tuwen hiredmen to
blisse wes on londe a feole kunne þinge
Heo heold swiþe god griþ ne breac na man his friþ
Cnihtes he hæfde gode stronge and wode
heo wilneden after worre for heom wes heora Drihten wroþ
Þe king hit wel wuste þeh he hit suggen ne durste
He lætte bi sæflode ȝearkien scipen gode
vmben ane stunde þa scipen ȝaru weoren
 and he dude þerinne his drihtliche cnites
 and sende heom into France mid muchelere ferde 
 and heo herȝeden France and feor þer biȝeonden
 and alle þa londes þa þerto leȝen
Muchel wes þa gersume þe heo hæfden inome
 and comen eft hider ham al isund and ihal
Þes wes þe æreste king þe ferde vt to ræuing
þat ouer sæ wende vt of þisse londe
Swiþe longe þerafter wes al þis leodisc folc
vnimete riche of þere ræuinge
Þa com hit to mode Ebrauc þon gode
þat he wolde bulden twa burh stronge
He nom his folc and ferde forþ and droh him rites norþ
a þas half Scotlonde þer he wolde atstonde
Ærest he makede ane burh and Kaer Ebrauc heo clepede
þa oþer on are dune Adud he heo hahte
Þa heo wes icleped Kaer Ebrauc seþþen wes icleped Eborac
Seoþþen comen vncuþe men and Eoverwic heo hahten
 and þa norþerne men nis hit nawiht ȝeare
þurh ane unþewe Ȝeorc heo ihæhten
Þa ferde þe king norþur ma and ane neowe burh makede
vppen Angnetes munte mærliche feier
Maidene Castel he wes icleoped nat ich for wan hit was swa idon
Ebrauc leofede swiþe longe and lond heold mid mensce
Sixti winter he wes king i griþe he heold his kinelond
Ah he hæfde moni wif þe his cun of awachede
he hefde on liue tuenti sunen and alc hefde sundri moder
he wes þritti dohtrenne fader þeo wifmen weoren feire
Of his sunen hercne þa nomen and ich heo þe wulle nemnen
Brutus Uært Escut Margadud Sisiluius Regin Bladud
Moruit Lagon Ebedloan Ricar Spaden Gaul Pardan
Ældad Gangu Kerin Luor Ruc Assarac Buel Hector
Þeos weoren Ebraukes sunen þes aþeles kinges
His dohter nomen hercna nu þa hæȝe weoren iborene
Þa eldeste was ihaten Gloigin Ocidas Ourar Ignogen
Guardid Radan Guendlian Angarad Guenboden Meþelan
Malure Ecub Zangustel Scadud Kambreda Methahel
Gaz Echem Nest Gorgon Wladus Ebræn Blangru Egron
Bedra Aballac Eangnes Andor Scadiald Galoes 
Efter þissere Galoes Wales wes inemned
Galoes wes feirest of alle þan oþren
leouest þone kinge of þan sustren and of þon breoþeren
 and Anoþer wes alre best itowen hire tuhtlen weren gode
Gloigin hehte þa alre elduste þeo wes þurh alle þing þa æþeleste
alle heo weoren wel bihedda
Þe king of Lumbardie Siluius he wes heora nexta cunnesmon
richeliche he nom his sonde and sende to Ebrauke kinge of þisse londe
He bad hine senden him alle his dohtren
 and he heom wolde ȝeuen richen his monnen
swiþe riche cnihten of Troinisce cunne
þa weoren in Lumbardie of heore strund þah stræmes heom todæleden
 and þa wifmen of Lumbardie weoren heom swiþe laþe
for þi þe king sende after þisse maidenen to ȝeuen his riche monnen
swa he dude and þus hit wes wa wes Lumbardisce folc þes
Þa hefde þe king Siluius his wille and Lumbardie he walde
 and al his Troinisce cun tuhten to himseoluan
Summe þa breoþeren Ebraukes sunen comen þider mid heora sustren
Heo biȝeten wepnen heo biȝeten scipen heo biȝeten men þe heom cuþen witen
heo senden ouer al þan ærde to biȝeten muchele ferde
Þa comen þas cnihtes ut of Brutaine ferden of Lumbardie to Alamaigne
Assarac þe com ut of þissen eard his broþren hine cleopeden heora lauerd
Heo færden mid ȝeapscipe and mid wisdome swa longe þat heo to Alamaine comen
Muchele castles heo bigunnen heo slowen heo barnden and þæt lond biwunnen
Ebrauc heora fader heold þis lond sixti winter he wes heore king
He hæfde her his eldeste sune iholden mid himseoluan
his nome wes wel wide cuþ he hehte Brutus Uært Escud
Tueolf ȝer he heold þis kinelond seoþþen his fader hit bilefde
Ænne sune he hefde ihaten Leil he heold þis kinelond after him
fulle fif and twenti ȝer æfter his fader daie
He makede ane heȝe burh feier and hende
to imonien Leil þene king and Kaer Leil heo clepede
In alle þon norþ ende nes nan burh swa hende 
Leil þe king heold wel þis lond and lawen he hafde stronge
ah toward his lifes ende him ilomp wel luþere
þat alle his riche eorles and alle his heȝe beornes
makeden muchel unfriþ and for þon kinge heo nolden holden griþ
Nefden heo of heore kinge buten heora scærninge
 and euerælc wilde mon hefde al his wil to don
Þa iwerþ þe king sec þurh hefeȝere seorwe
 and sone þerafter com þe dai þat þe king dead lai
Þes king hefde enne sune þe wes swiþe god mon
he wes swiþe god knit Ruhhudibras ihaten
Þe cniht nom þæs riche and þene kinedom æke
 and niȝen and þritti winter he heold þæs leoden
æfter leuen his fader þe Leil was ihaten
He sette þis lond he sahtnesse wrohte
he sette stronge lawen he wes sturne þon dusien
he luuede þeo leoden þe his lawen heolden
Æueralcne godne mon he aþelede mid gode
he hehte hælden griþ and friþ vppe leome and vppe lif
He makede ane riche burh and hehte heo Winchestre
swlc werc him þuhte swiþe muri and seoþþen he makede Cantwareburi
 and Cestesburi castel an Waladunes dune
Ne com nauer seoþþen nan swa seolcuþ þing
þat an muchel ærn spec a þon castle þer he set
þet Ruhhudibras þe king himseolf hit iherde
 and alle his cnihtes þe mide him weoren
Þes fuȝel tacnede faiesiþ þes kinges
Ruhhudibras was sone dead wa wes his duhþen
His sune hehte Bladud he wes a swiþe bisi mon
he wes strong and swiþe muchel riche he wes and mæhti
he cuþe þene vuele craft þat he wiþ þene Wurse spæc
 and al þat euer he wolde þe Wurse him talde
Þes ilke king Bladud Baþen iwrohte
þurh swiþe muchele ginne mid ane stæncunne
al swa great swa a beam þe he leide in ane wallestream
Þe ilke makeþ þat water hot and þan folc halwende
He makede an temple onfest þe baþe an ære hæhtnesse nome
þe hire nome wul iheren Minerue heo was ihaten
To hire he hefde loue and læfdi heo hehte 
In þere temple he lette beornen enne blase of fure
þe neuer ne aþeostrede wintres ne sumeres
ah euer me þat fur bette swa þe king haihte
to wrþscipe his læfdi þe leof him wes on heorten
Þus dude Bladud þe king þat him wes wide cuþ
Þa he hefde þus idon þæ þohte he on oþer
He ȝealp þat he wolde fleon on fuȝeles læche
þat al his folc mihte iseon and his fluhtes bihalden
He makede his feþerhome and þaruore he hæfde muchel scome
To Lunden he ferde mid muchelen his folke
his feþerhome he dude him on and he his fluht þer bigon
Mid wiȝeful his fluhte tæih him to þon lufte
he ferde swiþe hehȝe þere weolcne he wes swiþe nih
Þe wind him com on wiþere weoþeleden his fluhtes
brecon þa strenges þe he mid strahte
 and he feol to folde þe king wes feie
vppen are stouwe þe i Lundene stod
Appollones temple þe wes þe tirfulle Feond
þe king feol on þene rof þat he al todraf
Þus wes þas kineriche of heora kinge biræued
Tuenti winter hafde Bladud þas kinelond an hond
æfter his fader Ruhhudibras þe Leil sune þes riche kinges wes
Bladud hafde enne sune Leir wes ihaten
Efter his fader daie he heold þis drihliche lond
somed an his liue sixti winter
He makede ane riche burh þurh radfulle his crafte
 and he heo lette nemnen efter himseoluan
Kaer Leir hehte þe burh leof heo wes þan kinge
þa we an ure leodquide Leirchestre clepiaþ
Ȝeare a þan holde dawen heo wes swiþe aþel burh
 and seoþþen þer seh toward swiþe muchel seorwe
þat heo wes al forfaren þurh þere leodene uæl
Sixti winter hefde Leir þis lond al to welden
Þe king hefde þreo dohtren bi his drihliche quen
nefde he nenne sune þerfore he warþ sari
his manscipe to halden buten þa þreo dohtren
Þa ældeste dohter haihte Gornoille þa oþer Ragau þa þridde Cordoille
Heo wes þa ȝungeste suster a wliten alre vairest
heo wes hire fader al swa leof swa his aȝene lif 
Þa ældede þe king and wakede an aþelan
 and he hine biþohte wet he don mahte
of his kineriche æfter his deie
He seide to himsuluen þat þat vuel wes
Ic wlle mine riche todon allen minen dohtren
 and ȝeuen hem mine kineþeode and twemen mine bearnen
Ac ærst ic wille fondien whulchere beo mi beste freond
and heo scal habbe þat beste del of mine drihlichen lond
Þus þe king þohte and þeræfter he worhte
He clepede Gornoille hes guþfulle dohter
vt of hire bure to hire fader deore
 and þeus spac þe alde king þer he on æþelen seat
Sei me Gornoille soþere worden
swiþe dure þeo eart me hu leof æm ich þe
Hu mochel worȝ leste þu me to walden kineriche
Gornoille was swiþe wær swa beoþ wifmen wel ihwær
 and seide ane lesinge heore fædere þon king
Leofe fæder dure swa bide ich Godes are
swa helpe me Apollin for min ilæfe is al on him
þat leuere þeo ært me æne þane þis world al clane
 and ȝet ic þe wlle speken wit þeou ært leouere þene mi lif
 and þis ich sucge þe to seoþe þu mith me wel ileue
Leir þe king ilefde his doster læisinge
 and þas ænsware ȝef þat waes þe olde king
Ich þe Gornoille seuge leoue dohter dure
god scal beon þi meda for þira gretinge
Ic eam for mire ælde swþe vnbalded
 and þou me leuoste swþe mare þan is on liue
Ich wille mi dirhliche lond a þroe al todalen
þin is þat beste deal þu ært mi dohter deore
 and scalt habben to lauerd min alre beste þein
þeo ich mai uinden in mine kinnelonde
Æfter spac þe olde kinge wit his oþer dohter
Leoue dohter Regau waet seist tu me to ræide
Seie þu bifore mire duȝþen heo dure ich am þe an herten
Þa answærde mid rætfulle worden
Al þat is on liue nis me swa dure 
swa me is þin an lime forþe min ahȝene lif
Ah heo ne seide naþing soþ no more þenne hiire suster
Alle hire lesinge hire uader ilefede
Þa answarede þe king hiis doȝter him icwemde
Þea þridde del of mine londe ich bitake þe an honde
þu scalt nime louerd þer þe is alre leowost
Þa ȝet nolde þe leodking his sothscipe bilæuen
he hehte cumen him biforen his dohter Gordoille
Heo was alre ȝungest of soþe ȝærwitelest
 and þe king heo louede more þanne ba tueie þe oþre
Cordoille iherde þa lasinge þe hire sustren seiden þon kinge
nom hire leaffulne huie þat heo liȝen nolden
hire fader heo wolde suge seoþ were him lef were him laþ
Þeo queþ þe alde king vnrad him fulede
Iheren ich wlle of þe Cordoille
sua þe helpe Appollin hu deore þe beo lif min
Þa answarede Cordoille lude and nowiht stille
mid gomene and mid lehtre to hire fader leue
Þeo art me leof also mi fæder and ich þe also þi dohter
Ich habbe to þe sohfaste loue for we buoþ swiþe isibbe
 and swa ich ibide are ich wille þe suge mare
Al swa muchel þu bist woruh swa þu velden ært
 and al swa muchel swa þu hauest men þe wllet luuien
for sone heo biþ ilaȝed þe mon þe lutel ah
Þus seide þe mæiden Cordoille and seoþþen set swþe stille
Þa iwarþe þe king wærþ for he nes þeo noht iquemed
 and wende on is þonke þat hit weren for vnþeawe
þat he hire weore swa unwourþ þat heo hine nold iwurþi
swa hire twa sustren þe ba somed læsinge speken
Þe king Leir iwerþe swa blac swlch hit a blac cloþ weoren
iwærþ his hude and his heowe for he was suþe ihærmed
mid þere wræþþe he wes isweued þat he feol iswowen
Late þeo he up fusde þat mæiden wes afeared
Þa hit alles up brac hit wes vuel þat he spac
Hærne Cordoille ich þe telle wlle mine wille
Of mine dohtren þu were me durest nu þu eært me arle læþest
Ne scalt þu halden dale of mine lande 
ah mine dohtren ich wlle delen mine riche
 and þu scalt worþen warchen and wonien in wansiþe
for nauere ich ne wende þat þu me woldes þus scanden
Þarfore þu scalt beon dæd ich wene fliȝ ut of min eæhsene
Þine sustren scullen habben mi kinelond and þis me is iqueme
Þe Duc of Cornwaile scal habbe Gornoille
 and þe Scottene king Regau þat scone
 and ic hem ȝeue al þa winne þe ich æm waldinge ouer
 and al þe alde king dude swa he hafuede idemed
Ofte wes þen mæidene wa and næure wors þenne þa
wa hire wes on mode for hire fader wærþe
Heo uende into hire boure þar heo ofte sætte sare
for heo nolde liȝen hire fadder leoue
Þat maide wes swþen swomefest for hire fader heo scunede
 and dude þene beste red in hire bure heo abed
 and þolede þene modkare and mornede swþe
 and þus ane stonde hit stod æ þon ilka
In France wes a king riche and swiþe kene
Aganippes wes ihaten hæleþen he wes ældere
He wes a ȝenge king ah quene nauede he nane
He sende hiis sande into þisse lande
to Leir þan king and leofliche hine gret
He bæd hine don is iwille ȝeuen him Cordoille
 and he heo wolde habben hæȝe to are quene
 and æfter hire don ærest þat hire were alre leofust
Feor haueden liþende men ispeken of þan mæidene
feiȝernesse and freoscipe atforen þan Frensce kinge
of hire mucla fæira wlita of hire muchela monschipe
hu heo wes þolemod of fæire hire þeæwen
þat nes on Leir kinges lond nan wifman al swa hende
 and þe king Aganippus igrette Leir kin þus
Leir kin hine biþohte wat he don mohte
he letten writen a writ and wel hit lette dihten
 and sende hit bi his sonde in Frauncene londe
Þus spec þes kinges writ hit wes widen icuþ
Þe kinge of Bruttaine þe Leir is haten
greteþ Aganippus þene aldere of Fraunce
Worþschepe haue þu þire weldeda
 and þire feire sonde þat grete þu me woldest 
Ac ich do þe wel to witene hær bi mine writ rith
þat mi drihliche lond atwa ich habbe ideled
iȝeuen hit mine twam dohtren þe me beoh swiþe deore
Dohter ich habbe þa þridda ac ne ræcche ich wær heo libbe
for heo me forhuste and heo hold me for hæne
 and for mire halde heo me unælede
heo makede me swa swiþe wraþ þe worse hire scal iwurþen
of alle mine londe ne of alle mine leode
þe ich auere biȝeat oþer biȝete mæie
ich þe sucge soþriht na scal heo habbe nawiht
Ac ȝef þu heo wult habben for mæide heo is hende
ich heo wulle þe biwiten and senden ha þe in ane scipe
mid seoluen hire claþen of me nafþ heo na more
Ȝif þu heo wult underfon al þis ilka ich wulle don
Iseid ich habbe þene grund and þu seolf wurþ al hisund
Þis writ com to Fraunce to þan freo kinge
He hit lette raden leof him weren þa runen
Þa wende þe kinge þat hit were for vuele
þat Leir kinge hire fæder heo him wolde atleden
 and he mochul a þa wodeloker wilnede þeos mæidenes
 and seide to is bornen þat wes þa bisie king
Ich eam riche mon inoh þat na mare ich ne recche
ne scal neuere Leir king þat mæiden me attlede
ac ich heo wulle habben to hæhȝere are quene
Habben heore fader al is lond al hiis seoluer and is gold
Ne bidde ich nanne maþmes me seolf ich habben inoȝe
bute þat mæiden Cordoille þenne hæbbe ich mine wille
Mid writ and mid worde he sende eft to þisse londe
 and bad Leir king him sende his dohter þe wæs hende
 and he wolde wel don mid muchele worþescipe heo underfon
Þa nom þa olde king æþele his meiden
mid seoluen hire claþes and lette heo forþe liþen
ofer þa stremes hire fader hire wes sturne
Aganippus þe Frennsce king vnderfeng þis meiden child
al hiis folc hit wes iqueme and makeden heo to quene
 and þus heo þer bilefde leof heo wes þon leoden
 and Leir king hire fæder luuede i þisse londe
 and hadde iȝeuen is twain dohtren al his drihliche leand 
He ȝef Gornoille Scotlondes kinge
he hæhte Maglaunus his mæhte weren store
Cornwailles duke Regau is dohter
Þa ilomp hit seoþþe sone þaræfter
þat þe Scottene king and þe duk speken togaþere
mid heore stil rune nome hem to reda
þat heo wolden al þis lond habben on heora hond
 and feden Leir þane king þe while þe he leouede
dæies and nihtes mid feowerti hiredcnihtes
 and heo him wolden finden hauekes and hundes
þat he mihte riden ȝeond alle þanne þeoden
 and libben on lisse þe while þe he leouede
Þus heo þa ispeken and eft hit tobreken
 and Leir king hit iherde and eft him wes þe worsse
 and Leir gan liþe to Scottenæ leoda
Mid Maglaune his aþume and mid þere eldre dohtre
Me vnderfenge þene king mid mochele feirnusse
 and wel me him dihte mid feowerti hiredcnihtes
mid horsen and mid hundes mid al þet him biheovede
Þa hilomp hit seoþþen seone þerafter
þe Gornoille biþohte whet heo don mihte
Heore þuhte swiþe eille of æþelene hire fædere
 and heo hit bigan to mainen to Maglaune hire louerde
and seide him ibedde þer heo leiin iueore
Seie me mi lauerd monne þu ert me leouest
me þuncheþ þat mi fæder nis nowhit felle
no he wurhscipe ne can his wit he hauet bileued
Me þuncheþ þe alde mon wole dotie nou nan
He halt here fauwerti cnihtes daies and nihtes
he haueht her þas þeines and alle heore swaines
hundes and hauekes þeruore we habbet harmes
and nowher heo ne spedet and auere heo spenet
 and al þat goud þat we hem doþ heo hit bluþeliche vnderfoþ
and cunnen us vnþonc for ure weldede
Heo doþ muchel bisemære ure men hi tobetet
mi fader hauet to monie of idele manne 
Ale þa feorþe dale lete we forþ fuse
inoh he hauet on þirti to þirngen to borde
Vs selve we habbet cokes to quecchen to cuchene
vs sulue we habbet bermen and birles inowe
Lete we sum þis mochele folc fare wher ha wulleþ
swa ich æuere ibiden are iþolien nulle ich hit mare
Þis iherde Maglaunus þat is quene spilede þus
 and he hire andswarede mid aþelere spiche
Leiuedi þu haues mochel wouh nauest þu richdom inoh
Ah hald þine fæder on lisse ne luueþe he nowiht longe
For ȝef ferrene kinges hiherde þa tidinde
þe we swa takede him on heo us wolden tælen
Ah late we hine welden his folc on his willen
and þis min aȝe ræd is for sone heræfter he beþ dead
 and ac we habben in ure hond al half is kinelond
Þa seide Gornoille Lauerd beo þeu stille
let me al iwurþen and ich ham wulle atwailden
Heo sende mid hire ginne to þare cnihtene inne
heo hahte hem faren here wæi for heo nolden hem no more feden
moni of þen þeinen monie of þen sweinen
þe þider weren icumene mid Leir þanne kinge
Þis iherde Leir king þarfore he wes swuþe wrah
þa iȝedede þe king mid ȝemeliche worden
and þus seide þe kinge sorhful on mode
Wa worþe þan monne þe lond haueþe mid menske
and bitachet hit is childe þe while þe he mai hit walden
for ofte hit ilimpþ þat eft hit him ofpincheþ
Nu ich wulle hunne faren forþrihte to Cornwalen
ȝernen ich wulle rædes to Regau mire dohter
þe hauede Hemeri þe duc and mi drihliche lond
Forhd þe king wende into þan suþ ende
to Regau is dochter for rædes him trukeden
Þa he to Cornwale com he wes feire þer vnderfon
swa al þet halue ȝer mid al his hirede he wes þer
Þa saide Regau to hire duc Hemeri
Lauerd herne þu me to fulle soþe ich sucge hit þe
We habbet idon unwisdom þat we mine fader habbet vnderfon 
mid þirtti cnihten hit nis me noht iqueme
Do we awai þane twenti a tene beoþ inohȝe
for al heo dringket and eteþ and na god heo ne biȝeteþ
Þa seide Hemeri þe duc þe his alde fader biswake
Swa ich eæuere beo on liue ne scal he habben beote fiue
for þer he hauet hirde hinoh for he nauyt no doþ
 and ȝef he wille henne faren fuse we hine sone
Al heo ispedden ase heo ispeken hafden
binomen him is doȝeþe and al his drihliche folc
nolden heo him bileafuen cnihtes beoten fiue
Þis iseh Leir þe king wa wes him on liue
His mod him gon mengen he morȝnede swiþe
and þas worde seide mid seorhfulle laichen
Wela weolla wella hu þu biswikest monine mon
Þenne he þe treoweþe alre best on þenne biswikes tu heom
Nis hit nowit ȝare noht fulle twa ȝere
þat ich was a riche king and held mine cnihtes
Nu ich habben ibiden þat ich bare sitte
wunnen biræued wa is me on liue
Ich wes at Gornoille mire godfulle dohter
wuneden on hire leoden mid þritti cnihtes
þe ȝet ich mihte libben ah þenne igonne liþen
Ich wende swiþe wel to don ac wurse ich habbe vnderfon
Aȝen ich wulle to Scotte to scone mire docter
ȝernen hira milcea þat heo me nele wurdea
bidden heo me vnderfon mid mine fif cnihten
Þer ich wulle wunie and þolie þeos wænen
ane lutele stunde for ne libbe ich nowiht longe
Leir þe king wende forh to is dohter wunede norþ
Fulle þre nihtes heo hærabarewude hine and is cnihtes
heo swor a þane ferþe dæi bi al heuenliche main
þat ne sculde he habben mare bute enne kincte þere
and ȝef he þet nolde ferde wuder he wolde
Wel oft wes Leir wa and neuere wurs þanne þa
Þa seide þe alde king æruu e was on herten 
Wallan dæþ wela deaþ þat þu me nelt fordemen
Seoþ seide Cordoille for cuþ hit is me nouþe
mi ȝengestte dohter heo was me wel dure
seoþþen heo me wes leaþest for heo me seiden alre sohust
þat me biþ vnworþ and lah þe mon þe litul ah
and ihc nas na wurdra þenne ich nes weldinde
Ouer soh seiden þat ȝunge vifmon hire folweþ mochel wisdom
Þa wile þe ich hæuede mi kinelond luueden me mine leoden
for mine londe and for mine feo mine eorles fulle to mine cneo
Nu ich æm a wrecche mon ne leouet me no mon for þan
Ah mi dohter me seide seoh for nou ich hire ileue inoh
 and ba twa hire susteren lasinge me seiden
þat ich ham wes swa leof leuere þenne hire aȝe lif
 and Cordoille mi dohter dohȝeþe me seide
þat heo me leouede swa feire swa monnes fader scolde
Wet wold ich bidde mare of mire dohter dure
Nu ich wullen faren feorþ and ouer sæ fusen
ihiren of Cordoille wat beon hire wille
Hire seohþe word ich nam to grame þarfore ich habbe nu muchele scame
for nu ich mot bisecchen þat þing þat ich ær forhowede
Nule heo me do na wurse þanne hire lond forwurnen
Leir ferde to þere sæ mid ane alpie swein
into ane schipe he bicom ne icnwo hine no mon
ouer sea icomen hauene sone anomen
Forþ wende þe king Leir nauede he bute enne swein
Hi axeden þa quene þat heo comen hire a neweste
tahten heom leode wer wes þes londes quene
Leir king wende on anne feld and reste hine on folden
and is swein he forþ sende þe wes iradmon hende
to þere quene Cordoille and seide hire wel stille
Hail wurþ þu feire quene Ich eam þines fader sweine
and þi uader is hider ikimen for al is lond is him binomen
Beoþ ba þine sustren touward him forsworene
He cumeþ for neode into þisse leode
and help him nu for þu miht he is þi fader alse hit is riht
Þe quene Cordoille seæt longe swþe stille
Heo iward reode on hire benche swilche hit were of winescenche
and þe swain sæt at hire fæit sone þerafter him wes þe bet 
Þa alles vppe abræc hit wes god þet heo spæc
Appollin mi lauerd ich þankie þe þat mi fæder is icumme to me
Tidinge ic ihire leoue þat mi fader on liue is
Of me he habben scal goudne reæd bute ich beo þe raþer ded
Seie me nuþe leof swein and harne mine lare
Ich þe wulle bitache a male riche
peniȝes þer buoþ an sunda to iwisse an hundrad punda
Ich bitæche þe anne hængest godna and strongna
to læden þis garisume to leuene mine fadere
and seie him þat ich hine gret godere gretinge
 and hatine fare swiþe to hare feire burȝe
and rumen him herberia i summe riche burie
 and bugge him alre errust þat him wes alre leouust
metes and drinches and hende claþes
hundes and hauekes and durewurþe horses
halde in is heose feuwerti hiredcnihtes
heȝe and riche bihongen mid ræue
makie him god baid and ofte hine baþie
 and him blod lete lutlen and ofte
Wenne þu wult more suluer sæche hit at me suluen
 and ich him wulle senden inoh of þisse ende
swa neuer he ne cuþe of his alde cuþþe
cnihte ne sweine ne nauer nanne þeine
Þenne feowerti dawes beoþ agan þenne cuþe he anan
to leue mine lauerd þat Leir is an is londe
icume ouer sæstreme to isen is eastresse
 and ich hit wulle swa nimen alse ich hine nusten
liþen him toȝænes mid mine lauerde
fainen mines lauerdes and is fæirliche cume
Nute hit neuere nane gume buten he beo neowene icume
 and þus hit writen sende to mine lauerd kinge
 and þu þas æhte onfo and loca þat þu wel do
and ȝef þu heo þus dalest to godere þire hæle
 and þe swein onfeng þas ahte and to is louerd ferde
to Leir þon kinge and seide þas tidinge
þer he læi on felde and reste hine on folde
Sone werþ þe alde king wunliche iæþeled
 and þas wuord seide mid soþere stefuene
After vuele cumeþ god wel is him þe hit habbe mot
Heo ferden to hare æȝene burh ase þe quene hæhte 
 and al heo iduden efter hire lare
Þa forþ wuren agan feuwerti daȝene
þon nom Leir þe king is leouste cnihtes
 and gret Aganippum þat was his leue aþum
 and seide him bi his sond þet icume he wes to is londe
to speken wit his dohter þe wes him swuþe dure
Aganippus wes bliþe þet Leir wes cumen liþen
ferde him toȝenes mid alle his þeines
and þa quene Cordoille þa hauede Leir is wille
Heo comen togadere and ofte heo custen
heo uenden to burȝe blisse wes an hirede
Þer wes bemene song þere ȝeden pipen among
al weren þe hællen bihongen mid pellen
alle þa meteburdes ibrusted mid golde
Ringes of golde ælc mon hafte on honde
mid fiþelen and mid harpen hæleþes þer sungen
Lette þe king gan awal and lude clepien oueral
and seide þat Leir kin icume wes to londen
Nu hateþ Aganippus þe is þe heȝest ouer us
þat ȝe Leir king alle wurþe liþe
 and scal beon eouwer lauerd inne þissere leoden
al swa fele ȝere swa he wonien wulle here
 and Aganippus ure king scal beon is vnderling
Whaswa wulle libba alde þas sibba
 and ȝef o man hit wille breken on ueste it biþ iwreken
 and wite he alle is mon þat he here haldet on
Þa answareda þa duȝeþa Don we hit wullet
lude and stille al þes kinges wille
Þurþout al þat ulke ȝer heo duden al þus þer
mid muchelere sibba mid mocheleære seahte
Þa þeos ȝer wes agon þa wold Leir king fare ham
to þisse londe liþen and ȝernde þeos kinges leue
Þe king Aganippus answerede him þus
Ne scalt þu neuere þider faren bute mochelure ferde
ah ich þe wulle lanen of mine leodefolc
fif hundred schipes ifulled mid cnihten
 and al þat heom bihoueþ to habben on fore
And þine dohter Cordoille þa is þisse londes quene
heo scall mid mochelure ferde faren mid þe 
an liþen to þen londen þer þu were leodene king
and ȝef þu miht æine finden þe þe wulle aȝenstonde
binimen þe þine rihte and þine kineriche
þu ahliche ueht and fel heo to grunde
 and irum al þat lond and sete hit Cordoille an hond
þat heo hit al habbe efter þine daie
Þas wordes seide Aganippus and Leir king dude þus
and al he iworhte swa his freond him tahte
To þisse londen he com liþen mih leoue his dohter
He higreþede mid þane beste þe him buwen wolden
 and alle he ham fulde þe him wit feohten
and he al þis kinelond biwon to his aȝere hande
 and ȝef hit Cordoille þe wes Francene quene
and hit ane stunde stod a þissene ilke
Leir king one leoden þreo ȝer leouede
þæ com his endedæi þat þe king ded læi
Inne Leirchestre his dohter hine leide
