inne Ianies temple al swa þe boc tellet
and Cordoille heold þis lond mid hæȝere strenþe
fulle fif ȝere quene wes here
þa while Francene king fæisiþe makede
and Cordoille com þat wourd þat heo was iworþen widewe
Þa come þa tidende to Scottlondes kinge
þat Aganippus was dead Leir king idæied
He sende þurh Brittaine into Cornwaile
 and hehte þane duc stronge heriȝen in suþ londe
and he wolde bi norþen iahnien þa londa
For hit was swuþe mouchel scome and ec swiþe muchel grame
þat scholde a quene beon king in þisse londe
 and heora sunen beon buten þa weren hire beteren
of þan aldre sustren þa þa æþelen sulden habben
Nulle we hit namore iþolien al þat lond we wulleþ habben
Heo bigunnen werre wanne com on west
 and þere quene suster sunen sumneden ferde
Heore nomen weren ihaten þus Morgan and Cunedagius
Ofte heo ledden ferde ofte heo fuhten 
ofte heo weren buuenne and ofte binoþen
Þat com at þan laste þat heo wes alre leofust
þe Bruttes heo sloȝen Cordoille heo nomen
Heo duden heo in quarterne in ane qualehuse
heo werþede heore moddri mare þene heo sulden
þat þe wimman was swa wroþ þat hire sculuen heo was laþ
Heo nom enne longne cnif and binom seoluen þat lif
Þat wes an uuel ræd þat hire suluen makede dead
Þeo wes al þis kinelond an Morgan and Cunedagies heond
heo fengen to þissen lond and mid fuhten hit biwunnen
Þa dælden þa broþeran al þis drihtliche lond
Cunedagius bi þare Humbre hauede al þet west Morgan hauede norþ and est
 and swa heo heolden al þis lond ale þe twa ȝere on heore heond
Þa þe twa ȝer weren agon þa twineden here þonkes
Morgan wes in Scottlond þene norþ ende he hauede ane honde
inne Cornwale Cunedagies he hauede moni god hus
Morgan hafte on hirede swiþe monie cnihtes
þeo ne luuede noht þas leoden ah laiþ heo hem weoren
He taleden wiþ Morgan and is cnihtscipe tælden
and þus him to seiden þa vnselie mon
Lauerd Morgan whi nult þu faren and fusen þine ferden
and faren ȝend al Brutlond and nimen hit to þire heonde
Þerof we habbeþ sceome and at oure herte muche grame
þat þu dalest þis lond þe sculde beon o þire hond
Þu eært a swa hende gome and þere eældre suster sone
Delest þine lond wiþ þine mæi þi monscipe is þa lasse
Þus speken þeos swiken and spileden mid worde
swa long heo hine lærde þat he heom ileuede
He gaderede ferde þe wes feondliche stor
he ferde ouer þe Humbre and hermes he worhte
he herȝede he brande folc he amærde
Heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo aneh comen
Þat word com sone suþ for hit wes widen cuþ
þet Morgan ledde muchele here and hærmes dude þas leoden
Þa ihurde Cunedagius þat Morgan is mæi ferde þus
þa iwerþ he swiþe wraþ and þas word seide
Ȝetsinge a wurþe þe wa monie mon þu bicherrest 
þurh þe haueþ Morgan mi mæi is monschipe afallet
ah he scall hit abuggen ȝif ich mot libben
Þa nom Kunedagius and send ȝeond his cuþþe
 and gaderede muchel folc and ȝeærwede his ferde
He fusede mid monschipe toward Margane his mæie
Þa heo sculden fehten þa fleh Morgan awaie
from londe to londe and he him after liþde
Into Wales he flæh he him after ferde
þer he oftoc Morgan mid muchele strengþe
 and sloh he him of þat hæued his hap wes þa wurse
 and al his men slowen þat heo neh comen
buten wuhlc wræcche swa cwic cuahte to holde
Heo nomen Morganus liche and leide hit on vrþen
wel heo hine buriden þe wes þes Wales lauerd
Wes þet lond þurh Morgan Margan ihæten
Cunedagius heuede al þis lond þerof he wes lauerd
þro and þritti wintere he welde þas riche
inne griþe and in friþe his frenden to blisse
A Cunedagius dawe þe king wes on leode
Remus and Romulus Rome iwrohten
beine iweren ibroþeren ah þe an sloh þene oþren
After þritti wintere com þe dæi þat Cunedagius deæd læi
He hefte anne sune ræhne Riwald wes ihaten
he wes wis he wes fæir he welde þat riche hær
al hit hine luuede þat liuede in londe
An þan ilke time hær com a selkeþ taken
sulche hare nere eær ne com ne neuer seoþþen hiderto
From heouene her com a sulcuþ flod þre dæȝes hit rinde blod
þreo dæies and þreo niȝt þat wæs swuþe mochel pliht
Þa þe rein wes agan her com hider taken anan
Her comen blake fleȝen and fluȝen in mone eȝene
in here muþ in heore neose heore lif heom eode al to leose
swulc fare of fleoȝen her was þat heo freten þet corn and þat græs
wo wes al þen folke þe wuneden an folden
Þærafter com swulke monqualm þat lute hær cwike læfden
Seoþþen her com a strong ræd þat Riwald kinge iwerþ dead 
Riwald king hafuede anne sune Gurgustius ihaten
his lond he huld half ȝer and suþþen he adun halde
Þerefter com Sisillius he wes sone her deæd
Suþþen com Lago þa æhte wike liuede
Suoþen com king Marke he wes þritti wiken king
Þeo com Gorbodiago he wes fif ȝere god king
Þe king hauede tweie sunen beiene vniselie
þe eldere heȝte Fereus þe ȝengere hehte Poreus
Þas breþren weren swa wode and swa wiþerwarde
þat al heo weren vnsahte and al heo weren vnsome
 and eiþer hateden oþer swa ne sulde nawiht breoþer
and beien mid onde heo weoren in þisse londe
þat Gorbidiagus heore fader of his sunen wes afered
for ofte biforen himsuluen heo bigunnen to fuhten
Þe aldre seide þat al þis lond he wolde halden on is aȝere hond
þe ȝengere him ȝef swuh enswere Ær ich þe slæ mid mine spere
ar þu hit sule aȝen þa while ich beon on liue
Poreus hauede þe heorte swa luþer and swa loþ him wes his broþer
þat swiken he him wolde a summes kinnes wisen
Fereus hit iherde suggen þorh soþfaste worden
þat his broþer hine wolde slæn þerfore he wes ful sari
He ferde awæi ouer sæ þat him þuhte selest
he funde inne Francene eærd þene king þe hehte Sward
he bad him herdsumnesse heren þat he him wolde
beon him for hold cniht ba bi dæie and bi niht
Þe king wes gled for his kime and for þen cnihtes þet come mid hine
 and heold hine on erde and hæhliche hine clepede
Ful soue ȝere mid þon kinge he wunede þere
þat king he hauede iquemed and alswa þere quene
Þa seoue ȝer weoren aliþene þa bad he leue
færren þat he wolde into þisse lond
Þe king him lende ane ferd of his kennest folke
himseolf he sende sonde wide ȝen þat londe
after alle þen cnihten þe he biȝete mihte
and he toclipede muchelen his ferde
 and al mid isunde come to þisse londe
Anan heo bigunne fuhte and falde þas leoden 
 and is broþer Poreus ferde him toȝenes
mid þon stronge fæhte Fereus he felden
and alle his ferde he leiden to folde
Iudon hæhte here moder þe riche was and onmære
swiþe heo was sari for sorehfulle þan slehte
þat heore sune ȝeongere sloh þene eldere
Þe deæde heore wæs leouere þe quike here wes leoþere
Þe quike hire wes swa swiþe leoþ þat binimen heo him þohte his lif
Poreus lai on bure þer him muchel plihte ilomp
þer he læi softe and he siker slepte
Com is moder liþen mid leoþlichen creæften
mid oþer six wiuen mid six longe cniuen
Þeo uniseli moder þus hire sune murþde
heo cærf him þene swure atwa a wurþe hire wa
þe uniselie moder mid sexe hine to snæde
 and al todælde lim from oþere
Þa wes þe muchele speche ȝend þat kineriche
of Iudon þere quene þa heore sone acualde
 and of þare seoreȝe þe isiȝe wes to londe
Þa weas dæd Fereus alswa wes Poreus
binumen wes þere moder monschipe on leode
þa nes þer noht of þen kunne þe mihte þis kinelond walden
wepmon ne wifmon bute þa seorhfulle iudon
Gumen heom igadereden and wurpen heo to sagrunde
Þa aræste here vnfriþe oueral me brac þene griþ
sterce weren þe reæmes mid stronge raflake
elc mon ræuede oþer þeah hit weren his broþer
wrake wes on londe wa wes þone vnstronge
Her wes hunger and hete her wes alre hærmene mest
her wes muchel monqualm þat lut her quike bilefden
Feowere here weren riche þe haueden ferden muchele
þeo nedden al þæ oþere and heom neþþer sætten
 and speken heom togadere and speleden þa hæȝe
þat heo wuolden al þis lond dælen heom bitwenen
Þus heo hit idemden and þeræfter swa duden
In Scotlond wes king Stater i Logres wes king Piner
Cloten hafte Cornwale Rudæuc hauede Norh Wales 
Ah Cloten hæfde mest riht to aȝen þas riche
ah þa oþere weoren ræhere and eke heo weoren richere
of golde and of garisume and of gode londe
Cloten heo oscuneden and his færedene forhowede
Cloten hauede Cornwale þat he heold wel one griþe
Cloten hauede enne sune þe sel wes on eorþe
he wes feir he wes muchel to feahten he wes mære
cniht he wes kene and he wes ȝeua custi
monie þewes gode he haueda on his moda
His nome wes ihote þus Donwallo Molinus
Þis wes þe feiruste mon þe æuere æhte ær þisne kinedom
þa he mihte beren wepnen and his hors wel awilden
he liþde ȝeon þeos leoden sulch hit an liun were
he sloh Piner þene king his folc he al aqualde
þa him wihstoden he felde heom to his foten
 and al Logres þat lond he æȝenede to his æȝere hond
Suþþen he turnde his fare and ferd feorhriht to Wales
þer he funde Rudac king þe reh wes to fehte
toȝeines him he funde þer Scotlondes king Stater
Heo speken þer to sæhte to sibbe and to some
aiþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nolden
Þus heo makeden heore fære Aȝen ferde Dunwale
 and his mochele ferde to Cornwale his eærde
Þa iherde Stater þat Dunwale wes swiþe fer
Mid muchele Scotferde he scraþ to þisse londe
Rudauc mid his Welscen þat wæl wes þe more
Into þisse londe heo comen þis floc heo hær slowe
wide heo ærnde tuones heo forbarnden
mochel dal heo iwesten mid harmen þan mesten
Þat word com to Dunwale þer he wes i Cornwale
wet Ruwak king dude her and þe king Stater
Þa seide Dunwale þat was þe duȝende mon
Nu heo beþ forsworne mid heore swikedome
Bi Appollines ære ne ileue ich hem neueremare
Nu we sculle ræmen and ræisen togadere
Vnder þissen luften leten riht scuften
Sendeþ mine sonden ȝend alle mine londe 
and biddeh alne godne mon þe griþ wulle halden
 and alle þe me of haldeh cumen ær sone
 and sendeþ liþinde men æfter oþere leoden
to folien me in mine londe for seoluer and for golde
 and ich wulle mine rihte faren to stalfehte
toȝene þene swerd broþeren þe beiene beoh forsworene
For wel often he beoþ awald þe stondeþ o þen woȝe
ne mai neuere monsware monscipe longe aȝen
Þe Dunwale hauede isæd al his folc luuede þene ræd
He somenede færd swulc nes næuere eær on erde
swoþþen wes þa time þe Bruttes come hær liþen
Heo fulde his ferde and for a mucla costa
toȝenes þan twam kingen þer he hem funde on walde
Heo heolden togædere and hardeliche fuhten
feollen þa fæie falewede nebbes
Weoren al þa feldes ifayed mid blode
þer wes moni hard gume mid sworde tohewen
Dunwal i þan fæhte wes feondliche kene
þat fæht wes swuþe strong and swuþe stærc and swuþe longe
Dunwal i þan fahte hauede swuþe gode cnihtes
wise and wære monie heo afelden
Dunwale him biþohte wat he don mihte
He nom of his ferde six hundred cnihtes
of þan aldre hexten to wiȝe alre hardest
 and þus heo heom seide on his somrunan
Nime we þis wepnen þe bi þisse walle liggeþ
 and halden biforen bresten sceldes þa brade
 and fare we bihalues alse we of heoren weoren
þe wille sullen ore ferden fæhten biliue
Þenne Stateres floc iseoþ ore fæire sculdes
cumen on feste hit buh heom wel iqueme
for þan wepnen heo wullet wenen þat þeo beon heore iferen
We scullen ous biredien and slen Rudauc þane king
and feorhrihtes þære slen þane king Statere
Mid strengþe we sullen wenden þurh ure wiþeriwinnen
 and fellen ure feondes for alle heo buh fæi
Þus spac Dunwale þat was þe duȝenede mon 
 and al he iworhte swa his word tahte
Heo nomen þa seeldes þa leien in þan feldes
brade and gode ihelede mid golde
heo wenden to þan kingen þer heo weren on kompen
Þe kingges weren bliþe heo wenden bi þan bordden
heo wenden bi þen scelden þat hit heore scalkes weoren
Sone so Dunwale heom næh com swa he hæhte slæn heom
Slæþ heom mid sweorde for alle heo beoþ forsworne
Rudac heo slowen and Stater heo nomen
 and al hene toliþeden lim from þen oþere
heoræ sceaftes weoren strake of his flæsces heo makeden here marce
Anan heo ferden towærd heore iueren
þa heo togaderen comen somed heo onsloȝen
Þa kingges weoren deædde heore duȝeþe todealde
twinseden cnihtes here tir wes atfallen
Dunwales men sloȝen al þat heo aneh comen
al þa ferde heo falden to grunde
buten swulc forwonde man þe mid sorwe atwand
Þa hauede Dunwale þis lond al biȝeten to his hond
suþþen he wes heh king coþ hit wes wide of him
beoþ on beoken feolefeld bisnen
Þet wes þa eæraste mon þe guldene crune dude him on
here inne Bruttaine seoþþen Bruttes hit ieode
He makede swulc griþ he makede swulc friþ
monien laȝen gode þe long souþþen stode
Heo makeden ane sætnesse and mid aȝe heo semde
þe ælc cheorl eæt his sulche hæfde griþ alswa þe king sulf
alken farinde mon ȝef slaht oþer þeofþe hæfde idon
and he ætsturte into are burie þat heo weren iborȝen
þenne and aueremare heo swulden habben are
to fuse into hame and habben his æhte
and ȝef æi mon him liþere dude he sculde dom þolien
 and þus ælkene forme gult þe king sulf hine forȝef
Þe king makede monie laȝen þa ȝet beoþ on londe
 and alle laȝen gode bi his daȝen stode
Feowerti wintre he walde þes leode a blisse hit stod on his hand
Seoþþen dæide þe king wa wes his duȝeþe 
Togadere come his eorles and brohten hine to eorþe
inne Lundene burh feire hine leiden
in are riche temple mid golde heo hine bitunden
Þe king hauede bi his wiue twene sonen on liue
þe ældre hæhte Belin þe ȝeonggere Brenne
Þas breþren iwurþen heom swahte þurh sele monne rede
Belin ȝef his leue broþer anne dal of his londe
biȝende þere Humbre mid monscipe to halden
norþ into þare sæ sel þat heo iworþe
Þerfore his mon he bicom and hærdsumnesse him solde don
Belin heold þis suþlond and Cornwale on his hond
 and Wales þer forþ mid and faire hit dihte
Fif ȝer heo heolden þus þis lond and leoue heom wes bitwune
þet æuere eiþer oþer luuede alse is broþer
Ah Brennes hauede vuele men his æþelene heo amerden
þeo ælche dæie hine larden luþere craftes
þat he sculde wih his broþer forewarde breken
Anne hirdcniht he hauede þe æht wes on þen weorede
þe þane balew mæinde and þus spec wih Brenne
Seie me mi lauerd leouest alre monne
whi þolest þu þat Belin þe is þin aȝene broþer
hauet swa mochel of þisse lande and þu hauest swa lutel
Nefde ȝe ba enne fader and beie enne moder
beiene of ane cunne cuþ hit is on folke
Nu stond al þis muchele lond a Bailenes aȝere hond
 and þu eært his mon and is cniht þat is woh and nawiht riht
Eært þu þenne cheuesboren þat þu wult beon forloren
Oþer þu eart swa eærȝh cniht þat of londe ne rehchest nawiht
oþer þu þenchest beo raþe dead and þine duȝeþen al bilaiuen
Bileæf þe treuweþe bilef þene æþ for al þis folc is swiþe wraþ
Hercne þine herdes ræd and heo þe wullet helpen
Hit us þinchet wunder ȝef þu hine nelt awalden
Þu eært muchele betere cniht to halden comp and ifiht
 and þu eært muchele ahtere and ec mare hærdere
Cheflon þu ouercome and Scotlond him binome
of Muraine he wes king and he wiht þe othliche fæht
eærst þu hine ouercome and seoþþen þu hine slowe
and al his ferde þe he brohte to þan eærde 
Ah wel ich hit ileuen þat we þe sunden loþe
þat þu þi þanc al forhele wih þine hiredmonnen
Ah for nauer nare teonen nulle we þe trukien
neuer ane siþen bi ure quike liuen
And fær bi ure ræden and mid þe þu læden
tweolue of þine witiȝen of þine wisuste monnen
 and fær forh nu toniht into Norewaieȝe forhriht
to Alfinge kinge þu bist him cume deore
 and gret þu londes king and al his leode
Þe king haueþ ane dohter þe him is swuþe dure
Bide heo to þire bihoue to habben to are quene
Þenne he siþ þe swa hende cniht he þe ȝeueþ heo forþriht
Seoþþen ȝern to þan kinge þat he þe læne ferde
to lede to þine londe to balden þine leoden
Bide auerælcne cniht þet þu þer biȝeten miht
for seluere and for gold cume mid þe to þisse londe
 and we sullen þe wile biwiten þine riche
Derneliche þu scalt don þeos ilka deda
þat hit nute Belin þe is þin aȝene broþer
Ah fær swiþe and cum raþe for þus we þe radeþ
Þenne þu cumes faren ham we swulleþ beon al fuse
mid mochelen ure ferde to færen ȝeon þan eærde
to owreken þe uppon Beline þe þe bismar haueþ idon
Þus spec Malgod swike he wes ful god
Þe oþere him radden al swa þerfore hem wroþe wide wa
Þa Brennes hauede ihirde his hirdemanne lare
þa gladede is mod þe rad him þuhte swiþe god
 and seide hem þis answare After eore rade ich wulle færen
He greiþede his cnihtes and feorh færde bi nihttes
swa longe þat he bicom to Ælfinge kinge
Þonne king heo igrette and his gumen alle
and þe king him answerede swiþeliche fæire
Þa spec Brennes and his ærnde abed
he ȝirnde þeos kinges dohter to habben to are quene
 and þe king him ȝette al þat he ȝirnde
gold and gærsume feoh and færde
Þa wes Brennes swiþe bald on heorte he wes bliþe 
þat mæiden he weddede and nom heo to his bedde
Seoueniht he wes þære hit þutte him seoue ȝere
ær he aȝen come to fæhten wih his broþer
Of witten heo weoren amadde þe him swa rædden
Brennes wes in Norwæye Belin in þisse londe
Belin ihærde sugge þurh summe sæg treowe
of his broþer wifþinge and for wulche þinge
 and for wulchere neode he to Norwæiȝe færde
Belin hine biþohte of swulchere dede
 and þas worde seide þe sæg wes itreouwe
Wa wurþe a þon broþer þe biswikeþ þene oþer
Whær beo ȝe mine cnihtes whar beo ȝe mine kempen
whar beo ȝe mine leoue men nu we scullen liþen
Heo ferden to Humberlonde þer weoren castles stronge
Þe castles heo nomen alle and strangede þe walles
He lette blauwen bemen and nam al þa burhwes
þa weoren on his broþer londe þe he hafde an heonde
He dude þerinne mæte inoh and wepmen unifoh
þat me mihte heom walden wih Brennes anwalde
His cnihtes mid himseoluen to þare sæ færden
þar laien bi þan brimme and bisilichen hit wisten
Brennes wes in Norweȝe and noht herof nuste
he wende þat his broþer nuste noht of his fære
Leaf he nom at Ælfing þe wes Norweine king
 and he him ȝef answere A mote þu wel færen
 and Delgan mi dohter þe me is swþe deore
Þis understod þe ȝeonge quene faren þat heo scolde
heo hauede enne leouemon þa heo swuþe ileoued hæfde
þene king of Denemark þe leof hire weis on mode
He wes swiþe god cniht Godlæc he hahte
Þa sende Dalgan þa quene into Denemarke
 and guþde Godlacke þa wes hire gome deore
stille bocrunen heo senden him to ræden
 and seiden him þat Brennes a king of Britaine
hauede heo biwedded and ihaued heo to bedde
al hire vnþonkes þerfore hire wes uneþe
and heo he wolden læiden toward his leoden 
næuede heo bute þreo nihte feorst faren þat heo scolde
Sone hit mæi ilimpen þanne ihc hunnen liþe
þah þu habben blisse and griþ ne speke ich þe naueremore wiþ
and ihc sende þe gretinge of mine gold ringe
Þa Godlac isæh þis wa him wes ful iwis
Stille he wes iswoȝen on his kinestole
Me warp on his nebbe cold wellewatere
Þa þe king wes awaht he wes swuþe idraht
he seide forþrihtes Whar beoþ mine cnihtes
Fare we swiþe to þare sæ sele mine dranches
Godlac king on ueste mid gudfulle folke
to þere sæ wenden scipen þer heo funden
makede muchul sæflot and ferden mid streme
toȝenes þare hauene þer Brennes from halde
Þa Brennes com i wide sæ he imette his wiþeriwinne
scip ærne toȝen scip þa hit al towonde to scifren
horn aȝen horne halde þe wacre
Þer wes moni breoste mid brade spere iþurlud
helmes þer gullen beornes þer fullen
balluw þer wes riue Brennes flæh bliue
 and Godlac hæld æfter monie scipen he þer cahte
He iseh a scip þar hit laþ sulkene wes þat seilclæþ
he clupede to his dringes: Nu forh nu niþinges
Þet is þere quene scip: þe us biforen queccheþ
Haldeþ alle þerto and ȝif ȝe hit mawen ifon
æueremare ich æu leouie þa wile þa ich liouie
Mid strengþe heo halden to schipen and þa quene heo igripen
Godlac sloh þa scipgumen and alle heo nom þat garsume
and ladde þa quene Delgan toward Denemarke anan
He þoþte heo to habben to his awere bihoue
 and oþer weis hit sæht
Godlac forh geinde glad he wes on heorte
he þohte to habben Delgan to quene of Denemarke
ah him com muchel lætting swa him wes alre laþest
Æft aras a ladlich weder þeostrede þa wolcne
þe wind com on weþere and þa sæ he wraþede
vþen þer urnen alse tunes þer burnen
rapes þer braken balu wes fulle riue 
Scipen þer sunken
þer þreo and fifti scipen feollen to grunde
in þa teonfulle sæ torneden sæiles
Godlac hauede a god scip ne gomede him towiht
he hine biþohte weht he don mihten
He igrap ane wiæxe muchele and swiþe scærpe
he forheow þænne mæst atwo riht amidden
he lette seil and þane meæst liþen mid vþen
Þus seide Goþlac sære him gromede
Æuerælc æhte mon: help þat we libben
Þat we comen to londe ne recche we on wulche leoden
Heo ferden mid þon wedere nusten heo nauere whudere
vnder fif dawene ȝeong heo comen to þisse londe
Comen þes kinges cnihtes þe þæ sæ wusten
and nomen Godlac þene king and Delgan þæ quene
Heo seiden heom enne strongne ræd Nu ȝe beon alle dead
ah ȝef ȝe wullen us seuggen ȝet ȝe mawen libben
whonene ȝe beþ icumene and whet ȝe her sohten
Godlac answerede mid godlichen worden
We beoh sæwerie men and we wullet soþ sucgen
ah nuten næuere þæs gumen into whuche londe heo beoþ icume
ne þas strond we ne cnoweþ þe we isoht habbeþ
þis lon ne þas leoden ne wha her lauerd is
ne we nuten na þe ma þat we ne speken wit ure ifæn
Ah ich eow bidde leoue men leddeþ us to þæn kinge
 and ich him wulle suggen of blissen and of sorwen
And þa cnihtes heom lædden to heore leodkinge
Godlac and þa quene heore æhte and his iferen
 and seiden him þat he wes i Brutaine i Belin kinges londe
Sone swa he to þan king com wisliche he clupede him an
Hail wurh þu Belin king Brennes is þi broþer
 and ich hatte Godlac gumenen ich wes lauerd
Denemarkene king þeos wifman hatte Delcan
Brennes com to Norhweie to Ælfinge kinge
Þe king him ȝef Delcan þe ȝare wes mi leouemon
Sonden commen bitwenen þe soþe word me seiden
whennen Brennes wolde liþen and mine leouemon leden
Toȝenes ich him ferde mid feowerti scipen gode 
and mid al swa fele cnihtes swa þa scipen beren mihten
 and ich wulle suggen þe an wunder he haueden scipen seouen hundred
And ich bigon strong fæht and Brennes to flenne
his men ich awelde and monie ich aquelde
and þer ich nom Delgan þe ær wes mi leouemon
 and ich sugge þe to soþe þat ȝet leoueþ þi broþer
for he hald to þen londe and wel com to hauene
And ich isæh þare quene scip quecchen mid vþen
 and ich ferden þeræfter and biwan hit mid fæhte
Þa wes ich bliþe on mine quike liue
Þa ich wes i wide sæ wiþer com toȝenes
þet weder wes swa wilde and þa sæ wrædde
and draf me to þisse londe into þire leode
And me do þine milce for þu eart mihti ouer me
Þe king heom lette halden in swiþe feire benden
in ane stronge castle þer he heom wel biwiste
Nes hit buten feower wiken þat þas þinge ifaren weoren
cam Brennes riden into Scottelonde
mid feower hundred schipen folc þer wes fæie
He sende his boden: to Belin his broþer
 and bad hine quicliche aȝeuen him his quene
 and þane kinge Gudlac: þe his gumen hauede afalled
 and ȝef he hit nolle him sal beon þa wurse
In his londen ich wulle gon and slæn al þat ich finde
mid fehte and mid fure þis feoreward ich him halde
bute he me wullen ȝeuen þat ich him toȝeurne
 and mi londe rume and fare to his riche
and aȝeue me mine burȝes and mine buri gode
castles and toures þe he me halt a teonen
Forþ ferde þas sonde to Belin king
 and seide him þeos ibeod from Brenne his broþer
 and Belin him warde al þat he ȝernde
þat ne sulde he nauere ibiden þe while þe he mihte riden
Þe sonde aȝan ferde and seide hit Brenne
Brenne wes swiþe wraþ and bannede is ferde
scheldede his scalken alse heo to wiȝe solden
folkede his cnihtes alsa heo scolden fehten 
Belin an halue hæiȝede him toȝeines
Muchel æie wes þære vnder þan wude of Kalatere
þer heo heom imetten and vuele hem igretten
Togædere heo comen heo graneden sone
feondliche heo feohten bi þeosende heo fellen
Swiþe faht Belin king swa duden his Bruttes
heo weoren swiþe ohte men þat æþel heo biwunnen
Brennes heom from bæh and mid his folke he fleh
al toward þare sæ mid muchele vnsælþe
 and Belin heom æfter and heo adun leide
sixti þusende he leide to þen gronde
A schip funde Brennes bi þon brimme stonden
he bicom þerinne mid his twelf monnen
ne leædde he na ma isunde of alle his monnen
Ouer sæ he ferden in toward France
and þeo forwundede men wende into holte
Þa al þis wes ifarren and Brennes wes awæi ifloȝen
Belin in Euerewic huld eorlene husting
he bed þat his riche men rihtne read radden
whet him weore to donne bi þon ilke monne
 and bi Godlac kinge þe he huold i bende
For Gudlac him sende word bi ane wise monne
þat if he him wold leoþien of laþe his benden
þat he wolde his mon beon mid alle his monueorde
 and he him wolde ȝeuen al þat gold þe he haueden i Denemark lond
 and ælcche ȝere him senden þreo þusund punden
herto him wolden finden ȝisel of his gilde
wih þon þe he lette sckere hine and his ifere
 and his leouemen swa deore to Denemark leoden
Belin king him ȝette þat forward þat he ȝerde
and freoliche hine lette faren and alle his iueren
Belin hauede þeo ȝeseles and þa ȝeuen gode
 and his monræidene mid monschipe biwunnen
 and Gudlac ledde forh þa wifmon swiþe fæire
 and he heo bohte swiþe deore bruken he heo þohte
Belin huld þas riche wel feole ȝere
 and he swiþe freolic al his folc he ladde
he makede swiþe god griþ his gumen hit wel heolden
Þa weoren i þissere leode laȝen swiþe gode 
 and al leouede þeone king þe quic wes an londe
Þa hauede Belin an heond al Brutteines lond
he ferde ȝeond al and lawen sette
he scawede þa wuodes and þa wildernes
meduwen and mores and þa hæȝe muntes
burwes and tunes and al hit ȝeorne bihold
Þe king hine biþohte whet he don mihte
He bigon ane stræte muchele and swiþe græte
feiȝer and swiþe long þurhut al þis kinelond
 and þe king and his folc Fosse heo clupeden
Heo liþ hut of Toteneis a þet cume to Catenes
Toteneis is in Cornwale Cateneis in Scotdale
Anoþer stret he makede swiþe hendi from Suþhamtone to Seint Deuwi
Seoþþe he makede þe þridde þe kærf þis lond amidde
Þa þeos stræt weoren idon þa leide þa king heom laȝen on
þat whaswa i þen stræten breken griþ þe king him wolde binimen his lif
ah whaswa oþerne imette þer fæire hine igrætte
Þis weoren þeos kinges strætte þe ich ikenned habbe
I Frænce wes Brennes þe wes þeos kinges broþer
on his heorte he hauede grome on his mode muchele scome
þat he hæuede iloren his kinelond and his quene þe he leouede
 and him swiþe scomede þat he swa iscend wes
He wunede inne France mid his tweolfe iferen
he herde þon king and wel him iquemde
 and al þa Frensce leoden swiþe heo loueden Brenne
for Brennes biȝet muchel feoh and feire hit dælde
Nes he noht ȝælpinde ah he wes ȝeuecusti
he wes þer swiþe oht mon and æþele weore hid deden
 and him þer ofte wel ilomp þerfore he wes þe leofere
þa he wes þere wel cuþ and oueral icnawen
 and þe king hine leouede and al his leoden
Þa nom he his iferen and bisohte þeos folkes king
þat he him sculde fulste mid his gode folke
his lond to biȝetene of Belin his breoþer
Þe king him bihette and wel hit him ȝette
Þa bead he leaue and he furþer laþ
to Seguine Duc þe lauerd wes of Burguine
 and of þen Brutlonde þe is biȝeonde sæstronde 
Feire he igrette þeone duc þa he his griþ sohte
he seide þat he him wolden hæren and halden hine for herra
leofliche him buwen and halden hine for lauerd
Þe duc þerfore fain wes and hine fæire onfeng
Brennes wes swiþe hende his hap wes þe betere
Brennes cuþe on hundes Brennes cuþe an hauekes
he cuþe mid his honden hanlie þa harpe
þurh his hændecraftes hiredmen hine leouede
 and his lauerd alse wilcume swa he weoren his aȝene sune
Þe duc hauede æne dohter þe him wes swiþe deore
ah he neuede nenne sune þerfore he wes sari
Þe duc bisæh a Brenne þe hauede bodi hende
 and him to seide mid sohfeste huȝe
Brennes þu ært hende and þu ært hæh iboren
 and þu eært cniht swiþe god and þu eært me iqueme
Þu come ouer streme þu eart kinges istreonne
þu eært me swiþe iliþe and ich þe leouie swiþe
Al þat ich þe bihate ich hit þe wulle halden
ich wulle ȝeuen þe mine dohter þa me is swiþe deore
 and æfter mine dæie al mi drihliche lond
for wel hit luuieþ alle mine burnes
þat hit þus beo idon and þat þu þis vnderfon
Þa answerede Brennes mid beienliche worden
Ich hit þankie þe and alle þine þeode
for eouwer muchele wurhchipe wel þat ȝe me vnnen
Al þis wes idon alse þe duc demde
Blisse was on hirede þeo Brennes þis mæide nom
mid muchelere wurhschipe he wunede mid þan ducke
Þa þat forme ȝer wharþ forþ igan
þa wes þe duc dead and Brennes hauede his duweþe
al þon folk he wes leof ase heore aȝene lif
for he heold swiþe god griþ and glæd wes wiþ his monnen
He hauede swiþe mucchel lond þat al stod an his hond
and he hæfde a swiþe god wif and he heo leouede alse his lif
Wiþinnen a lut ȝeren Brennes hine biþohte
an his broþer Belin þe his lond binom him
He sende his sonde ȝeond Burguine londe
Þe ferde wes swa muchel þat heo wes vnimete 
Into Normandie he com and þer he þa sæ nom
 and he ferde mid sunde into þisse londe
Brennes bæh a þat lond mid his leodeferde
Sonde com to Belin þa him soþ sæide
þat Brennes his broþer hefde isoht his riche
mid vnimete ferde icommen to his eærde
Belin lette beoden ȝeond al his londe
and bæd al þa kempen þe wiþinne sæ wuneden
þat heo comen to his neode to driuen vt þa vnleoden
Ȝeærwe wes þat ferde and forþward ifusede
heo comen swa næh þere twam ferden
Þa ȝet leouede þa ælde quene a wifmon wis and kene
heo wes ihaten Tonuenne ho iber Belin
and þat heo wel cudde
Heo nom hire on anne curtel þe wes swiþe totoren
hire hem heo up itæh hire cneon he wes swiþe neh
Heo eode on hire bare foten al heo hit dude for gode
Heo com to þere ferde þe icumen wes to þissere eærde
heo axede æfter Brenne þer he wes bi ferde
þer he hine wepnede alse he to fihte þeohte
 and alle his burnes duden on heore burnen
Swa leonge me hire tahte þat heo him to com
Vfenen heo him orn bitwixen hire ærmes heo hine nom
ofte heo hine clupte and ofte heo hine custe
A whet wult þu Brenne Whet wult þu balwe menge
Ȝif þu sleast þine broþer ne bistz þu neuer oþer
Ne beon ȝit bute tweien mine sunen ȝit be beien
Biþenc o þire monschipe biþenc o þire moder
biþenc a mire lare Þu eært mi bærn deore
Loka her þa tittes þat þu suke mid þine lippes
Lou war hire þa wifmon þa þe a þas weoreld ibær
Leo wær here þa wombe þe þu læie inne swa longe
Leo war here þa ilke likame Ne do þu me neuere þane scome
þat ich for þine þinge mid sæxe me ofstinge
Nu hit is vmbe seoue ȝere þat þu weren here
and al forewarde þu breke toward þine breoþer
Þu weore his mon bicumen and he þe leouede also his sone 
Aþes þu him swore swiken þat þu noldest
Þu hauest woh and he haueþ riht þat is þe swiþe muchel pliht
 and ouer sæ þu liþe al buten læue
to Alfinge kinge and nome his dohter ȝeonge
Swa þu woldest mid ferde faren to þissen eærde
and don þe seoluen bisemar fehten wit þine broþer
ȝif Denemarkene king idrecched þe neuede
 and suþþen þu come and herm her iuore
 and æft wendest ouer sæ and nu þu ært sel icumen
Nu þu eært londes weldent and us scal beon þe wurse
Mid uncuþe mannen þu wlt þi cun quelle
Ne sculde na cniht hærȝien þær he hauede hames iwald
no eæft on his cuhþe quedschipe wurchen
Ah leoue sune Brennes bei þi starke þonc
leie adun þin hærescrud and þinne rede sceld
and þi sper longe and þi swerd stronge
and ilef þire moder and leoue þinne broþer
Vrnen ire teares ouer hire leores
Brennes þat isæh and sorȝeden on his heorte
let cliden his gare þat hit grund sohte
He scæt his riche sceld feor ut in þene feld
awei he warp his gode breond and of mid þere burne
Brennes and his moder mildelichen ferden
in ænne bradne feld and Belin him toȝennes
Þa weop þe breoþer al swa dede þe oþer
Þa spec þe moder milde mid muþe
Ȝit buþ mine leoue sunen liþeþ tosomne
 and iwurþeþ sæhte and euer on blisse
Cusseþ and cluppeþ cuþie meies
Cnihtes ȝit beoþ boþe kene while ich wes quene
Nis hit noht unhuhtlic incker moder inc hateþ
Þer heo hom custen þe weren kinges bearn
bifeoren þa twam ferden freondscipe makeden
Bemen þer bleowen blisse wes on folke
þer weore segge songe þer were pipen imagge
þer wes swa muchel murehþe þat ne mihte heo beon namare
Þus iweraþ Brennes sæht whit his broþer
Þa makeden heo ane laþunge of heore leoue folke
þat al comen to Lundene uppe wite of feowerti punden 
to þan hustingge biforen Belin kinge
Þa weoren al þas leoden at Lundene isomed
Þer wes Belin þe king and al his kineriche
Bruttes and Scottes and moni scone þein
Þer wes þe Duc of Burgoine Brennes ihaten
Weoren þa broþerne bliþe on here mode
 and al þa twa ferden of moni ane eærde
Þe kingges nomen to ræde at riche heore monnen
þat heo wolden mid ferde faren into France
In France weore læwen sulkuþe a þan dawen
 and selcuþe tidende for þer were feower kinges
Belin seide to Brenne Fare we bliue
in touwarde France and mid fehte hit biwinnen
Heo bleuwen heore bemen and buden here ferde
and to þere sæ wenden and wel ouer commen
Mid nihen hundred scipene heo commen into hauene
heo commen into þen lond and neoþereden þa leoden
Com þa tiþende to þan feouwer kinggen
þat Belin king wes icumen and þe duc Brenne
mid unimete ferde to biwinne France
Togadere þe kinges come and æþes heo sweoren
þat heo wolde libben togadere oþer liggen
 and euerælc oþer halden for broþer
Mid aþen heo hit bihæten and ful wel hit heolden
Heo sommeneden heore ferde þe wes feondliche stor
 and heo ferden bliue toward Beline
Brennes mid his ferde wes biforen Beline
Togædere come þeos kinges mid heore hereþringes
Ferde whit ferde feonliche feuþten
Scottes and Bruttes beiene togaderes
Belin here læuerd heom biforen wende
Brennes bisides mid his folke of Burguine
Heo smiten togædere helmes þere gullen
breken brade sperren bordes þer scænden
redde blod scede rinkas feollen
þer wes muchel gristbat þer wes cumene fæl
weoren þa hulles and þa dæles iwriȝen mid þe dæden
Belin ibræid up his helm and clipede to Brennes 
Ne isihst þu leoue broþer heou breoþeþ þa Frensce
 and þa ferde of unker londe isund ȝet stondet
Greiþe we us seoluen mid grimme oure ræsen
 and heom on ileggen mid orde and mid egge
Brennes wes swiþe bald and þis wel bileouede
Al heo heom slowen þe heo aneh comen
and þas feower kinges heo leiden to þan grunde
Whulc riche mon þer atfleh into castle he abeh
 and heo him after ferden mid spere and mid swerde
Nes þer nan oþer liþ ȝif heo nalden ȝernen griþ
þene castel heo nomen hine seulfne and his folke sloȝen
Þus heo þurheoden Francene þeode
In þan ilcan ȝere wes Belin kaisere
and Brennes his broþer beiene togaderes
for heo hauede France mid fehte biwunnen
and alle þa fre londes þe leien into France
Þa hauede heo muche riche irumed to honde
þeo speken heo togadere þa sele ibroþeren
and seide þat heo wolden halden hustinge
of allen þat leoden þe heore læwen leoueden
 and of al þan londen þe stoden on heore heonden
and þurh heore alre dome heo wolden fære to Rome
to wreken o þon folke Remus þene feire
þe Romulus his broþer in Rome ofsloh
þer biforen fele ȝere for al þat monkun wes þa ȝet þere
Al þa kinges þus duden swa heomself demmeden
heo gaderede heore ferde in Francene eærde
Þa þat folc wes icumen sone heo fusden
for þer wes swa mochel folc and swa vnimete
þat a neuere nane walde ne mihte hit al halde
Heo ferden ouer Mungiu mid muchelen here ferden
seoþþen heo ferden ful iwis þer me clipþ Munt Senis
heo nomen al Taurins and Iuorie and alle þe burȝewes of Lumbardie
Versæus and Pauie and Cremuinne Melan Plæucence and Buluine
þet wæter heo ouerferden of Taurim and seoþþen heo ferden ouer Bardun
Tuscan heo habbeþ al biwunnen i Salome heo slowe monie þusend monnen 
Swa heo nehlehte toward Rome to late heom þuste are heo þer comen
 and þat Romeanisce floc swiþe wes offered
for heom comen stronge tidinge from Belin þon kinge
Haueden al þa reuen þe wunede in Rome
and alle þa riche gumen þa Rome burwe walden
iloked tweiene eorles i þon ilka ȝeære
þe sculden witen þat lond and wissien þa leoden
 and læden here ferde wher hit neod weore
for heore beire nome ich þe wulle telle
þe an hehte Gabius þe oþer Prosenna
Þeos ilke eorles weren kene ohte men and wel idone
and al þat Romanisce folc ferde bi heore ræde
Þeos eorles comen to Rome to þan redfulle monen
axeden heom ræddes of swulchere neode
wheþer heo boden ferde whit Belinne to fehten
þe heo speken him wit and seoþþe axeden his griþ
Þa weoren in Rome wise men on dome
and þohten bipechen Belin mid heore prætwrenchen
Heo nomen heom to ræde and to somrune
þat noht heo nolden fehten no heore ferd leade
Ah we wullet gan a leoþe and leoue we wulleþ wurchen
we wulleþ setten heom an hond al þis Romanisce lond
 and wurþien heom in leoden al swa mon lauerd scal
ȝeuen heom seluer and gold and bitechen heom al þis lond
ȝeuen heom garisum swa heo wulleþ kepe
vre childre to ȝisle ȝef heo swa wulleþ
ælcches barunes sune þe i þissere burh wuneþ
þeo scullen beon icorne and swiþe wel iborne
childre swiþe hendi ȝisles feor and twenti
 and ælche ȝer of golde ten hundred punde
Þa kingges buh stronge and of ferrene lond
Heo habbeþ swa muche folc swa nes næuer eær on ferde
Þe kinges beoþ ȝunge of æhte ȝissinge
Sone swa heo ihurden swulch worde don heo hit wulleþ
for heo ne mawen bidde mare buten þat we ȝernen heore ære
 and ȝif we mawen swa wel don þat heo þis wullen vnderfon
 and bileuen oure leoden and faren to heore londe 
seoþþen we sculleþ biginnen to don ure wille
for betere is þat we leosen leoue oure children
þanne we nimen swulne ræd þat we allen beo deade
and al Rome burh mid fure forberned
 and al þat liggende lond þat liþ into Rome
beo al biræiued þe nu stondeþ riche
For ȝif hit wulleþ Teruagant þe is oure god of þisse lond
hermid we sculleþ heom bicharren and seoþþen heom amarren
þat ne sculleþ heo nauere isunde cumen to heore londe
Þa seiden heo in halle Þisne read halde we alle
Þeos eorles heom gereden mid godliche scruden
 and nomen mid heom cnihtes swa feole swa heom þuhte
ha leopen an heore feire hors biwriȝen mid fæire palle
Ælc mon nom an honde ane scale of rede golde
Feouwer daies fulle forþward heo wenden
þat heo comen to þon eærde þer Belin wes mid his ferde
 and Brennes his broþer beiene tosomne
Heo axeden aþelinges wer leye þa kinges
Me heom tahte þa feldes þer weoren þare kingene tælddes
Heo ferden biliue þat þider heo comen liþe
Heom þuhte muchel ferlich of al þeon folke
wher hit al inumen weore þat heo iseiȝen þere
Heo iseiȝen Belin king buȝen ut of telde
 and heo lihten adun and leofliche on cneowen
forn at þan kinge heo fullen to folde
Læuerd þine ære for þu ært leodene king
We þe aȝeueþ Rome and al þa riche
 and al þa londes þe liggeþ into Rome
 and alle þe madmes þat we on horde habbeþ
 and swa muchel garsumme swa þine gumen kepeþ
 and æþes we sulleþ þe swerien þat we þe nulleþ swiken
uppen ure godd wel idon þe is icliped Dagon
We swullen þine men bicomen and þine monscipe heien
mid allen oure mihten daies and nihtes 
and we þe wulleþ bitechen ut of þissere riche
feur and twenti ȝunge riche monne childere
þe scullen beon alle icorne and swiþe heiȝe iborne
We scullen of þissere þeode cumen to þire neode
and whuder þu hatest for þu ært ure hærre
 and to swulche forward we beoþ hidere isende
 and we biddeþ þine ære nu and aueremare
Þe king wes stille and þa swiken speken ille
he weonden þat hit weoren soþ þat heo iseid haueden
ah al heo þohten oþer to slæn Belin king and his broþer
Þeo hit up bræc hit wes god þat he spec
Wel ȝe me bihatet halde ȝeif ȝe wulleþ
eow swal beon þe betere
To swuche forewarde fon ich hit wulle
 and ȝe scullen of me halden and habben me for harre
 and habben freoliche eoure lond and we freond iwurþen
Todaie a seouennihte bringeþ me her rihtte
gold and gersume ȝeoue and eower ȝisles
 and cumen her on fore þe hæxete of Rome
 and swerie me æþes þat æþ heom scel iwurþen
 and bicumen nu mine men and mine monscipe hæien
 and ȝif ȝe þis nulleþ alle ich ȝeow aquelle
Ah swiþe ham rideþ leou wer here ich eow abide
Ȝif ȝe spekeþ mid rihte comeþ todæi a seouennihte
and ȝif ȝe spekeþ wowe bilæuet inne Rome
 and ich eou wullen to faren and bringen eou sorwen an kare
Þeos swiken gunnen ride ham into Rome
 and ȝarekeden heore ȝeouen and alle heore ȝisles
 and to heore dæie brohten to Beline kinge
 and he heom faire vnderfeng and freondscipe bihehte
Ȝisles heo him ȝeouen sone and his men bicome
and he mid þan ilke foreward fusde eft aȝenward
 and þa swiken sone ferden to Rome
Belin and Brenne beie tosomne
nomen heom to ræde and to somrune
þat heo wolden liþen þurhout Lumbardie
and faren to Alemainne and þa aþelene biwinnen
Þa Almainnisce men weoren of here cume warre
 and heo gadereden heom toȝeines strongliche ferden 
of alle þeon londe þon keiser hæfde an honde
 and þa Romanisce men ful ȝære hit iseȝen
þat Belin and Brennes beiene weoren ifarenne
Heo ȝærkeden ræhþen twa þusend rideres
and swiþe an hiȝende senden heom efter
Heo letten forþ bisiden anoþer folc riden
ten þusend kempen alle icudde
þat heo biforen comen þan kaiser to helpe
þe wolde aȝen king Belin feht ihalden
 and þat Romanisce floc riden heom bihinden
Heo þohten heom beon onfest þer þe hulles weore mest
 and senden heom arewen i þon weie narewe
slean heore lauerd Belin and his broþer mid him
Heo forȝeten here ȝisles and þat griþ þat heo ȝurden
æþes and þa treuþen þerfore heo hauede teonen
Belin and his broþer beien weoren warre
of þon swikedome þe heom com of Rome
þa haueden heo þa mære æie of þan Alemainnisce kaisere
Þa speken heo mid ræde for heo haueden neode 
þat Brennes and his ferde aȝen faren sculde
fehten wih þat Romanisce folc and fellen ȝef heo mihten
 and Belin bæh ouer munt mid muclen his strengþe
to feahten wiþ þon keisere and wih þon Alemainisce here
fondien on fehte ȝif he hine ouercumen mæhte
 and wheþer heore of þen broþeren þe ærht his fæht ouercome
come onȝean sonen to helpen þon oþer
Þe folc of Burguine ferde aȝan mid Brenne
of France and Peitou sworen him and plicten
of þan Maine and of þan Turuine treuliche him hærden
of Normandie and of Flaundres freoliche him fulsten
 and of Lohærenne heo liþe to mid strengþe
 and þat folc of Cascuine þe noht nælden griþien
 and folc of fele leode þe liþe forþ mid Brennen
to þan Romanisce men þe heom æfter uoren
Brenne and his folc heom to comen
Anan swa heo iseiȝen Brennes buȝe heom toȝennes
swa þat Romainnisce folc sohte to flæinde
 and heo heom æfter foren and monie þer fullen
 and swiþe monie þer fluwen and ferden to Rome
 and Brennes þe riche softe heom beh æfter
mid starkere fore ferde toward Rome
and Belin þe aþel king wes in Alemainne
Ferde he hauede inoh muchel and vnifeie
Bruttes and Wailsce Scottes and Densce
þer wes Godlac þe king þe god wes to neode
Þa iherden tellen þe ten þusend cnihtes
þe weoren icumen of Rome þan keisere to fulsten
þat Brennes þe riche ferde touward Rome
and summe heore men islæȝene and summe todriuene
nomen heom ræde þat þeonenen heo wolden riden
riht touward Rome eære Brennes þider come
Þat word com to Belinne of Brennes his broþer
heo he hauede itaken on and al whet he haueden idon
And oþer sonde þer com þe sone him talde
þat tweie þusend cnihtes þe werren i þon Alemainnesce fehte
wolden aȝen sone faren into Rome
 and al makeden heore faren alse ha wolden a þare niht faren
Belin wes swiþe wis and warscipe him folweden
he hauede monie Alemains mid agge toheowen
and monie he ledde isunde mid him ibunden
He hauede tweine wisse men i þon fuhte biwunnen
þeo cuþe þes londen lawen and speken whit þon leoden
Belin king heom to spæc and þus heom wiþ spilede
Ihere ȝe cnihtes whet ich eow wulle cuþen
Ic inc habbe beiene an inne mine benden
Ȝif ȝet wulleþ after ræde faren ich inc wulle freoiȝen
mid gode ræue bihon and makien inc riche
faren mid me suluen and ich inckere freond wurþe
ȝif ȝit me wulleþ laden þe cunne þas leoden
riht to þan weie þe ȝit witen ful wel
þar þis Romanisce folc forþ wulleþ riden
and we heom sculleþ fon on and heom wiþ fahten
feollen oure feondes and faren after Brenne
 and liþen mid ræde and Rome biliggen
and þis ich inc biseche þat al we wurþen sele
Þa cnihtes weoren wise and ful ȝerewitele
 and al ham iwurden þe Belin heom toȝernde
and heom markede forþ touward Muntgiu heo ferden
into ane mucele bæche þa munte bihalues
þer heo forþ sculden cumen þa weoren þa gumen feie
Belin wes bi hullen swiþeliche stille
þa comen liþen þa weore Romleoden
Belin heom to leop biforen and bihinden
Þeo cnihtes weoren vnwepned þa þe wæne heom wes ȝeueþe
heo wenden to beon sikere þeo Belin heom on sohte
Ne nomen heo nonne cniht quic ah alle heo heom aqualden
for nauede Belin nan cnihte þet he næs þere god kimppe
ne neauere nenne herdswein þat he ne fahte alse þein
ne næuer nænne hirdcnaue þat he nas wod on his laȝe
Þat faht bigon at midniht and laste þat hit wes dæiliht
 and swa þene dæi longe heo wenden seoþþen þa muntes
and qualden alle þa ilke þe aniht weoren atcropene
Belin a þene mærȝen letten blawen his bemen
 and beonnede his ferde hahte forþrihtes
riden þenne ilke wæi þe forþ into Rome læi
æfter Brenne his broþer þe heom biforen wes
Brennes hit hirde suggen and his broþer abad
Forþ heo buȝen beiene þat heo come to Rome buri
Þa burh heo bileien mid heore leodferden
Þet folc þer wiþinnen heom ohtliche wiþ fehten
Belin and Brenne heo bileien al abeoten
and þa oþere hem scuten to scærpe gares
Ofte heo letten grundhat læd gliden heom an heore hæfd
stockes and stanes and strales hate
and swiþe wel heo wereden þa walles of Rome
Þer fore alle þan cræften þe heo uten cuþþen
ne for alle þen fuhte þe heore ferde makede
ne mihten heo Romewal nawiht onwalden
ah heo loseden monie þusend godere monnen
 and tuwen heom fram þan walle wa wes heore herten
Þe king him biþohten whet heo don mihten
and seiden heom bitwenen Leteþ comen sonen
þa feouwer and twenti children þe we habbeþ to ȝislen
and doþ up an waritreo þeron heo scullen winden
 and wreken þan siþes and ure wiþeriwinnen
for ȝet we scullen heom to liþen swa heom biþ ælre læþest
Þe furken weoren aræred heo teuwen up þa ȝisles 
and heom þer hengen biforen heore eldren
Wa wes heore faderen þeo heo iseiȝen heore beærn hangen
Mid muþen heo seiden mid aþen heo hit sworen
þerfore hit sculden iwurþen muchele þa wurse
swa þat for deaþe ne for lif nalden heo nauere makien griþ
for þat weoren þa richcheste and þa alre hæhȝeste
 and þa radfulleste þe wuneden in Rome
þat biforen heore eȝenen bihulden and iseȝen
þat heore bern me onheng on heȝe trouwen
Þa orles weorne iwende swiþe for þeonne
þe heom wite solden Gabius and Prosenna into Lumbardie
into þon leode efter monkunne þe heom sculden fulsten
to helpene heore monne aȝen Belinne and Brenne
Þa com þer a mon irnen from þan twam eorlen
þe brohte writrunen into þere burh of Rome
þat seide heom to soþe þat þa eorles comen
in þer ilke nihte mid ten þusend cnihten
 and mid ferde vnimete of monnen on foten
þe sculden cumen bihalues and Belin king aquellen
and Brennes his broþer beiene togadere
Ȝif ȝe me wulleþ ileuen anan swa hit beoþ auen
sendeþ ut cnihtes and biginneþ to fihten
ær hit beo midniht ich sugge eow hit soþriht
comeþ mid heore mannen Gabius and Prosenna
þe sculleþ eow wurþliche wreken on eower wiþeriwinnen
Anan swa þe dæi wes agan swa heo ȝeten openeden
letten ut cnihtes bigunnnen muchele fihtes
swa heo fehten al niht þat hit wes dæiliht
Þa com þer fusen vnimete ferde
Gabius an Prosenna mid muchele monkinne
ut of Lumbardie and liþen touward Brenne
 and he heom faht wiþ feondliche swiþe
 and Belin him resde to to þan Romanisce folke
 and heo fusden swiþe Þe faht wes unimete
þer wes ballu riue Bruttes þer fullen
Belin and Brennes burstes þare hæfden
 and þa Romanisce men remden heom uuenen
Whet wolde ȝe her niþinges mid þe Bruttisce kinge 
wende ȝe mid ginnen Romen biwinnen
wenden ȝe mid fehten to fellen uren leoden
 and beon eow seluen riche and welden al Rome
Ȝe scullen drinken eowre blod balu eow is ȝeueþe
Ȝe beoþ ure bernenne bone þerfore ȝe sculleþ breoþen
fallen and ure leoden swa eow biþ alre læþust
Belin and Brennes buȝen heom fram þan fuhte
wihinnen are muchele dic þe heo hæfden ilet dælfen
þat heore folc mihten swiþe wel wunien wiþinnen
Þerinnen heo speken þerinne heo runden
ane lutle while ne leaste hit nawiht ane mile
and þus heo seiden heom bitwune
Ȝif we hennen fareþ þus alle heo wulleþ æfter us
and ȝif hit swa ilimppeþ þat we ham cumen liþen
heorten we haueden sare and ure cun ædwit aueremare
Ah ga we heom on mid sweorde for al heo beoþ forlorne
 and ureke ue ure winemæies
for leouere us is here mid manscipe to fallen
þanne we heonne isunde farren ure frenden to scare
Þe while þe heo þus speken and spileden mid worden
wende þa þeodisce men þat Belin wolden þenne
and seiden heom bitwenen in þere burh of Rome
Nu heo wulleþ heonnen nulleþ heo namare fehten
ah Belin and his broþer al heo þoþten oþer
Heo senden ut of Rome cnihtes wel idone
feowerti hundred to hæȝen ane castele
to kepen Belin king and his broþer Brennes
and baldeliche whiþ fehten
and þa oþere of Rome riden heom bihinden
and slæn heom bitwenen and wreken ore tounen
Þe cnihtes weoren on fore fer ut of Rome
Þa hehte Belin and Brennes his broþer
Lihteþ of eowre blanken and stondeþ on eowre sconken
and kerueþ eowre spere longe and makiet heom scorte and stronge
scradieþ eower sceldes al of þe smal enden
and we eow wulleþ biforen libben oþer liggen
 and aueralc god mon harde hine sulue
for her scullen þe wædlen alle iwurþen riche 
Blawen ore bemen and banneþ ore ferde
and maken we of ure uæren fihtie ferden
and on aueralche hæpe hertoȝe stæpne
þa heom makie balde and togadere halde
 and wenden to þen walle on æuerælchere halue
hiȝendliche fo we on for alle we scullen wel don
Þeo blewen heo here bemen þat heo of Rome hit sculden iheren
and heo ut iwenden ohte kempen
Þa iseȝen heo of Rome Belin and his broþere
þa clupeden heo lude ȝeond þare leoden
Nu fleþ ure ifan nu we sculleþ heom to gan
Mid þe forwarde monnen ut wenden Prosenna
Gabius him com æfter mid fifti hundred cnihtes
mid alle heore wepnen þe weoren vniwælde
Þa oþere weoren swifte heore wepnen weoren lihte
heo leiden togadere and feonliche fuhten
Weoren heo of Rome alle ridinde
þa oþere afoten and fengen heom toȝæines
and slowen alle heore hors here hæp wes þe lættere
Gabius heo slowe Prosenna heo nomen
heo duden heore wille of þan Rommonen
alle heo slowen þat heom aȝen stoden
Heo breken þa Romwalles on auerache halue
and binnen heo iwenden and þa burh awelden
Biwunnen heo Rome þe riche burh wel idone
þer heo funden michel gold and gærsume unimete
Heo unbunde þa locun drowen ut þa baiȝes
þa palles and þa purpres þe iworht weore in Puill
alle þa maþemes þe weoren monie kunnes
Þer wes moni wrehche sone iworþen riche
al þa seouen nihte his iwil þar hefde ælc cniht
of seoluere and of golde inoh of þon londe
Letten þa kinges don fæire þinges
timbrien þa hallen bæten þa walles
þe þer weoren tobrokene mid þeon balu fehte
Letten heo climben on hæh cleopien to þon folke
þat þe kinges heom speken wiþ and þer setten heore griþ 
þat ne wurþe na man swa wod þat of oþere falle his blod
ne of his æhte ȝerne buten he hit ȝeuen him wulle
And alle þe flæmen þe iflowe buþ of Rome
þe aȝan wulleþ cumen þes kinges griþ wilniæn
and bicumen þes kinges mon alse we hit ær cuþden
cumen al mid sibben and her heore lif libben
and habben þa ilke læȝen þe stoden bi heore ældre dæwen
And Belin ure hæȝe king hit bitæcheþ Brenne
þe scæl bilæuen here and beon eower kæisere
and himseolf wule liþen and eower læue habben
nen he wule buȝen into Bruttæine
Wælle muchel wes þa wop þæ Belin þeonne wende
ah heo weoren ifrouuerd sone for þan richedom of Rome
Brennes þer boȝede king of Lumbardie
and Belin gon wenden into þisse londe
Lette he ȝeond his castles makie kinewurþe werkes
rihten alle þæ hallen and stronginen þæ walles
bulden þa bures hæien þa toures
and swa þis wunliche lond mid wurþscipe wælden
 and Brennes walde Rome fulle fiftene ȝere
þa endede Brennes wel wes Romanisce folc þæs
Heo seolf nomen heore lond and heolden on heore hond
burh and heore blissæ seoþþen Brennes wes deæd
 and Belin i þisse londe makede læȝen stronge
 and laȝen swiþe gode þe bi his liue stoden
Belin ferde to Wales and anne burh makede
he heo makeda æþþele uppen Uske þan wætere
Of þon ilke flode þe king hire nome funde
þan king heo wes deore Kæir Usch heo næmde
and seoþþen heo wes ihæten Kair Lion ich wullen seggen þe for wan
Vmbe feole ȝere æfter Belinnes forþfare
herden þe men of Rome of Belinnes deaþe                   *
and seiden heom bitwenen While he dude us tuone
Nu is þe king iburied Wrake we us on Bruttes
 and into þan londen we sullen faren bringen þer sorwen and kare
Hider heo gunnen senden of Romanisce ende
feower ferrædene þa we clipieþ ferden
þe weoren on þan ilke dæȝen legiuns ihaten
werren on alche legiun þus feole leodkempen 
six þusend and six hundred and sixti iferen
Þeos comen bi wateren of weorren heo weoren wise
heo duden i þisse londe alle leode sorwen
and auer o þon ende heomseoluen weoren isunde
 and aueralche wintre inne Wales heo wuneden
Heo iwunne þe burh Kair Uske and þerinne heo wuneden
a þat her com liþen ma of heore leoden
For ilke legiuns heo clupeden Kair Usc Kaer Liun
Seoþþen her com oþer moncun þe heo cleopeden Kaerliun
Nu ich þe habben iseid hu hit is igan of Kaerliun bi Glommargan
Fo we ȝet to Beline to þan blisfulle kinge
þa he hæuede imaked þas burh and heo inemned Kaer Usc
Þa þe burh wes strong and hende þeo gon he þonnen wenden
he wende riht to Lundene þe burh he leouede swiþe
He bigon þer ane ture þe strengeste of al þe tune
and mid muchele ginne a ȝæt þervnder makede
þeo clupede men hit Belȝæsȝate
nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þare
Leouede Belin þe king in alre blisse
and alle his leoden leoueden hine swiþe
An his dæies wes swa mochel mæte þat hit wes vnimete
þat folc þurh heore drunken moni þusend swulten
Þe king leouede longe þat hit com touward his ende
þat i Lundene he wes dæd sari wes his duȝeþe
wa wes heom on liue for þæs kinges dæþe
Heo ferden to his horde and nome þer muche deal goldes
heo makeden ane tunne of golde and of ȝimme
þene king heo duden þerinne þat wes here louerd Belin
vp heo hine duden heȝe an ufenmeste þan turre
þat me mihte hine bihalden wide ȝeon þeon londe
Þat heo duden for muchelere luue for he wes here dure læuerd
Þus iuor al Belin king seoþþen com his sune Gurguint
Gurguint Bertruc hehte his sune wellen æþele wes þe gume
welle witer wes þer a mon and wisliche heold his cunedom
Sæhte and sibbe he luuede unstronge monnen he leoþede
griþ he heolde alse his fæder god mid þon bezste
bute þat þa Densce men dunriht atsoken
þat heo to Brutlonde nolden maren senden 
gold ne garsume ne gauel of þon londe
Gurguint hine biþohte what he don mæhte
he seonde his sonde wide ȝen his londe
he beonnede his folc and ȝærekede ferde
muchele and grete mid monnen vnimete
He to scipe wende and fram þan londe hælde
ofer þane saltne strem sel hit him þuhte
A þene oþerne dæi he com to Denemarke
he iwende uppe þat lond æfter his iwille
he axede gauel of þan londe þe his fader hauede an honde
þe Gudlac king him ȝaf mid godene iwille
Þa seide Gudlakes sune mid gromiende speche
Ȝif mi fæder dude his wille nulle ich hit naht iwurþen
ah fare he ut of mine londe ȝif he wulle libbe
Þat word com to Gurguint þe wes Brutlondes king
Wher beoþ mine þeines wher beoþ mine sweines
wher beoþ mine kempes and mine kene men
Eorneþ and eærne and al þis lond bearneþ
and alle þa men slæþ þe ȝe cumeþ neh
and heore children and heore wif werpeþ into þe wæteren
and brekeþ heore walles and berneþ heore halles
seælleþ heore tures and swaleþ heore bures
 and swa heo sculden understonden þat ich am king of Brutlonde
and þat heo aȝen me to ȝelden alse heo duden Belin kinge
Forþ iwende þat hired swa þæ king hæhte
heo dude þer muchele hermes mid hæhȝere strengþe
Þe king of þan londe mid muchelere genge
com toȝeines Gurguint mid godliche strengþe
Heo fuhten wunderliche inoh and Gurguint Denemarkene king ofsloh
 and his Densce ferde he felden to þan grunde
He ferden to þan burȝen and him alle onbuȝen
and alle he awælde betere and wurse
His men heo bicomen and æþes him sworen
 and æfter cure heo him ȝeuen þreo hundred ȝisles
and al swa muchel gærsume swa Gudlac king bihehte
þa Belin inne freode and alle his iueren
And Gurguint þa iuende aȝæn into þisse londe
Ase he ferden on his wæi bi þan ende of Orcanai 
þa fonde he i sæflod þritti scipe gode
of wapmen and of wifmen þe schipe wel afulled
mid fele cunne wepnen swiþe ibone
Þuhte Gurguint þon kinge hærof swiþe sællic þing
whet þat scipen weoren þe he ifunde þere
He sende ane sonde him to and hæhte heom suggen
wannen heo weoren and whet heo þer sohten
and ȝif heo wolden speken him wih and ȝernen þes kinges griþ
Þa enswerede heore alre lauerd
We wulleþ speken him wiþ and ȝeornen his griþ
Heo togaderen come and griþ heo nomen sone
Þa queþ Pantolaus wiþ Gurguint he speke þus
We beoþ sæwerie men mid wedere bidriuene
Ich hæhte Pantolaus and þu art læuerd ouer us
we beoþ a þine londe bicumen þine laȝen we biluuieþ
and us alle þu miht walden æftere þine iwille
Of Spaine ich wes ut idriuen and al mi drihtliche folc
swiþe muchel we habbeoþ isoht bi þisse særime
a lond þe us were liþe þe we mihten on libben
ne maȝe we hit ifinden for næuer næne þinge
lond to ure leoden þer we maȝen to liþen
We habbeþ ihaued moni burst moni hunger and moni þurst
moni walc moni wind bi wilde þisse watere
Nu we biddeþ þin ære ne maȝe we drien hit namare
and ȝif hit weoren þin iwille and þu hit don woldest
to ȝifuen us an ende i þine kinnelonde
we wulleþ þine men beon þine monscipe herien
 and þe leofuen wiþ a to ure liue
Þa enswærde Gurguint þat wes Brutlondes king
Nulle ich na so don ah eower monradene ic wulle fon
and ich eow wulle senden into ane londe
for ich nat whet ȝe beoþ ne whannen ȝe icume beoþ
Ah ȝe scullen habben lædesmen and forþ ȝe scullen liþen
 and ich eow wullen lanen of mine leodfolke
fouwerti hundred cnihtes þe gode beoþ on fihte
Heo sculleþ eow þat lond bitaken þer ȝe sculleþ libben
and eower laȝen setten to rihten eore leoden
Gurguint heom sende into Irlonde 
þar nas nauer nan man seoþþen Noes flod hit hauede ouergan
 and Gurguint forþ wende into þisse londe
and Pantolaus þer ȝeonde wunde wel mid þon beste
and lette hine clepie king and his wif quene
And he sette stronge lawen to steowien his folke
for heo haueden inne sæ seorwen ibidene
fulle seouen ȝere heo misliche foren
Heore claþes weoren iwerede and vuele heo weoren igærede
nakede heo weoren and naþing ne rohten
wha heore leome sæȝe alle þe on heom weoren
 and þus heo ladden heore laȝen and longe heo ilæsten
 and Gurguint i þisse londe leouede mid blisse
 and he huld god griþ þe while þe ilaste his lif
in Kaer Liun he wes dead seorhful wes his duȝeþe
Anne sune he hauede aht mon Guencelin ihaten
he walde þis lond and þas duȝeþe æfter his fader dæie
Þes wes þurþut alle þing clæne mon and god king
he ledde swiþe feir lif and he hæfde a god wif
Marcie men heo clupede þat is ȝet widene cuþ
nu and aueremare is taken of here heare
Þeo quene leornede anne craft heo wes a boken wel itaht
heo leornede hire lære leofliche on heorten
of hire wisdome sprong þat word wide
þat heo wes swiþe wis of wordliche dome
Þa makede heo ane læȝe and læide ȝeon þat leode
þeos laȝe wes al iworhte
Bruttes nemneden þa laȝen æfter þare lafuedi
to soþen wihuten wene þe laȝe hehte Marciane
Seoþþen þeræfter monie hundred wintre
com Alfred þe king Englelondes deorling
and wrat þa laȝen on Englis ase heo wes ær on Bruttisc
and whærfde hire nome on his dæȝe and cleopede heo Mærcene laȝe
Ah þet I þe sugge þurh alle þing ne makede heo noht ærst Ælured king
ah heo makede þa quene þe me Mærcie cleopede
and Ælured heo seide on Englisc þis is seoþ ful iwis
Hæfde þas wise quene bi hire weoreldkinge 
ænne lutelne sune Sillius ihaten
nefde heo children na ma þerforen wes þere quene wa
Nefde þis child Sillius buten seouen ȝeæra
þa his fader wes dæd and his duȝeþe bileæfde
His moder nom þas riche and mid ræde heo walde
 and wiste wel hire sone a mid hireseolue
Þa þe sune wes swa ald þat he wes an horse bald
þa makede heo hine king his folke hit wes iqueme
He wes a god mon and softe he wolde libben
ne leouede he noht half his lif þat him ne com his dædsih
He bilefde tweie sunen þa tuwen þes fader þæuwes
Þe aldre hæhte Rummarus þe ȝungere hæhte Damus
Rummarus wes ane while king and seoþþen Damus hit onfenge
Þes Damus on his deie ane chiuese him ichæs
he hauede bi þare wimman enne swiþe wandliche sune
Morpidus ihaten monnene strengest
of maine and of þeauwe of alle þissere þeode
Þes biȝet þesne kinedom þurh kenschipe muchele
cniht he wes swiþe strong kene and custi muchel and long
of alle þingen heo weore god ȝif heo neore towamed
Anan se he wes wraþ wiþ eni mon i þan stude he hine wolde slæn
nere he na swa riche cniht þat he hine ne sloh forþriht
weore hit riht hit woh i þon stude he hine sloh
 and sone swa he iwraþ glad he dude al þat me hine bad
Ah hit wes muchel hærme of ane mon swa hende
þat þurh his wraþþe his wit wes awemmed
A þon ilke time com þe duc of Moraine
into þisse londe leode to hærme
ferde bi þere sæbrimme and monie burstes dude
he makede muchel ræflac ræh he wes on fihte
Æfter sæ he forh laþ to Norþhumberlonde
þer he gon bulde castel swiþe strongne
al abuten him þat londe he nom to his aȝere hond
Morpidus þe balde iwærþ him abolwen
and sende ȝeond þæs ærde and sommnede ferde
and com to þon duke al bi lihte dæie 
Þer wes moni god Brut and moni bisi kempen
þeo fihten wiþ þone duke al þene dæi longe
Þa hit wes muchel uppe non þe king þene duc ouercom
he turnde to fleme and he æfter him ferde
Þer he sloh þene duc and al his duȝeþe
ær þe dæi weoren agon dæd heo weoren alle
mid swiþe stronge fihte þet wes mid rihte
and alle þa he funde amarwe in þon londe
oþer mid fure he lette hom slæn oþer he heom lette quic flan
Mid muþe heo hit seiden þeo þat hit iseȝen
þat Morpidus mid his honden þurh hæhȝere strengþe
seouen hundred ofsloh and swende mid wepnen
He lette makien ane dich þe wes long and swiþe deop
and he lette al þat wel weorpen þer an innen
Þa huld he ane stunde his lond mid isunde
inn griþe and inne friþe and freoliche on folke
Wnder þon hær com tidinde salcuþ to londe
and hit wes sone icuþ Morpidun þan king
þat wes icumen of þare sæ a deor swiþe sellich
frommard Irlonde com hider liþen
and bi þon særime rasde to þon folke
Oft an one dæie hit makede an hundred fæie
and æft to þare sæ wende þe wældscæþe luþere
þenne hit æft wende aȝan wærþe hit heom grætte
Þus hit to londe bæh and werede þeos leoden
þat folc hit agaste tunes hit aweste
þat folc awai hald an aulchere halue
Þe king hit harde seggen and særi wes an hurten
þiþerward wende þe king himseolue to wæine
toward þon deore þer he dæþ fæhte
Þa he com suþ swa feor þer þe feond wunede
þa hahte he al his hirdfolc faren to are burȝe
and hæhte heom þer abiden and ane he gon riden
Þa he forþ wende wapnen he ladde
þat wes a kene sweord and enne koker fulne flan
enne boȝe swiþe strong and a spere swiþe long
æt his sadele an æx and æt þe oþer hælue an hondsæx
and forþ he gon wenden towarde þan ende 
þer he herde suggen þat þe feond wonede
Swa longe he ferde þat he hit ifunde
and he lette fuse him to flan swuþe kene
and alle him to sende and seoþþen him neor wende
he ferde on his stede sulc he walde awede
Þa his flæn weoren iscoten þæ iwærd his boȝe tobroken
he igrap his spere stronge þer he pihte hit o þon londe
and he ærde to þon deore and smat hit a þan sweore
þat þe deor feol abac and þe scæft al tobrac
And þat deor up astod and ræsde o þene stede
and forbat him þa breste ban and þa senuwen
þat þa lihte and þa liuere feollen on eorþen
And þe king droh his sweord þe him wes itase
and þet deor he smat anan uppe þat hæuedbæn
þat þet sweord in deæf and þa hilt on his hand bræc
And þat deor todede his chæfles and to þan kinge weoþede
and forbat hine amidden a twa þat wes þat fiht idon
Þus ferde þe king for he wes to kene
for þe mon is muchel sot þe nimeþ to himseoluen
mare þonne he maȝen walden he sæl halden þe raþer
for vnræd is swiþe ræh his lauerd he let reosen
and auer vmbe stunde felleþ hine to þe grunde
Þet folc wes swiþe særi for sorwen þes kinges
and hit wes bliþe for dæþþen of þon deore
Þe king hæfden fif sunen bi feire his quene
Þe aldest hehte Gorbonian welle æþel wes þere a mon
Argal hæhte þe oþer þe wes Gorbonianes broþer
Þe þridde hæhte Elidur þe feorþe Ingenes þe fifte Peredur
Þe ældeste broþer Gorbonian he iwærþ king in þisse londe
he wes swiþe soþfest and swiþe wel iþæwed
radful and rihtwis and a mete runhende
He heold þis lond stille al æfter his iwille
mid treouscipe gode þe while his tir læste
and þus he hine huld an hæfne þat com his liues ende
inne Lundene he liþ særi weoren his leode
Þeræfter com þe oþer Argal his broþer
þe wes next him iboren seoþþen he wes king icorn
Þis wes þe forcuþþeste mon þe æfre hedde kinedom 
vnriht him wes leof and rihtwisnesse him wes laþ
whatse hæfde richedom he hine makede wræcche mon
his gode men he hatede þa uuele he hæhȝede
al his motinge was ful of ȝitsinge
He somnede togædere gærsumme muchele
 and æuere he þohte embe uuel and swulche weoren his dede
Þus ladde Argal his lif fram ȝuȝeþe to his dædsiþ
Togædere commen þa riche men þe aȝe weoren and mæhti
 and makeden heore hustinge mid hæhere wraþþe
Plihten mid honden þat heo wel hulden
þurh alle þing flemen Argal heore king
and ut heo hine flemden feor of þissen earde
and nomen þene oþer Elidur his broþer
Þis wes þe þridde heo afengen hine mid sibbe
 and makeden hine to kinge þe cniht wes swiþe kene
he wes of his speche ælche monne imete
wiþ þa goden he wes duhti and sturne wiþ þa dusie
Argal þe wes idriuen ut drof him wes on heorte
he ferde feor ȝeond moni lond and fondede þan leoden
he bisoþte monienne king and monienne keiser
monienne richene þein monienne baldne swein
he bisohte al þat folc þer he forþ ferde
þat heo him solde helpen to muchelure neode
mid strengþe oþer mid ginne his lond to biwinne
Ne mihte he neuere finden mon þe him wolde ȝette beon
þe him oht wolde fulsten þat he hider fore
ne naþing him bihæten þat heo him wolden helpen
Þa wes Argal þe king ærm on his mode
seorhful on heorte for his muchele burste
Argal hine biþohte whet he don mihte
þat he wolde aȝen fare and fondien his broþer
and war he mihte of his monnen æie milce ifinden
Hit wes vmbe fif winter seoþþe he heonne ferde
seoþþen he þas seorȝe himseolfen hæfde itimbred
þa lette he hine atlichen and wende to þissen londe
wiþ his aȝene kun he hine vncuþ makede
ne icneow hine nauere na man þe hine ær iseȝen hæfden
He fræinede þis leodfolc æfter heore kineleouerde
 and heo him þene king tahten þer he huntede on comelan 
wiþ his hirdiferen i þon wude of Kalatere
Þeone king he imette and mildeliche hine igrætte
Læuerd king quaþ Argal hæil wurþ þu an isunde
Þu ært mi broþer Elidur eædi beo þu æuere
ne der ich noht kennen for þisses londes monnen
þat ich her king weore leste heo me icneowen
ah ich bidde þine ære nu and æueremare
Þa quaþ Elidur þe king þi cume me is iqueme
To his broþer he com and leofliche hine custe
þer Elidur þe king weop mid his eȝenen
and mid muchelen ædmeden æþelede his broþer
and lette hine læden leofliche and stille
into ane castle Clud wes ihaten
and lette hine baþien and beddien feire
and duȝeliche hine biwitten and his namen dærnen
What iherden auere suggen a sæȝen oþer a spelle
þat æuere æni broþer dude þus for oþer
þat Elidur þe king dude for Argale
Þe king hine braeid sæc alse þeah hit seoþ weore
þe king læi on bure særiliche on beadde
He sende his sonde ȝeond his kinelonde
lette laþien him to al his leodþeines
mid wurden and mid writen þe dude heom wel to witen
þat ne mihte he no lengere libben on eærþe
ah of heom þe king wolde habben read for hiȝenliche he weoren dæd
and heo him redden wher his lich mihte bezst leggen
Þet word wes cuþ ȝeond þis lond and come þeos cnihtes
to burh þis kinges to muchelen hustinge
Þe king and his broþer weoren in ane bure
þeær heo hæfden wel iȝeten and seoþþen idrunken
Þe king eoden to bedde and his broþer hiine hudde
and mid him his leoueste men þe he wuste on liue
feowerti gode cnihtes mid burnen wel idihten
mid sweorden and mid schelden alse heo to fehte sculden
Þe king læi in his bædde alse þæh he ne mihte libben
in þære burh he sende word bi his beste wikeneren
and hæhten his drihliche folc stilleluker dremen
for his hæhued oc sæ sweþen þat he ne mihte idriȝen
to ihæren þene muchele drem of swa feole mannen 
Þe king lette witen his durren þat ne moste þer na mon in cumen
ne wiþinne þon castelburi na quic mon iboren
bute þe king mid his seonden æfter him sende
Þe king aras of bedde and burne he warp on rigge
and nam onne his honde ane wiæxe stronge
and cluppede into bure Argal his broþer
And nomen heore sonde and into þere burh senden
æfter þon hehste þringe þat he comen to þen kinge
Seone swa he to bure com þe king hine inom
and he him wræþ to ase he hine wolde anho
 and him abuten urnen cnihtes swiþe sturne
alse heo wolden mid heonden al hine toheowen
Þus seiden Elidur þe king Nu ich þe wulle quellen
bute þu beo stille and don al mine wille
Þus andswerde þe þein Ich hit wulle don fæin
Bicum her mines broþer mon ȝif þu þi lif wult habbe
Þis is Argal þe king þe of eærde wes iflemed
þe is nu hider icumen and eower king scal iwurþen
Þe þein swiþe stille dude al þes kinges wille
and seoþþen þe king hine lette don into ane derne bure
 and lette enne cniht eærne æfter an oþer eorle
and swa he þer agon ase þe oþer hæfde idon
Þus dude Elidur þe king bi allen þeos eorlen
bi ane and bi ane þat he heom hæfde al clane
Þa dude he anoþer nom he his broþer
mid muchelere blisse to Eowrwik hine brohte
þer weoren þeos leoden iliþenned togadere
Atforen al his folke he his kinehelm onfeng
 and sette hit on his broþer hæfd and hæf hine to kinge
Æuer seoþþen iwarþ Argal aþelest ærle kingen
þat vuel he al forlette þat gode he imette
iwærþ he swiþe milde þan ȝunge and þan alden
 and wiþ alle monnen ful iwis iwærþ þe king rihtwis
Þis lond wes istaþeled and stod i þon ilke
fulle ten ȝere þa iwærþ þe king vnfere
swa þe king seoc læi þreo wiken and enne dæi
ne mihte he þerof beon hæl ah dæd wes þe king Argal
Þa comen al þeos leoden liþen tosomne 
and nomen eft Elidur and duden hine to his aþþelen
heuen hine to kinge mid hæȝere blisse
and hit ane stunde stod on himseolue
 and Elidur wes æþelest of alle his moncunne
Iuienes and Perredur iseȝen þat Elidur
wes eft iwurþen leodking ouer þisse londe
Heo somneden muchel folke of feole cunne monnen
and ledden here ferde wide ȝeond þissen ærde
Togædere com Elidur Ingenes and Peredur
særliche heo feohte and fælden heore cnihtes
Þa sette i þon fuhte Elidur to flænne
and his broþeren him æfter mid alle here mæhte
Ingenes and Perredur nomen þene king Elidur
heo hine lædde to Lundene særi weoren his leoden
In are swiþe stronge tur heo duden þene king Elidur
moni ȝer and moni dæi þe king in þære ture læi
and his broþeren gunnen liþen wide ȝeond þeos leoden
Iuienes hæfde half þis londe riht bi þere Humbre
al þesne suþ ende he heold an his heonde
 and Peredur hæfde norþ al bi þere Humbre forþ
 and seoþþen þeræfter al togæderen he hit ahte
for Ingenes ne leouede buten seouen ȝeren
Þa nom Peredur al þis lond and sette an his aȝere hond
 and he iwarþ him swuþe luþer and læh al his folke
Þæ com þe færliche dæd and falde hine to grunde
swa vuele he luuede his lif þat þe Scucke hine ifenge
Þæ somnede al þis leodfolc into Lundene ferden
 and nomen ut Elidur þer he læi in are tur
and duden þer a selcuþ þing makeden hine þridde chærre king
Þa iwarþ he swa duhti swa þe dæi feire
alle folc he dude riht wel wes þisse londe idiht
inne blisse leouede his leode to murhþe
 and þa he sculde of liue wende he hæfde feiren ende
Þa com his broþer sune Gorbonianes
þe wes þe formeste of þæn fif broþeren
þe cniht wes ihaten Lador he wes þisse londes king
ah Lador ne luuede buten ane lutle wile
Æfter him com Morgan sune Argales 
a ȝer he hulde þas leoden and seoþþen he dun læi
Ænmaunus hæhte þe oþer þe wes Morganus broþer
þeos weoren mannes sunes þeos ær weoren kinges
Þes ilke Enmaunus heold his kinelond þus
þat nas na þein in þissen londe þat nalde hine fæin slæn mid his honden
and al his folc he hatede and al he hit hænde
wiþ al folc he wes wiþerward þe Wurse hine leouede
and his aȝene heredmen hine to deaþe hateden
Neoþeles on ende þat folc of þissen londen
fusden hine and flæmden feor of þissen ærde
for he wes swa wiþerward heo driuen hine of þis ærde
mid seorwen and mid seore ne com he her nauermare
Togadere commen þe hæhste eorles of þissen londe
and curen heom enne king of ane cnihte þe wes kene
he wes Inienes sune of Peredures kunne icume
Iwallo hæhte þe king he wes god þurh alle þing
wel he braid on deade efter his alderen
of alre godnesse þe gume wes ilæred
he hæfde gode þæwes his þeode wes þæ betere
Ac hit wes ladlich burst þat he ne moste libben
na lengere þene seouen ȝere ne mosten he luuien here
dæd wes Iwallo þe king his duȝeþe he bilæfde
Seoþþen her rixlede a king Rime wes ihaten
he wes Peredures bæren he wes Elidures broþer
Seoþþen com Goronces sune Elidures
Seoþþen wes Catulus his fæder hæhte Goroncius
Seoþþen com Coillus his broþer hæhte Catulus
Seoþþen com Porex king he wes of þeon kunne
Seoþþen com Cherin he wes Porexus cun
Ah Cherin leouede longe inne þisse londe
ah þa oþer six kinges þe ær weoren on londe
ne leouede nan here fulle æhte ȝere
ah longe leouede here Cherin muchel he dronk mede and win
weoren al his duȝeþen bilefed oppe drenche
and al he leas his wurþscipe for þon winscenche
ne dude nauer oþer god ne greiþe on his þeode 
Ah selliche þinges weoren of þissen kinge
swa he leoueden here wel feole ȝere
swa næuere vnleoden þis lond ne iseoþten
ah þis lond wes on griþe and ifulled mid gode
Þa com þe ilke dæi þat þe king deæd læi
þa hæfde he þreo sunen bi hæȝere his quene
þe aldeste hæhte Fulgenius Aldus and Andragus
Ah ful lutle wile liuede þas ilke
ælc of heom an stunde wes king in þissen londe
ac wiþinne feouwer ȝere alle heo weoren dæde her
Þe ȝungeste of þan breþeren þe wes þe bezste
Andragus he hæhte enne sune he hehde
Urrian hæhte þat childe þe iwærþ þisse leodes king
a ȝer he leouede and seoþþen he dæd þolede
Æfter þon kinge Vrian wes Eliud his kunnesmon
Þa com Cledaus Doten and Gurguincius
Þeos ilka þreo kinges heolden þas þeode
an efter ane þæt dæd heo weoren alle
ah nawiht heo her ne duden nouþer god ne ufel
Seoþþen com Merian þes wes a swiþe hende mon
hundes and hauekes he hæuede vnimete
þat æuereelche dæi he pleuwede mid his deoren
Ah he wes swa feir mon þat wifmen hine luueden
þerof he nom ȝemen ah hit nes him noht iqueme
ah he luuede his quene æuere bi his liue
Seoþþen wes Bledon his sune and blæþfest king
he hæfde inoh god and hit his gumen dælde
nes neuer seoþþen næ king swa custi þurh alle þinge
Seoþþen wes his sune king Cap wes ihæten
Æfter Cap Oein for elchen vuele he wes fein
Seoþþen com Sillius þe wes Oæines sune
Seoþþe sone æfter þet com a king Blæþgabreat
Seoþþen þeos worle wes astolled ne cuþe na mon swa muchel of song
of harpe and of salteriun of fiþele and of coriun
of timpe and of lire gleomen him weoren deore
he cuþen al þeos songes and þat gleo of ilcche londe 
Of him wes muchel speche ȝeond þas woruldriche
swa þat al þis moncun þat of him iherden tellen
seiden þat he wes god of alle gleocræften
Æuer wes þe king glad and æuere he gomen luueden
 and þus he lædde his lif þe while þe hit ilæste
Seoþþen wes his broþer king Arkinaus ihæten
he hit heolde seouen ȝeore i griþe he wunede here
Seoþþen wes his sune king þe vniseliche luuede
Ældolf men cleopeden þene king his deden weoren forcuþe
Nes nan swa god wif i þon londe þe he walde
ȝif heo wes a wiht hende þat he ne makede hore
þæh hit weoren an eorles wif he binom hire al hire æþelen
þe ȝunge wifmen and þe ælde he makeden to sconde
For þisse vniwærste laȝe his leode hine hateden
into þan bare dæþe nalde he for þon hit bileæfue
Seoþþen com Redion and rædden þissen þeoden
half ȝer and seouen niht þa wes he dæd forhriht
Seoþþen Redært his broþer lasse while þenne þe oþer
Seoþþen com an þe leouede wel he hæhte Famulpenicel
on his liue he wes swa riche alle þon oþere vniliche
Seoþþen com a king þe hæhte Pir his hæd wes swulc swa beoþ gold wir
þet al folc wundreden on wheonene com swa feir mon
Æfter him com Capor þe king wes on þeode
Æfter him com Eligille þe heold þis lond ful stille
þes wes a swiþe wis mon and of alle þinge wel idon
mid blisse he luuede here fif and twenti ȝere
Seoþþen wes king his sune Heli ȝeres fulle feouwerti
oþer wile he heold griþ and oþer while me fæht him wiþ
He wes a swiþe æht gume and he streonde þreo snelle sunen
Lud wes ihaten þe an he wes a swiþe æht mon
þe midlest Casibellaunus þe ȝungeste hehte Nennius
Æfter Heli king æhte þis lond Lud his sune wel longe
þes wes swiþe oht king and vnimete kene
and he wes swiþe riche for rædes he luuede
He ferde ȝeond al þis kinelond and ælche burh he makede strong 
castles makede Lud þe king and Lundenne he luuede þurh alle king
Þe ȝeht þe Lud king ahte þis lond hehte Lundene Trinouant
and of castles ner þer naþing bute þat tur þe makede Belin king
al swa þes boc her telleþ biuore a þissen spelle
Lud king lette legge þane wal abuten þe burh of Lundene al
þe auere ȝet haueþ ilast and swa he wule ȝet wel longe
He letten bulden þe hallen swiþe muchele mid alle
he hehte ilchene riche mon þat he dælde his æhte atwam
 and nome þa hæluendale and hæh bold him makede
and alle þæ vnstronge men þere burh he duden wiþuten
 and heȝede þæ burh and makede heo swiþe hende
He leide adun þere burhȝe nome and nemnede hire æfter himseoluen
 and hehten heo Kaer Lud and oueral hit let cuþen
Þat he duden al for þon þat seoþþen sculden moni mon
þennen þe king weoren dæd demen of his weorken
Seoþþen her com vncuþ folc faren in þessere þeode
 and nemneden þa burh Lundin an heore leodewisen
Seoþþen comen Sæxisce men and Lundene heo cleopeden
þe nome ileste longe inne þisse londe
Seoþþen comen Normans mid heore niþcraften
and nemneden heo Lundres þeos leodes heo amærden
Swa is al þis lond iuaren for uncuþe leoden
þeo þis londe hæbbeþ biwunnen and eft beoþ idriuen hennene
And eft hit biȝetten oþeræ þe uncuþe weoren
 and falden þene ælden nomen æfter heore wille
of gode þe burȝen and wenden heore nomen
swa þat nis her burh nan in þissere Bruttene
þat habbe hire nome æld þe me arst hire onstalde
Þa gon þis lond wenden þat com þis kinges ende
Lud king iwarþ dæd in Lundene me hine leide
þer weoren eorles swiþe whæte and leiden þene king bi ane ȝate
þat ȝet me cleopeþ ful iwis Port Lud a Bruttisce
Seoþþen comen Ænglisce men wel waht and cleupeden hit Ludesȝate
and swa hit haueþ wel longe o þon nome istonde
Þa weoren þer twa children Ludes sunen kinges
þe ældre hæhte Androgeus þe oþer Temelcinus 
Þas children uueren lutle þa here fader deȝede
Þa com heore fader broþer Cassibelaunus
and iwærþ himsulf to kinge and biwuste þas children
and leofliche heom fedde for luue of his broþer
Þes Cassibellaunus wes þisses londes king
þe leodes hine luueden for his laȝen weoren gode
he sette feire þeauwes in þissen þeoden
and he wes swiþe god king and god cniht þurh alle þing
Þeos children weoxen an hond þat heo mihten halden lond
þe king heom ȝef gode tweien eorldomes
Androgeus him wes leouere and he him Lundene ȝæf
 and þermid he ȝæf him al Kent for he him wolde iquemen
 and he hehte Tennancius to Cornwale temen
and freoliche þas twein broþerne heolden þas eorldomes
buten þat heo icneowen þene king for heore herre
for he wes heore lauerd and al þissere leodene
Þa wile þa heo weoren sæhte and heore men on some
þis lond ferde swiþe wel mid sibbe heo hulden
ah seoþþen heo iwærþen wærþe and hit iwærþ þa weorse
swa þat Romleode comen to þissen þeoden
and sette ȝeld a þisse londe æiþer seluer and gold
þe næuer eær on liue ne dursten hider liþen
axien king of þissen londe þat he ȝefue ȝeld into Rome
Þa wes hit ilumpen o þan daȝen ase we soþ suggen maȝen
þat Iulius Scezar wes iuaren mid vnimete ferde
from Rome into France Þe feond wes iwraþþed
Al þa londes he biwon þe he mid eȝene lokede on
he þohte to biwinnen mid strengþen and mid ginnen
al middeleærdes lond and halde þat worlde in his hond
Ah he ne mihte hit don al þas wurlde under fote
ah þa þreo dale he biwon of þissere wurlderiche
fif and fifti kinelond he biwon to his aȝere hond
wiþuten his riche þe ær læi to Rome
Cniht he wes kene ȝeond al middelærde cuþ
he wes þe wisseste mon of al þe worulderiche
he makede þane kalender þe dihteþ þane moneþ and þe ȝer
he dihte feole domes þe ȝet stondeþ ine Rome
Wale þat eæuere ei sucche mon into helle sculde gan
Iulius wende of Rome mid folke wel idone 
he ferde ouer Lumbardie swa he dude ouer Muntgiwe
he biwon Loherne and Gascunne Peytou
Normandie and Brittaine and Luueine and Alemaine
