Seoþþen he hæfde iwunnen Gascunne he charde aȝen into Burgunne
into Flandres he ferde and makede his schipfærde
Hit wes an ane time
þat þe dæi wes liht and þe sunne wes swiþe briht
and Cezar rad ȝeond Flaundre lond an scewede þære sæstrond
Þat weder wes swiþe liþe and he þis lond ikende
Þa freinede Iulius and wiþ þon folke he spec þus
Wat his þat ilke æitlond þat ich mid æȝen iseo
feor ouer sæstram feir hit me þuncheþ
A wis mon þus quaþ and mid þæne kæisere spæc
Þæt is a muchel æitlond of alche gode hit is strong
þet Bruttes ærest ifeng þer beoþ duhtie men
Brutaine hit hatte þat lond þe þu bihaldest
Þa spæc Iulius Cezar he wes wis and swiþe iwar
Wel ich hit wæt what Bruttis wæs for mine bæc hit me suggeþ
alle we comen of ane kunne alse þe bæc hit us cuþþeþ
Vre aldren weoren i Troie þer heo teone þoleden
æt þon muchele fæhte moni þeosend þer weoren fæie
Þa heo weoren ouercumen þæ quahten heo wide
and ferde sichinde lond þer heo mihten on libben
Þer Bruttus bicom and to his liue he wunede þeran
Þeonnenen come þa kinges þe weoren wunder kene
Belin and Brennes þe Rome biwunnen
Heo forferde Rome þa burh wel idone
heo nomen of Romanisce londe muchel seoluer and gold
heore ȝisles heo letten anhon heore folc heo letten fordon
Þet dude Belin and his broþer ah nou þer is anoþer
Ich hahte Iulius Cezar þerfore is min herte sær
þet me mine ældre dude scome ær ich weore mon ibore
Ah nu ich wulle sende into þon lond
to iwiten at þon bezste ȝif heo me wulleþ buȝen
and ȝif heo me wulleþ senden gauel of heore londe
for ȝif heo wulleþ ȝirne griþ nulle ich heom noht fehten wiþ
Findeþ me tweien wise men þe wel cunnen a speche 
He bitæhten heom forþriht a writ þe wes al idiht
and grætte Cassibellaune þene king of Bruttaine
Þus seide þat writ þe wel bar þe ernde
Ich æm Iulius Scesar þe of Rome em icumen her
Ȝif þu wult ȝirne griþ nele ic þe noht fehten wiþ
And hiȝendliche me sende gauel of þine londe
þu sulf mi mon bicumen and for kaisere me halden
for al hit is min aȝen þat ic iseo mid min æȝen
Cassibellane iseh þat writ þerfore he wes abolȝen
he wes wunderliche wrah for þes tidinde him wes læþ
A writ he lette makien mid muchere wraþþe
al wiþute grætinge sende hit Cesar þon kinge
Þat writ to þon keisere com þeos wordes weoren þeron idon
Sillich us þuncheþ Cezar þu ært swa wis and swa war
þat þu þenchest to beon keisere of alle quike monne
Þu ært icumen of Rome þine word beoþ swiþe store
Of ure londe þu axest ȝeld and ne scelt þu þerfore ȝælpen
Þu sulf ært swiþe gripel þine gumen sunden ȝefere
þu þenchest to setten o þin hond al middelærdes lond
We beoþ in ane æitlonde at þere worldes ende atstonde
þe Bruttes biwunne and we wunieþ þeron
 and freoliche we hit haldeþ wiþ alle weoruldkingen
 and þe nulle we næuere sende gauel of ure londe
for ȝif þu weore al swa wis swa ich wende þat þu weore
þenne woldest þu vnderstonde þæt we beoþ in ure londe
freo and swa scone swa þi folc is of Rome
for ure ældere ut of Troye fluȝen and of anne kunne we beoþ icumen
þine aldren and ure at Troye wuren ifeire
Ȝif þu me wult ilæiuen boten þu us wullen bilæiuen
þu scalt of Brutten muchel balu habben
þu and þine iferen ȝif þu auere cumest here
For ure aldren weoren kinges inne þisse londe
Belin and Brenne beiene tosomne
heo biȝeten Rome mid richere strengþe
and hit is ore irihte þat þu an rixlest
 and forþi þu ahtest me to ȝulden gauel of þine londe
and þu hit halst on unriht þerfore þu scalt habben pliht
for þu waldest beon min hærre and þu me sculdest buȝen 
Cezar iseh þis writ and he hit wraþliche biheold
abolȝen he wes on mode he weorp hit to his foten
Wær beo ȝe mine cnihtes þe gode beoþ to fihte
Leteþ ȝarkni mine scipen for nu we scullen wende
and forþ we scullen buȝen into Bruttaine
and nimen þer þis londes king and quic hine forbærnen
 and biȝutten al þat lond to ure aȝere hond
Sixti scipen heo makeden vnimete muchele
þeos weoren al neowe stronge and wel itreowe
of lasse scipen þar weoren swa feole þat nuste na man þe tale
Þeo com heom a wedere wunderliche feire
heo ferden from stronde touward þisse londe
heo turnden to hauene inne þare Temese
þer þa Temese and þa sæ heomseoleuen imetteþ
Sone come þa tiþende to þisse londes kinge
 and he hit letten cuþen wide ȝeonde þissere þeode
þat Cezar wes hider icomen and wraþ he hafde þis lond inumen
Cassibellaune þe king wes war þurh alle þing
he wuste wel of heore cume þat hauen of Douere he hauede inumen
Þer lai mid his ferde þe king of þissen earde
þider com tiþende þat him wæs sær þat icumen wes Iulius Cezar
Moni wes þe kempe þe wes mid Cassebellaune þe king
 and he hafde enne stiwarde þene wisseste mon of al þis ærde
Belan he wes ihaten bæȝes he dælde
he wes cniht swiþe ræh to ræden ane kinge
vnder þen kinge he heolde þis lond and þas leoden him hereden
Þe king hehden his broþer sune beiene tosomne
þe aldre hæhte Androgeus þe ȝungere Tennantius
þeos weoren beien him biforen eorles swiþe balde
Nennius wes þeos kinges broþer næfde he nenne oþer
He ferde ut of Cantuarieburie mid balden his ferden
Androgeus of Lundene mid Kentisce leoden
Tennantius of Cornwale his kempen weore kene
Æridius þe king his Scottes he lædde
and Britael com to neode Norþ Walene king
 and Guærtaæt þe mode mid þon Suþ Walscen
Com of Galwæie Æssel þe gode
com of Muriene moni spere kene 
of alle þissen þeoden come to þære neode
to Cassibellaune kinge of þissen londe
 and þene king lærde al þas leodcnihtes
þat he his freoscipe mid fehte biwunne
 and he heom an hond salde swa þat he wolde
þat fehten he wolde wiþ Cezar þe axede longauel her
Forþward heo wenden and his folke fusde
to þere sæ heo wenden and Cezar þer funden
Of heore cume wes war Iulius Cezar
he cleopede on his cnihtes Ȝarewieþ eow to fihte
for nu is mid ferde icumen Cassibellaunus
Heo liþede togadere mid heore speren longe
mid axen mid sweorden mid scærpe speres orde
hardliche heo heowen hælmes þer gollen
feonliche heo feohten hafdes þer feollen
And Cesar þe keisere wes vnimete kene
his longe sweord he adroh and moni mon þermide asloþ
he swonc i þon fehte þat al he lauede asweote
He sloh þa him neh weoren alle buten iferen
he dude þer muchelne wunder he sloh þer an hundred
of ahtere monnen þe feond mid his mæche
Þat iseh Androgeus and cleopede his fader Nennius
and beiene þa eorles buȝen heom togaderes
mid swiþe muchele folke togæderen stoden faste
Iseȝen heo Iulius Cesar fæhten al swa a wilde bar
and heo him to fusden mid ladliche fehte
 and monie of heore feonden heo fælden to þon grunde
Þa iseh Nennius wær fæht Cesar Iulius
and he him to rasde mid ræhæm his sweorde
vppen þene helm he hine smat þat þet sweord in bat
Selkuþ hit þuþte moni cnihte
þat he durste cumen him næh for þa þe keisere wes swa hæh
Iulius Cesar ne queþ nan word ah he bræid ut his sweord
and Nennium he smat þa uppen þene helm swa
þat þe helm tohælde and þat hæfde bledde
ah he ne blakede no for he wes cniht wel idon
 and Iulius nefde na bræþ ah his brond he up ahæf
and Nennius hæf vp his sceld scilde hine sulue
Iulius adun smat and þat sweord a þene scelde bat
Iulius hit wraste and þat sweord stikede feste 
Iulius þat sweord heold and Nennius þene sceld
 and þus heo hit longe bituȝen ne mihte he þat sweord ut draȝen
Þat isæh Androgeus hu uerden Cesar and Nennius
 and heo hem to fusde monie to fulste
Þa isæh Cesar tiþend þat him wes sær
he forlette þene brand þa nefde he noht on his hond
æ he þa feondliche turnde to flæme
Nennius wende i þane felde and he turnde his sceld
droh ut þene brande þa wes þe eorl swiþe bald
Monie Romanisce men mid þon sweorde he leide adun
he wes moniennes monnes bone and monianne he dude scome
Ah þat he mid þan sweorde smat þerriht hit iwat
al þat he þermid atran weore hit flæs weore hit ban
þurh þeos sweordes wunde heo fullen to þon grunde
Alle dæi wes þat fihte a þet com þe þestere niht
Iulius þe kaisere mid alle þan Romanisce here
dalden from þan fihte al bi þustere nihte
to hærberȝe heo wenden uppen þare sæstronde
heo bilefden biæften twenti hundred cnihten
þeo leien under scelden islæȝen ȝeond þon felden
Cesar iwende to his bedde his men weoren ofdredde
inne biwakeden in þere nihte þritti hundred cnihten
mid helmen and mid burnen and mid stelene sweorden
Iulius Cesar he wes ȝep and swuþe iwær
he isæh his muchele lure and of mære he hæfde kare
he aras to þan midnihte and bannede his cnihtes
and seide heom þat heo wolden faren and fleon of þissen londe
faren into Flandre and beo þer wuniende
a þat he iseȝen his time þat he mihten æft cumen liþen
Heo ferden forhrihte to scipe al bi nihte
heo hæfden swiþe fair weder and wenden into Flandre
Amarȝen þa hit dæi wes þe king mid his duȝeþe
ȝarekede his ferde and wende to þan fihte
Þeo was Romanisce folc iuaren from here londe
þat ne funden heo nauer enne of Cesares monnen
Þa weoren Bruttes bliþe an heore mode
muchel wes þa blisse þat heo makeden mid iwisse
and sone þeræfter særi heo wurþen
 and Cassibellaune þe king iwarþ særi þurh alle þing
for Nennius his broþer ne mihte finden bote 
of his hæfuedwunde þe Iulius smat mid honde
ne þurh nenne læchecræfte ne mihte he lif habben
Nes þer nan oþer ræd buten Nennius iwarþ dæd
 and Nennius was ilæid at þon norþ ȝæte i Lundene
Þe king næm enne marmestan and lette hine mid golde bigon
mid golde and mid ȝimme his broþer he leide þerinne
mid richedome þa Bruttes Nennium biburden
Nu þu miht iheren sulkeþ word þe king nom þat ilke sweorde
þat Nennius his broþer biwan of Iulius Cesare
and læide hit bi his broþer þat hit his bone weore
Wæs þe stelene brond swiþe brad and swiþe long
þeron weoren igrauen feole cunne bocstauen
æ þere hilte wes igrauen
þat þa sweord wes icleoped inne Rome Crocia Mors
swa þat sweord hæhte for hit hauede muchele mahte
Þermide þe keisere þrætede ælches londes here
for nas næuere þe ilke bern þe auere iboren weoren
þat of þen ilke sweorde enne swipe hefde
þat he of his likame lette ænne drope blod
þat he nes sone dæd neore he noht swa dohti
Iulius mid his ferde læi inne Flandre
Þat word com to France heou he iuaren hæfde
 and hu he wæs mid his færde iflæmde of þissen earde
Þa weoren þa Frensce men þerfore swiþe uæine
for toward Iulius heo hæfden grome and for þi weoren fæin of his scome
Ælc Frenscmon þe wes aht hæfþ hine selfne biþoht
and seide to his iuere Ne wurþe he nauere isæle
þe nu and aueremare buȝe to Cesare
þe Bruttes habbeþ ouercumen and of heore londe idriuen
Nulle we him nauere hæren ne hælde for ure hærre
ac wih him we scullen ure freoscipe mid fehte bitellen
for ne sunde we na bliþere þenne beoþ þa Bruttes
þe hine habbeoþ ut idriuen and his cnihtes islæȝen
Þis ihærden segge Iulius þat þa Frenscen speken þus
 and þat heo speken of þrætte and of prute ibeote
He wende into France mid muchelen his ferde
alse heo noht ne cuþe þat heo him vuel walden
 and sende ȝeond al France æfter his freo monnen 
þat heo comen him to alswa heo sculden to heore herre don
Alle heo comen him to and alle hine custen
 and alle hine grætten and heore grame dærnden
Iulius wes swiþe wis and war on his þonke
he lette bringen muchel gold and gærsume store
ærst he ȝæf þæn hæhste þe eoden him næxte
ȝefuen swiþe riche of ræden his golde
auerelcne cnihte he ȝef ȝeoue brihte
mid þere ȝeue he heom ouercom þat wes þa þat bezste iwan
 and freoliche him bihæhte habben þat heo scolden
Þa weoren heo his freond þe ær weoren his fulle fon
Whær is þe ilke mon þat me ne mæi mid mede ouergan
þurh þa luue of þan feo feondscipe aleggen
makien feolle ifreond þæh heo weoren iuæiede
Nu spac Iulius Cesar he wes wis and swiþe iwar
Ihereþ mine Frensce men mine freo cnihtes
Ich wulle sende to Rome to mine monnen wel idone
þat heo me sende forþrihtes fif hundred cnihtes
for ȝet ich wulle wenden into Brutlonde
 and ȝe me scullen uæren mid mid muchelere strengþe
 and þat lond ich wulle biwinnen and þa bet eow scel iwurþen
for eowre muchele wurþscipe weole ȝe scullen habben,
Alle eowre flemede men mid mire freondscipen cumen aȝæn
for ȝifuen ich wulle witen and þe wræcchen makien richen
freo ȝe scullen iwurþen and mine freondscipe habben
Þa answarede þat hired mid hæhȝere stefne
Mid þe we wulleþ libben and mid þe we wulleþ liggen
and wurþscipe þe biwinnen mid strengþe and mid ginnen
 and mid þe we wulleþ buȝen mid baldere strengþe
ouer sæ to Brutlonde to Cassibellaune þa kinge
 and wiþ him we scullen fihten and wærken þine cnihtes
 and iwinnen al þat lond and setten hit in þire hond
 and þer moste mare to ær þis weoren al idon
for al heo weoren særi ær hit soþ weore
Þa Cesar hæfde þis idon and his gærsume idæled
 and æc hæfde freondscipe mid his feo biwunnen
þa ferde he into Buluine þer him bezst þuþte
He hehte wurchen ane tur wunderliche fæier
þe tur wes muchel and hæh and þere sæ heo stod wel neh 
Þe kæisere hire ȝæf nome and Oþeres heo cleopede
in þare tur stronge kæisere wunede longe
þreottene monþes wunede Iulius in Oþeres
and þider he lette al cumen gold and his gærsume
Næs næuere na tur þe swa weore itimbred
mid crafte swa gode swa þa tur of Oþeres
Þer mihten sitten in þon grunde cnihtes sixti hundred
 and þa turres cop mihte wreon a cniht mid his capen
Þa þe tur wes al ȝaru þa hæfde Cesar þe lasse kare
into France he wende and sette his wike
ȝeond al he sette reuwen stronge and hæȝen
þe fengen þa londgauel and mid þan feo sculden faren
æueralcne ȝere to Oþres þeon ture
Þa lette he wurchen wunderliche muchele
six hundred scipen and sette heo to hauene
Þa þat wærc wes idon and al þat þer bihouede to
þa seide þe keisere þat to Brutlonde he wolde faren
forþ bi his quike liue nalde he heom swa bilæuen
Six hundred scipe gode he fusde i sæflode
 and nuste na mon þat itel of þan scipen þat seileden after
 and forþriht heo wenden into þere Temese
Nu þohte Iulius Cezar ah þer he wes to vnwar
he þohte swa forþ teon æfter þere Temese
rouwen swa longe þat he come to Londen
 and þær heo wolden up faren and fehten wiþ Bruttes
 and iwinnen al þis lond to his aȝere hond
Ah nas hit noht swa iloten for lettinge com on ueste
for sæliþende men seiden þon Brutten
þat þe kaisere Iulius wolde i Temese cume þus
faren forþ to Lunden and fehten wiþ þan leoden
 and þa Bruttes iwurþen war and wisdom biþoþten
 and nomen longen ræftres stronge and rihte
mid stronge irene heo weoren iscod and setten heom i Temese flod
Þer weoren fifti hundred faste i þon grunde
 and þa herre endes ihodede mid irene bendes
toȝænes heom heolden inne þere hauene
 and swa heo þer stoden biwriȝen mid þon flode
Þa com Iulius Cesar and hæræf næs nawiht war 
Þæt weder heom strongliche drof stermen þer sungen
weder heom stod on wille heo wenden wel to speden
heo urnen touward hauene scipen gunnen helden
bosmes þer rendden water in wende
seiles þer helfden aþeles adrunken
 and þa Romleoden rameden ȝeond uþen
Þa scipen wenden to wundre oþer half hundred
Þerafter com Iulius Cesar on his hurte him wæs sær
heo scuuen ut heore lof and læiden to þon londe
 and þeo þeræfter comen weoren war sone
and heom sælliche ilomp þæt mesten dæl com a lond
Heo sloȝen heoren teldes wide ȝeond þa feldes
 and sære menden heoren wines þe adrunken weoren
Þa wæs þe king war Cassibellaunes
þat Iulius þe kæisere wes a Lundene mid his hære
Þa ȝeddede þe king Cassibellaune
Welle broþer Nennius þat ich þe quic nabbe
 and þat sweord Crocea Mors þe þu biwunne a compe
 and þe bi mire side isund seȝe riden
an oþer half Androchius and his broþer Tennancius
sikerlichen we sculden uaren and fehten wiþ þon kæisere
 and forþ we sculen liþen and fellen his leoden
Cassibellaune Bruttene king wes god cniht þurh alle þing
He somnede vnimete here and ferde touward þon kæisere
 and pus spec wiþ his folke and luueliche spilede
Biþencheþ eow ohte cnihtes to bitellen eoweore rihtes
biþencheþ a Belin þone king and Brennes his broþer
hu heo biȝeten Rome mid riche here ferde
 and biwunnen al þa richen þe læien into Rome
 and swa heo hit walden wel feole wintre
 and swa heo þer boȝeden þe wile þe heo luueden
 and ich hit sugge eow cnihtes Rome is eowre irihte
nu hit halt Iulius Cesar þe is tweien icumen her
 and halt þer eower icunde and her eow wule driuen of londe
 and hateþ eow swa swiþe þat awei he wule eow driue
Ȝif ȝe leoseþ þis lond oueral ȝe wurþeþ laþe
Ah heo ȝe swiþe bisie for we beoþ ohte Bruttes
Cesar is in ure londe and liþ her bi sæstronde
Ohliche liþe we him to swa him alre laþest beo
 and awalde we þe keisere and al his Romanisce here 
 and aredden ure lond of þan Romleodene
Þa andswereden þa ferde Varen we biliue
for Iulius is fæie mid al his Romfolke
Forþ heo ifusden and ferden biliue
þat heo þidir comen þer læi þat folk of Rome
 and heo heom to ræsden mid ræhere strengþe
Laþliche heo feohten and Romware feollen
þer Cesar folk folden isohten
noht bi tene no bi twenti ah bi twenti þusende
Swa heo fehten al dæi monie þer weoren fæie
þet hit com to þere nihte ne mihte Cesar namare fihte
Cesar wes swa swiþe wa and biþohte hine þa
þat he wolde a þere nihte fleon awæi mid his cnihten
Iulius Cezar of his lure wes þer war
he lette blawen his bemen and bannen his ferden
 and lette leode cleopien and oueral cuþen
þat heo comen to heore innes and ȝarekeden heore ginnes
 and fæȝeden heoren wepnen amarwen heo fusden to fehte
Þis ihærden þa bisie þe weoren þer bihælues
forþriht heo comen to Cassibellaune
 and seiden him þat Cesar wulde þe ȝet wunnien þar
 and amarwe he weolde fehten mid alle his cnihten
 and fallen þa Bruttes oþer himsulf beo fæie
for þus heo letten cleopien and cuþen ȝeond his ferde
Ah wa la wa and wala wa þat Cassibellaune nær iwar
þa he wende swiþe wel don ah ne dude he hit no
He droh in ane hælue and toc þan herberwe
 and alle þa nihte greiþeden his cnihtes
heore scæftes and heore sceldes þa scælkes weoren bischærred
For Iulius Cesar of his hærme wæs wær
abuten midnihte he warnede alle his cnihtes
 and to scipen ferden and fusden an veste
Heo hafden swiþe god weder and wenden mid vþen
heo ledden in heore scipen æiþer deade men and quiken
moni sorhfulne sæg sare iwunded
monienne deadne cniht of Cesares duhȝeþe
Swa heo wenden mid þon flode to þon tur of Oþres
þer wes Iulius Cezar an heorte he hafde sorȝe and sar
Amarȝen þa hit wes dæiliht hit wes cuþ forþriht
 and æc iseid þon kinge Cassibellaune 
hu Iulius þe kæisere wes from þissen londe ifaren
 and al hu he fusde and flæh mid þon vþen
þat næs þer bilæued nan of Romleoden
Þa wes þon kinge wa and þus ȝeddede þa
Wale wale vnræd mani cniht þu makest dæd
Welle þat ich nas ær war þat Iulius wolde wenden
Ful soh seide þe seg þe þeos saȝe talde
Ȝif þu ileuest ælcne mon selde þu sælt wel don
Swa ic wende wel þat þe sæȝe soþ weoren
þe me wes toniht itald bi an eorl swicful and bald
þat Cesar wolde nu todæi Brutlond biwinnen
oþer her mid sweorde liggen toswungen
and al his iuere þe mid him comen here
Nu wes þis ilke iseid me to biswiken
Wæila wæi wæila wæi þat he is þus ifaren awæi
 and naþeles ich em bliþe for auere to ure liue
we maȝen ouersitten þis lond ær he us æft isechen
for æueremore he mai imunnen þat he him her imunten
for her liggeþ toȝere ten þusend of his iferen
wiþuten his drihtliche scipen þe i sæ idrunken
Ah wel ich þonkie mine gode for wurþscipe ich habbe ibiden
 and twien iflemed þene keisere mid alle his Romanisce leode
 and nu ich wulle to Lundene þa burh ich luuie swuþe
 and þer ich wulle halinesse to mine goden halden
 and swiþe heom wurþen for heore weldæde
Þe king lette blawen and bonnien his ferden
 and hehten heom alle faren heom and hiredmen beon bliþe
 and fæien heore steden and græiþen heore iweden
 and þas dæies æn þreom wiken wenden to Lundene
mid wif and mid bernen blisse to makien
eorles and þeines cnihtes and sweines
 and al þat freoliche folc of Brutlondes ærde
þene dæie heo vndernomen and to Lundene heo comen
mid swulche richedome al swa hit weoren i Rome
Þe king bigon seruise on ælches cunnes wise
æfter þan heþene laȝen þe stoden o þen ilkæ daȝen
Þer stoden in þere temple ten þusend monnen
þet wes þe bezste cure of al Brutlonde
biforen heore mahun þe heom þuhte mære 
Apolin wes ihaten heo heolden hine for hæhe godd
Ælc beorn hæfde on heonde ane þechene bærninde
wæs ælc bald beorn iboned mid golde
þe king hafde his kinehelm hæhliche on hæfde
Wæs atforen þan wæfde imaked an wunlic fur
þe king warp riches þerin and alle his hæhste men mid him
seoþþen heo þer offreden aþþeles madmes
 and þonkede Appollin his gode þe þa muchele wurþscipe uþen him
Þa þe seruuinge wes idon þat hit to þe mete com
þerof ich wulle þe tellen selcuþe spelles
Weoren in þeos kinges cuchene twa hundred cokes
 and ne mæi na man tellen for alle þa bermannen
Islaȝene weoren to þon mele twælf þusend ruþeren sele
 and þritti hundred hærtes and al swa feole hinden
of þan fohȝelcunne ne mai hit na mon kennen
 and al þat wæl and al þat gold þe wes ȝeond al þeos kinges lond
hit wes al isomned at þere sereuunge
Nes hit nauer mid soþ itald seoþþen þeos weoruld wes astald
þat weore on ane stude swulc ȝifueþe istured
ne of alche þinge swulc richedom iȝiuen and underfon
Muri wes þe dæi and liht and þa sonne wes swiþe briht
weoren þa bernes iscængte mid beore
 and þa drihliche gumen weoren windrunken
Heo ferden ȝeond þa feldes mid scæftes and mid sceldes
Summe heo gunnen ærnen and somme heo gunnen eornen
 and summe heo gunnen pleien pliht com on ueste
Summen pleoden on tæuelbrede and summen ærnden heore stede
Þa weoren þer tweiene prute heo weoren beien
Herigal hehte þe an Æueling þe oþer
Herigal wes þes kinges mæi þet wes hærm a þen ilke dæi
ahte cniht wes Auelin Androgeus wes is hem
Þeos tweien cnihtes bigunnen mid sceldes to scurmen
ærst heo pleoweden and seoþþe pliht makeden
þer Herigal smat Æuelin swiþe vuele a þane chin
Heo bigunnen to chiden cnihtes come riden
Euelin wes swiþe wraþ and mid þan stæue todraf
and smat Herigal a þon ribben þat þe stæf tobræc amidden
Þa queþ þe cniht Herigal Euelin þat is swiþe sar
þu me smite bi þon rugge ah sare þu hit slat abuggen 
for nu þi stæf is tobroken balu þe scal beon ȝifueþe
Euielin wes swiþe sari þat him wes swa ilumpen
þe oþer wolde him habben dæd hit þuhte him swiþe hærd ræd
 and he hine biþohte wæt he don mihte
nefde he noht on his hond bute enne luttelne sceld
Isæh he enne hendlicne mon þe þer stod bihaluen
þe wes þudere icumen for to iseon þare cnihte gomen
þe ȝunge mon heold on his hond enne stelene brond
Euielin þene brond igrap mid grimliche lechen
 and braid hine of þere scæþe þa wes his hurte æþe
He ræsde to Herigale and smat hine swiþe sare
þat his neb and his neose niþer ba heolden
æft he him to sweinde and þa hond him ofswipte
dunt he him ȝef þane þridde and forsmat hine amidde
Swa endede þæ pleowe þat Herigal læi ofsloȝen
and Euelin þonene wende his sweord he bar on honde
ne funde he nonne swa kene mon þat hond him durste leggen on
al þat folc he bibæh to Androchies inne he flæh
Þet iherde þe king icud hit wes him sone
hu hit al wes ifaren and hu Herigal læi ofslæwen
Þe king nom þreo aldere men and sende to Androgeum
and hehte hine bringen his mæi to þon kinge
to þolie þes kinges dom for þan slæhte þe he hafde idon
and ȝif he swa nolde he hine flæme wolde
Þa answerede Androgeus and toward þan kinge he spæc þus
Nulle ich hine bringen for nauer nane þinge
þat me Euelin fordo noþer slæ ne na aho
Ah ich habbe freo lond þat freoliche stont a mire honde
 and ich habbe min hired heh vnder þon kinge
Ȝif her is æni cniht þe of Eueline axeþ riht
come to mine herede and þer he hit scal habben
 and ich sugge eow to soþe nis þer ræd nan oþer
Þis wes sone icuþ to Cassibellaune
Þe king iwarþ him swiþe wraþ swulc he weore of witte
 and þeos ilkæ word him seide Cassibellaune
Ut of min æhsenen Androgeus and his iueren
 and ȝif ich hine mai eower ifon in þon stude he beþ fordon
Androgeus forþrihtes nom alle his cnihtes
 and anan gon liþen ut of Lundenne
 and iwenden into Kent to his ane castle 
and hine strongede wel mid mete and mid wepnen
 and þe king nom Lundene and þat lond to his aȝere hond
 and seoþþen fusde into Kent mid muchelere ferde
mid here and mid fure þat lond forferde swiþe
Androgeus nom tweie cnihtes and sende to þon kinge
 and þus þe cnihtes him spæken wiþ King Androgeus ȝeornneþ þi griþ
Androgeus is þin aȝene mon al þine wille he wule don
wiþ þon þe þu him ȝeue griþ and late hine sæhtne þe wiþ
and leten bileuen þine brune his lond þe þu forbærnest
Iþench þat he wes Ludes sune of þine broþer he is icumen
 and his fader ahte al þat lond þat nu stondeþ a þire hond
And al hit þuncþ him wel idon ȝif þu his sæhtnesse wult vnderfon
bute nele he þe nauere Euelin mid ærhþe bitæchen
þat þu him sculle oþer don oþer slæn oþer ahon
Þa þe king iherde þis þa wes he wræþ ful iwis
and þus seide þe king Cassebellaune
Whar beo ȝe mine kemppen
mine drihtliche men Wrekeþ me of Androgeum
His lond ich wulle forbærnen and his bone iwurþen
Þis iherden suggen Androgeus and he answerede þus
Whilen hit wes iseid inne soþ spelle
þat moni mon deþ muchel vuel al his vnþankes
Swa ich moht nu neode for muchere neode
Þe mon þe þoleþ þat me hine wule fordon þat ich telle vnwisdom
þe while he mæi þurh æni cræft i compe hine werien
Ælc cniht ah an uuel to don ær he wurse vnderfon
and swa ich æuere bere sceld and spere sende ich wulle to þon kæisere
 and græten Iulius Cesare and mænen to him mi sar
 and bedden þat he me ræde for nu ich habbe neode
Androgeus þe riche cnihte makede a writ wel idiht
 and nom erendrake godne and sende him to Oþres
to Iulius þon kæisere mid al his Romanisce here
 and þus wes þat writ idiht and þus hit spæc forþriht
Hail beo þu mid þine here Iulius þe keisere
Þu hattes Iulius Cezar to þe ich mæne mi sær
Androgeus þin aȝene mon þis nis nan swikedom
for þat weord þat ich þe sende bi mine liue ich hit halde
 and þu hit nult ileuen beoten hit læssingge beo
ich hit wulle trousien þurh minne tirfulne godd
þurh mine lauerd Appollin þe leof me is on heorte 
For ofte hit is ilumpen inne feole leoden
þet æfter muchele hatinge hehȝe men heom luuede
 and æfter muchel weorldscome wurþscipe wurhten
Twien þu hafuest ibeon ouercummen and þine men we habbeþ islæn and inome
 and idriuen þe of Brutlonde mid feht swiþe stronge
mid us þu hæfuest bileued moni þeosend kempen
Þat nes noht þurh ure kinge Cassibellaune
ah hit wes þurh me seolfne and þurh sele mine folke
for ich lædde mid me Lundene uerde
 and eke al þa Kentwærre þe kempen weoren gode
 and þerwiþute monienne Brut þe bald wes to fehten
Seoþþen we þe hafden ouercomen and þi folke islaȝen an iinomen
Nu is Cassibellaune and his men swa modi iwurþen
þet mid fehte heo wulleþ me sende ut of Brutlonde
fleme me from leoden feor from londe
Mi lond heo habbeoþ me al iwest and Lundene me biræued
 and me sulfne heo þencheþ quellen and alle mine kempen
Ȝif þu þis writ iheren wult hit wule þe suggen minne gult
Þa þu weoren from us iliþe at þa latere cherre
þa wes þa king swa bliþe swa he nas nauer ære on his liue
 and on oþer halue he hæfde kare for he nusten þat þu woldest faren
Noþeles he seide atforen al his duȝeþe
Nu is Iulius awei ifloȝen tweien he is aflemed
tweien he com to Bruttene þer him wes balu ȝeueþe
ne þurfe we nu nauermare iseon hine cumen here
for her beoþ his bezste cnihtes islæȝen in ure fehte
 and nu we sulleþ for heore beone bliþe iwurþen
Scullen alle mine Bruttes mid baldere prute
liþen to Lundene and þer lof makien
vre lauerde Appollin and alle ure goden mid him
for þere muchele wurþescipe þe ich nu walde
Þus liþden to Lundene alle Brutleoden
cnihtes and þringes mid wifue and mid children
 and mid alle þe wurþscipe þe heo weoren wældinde ouer
Þa we þus comen to Lundene we gunnen lof makien
ure lauerd Apollin and alle ure goden mid him
Seoþþen þeos weorld wes astalled nes hit nowher itald
þat weore nowhar swa muchel mete iuorþþed to ane mele
ne swa muchel god dringe folke ideled
Muchel wes þa gladscipe þa gunnen heo to pleien
summe mid foten ueire igerede
summe an heorse hehliche iscrudde
Þa weoren þar tweien scalkes and ifengen here sceldes
scriþen under bordes and skirmden mid mæine
þe oþer wes mire suster sune Euelin hehte þe gume
þe oþer Herigal heh he wes on hirede
of þes kinges kunne icomen he wes his hæluesuster sune
he wes þon kinge arle deorest of alle his drihtfolke
Herigal smat Euelin swiþe vfele i þene chin
 and Euelin iwarþ him wraþ and werede hine sulue
a þere side he smat Herigal þat þe dunt him þuhte sar
Herigal þa seide and mid muþe hit sweor
þat Euelin i þon dæi dæd sculde þolien
Euelin wes swiþe ofdred for me him dead bihæhte
 and smat on Herigales sceld þat his stæf atwaie wond
Ofte wes Euelin wa and næuere wurs þene þa
scilde him mid his scelde nefde he elles noht an honde
 and Herigal him soþte on mid hehære strengþe 
Euelin iseh enne gume ȝungen him bihalfues
 and bar an his riht hond ænne stelene brond
Euelin him ræsde to and hine ræhliche græp
an hiȝinge he þat sweord adroh and Herigal ofsloh
Þat iherde þe king Cassibellaune
þat Herigal wes ofslaȝen and Euelin awæi ifloȝen
to me he sende his seonde wiþuten gretinge
hehte me bringe to him mine mæi Euelin
swiþe bringe hine him to to þolien his hirdes dom
for an of þon he weolden him don oþer slan oþer anhon
 and ȝif ich þat nalde ich scolde fleon of his onwalde
 and ȝif he mihte me seoluen ifon he me walden slæn oþer anhon
Ich ȝirnde þes kinges griþ and walde sæhtnen him wiþ
 and riht him don i mine hirde for ich wes his eorl þe hehste
ah nolde ich him neuere Euelin to ærmþen him bitache
 and he me aflemde sone from hirede
Lundene he hæfueþ me binome and mine cnihtes ofslaȝen
Naþeles ich habbe an hirede twa and fifti hundred
 and ȝet ich habbe an honde twenti castles stronge
 and miseolf ich wunie inne Kent mid kene mine beornnen
 and þe king me fehteþ wiþ and nule me ȝeuen na griþ
Nu þu hauest iherd mi sær lauerd Iulius Cesar
al mid soþe worden alse þis writ þe telleþ
A þisse write ich habbe idon þat ich wulle bicumen þin mon
 and halden þe for herre for hehne mine lauerd
wiþ þan þe þu me helpe at heȝere neode
 and aredde me of þon kinge Cassibellaune
Þas weord ich wulle þe treosien þurh mine tirfulne god
þat ich hit wulle soþien ase ich hit bi write suggen
 and cum hiȝendliche to Britteine þat lond ich þe biteche
þurh me þu hit bilæfdes and þurh me þu hit scalt habben
Þis writ iherde Iulius þe him hafde isend Androgeus
þa enswerede Iulius þe keisere
Nulle ich him ileuen þurh alle leodene aþ
bute he me sende anan his feire sune Cenan
 and þritti oþere ȝisles to Oþres me sende
þeo beon alle icornne and hæȝe ibornne
Ȝif he þis wule don his bod ic wulle afon
 and cumen him to helpe mid hæȝere strengþe
Þas word sende Iulius mid write to Androgeus
Androgeus forþriht anan sende his sune Cenan
 and þritti ȝisles oþere he sende him to Oþeres 
And Iulius þe sele to þere sa iwende
mid alle his folke fusde touward Burttene
anan swa hit daȝede he com up at Douere
Þat word him herde Androgeus and sone þider wende
 and þas wordes seide Androgeus Wulcume ært þu Iulius
swiþe leof þu ært me þis lond ich þe bitæche
Heo speken tosomne and spileden mid sehte
Þeo while hefede þe king Cassibellaune
ȝeond al his kinelond isomned ferde stronge
to Lundene he wolde liþen and enne castel biliggen
þe Androgeus þe stronge hafde þa ȝet an honde
Þa þe ferde wes al igadered þa com an gume ærnen
 and anan he þus cleopede to Cassibellaune
Hal seo þu ure king Ich þe bringe tiþende
of þon Romleoden þe laþe þe beoþ an heorten
Alle heo beoþ i Doure þine dædliche iuan
 and þer is Androgeus to speken wiþ Iulius
Þeos word beoþ soþe þe ich her sugge
and þench mid wulche deden þu miht werien þine leoden
Þa wes særi þe king Cassibellaune
 and lette biliue blawen his beme
cuþen his kempen þa tiþende neowcumene
þat Iulius þe kæisere mid his Romanisce here
wes þerriht icumen and þa hauene at Doure hafde inomen
Þa sæide þe king Cassibellaune
Lundene we mote bilæuen and to Doure liþen
Bonnieþ ure ferde and fare we biliue
Forþ ferde þe king mid vnimete folke
riht towarde Doure to his muchelen vnbihoue
Þat iherde Iulius Cesar he wes wis and swiþe iwar
þat þuderward com on ueste Cassibellaune
Þa wes Iulius bliþe for þe tiþende leofue
he ferde ut of Doure bi þe sæoure
into ane muchele slæde and slahliche his folc hudde
And Androgeus wende into ane oþere ende
to ane wilderne into ane wude muchele
 and þus spec Androgeus and wiþ his folke spilede þus
Ne wurþe nan cniht swa wod ne kempe swa wilde
þat he æuere speke worde furþer þene his speres ord 
ne from his ifere ride for tosomnen we scullen gliden
faste togadere and ure ifan fællen
 and ȝif here is æi heredring þe maȝen nimen þene king
nime hine mid isunde and ne ȝefue him nane wunde
for he is mi lauerd and mi cun nulle ich hine quellen
ah we scullen al his folk feollen to grunde
 and ȝemen þes fehtes and nawiht þes fenges
fællen þa ræȝe and læten þa ræf liggen
 and al swa lerde Iulius leoue his cnihtes
Iulius hæfde to iueren þritti hundred riderne
cnihtes icorene kenewurþ kempen
 and Androgeus hæfde to iueren ten þusend rideren
Alswa heo þus leien stille and bidiemden heore wille
þer com þe king riden Cassibellaune
mid vnimete ferde mid vnimete folke
 and com heom bitweonen þer heo þoleden teonen
Iulius him wes biforen Androgeus bihinden
ah Androgeus ær awoc and ut of wude wende
 and al þat folc þe he lædde lude hit grædde
bleowen here bemen belden heore beornes
 and heom toward wenden on euereelchen ende
Þis iherde þe king Cassibelaune
iherde he þene muchelne dræm and þene dune muchelne
he seide forþrihtes Wepneþ eow cnihtes
Þes kinges heorte wes ful sær he wende þat hit weore Cesar
ah Cesær mid his ginne biuoren wes ful stille
and ihærde þane dræm wel of Androgeus folke
 and Iulius wes al rædi alse he to wolde ræsen
 and Cassibellaune þe king nuste herof naþing
ah he wepnede his cnihtes and ȝarewede heom to fehten
Ær heo weoren hælf ȝaru þer com Androgeus faren
and he fusde heom to mid feondliche strengþe
Þe cnihtes þe weoren igarede bigunnen to fæhten
 and Androgeus heom to mid aþelere strengþe
æt þon frumræsen he feolde of þon folke
feowerti hundred þat folke wes þæ læsse
Þa wolde þat folke fleon þer com Iulius teon
forn aȝæien heore hæued and heom to heolde 
of þon folke he sloh muchel and unifoh
Þa fleh Bruttene king Cassibellaune
wel ofte him wes wa neuer wurse þene þa
Iulius him wes biforen Androgeus him bæften
 and on ælche side siȝen to his hærme
Þe king hine biþohte Cassibellaune
isæh him bihælues ænne holt hæhne
bi ænnes wudes ende þider he gon wenden
and muchel of his folke floȝen mid þon kinge
 and astiȝen uppe þen hul mid muchele modsorȝe
naþeles þer up þurngen fiftene þusunde
Wes þe munt swiþe hæh hasles þer greowen
swiþe wes þe hul biclused mid cludes of stane
Heo bigunnen þene wude feollen and heo biforen leggen
mid stocken and mid stanen and mid stelene orden
heo gunnen heom to werien wiþ heore wiþeriwinnen
Þene hul makede þe king to strongge enne castle
an are nihte firste þat worc wes iforþed
for þer worhten sweines þer worþten þeines
 and þe king mid his honden Cassibellaune
wurhte ful swiþe to burȝen his liue
Þa þet work wes up iset heom wes alles þa bet
 and Iulius Cesar bilai heom abute þer
A þen hulle wes þe king Cassibellaune
þer he þolede muchelne burst nes þer neouþer win ne must
þreo daȝes and þreo niht ne æt þer næuer na cniht
Heo weoren swiþe uuele ilæd for þe king heom hauede al forrad
þe nold sæhtnesse afon at his mæie Androgeum
þerfore he læi on hulle hunger him derfde
Nearew wes þe king ilæd nuste he nenne ræd
for nuste he a nare halue helpen þat him mahte
isæh alle dæi biforen his fulle iuan alle icoren
Iulium þene kæisere mid alle þan Romanisce here
mid alle þan Romleoden to þes kinges unneoden
 and alle dæi þus cleopeden to Cassibellaune
Nu þu scalt adreden for þine ærdæden
hit þe likede wel þat þu us adun læidest
mid þine fehte and ure kun feldest
nu is icumen þin wadæi for dæþ þu scalt þolien 
mid hungere and mid hæte and mid sceome muchele
Þa wes wa þeon kinge Cassibellaune
 and nom him enne ræd for him wes muchel neod
He nom enne wisne cniht and sende hine forþriht
vt to þon folke þer weoren his iuan
 and grette Androgeum mid griþfulle worden
bed hine cuþen þat he his cun weoren
 and þa bet æt þære neode for he wes his broþer sune
For nabbe ich þe noht swa uuele idon þat sculde þerforen dæd onfon
for þat is muchel unriht ȝif æuere æi god cniht
wule his godliche cun bute gulte aquellen
Æt heȝere neode nu þu must me ræden
sæhtnien me wiþ þene kæisere and wiþ þon Romanisce here
 and seoþþen ich wullen þe speken wiþ and makien æfter þine wille griþ
togaderen wit scullen libben togadere wit scullen liggen
Þenc of mire neode and sæhtne me wiþ Romlede
for ȝif ihc her forwurþe auerst þe beoþ þa wurse
for ȝet heo wurþþeþ þe laþe þe me fulsteþ nu to dæþe
Þa answerede Androgeus and wiþ þene cnihte he spec þus
Heu ȝare wes hit iwurþen inne worlderiche
þat mines æmes muchele mod swa milde is iwurþen
 and swa swiþe ræh mon rihtes icnawen
Ȝet ne beoþ fif dæiȝes allunge iurede
þat he me nolde vt driuen binimen me æt þan liue
Þærto he duden al his mahte he biræuede mine æhte
 and al þat me wes leof him wes wunderliche læþ
Þe king dude vnwisdom þat he swulc mod him droh on
for he fæht wiþ Cesare þan Romanisce keisere
 and he hine twien ouercom and his folk sloh and nom
Ne dude hit noht þe king ane ah we alle clane
þer ich wes o þon fihte mid alle mine cnihten
hærde biþrungen i wel feole stunden
Ah ich miseolf neore and mine gode cnihtes
inumen weoren ure king and his Bruttes alle aqualde
ah we biforen þon kinge fuhte ful swiþe
 and driuen ut þene kæisere mid his Romanisce here
Ne dude hit noht þe king ane ah duden we alle clæne
Þa we hafden swa idon and muchele wurscipe anfon
þa iwarþ þe king on mode prut ah ne draf he hine noht ane ut
Seoþþen hit is nu herto ibroht nu is min eam wel biþoht 
mid mildliche worden he ȝerneþ mine milcne
for itemed is þe wode nu beoþ his word gode
Nu ich wulle wende mi mod aȝenes uuel ich wule don god
 and lutlien ich wulle his kare and sæhtnien him wiþ Cesare
ær cumen þe ende of þisse dæi helpen him ȝif ich mai
Androgeus wes swa god sone he dude hine barfot
 and alle his bezste cnihtes þe mid him weoren an fuhte
 and eoden to þon kaisere þer he wes i þon here
 and feollen to his foten and folden and isohten
mildeliche spæc þus þe treowe cniht Androgeus
Lauerd Iulius þin are nu and æuermære
Lett me speken þe wiþ ich ȝerne mildce and þi griþ
Þu hauest ouercumen minne æm inne þine fehte he nam flem
i þissen hulle he liþ and ȝeorneþ þe lifgriþ
for al þu hauest ouercumen Cassibellaune
 and muchel of his folke iualled to grunde
 and þene kinge and al his lond biȝiten to þire aȝere hond
Ȝif him nu lifues griþ and let hine speken þe wiþ
Ær he wes freo king
nu þu ært iwreken him on let hine bicumen þin aȝene mon 
and ælche ȝer þe sende þat gauel of Brutlonde
madmes and muchel feoh þe monscipe is þin aȝen
Þis iherde Cesar of þissere specche he wes wær
aweiward he halde and nolde hit iheren
makede hine swulc he weore wraþ for þon wurde þe he iherde
Androgeus wes wis and war þæne kæisere he eode neor
and græten worden þæne keisere igrætte
and þus queþ Androgeus Hærcne hiderward Iulius
Wiþ me ne beo þu noht wiþerward Ilæst ich habbe þe min foreward
 and al þat ich þe bihehte biforen vnkere cnihte
Ich bihæhte þe al Brutlond to setten a þire aȝere hond
 and swa ich habben nu idon and þu hit hauest al underfon
ah ne bihæhte ich þe nauere to slæn Cassibellaune minne æm
mid nane rihte ne mai ich hine fordon for ich eam his mæi and his mon
ne scal he næuere dæd þolien þe while þe ich mai him freoien
Ah ȝif mine eame lifues griþ and let hine sæhtnie þe wiþ
Þi mon he sæl bicumen to ȝisle biteche þe his sune
 and ælche ȝere senden þreo þusend punden
 and þat ich þe wullen swerien uppen mine sweorden
Ȝif þu þis nult iwurþen þe wurs þeo scælt iwurþen
ne scalt þu nauere mid þine here isund of Brutlonde faren
Þa wes adrad þe keisere mid his Romanisce here
leouere him weore þane al his lond þene al his seoluer þæne al his gold
þat he weore in Oþeres in his castel gode
for þa hefde swiþe muchel care Iulius þon kæisere
þe wende þat Androgeus swiken hine wolde
Iulius wes wis and war þat he wel cudde þær
Þus seide þa Iulius to þan eorle Androgeus
Androgeus mi leofue mon al þine wille ic wulle don
don ich wulle þin ræd for þu me hulpe þa me wes neod
for ne funde ich nauere treoure mon bitweonen þis and Latran
Þis wes sone icud to Cassibellaune
þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes neuere on his liue
Vt wende þe king Cassibellaune
adun of þan hulle bliþe on his mode
Ah þer Iulius dude wel and wurþscipen muchele
he hine lette ueden he hine lette scruden
he hine lette baþien ær he him biuoren come
Þa hit wes al igreiþed þa comen heo togæderes
griþ þer heo astalleden and wel hit wes ihalden
heo makeden heore foreward biforen heore duȝeþe
Cassibellaune bicom Iulius aȝene mon
 and ælche ȝere him sende þreo þusend punden
Æþes þer weoren isworene and neoren heo nauere forlorne
for treowe men heom astalden and alswa heo gunnen heom halden
Neoþeles Iulius wes þæ ærste mon þe dude þis lond inne þeowdom
seoþþen Noe and his sunen of þære arche weoren icumen
Þeo al þis wes iuaren þa todælde þa verden
 and þe keisere and his iueren al þat winter heo wuneden here
mid sæhte and mid sibbe mid selcuþe murȝeþe
Touward þan sumere heo ouer sæ wende
 and lædde mid him Androgeum þe wes his deoreste mon
 and Androgeus walde al þat he wolde
heonene into Rome hit stod on Androgeus dome
Ne com he naueremare here ne nan of his iuere 
ne leouede he neuer seoþþen buten seouen ȝere
Cassibellaune þe wes þisse londes king
þa his endedæie com in Eouerwicke heo dæide
Ær þe king were dæd dæide his quene
þe king wes al bærnles Bruttes weoren særi
Þis iherde Tennancius þe i Cornwale wes dux
þat his eam wes idæied and his aþelene ætfallen
and his broþer Androgeus iuaren uorþ mid Iulius
 and muchel of his cunne quehten mid himseolue
Tennancius hine biþoþte hu he faren mihte
 and hu he mihte gan on þat he hafde þisne kinedom
þe Lud king his fader walde wel longe
Tennancius nom his sonde and sende into Brutlonde
bad heom buȝen him to þa bet heom sculde iwurþen
hebben hine to kinge al buten compe
bitachen him al þat lond þe Lud his fader hafde an hond
 and he heom wolde luuien þa while þat he luuede
 and ȝif heo þis wolde habben he hit wolde
oþer he wolde mid fehte fallen heom to grunde
Bruttes ferden heom to Lundene to muchele hustinge
þat heom þuhte þe bezste ræd to don þat Tennantius heom bæd
Æfter him heo senden and heouen hine to kinge
þa weoren inne Bruttene blissen inouwe
Tou and twenti wintre þis lond he iwalde
seoþþen com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi
inne Lundene he liþ særi weoren his leoden
Þeos kinge hæfde enne sune Kinbelin ihaten
he wes iuaren mid his æme forþ into Rome
Augustus Cesar hine makede cniht þat wes swiþe muchel riht
for seoþþen Iulius wes dæd and duȝeþen bilæfden
ne bilæfde he næuer nænne of Androgeus cunne
þat heold feht and iwin swa dude Kinbelin
 and weorede Romeþeode wiþ vncuþe leode
Þis iherde Bruttes þe weoren swiþe bisie
þat Kinbelin þe kene wunede inne Rome
þe wes Tennantiusses sone and of Lud kinge icume
Tweien cnihtes heo nomen sone and senden to Rome
 and þeo cudden Kinbeline þat his fader wes of liue
 and beden hine stilleliche iuaren of þere riche
Nes hit noht longe þat he ne com hider sone 
and Bruttes hine onfengen and heouen hine to kinge
On Kinbelines dæie þe king wes inne Bruttene
com a þissen middelærde anes maidenes sune
iboren wes in Beþleem of bezste alre burden
He is ihaten Iesu Crist þurh þene Halie Gost
alre worulde wunne walden englenne
Fæder he is on heuenen froure moncunnes
Sune he is on eorþen of sele þon mæidene
 and þene Halie Gost haldeþ mid himseoluen
þene gast he wel daleþ to þan þe him beoþ leoue
alswa he dude Peture þe wes a wræche fiscære
þe makede hine an mancunne hehst of alre manne
Kinbelin Bruttene king wes god mon þurh alle þing
 and he luuede here twa and twenti ȝere
An his dæie her luuede a mon inne þisse leoden
feorliche þing fuleden him he wes ihaten Teilesin
heo heolten hine for witie þurh his witfulne cræfte
 and al heo hit ilæfden þat Teilesin heom seide
he seide heom seolkuþ inoh and al heo hit funden soþ
he seide heom ælche ȝere wæt heom to cumen weore
Þe king him sende æfter wise twalf cnihtes
bad hine comen him to þat he nan oþer seolden don
 and heo hine broþten sone biforen þen folkekinge
Anan swa þe king hine imette fæire he hine igrette
Swa me helpen min hefde and mi chin welcume ært þu Teilesin
 and leouere me is þine isunden þenne a þusend punden
Þa andswerede Teilesin and þus seide to Kinbelin
Swa ich mote gode iþeon al þu hit sælt wel biteon
Þa wes glad Kinbelin and þus seide to Teilesin
Her beoþ to þisse londe icumen seolcuþe leodronen
 and fromward þeon londe of Ierusalem iwurþen heo beoþ in Beþleem
Þer is iboren an luttel child inne þere leoden
Muchele is and stor þe eiȝe tacnen þer beoþ on sterren
an monen and on seonnen eie is on moncunnen
Þis is widen icuþ and þa writen me beoþ to icume
 and ic wolde iwiten æt þe þu ært mi wine deore
to whan þis tocne wule ten to wulche þinge temen 
for herfore is alches londes folc lædliche afered
Þa answerede Teilesin and þus seide to Kinbelin
Hit wes ȝare iqueþen þa quides beoþ nu soþe
þat scolden beon a child iboren of alle folke icoren
 and þat scolde beon ihaten Hælend and helpen his freondes
alesen his leofue wines of læþe heore bendes
of helle bringen Adam Noe and Abraham
Sadoc and Samiel and Symeon þene alde
Iosep an Beniamin and alle his broþeres mid him
Iohel and Eliseon Asor and Naason
Ysaac and his broþer and monienne oþer
moni hundred þusend þe iþud beoþ to hellen
 and for swulchere neode he is icumen to þere þeoden
Þeos word seide Teilesin and alle heo weoren soþe
Þa þan kinge wes icudde þas quides þa weoren soþe
þa weoren þa tiþinde cuþe ȝeond his kineriche
Bruttes herof ȝemden and noht hit ne forȝeten
Kinbelin wes god king and griþful þurh alle þing
 and þa Romleoden swiþe hine luueden
 and ȝif þe king wolde wiþ heom wiþerheolden
he miþte æthalden heore feoh þe Iulius her fætte
ah æueremære bi his liue he hit heom leofliche ȝeaf
Seoþþe him comen þæ tiþinde of Crist Godes childe
ne leouede þe king mære buten ten ȝere
Seoþþen þe king bilæfden his lif inne Eowuerwike he ȝet liþ
Her he bilæfden tweien sunen Wiþer and Aruiragune
Wiþer wes þa ældere Aruiragun þe ȝungere
ah þe king biqueþ Wiþer al his kineriche
 and he dihte and delde æfter his fader dæie
He wes swiþe god cniht and hæfde ihælden moni fiht
ah he wes swiþe sturne and stærc wiþ þeon folke
He nalde for nane dome mare heren to Rome
ne na gauel heom senden vt of þissen londe
ah whæreswa he fonde enne gume þe of Rome weore hider icumen
he lette smiten him of þat hæfde biræiuie hine at liue
 and þus he heom græiþeden mid grimme his gomene
An kæisere wes in Rome Claudius ihaten
iherden þa tiþende of Wiþer þon kinge
whulcne scome he him hæfden idon and mare him bihehte 
Þe kæisere hine wrædden þe Wurs him wes on heorte
 and swor bi his rigge þat Wiþer hit scolde abiggen
He bigon to senden ȝeond al þan Romleoden
he hætte al þa ræiȝe and alle þa radfulle
alle his hæȝe men his hustigge isechen
 and heo togædere comen i þere burh of Rome
Heo buden heore ferden wide ȝeond þon ærde
Mid unimete dome heo ferden vt of Rome
heo ferden swa longe þat heo comen to þisse londe
Claudius þe kæisere and al his Romanisce here
At Portchæstre heo comen alond and stepen up a sæstrond
 and bilæien anan Portchæstre mid heore folke swiþe faste
Heo letten deluen diches vnimete deope
 and al abuten oueral he makede stænene wal
Þa wes Portchestre burh mid þan bezste
ah mid þan windræsen al heo gunnen toreosen
mid fure and mid fehte foruaren þurh Glaudius þan kæisere
Þis iherde Wiþer þe wes Bruttene king her
þat icumen wes i þisse lond Claudius þat wes swa strong
Þe king gæderede uerde wide ȝeond his eærde
 and Aruiragus his broþer gæderede anoþer
 and ferden toward þære sæ mid selkuþe folke
þat heo comen mid heore here to Claudiene þan kæisere
Feondliche heo feohten fullen þa fæie
and þe eorl Aruiragus mid æþele help his broþer
Claudius hæfde enne richene mon þe wes icleoped Haumund
he redde þæn kæisere and al þan Romanisce here
Hamund biheold Wiþer and his wiþerhappes
 and heu ladliche i þon fihten he sloh þa Romcnihtes
 and al þat him biforen stod he falden to his foten
Hamun hine biþohte whet he don mihte
hv he mihte þene king Wiþer aquelle
Hamun ferde ȝeon þat wæl and wende þa deden
funde þer enne cniht þe islæȝen wes þerriht
nom he his burne and his goldileired bord
leoup he an his stede and bihælues he gon riden
þer he isæh Wiþer king þe wiþer wes an compe
Hamun þe ridere smat his aȝene ifere 
 and warþ him swiþe bisi swulc he Brut weore
Wende þe king Wiþer þat he weore his iuere
ah þer he na ne come ȝif hit nere for swikedome
Hamun arnde upward and oþer while adunward
þenne he isæh Romanisce mon he rasden him ouenan
his speche wes al Brutisc Brut swulc he weoren
Swa longe he gon riden þat he wes bi þæs kinges side
 and fæht þan kinge biforen swulc he weoren his mon iboren
 and sloh is haȝen iueren muchel swikedom wes þere
Þe king him treousede on for he wes swa æht mon
 and wende for soþ riht þat he weore his aȝen cniht
Þe king wende forþrihtes bihælues þan fihte
he wes swiþe ofhæt þat al his burne wes biswæt
he lette his burne of his rugge eorne
 and Hamun him to strac mid toȝen his mæine
mid his spere he wes wæht þes kinges breosten he tobræc
þane king Wiþer he ofsloh þer wes swikedom inoh
 and seoþþen rehliche fleh to his Romleode
kudde hit his kæisere whet he dude mid his spere
Þis isæh Aruiragus þat his broþer islæȝe wes þus
mid muchelen hiȝinge he leup to þan dæde kinge
igrap his stede and alle his iwede
 and sturede i þon compe alse hit þe king weore
Mest alle þa Bruttes þe weoren þere wenden þat hit weoren Wiþer
heo ræsden to Romleoden and heo remden to flonne
heo sloȝen forþrihtes Claudienes cnihtes
niȝen þusende heo læiden to þon grunde
Claudien þe kæisere sad wes of þon compe
his folc flah into scipen and from þæn londe iwenden
forþ mid þon vþen feondes heom uereden
Fif þusend heo lefden uppen þon londe
þat ne mithte no to scipe cumen þat heo neoren islæȝen oþer inomen
Wunderliche awei heo riden touward ane muchele wude
Aruiragus heom æfter mid twenti þusend cnihtes
heo sloȝen heo nomen mid honden heo todrowen
Hamun þurh þene wude flæh riht touward þere sæ
he ærnde to are hæuene he wenden scipen habben
Þe sæ wes iȝeonged þe scipen stoden a londe 
Þæ wile þe he þa scipen vt scæf Aruiragus him to draf
Nefde Hamun to iueren bute þritti rideren
Aruiragus heom alle sloh and Hamun mid heorsen todroh
for his broþer dæþe him wes swiþe unneþe
 and an oþer halue he wes glæd þat his ifon weoren dæd
for Hamundes dæþe Hamton heo hit hæhte
nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere
Nu þu iherest of wuche gomen aras þer þe tonome
swa doþ a feole wise tonome ariseþ
 and ofte of lutle þinge þe longe ilasteþ
for his nauere nan oþer gomen þat cleouieþ alswa ueste
Þa Hamun and is iueren weoren dæd Aruiragus wes swiþe glad
ah sone þeræfter him com særinesse
He and his cnihtes þeonene forþrihtes
tuo Winchestre wenden wæne com on ueste
heo wende to soþe þat heo siker weoren
Claudius þe keisere mid alle his Romanisce here
ouer sæ wende al mid isunde
Nes he þer buten enne niht þe wind wende forþriht
fromward þan stronde into þissen londe
Claudius wenden aȝan weder him stod an wille
hiȝenliche sone to Portchestre heo comen
Up iwende þe kæisere mid al his Romanisce here
iwepned wel alle heo wenden to þan walle
to heo eoden alle afoten and swiþe freche weoren
ouer þene wal heo clumben and binnen heo þrungen
þat folc heo al slowen þa æhte heo nomen
al þa wunliche burh heo barnden to duste
Þus Portchæstre toræs and nauere seoþþen heo ne aras
þat heo swulc weore swa heo wes eare
Claudius þe keisere mid wunderliche here
ferde to Winchæstre and bilæi þa burh swiþe feste
Þer binnen wes Aruiragus ærmliche biþrungen
and muchel dæl of his cunne of Bruttisce monnen
Wa wes þon kinge Aruiragus and to his cnihtes seide þus
Suggeþ me gode men godfulle kempen
wulle ȝe me helpen mid hæhȝere strengþe 
her to biwinne wurþscipe minne
Þa answereden aþele cnihtes
Nulle we þe bilæuen for liue ne for dæþen
On heo duden heore iweden and leopen on heore steden
cnihtes þer weoren swiþe iwhæte heo duden up þere burhȝæten
heo makeden heore sceldtrome þa scalkes weoren gode
Weoren alle þa cnihtes ȝærewe to þon fihte
Þa somnede alle þa alde þe to fehte heom scolde halden
bi are halue heo riden and spileden of ræde
 and nomen tweien cnihtes and senden to þon kæisere
 and axeden wheþer he wolde griþ þe he wolde vnfrih
Ær þer come mare lure hefde he þene cure
Þa andswerede Claudius and wiþ þan cnihten he spec þus
Wel is þe man nut þe sæhtnesse wurcheþ
Ich æm ræh mon inoh Rome is min riche
 and alle þa londes stondeþ a mire honde
þa biȝet me biuoren Iulius þe kæisere
 and æfter mine dome hæreþ into Rome
buten þes ilke kinedom nulle me noht icnawen
na þissere leodes folke for lauerd me halden
 and me pugcheþ muche scome at mire heorte ic habbe grome
ȝif Rome scæl forleosen þa while þe ich leouie
heore muchele wurhscipe þat mine ældere hire biwunnen
For nare ȝitsunge for nare ȝiuernesse
ne com ich to þissen londe to halden fiht stronge
ne for nane plihte buten to biȝiten mine rihte
 and ic heo wulle biwinnen oþer an wæle liggen
Æc cnihtes ȝit beoþ hider icumen from þon kinge Aruiragune
Fareþ swiþe aȝen to þan folckinge
suggeþ him to soþe for hit cumeþ him to cuþe
þat ȝif he wule a leoþ gan and halden me for lauerde
 and he me wulle buȝen þa bet him scal iwurþen
ȝif he me wule sende mine rihten of his londe
ic hine wulle wurþien mid wurhscipe muclen
 and suggeþ him ful iwis ich ȝifuen mine dohter Genuis
to sibben and to some þe bet wit mawen libben
 and ȝif he þis nule don he scal wurs vnderfon
faren wit swullen tosomne and mid fehten hit todælen
makien wænslæhtes þænne beoþ þe wurse 
Þa cnihtes wenden forþriht to þan folckinge
cudden him soþ quides from Claudien þæn kæisere
Þe king isæh þe neode and droh to his ræde
and he mid wurþscipe þas cnihtes awurþede
þat he of his kinedome wulde heren into Rome
and seoþþe wurþscipe him don his dohter to quene vnderfon
Togædere heo comen and sæhten heo weoren sone
 and seoþþen heo alle iwenden into Winchæstren
þa weoren in þissen londe blisfulle songes
Heo wuneden inne Winchæstre an and twenti wikene
 and senden to Rome ful iwis æfter þan maidene Genuis
Þat maiden mid isunde com to þisse londe
 and Claudien þe kæisere ȝæf heo þisse kinge
ȝet hit is isene þat heo wes her quene
þat þe king Aruiragus to quene hæfde Genuis
Þes þinges weoren idone and Claudien hæuede isend to Rome
þa while iwende Claudius and þe king Aruiragus
into Orcaneiȝe and þat lond al bilæien
ah muchel lond þerabuten al heo hit biȝeten
two and þritti æitlond heo setten on heore aȝere heond
heore griþ heo setten fæste and wenden to Winchæstre
From Rome wes icumen ful iwis þat fæire maide Genuis
isund and hire iuæren sixti rideren
þat maiden wes iwedded þe king heo hafde to bedde
Muchel wes þa blisse þe wes þanne i Bruttene
mid þan kinge Aruiragus and þæn kæisere Claudius
þa wes þis folk swa bliþe heo nære nauer ær on liue
for þere muchele blisse heo arærden enne burȝe
an enne swiþe feire stude uppe Sæuerne
Þa þe burh wes al imaked mid muchelere strengþe
þa burh ȝæf Aruiragus þæn kaisere Claudius
and þat lond þerabuten muchel and noht lutel
He hæhte setten hire on nome þe hire mihte isemen
hu þe king Aruiragus nam to quene Genuis
 and þer þe king heo ȝef Claudiene þan Romanisce kæisere
Claudien þe heȝe Kairclou heo hehte
ac nas hit noht longe þat þe nome moste stonden
ac for Claudiusses wurþscipe swa wes þe nome iqueþþen
Ah þa Claudius ærest in þissen londe com he funde enne feire wimman 
heo wes witer heo wes wis heo wes maiden ful iwis
Claudienes cnihtes heo biwunnen i þon fihte
inne Portchæstre and heolden heo wel fæste
 and ȝeuen heo Claudiene hit wes him swiþe iqueme
 and he hire rædde and forþ mid him ladde
 and leouede þe wimman leofliche swiþe
Þe wifman iwarþ mid childe bi Claudiene þan balde
þa þet child wes iboren wel wes Claudiene þerforen
Þa þe time wes ifulled þat hit fulleht sculde habben
æfter þan haþene laȝen þat stoden o þen ilke dæȝen
nome heo him aræhten and Gloi þat child hahten
Þis child wæx and wel iþæh and muchel folc him to bah
 and Claudien him bitæhte þa burh þe he ahte
 and sette heo mid cnihten þe gode weoren to fehten
and hæhte heo wite wel faste and heoten heo Gloichestre
al for his sune luuen þe leof him wes an heorten
þe seoþþe biȝæt al Walisc lond to his aȝere hond
and þerof he wes deme and duc feole ȝere
Þis child me biwuste inne Gloichæstre
 and þa þeos þinges weoren idone Claudius ferde to Rome
 and ladde þes childes moder for quene nauede he oþer
Þa Claudius com to Rome tiþende him com sone
þat þer wes cumen liþende into þere leode
an swiþe selcuþ gume of Antioge he wes icome
Petrus he wes ihaten he dude þer feole teonen
he uerde ȝeond al þat lond and turnde hit to Godes hond
Heonene wes iuaren Claudius þis lond heold Aruiragus
 and Genuis his quene þe wifmon wel idone
þa isæh þisses ledes king þat him ne derede naþing
þus he wunede here mid blisse twenti ȝere
Vnder þan comen tiþende to Aruiragus þan kinge
næs þer nan oþer ræd bute Claudius inne Rome wes dæd
Wa wes þisse kinge swa wes þere quene
swa wes alle þon bezsten þe wuneden an Bruttene
An þan timen hit wes þat Gloi wes swiþe god cniht
Þa þeo tiþende weoren comen to londe
of Claudius þen kæisere and hu hit wes al iuaren
þa seide þe king Aruiragus and wiþ his duȝeþe he spac þus
Swa ich auere ibiden are nulle ich naueremare 
þurh nane dome heren into Rome
næ naueremare heom senden gauel of mine londe
Ah ȝif heo hider cumeþ liþen leoden to biwinnen
her heo sculeþ ibiden bitterest alre baluwen
næ biȝeten nan oþer god buten here ȝeoten heore blod
scullen alle heore wif widewen iwurþen
Þus seide þe king þeh hit soþ neore
þer he sæt mid his scenche an his kinebenche
Ah al oþer hit iwarþ inne þan twam wintren
for þa Romleoden sende to þissere þeoden
hæhte heom senden here gauel of þissen londe
And þe king Aruiragus wradliche heom answerede
hehten heom mucle eiȝe ut of his æhseone
fleon of þissen londe ær heo fæiȝe iwurþen
forþ heo iwenden, into Romlonde
Þa wes i þon ȝere Vaspasien kæisere
þes tiþende him wes læþ and herfore he was wraþ
He clupede to ræde alle Romleode
 and seide bi his liue þat he wolde to Bruttlonde
bitelen his irihten þat Claudius ær ahte
 and ȝif heo nolden gan an griþ he wolden fehten heom wiþ
and al Romleoden þis him gon ræden
Vaspasien him forþ wende þat he com to France
þa ȝet hit wes al his aȝen þat he isæh mid his aȝene
ladde he þere leodene king þe hine for lauerd icneou
vorþ mid imseoluen touward þissen londen
To þere sæ he wende scipen he þer funde
þat toȝenes him weoren ibonned þe ȝet þe he wes i Rome
He ibad þes wederes wind com on oueste
in he wende at Witsond and æt Doure he þohte nimen lond
Aruiragus þerof wes war and atliche him biuore uerde
 and draf hine ut mid strengþe forþ mid sæstrame
Mid him hafde Vaspasien swiþe gode sæmen
strahten vt here lof and leiden æfter vþen
forþ bi sæside seileden swiþe
An hiȝende ful sone to Tottenas heo come
strahten scipen to þan londe and eoden uppen stranden 
Heo nomen heore wepnen and forþ gunnen wenden
tosomnen heo riden uaste þat heo comen to Æxechæstre
he wenden wel to bistelene into þare burhȝe
Ah þet burhfolc wes war and wel hine wusten
wel heo closden heore ȝeten and ȝareweden heom to fehten
 and þa burh biwusten wel mid þan bezsten
Seouen daȝes fulle Vaspasien mid his monnen
læiȝe at Exchæstre and bilaie heom swiþe ueste
Þat iherde Aruiragus þat he wes icume þus
he nom al þa ferde of Brutlondes ærde
 and sone he gon faren in toward Cornwalen
into Exchæstre þa burh wes þa fæstre
Aruiragus wes þerinnen mid Bruttisce mennen
Vaspasien þervte þa burh bilæi abute
Amarȝen þa hit dæi wes duren heo vntunden
cnihtes heom gereden grundliche feire
blewen þa bemen heornes gunnen dremen
heondleden scæftes and goldfaȝe sceldes
riden ut tosome ræȝe Brutes
þritti þusend þe þræt wes þa mare
Þerute wes heom toȝæn þe kæisere Uaspasien
togadere heo tuhten and laþliche fuhten
hardeliche heuwen helmes þer gullen
stercliche tostopen mid steles egge
Alle dæi þer ilæste fæht mid þan mæste
a þet þat þustere niht todælde heore muchele fiht
læien a ba halue cnihtes toheouwen
þær wes hærm mid þon meste biuoren Exchæstre
Þat biheold þa quene Genuis ihaten
særi wes hire heorte mid hermen afulled
cleopede to hire lauerde þe leof hire wes on heorte
to þon kinge Aruiragus þæ quene spac wiþ him þus
Lauerd biþenc þe Þine þeowes beoþ gode
þu hauest mucle treowscipe treowþe staþeluæste
þat beoþ þa þingges þe biriseþ to ælche kinge
riche men and hæne ȝif wiþ seoumen he wule beon clænen
Biþenc þu a þine quides þe þu sulf quiddest
wiþ Claudien minne fader þe wes þi cudliche freond
þe dude þe þa wurhscipe bitahte me þe to wiue 
 and þu ært me swa leof swa mi kinelauerd
Mi cun is her wiþvten and þi kun her wiþinnen
Ȝif þu brekest þine quides and mi cun quellest
soþ ich þe habbe iseid wiþ þine sune þu beost iuæid
 and ȝif mi cun clembeþ and bineoþen þe ibringeþ
 and þe seoluen and þin folc falleþ to grunde
ȝif þu and þine þer wurþeþ dæd þeonne beo ich wiþ mine sune iued
betere weore sæhte þene swulc vnisibbe
 and biþenc þe of þan fore hu þu mine fader swore
to lasten alche ȝere al to þine liue
gauel into Rome of þine kinedome
 and ȝet ilæsteþ þi lif swa hit do longe
for þi þu most holden þat þu ær bihæhtest
Al þa heredcnihtes heolden mid þere quene
Þe king and alle his cnihtes wakeden alle nihte
al niht heo runden whæt heom weoren to ræde
Ne mihte heo finde nænne ræd þe heom þuhte al swa god
swa heom þuhte þe soþe quides of þere quene
Amarwe þa hit dæi wes duȝeþen heom gereden
togædereward heo uusden alswa heo wolden fehten
Forþ com þa quene and rad heom bitweonen
ærst heo nom griþ and seoþþen heo heom spac wiþ
sette sæhtnesse somnede cnihtes
þa ær weoren ifeonde makede heom to fronde
And þe king heom bihehten his foreward to haldene
 and swa he hit ilæste þe while þe he luuede
Þus heo weoren sahte and þus heo weoren some
Þa wes þeos Bruttene swiþe iblissed
 and Vaspasiæn and his iueren al þat winter wuneden here
from burie to burie ferden mid blisse
Anan swa seomer come þa ferden heo to Rome
Brutlond wes bliþe a to þeos kinges liue
Nu hauede þe king Aruiragus enne sune þe hehte Maurus
he wes isende to Rome to leornien in scole
þer him wes swa wel idiht he wes clærc and god cniht
Þider him com sonde ut of þissen londe
þæt her nes nan rad for þe king his fader wes dæd
 and he mosten cume sone to his kinedome
Swa wes þat writ idiht and he hit dude forþriht 
to þisse londe he com and underfeng þene kinedom
Wel riche wes Aruiragus and mucle ricchere Maurius
a þisse londe he heold griþ a þisse londe he hulde friþ
her wes blisse her wes mete and alre godene mast
A þissen ilken hit stod þet com ouer sæflod
an king þe hæhte Rodric elche oþer unilic
he com ut of Scice elches londes vniliche
he brohte mid him þe Peohtes folc of muchele mahte
Seoþþen Rodric wes ærst mon and he mihte uuel don
a he ferde bi sæflod and dude he uuel and næuere god
monie hundreþ buriȝe he hæfde imakede blæþe
He ferde bi sæstronde into Scotlonde
þat lond he al wæste mid hermen þan meste
þurh þat lond he ærnde and hærȝede and hærmde
Comen þa tiþende to Maurius þon kinge
hu þe king Rodric his ræflac makede
Sone he sende sonde ȝeond alle þisse kinelonde
hæhte æuerælcne mon þa his monscipe uþe
þat he wel iwepned comen to hirede
Þis folc wes isomned and þe king fusde
ferde into Scotlonde þere he Rodric king fond
Heo fuhten swiþe feondliche and feollen þa Peohtes
 and Rodric þer wes ofslaȝen and seoþþen mid heorsen todraȝen
Þer dude Maurius þe king a wel swuþe sællech þing
uppen þen ilke stude þer he Rodric uordude
he lette aræren anan enne swuþe sælcuþ stan
he lette þeron grauen sælcuþe runstauen
hu he Rodric ofsloh and hine mid horsen todroh
 and hu he þa Peohtes ouercom mid his fæhtes
Vp he sette þæne stan ȝet he þer stondeþ
swa he deþ al swa longe swa þa woreld stondeþ
Nome him scupte þe king and hehte þene stan Westmering
a muchel dæl londes þe þer liþ abuten
nom þe king to his hond and hæhte hit Westmerelinge lond
Nu þu hafuest soþ iherd for wham hit swa hatte
Þa þe þeo Peohtes weoren ouercumne i þon fehte
and Rodric wes dæd and his iueren fordemed
þa fluȝen þer bihælues fiftene hundred
þat weoren þa feirest men þe weoren i þon fehte
hæfden he to heretoȝe enne hæhiborene mon 
Þeos weolden heom iburȝen and bihalues fleon
 and buȝen vt of londe to helpen heore liue
Þat isehȝen þreo eorles þe i þeon fehte weoren ohte
whudereward þa ferde heore flæm makeden
Þe eorles heom siȝen to mid selen heore cnihtes
driuen heom into ænne hæhne wude þer heo heærm þoleden
Stod þe wundliche wude amidden ane wælde
biuoren na bihinden ne mihten þær nan atwinden
ah alle hi heom nomen and nane heo ne asloȝen
fæste heom heo bunden and brohten to þen kinge
þat þe king heom sculden don oþer slan oþer hon
Anan swa þe king heom spec wiþ swa heo ȝeornden his griþ
ȝeorne heo hine beden þurh his ædmeden
þat he nomen heom to þrallen and heo him wolden þiwien
 and heo him wolden beon liþe a to heore liue
Al þe king weorhte also heo bisohten
 and heom an heond sælde muchel dæl of londe
al abuten Catenes þer heo caþel wrohten
Þat lond wes swiþe god ah seoþþen wes þe muchel flod
nes hit neuere itiled þurh nænne eorþeitilie
no nauere þer ne wuneden on nanes cunnes quic mon
Sonen heo gunnen to ærien þat lond wes swiþe æþele
heo tileden heo seowen heo repen heo meowen
wiþinnen þan þrom ȝeren þa nomen heo twælf iueren
 and heo uerden sone þat heo to þisse londe comen
Bruttes heo gretten mid græiþlichen worden
beden heom beon on sele and alle isunde
We eow toȝerneþ ȝeue swiþe deore
þet ȝe us ȝiuen wifmen to habben to wiue
þenne maȝe we heolden luue to þissen leodfolke
Þa þis iherden Bruttes heokerliche heom þuhte
 and hehten heom faren awæi and fleon of heore londe
for nolde heo heom ȝetten þa þinges þe heo ȝernden
Peohtes weoren iscende and heore wæi forþ wende
ham to heore cunne and cudden heom heore erende
Heo nomen heore sonde and sende to Irlonde
to þes londes kinge Gille Caor ihaten
 and biden hine heom senden wifmen of his londe
 and þe king heom ȝette al þat heo ȝeorenden 
Þurh þa ilke wifmen þa þer wuneden longe
þat folc gan to spelien Irlondes speche
 and auer seoþþen þa laȝen wunieþ a þan londe
swa heo beoþ þere nu and æueremare
Hæfde Maurius þe king god griþ ȝeond his lond
a to his liue his leoden weoren bliþe
Þa com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi
forþ com þes kinges sune Coil wes ihaten
Þes wes ræh þes wes strong þes wes stiþ an þonke
þes cuþe alle þa domes þe stoden inne Rome
ah he ne luuede noht longe þat wes his leodene hærm
ah þa while þe he luuede his lond he huld a blisse
Hæfde Coil þe king þe wes Bruttene aþel
enne leofue sune Luces ihaten
þes wes þe bezste mon þe auere hæfde kinedom
seoþþen to Brutlonde com Bruttes þe hit biwan
Luces wes kineboren Luces wes wel itoȝen
 and he wes swiþe blæþfæst Bruttes hine luueden
Moni wes þat gode þing þat cuþe Luces þe king
nes þa na man vnder lufte þe cuþe betere cræftes
Þurh þisne ilke æþele mon vnderfeng þis lond Cristindom
þe mon þe wule lusten hu hit ærest ilomp
þeos boc him wulle suggen soþþere wordes
hu Luces þe king ærst Crist luuede
Men wel idone comen ut of Rome
comen to þan kinge and talden him tiþende
of alle þere fore þe Petrus dude in Rome
and whulcne martirdom hauede vnderfon
 and þa oþere halȝen þe mid Godde hah weoren
Þa longede swuþe Luces þon kinge
ære he mare wuste of þan Lauerd Criste
Þa weoren inne Rome men wel idone
 and an hali mon þer wes Pape Elæudarius wes ihaten
Nom Luces þe king of his leofuste monnen
sende to þa Papen and feire hine gon greten
 and bed hine on Godes nomen þat him god uþe 
þet he senden him anan sumne godcunde mon
for þe king wolde wel don and Cristes laȝen vnderfon
libben mid rihte and luuien his Drihte
he an alle his leoden þe wuneden inne þissere þeoden
Þa þuhte Elæuþerie þat tiþende swiþe murie
nes na mon on liue þat weore alswa bliþe
alse wes þe hali man þa he þis iheren gon
Þe Pape hafden tweien biscopes þe luueden Godes rihten
hiderwardes he heom senden þa biscopes forþ wenden
þat comen þa Godes sonden into þissen londe
to Luces þon kingen and to al his hereþringen
Þa spac Dunian and þe oþer biscop Fagan
seiden þan kinge larspel and he hit hærcnede wel
ær þat lærspel weoren idon þe king ȝeornde Cristindom
 and alle his duȝeþecnihtes hit ȝeorde forþrihtes
Þe king fulluht vnderfeng and alle his gode men mid him
 and alle his Bruttes þe him buȝen wolden
 and þa fulluht nulden vnderfon þe king heom letten fordon
Þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weise on
beiene þa biscopes ferden ȝeond þas Bruttene
alle þa templen þe þa heþene hafden itimbrid
Heo letten alle þa scrud at þere dure werpen vt
wascen þa waȝes wel mid þan bezsten
þa nomen anlicnes þe Mahun weoren ihatene
heo letten heom draȝen vt oþer bi hondes oþer bi fot
heo heom letten swalen inne swærte fure
Þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weiis on
heo ferde forþrihtes þurh Godes mihten
from stouwe to stouwe and stureden heomseoluen
hælȝeden alle þa templen a þes Helindes nomen
Þa þet wes all idon þo token heo oþer weis on
þa setten heo biscopes þan folken to dihten
þerouer ærchebiscopes þat clærcscipe to rihten
chirchen he letten areren monie and wel iwhare
preostes heo þer setten ase þerto mihte semen
Þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weis on
þa com Luces þe king and lond þerto leide
 and sette þeron Godes friþ and freoden alle þe chirchen 
 and þa laȝen beoþ a monie studen alswa Luces heom on dude
Naþeles heo weoren soþþen swiþe awæmmed
ladliche iniþered þurh niþfulne craft
 and eft heo weoren irihte swa hit weolde Drihten
Þa alle þas þinges weoren idone þa ferden þa biscopes to Rome
 and bileæfden in þisse londe þat folc a Godes heonde
 and Luces heore lauerd þe leof heom was an heorte
þus hit ferde here wel feole ȝere
Luces þe leodking leouuede wel longe
twa and feowerti wintre mid muchere winne
her wes mete her wes drænc men þerof dræmden
her wes unimete fare a þissere folc riche
Þus heo gunnen driuen and forȝeten to swiþe
þat heom tæhte þe hehȝe mon þe gode biscop Dunian
 and Fagan his iuære þe while þe heo weoren here
Inne griþe þurh alle þing wunede Luces þe king
þat com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi
leof him wes griþ and ræd inne Gleochæstre he wes dæd
þær hehȝe Bruttes þene king bureden
Þa wes þe weorlde swa uorþ iuaren seoþþen ure Drihte wes iboren
an hundred ȝere and sixti þa þe king sah to grunde
Seoþþen Luces king wes dæd her wunede a swiþe strong red
ne bilæfde he her neouþer suster ne broþer
ne quene ne næh cun þe his caþel mihte heolden
To Rome comen tiþende of Luces þon kinge
hu þe king wæs hære dæd and i þisse londe nas na ræd
Heo makeden heore uerde and senden to þissen ærde 
Seuarus wes heore hæretoȝe inne Rome he wes ibore
Þe ferde wes swiþe strong þeo comen heo to þisse lond
Seuerius wende anan to hæbbene þisne kinedom
ah Bruttes weoren bisie and ofte hine abæileden
ofte heo him wiþ fuhten a feole cunne wisen
Seuarus hine biþoþte whet he don miþte
in his herede he makede griþ and lette awæi þat vniriht
þat na man ne wurþe swa wod ne witte bidæled
þat in his hirede breke griþ uppe leome and uppe lif
of nauere nane þinge þat come to his cleopinge
Þis iseȝen Bruttes þe weoren swiþe bisie
þat Seuarus in his hirede hæfde hehliche griþ
 and mong heomseoluen vnimete seorȝen
Bruttes siȝen togæderes fulle seoue þusend
 and speken Seuarium wiþ and ȝirden his hiredes griþ
 and he heom ȝette and ȝef ȝiues swiþe gode
Þa wes Seuarus hired selcuþliche istronged
alle þe ær weoren buuen he heom sette bineoþen
 and muchele luue heold wiþ alle þat ȝirnden his griþ
He uærde to Lunden and heo hine vnderfengen
he uerde þurh þis kinelond and sette hit in his aȝere hond
 and æuere heo fluȝen him biuoren þe his feond weoren
Swa swiþe he heom hænde þat heo fluwen ouer Humbre
heo fluȝen forþrihtes þat heo comen to þan Peohtes
 and heo heom vnderfengen and nomen heom to iuaren
Heo makeden enne hehne cniht heore heretoȝe forþriht
fæier cniht and hende Fulgenes wes ihaten
he heom scolde læden and he heom sculde ræden
Enne ende of Scotlonde nom Fulgenes to his honde
þe ende him wes deore he hæhte Dæire
Sæuarus from Scottewærd seoþþe aȝæn wende
 and his folc lædde into Lundene
 and Fulgenes vt of Scotlen muchel scaþe makede
He leop into Brutlond mid muchele baluræssen
æhte he nom men he sloh he duden seorȝen inoh
 and þus he uerde longe inne Scotlonde
Þis iherde Seuarus þe inne Rome wes kæisere
and seoþþen hider al þa lond stod an his aȝere heond
þe kæisere sende his seonde ȝeond feole londe
lette him to beoden swa monie of weorcmonnen
þat he lette makien ænne dic þe wæs wunderliche deop
muche and swiþe stronge bisides Scotlonde
from sæ to sæ eode þæ dich ælche oþere vnilich
Þervfenen he makede scid wal wunder ane cræftie
seoþþen he sette cnihtes to witen hit dæies and nihtes
þat neuere Poht þerouer ne com ne næuere nan oþer mon
bute whaswa walden ȝernen griþ and speken þan kæisere wiþ
 and wunien forþ here mid Seuare þan kæisere
Þat iherde Fulgenes þat þis weorc iuorþed wes 
þat he into þisse londe ne mihte ne dæies ne nihtes
Nuste he þa nænne ræd þe him æuere þuhte god
he cleopede alle his dringches þat heo comen to hustinge
heore kinge to ræden of his muchele neode
Heo him rædden to faren riht into Cise
færliche he þider com and fæire wes underfon
He spac wiþ þan Peohtes and swa muchel heom bihæhte
þat heo gædereden in þan ærde mucle scipferde
 and ferden bi sæstronde into þissen londe
He uerde riht to Euerwicke Brutten þutte sellic
þa burh he anan bilæi mid baldere strengþe
Seoþþen he dude to witen þurh worde and þurh writen
alle his freonden þe weoren in þissen londe
þat heo scolden wel don and alle comen him to
he heom wolden mucle wele and wurþscipe itæchen
 and æuere to his liue heo sculden beon him leoue
Þis iherden Bruttes þerfore heo weoren balde
 and wenden from Seuere þan Romænisce kæisere
moni þusend Bruttes to Fulgenes
 and he heom faire onfeng and muche feoh bihæhte
Þat iherde Sæuarus þat Fulgenes dude þus
he somnede uerde of folke of þissen ærde
he uusde touwærd Euerwic to his fæisiþe
Þa he to Euerwic com Fulgenes him wes aforen on
heo bigunnen fehten feondliche swiþe
a ba hælue þer ful folc unimete
Sæuare þer wes ofslæȝen and feole his Romwæren
Fulgenes wes iwunde wunderliche sære
þat i þan þridden dæie he sarne dæd þolede
Of Sæueres dæþe Bruttus þer demden
sæiden heom bitweonen þa þat tir ahten
Seuarus wes god cniht and he heold us swiþe riht
þæ while þe we him walden heren ær we turnden to Fulgene
þurh heore vuele ræde beien heo beoþ dædde
Nime we Sæuarusses lic and lede we hit into Eouuerwic
 and þær we hit sculleþ biburien mid muchelere blisse
 and forþ ȝelden þa duȝeþe þe he us dude whilen
Al weoren þa dæden alse heo idemden
Sæuarus bilefde here tweien sunen þus hæhten heore nomen
þe ældere hehte Basian þe ȝungere hahte Gezan 
Þe beiene heo weoren ibroþeren ah noht of are moder
Basianes moder wes of Brutlondes ærd
 and Gezanes moder of Romanisce monnen
Bruttes nomen Basian and bitahten him þisne kinedom
 and þa Romanisce men to kinge makede Gezan
Bruttes weoren bisie and Basian heo luueden
 and þa Romanisce men luueden swiþe Gezan
Þær aras muchel ballu bitwenen þissen broþeren
heo nomen here uerden and comen to stalfehte
and þer þe king Basian sloh his broþer Gezan
 and þat Romanisce folc fleh of þissen londe
ac monie þer weoren ifalled i þan muchele fehte
I þisse londe wes a ȝung mon vnder þon kinge Basian
Carrais wes ihaten his nome þes wes a sellich gume
His fader wes an unstrong cniht ah þe sune wes swiþe sturne
þat wes þe bisegæste mon þe wunede inne Bruttene
Of nane quike monne næuede he care nænne
wa wes him þurh alle þing þat Basian wes Bruttene king
Basian wes griþful king and Carrais ne likede hit naþing
Þa a þan ilke time verden bi særime
vtlaȝen to iwiten fulle sixti scipen
Carrais hine biþohte of ane hindere cræfte
þat he wolde sone faren into Rome
Forþ he iuusde and into Rome ferde
 and spac wiþ þane kæisere and wiþ þan Romanisce here
 and þus seide Carrais he wes swike fuliwis
Hæil seo þu Cyrian þe king þe græteþ Basian
and dæþ þe ful wel to witen ba bi worden and bi writen
þat ne mæi he þe no mare senden þat gauel of Bruttlonde
for twien haueþ bigunnen to senden hit bi his monnen
i sæ heo funden vtlaȝen and habbeoþ alle his men islaȝen
 and iræued al þat gærsume þe scolde þe to cume
Þa vtlaȝes beoþ swa stronge bi watere and bi londe
þat ne mæi na man ouer sæ uaren bute mid swiþe mucle care
Ah ȝif þi wille weore þat þu woldest me ihere
 and bitachen me þine writen and senden me twælf scipen
 and hælden me to munde a þire aȝere hond
into sæ ic wolde faren and slæn alle þa utlaȝen
 and þi gauel þe sende ut of Brutlonde
For ich æm ennes cnihtes sune and cun ich habbe iwide 
haueþ mi fader bi þære sæ castel swiþe sæle
 and cnihtes inowe and men unifoȝe
alle heo wulleþ to me draȝen to quellen þa utlaȝen
 and þus ich wulle þurh mire hond witen þi feh and þi lond
Þis ihærde Cyrian speken þene swikeful mon
 and al he ȝette him þat he him to ȝirde
writen he him bitehten and wapnen him aræhte
 and forþ hine senden touward þissen londe
Forþ he ferde Carrais þat he com to France
æuere his writen he vnfeold þer he forþ ferde
 and seiden al þan monnen what he i Rome hæhde biwunnen
 and folc him wende an æuerælche ende
Carrais com to sæ mid selcuþe uolke
he hafde to iueren fif hundred rideren
 and folc he hafde a foten muchel and vnnimete
Al þa scipen bi sæstronde he nom to his honde
he uerde forþ in sæ uerden hine vþen
 and he sone bicom into Brutlonde
 and anan bigon ræuinge uppen Basian þene kinge
Carrais nom his sonde and sende ȝeond þisse londe
bad ælcne ȝungne mon þe weorces nalde ȝeomen
 and æuereælcne utlaȝe þe his lond hadde biboȝen
 and auerælcne cnihtes sune þat his main wolde cuþen
and ælcne wiþerfulne mon þe god wolde biwinnnen
þat him to scolden comen for golde and gæirsume
Þas weoren cuþe wunder ane wide
 and þa wiþerwarde sumnede uerde
heo comen to Carrais þritti þusend fuliwis
 and heo uorþ iwenden bi þan sæstronde
Heo rupten heo ræfden noht heo ne bilæfden
castles heo nomen Bruttes heo sloȝen
monie heo forbarnden aþele Bruttus
heo uerden norh heo uerden æst al þat lond heo makeden west
heo ferden into Scotlon þer heo scaþe worhten
 and aȝan to þisse londe þas leoden heo foruerden
He nom ænne bisine mon and sende to Brutten
 and þas word heom sæde þe Carrais heom sende
Carrais þe stronge wunieþ inne comela
 and send her bihalues and grætet wel Bruttes
Ȝe buþ godliche gumen and ich eow wulle griþien 
 and freoscipe eow ȝiuen and freondscipe halden
ȝif ȝe on eowre cuþþe king me wulleþ makien
 and Bruttus andswereden for heo weoren aþele men
 and seiden þurh alle þing þat heo nalden swiken heore king
for næuere quicne mon swiken þene king Basian
 and þis word aȝæn com to Carrais þon stronge
Carrais hine biþohte whæt he don mæhte
bi twam wittre cnihten he sende to þan Pohtes
þa Pohtes weoren on londe next Basiane þan kinge
To heom com þa sonde from Carrais þon stronge
 and muchel heom bihæhte of worliche æhte
Þa Pohtes weoren uuele he leoseden heore aþele
heo sworen forþrihtes and treoþen heo plihten
þat heo wolden Basian inne fehte biswiken
Þis word com to Carrais þa wes he glad ful iwis
forþriht he nom his sonde and sende to þan kinge
 and seide him forþrihtes þat wiþ him he wolde fehte
buten he him wolde rumen and bilæuen þæs riche
Þa seide þe king Basian Ær ih wulle dæd beon
Wiþinnen seouen nihte heo comen to þan fihte
biforen þere burh Eouerwic þat feht wes swiþe storlic
Þa heo scolden bezst fehten þa fluȝen al þa Pohtes
 and heo Basian þe king mid alle bilæfden
 and Carrais him on þrong and mid spere him ofstong
Bruttes heo sloȝen and moni hundred þer nomen
Þa stod al þis lond a Carrais aȝere hond
þa nom he al þa Peohtes and sende into Scotte
 and ȝaf heom þere muchel lond inne Scotlonden
 and heore cun wunede þære seoþþen aueremare
Þis word com to Rome heræfter ful sone
hu Carrais hæfde iuaren and Basian þene king ofslæȝen
Heo somneden twa ferden of Romanisce ærden
 and nomen tweien eorles þe weoren swiþe aþele
Allec hæhte þe an wes wis and strong mon
þe oþer wes icleoped þus Liuius Gallus
Heo ferden of Rome and to þisse londe comen
þat heo bicomen to Carrais þan kinge
