Carrais heo ofsloȝen his cnihtes heo nomen
Þus þa Romanisce men ræsden to leoden 
 and Allec nom to his honde muchel of þisse londe
Þa ȝet þer weoren Bruttus monie bihælues
þe castles heolden stronge burhȝes brade and longe
Heo lætten hiȝendliche varen seoþ into Cornwalen
æfter Asclepidiot þe wes i Cornwale duc
He com an hiȝenge and heo hine heouen to kinge
Þa somneden Bruttus sele þeines
hehte alle þa cnihtes cumen to þan kinge
and æuerælcne ohte mon biwinnen his aþelen
heo buden heore uerde uppe niþinges bærde
Þa wes Allec þe king iliþen into Lunden
 and Bruttene king sone him bæh æfter
Hit wes an anne hæhȝe dæie halȝeden leoden
wes Allec þe king in are temple
in Lundenne mid his Romleoden
Þa iherde þe king mucle ludinge
in Lundene stureden þa leoden
Allec him ut leop and his wepnen he igrap
 and al his Romleoden þa i Lundene weoren
 and comen ut of þere burh and iseȝen heom bihæluen
iseȝen heom bisiden sillic heom þuhte
wha hæfde al þa monuerede þidere isende
Bruttes heom buȝen to mid bittere ræsen
Allec heo sloȝen muche folc heo nomen
 and sum on uæste bæh into þere burh
 and þe eorl Liuius into Lundenne flæh
lette luken þa ȝeten and himseolf læþ to walle
and Bruttes þa burȝen gunnen biriden
 and bileien þa burh wel mid þe bezsten
Þe king Asclepediot þe wes cniht swiþe god
sende his sonde into Scotlonde
into Muriane æfter monweorede
 and æc into West Wales æfter WælBrutten
 and swa he lette sone uaren soþ into Cornwalen
hæhte ælcne mon of þan ærd þe hæfde on his chinne bærd
uppe leome and vppen lif to Lundene liþen
Inne seouen nihte isomned heo weoren
heo heolden to walle mid wunderliche strengþe
 and Liuius Gallus godliche werede 
Bruttes a þan ende breken þa walles
 and iwenden binnen þa wes þa burh biwunnen
 and Liuius Gallus gæinde to anne castle
 and þer binen him ræsde mid his Romanisce uolke
 and Bruttene king bæh to þæn castle
 and lætte to læpen alle þa Brutleoden
Þa isæh Liuius Gallus þat his help wes swiþe wac
þa leonede he ouer wal and lude gon cleopien
Asclepidiot þene king Þu ært swiþe kene
ich wullen þe speken wiþ and ȝirne þe liues griþ
þat þu mid griþe me leten uaren forþ touward Rome
 and mid me mine leoden þe ȝet beoþ an liue
 and ich þe wulle swerien vppen mine sweorde
þat nulle ic naueremare aȝen cumen here
Asclepidiot iherde þat þeos word him þuhte god
 and al him iȝette þat Gallus þer ȝerde
Of þan castle heo ut foren and aþes heo sworen
 and swa heo gunnen wenden uorþ ut of londen
Þa com Scottene king scriþen to hirede
 and imætte Gallus and his gumen alle
Sone cleopede Columban þe wes Scottene king
Whar beo ȝe mine gumen vt of Galwæiþa
Whar beo ȝe mine men ut of Mureine
Whar beo ȝe mine Scottes Scriþeþ me biside
Her we sculleþ wel whreken ure wines deore
 and ure uulle iuan fallen to þan grunde
Ȝif þe king Asclipidiot þe is cniht swiþe god
haueþ heom speken wiþ and iȝefuen heom liues griþ
nes ich noht þere ne nan of mine iuaren
ne we hit nulleþ halden for ure freond heo habbeoþ aqualde
Heo leiden heom bitweonen heore speren longe
 and ladlichen swiþe feolen Romleoden
 and Gallus heo nomen and þat hafd him of sloȝen
 and wurpen hine in ænne broc þe þer heom bi stod
 and al þæt wal heo brohten into þan broke
þer Gallus i þan broke at grunde was biburied
Þa wes þas þeode iclansed of Romleode
and Bruttes þan broke nome bitæhten
for Gallus wes islaȝen þerbi hæhte hine nemni Galli
 and a þere Ænglisce boc he is ihaten Walebroc 
Nu ich habbe þe iraht hu he hauede þene nome icaht
for nu and aueremare is þe nome þere
Þa wes king Asclepidiot þe wes cniht swiþe god
fulle ten ȝere mid Brutten heo luuede here
seoþþen his ende bicom þat was uuele idon
þat he sculden swa raþe uaren of þissen lifdaȝen
for he wes swiþe læfful alle Brut luueden
I Glouchæstre wes an eorl of aþelene moncunne
þe alre hæheste iborne mon þe wunede inne Bruttene
Coel wes ihaten hæhst of þan Brutten
he wæs of Gloies cunne þe Glochæstre ahte
swa þat mid alle heore mihte heo comen to ane fihte
Coel eorl i þan fihte stod and sloh þene king Asclepidiot
Imong þissen imonge com reouþe to þisse londe
swa þat þe kæisere Dioclician sende to þisse londe Maximiæn
hider he com faren mid muchelere ferde
Þa he com to londe Coel he uunde
mid compe hæfde biuunnen þat he king was himseolue
Coel and Maximien cuþliche speken
 and freondscipe makeden iuastened mid treoþen
Þa seide Maximien Mi broþer Dioclician
haueþ me al þa londes bitaht a mire honde
bitwixe Muntgiu and Scotlonde þat ic heo scal þurhscriþen
 and alle þa ilke men fordon þat luuieþ þene Cristindom
Þa wes wa Coel þe king wæs on Bruttene
þat isæhtnesse mid treoþe hafde isemed
Coel heold hine stille and Maximien dude his wille
elcne Cristine mon at þan hefde he binom
 and þa wiþsaken wolde Cristindom he dude his marken him on
Þus ferde Maximien he martrede Seint Alban
 and Seint Iulien and Seint Aaron and tweien ancres of Kærlion
Næs nan biscop næs nan clærk ne cniht neore he swa sterc
bute he wiþsoke Cristindom þat he nes anan fordon
Þa þis wes al idon þa uerde forþ Maximian
 and Coel bilæfde king inne Bruttene 
Þes king hæfuede enne dohter þe wes him swiþe deore
 and he al kinelond bitahte þan maidene an hond
for næfde he nan oþer child þe mihte i þissen londe beon king
Þat mæide hehte Elene seoþþen heo wes quene
i þan londe of Ierusalem leoden to blissen
Þis maiden wes wel itæht on bocken heo cuþe godne cræft
 and wunede in þisse londe mid hire fader stronge
Heræfter sone þat word com to Rome
Þat Coel hæfden iquald Asclepidiot þene king
Þa weoren Romleoden bliþe on heore mode
for he hæfde an his daȝen muchel of heore cunne islaȝen
Ȝet ne com Maximien neuere to Rome aȝen
Þa nom Dioclicien ænne eorl wel idon
þat wes þe ræhȝeste mon þe wuneden inne Rome
 and hæfde moni lond ilæid under his hond
nas na man in his dæȝen þat dursten him derf makien
Þe kæisere hine sende into þissen londe
into þissen ærde mid vnimete uærde
Custance hehte þe eorl æþelest alre cnihten
Þis iherde Coel þat icumen wæs Custance
adræd he wes swiþe of his ahȝene liue
he nom forþrihtes six wise cnihtes
to Custance heom sende and wilcumede hine to londe
 and he seolf him wolden specken wiþ ȝef he him wolden ȝifuen griþ
 and Custance him sende æfter þat he come mid twalf cnihten
tosomne heo comen togædere heo speken sone
Þa queþ þe kin Coel Custance lust me nu wel
Ich sugge þe þurh alle þing ich sloh Asclepidiot þene king
þe hæfde þurh his wiþerlaȝen muchel of þine cunne ofslaȝen
 and mid strengþe eow atholden wolde þat gauel of þissen londe
 and muchelne scome he eow dude þe ræþer he dæd þolede
For ich wes an of þan hæhste þat swore eow hersumnesce
to Romen þat we sculden senden þat gauel of þissen londe
Þas aþþes þe king bræc þerfore he is nu dæd
Ah aswike wit vnker fihtes and lokien we to þan rihten
 and ich wullen halden to and halden þe for hærre
 and beon þe ful liþe and halden þe for lauerd
 and ælche ȝere þe senden þat gauel of Brutlonde
Þa answerede Custance riche mon and swiþe bald 
Coel þu ært wis mon and wisdom þe folleweþ
Beo nu godful king and gumene þu beo lauerd
 and al ich þe ȝette swa hit ȝirnest
 and ich wulle mid monscipe þine monradene onfon
for þu us dedest monscipe and god þa þu sloȝe Asclepidiot
Mid muchelere wurscipe sæht heo iwurþen
mid muchelere blisce heo wuneden in burȝen
Ah nes hit buten ane while þat þer anoþer time
neoren noht feouwerti daȝen allunge iuæreden
þat Coel þe king seoc lai an comlen
his hæfde swiþe oc and þe king wes wunderliche seoc
Seouen niht and ænne dæi þe king swiþe seoc lai
hit heold hine bi þan ribben þat ne mihte he na leng libben
 and he cleopede him to riche his þeines
þat heo him sculden ræden at swulchere neode
hu he mihte dihten Ælene his dohter
Þa heo hafden al iseid þat wes þe utemæste raþ
þat heo ȝeue Ælene Custance to are quene
 and al his kineliche lond sette in Custances hond
 and Coel him dude swa þe king wes inne Bruttene
Þa nes þer nan oþer rad bute Coel iwarþ dæd
 and Custance hauede Ælene biwedded to quene
þet wes þa wiseste wifman þa wunede a Bruttene
Custance hauede his quene a child heom wes imene
Þa þat child wes iboren God sulf hit hauede icoren
þerfore wes al bliþe þat wunede inne Bruttene
Þa comen tosomne weorldseli men
heo funden þat child nome swiþe hende
heo luueden his licame and ȝeuen him his fader nome
Custaz hæhte þe king and Costantin hæhte þat child
þe lef wes on heorten alle Brutlonden
his moder Elene wæs þisses londes quene
Þat child wæx and wel iþæh Godes mildce him wes neh
Bruttes him weoren liþe and he hom luuede swiþe
heo weoren his moder cunnesmen icomen heo wes of Brutten
 and Custanz his fader inne Rome wes iuostred
Al þat þet child mid æȝen isæh al hit to bæh
Þeo þat child wes uorþ iuæred and wes of twealf ȝere
nes na man i þis ærd þat weore of heorten swa hærd 
Þene Costantin wes wraþ ne dursten na mon speken him wiþ
 and þenne he wes bliþe he wes uule liþe
Swiþe he luuede alcne cniht þe wæs leof to deme riht
 and his Bruttisce cun swiþe hine bihoȝeden
 and his Romanisce cun wurþliche him radde
Þa þat child wes of þrittene ȝere þa iwærþ his fader vnueren
þat wes þe utemesten ræd þat Custance þe king iwærþ dæd
 and Bruttus nome þat child and makeden heom þerof anne king
 and Costantin þe ȝunge king mid wisdome heold þis lond
swulc he weore an æld kingen alre baldest
Þa wes a þen ilke time a kæisere inne Rome
he wes ihæten Maxenz þe Wurse hine luuede
þat wes þe forcuþþeste mon þe quic wes on liue
Al Rome he fordude þurh his muchele misbode
alle þa heȝe men he hatede to dæþe
 and alle þa hæne mid harme he igrætte
Þer weoren monie i Rome riche and wel idone
þe bilæfden al þat leoden and fluȝen of þan londe
for þan scamen and for þan bisemare þe heom dude þe kæisere
 and comen to þissen londe to Costantine þan kinge
 and menden to him heore sær and heore sorhsiþes
 and þan vnimete scome and þenne muche grome
þe Maxenz heom hæuede idon and idriuen of heore londe
For nusten heo nenne king þe heo mihten to kennen
swa heo mihten to Costantine for he wes of heore cunne
Ȝeorne heo hine beden þat he heom scolden ræden
hu heo mihten awræken heore wansiþes
vppe Maxenze þe heore monscipe hæfde auælled
Swa longe heo ræd ȝeornden þat he heom ræd ȝette
þat he wolde riden wiþ ræiȝere strengþe
forþ into Rome and þa riche biwinnen
 and wreken heom on Maxenz þe his cun hæfde iscænd
 and Costantin þe king gode gaderede uærde
vnimete folc monianes cunnes
Þe king gon to riden touward Romleoden
þat he com to Rome mid ræȝere strengþe
Þe king wes swiþe god cniht and he ȝarkede his fiht
 and he Maxenz ofsloh þer wes blisse inoh
þa weoren Romleoden bliþen on heore þeoden 
Þa wes Costantin þe king kæisere of Rome
and þer wes Elene þe halie quene and hire þreo æmmes
þe ældeste hæhte Leonin Trahern and Marin
þe eorles weoren wel idone Costantin heom bitæhte Rome
to ræden þa leden to dihten þere þeoden
 and þa læuedi Ælene þa halie quene
to Ierusalem wende mid richere genge
 and spæc wiþ þan elde of þan Iudean þe weoren balde
 and heo heom bihehte swiþe muche æhte
þat heo hire scolden ræden to vinden þa Rode
þe Crist ure Lauerd alisden on þes middelærd
Þeo Iudeus heo sohten and þere quene heo itæhten
Þa wes heo swa bliþe swa heo nes neuere ær on liue
 and heo vele ȝere þurh þan wunede þere
þe while hire æem Leonin wes in Rome mid Costantin
Of þan broþeren he wes ældest of wisdome alre selest
nomen þa Romwisen and wimman him ȝeuen
of þan hehste cunne of Romanisce monnen
Þa wifman wes biwedded and Leonin heo hæfde to his bedde
he dude alse hit is wune he streonede hire on enne sone
Þa þat child wes iboren þa funden heo him hehne nome
heo hehten hine forþriht anan þene hæȝe Maximian
 and Costantin þe king luuede swiþe þat child
Þus hit ferde þære wurs hit ferde here
Þa wes inne Walsce londe a duc þe wes swiþe strong
Octaues he hehte he wes of heȝe cunne
he cleopede to Brutlonde þat hit wes his icunde
 and al þat þe sæ bigæþ Octaues wes swiþe mah
he nom muchele uærde and wenden ȝeond þissen ærde
ærst he sloh þæ eorles and þrallede þæ chærles
he heomelede þa reuen nalde he nænne bilefuen
al þis kineliche lond Octauus nom to his hond
Þis word com to Costantin in Rome þer he wunede in
hu Octauus hauede idon his folc islaȝen and ihon
Særi wes þa Costantin and sorhful an heorte
for he ne mihte nanes weies cumen to þissere kineriche
for he hauede al Romelond þe stod an his aȝere hond 
 and his moder Elene him hafde isend æfter
Þa nom he Traher his æm and tæhte hine to rade
 and þis lond him bitahte biwinnen ȝef he hit mahte
for himseolf Costantin ne com he naueremare herin
Ah he nom folc and æhte and Traher bitehte
mid muchelere uerde sende hine to þissen ærde
 and for he wes his moder æm ȝef he mihte Octauus slæn
 and he mihte swa wel don halde himseolf þisne dom
Traher forþ wende toward þissen londe
mid ferde mid þan mæste he com to Portchæstre
Þa Bruttes weoren swiþe whæte and heolden fæsten heore ȝæte
 and Traher heom fæht wiþ and þæne þridde dæi heo ȝerden griþ
 and Traher ferde binnen and Portchæstre wes biwunne
 and þonnene he gon wende riht to Winchæstre
 and Octauus wes icumen biuoren into þære burhȝe
Togædere heo comen heo fæhten and sloȝen
þat slæht ne mihte na mare beon i fihte
He isæh his muchelne lure and nom him oþerne cure
 and ferde bi nihte to þære sæ rihte
Ær Bruttes hit mihten iwiten his ferde wes al iscipen
 and forþ heo gunnen wenden i Scotlonde
 and he al Scotlond iwon to his aȝere hond
 and he wende ouer Humbre mid hæhȝere strengþe
 and in þissere Bruttene burȝes he aweste
Octauus þat iherde þe king wes an ærde
 and he mid his folke þiderward fusde
togadere heo comen and fuhten ful sone
Nu hæfde Traher swiþe muchel folc þer
Scottes and Peohtes and Romanisce cnihtes
Traher feht wiþ Octaues and he hine sone ouercom
Scottes huuen up muchelne ræm and Octaues folc nam flem
 and Romanisce beornes sloȝen þa Bruttes
Þa wes Octaues wa and he wende to þere sæ
bi þere sæstronde þer he scipen funde
into þane scipen he laþ and into Norwæiȝe he draf
Nafde he of his fihte bute an and þritti cnihtes
 and alle þa oþere weoren inomen and Traheres men bicumen
 and fiftene þusend islæȝen and idon of heore lifdaȝen
Þa wes in Norweoȝen ærd a king þe hæhte Compert 
Octaues him spæc wiþ and ȝernde mildeliche his griþ
 and seide him hu Traher mid teone hine hauede iflæmed
 and ȝif þu me wult wlsten mid muchele þine ferden
þat ich maȝen aȝæn cumen to mine kineriche
ich þe wulle luuien and halden þe for lauerd
mid sæhte and mid sibbe þa while þat ich libbe
 and after mine dæiȝen mine duȝeþe þe bitachen
Þa ænswærede Compert þe king wes of þan ærd
Þu sælt in þisse ȝere beon mid me hære
 and deornliche sende into Brutlonde
mid weorden and mid writen bi monnen þe heom cunnen witen
 and senden þine sonden to þine bezste freonden
bihæten seoluer and gold muchel æhte and lond
ȝif ai mon mihte Traher king tuhten to dæþe
mid drenche oþer mid dweomerlace oþer mid steles bite
oþer mid æie crafte biwinnen him his mahte
þenne mihtes þu aȝen faren mucle þe lasse weoren þi kare
þenne wlle I þe aȝan bringen and makien þe to kingen
Al dude Octaues Compertes lare
sende his sonde into þisse londe
þurh þan ilke crafte þe Compert king him tæhte
 and Traher wes on Bruttene king swiþe bliþe
næfde he of Octaue caræ næuer nane
na mare þeh he nære iboren oþer i watere forloren
Traher wes i Lundene bliþe mid his leoden
fulle seouen nihte bliþe mid his cnihten
Þa wes i Kent an eorl Aldolf ihaten
feond he wes þes kinges for Octaues þingen
ofte he ferde to þan kinge and hernede tiþinge
Chæpmen bunden heore ware þa wolde þe king faren
Aldolf ferde him biforen mid feower hundred cnihten
 and leop ut of ane wude wunder wel iwepned
Traher king he þer fond and mid spere hine stong
 and his muchele uerde sette to fleonde
 and Aldolf heom after droh and muchel folc he þer ofsloh
 and seþþen he uerde into Kent into ane stronge castle
 and sende an hiȝinge after Octaue þan kinge
 and he anan com to þissere kineriche
to kinge he wes vnderfon þa þuhte hit him wel idon
Heo ferde ȝeond þas þeoden and sloh þa Romleoden 
þa hæhne and þa riche alle heo sloh iliche
wharswa he mihte hine kennen ne læuede he nauer ænne
 and twa and twenti ȝere he wuneden seoþþen here
inne griþe and inne friþe mid freondscipe of Brutten
Þa þe he wes wel ald mon þa com him uuel on
þat vuel hine heold stronge ah he þreowede longe
Þe king hine biþohte what he don mihte
wham he mihte bitæchen al his kineriche
and al his duȝeþe æfter his dæie
Mid carte he for to Lundene and sette his hustinge
eorles þer comen riche and wel idone
 and alle þa wise þe wuneden on Bruttene
Þa þe king heom hauede isæid and bæd heom ræden him ræd
whæm he mihte bitæche al his kineriche
for nefde he nenne sune þe his land mihte halden
ne child bute ane dohter þe him wes swiþe deore
 and hire he wolde bitachen al his kineriche
 and ȝefuen hire lauerd þene hæhste mon of þis ærd
Summe him ræden anan þat heo ȝeuen þan eorle Conan
he wes wis and riche him heo mihte bitæche
oþere þer weoren þe þis nalden ihæren
I Cornwale wes an eorl god þe wes ihaten Cradoc
he stod up i þan hustinge and þus spæc wiþ þan kinge
Hercne me Octaue hercne me kinelauerd
No here ich nenne godne ræd þe þe ȝet beo isæd
Ȝif þu bitachest Conan þine kineriche
þat word comeþ sone vorþ into Rome
For nu is Ælene Ierusalem quene
 and þe king Costantin and alle his cnihtes mid him
 and dæd his þe riche Leonin and his broþer Marin
 and Maximien þe ȝunge cniht i Rome haldeþ muchel fiht
 and Traher i þisse londe mid spere wes ofstungen
 and ælche dæi inne Rome Maximien þe wel idone
haldeþ swiþe muchel iwin wiþ Gracien and wiþ Valantin
 and Costantin þe king of us ne þencheþ naþing
 and þus we beoþ of Bruttene freonden biræued
Bute þu wisliche bitæche þine kineriche
wulleþ Romleode cumen to þissere þeode 
 and foruaren vs mid fehte and ure freond ivallen
 and maken vnsæhte and binimen us ure irihten
Þenne þu beost forþfaren ne beon we næuere buten caren
Ah send into Rome æfter Maximien þan wel idone
he is swiþe hende gume and he wes Leonines sune
his fader wes Ælenen æm he is of aþele cunne
 and ȝif him þine dohter þa þe is swiþe deore
 and make hine to kinge and þine dohter to quene
þenne maȝe we libben mid sæhte and mid sibben
 and a to ure liue witen ure leoden
mid winne and mid wurþscipe mid muchele wisdome
Þa aras Conan and stod biuoren þan kinge
he wes wunderliche wraþ for þeos speche him wes laþ
he spæc aȝen Cradoc alse he hine wolde fordon
Ah ne rohte næuere Cradoc of al þat Conan eorl spæc
for al þat hustinge þe wes biuoren þan kinge
biluueden Cradockes ræd for heo iseȝen þat hit wes neod
Þa cleopede Octaues Brutlondes lauerd
Hail seo þu Caradoc
Herfore þu scælt habben wurhscipe muchele
Læn me Mauric þinne sune þe is a swiþe wis gume
to uaren a mire neode into Romþeode
æfter Maximiane þane richen and þane kene
þæt he cume swiþe þe while þe ich beo on liue
and ich him wulle bitæchen mine kineriche
and mine dohter Orien to habben to quene
 and ic wulle Maurike mede bitæchen
ich ȝeue him Norhhumberlond here mid mire aȝere hond
þis ich him bitæchen of mine kineriche
wiþ þan þe he me bringe Maximien þæ hende
Al swa þe king ȝirde Mauric hit him ȝette
he ferde uorþrihtes mid þreom wise cnihtes
þat he com to Rome to Maximiene
Þer wes muchel vnfriþ in al þan londe nas na griþ
ah mid vnfriþe þer wes muchel win mid Gracien and mid Ualantin
Heo duden Maximiene vnimete teone
muchel lond heo hæfden binomen ære þider come Maurich þe gume
Sone swa Maximiane isæh swa he him to bæh
 and fæire hine igrætte mid guþfulle worden 
 and he iradliche lædde hine to ræde
 and he þus spæc wunderliche feire
Hercne Maximian þu ært of muche cunne
þu weore Elene æmes sune of hæhȝe cunne þu ært icumen
Ær ich hider uore nis nawhit ȝære
Octaues ure king i Lundene heold his husting
þat hustinge wes god hit wes witeneimot
vnhæle and ælde hæueþ þene king vnbalded
Þer wes moni cniht god and þe king heom æxede ræd
wham he mihte bitæchen his dohter and his riche
 and alle his doȝeþe æfter his dæie
Þreo eorles anan icure þe eorl Canaan
þat me sculde him Brutlond bitachen al on his hond
 and þa fæire Oriene þes kinges dohter to quene
Conanes eorldom Kent is ihaten
 and mi fader is an icorren eorl Cornwalen lauerd
he is ihaten Caradoc he is of þine cunne
 and ich hatte Mauric þe mæste of his childeren
Þa heo hæfden anan þus icoren Conan
þa lep mi fader up swulc hit an liun weore
 and wiþseide þene cure biforen ure kinge
Þer wes swiþe muchel dune þeines þer dremden
 and mi fader Caredoc makede lust and þus spæc
While wes Elene Custances quene
Ælene hæfde enne æm þe æþele wes on londe
he wes ihaten Leonin uorþ he ferde mid Costantin
Traher hæhte his broþer and Marin þe oþer
Traher i þissen londe wes islæȝen mid wornge
Conanes fader hine sloh þat wes swiþe muchel woh
for Traher king wende þat heo weoren ifreonde
Lusteþ wel Bruttes þe her beoþ bihælues
Leonin hadde ænne sune and inne Rome he wuneþ
Maximien he hatte of þan aþele cunne
Sende we to Rome and haten hine cumen some
 and in ure hustinge hæhuen hine to kinge
 and þa feire Oriene bithæchen him to quene
þenne maȝen we libben mid sæhten and mid sibben
Þus spæc mi fader Caradoc biforen þan folke
Þa andswerede þe king hit wes him swiþe iqueme
 and alle his beornen þe wunieþ on Brutene 
bute Conaan wes swiþe wræþ for þe cure him wes læþ
Cleope nu to ræde þine rædȝiuen gode
 and sæie me her of andswere for nu tomarwen ich wulle faren
Þa wes Maximien for þisse worde swiþe fæin
he cleopede his rædȝiuen and eoden to rune
þe ræd wes sone iræd al swa Mauric hit bad
Stille iwende sone Maximien of Rome
i þan seouennihte mid alle his cnihten
wenden þa Romleoden þat he wolde to heore vnneode
þat he wolden fehten aȝan Valentin and Gracian
for a heo weoren auared of Maximian and of his hirede
Ah anan heo wende toward þissen londe
 and swa he gon liþen into Londenne
fairlac he gon bringe Octaue þan kingen
 and þe king him forȝef his dohter to quene
Þa wes king Maximien hit þuhte Bruttes idon wel
 and Conaan eorl mid wraþþen wende to Scotten
 and monie Scottes him buȝen to and ane burh bigunnen
næs þa in al þan ende burh al swa hende
Þa þeo burh wes al imaked mid muchelere strengþe
he sette hire æne nome æfter himseoluen
ofte he ræd hire þurh and þurh and hehte heo Cuningesburh
nu and æueremare þe nome stondeþ þere
Conaan ledde ferde in þan norþ ærde
he hatede Maximien þat abohte moni mon
Þa wise men of þisse londe þe luueden þas leoden
makeden hustinge bitwexen Conaan and þan kinge
þer heo iwurþen sæhte and þer heo iwurþen somme
 and makede i þissen londe griþ god mid þan bezste
 and þe king him bihæhte anan to makiene riche mon
swa he dude seoþþen þet abohte moni mon
mid griþe he wuneden here fulle fif ȝere
Þa hefde Maximien gærsume vnimete
for he næfde of his londe na gauel isende to Rome
Þa þe fif ȝer weoren agan þa sæide Maximian
þat he wolde ouer sæ uaren and fehten wiþ þan Frenscen
 and ȝif he þere mihte speden toward Rome he wolde riden
to wreken his teone on Gracien and on Valentin 
þe monie him hæfden idone teonen inne Rome
Þus spæc Maximien uor him wes to murie
for þis lond wes þa swiþe god and he hit hæfde al vnder fot
 and him ne stod æie to naþing for dæd wes Octaues þe king
Maximien bæd ferde feorliche store
þe king hafde kene men and vnimete gærsume
forþ he gon wenden ut of þissen londen
forþ he gon liþen ut þissen leoden
he makede himseluen muchel clond ne isæh he nauere æft þis lond
Ouer sæ he wende and wel com to londe
in ane londe swiþe riche þe hehte Armoriche
Þa scipen urnen a þen lond þat folc wenden uppe strond
Heo bigunnen ænne castel god mid þan bæzsten
heo riden ȝeond þæn leode and nomen þer muchele prude
heo funden herrefeng inoh and lædden to heore ferde
 and æc heo nomen wummen wunder ane monie
 and duden þat heo wolden ȝeond Ærmoriche londe
Þis iherde Humbald þe wes lauerd i þa lond
hu þe king Mæximien amerde his riche
Humbald sende sonde ȝeond al þan londen
þer he æine freond hæfde þe him helpen wolde
 and þohte þat he wælde heom driuen of his londe
Heo comen bi dæielihte to ane stronge fihte
Bruttes heom ouercomen and Humbald heo sloȝen
 and fiftene þusende þer weoren islaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
Þa þis feht wes idon þa wende Maximien
aȝen into herberȝe to resten hine seolue
Amarȝen þa hit dæi wes duȝeþen heom gereden
heo wenden to þere heȝe burh þe Nantes is ihaten
ne funden heo þerinne noht of moncunne
þe heom wiþ wolde stonden and þa burh heolden
al hit wæs awæi ifloȝen and of þan londe iboȝen
buten a lute wifmen þe weoren þer wiþinnen
Þa burh nom Maximien and sette mid his monnen
þeo cleopede Maximien to þan eorle Conaan
Conaan þu ært god cniht þu hæfuest ihalden wel mi fiht
 and ich þe wulle mede muchele bitæche
for þu hæfdest al Brutlond i þire aȝere hond 
ȝif ich hit nere þu weore king þere
and þe eorl Caredoc þe is of mine cunne
ȝet hit mai ilimpe hit is þe an vnþonke
Ah loke wulche wætres and wunliche londes
whulche wurþliche wude whulche wilde deores
whulche liþe londe on to libbenne
Þis lond hehten Armoriche þis ich þe bitæche
 and muchele mare herto ȝif ich hit mæi ifo
herof þu scalt beon king and þas riche aȝen
Vt ich wullen driuen al þat ich finde on liue
ȝungen and alde vt of þisse londe
and wulcne swa ich mai here ifon i þan stude he beoþ fordon
 and sende ich wulle to Aþionærd þe is min aȝene stiward
eorl he is treowe for æuer he is aþneowe
for him ich habbe wel bitæht Brutlond to witene
 and he me scal senden into þisse londe
wapmen and wifmen of wel feole cræften
cnihtes and þeines and al heore sweines
sixti hundred cnihten þe gode beon to fihten
ten hundred þeines seoue þusend sweines
seoue þusend burhmen þe sæle beon on æhte
þritti þusend wifmen þe wel beon ifunden
Þenne þis folc biþ hider icumen and heo stude habbeþ inumen
þenne biþ al þis fæire lond iset Brutten an hond
æfter þine leoden bitæche heom name
Brutlond þat lasse
Nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere
 and þus Armoriche nome niþer wes auælled
swa þat næueremare ne biþ he aræred
Conaan þeos ȝeue afeng and iwraþ þeos kinges freond
mid muchelere wurþscipe and wel heo hit heolden
And þe king sende into þisse londe
 and hæhte Aþionard þe biwuste Brutlondes ærd
þat he him swiþe sende þat folc of Brutlonde
 and folc of ælche cræfte sundri scipen bitæhte
 and mong þan wifmonnen wepmon næuer enne
buten þa seoluen scipmen þe heom scullen læden
Al eoden þeos ræd swa þe king hæfde iseid
 and Conaan þer heold to mid hæhȝere strengþe 
 and þe king ferde uorþ toward France
 and biȝæt al þat kinelond and sette hit on his aȝere hond
 and þeonne he gon liþen into Lohernne
al þat lond he biȝæt swa he dude Liuieine æc
swa he gon liþe into Lumbardie
al þat lond he biȝæt þær wes Caradoc dæd
þa hauede Mauric his sune sorȝen inowe
nes þer nan oþer ræd buten þe Mavric iwærþ dæd
To Rome wende Maximiæn uppe Valentin and vppen Gracien
i fehte he nom þene oþer þa ȝirnde griþ þa oþer
Cnihtes heo weoren hende þe king heom dude i bende
 and he anan sone ahnede al Rome
Þat word com to Conaan hu iuaren hafde Maximiæn
 and þat Caradoc wes dæd inne Lumbardie
 and alswa Mauric his sune for muchele sarinesse
Þa nom þe eorl Conaan ænne swiþe wisne mon
 and sende to þissen londe to Adionard þan stronge
þe wes stiward swiþe bisi inne þisse Bruttene
To Adionard me brohten writ þat dæd wes his broþer
Caradoc þe mære and Mauric his sune deore
þa næfde Caradoc i þis ærd broþer bute Adionard
 and he forþriht nom an his hond al Caradokes lond
Þa iherden þa Frence men þat at Rome wes Maximien
 and Cradoc wes dæd þa nomen þa Frence ænne ræd
þat heo wolden flæme Conaan þene kene
vt of þan londe þe Maximian him ȝæf an honde
þe is bihalues France and Bruttaine is ihaten
 and Conaan ne ȝirnde na griþ ah festliche heom feht wiþ
 and wel he makede his castles treowe and swiþe uæste
 and alle his beornen he wes leof þe comen of þissen londe
For alle he hæfde þa cnihtes þe Maximien him bihehte
 and ec þa eorles and þa sweines and þa cheorles
 and alle þa burhmen þa him bihehte Maximien
Wifmen neuede he noht feole buten fiftene hundred
for wifmen nolden noht liþen vt of þissen londe
buten þe eorl Adionard þe wes þe hæhste i þis ærd
walde heore borh beon þat heo scolden heore while wel biteon
Þa hæhuede Adionard ænne dohter swiþe deore
heo hæfde al þat hæreword of þan maidenen of þis ærd
þeo wimman wes on sele heo hæhte Vrsele 
Conaan sende to þis ærd to þan eorle Adionærd
 and bed þat he him ȝeue his dohter to quene
Adionard ȝæf andswere wurþscipe habbe he þerfore
Monscipe habbe Conaan þat he mire dohter wel on
Nu todæi a seouen nihten ich heo senden him bi mine cnihten
 and alle þa wimmen þe him ȝef mi lauerd Maximien
þider heo scullen liþen ȝif heo wulleþ libben
oþer ich heom wullen alle fordon and bi þan titten anhon
Þa ȝarkede Adionard þisses londes lauerd
his dohter Ursæle þe wimman wes wel sæle
he þohte heo to sende ouer sæstrames
into Bruttaine londe to Conaan þan stronge
Þa iherden þa wimmen wide ȝeond þas Bruttene
þat me wolde senden Vrsele to þan londe
hire comen to inoȝe monie and vnifoȝe
þat wolden mid hire uaren to þan kinge Conaane
swiþe feole heo bisohte ma þeone heo rohten
Þa þe dæi wes icumen þe Adionard hafde inumen
þat forþ scolde uaren þat mæiden Vresele
þa hafden to iwiten seouen and twenti scepen
alle heo weoren isunde i þere burh of Lunden
Inne þere Temese heo teuhten heore seiles
wind heo hæfden wunsum weder mid þan bezsten
 and heo seileden forþ þat inne sæ heo comen
þa vmbe stunde ne sæȝe heo noht of londe
Þa aras heom a wind a þere wiþer side
swurken vnder sunnen sweorte weolcnen
haȝel and ræin þer aræs þe hit iseh him agras
vþen þer urnen tunes swulche þer burnen
bordes þer breken vimmen gunnen wepen
Þa scipen þa urnen biuoren twelue þer weoren forloren
þa oþere weoren al todriuen and forþ mid þere sæ iliþen
nes þer na steoresmon þat æuere aht cuþe þeron
Nes næuere na mon iboren ne of nane londe icoren
þat hæleþ weore swa stærc ne swa hærdiheorted
þe iherde þesne weop and þisne wunderliche ræm
 and cleopien to þan halhȝen mid hæhȝere steuene
þat his heorte neore særi for þan vnimete sorhȝen
Seoþþen þis world wes astald and monnen an honde isælde 
ne com nauere wurse hap to nane wummannen
Summe þe scipen wunden forþ mid þan wederen
fulle fiftene i þan ane wes Vrsele
þe sæ wes wunder ane wod and ladliche iwraþþed
 and þa scipen i þere wildere sæ
æuere norþ forþriht þreo dæies and þreo niht
Þa weoren ut of Norweiȝen tweien eorles iuaren
Mælgam and Wanis heo weoren kene ful iwis
of Denemarke and of Norweiȝe heo weoren iqueþen vtlaȝen
 and heo ferden bi sæsiden vnimete wide
Heo icneowen wel a þan wolcnen þas wederes custes
heo droȝen to ane aitlonde þer heo leoþe hafueden
Wanis wes in Hungrie þer he harm worhte
Mælga wes inne Scise þer he scaþe makede
þat he ne mihte i þan londe na lengere atstonde
 and of Norweiȝe iflemed þer heo fiht þoleden
 and inne sæ heo weoren iuaren uulle seoue ȝeren
 and swa heo leien i þan æitlonde and iseȝen þat weder stronge
iseȝen scipen an and an while ma while nan
þeonne feowere þenne fiue sellic heom þuhten a þissen liue
whæt weoren þa ȝemere scipen þa ȝeond þa sæ weolken
Þe wind gon aliþen and þat weder leoþede
 and Wanis isæh i þere sæ þa scipen wandrien
 and þus spæc þere wiþ Malgan his iuere
Forþ wit nu swuþe and after heom biliue
mid gode fiftene scipen faren we heom æfter
mid ure bezste cnihten þe gode beon to fihten
 and leten ælle ure oþere scipen ure herberwe biwiten
for þis is sum riche king rædes bidæled
þe wolde mid his folke uaren to summe londe
 and haueþ þeos wind and þeos weder awider him istonden
þat wa is him aliue Nu wende we him to biliue
 and ȝif hit wule Appolin þat is deore lauerd min
þat we maȝen mid fihte biwinnen hine and his cnihtes
 and heo ne beon of ure laȝen we scullen him don of lifdæȝen
 and swa we scullen nimen a hond heore seoluer and heore gold
 and faren to ure inne and ȝeolpen for þere winne
Forþ heo wenden mid flode fiftene scipen gode
þe strengeste þe weoren a þan dæȝen and fulled mid utlaȝen 
 and anan oftoken fif scipen of wimmonnen afulled
Seolcuþ heom þuhte what hit beon mahte
 and heo cleopeden heom on nes þer nan ændswere
for al weoren þa wimmen awald to þan deþe
To heom heo droȝen and þas fif scipen nomen
and furþer heo iwenden and niȝene heo iuengen
and heo mid þan feowertene scipen ferden to þan londe
Seoþþen þis worlde wes astald nes hit neowhær itald
on songe no on spelle ne miþte hit na mon telle
þat weoren æi wimman swa wræcchelichen atoȝene
ne swa reoliche inne sæ forradde
Melga nom Vrsele þa scolden beon quene
 and scome hire bihedde and ladde heo to his bedde
Þa þe heþene mon hæfuede on hire his wille idon
he ȝæf heo his hiredmonnen sone to makien to heore
 and summe heo heom salden for seoluer and for gold
 and monie and vnifoȝe heo þer ofsloȝen
 and summe heo heom drengte in þere sæ deope
 and summe heo Godd wiþsoken and to haþenescipe token
 and þus heo weoren forradde mid reowþe þan mæste
Melga and Wanis ihurden suggen ful iwis
þat þas Bruttene wes of cnihte bidæled
for Conaan hauede swiþe monie ilæd to Armoriche
 and Maximiæn ladde to Rome monie and wel idone
swa wes þis kinelond of folke swiþe vnstrong
Melga and Wanis iwenden into Scotten
þat lond heo þurh arnden and herȝeden and barnden
þa ahte heo nomen þat folc heo ofsloȝen
 and swa heo wenden hiderward ouer þere Humber
hermes heo worhten and hene lond makeden
Þis iherden Bruttes and weoren þerfore særi
heore sonde heo nomen sone and senden touward Rome
Heo grætten Maximian and talden him of Melgan
 and of Wanis his iuere whet heo duden here
 and beden hine heom ræden oþer ælles heo weoren dæde
Maximien wes sari for swulche tiþende
 and anan dude ut of bende Gracien þene hende
anan swa he him to com þus he cleopede him on
Gracien bicum mi mon and þu scelt seoþþen wel don
 and ich þe wullen senden into Brutlonde 
ich wulle al þat kinelond bitechen þe a þire hond
 and þu scalt beon mi stiward swa wes þe eorl Adionard
 and ȝif þu wult wel don ich wulle þe makien riche mon
and driuen of mire þeoden vncuþe leoden
Þa andswerede Gracien mid griþfulle worden
Al ich wulle wurchen after þine willen
liþen wuderswa þu wult and halden þe for lauerd
Þe aþes weoren isworene and æft heo weoren forlorene
Maximien þe keisere bæd swiþe muchelne here
 and he chæs of þan iwihte ten þusend cnihten
 and makede Gracien gumene ælder
 and swa heo gunnen wenden into þissen londe
 and her he fæht ful iwis wiþ Melga and wiþ Wanis
þat wes swiþe wel idon þat he heo æt compe ouercom
 and draf heom ouer sæstronde into Yrlonde
 and seoþþen ferde ȝeond þis lond swa him wes alre leofuest
 and þe kæisere Maximiæn inne Rome wes hæh mon
 and hæuede Valentin wel uaste biclused in ane castle
Þa hefde Valentin and Gracien inne Rome muchel cun
 and iseȝen þene enne broþer idæled from þen oþer
Heo senden heore sonde into Puille londe
 and heo senden to Gradie þan Duc of Lumbardie
 and into Alemaine to aþelen þan folke
and into feole londe þæ læien þerabeoten
 and beden of heore ærde alle gaderen værde
 and to ane isette dæie sone cumen abeoten Rome
 and wreken uppen Maximien Valentin and Gratien
Herof nuste naþing Maximien þe riche king
ah he wunede inne Rome mid muchele richedome
Vmbe lutle virste þa comen þa uerden
al abeoten Rome riden seouen kinges
heo tobreken Rome wal and eoden in oueral
Rome burh heo nomen and Maximien heo sloȝen
 and duden vt Valentin and alle his iueren mid him
of þan stronge castle and keiser hine makede
 and nomen heore sonde and senden to þisse londe
 and senden Gratien word whæt þer wes iwurþen
 and Gratien forþriht anan ahnede þisne kinedom
þisne kinedom haueden Gratien þe ær ahte Maximien
 and Valentin of Rome ahte þa riche 
Þus riht þurh swulne ræd wes Maximien dæd
and Gracien wes king her þat wes cuþ wel iwar
Wiþinnen ane ȝere nes þer first namare
iwraþ þe king Gracien gumene forcuþest
al he foruerde þis lond þa leoden him weoren laþe
þa riche he foruerde þa wræcche he drof of ærde
ne durste þa riche þeines nowhær him cumen toȝeines
ah alle heo hine fluȝen and alle heo hine bibuȝen
Þa weoren in Æst Ængle aþele iborene cheorles
twene ibroþeren itwinnes heo weoren
þe oþer hehte Eþelbald and þe oþer Ælfwald
Heo isehȝen on feole studen hou þe king þis lond fordude
Þas cheorles heom biþohten whæt heo don mihten
 and speken heom ful stille þat þene king heo walden quellen
 and senden in Æst Ængle wide ȝeond þan londe
 and sumnede on ærde seouen hundred cheorles
 and seiden þurh alle þing þat heo walden bisechen þene king
 and bidden hine mildce þurh þene milde Godd
þat he þurh his mihte heolde heom to rihte
Ah Ælfwald and his broþer al heo þuhten oþer
heo uerden swiþe warliche mid wunsumme lades
 and ælc bær an honde ænne saȝel stronge
and bisiden heo gunnen heongen cniues swiþe longe
vnder heore barme to scilden heom wiþ hærme
 and swa heo forþ ferden alle isunde
 and vmben are mile heo ræsten ane while
 and auerælcne hiredgume feire heo igrætten
 and mildeliche þurh alle þing fræineden whær weoren þe king
 and hiredmen heom tahten whær heo hine finden mæhten
whær he wes in anne wude in ane wilderne
 and æfter ane bare he hine abohte ful sære
Þa cheorles wenden to þan wuden and warliche heom hudden
alle bute tweien toward þan kinge heo weoren beien
and iuunden þene king þær he wes an slæting
 and him to cleopeden quickere stæuene
Hiderward lauerd king we þe wulleþ cuþen a wunderlic þing
of ane swulche bare þe her is bihalues
vnder ane berhȝe þer he burh hafueþ ichosen
ne iherde we næuere on liue tellen of swulche swine
ȝif þu þider wult riden þer he þe abideþ 
Þerfore wes þe king glad and þiderwærd wes swiþe ræd
 and þa cheorles him biuoren beien togædere
Þa cheorles up þreowen þene king heo icneowen
 and heo hine niþer setten and al hine toheowen
Þus Gratien þe king for ut an slæting
Sone hit wes oueral iseid þat þe luþere king wes dæd
þa weoren inne Bruttene blissen inowe
ah sone þeræfter sorȝen heom weoren ȝiueþen
Þa wes æuerælc cheorl al swa bald alse an eorl
 and alle þa gadelinges alse heo weoren sunen kinges
Þis word com to wel iwhare hu þe king wes iuaren
comen sæliþende men uorþ into Irlonde
 and funden þer ful iwis Melga and Wanis
 and talden heom tiþende al of þissen londe
hu hit al wes iuaren and þat cheorles næfden nane kare
 and hefden al þis kinelond iset a cheorlene hond
Þa weoren glade ful iwis Melga and Wanis
 and seiden þat heo walden toward þissen londe
Mid muchelere uerde heo comen to þissen ærde
heo hæfden of Gutlonde utlaȝen stronge
of Neorewæi and of Denemarke men swiþe starke
 and of Yrlonde Gillemaur þene stronge
of Scottene heo hafden alle þa hæhsten
 and of Galeweoþe gumen swiþe kene
 and swa heo gunnen wenden ut to Norþhumberlonde
ahten heo nomen folc heo þer sloȝen
castles heo ararden and ahneden þa arde
þa burhȝen heo nomen and al þat heo neh comen
Þa iseȝen Bruttes þat balu wes on londe
nusten heo nænne ræd heo wenden alle wurþen dæd
Sonden heo nomen sone and senden toward Rome
 and beden heore are þa and aueremære
ȝif heo heom wolde helpen to hæȝere neode
a to heore liue heo walden heom liþe
 and luue to heom halden ȝif heo heom helpen wolden
Þis word wes isend bi write swiþe deore
 and þat writ wes irad imæng þan Romleden
Þa speken sone þæ wisseste of Rome
Bi vfelen iwurhten sculden we heom to wenden
for Gratien heo sloȝen his men heo forforen 
 and neoþeles we heom scullen senden ferde of þissen ærde
of þissen ænde ænne ælpi verde
Vt heo senden of Rome cnihtes wel idone
fif and twenti hundred comen into Lunden
 and buden al þa ferde of Brutlondes ærde
 and ferden forþ ful iwis to Melga and Wanis
 and heo fehten heom wiþ and sloȝen heore uerde
 and heo sulf mid ærhscipe arnden to heolte
 and letten slæn heore folc heore vnimete uerde
 and heo seolf liþden forþ biuoren Scotlonde
 and Febus heom æfter mid his Romanisce cnihten
ah heo ne mihten for nane þingen Melgan iuinden
 and heo bigunnen feorlic ane swiþe deope dich
 and þerouenon oueral ænne strongne stanene wal
bi þere sæstronde biside Scotlonde
þer weoren æuere iwuned þe vtlaȝen to londen cumen
 and seoþþe heo heom dihten to biwiten þa dich mid cnihten
Þa dic and þa wal weoren ȝare þa næfde Bruttes nane kare
aȝan heo gunnen wenden to þare burh of Lunden
 and Febus of Rome hustinge bad sone
Þer com moni riche mon to þan hustinge anan
moni cniht moni eorl moni þein moni cheorl
moni riche burhmon þer wende beon bliþe anan
þa sorhfulle weoren an heorten ær þe dæi weoren agan
Febus þe feire cniht lette beoden his ferde uorþriht
þat heo comen to hustinge mid alle heore þringe
 and þa sweines at hærberwen letten heore hors wel ȝærwen
 and makien þa heors al swa ȝare swa heo sculden forþ faren
 and al þat folc duden þus swa hit hæhte Febus
 and swa heo gunnen wenden to heore hustinge
Þa þat folc wes al icumen and ælc his stude hafde inomen
þa hehte me lusten inne Lundenne
Þa stod him up Febus þe riche cniht and seide þus
Lusteþ me nu Bruttes þe her beoþ bihalues
Ich habbe eow to suggen soþ word of Rome
Ȝe us sende sonde into ure londe
of þare sorhȝe ful iwis þe eow duden Melgan and Wanis
 and ich mid mire ferde com to þissen ærde
 and ich habbe eower iuan iualled to þan grunde
 and iflemed ut of ærde Melgan buten uærde 
Nu ȝe maȝen toȝere careles wunien here
of þare ilke uerde þe islaȝen is on ærde
Ȝe us habbeþ ofte imaked wraþ þeruore inne Rome ȝe beoþ laþ
for ofte ȝe us habbeþ athalden þat gauel of þissen londe
 and æc ȝe habbeoþ ufele idon islæȝe þene king Gratien
 and ofte ȝe us bihateþ treoþe to halden
 and æuere a þan ænde ȝe wakieþ an honde
We habbeþ for eower luuen ilosed ure leoden
cnihtes i þissen londe an hundred þusende
seoþþen Iulius Cesar ærst bicom her
ah swa we ibiden are nulle we no mare
ah we wulleþ sone uaren into Rome
 and bitachen eow þis kinelond and haldeþ hit on eowre hond
 and brukeþ hit mid wunne
for nulle we naueremare aȝan comen here
We habbeþ of þisse londe ihaued monie þusend punde
þa we habbeþ her bisoht ah heo beoþ ful deore aboht
we beoþ ofte hider ifaren mid wandreþe and mid care
 and nu ȝe maȝen wel don bisecheþ eow wepnen anan
 and werieþ eow seoluen wiþ vncuþe leoden
Neoren eower ælderen aþelene cæppen
Heonne to Rome al þat lond stod on heore aȝere hond
 and al þat lond þat heo iseȝen sone heo hit biwunne
al heo hit biwunnen mid heore ahte wæpnen
Ah makieþ in eowre londe castles swiþe stronge
and werieþ eowre þeode wiþ vncuþe leode
 and wunieþ her hal and hæil and habbeþ alle godne dæie
Þa þeos word weoren isæid þa wes her a strong ræd
næs nauere þe mon iboren inne nare burhȝe
þe auere mihte tellen þurh nane spellen
of þere muchele særinæsse þa isiȝen wes to folke
Þa weoren inne Lundenne laþliche iberen
þer wes wop þer wes rop and reoþen vnimete
þa þeo Romleoden riden toward scipene
 and Bruttes bilafden inne þisse londe
mid vnimete reoþe ne cuþe heo ræd nænne
Þas tiþinde ful iwis iherde Melga and Wanis
heo hefden ane verde of vnimete folke
 and heo gunnen wenden into Norhhumberlond 
ȝeond þat lond heo arnden and sloȝen and barnden
 and swa heo forþ wenden þat heo comen to þan walle
þeo þa Romleoden hæfden aræred
Bruttes weoren wiþinnen mid swiþe feole monnen
 and Melga wiþvten and ȝeorne wes abuten
hu he mihte aȝeinnen þat he weoren binnen
Heo ræsden to þan walle ræiȝe þeines
somned alle þa uerde feole cunnen ærde
þa dich wes swiþe wid and deop and þa ferde toleop
 and Bruttes weoren igærede and þene wal weoreden
heo scuten in heo scuten ut scalkes þer feollen
arwen fluȝen ouer wal al abuten oueral
swa þicke wes heore uæræ swulc hit haȝel wæren
þat for þa arewen ne mihte þa Bruttes ȝemen nanes fihtes
ah adun of þan walle iwenden heo alle
 and setten to fleme feondliche swiþe
 and þa oþer breken þane wal and eoden binnen oueral
 and after heo droȝen and swuþe heom sloȝen
heo sloȝen þer muchel wunder twa and fifti hundred
al of Brutten seoluen wiþuten þan Scotten
 and wiþutten þan Dænscæn þa inne þere dic bilæfden
Þus iþæh þis kinelond a þere Bruttene hond
Whæren Bruttes cnihtes icorene
ah nu heo weoren alle swiþe forlorene
ne beoþ heo neuere hæȝe buten heo hælp habben
of oþere moncunne for heo seolf ne cunne
Þus ferde ful iwis Melga and Wanis
Þa Bruttes of Lundene to Rome sende sone
beden heom swiþe cumen and don alse heo ær weoren iwuned
þat heo arædde þis lond and nomen hit al to heore hond
for heom heo hit vþen bet þane þan vncuþen
Þa ȝeuen heo þus answære Nulle we nauere þider faren
to þolien þat swinc and þat iwin aȝæn þat heþene cun
for þat is Goddes wiþersake Wanis ihaten
 and Melgan his iuere nulle we nauere cumen þere
þat is al þe ende nulle we þuder wende
anoþer halue we habbeoþ mare þene we maȝen anhebben
Nes þer nan oþer andswere and þas sonden gunnen aȝæn faren
Þa heo aȝan comen þa Bruttes from Rome
þa tiþende talden þe Romleoden heom salden 
þa wes Lundene folc mid sorȝen ibunden
Þa wes þer an ærchebiscop þat wes hali mon and god
 and mid Godde swiþe hæh Guencelin ihaten
He sende his sonde ȝeond alle Brutlonde
æfter alle þan clæreken þe Godes lare cuþen
alle þaie ihadede gumen hiȝendliche him to comen
 and heo ful sone to Lundene comen
Þus Guencelin heom spæc wiþ Mid us wunien Godes griþ
þat is on Latin ful iwis þat me sæiþ Pax vobis
 and heo him seiden forn to Et cum spiritu tuo
Þa bigon he larspæl and of gode spæc swiþe wel
A þan daȝen at Seint Pauwel wes þe ærchebiscop stol
 and wel feole ȝere þe ærchebiscopes weoren þere
ah seoþþen þa Seint Austin com hit wes to Cantuareburi idon
Nu seide Guencelin þa wes þa heolie mon
Lusteþ lauerdinges of ure tiþendes
þa þes haþene mon þe is ihaten Melgan
 and Wanis and heore uerde habbeþ ibroht wa to þissen ærde
 and wulleþ þesne Cristindom al forfaren and fordon
 and ich wulle habben leue forþ ich wulle liþen
 and ouer sæ wenden to summe hæȝe kinge
 and bidde þane hæȝe king þat hæ us hælpen þurh alle þing
 and ȝif ich mai iuinden to speken wiþ swulche kinge
þenne wulle ich wel fain cumen hidere aȝæin
oþer ælles næueremare nulle ich cummen here
 and ȝe bidden for me on eower bare cneowen
 and habbeþ alle godne dæi cumen ich wulle ȝif ich mai
Þa wes þat folc særi and sorhful on heorte
ne biden nauere Brutware an heore liue swulche care
Forþ wende Guencelin and his clærkes mid him
riht forþ to þere sæ þær heom sæl þuhten
Scipen heo þer funden and sone in wenden
 and heo ful sone ouer sæ comen
into Bruttaine þerforen heo weoren faine
þa þe king Maximien ȝæf þan eorle Conaan
ah dæd wes þa Maximiæn swa wes þe king Conaan
Ah Aldroein hæhte his sune þe wes of Conaan icumen
Brutaine þat lond he hafde al in his hond
Armoriche hæhte þat lond ah þene nome hit losede an hond 
Aldroein wes þer king vnder him wes moni hæh dring
Guencelin to þan kinge com and he hine lette wel afon
þe ærchebiscop feol to þes kinges fot and bæd hine biþenche uppen Godd
Lauerd king Aldroein ofte þe wurþe Godd fæin
Iþenc þat þu weore Conaanes sune of Brutten þu ært al icumen
Ich æm icumen to speken þe wiþ and ȝeornnen þe liues griþ
Into ure londe beoþ icumen twæine hæþene gumen
Melga and Wanis muchel ufel heo doh us
heo habbeoþ of ure londe al þene norþ ende
 and swiþe we beoþ auæred þat heo nu habben mare
 and ȝet heo þencheþ ufele don to fallen þæne Cristindom
 and turne to heþenesse þa hæȝe and þa læsse
For þi fader nom of Brutlonde alle þa cnihtes stronge
 and moni þusend ladde to Rome Maximien þe wel idone
 and nu liggeþ ofslaȝen þa heo bilæfden an ure daȝen
 and þus is Brutlonddes ærd of folke bidæled
Sonde we sende to Rome and beden þat heo comen
and heo us habbeoþ word isend bi vre sondmonnen
þat we don þat bezste þat we muȝen for nulleþ heo nauermare cumen
ah hateþ us biwinnen hælp ȝif we cunnen
 and habbeþ iqueþen us scere nu and aueremare
Ah wel mæi don hu hit ga for wræcches we beoþ æuerema
Whilen weoren Bruttes þa bezste men of londe
al þat heo bigunnen al heo hit biwunnen
Nu heo beoþ ouercumen æiþer islaȝen and inomen
 and awæi ivaren mid Maximian and mid þi uader Conaan
þat nis þer bileued wel neh nan þat auere beo æi tale on
Ah þu ært of ure cunne of us naue þu nane sunne
help us nu for þu miht ælles we habbeoþ muchel pliht
Þus spæc þe ærchebiscop þat Aldroein king hit vnderstod
þe king gon siche sare him gunnen glide teores
 and urnen his æȝene þat his hiredmen hit iseȝen
Þa ȝæf þe king andswære and wiþ Guencelin he spæc þus þere
Ich eow wulle helpen mid hæȝere strengþe
ich þe wullen bitæchen twa þusend cnihtes
þat scullen beon þa bezste þæ wunieþ inne Brutene
 and Costantin minne broþer swulcne nat ich nænne oþer
swa wid swa is pes dæiliht nat ich nenne betere cnihte 
ne nat ich a wærulderiche cniht his iliche
makieþ hine lauerd ouer al Brutlondes ærd
Þa axede Aldroein þe king his deore broþer Costantin
 and he forþrihtes bitahte him þa cnihtes
Forþ ferde Costantin and þe ærchebiscop mid him
 and þe king himseolf walde uaren ah of Frensce monnen he hæfde kare
Hiderward wende Costantin þe hende
and al his uerde isund at Totteneis heo comen a lond
þeder com þe ohte mon wælla wel wes he ibon
 and mid him twa þusend cnihten swulche na king ne æhte
Forþ heo gunnen liþen into Lundenne
and senden æfter cnihten ȝeond þat kineriche
and æuerælc oht mon þat hiȝenliche come anan
Þet iherde Bruttes þer heo wuneden i þan puttes
inne eorþen and inne stockes heo hudden heom alse brockes
i wude i wilderne inne hæþe and inne uærne
þat ne mihte wel neh na man nenne Brut iuinden
buten heo weoren in castle oþer y burhȝe iclused uaste
Þa heo iherden of þissen worde þat Costantin wes an ærde
þa comen ut of munten moni þusend monnen
heo leopen ut of þan wuden swulc hit deor weoren
Liþen toward Lundenne moni hundred þusend
bi straten and bi walden al hit forþ hælden
 and þa æhte wifmen wæpmonnes claþes duden heom on
 and heo forþ wenden towward þere uerde
Þa isæh þe eorl Costantin al þis folc cumen to him
þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes næuer ær an liue
Forþ heo nomen heore wæi twa niht and enne dæi
þat heo comen ful iwis to Melga and Wanis
Togadere heo ræsden mid ræȝe strengþe
fuhten feondliche feollen þa uæie
ær þe dæi weoren agan islaȝen wes Wanis and Melgan
 and Peohtes inowe and Scottes vnifohȝe
Densce and Norenisce Galewaȝes and Irreisce
Þa while þat þe dæi wes liht ilæste auere þis slæht
þa com hit to þan æuentime þa cleopeden þe æorl Costantin
 and bad þa wæiwitere forærnen þa wateres
and snelle men toward þære sæ þet þer heom sculden sechen
Þe mon þe iseȝen þat gomen hu forþ gengden þa quenen 
ȝeond wudes and ȝend feldes ȝeond hulles and ȝeond heldes
whærswa heo funden æine mon atwunden
þe weore mid Melga þan hæþene kinga
þa quenen lude loȝen and al hine todroȝen
 and beden for þere seole þat hire neuere sæl nere
Þus þa Bruttisce quenen moni þusend aqualden
 and þus heo areden þæsne kinedom of Wanis and Melgan
 and Costantin þe ohte ferde to Selechæstre
 and heold his hustinge of alle his Brut þringen
alle þa Bruttes buȝen to þan mote
 and nomen Costantin aþeling and makeden hine Bruttene king
Muchel wes þa murþe þat wæs a mancunne
 and seoþþen heo him ȝefuen wif wunder ane hende
iboren of þan hæsten of Bruttene þan alre bezsten
Of þissen hæȝe wiue Costantin hæfuede
inne þissere leode þreo sunen lutle
Hæfde þe æreste sune wel neh his fader nome
Costantin hæhte þe king and Costanz hæhte þat child
Þa þis child wes iwaxen þat hit cuþe riden
þa lette his fader hit munekien þurh luþere monnene ræde
 and þat child munec wes inne Winchæstre
After him wes iboren anoþer þe wes þe midleste broþer
he wes ihaten Aurelius his tonome hæhte Ambrosius
Þa wes alre last iboren a child wes wel icoren
he wes ihaten Vther his aþelen weore store
he wes þe ȝungeste broþer ah he leouede lengere þane þa oþere
Guencelin þe ærchebiscop þe toward Gode wes ful god
he biwuste þa twa childere for luue of þan kinge
Ah wale þat heore fader na lengere ne moste libben
for he hafde gode laȝen þa while þe he luuede
ah he nes king here buten twælf ȝere
 and seoþþen wæs þæ king dæd hercne nu þurh wulcne ræd
He hafde in his huse ænne Poht hende cniht and swiþe aht
he uerde mid þan kinge and mid alle his dringen
nanes weies oþer bute alswa his broþer
Þa iwarþ he swa riche al his iferen vniliche
þa þohten he to swiken Costantin þene richen
he com biuoren þan kinge and feol an his cneowen
 and þus leh þa leodswike biuoren his lauerd 
Lauerd king cum uorþriht and spec wiþ Cadal þinne cniht
 and ic þe wulle tællen of uncuþe spællen
swulc þu næuere ære an ærde ne herdest
Þa aras þe king Costantin and eode forþ ut mid him
ah wale þat hit nusten Costantines cnihtes
Heo eoden swa longe forþward þat heo comen in ænne orchærd
Þa seide þa swike þere Lauerd beon wit here
Þe swike set adun alse he wolde holden run
 and he bah to þan kinge alse mon dæþ of runinge
He igrap ænne cnif swiþe long and þene king þermid ofstong
into þere heorte and he himseolf atsterte
þer þe king dæd læi and þe swike fleh awæi
Þat word com to herede hu þe king iuaren hafde
þa wes muchel reoþe and rumede to folke
Þa weoren Bruttes bisie an þonke
heo nusten þurh nane þinge whet heo mihten to kinge
for þas kinges sunen tweien lutlen heo weoren beien
neþe riden an horse
 and Vther his broþer þa ȝæt sæc his moder
 and Costance þe aldeste wes i Winchæstre
munecclaþes he hauede an alse an of his iueren
Þa comen to Lundenne al þis leodisce folc
to heore hustinge and to ræden heom of kinge
wulche weis heo mihten don and heu heo mihten taken on
 and wulc an of þissen children heo mihten habben to kinge
Þa curen þas leoden Aureliæn Ambrosian
to habben to kinge ouer heom
Þat iherde Uortiger ȝæp mon and swiþe war
imong þan eorlen he stod and fastliche hit wiþsoc
 and he þus sæide soþ þæh hit nære
Ich eow wulle ræden ræd mid þan bezsten
Abideþ feouwertene niht and cumen we æft her riht
 and ich eow wullen suggen soþþere wordes
þat mid eower eȝenen ȝe scullen iseon and eowre while wel biteon
þis ilke we scullen ibiden and to ure londe þa while riden
 and halden griþ and halden vriþ freoliche on ærde
Al duden þat hird swa Uortiger demde
 and he himseolf wende alse he walde to his londe 
 and turnde riht þene wæi þe into Winchæstre lai
Vortiger hafde Walisc lond þat haluendæl an his hond
feouwerti cnihtes gode he hauede on his hirede
He wende to Winchæstre þer he Costanz funde
 and spæc wiþ þæne abbod þe þat munster biwat
þer Costanz wes munec þas kinges sune of Bruttene
He wende into þan munestre mid mildere speche
he sæide þat he wolde speken wiþ Costance
Þe abbed hit him uþe and he hine ladde to spæchuse
Þus spæc Vortiger wiþ þene munec þa þær
Custanz hærcne minne ræd for nu is þi fader dæd
Þer is Ambrosie þi broþer and Vther þe oþer
Nu habbeþ þa ælde þa aþeleste an londe
icoren Aurilien his tonome is Ambrosien
ȝif heo maȝen þurh alle þing heo wulleþ makien hine king
 and Vþer þi broþer sukeþ ȝet his moder
Ah ic heom habbe wiþsæid and forsake þenche
for ich habben ibeon stiward of al Brutlondes ærd
 and eorl ich æm riche mine iueren vniliche
 and ich habbe Walsce lond haluendæl in mire hond
mare ich habbe ane þane þa oþere al clæne
Ich æm icome to þe for monne leofuest ært tu me
ȝif þu wult me swærie aþes ich wulle don of þe þas claþes
ȝif þu wult æchen mi lond and þin ræd don in mire hond
 and makien me þinne stiward ouer al Brutlondes ærd
 and þurh mine ræde don al þine dæde
 and þu wulle me an hond plihten þat ich hit scal al dihten
ich þe wulle þurh alle þing makien Brutlondes king
Þes munec sæt wel stille þa spæche him eode an wille
Þa andswarede þe munec mid muchelere liste
Wel wurþe þe Vortiger þat þu ært icumen her
ȝif aueremare cumeþ þæ dæi þat ich king beon mæi
al mi ræd and al mi lond ich wulle don i þire hond
 and al þat þu wult don mine men hit scullen vnderuon
 and aþes ich þe swerie þat þis ich wulle uorien
Þus seide þe munec he murnede swiþe
hu hit al weore þat he munec neore
for him weoren blake claþes wunder ane laþe
Vortiger wes ȝæp and war þat he cuþde wel iwar
he nom ane cape of his ane cnihte 
on þene munec he heo dude and ladde hine ut of þan stude
he nom ænne swein anan and þa blake claþes dude him on
 and heold rune wiþ þane swæin swulc hit þe munec weore
Munekes eoden vpward munekes eoden dunward
iseȝen bi þan weien þane swein mid munecclaþen
þe hod hongede adun alse he hudde his crune
wende æche oþer þat hit weore heore broþer
þe þer sæt swa sære i þa spæchuse
a þan dæilihte imong alle þan cnihten
Heo comen to heore abbede and hine gretten þurh Gode
Lauerd benedicite we beoþ icumen biuoren þe
for sellic us þencheþ whet Vortiger þencheþ
in ure spæchuse þer he spel haldeþ
þurhut þesne dæi na munec þerin cumen ne maie
buten Costanz ane and þa cnihtes al clane
Sære we adredeþ þat heo him misræden
Þa answerede þe abbed Næi ac heo him radeþ god
biddeþ hine halden his hod for nu is his fader dæd
Vortiger þer abed þe while Costance awæi rad
Vortiger up aras of þan munstere vt laþ
 and alle his cnihtes ut wenden forþrihtes
Munekes þer urnen þider anan wenden to uinde Costance
þa iseȝen heo þa claþes liggen bi þan waȝes
þa ælcan to oþer mænden of heore broþer
Þe abbed an horse leop and æfter Uortiger rad
 and sone gon ofærne þe eorl Uortigerne
Þus seide þe abbed to Vortigerne þer he rad
Seie me þu wode cniht whi dest þu swa muchel vnriht
Þu binimest us ure broþer Let hine and nim þene oþer
Nim Ambrosie þat child and make of him ænne king
 and ne wraþ þu noht Sæint Benediht ne do þu him nan vnriht
Þis iherde Uortiger he wes ȝæp and swiþe iwar
sone he aȝan com and þe abbed he nom
 and swor bi his honden þat he hine wolde anhongen
buten he him plihte þat he wolden vorþrihtes
vnhadien Costanz þas kinges sone of þis londe
 and for swulchere neode he sculden beon king of þissere þeode
Þe abbed ne durste nan oþer þar he vnhadede his broþer
 and þat child ȝef þan abbede an hond twenti sulhene lond
 and seoþþen heo liþeden forþ into Lundenne 
Vortiger þe hæȝe forbad his hiredmonnen
þet heo nane manne ne tælden whæt heo hæfden
Vortiger i Lundene læi þat com þe ilke isæte dæi
þat sculden to hustinge cumen þa cnihtes of þissen
To þan dæie heo comen monie and vniuoȝe
heo redden heo runden ræiȝe þa beornes
þat Ambrosie heo wolden habben and to kinge hæbben
for Vther wes to lutel þa ȝet he moste suken
 and munec wes Costanz þe ældest wes of heom
 and heo nalden for nane þinge munec makien to kinge
Þis iherde Vortiger þe wes ȝæp and swuþe iwar
 and an uoten leop swulc hit an liun weore
Nusten þa Bruttes na whon whæt Vortiger hæfde idon
he hæfde in ane bure Costanz þene deore
wel ibaþþed and iscrud and seoþþen mid twælf cnihten ihud
Þa spæc þus Vortiger he wes of ȝæpscipe war
Lusteþ lauerdlinges þe while þe ich speke of kinges
Ich wes i Winchæstre þer ich wel spedde
ich spæc wiþ þene abbed þat is hali mon and god
 and seiden him þa neode þe icumen is to þissere þeode
of Costantines dæþe þerfore him is vnneþe
 and of Costance þan childe þe he hæfde ihalden
 and ich bad hine for Gode don þat child of hade
 and for swulchere neode king he scolde beon on þeode
 and þe abbed nom his ræd and dude al þat ich hine bed
 and here ich habbe his munekes þe gode beoþ and mære
þat sculleþ witnesse beren eowe alle biuoren
Leo wær here is þat ilke child makien we herof enne king
 and her ich halde crune þa þerto bihoueþ
 and þat þis wule wiþsuggen he hit scal abuggen
Vortiger wes swiþe strong þe hæhste mon of Brutlond
nes þer nauer nan swa hæh þat his quides durste halsien
Wes i þere ilke wike þe ærchebiscop forþ iwiten
nes þer nan biscop þat forþ on his wæi ne scoc
na munec ne nan abbed þat he an his wæi ne rad
for heo ne dursten for Gode don þer þa misbode
nime þane munec child and makien Brutlondes king
Þis isæh Vortiger of ufele he wes wel iwar
up he gon stonden þe crune he nom an honden 
he setten heo vppe Costance þat him wes on þonke
Nes næuere na man þat don þer mihte Cristindom
þat mihte blessinge don in þan kinge
bute Vortiger ane hit dude for alle clane
Þe frume wes vnhende and alswa wes þe ænde
he forlette Goddes had þerfore he sorȝen ibad
Þus wes king Costance and Vortiger wes his stiward
Costanz al his kinelond sette i Vortigeres hond
 and al he dude an londe swa himsulf wolde
Þa isæh Uortiger of muclen vfele he wes wær
þat Costanz þe king ne cuþe of londe naþing
for he nefde ileorned nauer nane lare
buten in his munstre þat munec scolde drigen
Vortiger þat isæh þe Wurse him wes ful neh
ofte he hine biþohte wæht he don mahte
hu he mihte mid læsinge iquemen þan kinge
Nu þu miht iheren hu þes swiken him gon uaren
Weoren of Brutlonde þa bezste alle dæde
nu weoren þas kinges broþeren beien ful lutle
 and Guencelin ærchebiscop þer biforen wes dæd
 and himsulf þisses londes king of þare laȝe ne cuþe naþing
Vortiger þis isah and he to þan kinge bæh
mid mildere spæche his lauerd he gon greten
Hal seo þu Costanz Brutlondes lauerd
Ich æm icumen þe þus næh for muchelere neode
for suggen þe tiþende þe beoþ icume to londe
of swiþe muchele plihte Nu þe bihoueþ mihte
nu þe bihoueþ wepnen to werie þine þeoden
Her beoþ chæpmen icumen of oþere londen alse hit is iwune
heo habbeoþ ibroht to me tol for heore æhte
and heo habbeoþ me itald and treowþen iplihte
þat þe king of Norewæiȝe neowenliche wule hider uaren
 and þere Densemonne king þas Denen wulle atsechen
 and þe king of Rusie ræhȝest alre cnihten
 and þe king of Gutlonde mid ferde swiþe stronge
 and þe king of Frise þeruore me agriseþ
Þa tiþende beoþ stronge þe icumen beoþ to londe
heruore ich æm swiþe adred for ne con ich nenne godne ræd
buten we moten mid mihten senden æfter cnihten
þat beon gode and stronge and þat wel cunnen a londe 
 and setten þine castles mid kene monnen
 and swa þu miht þi kinelond werien wiþ vnleoden
 and þinne wurhscipe halden mid hæȝere strenþe
For nis nan kinelond na swa brad næ swa long
þat ne biþ sone inomen ȝif þær biþ to lute gumen
Þenne answerede þe king of londe ne cuþe he naþing
Vortiger þu ært stiward ouer al Brutlondes ærd
 and þu hit scalt walden after þine willen
Send after cnihten þe gode beon to fihten
 and nim al i þire hond mine castles and mi lond
 and do al þine iwille and ich wulle beon stille
bute þe anlæpi þing ich wulle beon icleoped king
Þa loh Uortiger he wes of vfele swiþe iwær
nes he nauere swa bliþe ær on his liue
Uortiger nam læue and forþ he gon liþe
 and swa he uorþ ferde
al þat lond he sette an his aȝere hond
and þe monraddene he nom æuere æwher he com
 and swa he nom his sonde and sende to Scotlonde
 and hæhte þa Pohtes þa alre bezste cnihtes
þreo hundred him cumen to and he heom wolde wel don
And þa cnihtes him to come þeræfter wel sone
Þus spæc þe swikefulle gume Cnihtes ȝe beoþ wulcume
Ich habbe i mire hond al þis kinewurþe lond
mid me ȝe scullen liþen for ich eow wullen luuien
 and ich eow wullen bringe biuoren ure kinge
ȝe scullen habbe seoluer and gold þe bezste hors of þis lond
claþes and fæire wif eore wille ich wulle driȝen
ȝe sculleþ beon me leofue for þa Bruttes me beoþ laþe
lude and stille ich wulle don eore wille
ȝif ȝe wulleþ in londe halden me for lauerd
Þa forþrihtes answarede þa cnihtes
Al we wulleþ don þine iwille
 and heo gunnen wenden to Costance þan kinge
To þan kinge com Uortiger of ufele he wes wel war
 and seide him of his dæde hu he idon hæuede
 and her ich habbe Peohtes þa scullen beon hiredcnihtes
and alle ich habbe þine casles swiþe wel bitæht
 and þas uncuþe cnihtes biuoren us scullen fihten
Al þe king bilufde swa Fortiger hoȝede 
ah wale þat nuste þa king of his þohte naþing
ne of his swikedome þe he dude þeræfter sone
Þas cnihtes weoren an hirede hæhliche iwurþed
fulle twa ȝere mid þan kinge heo wuneden þere
 and Uortiger þe stiward wes heore alre lauerd
A he seide þat Bruttes neoren noht to nuttes
ah he seide þat þa Peohtes weoren gode cnihtes
A weoren Bruttes godes bidaled
 and þa Peohtes walden al þat heo wolden
heo hafden drænc heo hafden mete heo hafden muchel blisse æke
Vortiger heom salde al þat heo wolden
 and heom wes al swa leof swa heore aȝene lif
swa þat heo al speken þer heo heore mete æten
þat Uortiger weoren wurþe to walden þas þeode
þurhut alle þinges bæt þene swulche þreo kinges
Vortiger ȝef þissen gumen swiþe muchele gærsume
Þa ilomp hit on ane dæie þa Uortiger at his inne laie
he nom his tweiene cnihtes and sende æfter þan Peohtes
hæhten heom cumen for for alle heo sculden æten þer
To him comen þa cnihtes to his inne forþrihtes
he uondede heom mid worde alse heo seten at borde
he lette heom bringen schenches of feole cunne drenches
heo drunken heo dremden dæi þer forþ eode
Þa heo weore swa drunken þat wakeden heore sconken
þa spæc Uortiger þat he hæfde iþoht ær
Hercneþ nu me cnihtes ich wulle suggen eow uorþrihtes
of mire muchele sorȝen þat ich fore habbe imurned
Þe king me bitahte þis ard for to beon his stiward
Ȝe beoþ me on liue alre monnen leofest
ah nabbe ich æhten to ȝiue mine cnihten
for þes king æh al þis lond and he is ȝung and þæh strong
and al ic him mot ȝelden þat ich nime of his londe
 and ȝif ich his forleose ich sal laȝe þolien
 and mine ahten ich habbe ispend for ich eo wulle iquemen
 and nu ich mot heonene uaren feor to summe kinge
heren him mid sæhte and biwinnen mid him ahte
ne mæi I noht for muchele scome habben here þesne wone 
ah forþ ich mot liþen to uncuþe leoden
 and ȝif auere cumeþ þe dæi þat ich æhten biȝiten mæi
and ich maȝen swa wel iþeon þat ȝe cumen a londe þer ich beon
ich eow wulle wel biwiten mid muchelere wurþscipe
And habbeoþ alle godne dæi toniht ich wulle faren awæi
hit biþ a muchele wæne whær ȝe iseon me aueremare
Nusten noht þas cnihtes wæt þe swike þohte
Vortiger wes fæc for her he his lauerd biswæc
 and þe cnihtes heolden hit for soh þat þe swike sæide
Fortiger hæhte his sweines sadeli his blonken
 and nemnede twælf scalkes to laden mid himseoluen
to horsen heo eoden swulc heo wolden of þeoden
Þat iseoȝen þa Peohtes þa fordrunkene cnihtes
hu Vortiger wolde uaren heruore heo hæfden muchelne kare
heo eoden to ræden heo eoden to rune
alle heo menden heore lif for Vortiger heom wes swa leof
 and þus seiden þa Peohtes þa drunkene cnihtes
Whæt maȝe we nu to rade Whæ scal us nu ræden
Wha scal us feden Wha scal us scruden
Wha scal an hirede beon ure lauerd
Nu Vortiger is iuaren alle we mote fusen
Nulle we for nane þinge munec habbe to kinge
Ah wulle we wel don forþriht faren we him to
diȝelliche and stille and don al ure iwille
into his bure and drincken of his beore
Þenne we habbeþ idrunken dreme we lude
 and summe sculleþ to þere dure mid sweorden stonden þer biuoren
 and summe forþrihtes nimen þene king and his cnihtes
 and slæn of þa hafden and we seolf hired haben
 and leten sone ofærnen uræ lauerd Uortigerne
 and seoþþen þurh alle þinge hæbben hine to kinge
þenne mah we libben swa us biþ alre leofuest
Wenden þa cnihtes to þan kinge forþrihtes
eoden heo alle þurhut þære halle
into þas kinges bure þer he sæt bi fure
Nes þer nan þat word spæc bute Gille Callæt
þus he wiþ þæne kinge spæc swiken he þohte þet
Lust me nu leodkinge Nulle ich þe liȝen naþing 
We habbeoþ ibeon an hirede hæhliche iwurþed
þurh þinne stiwærd þe haueþ iwiten al þis ærd
he us haueþ wel iued he us haueþ wel iscrud
 and to soþe ich sugge þe mai mid him we æten nu todæi
ah sare us ofþuncheþ nefden we noht to drinken
 and nu we beoþ in þine bure ȝef us drinken of þine beore
Þa ȝæf þe king answare þat scal beon eowre laste kare
for ȝe sculleþ habben to drinken þa while þe eow god þunche
Me heom brohte drinken and heo gunnen dremen
Þus sæide Gille Calæt to þere dure he wes ful wæt
Whær beo ȝe cnihtes Sturieþ eow forþrihtes
 and heo þene king igripen and his hæfde of smiten
 and alle his cnihtes heo sloȝen forþrihtes
 and nomen ænne sondesmon and senden toward Lunden
þat he swiþe sculde ærne æfter Uortigerne
þat he swiþe comen and þene kinedom nome
for þat wuste he þurh alle þing islæȝen wes Costanz þe king
Þet iharde Uortigerne þe swike wes ful derne
þus he hæhte þene sondesmon aȝan forþriht anan
 and hat heom wel biwiten al ure wurþscipen
þat nauer anne wende ut of þan ænde
ah alle me abiden a þat ich cume riden
 and swa ich wulle dele þis lond us alle imæne
Forþ wende þe sondesmon and Vortiger nom anan
 and sende ȝeond Lunden and to hustinge hehte heom
ræþen and ful sone þat heo alle comen
Icumen weoren þa burmen þe swiþe balde weoren
þa spæc Vortigerne þe swike wes ful deorne
swiþe he gon to wepnen and særiliche siken
ah hit wes an hafde and noht an his heorte
Þa axeden hine þa burhmen þe swiþe balde weoren
Lauerd Vortigerne whæht is þat þu murnest
Nert þu na wimman swa sære to wepen
Þa answarede Vortigerne þe wes swike ful deorne
Ich eow wulle telle for reoliche spelle
of muche særnesse þe isiȝen is to londe
Ich habbe i þis ærd ibeon eower kinges stiwærd
 and ispæken him wiþ and iluued hine swa mi lif
ah nalde he at þan ende nænne ræd luuien 
He luuede þa Peohtes þa vncuþe cnihtes
 and us nalde he god don ne neower feire vnderfon
ah heom he wes liþe a to heore liue
Ne mihte ic of þan kinge habben scipinge
ich spende mine ahte þa wile þa heo ilaste
 and seoþþen ich nam leue to mine londe liþe
and þenne ich hæfde mine gauel cumen aȝan to hirede
Þa isæhȝen þa Peohtes þat þe king nefde nane cnihtes
neo nauere nænne cunesmon þe heo wolden oht fore don
heo nomen heore uore into þas kinges bure
Ich suggen eow þurh alle þing islæȝen heo habbeoþ þæne king
 and þencheþ þisne kinedom and us alle fordon
 and wulleþ forþrihte makien king of ane Peohte
Ah ich wes his stiward wræken ich wulle minne lauerd
 and æueræche oht mon hælpen me þat to don
On ich wulle mid mine gæren and forþriht ich wulle uaren
Wenden ut of Lunden cnihtes þritti hundred
heo riden and heo arnden forþ mid Vortigerne
þat heo nehlæhten þer weoren þa Peohtes
 and he nom enne of his cnihtes and sende to þan Peohten
 and seide heom þat he com ȝif heo hine wolden vnderuon
Þa Peohtes weoren bliþe for heore fæisiþe
 and heo nomen heore gode gæren nes þer neowþer sceld ne spære
Vortiger forþrihtes wepnede alle his cnihtes
 and comen þa Peohtes and bruhten hæued þas kinges
Þa Vortiger þis hæued isæh þa hælde he to grunde ful neh
swulc he hafuede modkare mest of alre monne
mid his lechen he gon liȝen his heorte wes ful bliþe
Þa seide Vortigerne þe swike wes ful deorne
Auerælc oht mon mid sweorde leggeþ heom on
 and wrækeþ wel an ærde þe seorȝe of ure lauerd
Nænne heo ne nomen ah alle heo heom sloȝen
 and to þan inne wende into Winchæstre
 and sloȝen heore sweines and heore burhþeines
heore cokes and heore cnaues alle heo duden of lifdæȝen
Þus ferden þa tiþinde of Costanz þan kinge
 and þa weorldewis mon þa oþere childre biwusten
for heo hafden care of Vortiger heo nomen Ambrosie and Vþer
 and ladden heom ouer sæ into þere lasse Brutene 
 and fæire heom bitahten Budiz þan kinge
 and he heom feire vnderfeng he wes heore cun and heore freond
 and mid muchelere liste þa childere he biwuste
and swa wel fele ȝere mid him heo weoren þere
Vortiger a þissen londe wes ihoue to kinge
alle þa Bruttes stronge stoden an his honde
fif and twenti ȝeren he wes king here
He wes wod he wes wild he wes ræh he wes bald
of alle þinge he hæfde his iwille bute þa Peohtes neoren næuere stille
ah eouere heo wenden ȝeond þene norh enden
 and henden þis kinelond mid hærmen vnimete
 and wreken heore cun inoh þat Vortiger here ofsloh
Vnder þan comen tiþende into þissen londe
þat Aurelien wes cniht þe Ambrosiæn wes ihæten
 and alswa wes Vther god cniht and swiþe iwar
and wolden comen to þissen londe and leden here swiþe stronge
Þis wes feole siþe iqueþe ofte iquidded
ofte comen tiþinde to Vortiger þan kinge
þerfore him ofte scomede and his heorte gromede
for men hit sæiden wel iwhær Nu cumeþ Ambrosie and Vther
and wulleþ wræken Costance þene king of þis lond
Nis þer cost nan oþer wærken heo wulleþ heore broþer
and slæn Vortigerne and to duste hine forberne
þus heo wulleþ al þis lond setten an heore aȝere hond
Swa quiddeden ælche dæi al þat verden æfter wæi
Uortiger hine biþohte whæt he don mihte
 and þohte sende sonde into oþere londe
æfter vncuþe cnihten þa hine biwiten mihten
and þohte to beon wær wiþ Ambrosie and wiþ Vther
Vnder þan comen tiþende to Vortiger þan kinge
þat ouer sæ weoren icumen swiþe selcuþe gumen
inne þere Temese to londe heo weoren icummen
þreo scipen gode comen mid þan flode
þreo hundred cnihten alse hit weoren kinges
wiþuten þan scipenmonnen þe weoren þer wiþinnen
Þis weoren þa færeste men þat auere her comen
ah heo weore hæþene þat wes hærm þa mare
Uortiger heom sende to and axede hu heo weoren idon 
ȝif heo griþ sohten and of his freondscipe rohten
Heo wisliche andswerden swa heo wel cuþen
 and seiden þat heo walden speken wiþ þan kinge
 and leofliche him heren and hælden hine for hærre
and swa heo gunnen wenden forþ to þan kinge
Þa wes Uortigerne þa king in Cantuarieburi
þer he mid his hirede hæhliche spilede
þer þas cnihtes comen biforen þan folckinge
Sone swa heo hine imetten fæire heo hine igrætten
 and seiden þat heo him wolden hæren i þisse londe
ȝif he heom wolde mid rihten athalden
Þa andswerede Vortiger of elchen vuele he wes war
An alle mine iliue þe ich iluued habbe
bi dæie no bi nihtes ne sæh ich nauere ær swulche cnihtes
for eouwer cumen ich æm bliþe and mid me ȝe scullen bilæfuen
 and eouwer wille ich wulle driȝen bi mine quicke liuen
Ah of eou ich wulle iwiten þurh soþen eouwer wurþscipen
whæt cnihten ȝe seon and whænnenen ȝe icumen beon
 and whar ȝe wullen beon treowe alde and æc neowe
Þa answerede þe oþer þat wes þe aldeste broþer
Lust me nu lauerd king and ich þe wullen cuþen
what cnihtes we beoþ and whanene we icumen seoþ
Ich hatte Henges Hors is mi broþer
we beoþ of Alemainne aþelest alre londe
of þat ilken ænde þe Angles is ihaten
Beoþ in ure londe selcuþe tiþende
vmbe fiftene ȝer þat folc his isomned
al ure iledene folc and heore loten werpeþ
vppen þan þe hit faleþ he scal uaren of londe
bilæuen scullen þa fiue þa sexte scal forþ liþe
ut of þan leode to uncuþe londe
ne beo he na swa leof mon uorþ he scal liþen
For þer is folc swiþe muchel mære þene heo walden
Þa wif fareþ mid childe swa þe deor wilde
æueralche ȝere heo bereþ child þere
Þat beoþ an us feole þat we færen scolden
ne mihte we bilæue for liue ne for dæþe
ne for nauer nane þinge for þan folckinge
Þus we uerden þere and for þi beoþ nu here 
to sechen vnder lufte lond and godne lauerd
Nu þu hæfuest iherd lauerd king soþ of us þurh alle þing
Þa answærede Vortiger of alc an vfele he wes war
Ich ileue þe cniht þat þu me sugge soþriht
 and wulche beoþ æoure ileuen þat ȝe on ileueþ
 and eoure leofue godd þe ȝe to luteþ
Þa andswarede Hænges cnihtene alre fæirest
nis in al þis kinelond cniht swa muchel ne swa strong
We habbeþ godes gode þe we luuieþ an ure mode
þa we habbeþ hope to and heoreþ heom mid mihte
Þe an hæhte Phebus þe oþer Saturnus
þe þridde hæhte Woden þat is an weoli godd
þe feorþe hæhte Iupiter of alle þinge he is whar
þe fifte hæhte Mercurius þat is þe hæhste ouer us
þæ sæxte hæhte Appollin þat is a godd wel idon
þe seoueþe hatte Teruagant an hæh godd in ure lond
Ȝet we habbeþ anne læuedi þe hæh is and mæhti
heh heo is and hali hiredmen heo luuieþ for þi
heo is ihate Frææ wel heo heom dihteþ
Ah for alle ure goden deore þa we scullen hæren
Woden hehde þa hæhste laȝe an ure ælderne dæȝen
he heom wes leof æfne alswa heore lif
he wes heore walden and heom wurþscipe duden
þene feorþe dæi i þere wike heo ȝifuen him to wurþscipe
Þa þunre heo ȝiuen Þunresdæi for þi þat heo heom helpen mæi
Freon heore læfdi heo ȝiuen hire Fridæi
Saturnus heo ȝiuen Sætterdæi þene sunne heo ȝiuen Sonedæi
Monen heo ȝifuen Monedæi Tidea heo ȝeuen Tisdæi
Þus seide Hængest cnihten alre hendest
Þa answerede Vortiger of ælchen vfel he wæs wær
Cnihtes ȝe beoþ me leofue ah þas tiþende me beoþ laþe
eouwer ileuen beoþ vnwraste ȝe ne ileoueþ noht an Criste
ah ȝe ileoueþ a þene Wurse þe Godd seolf awariede
eoure godes ne beoþ nohtes in helle heo niþer liggeþ
Ah neoþeles ich wulle eou athælde an mine anwalde
for norþ beoþ þa Peohtes swiþe ohte cnihtes
þe ofte ledeþ in mine londe ferde swiþe stronge 
 and ofte doþ me muchele scome and þerfore ich habbe grome
 and ȝif ȝe me wulleþ wræken and heore hæfden me biȝeten
ich eou wullen ȝeuen lond muchel seoluer and gold
Þa andswerede Hængest cnihtene alre feirest
Ȝif hit wulle Saturnus al hit scal iwurþe þus
 and Woden ure lauerd þe we on biliueþ
Hengest nom læue and to scipen gon liþe
þer wes moni cniht strong heo droȝen heore scipen uppe þe lond
Forþ wenden dringches to Vortigerne þan kenge
biuoren wende Hengest and Hors him alre hændest
seoþþen þa Alemainisce men þa aþele weoren an deden
 and seoþþen heo senden him to heore Sæxisce cnihtes wel idon
Hengestes cunnesmen of his aldene cuþþen
Heo comen into halle hændeliche alle
bett weoren iscrudde and bed weoren iuædde
Hængest swaine þene Vortigernes þeines
Þa wes Vortigernes hired for hehne ihalden
Bruttes weoren særi for swulchere isihþe
Nes hit nawiht longe þat ne comen to þan kinge
cnihtes sunen uiue þa ifaren hafden biliue
heo sæiden to þan kinge neowe tiþenden
Nu forþrihtes icumen þa Peohtes
þurh þi lond heo ærneþ and hærȝieþ and berneþ
 and al þene norþ ænde iuæld to þan grunde
herof þu most ræden oþer alle we beoþ dæden
Þe king hine biþohte whæt he don mihte
he sende to þan innen after al his monnen
Þer com Hengest þer com Hors þer com moni mon ful oht
þer comen þa Saxisce men Hengestes cunnesmen
 and þa Alemainisce cnihtes þe beoþ gode to fihte
Þis isæh þe king Vortiger bliþe wes he þa þer
Þa Peohtes duden heore iwune a þas hælf þere Humbre, heo weoren icume
 and þe king Vortiger of heore cume wes ful war
togadere heo comen and feole þer ofsloȝen
þer wes feht swiþe strong comp swiþe sturne
Þe Peohtes weoren ofte iwuned Vortigene to ouercumen
 and þa heo þohten alswa ah hit ilomp anoþer þa
for hit wes heom al hele þat Hængest wes þere 
 and þa cnihtes stronge þe comen of Saxelonde
 and þa ohte Alemanisce þe þider comen mid Horse
swiþe monie Peohtes heo sloȝen i þan fehte
feondliche heo fuhten feollen þa fæie
Þa þe non wes icumen þa weoren Peohtes ouercumen
 and swuþe heo awæi floȝen an ælche helue heo forþ fluȝen
 and alle dai heo fluȝen monie and vnnifoȝe
Þe king Vortigerne wende to herberwe
 and æuere him weoren on uast Hors and Hængest
Hængest wes þan kinge leof and him Lindesaȝe ȝef
 and he ȝæf Horse madmes inoȝe
 and alle heore cnihtes he swiþe wel dihte
 and hit gode stunde stod a þan ilke
Ne durste nauere Peohtes cumen i þan londes
no ræueres no utlaȝen þat heo neoren sone ofslæȝen
 and Hængest swiþe fæire herede þane king
Þa ilomp hit in ane time þat þe king wes swiþe bliþe
an ane hæȝe dæie imong his duȝeþe monnen
Hengest hine biþohte what he don mihte
for he wolde wiþ þan kinge holden runinge
Þan kinge he eode toforen and fæire hine gon greten
Þe king sone up stod and sætte hine bi himseoluen
heo drunken heo dremden blisse wes among heom
Þa queþ Hengest to þan kinge Lauerd hærcne tiþende
 and ich þe wulle ræcchen deorne runen
ȝif þu mine lare wel wult lusten
 and noht halden to wraþþe þat ich wel leare
Þe king answarede swa Henges hit wolde
Þa sæide Hængest cnihten alre fæirest
Lauerd ich habbe moni a dæi þine monscipe ihæȝed
 and þin holde mon ibeon i richen þine hirede
 and in ælche fæhte hæhst of þine cnihten
 and ich habbe ofte ihærd hohfulle ronen
imong þine hiredmonnen heo hatieþ þe swiþe
into þan bare dæþe ȝif heo hit dursten cuþe
Ofte heo stilleliche spækeþ and spilieþ mid runen
of twam ȝunge monnen þat feor wunieþ hennen
þe an hæhte Vther þe oþer Ambrosie
þe þridde hæhte Costance þe wes king i þisse lond 
 and he her wes ofslaȝen þurh swicfulle laȝen
Nu wulleþ cume þa oþere and wræken heore broþer
al forbærnen þi lond and slæn þine leoden
þe seoluen and þine duȝeþen driuen ut of londe
 and þus suggeþ þine men þer heo somned sitteþ
for þa twene broþere beoþ beyne kineborne
of Androeinnes kunne þas aþele Bruttes
 and þus þine duȝeþe stille þe fordemeþ
Ah ich þe wulle ræde of muchele þire neode
þat þu biȝite cnihtes þa gode beoþ to fihte
 and bitache me ænne castel oþer ane kineliche burh
þat ich mai inne ligge þa while þa ich libbe
Ic am uor þe iuaid þærfore ic wene beon dæd
fare þer ic auer fare næm ich næuere bute care
buten ich ligge faste biclused inne castle
Ȝif þu þis me wult don ich hit wulle mid luue afon
 and ich wulle biliue senden after mine wiue
þat is a Sexisc wimmon of wisdome wel idon
 and after Rouwenne mire dohter þe me is swiþe deore
Þenne ich habbe mi wif and mine winemaies
 and ich beo i þine londe fulliche atstonde
þa bet ich wullen hiren þe ȝif þu þis ȝettest me
Þa answarede Vortiger of ælchen vuele he wes war
Nim cnihtes biliue and send æfter þine wiue
