 and æfter þine children þan ȝungen and þan olden
 and æfter þine cunnen and afeoh heom mid wunne
þenne heo to þe cumeþ þu scalt habben gærsume
hæhliche heom to ueden and wurþliche scruden
Ah nulle ich castel na burh nane þe bitechen
for men me wolden scenden i mine kinelonde
for ȝe haldeþ þa hæþene laȝe þat stod on eoure ælderen dæȝe
 and we haldeþ Cristes laȝe and wulleþ auere an ure dæȝe
Þa ȝet spæc Hængest cnihten alre hendest
Lauerd ich wulle þin iwil driȝen her and oueral
 and don al mine dæde æfter þine ræde
Nu ic wulle biliue sende after mine wiue
 and æfter mire dohter þe me is swa deore
 and æfter ohte monnen þa bezste of mine cunne
and þu ȝif me swa muchel lond to stonden a mire aȝere hond
swa wule anes bule hude ælches weies ouerspræden 
feor from ælche castle amidden ane ualde
Þenne ne mai þe atwite þe hæne ne þe riche
þat þu æi hæhne burhȝe hæþene monne habbe bitæht
Þe king him iȝette swa Hengest ȝirnde
Hengest nom læue and forþ he gon liþe
 and æfter his wiue sende sonde to his aȝene londe
 and he seolf wende ȝeond þis lond to sechen ænne brædne fæld
þer he mihte wel spræde on his feire hude
He com æn enne ende in enne fæire uelde
he hafde ane hude biȝite to his neode
of ane wilde bule þe wes wunder ane strong
He hæfden ænne wisne mon þe wel cuþe a craften
þe nom þas hude and a bord leide
and whætte his sæxes alse he schæren wolde
Of þere hude he kærf enne þwong swiþe smal and swiþe long
nes þe þwong noht swiþe bræd buten swulc a twines þræd
Þa al islit wes þe þong he wes wunder ane long
abuten he bilæde muche del of londe
He bigon to deluen dic swiþe muchele
Þeruppe stenene wal þe wes strong oueral
ane burh he arerde muchele and mare
Þa þe burh wes al ȝare þa scop he hire nome
he hæhte heo ful iwis Kaer Carrai an Bruttisc
 and Ænglisce cnihtes heo cleopeden Þwongchastre
nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere
 and for nan oþere gome næueden þæ burh þene nome
a þet come Densce men and driuen ut þa Bruttes
þene þridde nome heo þer sætte and Lanecastel hine hæhten
 and for swulche gomen þæ tun hafde þas þreo nomen
Vnder þan com liþen hider Hengestes wif mid hire scipen
heo hæfde to iueren fiftene hundred ridern
mid hire comen to iwiten muchele æhtene scipen
þer comen inne muchel of Hengestes cunne
 and Rouwen his dohter þe him wes swiþe deore
Hit wes umbe while þat com þe ilke time
þat iȝarked wes þa burh mid þan alre bezste
Hengest com to þan kinge and bad him gistninge 
 and seide þat he hafde an in iȝarked toȝeines him
 and bad þat he come þerto and he scolde beon fæire underfon
 and þe king him ȝette swa Hengest hit wolde
Hit com to þan time þat þe king gon forþ liþe
mid þan deoreste monnen of alle his duȝeþe
forþ he gon buȝen þat he to burh com
he biheold þene wal up and dun oueral
al him wel likede þat he on lokede
He wende into halle and his heleþes mid him alle
bemen heo bleowen gomen men gunnen cleopien
bord heo hetten breden cnihtes setten þerto
heo æten heo drunken dræm wes i burhȝen
Þa þe duȝeþe hafde iȝeten þa wes heom þa bet iloten
Hængest eode into þan inne þer wunede Rouwenne
he heo lette scruden mid vnimete prude
al þat scrud þe heo hafde on heo weoren swiþe wel ibon
heo weoren mid þan bezste ibrusted mid golde
Heo bar an hire honde ane guldene bolle
iuulled mid wine þe wes wunder ane god
Hæȝe iborenne men heo lædden to hallen
biuoren þan kinge fairest alre þinge
Reowen sæt a cneowe and cleopede to þan kinge
 and þus ærest sæide in Ænglene londe
Lauerd king wæs hæil For þine kime ich æm uæin
Þe king þis ihærde and nuste what heo seide
þe king Vortigerne fræinede his cnihtes sone
what weoren þat speche þe þat maide spilede
Þa andswarede Keredic a cniht swiþe sellic
he wes þe bezste latimer þat ær com her
Lust me nu lauerd king and ich þe wulle cuþen
whæt seiþ Rouwenne fæirest wimmonnen
Hit beoþ tiþende inne Sæxelonde
whærswa æi duȝeþe gladieþ of drenche
þat freond sæiþe to freonde mid fæire loten hende
Leofue freond wæs hail Þe oþer sæiþ Drinc hail
Þe ilke þat halt þene nap he hine drinkeþ up
oþer uuel me þider fareþ and bithecheþ his iueren
þenne þat uul beoþ icumen þenne cusseoþ heo þreoien
Þis beoþ sele laȝen inne Saxelonde 
 and inne Alemaine heo beoþ ihalden aþele
Þis iherde Uortiger of alchen uuele he wes war
 and seide hit an Bruttisc ne cuþe he nan Ænglisc
Maiden Rouwenne drinc bluþeliche þenne
Þat maide dronc up þat win and lette don oþer þerin
 and bitæhten þan kinge and þrien hine custe
 and þurh þa ilke leoden þa laȝen comen to þissen londe
wæshail and drinchæil moni mon þerof is fain
Rouwenne þe hende sat bi þan kinge
þe king heo ȝeorne biheold heo was him an heorte leof
ofte he heo custe ofte he heo clupte
al his mod and his main hælde to þan mæidene
Þe Wurse wes þer ful neh þe in ælche gomene is ful ræh
þe Wurse ne dude næuere god he mæingde þas kinges mod
he murnede ful swiþe to habben þat mæidene to wiue
Þat wes swiþe ladlic þing þat þe Cristine king
luuede þat haþene maide leoden to hærme
þat maiden wes þan kinge leof æfne alse his aȝene lif
he bad Hengest his dring ȝiuen him þat maidechild
Hengest funde an his ræd to don þat þe king him bed
he ȝef him Rouwenne wimmon swiþe hende
Þan kinge hit was icweme he imakede heo to quene
al after þan laȝen þe stoden an hæþene dæȝen
nes þer nan Cristindom þer þe king þat maide nom
ne preost ne na biscop ne nauere ihandled Godes boc
ah an heþene wune he heo wedde and brohte heo to his bedde
Maiden he heo hæfde and mærȝeue hire bitahte
Þa he hine an hire hafde iscend he hire ȝef Londen and Kent
Þe king hafde þreo sunen þe weoren swiþe hende gumen
þe ældeste hehte Vortimer Passcent and Katiger
Garengan wes an eorl þe Kent ohte longe
 and his fader biuoren him and seoþþen he þurh his cun
þa he bezst wende to halden his lond
þa hafde Hengest hit an his hond
sellic þuhte þan cnihte whæt þe king þohte
Þe king luuede þa hæþene and henede þa Cristine
þe hæþene hæfden al þis lond to walden under heore hond
 and þes kinges þreo sunen ofte þoleden sorȝen and kare
Heore moder wes þa dæd þeruore heo hafden þe lasse ræd 
here moder wes swiþe god wif and ladde swiþe Cristin lif
 and heore steopmoder hæþene Hengestes dohter
Nes hit noht longe buten ane stunde
þat þe king makede ueorme swiþe store
þe hæþene he laþede þarto he wende swiþe wel to don
þider comen þæines cnihtes and sweines
and alle þe cuþe a boken þa feorme forsoken
for þa hæþene weoren hæhst an hireden
 and þæt Cristine hired for hæne wes ihalden
þa hæþene weoren bliþe for þe king heom luueden swiþe
Hengest hine biþohte what he don mahte
he com to þan kinge mid are hailinge
 and dronc to þan kinge
Þa spæc þus Hængest cnihtene alre hændest
þat of hæþene laȝen leouede a þan dæȝen
Hærcne me lauerd king þu ært me leof þurh alle þing
þu hæuest mine dohter þæ me is swiþe deore
 and ich æm þe an folke swa ich þi fader weore
Hærcne mine lare heo sculleþ þe wurþen leofue
for ich wulle hæhliche to helpen þe ræden
Þin hired þe hateþ for me and ich æm iuæid for þe
 and þe hatieþ kinges eorles and þringes
heo uareþ in þine londe mid hære swiþe stronge
Ȝif þu wult þe awraken mid wurþscipe muchen
 and don þine vniwinen wa send after mine sune Octa
 and æfter enne oþer Ebissa his wedbroþer
þis beoþ þa hæhste men þe æuere hired lædden
 and i þan norþ ende ȝif heom of þine londe
Heo beoþ of muchele mæhte and stronge i fæhte
heo wulleþ biwiten þi lond wel mid þan bezsten
Þenne mihte þu mid winne þi lif al uorwerien
mid haueken and mid hunden hiredplæie luuien
ne þræt þu nauere habben kare of uncuþe leoden
Þa answarede Vortiger of ælchen uuele he wes war
Send þine sonde into Sexlonde
after þine sune Octa and after þine freonden ma
Do him wel to iwiten þat he sende his writen
æfter al þan cnihten þe gode beoþ to fihten
ȝeond alle Sæxþeoden þat heo cumen to mire neoden
 and þeh he bringen ten þusend gumen alle heo beoþ me wel icumen
Þis ihærde Hengest cnihten alre henddest 
þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes næuere an his liue
Hengest sende his sonde into Saxlonde
hehte cumen Octa and his wedbroþer Ebissa
 and al of heore cunne þat heo mihten iwinnen
 and alle þa cnihtes þæ heo biȝiten mihten
Octa sende sonde ȝeond þreom kinelonde
 and bad ælchene ohte gume hiȝenliche him to cume
þe wolden biȝiten lond oþer seoluer oþer gold
Heo comen to hirede alse haȝel þe ualleþ
þat was to iwitene mid þreo hundred scipene
Forþ wenden mid Octa þritti þusend and æc ma
ohte men and kene and Ebissa his iuere
æfter com liþen mid unimete leoden
 and he ladde to iwiten oþer half hundred scipen
þeræfter comen liþe fiue and fife
bi sixe bi seoue bi tene and bi ælleuene
 and þus heo comen liþen toward þissen londe
hæþene hæregumen to hirede þis kinges
þat þis lond wes swa vul of uncuþe leoden
þat nes nan swa wis mon no swa ȝerwitele
þat mihte todæle þa Cristine and þa hæþene
for þa hæþene weoren swa riue and auere heo comen biliue
Þa iseȝen Bruttes þat balu wes an londe
þeruore heo weoren særi and an heorte druri
 and ferden to þan kinge þe hæhste of þissen londe
 and þus him to sæiden mid sorhfule steuene
Lust us nu lauerd king of ure leodrunen
Þu ært þurh us bald king inne þissen Brutene
 and þu hafuest þe biwunnen hærm and muchele sunnen
ibroht heþene folc ȝet hit þe ihærmeþ
 and þu letest Godes laȝen uor uncuþe leoden
 and nult ne ihæren ure Drihten for þissen hæþene cnihten
 and we þe wulleþ bidden for alle Godes sibben
þat þu heom bilæuen and of þine londe driuen
Ȝif þu ælles ne maht we wulleþ makien muchel fæht
 and driuen heom of londe oþer heom adun fallen
oþer we usseoluen ofslaȝen wulleþ liggen
 and leten haþene uolc hælden þas riche
bruken hit mid winne ȝif heo hit maȝen iwinnen 
 and ȝif heo alle beoþ hæþene and þu ane Cristine
nulleþ heo nauere longe habben þe to kinge
buten þu a þine daȝen afo hæþene laȝen
 and bilæue þe hæhȝe Godd and luuie heore Mahimet
Þenne scalt þu forwurþen a þissere woruldriche
 and þi wracche saule siȝen to helle
þenne hauest þu aboht þe luue of þire brude
Þa answærede Vortiger of ælc an uuele he wes wær
Nulle ich heom bilæuen bi mine quike liue
for Hengest is hider icumen he is mi fader and ich his sune
 and ich habbe to leofmonne his dohter Rouwenne
 and ich heo habbe biwedded and ihaued a mine bedde
 and seoþþen ich sende after Octa and after his iueren ma
Hu mihte ich for scome scunien heom swa sone
driuen of londe mine wines deore
Þa andswarede Bruttes mid sorȝen ibunden
Nulle we naueremare þine iboden here
ne to þine hirede cumen ne þe uor king halden
ah hatien we wulleþ mid hæhȝere strengþe
alle þine hæþene wines and hærme igreten
bidden us to fultume þat is Crist Godes sune
Forþ iwenden eorles forþ iwenden beornes
forþ iwenden biscopes and þa bocilæred men
forþ iwenden þæines forþ iwenden sweines
alle Brutleoden þat heo comen to Lundene
Þer wes moni hæh Brut at þan hustinge
 and þeos kinges þreo sunes alle heo weoren þider icumen
þer wes Uortimer Pascent and Katiger
 and swiþe monie oþere þat comen mid þan broþere
al þat folc þider com þat luueden þene Cristtendom
Alle þa riche nomen heom to ræde
 and nomen þes kinges ældeste sune þe to þan hustinge wes icumen
 and mid muchele loftsonge heuen hine to kinge
Þa wes Vortimer Cristine king þer
 and Uortiger his fader fulede þan hæþenen
Vortimer þe ȝunge king wes swiþe kene þurh alle þing
he sende Hengest word and Horse his broþer
buten heo hiȝenliche uerden of þis riche
he heom walde ufel don baþe ablenden and anhon 
 and his aȝene fader he foruaren walde
 and alle þa hæþene mid hæȝere strengþe
Þa andswærede Hengest cnihtene alre hendest
Her we wulleþ wunien wintres and sumeres
riden and ærnen mid þan kinge Vortigerne
 and alle þa mid Vortimere uareþ heo sculleþ habben sorȝen and kare
Þat iherde Vortimer he wes wis and swiþe iwar
 and lette beoden uerde ȝeond allen þissen ærde
þat al þat Cristine folc come to hirede
Vortimer þe ȝunge king i Lundene heold his husting
þe king hehte ælne mon þe luuede þene Cristindom
þat heo þa hæþene hatien scolden
 and þa hæfden bringen to Vortimer þan kinge
 and twalf panewes habben to mede for his weldede
Vortimer þe ȝunge verde ut of Lundene
 and Pascent his broþer and Katiger þe oþer
heom wes icumen word þat Hengest læi at Epiford
uppen þan watere þe men nemneþ Darewente
Þer comen tosomne sixti þusend monnen
an are halue wes Uortimer Pascent and Categer
 and al þat leodliche folc þat luueden ure Drihten
an oþere halue weoren drenches mid Vortigerne þan kinge
Hengest and his broþer and moni þusend oþer
Tosomne heo comen and mid mæine onsloȝen
þer uellen to þan grunde twa and þritti hundred
of Hængestes monnen and Hors wes forwonded
Catiger þer com and mid his spere hine þurhnom
 and Hors forþriht þer forwundede Catiger
 and Hengest gon to flonnen mid al his drihtmonnen
 and Vortigerne þe king flæh forþ alse þe wind
heo floȝen forþ into Kent and Vortimer heom after went
uppen þere sæbrimme þer Hengest þolede pine
þer heo gunnen atstonden and fuhten swiþe longe
Fif þusende þer weoren islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
of Vortigernes monnen of þan hæþene cunnen
Hengest hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
iseh he þer bihalues ane hæuene swiþe mære
moni scipen gode þer stoden i sæflode
Heo iseȝen an heore riht hond a swiþe fæier æitlond
hit is ihaten Tænate þiderward heo weoren whæte 
þer þa Sæxisce men þæ sæ isohten
 and anan gunnen wenden into þan æitlonde
 and Bruttes heom after mid feole cunne craften
 and heom toheolden in æchere hælue
mid scipen and mid baten heo gunnen smiten and sceoten
Ofte wes Hængest wæ and nauere wurs þene þa
buten he dude oþerne ræd þer he sculden wurþen dæd
He nom ænne sperescæft þe wes long and swiþe stærc
 and dude a þene ænde ænne mantel hende
 and cleopede to þan Brutten and bed heom abiden
he wold spæcken heom wiþ and ȝirnen þeos kinges griþ
 and mid griþe sende Uortigerne to londe
to makien his forward þat he faren moste
wiþuten mare sconde into Sæxlonde
Bruttes wende to londe to Vortimere heore kinge
and Hengest spæc wiþ Vortigerne of rune swiþe derne
Vortigerne wende a þat lond and ber anne ȝerd an his hond
Þa while þa heo of griþe speken Saxes i scipe leopen
 and droȝen up to coppe hæȝe heore seiles
 and wenden mid wedere i þere sæ wilde
 and letten i þissen londe wiues and heore children
 and Vortigerne king þe heom luuede þurh alle þing
Mid muchele modkære Hengest gon awæi uaren
swa longe heo ferden þat inne Saxlonde heo weoren
Þa weoren inn Bruttene Bruttes swiþe balde
heo droȝen on heom muchel mod and duden al þat heom þuhte god
 and Vortimer þe ȝunge wes duhti mon þurh alle þing
 and Vortigerne his fader ferde ȝeond þas Bruttene
ah nes hit nan swa wac mon þat him ne hokerede on
 and swa he gon wondrien fulle fif wintren
 and his sune Vortimer riche king wuneden her
 and al þis leodisce folc luueden hine swiþe
he wes milde ælche cnafe and tahte þan folke Godes læȝe
þan ȝungen and þan ælden hu heo Cristindom sculden halden
Writen he sende to Rome to þan Pape wel idone
þe wes ihaten Sceint Romæin al Cristindom he makede fain
Biscopes he nom twæin hali men heo weoren bæien
Germain and Leois of Ceore and of Træis
heo uerden ut of Rome swa þat heo hider comen
Þa wes swa bliþe Vortimer swa he nes næuere ær her 
he and alle his cnihtes iwenden uorþrihtes
an here bare uoten toȝeines þan biscopen
 and mid michelere murhþe muþes þer custen
Nu þu miht iheren of þan kinge Vortimere
heu he spac wiþ Seint Germain for heore kume he wes fæin
Lusteþ me lauerddinges ich æm þissere leodene king
ich hatte Vortimer mi broþer hatte Catimer
Vortigerne hehte ure fader him uulieþ unrædes
He hafþ ibroht i þis lond hæþene leoden
ah we heom habbeoþ iflemed al swa ure uulle iuan
 and mid wepnen ifelled of heom ueole þusen
 and isend heom ouer sæstram þat heo nauere sel ne cumen aȝan
 and we scullen an londe luuiæn ure Drihten
Godes folc urofrien and freondliche hit halden
wurþen mils liþe wiþ þa londtilien
churichen we scullen hæhȝen and hæþenescipe hatien
Habbe alc god mon his rihte ȝif Godd hit an
 and ælc þrel and ælc wælh wurþe iuroeid
 and here ich biteche eou an hond al freo ælc chiriclond
 and ich forȝiue ælchere widewe hire lauerdes quide
 and þus we scullen an ure daȝen aniþeri Hengestes laȝen
 and hine and his hæþenescipe þæ he hider brohte
 and minne fader biswak þurh swike his craftes
þurh his dohter Rouwenne mine uader he uorradde
 and mi uader swa uuele agon scunede þene Cristindom
 and þa hæþene laȝen luuede to swiþe
þa we sculleþ sceonien þa while þa we luuien
Þa answarede Seint Germain for swulche worden he wes fain
Ich þonkie mine Drihte þe scop þes daȝes lihte
þet he swulche mildce sent to moncunne
Þas biscopes ferden ȝeond þis lond and setten hit al a Godes hond
 and þene Cristindom heo rihten and þat volc þerto dihten
 and seoþþen þeræfter sone heo iwenden to Rome
 and sæiden þan Papen þe Roumain wes ihaten
hu he hafden her idon iriht þene Cristindom
 and þus hit ane stunde stod a þan ilken
Vo we ȝet a Uortigerne alre kinge si he ærmest
he louede Rouwen of þan hæþenne cunne 
Hengestes dohter heo þuhten him wel softe
Rouwenne heo biþohte whæt heo don mahte
hu heo mahte hire fader wreken and hire freondene deaþ
Ofte heo sende sonde to Uortimere þon kinge
heo him sende maþmes moniare cunne
of seoluer and of golde þe beste of æie londe
heo ȝirnede his ære þat heo moste wonien here
mid Uortigerne his fader and foluen his rædes
Þe king uor his fader bone ȝette hire hir bone
buten þat heo sculde wel don luuien þene Cristindom
al þat þe king ȝirnede al heo hit ȝette
Ah wale þat Uortimer of hire þonke næs wær
Wale þat þe gode king of hire þonke nuste naþing
þat he nuste þene swikedom þe þohte þa luþere wimman
Hit ilomp an are tide heo nom hire to ræde
to don bi his ræde alle hire neode
and to wlche time heo mihte wel don vnderuongen þene Cristindom
Forþ heo gon riden to Uortimer þan kinge
þa heo hine imette uæire heo hine igrette
Hal wrþ þu lauerd king Bruttene deorling
Ich æm þe icomen to Cristindom ich wulle auon
an þan ilke dæie þe þu seolf demest
Þa wæs Uortimer þe king bliþe þurh alle þing
he wende þat hit weore soþ þat þeo scaþe sæide
Bemen þer bleowen blisse wes on hirede
forþ mon brohte þat water biforen þan kinge
heo seten to borde mid muchelure blisse
Þa þe king hafde iæten þa eoden þeinesmen to mete
in halle heo drunken harpen þer dremden
Þa swicfulle Rouuenne eode to are tunne
þer wes idon in þes kinges deoreste win
nom heo an honde ane bolle of ræde golde
 and heo gon scenchen on þas kinges benche
Þa heo isæh hire time heo fulde hir scale of wine
 and atforen al þan dringe heo eode to þan kinge
 and þus hailede him on þe swicfulle wimman
Lauerd king wæs hail Uor þe ich am swiþe uæin
Hercne nu muchel swikedom of þere luþere wimmon 
hu heo gon swiken þer þene king Uortimer
Þe king heo uæire underuæng to his fæiesiþe
Fortimer spæc Bruttisc and Rouuenne Saxisc
þan king þuhte gomen inoh for hire spæche he loh
Hærcne hu heo toc on þis swicfulle wimman
In hire bosme heo bar bineoþen hire titten
ane guldene ampulle of attere ifulled
 and þa luþere Rouuenne dronc þene bolle
þat heo hafde half don after þes kinges dom
Þa while þe þa king loh þa ampulle heo ut droh
þene bolle heo sette to hire chin þat atter heo halde in þat win
 and seoþen heo þa cuppe bitahte þan kinge
Þe king dronc al þat win and þat atter þerin
Þe dæi forþ eode blisse wes on hirede
for Uortimer þe gode king of þan swikedom nuste naþing
for he isah Rouuenne halden þene bolle
 and drinken half þat ilke win þat heo heuede idon þerin
Þa hit com to þare nihte þa todælleden hiredcnihtes
 and þa ufele Rouwenne wende to hire inne
 and alle hire cnihtes mid hire uorþrihtes
Þa heihte heo hire sweines and ec þaie þeines
þat heo an hiȝinge heore hors sculden sadelien
 and heo swiþe stille stelen ut of buruwe
 and wenden al bi nihte to Þwoncchestre uorþrihte
 and þer swiþe vaste biclusen heom in ane castle
 and luȝen Uortigerne þat his sune hine wolde biliggen
 and Vortigerne þe swikele king ilæfde þare læsing
Nu vnderȝat Uortimer his sune þat he hefde atter inomen
ne mihte na lechecraft helpen him næ wiht
He nom feole sonden and sende ȝeond his londe
 and hehte alle his cnihtes to him comen forþrihtes
Þa þat folc was icumen þa wes þe king swiþe untrumed
þa ȝirnde þe king heore griþ and þus he spac hem alle wiþ
Alre cnihten wrþ eow best þe heren æie kinge
þer nis nan oþer red buten hiȝendliche ich beo dæd
hir ich bitæche eow mi lond al mi seoluer and al mi gold
 and alle mine maþmes eowre monscipe is þa mare
 and ȝe forþrihtes senden after cnihtes
 and ȝeuen heom soluer and gold and hældeþ ȝe seolf eowre lond 
 and wrekeþ eow ȝif ȝe cunnen of Sexisce monnen
uor weonne so ich beo uorþfaren Hengest eow wul makien kare
 and nimeþ mine likamæ and leggeþ an chæsten
 and ledeþ me to þare sæstronde þer Saxisce men wulleþ cumen a lond
Anan swa heo me þer witen awæi heo wulleþ wenden
nouþer quic ne dead ne durren heo me abiden
Imong þissen dome dæd iwarþ þe gode king
þer wes wop þer wes rop and reuliche iberen
Heo nomen þes kinges licame and ladden to Lundene
 and bisides Bælȝesȝate fæire hine biburȝeden
 and nawiht hine ne ladden alse þe king heihte
Þus liuede Uortimer and þus he endede þar
Þa iueolen Bruttes a balufulle ræde
heo nomen Uortigerne anan and bitahten heom þesne kenedom
welle reoulich wes þer a þing nu was Vortigerne æft king
Uortigerne nom his sonde and sende to Sexlonde
 and grette wel Hengest cnihten alre væirest
 and bad hine an hiȝinge comen to þisse londe
 and mid him brouhte here an hundred ridæren
For þat wite þu þuru alle þing þat dead is Vortimer þe king
 and siker þu miht hider comen for dæd is Fortimer mi sune
Nis þe non neod to bringen mid þe muchel genge
leste ure Bruttes æft beon abolȝen
þat eow æft seorwen siȝen bitweonen
Hengest somnede uærde of feole cunne ærde
þat he hefde to iwiten seouen hundred scipen
 and ælc scip he dihte mid þreo hundred cniten
i þere Temese at Lundene Hengest com to londe
Þat word com ful sone to Uortigerne þan kinge
þat Hengest was in hauene mid seouen hundred scipene
Ofte was Uortigerne wa neuer wrse þan þæ
 and Bruttes weoren sari and seorhful an heorte
nusten heo an worldriche ræd þat heom weore ilike
Hengest was of ufele war þat he wel cudde þær
he nom sone his sonde and sende to þan kinge
 and grette Uortigerne king mid swiþe uæire worden
 and seide þat he was icumen swa fader sculde to his sune
mid sibbe and mid saihte he wolde on sele wunien
griþ he wolde luuien unriht he wolde scunien 
griþ he wolde habben griþ he wolde holden
 and al þis leodisce folc luuien he wolde
 and Uortigerne þene king luuien þurh alle þing
Ah he hefde ibroht i þis lond ut of Sexleoden
seouen hundred scipene of hæþene folke
þat beoþ þe alre wihteste men þat wunieþ under sunnen
 and ich wulle quaþ Hengest leden heo to þan kinge
to an isette dæie atforen al his duȝeþe
 and þe king scal arisen and of þan cnihten cheosen
twa hundred cnihten to leden to his fihten
þe sculen biwiten þene king durewurþliche þurh alle þing
 and seoþþen scullen þa oþere uaren to heore ærde
mid sibbe and mid sæle aȝen to Sæxlonde
 and ich wulle bilæuen mid monnen alre selest
þat is Uortigerne þe king þe ich luuie þurh alle þing
Þat word com to Brutten hu Hengest bihæhte heom
þa weoren heo uæine uor uæiren his worden
 and setten griþ and setten friþ to whulchen ane uirste
þe king an ane dæie wolde iseon þas duȝeþe
Þat iherde Hengest cnihten alre uæirest
Þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes neuer ær an liue
for he þohte swike þene king an his riche
Her iwraþ Hengest cnihte uorcuþest
swa biþ æuerælc mon þe biswikeþ þe him wel on
Wha wolde wenen a þissere weorldriche
þat Hengest swiken þohte þene king þat hæfde his dohter
for nis nauer nan mon þat me ne mai mid swikedome ouergan
Heo nomen ænne isetne dæi þat scolden þas duȝeþen
cumen heom tosomne mid sæhte and mid sibbe
an ane uælde þe wæs muri anuast Ambresburi
Þe stude wes Ælenge nu hatte hit Stanhenge
Þer Hengest þe swike æiþer bi worde and bi write
cuþde þan kinge þat he cumen wolde
mid his monuerde to wurþscipe þes kinges
ah he nalde bringen on drihte buten þreo hundred cnihten
þa alre wiseste men þe he mihte uinden
 and þe king brohte al swa ueole baldere þeinen
and þeo weoren þa alre witereste þe wuneden on Bruttene
mid goden heore iweden al buten wepnen
þat heom no towurþen þurh þrist of þan wepnen
Þus heo hit speken and æft heo hit tobreken 
for Hængest þe leodswike þus he his gon learen
þat ælc nome a long sax and læiden bi his sconke
wiþinne his hose þer he hit mihte hæle
Þenne heo comen tosomne Sæxes and Bruttes
þenne queþ Hengest cnihten alre swikelest
Hail seo þu lauerd king ælc þe is þin vnderling
Ȝif æuere æi of þine gume gære haueþ bisiden
send hit mid freondscipe feor from us seoluen
 and beon we on sele and motegen of sahte
nu we maȝen mid sibben ure lif libben
Þus þe baldefulle mon bispac þer þa Bruttes
Þa andswarede Uortiger her he wes to vnwar
Ȝif here is æi cniht swa wod þat wepnen habbe bi siden
he scal leosen þa hond þurh his aȝene brand
buten he hit sone heonene isende
Heore wepnen heo awæi senden þa nefden heo noht an honden
cnihtes eoden upward cnihtes eoden adonward
ælc spac wiþ oþer swulc he weore his broþer
Þa weoren Bruttes imænged wiþ þan Saxes
Þa cleopede Hengest cnihtene swikelæst
Nimeþ eoure sexes sele mine bernes
 and ohtliche eou sturieþ and nænne ne sparieþ
Bruttes þer weoren riche ah ne cuþe heo noht þa speche
whæt þa Saxisce men seiden heom bitweonen
Heo breoden ut þa sæxes alle bihalues
heo smiten an riht half heo smiten an lift half
biuoren and bihinden heo leiden heom to grunde
alle heo sloȝen þat heo neh comen
of þes kinges monnen sone þer feollen
feouwer hundred and fife wa wes þan kinge on liue
Þa Hengest hine igrap mid grimmen his gripen
 and bi þan mantle hine ibræid þat breken þa strenges
 and Sæxes him sette to and wolden þene king fordon
 and Hengest hine gon werien and nalde hit noht iþeuen
ah he heold hine ful faste þe while þat feht ilaste
Þer wes moni riche Brut biræfued þan liue
Summe heo fluȝen swiþe ofer þene feld brade
 and wereden heom mid stanen for wepnen næfden heo nane
Þer wes swiþe hard fiht þer feol moni god cniht
Þer wes of Salesburi an oht bonde icumen 
ænne muchelne mæin clubbe he bar an his rugge
Þa wes þer an aþele eorl Aldulf ihaten
cniht mid þan bezste he æhte Glochæstre
he to þan cheorle leop swulc hit a liun weoren
 and binom him þe clubbe þa he bar an rugge
æuere wulcne swa he smat þer forþrihtes he iwat
biforen and bihinden he laide heom to grunde
Þreo and fifti he þer sloh and seoþþe to ane stede droh
he leop uppen stede and swiþe gon him riden
he ærde to Glochæstre and þe ȝates læc ful feste
 and anan forþrihtes lette ærmi his cnihtes
ȝeond alle þan londe and nomen þat heo funden
heo nomen orf heo nomen corn and al þat heo quic funden
 and brohten to burhȝe vnnimete blisse
þa ȝæten heo tunden uaste and wel heom biwusten
Lete we hit þus stonden and speken of þan kinge
Sexes him leoppe to and wolde þene king fordo
Hengest cleopede uorþrihtes Aswikeþ mine cnihtes
ne sculle ȝe hine noht forfaren for us he haueþ ihaued mucle care
 and he haueþ to quene mine dohter þa is scone
ah alle his burhȝes he scal us bitæchen
ȝif he wule his lif broken oþer ælles him is balu ȝiueþe
Þa wes Uortigerne væste ibunden
giues swiþe grete heo duden an his foten
ne moste he nauere biten mete ne wiþ nenne freond speken
ær he heom hæfden isworen uppen halidom þat wes icoren
þat he al þis kinelond wolde bitæchen heom an heond
burhȝes and castles and al his comelan
 and al swa he idode ase hit idemed was
 and Hengest nom an his hond al þis riche kinelond
 and delde his leoden muchel of þisse londe
he ȝæf æne eorle al Kent ase hit bi Lundene went
he ȝæf his stiwarde Æstsex
 and his burþeine Middelsax bitahte
Þa cnihtes hit atfengen and ane while heo heolden
þa while Uortigerne ȝeond þis lond ferde
 and bitahte Hengest hæȝen his burhȝes
 and Hengest forþrihtes dude þerin his cnihtes
þa while muchel smal folc læi inne Suþsæxe
 and inne Middelsæxe muchel of þan kunne 
 and inne Æstsaxe heore aþeleste ȝuȝeþe
Mete heo ferden al þat heo funden
heo forlæiȝen þa wif and Godes laȝen breken
heo duden i þan londe al þat heo wolden
Þat iseȝen Bruttes þat balu wes on londe
 and hu Sæxisce men isiȝen weoren to heom
Bruttes scupten þan londe nome for Sæxisce monnen scome
 and for þan swikedome þat heo idon hæfden
for þan þe heo mid cnifen biræueden heom at liue
þa cleopeden heo þat lond al Æstsæx and Westsæx
 and þat þridde Middelsæx
Vortigerne þe king bitahte heom al þis lond
þat ne bilæfde him an honde a turf of londe
 and himseolf Vortigerne flæh ouer Sæuærne
feor into Wellisce londe and þer he gon atstonde
 and his hired mid him þe hæne wes iwurþen
 and he hæfde an horde gersume swiþe stronge
he lette his men riden widen and siden
and lette him to bonnen of ælches cunnes monnen
þe æuere wolden his feoh mid freondscipe ȝirnen
Þat iherden Bruttes þat iherden Scottes
to him heo comen þerafter ful sone
an ælchere side þider heo gunnen riden
monies hæȝes monnes sune for golde and for gærsume
Þa hæfde he tosomne sixti þusend monnen
þa sumnede he þa richen þa wel cuþen ræden
Gode men rædeþ me ræd uor me is swiþe muchel neod
whar ich mihte on wilderne wurchen ænne castel
þer ic mihte an inne libbe mid mine monnen
 and halden hine wiþ Hengest mid hæȝere strengþe
a þat ich mihte bæt burhȝen iwinnen
wræken me a mine feonden þa mine wines feolden
 and habbeþ al mi kinelond awræht ut of mire hond
 and þus me iflæmed mine fulle ifan
Þa andswerede a wis mon þe wel cuþe ræden
Lust me nu lauerd king ich þe cuþe god þing
uppen þan munte of Reir ich wullen ræden
þat þu castel wurche mid stronge stan walle
for þer þu miht wunien and libben mid winne 
 and ȝet þu hauest a þire hond muchel seoluer and gold
to halden þine hired þa þe helpen scal
 and swa þu miht on liue libben alræ sælest
Þa andswerede þe king Let hit cuþen an hiȝing
ȝeond muchele mire ferde þæt ich faren wulle
to þan munte of Reir and ræren þer castel
Forþ ferde þe king and þa ferde mid him
Þa heo þider comen dic heo bigunnen sone
Hornes þer bleouwen machunnes heowen
lim heo gunnen bærnen ȝeond þat lond ærnen
 and al Wæst Walsce lond setten a Uortigernes hond
al heo hit nomen þat heo neh comen
Þa þe dic wes idoluen and allunge ideoped
þa bigunnen heo wal a þere dic oueral
 and heo lim and stan leiden tosomne
of machunes þer wes wunder fif and twenti hundred
A dæi heo leiden þene wal a niht he feol oueral
a marwe heo hine arædden a niht he gon toreosen
Fulle seouen nihte swa heom dihte
ælche dæi heo hine aredden and ælche niht he gon reosen
Þa wes sari þe king and sorhful þurh alle þing
swa wes al þa uerde ladliche offæred
for æuere heo lokede whænne Hengest come anuuenan
Þe king wes ful særi and sende after witien
æfter worldwise monne þa wisdom cuþen
 and bad heom leoten weorpen and fondien leodrunen
fondien þat soþe mid heore siȝecraften
whæron hit weore ilong þat þe wal þe wes swa strong
ne moste nihtlonges nauere istonden
Þas weorldewise men þer a twa wenden
summe heo wenden to þan wude summe to weienlæten
heo gunnen loten weorpen mid heore leodrunen
fulle þreo nihten heore craftes heo dihten
Ne mihten heo nauere finden þurh nauere nane þinge
whæron hit weore ilong þat þe wal þat wes swa strong
æuereælche nihte toras and þe king his swinc læs
Buten witie þer wes an he wes ihaten Ioram
he seide þat he hit afunde ah hit þuhte læsinge
he seide ȝif mon funde in auer æi londe 
æuer æi cniht bærn þe næuere fæder no ibæd
 and openede his breoste and nomen of his blode
 and mengde wiþ þan lime and þæne wal læide
þenne mihte he stonde to þere worlde longe
Þat word com to þan kinge of þere læsinge
 and he hit ilefde þah hit læs weore
Sone he nom his sonde and sende ȝeond þan londe
swa feor swa he for dæþes kare dursten æies weies faren
 and in ælche tune hercneden þa runen
whær heo mihten ifinden speken of swulche childe
Þas cnihtes forþ ferden widen ȝeond þan ærde
tweien uerden ænne wæi þe westriht him læi
þe læi forþrihtes in þer nu is Kaermerþin
Bisides þere burh in ane weie brade
hefden ænne muchelne plæȝe alle þa burhcnauen
Þas cnihtes weoren weri and an heorte swiþe særi
 and seten adun bi þan plaȝe and biheolden þas cnauen
Vmben ane stunde heo bigunnen striuinge
alse hit wes auer laȝe imong childrene plæȝe
þe an þe oþerne smat and he þeos duntes abad
Þa wes swiþe grim Dinabuz touward Mærlin
 and þus quaþ Dinabus þe þene dunt hefde
Mærling vnwærste man whu hæuest þu me þus idon
þu hauest idon me muchel scome þerfore þu scalt habben grome
Ich æm anes kinges sune and þu ært of noht icumen
Þv nahtes i nane stude habben freo monnes ibude
for swa wes al þa uore þi moder wes an hore
for nuste heo næuere þene mon þat þe streonde hire on
no þu on moncunne nefdest fader nenne
 and þu in ure londe makest us to sconde
þu ært us imong icumen and nært nænes monnes sune
þu scalt i þissen dæie þeruore dæd þolien
þis iherden þa cnihtes þer heo weoren bihalues
heo arisen up and eoden neor and neodeliche ȝerden
of þissere uncuþe talen þe heo iherden of þan cnauen
Þa wes inne Kairmerþin a reue þe hehte Eli
þa cnihtes biliue comen to þan reue
 and þus him to sæiden sone mid muþe
We buþ herrihtes Uortigernes cnihtes 
 and habbeoþ her ifunde enne cnaue ȝunge
he is ihaten Merlin ne icnawe we nawiþt his cunne
Nim hine an hiȝinge and sende hine to þan kinge
alse þu wult libben and þine limen habben
 and his moder mid him þe hine bar to monnen
ȝif þu þis wult don þe king heom wule underfon
 and ȝif þu hit noht ne ȝemest þerfore þu bist flæme
 and þas burh al forbard þas leoden al fordemed
Þa answarede Eli þe reue of Kæirmerþin
Wel ic wat þat al þis lond stunt a Vortigernes hond
 and we beoþ alle his men his monscipe is þe mare
 and we scullen þis don fain and driȝen his wille
Forþ wende þe reue and burhmen his iuere
 and ifunden Mærlin and his plaȝeiueren mid him
Mærlin heo nomen and his iuæren loȝen
Þa þa Mærling wes ilad þa wes Dinabus ful glad
e wende þat he ilad weore limen for to leosen
ah al anoþer set þe dom ær hit weoren al idon
Nu wes Mærlinges moder wunder mere iwurþen
in ane haȝe munstre munchene ihaded
Þider iwende Eli þe reue of Kairmerþin
 and nom him þa lafdie þer heo læi on munstre
 and uorþ him gon ærne to þan kinge Uortigerne
 and muchel folc mid him and ladden þa nunne and Merlin
Sone wes þat word cuþ to Vortigernes kinges muþ
þat icumen wes Eli and brohte þa lauedi
 and Marling heore sune wes mid hire þer icumen
Þa wes an liue Vortigerne bliþe
 and þa læuedi aueng mid swiþe uæire læten
 and Mærlin he bitahte goden twælf cnihten
þa weoren þan kinge holde and hine witen scolden
Þa sæiden þe king Vortiger wiþ þa nunne he spilede þer
Gode læuedi sæi me sæl þe scal iwurþe
whar weoren þu iboren Wha streonede þe to bearne
Þæ andswarede þa nunne and hire fader nemnede
Þriddendale þis lond stod a mines fader hond
of þan londe he wes king cuþ hit wes wide
he wes ihaten Conaan cnihtene lauerd
Þa answarede þe king swulc heo his cun weore 
Lauedi sæie þu hit me sæl þe scal iwurþen
her is Mærlin þi sune wha streonede hine
Who wes him a folke for fader iholden
Þa heng heo hire hæfued and heolde touward bræsten
bi þan kinge heo sæt ful softe and ane lutle while þohte
vmbe while heo spac and spilede wiþ þan kinge
King ich þe wulle tellen for seolcuþe spellen
Mi fader Conaan þe king luuede me þurh alle þing
þa iwarþ ich on vestme wunder ane fæir
Þa ich wes an uore fiftene ȝere
þa wunede ich on bure on wunsele mine
maidene mid me wunder ane uæire
þenne ich wæs on bedde iswaued mid soft mine slepen
þen com biuoren þa fæireste þing þat wes iboren
swulc hit weore a muchel cniht al of golde idiht
Þis ich isæh on sweuene alche niht on slepe
Þis þing glad me biuoren and glitenede on golde
ofte hit me custe ofte hit me clupte
ofte hit me tobæh and eode me swiþe neh
Þa ich an ænde me bisæh selcuþ me þuhte þas
mi mæte me wes læþ mine limes uncuþe
selcuþ me þuhte what hit beon mihte
Þa anȝæt ich on ænde þat ich was mid childe
þa mi time com þisne cnaue ich hæfuede
Nat ic on folde what his fader weoren
ne wha hine biȝate inne weorlderiche
no whaþer hit weore unwiht þe on Godes halue idiht
La swa ich ibedde are nat ich namare
to suggen þe of mine sune hu he to worulde is icume
Þe nunne beh hire hæfde adun and hire huȝe dihte
þe king hine biþohte whæt he don mihte
 and droh him to ræde redȝiuen gode
 and heo him radden ræd mid þan bezste
þat he ofsende Magan þat wes a selcuþ mon
He wes a wis clærc and cuþe of feole cræften
he cuþe wel ræden he cuþe feor læden
he cuþe of þan crafte þe wuneþ i þan lufte
he cuþe tellen of ælche leodspelle
Magan com to hirede þar þe king wunede 
 and þene king grætte mid godfulle worde
Hail seo þu and sund Vortigerne þe king
Ich æm icumen to þe cuþ me þine iwille
Þa andswærede þe king and talde al þan clærke
hu þa nunne hafde isæid and axede hine þer of ræd
ord fram þan ende al he him talde
Þa sæide Magan Ich con ful wel heron
Þer wunieþ in þan lufte feole cunne wihte
þa þer scullen bilæfuen þat Domesdæi cume liþen
Summe heo beoþ aþele and summe heo uuel wurcheþ
Þeron is swiþe muchel cun þa cumeþ imong monnen
heo beoþ ihaten ful iwis incubii demones
Ne doþ heo noht muchel scaþe bute hokerieþ þan folke
monine mon on sweuene ofte heo swencheþ
 and monienne hende wimmon þurh heore cræfte kenneþ anan
 and monies godes monnes child heo bicharreþ þurh wigeling
 and þus wes Marlin biȝeten and iboren of his moder
 and þus hit is al igan quaþ þe clærc Magan
þa sæide Marling to seolue þan kinge
King þine men me habbeoþ inumen and ich æm to þe icumen
 and ich iwiten wulle what beon þi wille
 and for wulche þinge ich æm ibroht to kinge
Þa spilede þe king mid cwikere speche
Mærlin þu ært hider icumen þu nært nanes monnes sune
Swiþe þe longeþ after laþe spelle
Iwhiten þu wult þa uore nu þu hit scalt ihere
Ich habbe bigunnen a weorc mid grundliche strengþe
þe haueþ mine gærsume wel swiþe binume
fif þusend men wurcheþ þeron
Ich habbe lim and stan on leode nis betere nan
na in nare leode weorcmen al swa gode
Al þat heo leggeoþ a dæi to soþe ich hit sugge mæi
ær dæi amarwen al hit biþ dune
ælc stan from oþer iualled to þan grunde
Nu suggeþ mine wise and mine witie men
þat ȝif ich mine þi blod ut of þire breoste
 and minne wal wurche and do to mine lime
þenne mai he stonde to þere worlde longe 
Nu þu hit wost al hu þe iwurþe scal
Þis ihærde Mærlin and bælh on his mode
 and þas word sæide wraþ þeh he weore
Nulle hit nauere God seolf þe gumenene is lauerd
þat þi castel stonde for mine heorte blode
ne nauere þi stan wal stille ne ligge
For alle þine witien beo swiþe swikele
i sæiþ læssinge biforen þæ seolue
þat þu scalt afinde a þisses dæies ferste
for þis sæde Ioram þe is mi fulle ifa
þa tiþende me þuncheþ game ich wes iscæpen him to bone
Let cumen biuoren Ioram þine witie
 and alle his iuere forþrihtes here
þa þeos lesinge talden þan kinge
 and ȝif ich þe sugge soþe mine worde
of þine walle and whi he adun falleþ
and mid soþe hit bitelle þat heore talen sinde lese
ȝef me heore hæfden ȝif ich þi wærc hæle
Þa andswarede þe king mid quickere steuene
Swa me helpe min hond þis forwærde ich þe halde
To þan kinge was ibroht Ioram þe witie
 and seofue of his iueren alle heo weoren uæie
Marline gromede and he grimliche spæc
Sæie me Ioram leodswike laþ me on heorten
whi falleþ þes wal uolden to grunde
Sæie me whæ hit vælleþ þat þe wal reoseþ
What mai man uinden at þere dicgrunde
Ioram wes stille ne cuþe he noht tellen
Þa seide Merlin þas word King hald me forward
Let deluen þas dich seouen uoten deopere
Heo scullen uinden ænne stan wunder ane ueire
he is ueir and brad volke to bihalden
Þa dich wes idoluen seoue vet depre
þa uunden heo anan þerrihtes þene stan 
Þa sæide Mærlin þas word King hald me forward
Sæie me Ioram monne me laþest
 and sæie þisse kinge wulches cunnes þinges
vnder þissen stane staþel habbeoþ inumen
Ioram wes stille ne cuþe he noht telle
Þa sæide Mærlin wunder A water her is under
Doh awai þisne stan þat water ȝe findeþ anan
Heo duden awæi þene stan atforen þan kinge anon
þat water heo funden þa sæide Merlin
Æxe me Ioram þe is mi fulle ifa
umben ane stunde suggen þe of þan grunde
what wuneþ i þan watere wintres and summeres
Þe king axede Ioram ah ne cuþe he nowiht þeron
Þa ȝet sæide Mærlin þas word King hald me foreward
Let alæten þis wæter and wei weorpen
Þer wunieþ i þan grunde tweien draken stronge
Þe an is a norþ half þe oþer a suþ half
þe oþer is milcwhit ælche deore unnilich
þe oþer ræd alse blod wurmen alre baldest
Ælche middernihte heo biginneþ to fihten
and þurh hire fihte feollen þine wurckes
þa eorþe gon torusien and þi wal toreosen
þurh swulche wundre þi wal is afallen
þa iwraþ i þissen flode and noht for mine blode
Þis wæter wes al ilæde þes kinges men weoren glæde
muchel wes þa blisse biuoren þan leodkinge
 and sone þeræfter sari heo weoren
ær þe dæi come to ende heo iherden tiþinde
Þa þa water wes al ilædden and þe put wes ilær
þa comen ut þas tweien draken and muchel dunen makeden
 and fuhten grimliche dun i þere dich
Ne isæh nauere na cniht nan ladluker fiht
fluȝen of heore muþe fures leomen
Þis isah þe leodking grimme heore lates
Þa wes he awundred on þissere wurlderiche
what weore þis tacninge þa he isæh þer on grunde
 and hu Mærlin hit wuste þat nan oþer mon nuste
Ærest wes þe white buuen and seoþþen he wes bineoþen
 and þe drake ræde forwundede hine to dæþe
and æiþer wende to his hole ne isæh heom seoþþe na mon iboren
Þus ferden þeos þing þat isah Vortigerne þe king
and alle þe weoren mid him luueden swiþe Mærlin
 and þe king hatede Ioram and his hæfued him binam
 and his seouene iueren þe mid him weoren þære
To telde eode þe king and mid him lædde Mærlin 
 and seide him mid mucle luue Mærling þu ært wilcume
 and ich þe ȝiuen wulle al þat þu ȝirnest
of mine londe of seoluere and of golde
He wende þurh Mærlin þat lond al iwinnen
ah al oþer hit wende ær comen þes daies ende
Þus fræinede þe king his leofe freond Merlin
Sæie me nu Merlin monnen me leofuest
what bitacnieþ þa draken þe þene dune makeden
þe stan and þat water and þat wunderliche fæht
Sæie me ȝif þi wil is whæt bitacneþ al þis
 and seoþþen þu most me ræden hu ich scal me læden
 and hu ich mai biwinne kinedom minne
of Hengest mines wiues fader þe swiþe me hæfþ iharmed
Þa andswarede Merlin þane kinge þe spac wiþ him
King þu ært unwis and vnwiter a ræde
Þu fræinest of þan draken þe þene dune makeden
 and whæt tacneþ heore fiht and heore feondliche gripen
Heo tacneþ kinges þa sunde to cumene
 and heore fiht and heore uare and heore uæi uolc
Ah ȝif þu weore swa wis mon and swa witter a þoncke
þat þv fræinedest me of feole þine sorȝen
of þire mucle kare þa þe is to cumene
ich þe wolde suggen of sorȝe þine
Þa quaþ Vortiger þe king Leofue freond Merling
sæie me of þan þinge þe me to cumen sonden
Bluþeliche quad Mærlin baldere stefne
ich þe wulle suggen ah æuere hit wule þe reouwen
King king bisiȝ þe Sorȝen þe biþ ȝeueþe
of Costantines cunne his bern þu aqualdest
Þu lettest slæn Costanz þe wes king a þis lond
þu lettest þine Peohtes hine ladliche biswiken
þeruore þu ibidest alre baluwene mæst
Seoþþen þu tuȝen uuenon þe uncuþe leoden
Saxes to londe þeruore þu wurþest to sconde
Nu beoþ of Brutaine beornes ariued
hit his Aurilien and Vther nu þu ært þærof war
Heo cumeþ tomærȝen fuliwis i þis lond at Tottenæs
ich do þe wel to witene mid seouen hundred scipene
 and nu heo inne sæ seilieþ biliue 
Þu hauest heom muchel uuel idon and nu þu most þat laþ onfon
þu hauest a ba halue bone þe þe þencheþ
þine ifan þe biuoren and þine ifeond bæften
Ah flih flih þinne wæi and burh þine life
 and fleo þider þe þu fleo heo þe wulleþ after teon
Ambrosie Aurilien he hæueþ ærest þisne kinedom
ah he þurh atterne drench dæþ scal iþolien
 and seoþþen scal Vther Pendragon habben þesne kinedom
ah þi cun hine scal mid attere aquellen
ah ær he dæd þolie he scæl dune makien
Vther scal habben ænne sune of Cornwaille he scal cumen
þat beoþ a wilde bar iburstled mid stele
Þe bar scal forbærnen hæhȝe þa burhȝes
he scal alle þa swiken swenien mid eiȝe
he scal al þi riche cun mid witen aquellen
he biþ swiþe oht mon and aþele an þonke
heonenæ into Rome rixleþ þeos ilke
scal he alle his feond fallen to grunde
Soþ ich habbe þe isæid ah nis þe na þe softre
ah flih mid þine verde þine iuon þe cumeþ to herede
Þa aswac worden Merlin þe wise
 and þe king lette blawen þreottene bemen
 and forþ mid his ferde feondliche swiþe
Nes þer uorþrihtes bute uirst of ane nihte
þat comen þa broþere beien tosome
to sæstronde ful iwis at Dertenemuþe i Totenas
Þis iherden Bruttes and weoren bliþe ful iwis
Heo droȝen ut of þan wuden and of þan wulderne
bi sixti and bi sixti and bi seouen hundred
bi þritti and bi þritti and bi feole þusend
Þa heo comen tosomne ful sel hit heo þuhte
Þa broþeren to þissen ærde brohten vnimete verde
 and her comen heom biuoren balde þas Bruttes
vnimete uolc al hit wræh þa wolde
þæ ær weoren ȝeond wudes wunderliche todreued
þurh þene muchelne æie and þurh þe muclen ærmþe
 and þurh þene mucle hærm þa Hengest heom wrohte
 and hafde alle heore hæfdmen mid cniuen amurþerd 
mid sæxen tosnæþde snelle þe þeines
Bruttes heolden husting mid heȝe wisdome
heo nomen Aurilien þene ældre broþer anan
inne hæȝe hustinge and heouen hine to kinge
Þa weoren Bruttes mid blisse auulled
bliþe an mode þæ ær weoren murne
Comen þas tiþende to Vortigerne þan kinge
þat Aurilien wes icoren and to kinge iheouen
Þa wes Vortiger wa and æft him wes wurse
Vortiger uerde ver to ane castle
Genoire hæhte hæh an ane munte
Cloard hæhte þe munt and Hærgin hahte þat lond
onvæst Wæie þe is a water hende
Vortigernes men nomen al þat heo neh comen
heo nomen wepnen and mete a moni are wise
to þan castle heo brohten swa muchel swa heo rohten
þat heo inoh hafden þeh hit lutel hulpe
Aurilien and Vther weoren of Vortigerne war
whær he wes uppen Cloward biclused in castlen
Heo letten blawen bemen bonnien heore uerde
volc unimete of moni ane londe
ferden to Genoire þær læi Vortigerne
King wes wiþuten king wes wiþinnen
cnihtes þer fuhten mid feondliche ræsen
æuerælc god mon gurede hine seolfuen
Þa heo iseȝen þat heo siȝen næfden
þa to wude wenden wunder muche uerde
Heo uelden þæne wude adun and droȝen to þan castle
 and fulden al þæ dic þe wes wunder ane deop
Fur heo in sende on æuerælche ende
 and cleopeden to Vortiger Nu þu scalt þe warmen þer
for þu sloȝe Costanz þe wes king of þis lond
 and seoþþe Costantin his sune Nu is Aurilie icumen
 and Vther his broþer þa þe balu sendeþ
Þe wind wæht þat fur þat hit wunderliche born
þe castel gon to bernen bures þer swælden
feollen þa hellen floȝen to grunde
Ne mihten þer na cniht aȝeines þe fure makien fiht
þat fur eode oueral and barnde hus and barnde wal 
 and þe king Vortigerne þerinne he gon to berne
al hit forswælde þat þerinne wunede
Þus ændede þer mid muchele ærme Vortiger
Þa hafde al þat lond Aurilie an his hond
Þer wes þe aþele eorl Aldolf ihaten
he wes of Gloucestre cnihten alre glæuest
þær Aurilie i þan ærde makede hine stiwærd
Þa hæfde Aurilien and Vther his broþer
heore ifan auelde and weoren þerfore þe bliþere
Þis iherden Hengest cnihten alre strengest
þa wes he auæred feondliche swiþe
He fusde his ferde and flæh touward Scotten
 and Aurilie þe king æfter him uerde an hiȝinge
 and Hengest þuhte þat he walde mid al his monuerde
ȝif me onsohte him fleon into Scotte
þat he mihte mid wiȝele þanene atwinden
ȝif he ne mihte i þan londe uor Aurilie atstonde
Aurilie ferde uorþ and droh his folc riht norþ
mid alle his imihte fulle seouen nihte
Bruttes weoren balde and rehten ouer walde
þa hafde Aurilien vnimete uerde
he funde west lond leoden ofslæȝene
chiriches furbarnde Bruttes forswæled
Þa sæide Aurilie þe king Bruttene deorling
Ȝif ich mot ibiden þat ich aȝæn ride
 and hit wulle Drihte þe scop þes daȝes lihte
þat ich mote mid isunde biȝite mine ikunde
chirchen ich wulle arære and God ich wulle hæren
ich wulle alche cnihte ȝeuen his irihte
 and auerælche beorne þan ælden and þan ȝungen
ich wulle milden wurþen
ȝif Godd me wule ivnnæ min æþel to biwinnen
To Hengeste comen tidende of Aurilie þan kinge
Þa spac Hengest cnihten alre swikelest
Hærcneþ nu mi men monscipe eou is ȝiueþe
her cumeþ Aurilie and Vther his broþer eke
heo bringeþ swiþe muchel folc ah alle heo beoþ fæie
For vnwis is þe king swa beoþ his cnihtes
 and a cnaue is his broþer þe an alse þe oþer 
þerfore maȝen Bruttes beon muchele þe vnbaldur
þenne þat hæfd is unwræst þe hælp is þæ wurse
 and wel ȝe hit maȝen imunen þat ich wulle mæinen
betere beoþ ure fifti þænne heore fif hundred
þat heo feole siþen ifonded habbeoþ
seoþþen heo an londe fondeden leoden
For cuþ hit is wide of ure wiþerdeden
þat we beoþ kempen icud mid þan bezsten
We scullen aȝen heom stonden and driuen heom of londen
and walden þas riche after ure iwille
Þus bælde Hængest cnihten alre hændest
balde his ferde þer heo wes an felde
ah oþer weies hit was idiht ær come seouen niht
Forþ comen þa tiþinde to Aurilie þan kinge
whær Hengest wunede buuen are munede
Aurilien hafde to iueren þritti þusend rideren
baldere Brutten þe heore beot makeden
 and æc he hafde Walisce wunder ane monie
Þa lette he his cnihtes dæies and nihtes
æuere beon iwepned alse heo to wiȝe scolden
for auere he care hafde of heþene uolke
Þa iherde Hengest þat Aurilien wes onuast
nom he his ferde and fusde him toȝaines
Þa wes Aurilie wær þat Hengest wolde cumen þær
he uærde in ane velde wel iwepned under scelde
nom he forþrihtes ten þusend cnihtes
þa weoren bezst iboren and of his ferde coren
 and setten heom a þan felde auoten under scelde
Ten þusend Walisce he to wude sende
ten þusend Scottes he sende bihalues
þe hæþene to imete bi stiȝen and bi straten
himseolf he nom his eorles and his aþele kempes
 and his holdeste men þa he hæfde an londe
 and makede his sceldtrume swulc hit weoren an hær wude
Fif þusend þer riden þa sculden al þis folc biwiten
Þa cleopede Aldolf eorl of Gloucestre
Ȝif hit me on Drihte þe alle domes waldeþ
þat ich mote ibide þat Hængest cume riden
þa is a þissen londe swa longe atstonde 
 and biswac mine leofe freondes mid longe his sæxes
bisiden Amberesburi mid ærmliche witen
Ah ȝif ich mihte of þan eorlen þat aþel me biwinnen
þenne mihte ich suggen soþ quides mine
þat me hafde Godd seolf godes iunnen
ȝif ich mine ifan fallen to grunde anan
 and wræken mi deore cun þat heo habbeoþ ilæid adun
Vnneæþe wes þis spel isæid to þan ende
þa iseȝen heo Hængest halden ouer dune
Mid vnimete ferden feondliche heo fusden
tosomne heo comen and feondliche heo sloȝen
þer þa ræȝe men togæderen heom ræsden
helmes gunnen gullen cnihtes þer feollen
stel eode wiþ þan ban balu þer wes riue
urnen inne strete stremes of blode
faȝeden þa feldes and þat gras falewede
Þa iseh Hængest þat his help trukede
þa hald he fram fæhte and bihalues flæh
 and his folc after fusde biliue
Þa Cristine liþen after and heom on læiden
 and cleopeden Crist Godes sone beon heom a fultume
 and þe heþene leoden æc lude cleopeden
Ure godd Teruagant whi trukest þu us an hond
Þa Hengest isæh þa hæþene ibuȝene
 and þa Cristine men cumen heom anufene
þa fleh Henges þurh and þurh þat he com to Kuniggesburh
i þare burh he wende burh to brukene
 and þe king Aurilien after wende anan
 and clepede to his leoden ludere stæuene
Ærneþ æuere vorþ and vorþ Hengest is ifaren norþ
 and heo him after buȝen þat heo to burhȝe comen
Þa isæh Hengest and his sune al þa uerde heom after cumen
þa sæide Hengest cnihten alre wraþest
Nulle ich na mare fleon ah nu ich wulle fihten
 and mi sune Octa and his wedbroþer Ebissa
 and al mi monuerde sturieþ eouwer wepnen
 and fare we heom toȝænes and makien feondslæhtes
 and ȝif we hom ne falleþ þænne beon we fæie
ilæid on felde and freonde bidælde
Hengest bah a þene wald and bilæfde al his teld 
 and makede his sceldtrume al of his hæþene gumen
Þa com Aurilie þe king and moni þusend mid him
and bigunnen þer oþer fæht þe wes feondliche stærc
þer wes moni græt dunt idæld i þan compe
þer weoren þa Cristine wel neh ouercumene
Þa comen þer uaren fif þusend rideren
þa Aurilie hafde an horse to fihten
heo smiten a þan hæþene þat heo adun helden
þer wes feht swiþe stor eornest ful sturne
I þan fæhte com þe eorl Aldolf of Gloucetre
 and ifunde Hengest cnihten forcuþþest
whar he feondliche faht and þa Cristine feolde
Aldolf his gode sweord adroh and uppen Hengest sloh
 and Hengest warp þene sceld biuoren and ælles weoren his lif forloren
 and Aldolf smat i þene sceld þat he atwa toscænde
 and Hengest him leop to swulc hit a liun weore
 and smat an Aldolfes helm þat he atwa tofeol
Þa heowen heo mid sweorde þa swipen weoren grimme
fur flæh of stele ofte and wel ilome
Vnder are stunde þa leop Aldolf to grunde
 and isæh him Gorlois þat wæs a kene gume ful iwis
of Cornwale he wes eorl he wes widene cuþ
Þa wes þæ beorn Aldolf muchele þe balder
 and hæf hæhȝe his sweord and lette hit adun swippen
 and smat Hengest a þan hond þat he forlette his brond
an hiȝinge hine igrap mid grimme his læchen
bi þere burne hode þa wes an his hafde
 and mid muchelere strengþe hine adun swipte
and seoþþe he hine up bræid swulc he hine tobreken wolde
 and mid ærmen hine bisprædde and forþ hine lædde
Nu wes Hengest inumen þurh Aldolf þene æhte gume
Þæ cleopede Aldolf þene eorl of Gloucestre
Hengest nis þe noht swa murie swa þe wes bi Ambresburie
þer þu þa sæxes droȝen and Bruttes ofsloȝen
mid muchele swikedome þu mi cun sloȝe
Nu þu scalt læn leosen and losie þine freonden
mid reoliche witen an worlde forwurþen
Hengest eode stille ne isæh he help nenne 
Aldolf hine ladde to his leodkinge
 and grætte þene leodking mid leofliche worden
Hail seo þu Aurilien aþeles cunnes
her ich bringe þe biuoren þe wes þines cunnes bone
Hengest þene heþene þe hærm us hafueþ iuræmmed
Godd hit me iuþe þat ich hine igripen habben
Nu ich hine ȝiue þe uor monne leofuest ært þu me
 and let þine hiredchilderen pleien mid þissen hunde
scotien mid heore flan and his cun scenden anan
Þa andswarede þe king quicliche steuene
Edi seo þu Aldolf eorlene aþelest
þu ært me leof al swa mi lif leoden þu scalt beon alder
Þer me nom Hengest and þer me bond Hengest
þer wes þa Hengest cnihten alre ȝeomerest
Þis feht wes ouercumen and þa hæþene fluȝen
Þa iseh Octa þat his fader wes ful wa
 and Ebissa his wedbroþer buȝen heom togadere
 and fluȝen into Eouuerwic mid ærmþen inoȝe
 and greiþeden walles tohalden þa halles
Summe þa hæþene to þan wude iwenden
þær þat ganninde folc læiden heom to grunde
Þa wes Aurilian þe king iquemed wel þurh alle þing
he wende into Cuningesburh mid his drihtfolke
 and þankede Drihten swulchere mihten
Þreo dæies and þreo niht þe king wunede þarriht
to lechinien þa wunden of leofenen his cnihten
 and baþien on burȝe heore wærie ban
Þa þe þridde dæi com and þat folc hafde imaked non
þa lette þe king blawen and beonnede his eorles
þa heo comen to hustinge to Aurilie þan kinge
Þa heo togadere comen þe king heom axede sone
whæt heo him radde þat his richemen weoren
a wulchere witen Hengest scolde forwurþen
 and hu he mihte bezst wreoken his leofueste freondes
þe anfest Amberesburi leien biburide
Þa stod up Ældadus and wiþ þene king he spac þus
towardes Gode he was god he wes an hali biscop
Aldolf eorles broþer nefde he nenne oþer 
Lauerd king lust nu me what ic wullen tellen þe
Ich wulle makien þene dom hu he scal beon fordon
for he is on leode monnen us laþest
 and haueþ ure kun ofslæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
and he is an hæþene hund helle he scal isechen
þer he scal sinke for his swikedome
Lauerd king hærcne me wat ich þe wulle tællen
A king wes in Ierusalem Saul wes ihaten
þe wes in hæþenesse king of muchele mæhte
Agag wes ihaten Ierusalem he hatede
he wes king of þe Amalæh þe Wurse him wes ful nieh
auere he hatede Ierusalem mid hærmen þan mesten
nolde he neouere heom ȝiuen griþ ah auere he heom stod wiþ
he heom barnde he heom sloh he dude heom sorȝen inoh
Hit ilomp in ane time þat þe sunne gon to scine
þa sat Agag þe king inne his hæh sættele
meinde his fæie blod and muneȝede hine to fusen
He cleopede his cnihtes anan uorþrihtes
Swiþe to eouwer steden and forþ we scullen riden
we sculleþ bærnen and slæn al ibuten Ierusalem
Forþ wende þe king and muche ferde mid him
þat lond heo gunne þurhærnen and þa tunes furbernen
Þat iseȝen þa men þe wuneden inne Ierusalem
 and heo heom toȝeines cnihtes and sweines
 and fuhten wiþ þene king and mid fæhte hine ouercomen
 and al his folc sloȝen and Agag heo king nomen
 and swa heo mid him comen to Saul þan kinge
Þa wes Saul þe king bliþe þurh alle þing
þe king axeden ræd at his riche anan
whæþer he mihte him bet don oþer slæn oþer anhon
Þa leop up Samuel a witiȝe of Israel
he wes swiþe hali mon hæh touward Drihten
nuste na mon i þan dæȝen swa heh mon an Godes laȝen
Samuel nom Agag þene king and lædde hine a þan cheping
 and lette hine swiþe sterke to ane stake binde
 and nom mid his riht hond ænne durewurþe brond
 and þus cleopede him on Samuel þe gode mon
Þu hattes Agag þe king nu þu ært an ærming 
nu þu scalt fon þat læn þat þu forferdest Ierusalem
þat þu hauest þas hæȝe burh swa swiþe forworht
 and monienne godne mon islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
swa ich ibide are ne scalt þu nauermare
Samuel þat sweord anhof and hærdeliche adun sloh
 and al toswadde þene king in Ierusalemus chepping
 and þa stucchen tarueden wide ȝeond þa straten
þus tok Samuel on and swa þu aȝest Hengest don
Þis iherde Aldolf þe eorl of Glocetere
touward Hengest he leop swulc hit a liun weore
and igrap hine bi þan toppe and hine æfter him halede
 and ladde hine þurh and þurh and þurhut Cuningesburh
 and wiþuten þere burhȝe he hine lette binden
Aldolf his swored adroh and Hengestes hafd ofsloh
 and þe king hine nom forþrihtes for he wes swa oht cniht
 and læide hine in eorþe after heþene laȝen
 and bad for þere sæule þat hire neuere sæl neore
 and nu Aurilie þe king lette beode husting
 and lætte blawen bemen and bonnien his ferde
folc þer wes sellic and ferden riht to Euerwic
 and biclusden þer wiþinnen Octa mid his monnen
þe king lette deluen ænne dich al abuten Eouerwic
þat ne mihte þer na man neoþer ute no in gan
Þæt isæh Octa þerfore him wes wa
 and his hæþene folc þe he hafde an burȝe
heo nomen heom to ræde what heo don mæhten
 and þus spac Octa wiþ his iuere Ebissa
Nou ich habben me biþoht what ich don wulle
Ich and mine cnihtes scullen forþrihtes
in ure bare brechen gan ut of burȝen
ræmen a mine swore ænne raketeȝe
 and cumen to þan kinge his mildce biddinde
Ælles we beoþ alle dæde buten we fulien þissen ræde
Alle heo duden swa swa heom radde Octa
duden of claþes karefulle cnihtes
 and eoden ut of burhȝe blaþe þeines
tweiene and tweiene twenti hundred 
þis biheold Aurilien aþelest kingen
seolcuþ him þuhte of þan nakede cnihten
Tosomne comen þa ferde þat læi ȝeond þan ærde
iseȝen Octa cumen þat wes Hengest sune
He bar an his honde ænne raketeȝe longe
he com to þan kinge and biuoren his hæredringe
he feol uppen uolde þas kinges fæt isohte
 and þas word seide þa Hengestes sune Octa
Imilze mi lauerd king þurh þene milde Godd
for luue of God almihten haue milce of mine cnihten
for alle ure heþenescipe hæne is iwurþen
laȝen and ure leoden for laþe we beoþ Drihten
for us is itruked an hond Appollin and Teruagant
Woden and Mercurius Iubiter and Saturnus
Venus and Didon Frea and Mamilon
 and alle ure laue nu us sunde laþe
ah we wulleþ ileuen in leofen þine Drihten
for al hit trukeþ us an hond þat we to temden
We ȝeorneþ þine are nu and aueremare
ȝif þu me wult griþien and þu me wult friþien
we þe wulleþ to teon and þine holde men beon
luuien þine leoden and þine laȝen halden
Ȝif þu þet nulle do þine iwille
whaþerswa þu wult don þa us slan þa us anhon
 and þe king wes mildheorte and heold hine stille
he biheold a riht hond he biheold a lift hond
wulc of wiisen ærest spæken wolden
Alle heo weoren stille and swiȝeden mid stæuen
nes þer nan swa hæh mon þat durste word sciren
 and æuere læie Octa æt þes kinges foten swa
alle his cnihtes leien him biæften
Þa spac Aldadus þe gode biscop and seide þus
Æuere hit wæs and a hit biþ and ȝet hit us bihoueþ
þene we milze ȝeorneþ þat we milze habben
wurþe he is milze þe wurþeliche heo biddeþ
 and þu seolf læuerd king leoden þu ært ælder
imilze þu Octa and his iueren alswa
ȝif heo wulleþ Cristindom mid gode lefuen vnderfon
for ȝet hit mai ilimpen i summere leoden 
þat heo maȝen Drihten duȝeþliche hærien
Nu stont al þis kinelond a þire aȝere hond
Bitec heom enne stude þer he biþ iqueme
 and nim of heom ȝisles swulche þu wult ȝirnen
 and let heom wel halden in irene benden
finden þan ȝislen mete and claþ finden al þat heom biþ leof
 and þenne miht þu wel halden þis moncun i þine londe
 and let heom tilien þat lond and libben bi heore tilæhþe
Ȝif hit seoþþen ilimppeþ sone þerafter
þat heo trukieþ an hond treouþen to halden
 and wakieþ mid wærke and þe wiþer haldeþ
nu ich þe demen þene dom whæt þu miht seoþþen don
Let riden heom to ræhliche swiþe
 and let heom alle fordon spillen and æc anhon
Þis ich þe deme Drihten hit ihere
Þa andswarede þe king quickere stefne
Al swa ich wulle don swa þu hauest idemed
Þus spac þe kingþa Aris up Octa
þu scalt swiþe wel don vnderuoh Cristindom
Þer wes iuulȝed Octa and his iueren alswa
and alle his cnihtes i þan stude uorþrihtes
Heo nomen heore ȝisles and ȝeuen þan kinge
þreo and fifti children heo bitæhten þan kinge
 and þe king heom sende bisiden Scotlonde
aþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nalden
Þe king bitahte heom an hond sixti hidene lond
þeron heo wuneden wel feole wintren
Þe king wes inne Eouerwic aþele him þuhte
he nom his sonden and sende ȝeond his londe
hæhte his biscopes his bocilærede men
eorles and þeines cumen him toȝeines
to Aurilie þan kinge to muchele hustinge
Hit iwærþ sone þat heo gadere comen
Þe king his folc grætte mid fæire his worden
he wilcumede eorles he wilcumede beornes
 and þa biscopes and þa bocilærede men
Ich eou wulle suggen mid soþe worden
whi ich eou æfter sende and for wulche þingen 
Her ich aȝeuen ælche cnihten is cunden and his rihten
 and æuerælche eorle and æuerælche beorne
þat he mæi biwinnen bruken hit mid wunnen
 and ælche monnen bi his life ich hate griþ luuien
Ich hæten eou wurchen and bulden þa chirchen
bellen leten ringen Godes lof singen
heren mid ure mihten leofe ure Drihten
ælche mon bi his mæhte halden sibbe and sæhten
læten tilien þat lond nu hit is al a mire hond
Þa þis dom wes isæid alle heo leofden þisne ræd
Þe king heom ȝef leoue þenne to liþe
ælc uærde heomward swa heom bezst þuhte
Seouen niht fulle þe king læi þer stille
 and seoþþen he gon liþe into Lundenne
to gladien þat burhfolc þat ofte weoren bisie
He letten stronge walles he lette bulden halles
 and rihte al þa workes þe ær weore tobrokene
 and aȝef heom alle þa laȝen þe stoden bi heore ælderne dæȝen
he makede þer reuen þan uolke to reden
 and þenenen he gon wenden riht to Winchæstre
þer he lette wurcchen halles and chirchen
þer him þuhte swiþe muri seoþþen he uerde to Ambresburi
to þan leerstowe of leofuen his freonden
þa Hengest mid cniuen þer aquald hæfuede
He lette axien anan men þat cuþen hæuwen stan
 and æc gode wurhten þe mid æxe cuþe wurchen
he þohte wurche þer a werc wunder ane ueire
þat a sculde ilasten þa while men liueden
Þa wes inne Kaerlium a biscop þe hahte Tremoriun
he wes swiþe wis mon inne weorldrichen
mid þan kinge he wes ouenan þæ walde
 and þus Tremorien Godes dring spæc þer wiþ þene king
Lust nu me Aurilien what ich þe wulle cuþen
 and ich þe wullen suggen sælest alre ræden
ȝif þu hine wult luuien æft he þe likeþ
We habbeoþ ænne witeȝe Mærlin is ihaten
Ȝif æi mon hine mihte ifinden uppe þissere wælden
 and to þe ibringen þurh æies cunnes þinge
 and þu his iwille driȝen woldest 
he þe wolde runen selest ræden
hu þu mihtest þis weorc makien strong and sterk
þet a mihte ilæsten þa while men leoueden
Þa andswarede þe king þas wordes him weoren iqueme
Leoue freond Tremoriun al þis ich wulle don
Þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde
and bad æuerælcne mon axien after Mærlin
 and ȝif me hine mihten ifinden bringen hine to þan kinge
he him wolde ȝifuen lond boþe seoluer and gold
 and a weorlrichen driȝen his iwille
Þa sonden gunnen riden widen and siden
summe heo uerden riht norþ and summe heo uerden suþ forþ
summe heo uerden riht æst and summe heo uerden riht west
summe heo uerden anan þat heo comen to Alæban
þat is a wælle inne Wælsce londe
Þe walle he lufode and ofte hine þerinne baþede
þa cnihtes hine funde þer he sat bi þan stronden
Sone swa hine imetten fæire heo hine igrætten
 and þus him to forþrihtes sæiden þa tweien cnihtes
Hail seo þu Mærlin monnene wisest
Bi us þe gon græten þat is a godful king
Aurilian ihaten aþelest alre kingen
stont al þis muchele lond in Aurilies kinges hond
faire he þe bisecheþ þat þu him to buȝe
 and he þe wule ȝiue lond boþe seluer and gold
ȝif þu an riche ræde wulle þan kinge
Mærlin andswerede þa þæt cnihten wes ful wa
Ne recche ich noht his londes his seoluer no his goldes
no his claþes no his hors miseolf ich habbe inowe
Þa sat he stille longe ane stunde
þas cnihtes weoren afæred þat he fleon wolde
Þa hit alles up brac hit wes god þat he spæc
Ȝif beoþ tweiene cnihtes icumen herrihtes
ȝurstendæi ær none ich wuste þat ȝe comen
 and ȝif ich swa walde ne mihte ȝe me finden
Ȝe bringeþ me gretinge from Aurilie þan kinge
Ich cneou his cnihtes ær he come to londe 
 and ich icneou þene oþer Vther his broþer
ic icneou beien ær heo iboren weoren
þæh ich nauer nouþer mid eȝen ne iseȝe
Ah walawa walawa þat hit is idiht swa
þat þe leodene king leng ne mot liuien
Ah nu ich wulle fusen and beon eouwer ifere
to þan kinge ich faren wulle and driȝen his iwille
Forþ ferde Mærlin and þa cnihtes wiþ him
swa longe þat heo comen to þan leodkinge
Komen to þan kinge wiltidende
næuer ær an his liue nes þe king swa bliþe
for næuere nanes monnes cume þe him to come
Þe king to his stede and ut him gon ride
 and alle his cnihtes mid him to wulcumen Mærlin
Þe king hine imette and fære hine igratte
he hine iclupte he hine custe
he hine cuþlæhte
Muchel wes þe murhȝe i þan monuerede
al for Marlines cume þe nes nanes monnes sune
Wale þat an worlde næs nan witie
þat auere wuste here whes sune he weore
buten Drihten ane þe wlæt al clane
þe king lædde to bure Mærlin þe wes deore
he hine fræinien gon mid fæire his worden anan
þat he dude him to vnderstonde of þan weorldes ȝeongen
 and of al þan ȝeren þat to cumen weoren
for hit weoren him swiþe iwil þat he þerof wuste
Mærlin andswerede þa and to þan kinge seide swa
O Aurilie þe king þu fræinest me a sellic þing
loke þat þu na mare swulc þing ne iscire
For mi gæst is bæl iwis þa a mire breoste is
and ȝef ich among monnen ȝelp wolde makien
mid gladscipe mid gomene mid godfulle worden
mi gast hine iwarþeþ and wirþ stille
 and binimeþ me min wit and mine wise word fordut
þenne weore ich dumbe of æuerælche dome
Ah bilef swulche þinges quæd Mærlin to þan kingen
for whanswa cumeþ neode to aueræi þeode 
 and mon me mid mildescipe wulle me bisechen
 and ich mid mine iwille mote wunien stille
þenne mæi ich suggen hu hit seoþþen scal iwurþen
Ah ich þe wulle ræden of nexte þire neoden
 and sugen þe herriht what þu hauest an heorten
A ueld is bi Amberesburi þe is brad and swiþe muri
þer wes mid cniuen þi cun idon of liuen
þer wes moni bald Brut biswiken to þan deþe
 and þenchest þene stude mid wurþcipe igraten
mid sælcuþe wærcken wurþien þa dæde
þat þer scal stonden to þere worlde longe
Ah nauest þu neuere nenne mon þe cunne awiht þeron
þe cunne wærc makien þe nauere nulle trukien
Ah ic þe wulle ræden to swulchere neode
for ich what a wærc mid wundere bistonde
for þat weorc stondeþ inne Irlonde
Hit is a swiþe sellic þing
þat woerc is of stane swulc ne beoþ oþer nane
swa wid swa is weorlderiche nis nan weorc his iliche
þa stanes beoþ muchele and mahten heo habbeoþ
þa men þe beoþ unhal heo fareþ to þan stane
 and heo wasceþ þene stan and þermide baþieþ heore ban
umbe lutle stunde heo wurþeþ al isunde
Ah þe stanes beoþ muchele and unimete græte
for nis nauere na mon iboren i nauere nare burhȝe
þe mihte mid strengþe þa stanes þenne bringe
Þa andswarede þe king Mærlin þu sæist sællic þing
þe nauere nan iboren mon ne maie heom bringgen þenne
no mid nare strengþe of þan stude lade
hu mihte ich heom þenne heom bringen þeonne
Þa andswarede Mærlin þan kinge þat spac wiþ him
Ȝuse ȝuse lauerd king hit wes ȝare iqueþen
þat betere is liste þene ufel strenþe
for mid liste me mai ihalden þat strengþe ne mai iwalden
Ah somne þine uerde and far to þan ærde
 and þu mid þe lede gode monne uerde
 and ich wulle mid þe þi monscipe biþ þe mære
Ær þu aȝæn wende þine iwille þu scalt habben 
 and þat weorc þu scalt bringen mid þe to þissen londe
 and swa þu hit scalt leden to þere lichraste
 and wurþien þene stude þer þine wines liggeþ
 and þu seolf scalt þerin þine ban resten
þenne þi lif endeþ þer þu scalt resten
Þus seiden Mærlin and seoþþen he sæt stille
alse þeh he wolde of worlden iwiten
Þe king hine lette bringen into ane fære bure
 and wunien þerinne æfter his iwille
Aurilie þe king lette beoden husting
of alle þan londe þa stod an his honde
he bad him ræde to swulchere neode
and heo him wel rædden riche his beornes
þat he dude þene ræd þat Mærlin him hauede isæd
Ah heo nælden leden þene king ut of þis londe
ah heo curen heom to ældre Vther þene gode
 and fiftene þusend cnihten fæire iwepned
baldere Brutten þa þider sculde buȝen
Þa þas ferde wes al ȝaru þa bigunnen heo to faren
mid alle þan bezste scrippen þæ bi þære sæ stoden
 and ferden swa longe þat heo comen to Irlonde
 and þa hauene nomen þæ cnihtes wel idone
heo eoden uppen sæstrond and biheolden Irlonde
Þa spæc Mærlin and spilede mid worden
Iseo ȝe nu ohte men þene muchelne hul
þe hul swa swiþe hæh þere weolcne he is ful neh
þat is þat seolliche þing hit hatte þere Eotinde Ring
elches weorkes unniliche hit com of Aufrike
Slæþ eower teldes ȝeond al þas feldes
Her we scullen ræsten to þreom dæȝen uirsten
i þan feorþe dæiȝe we scullen heonne fusen
touward þan hulle þer is ure iwille
Ah we scullen us ær baþien and bonnien ure beornes
græiþien ure wepnen for wel heo us bihoueþ
Þus hit bilæfde and þer læie þa ferde
Þeo ahte Irlond a king þat wes swiþe strong
he hæhte Gillomaurus gomenen he wes lauerd
him comen þa tiþende þat Brutes weoren an londe
he lette beoden ferde ȝeond alle Irlondes ærde 
 and he gon þretien swiþe þat al he wolde heom todriue
þa þat word him com to þat Brutes wolden þer don
 and comen to þan anes to fæchen þa stanes
þa þe king Gillomar makede mucchel hoker and scarn
 and seide þat heo weoren sotten iueren
þat ouer sæ brade þider weoren iliþene
to sechen þer stanes ase in heore londe neoren nane
and swor a Seint Brænden Ne scullen heo læden ænne stan
ah for þan stanen heo scullen ibiden alre baluwenen mæst
heore blod ȝeoten ut of heore buken
 and swa me scal heom tachen stanes to sæchen
 and seoþþen ich wulle buȝen into Brutlonde
 and suggen þan king Aurilie þat mine stanes ich wullen werien
 and buten þe king beon stille and don mine iwille
ich wulle in his londe mid fæhte atstonden
maken him weste paþes and wildernes monie
widewen inoȝe heore weres scullen deȝe
Þus þe vnwise king plaȝede mid worden
ah al an oþer hit iwærþ oþer he iwende
Ȝaru wes hes ferde and forþ heo gon fusen
swa longe þat heo comen þer læien Brutes on
Togaderen heo comen and hærdliche onsloȝen
 and fuhten feondliche feollen þa fæie
Þa Irisce weoren bare and Bruttes iburnede
þa Irisce fullen and wriȝen al þa feldes
 and þe king Gillomar gon him to fleonne þar,
 and flæh forþrihtes mid twenti of his cnihtes
into ænne muchele wude wurþscipen biræiued
wes his Irisce uolc mid stele iualled
Þus wes þe king iscænd and þus he endede his ȝelp
 and þus to wude ferde and lette his folc fællen
Þa Bruttes biheolden þa dede ȝeond þan vælden
seouen þusend þer leien liues bidæled
Bruttes ȝeond þan uælden ferden to heore telden
 and heore gode wepnen wurþliche bihoȝeden
 and þer heo gunnen ræsten alse Merlin heom radde
I þan feorþe dæie þa gunnen heo fusen
 and ferden to þan hulle iwæpned wel alle 
þer stod þat seolkuþ werc muchel and swiþe sterc
Cnihtes eoden upward cnihtes eoden dunward
cnihtes eoden abuten and ȝeorne biheolden
iseȝen þer on londe sellic werc stonden
þer weoren a þusend cnihtes mid wepnen wel idihten
and alle þa oþer to iwiten biwusten wel heore scipen
Þa spæc Merlin and spileden mid þan cnihten
Cnihtes ȝe beoþ stronge þas stanes beoþ græte and longe
ȝe mote neh gon and neodliche heom fon on
ȝe mote uaste heom wriþen mid strongen sæilrapen
scuuen and hebben mid hæȝere strenþe
treon græte and longe þat beon swiþe stronge
 and gaþ to ane stane ȝe alle glæne
and cumeþ mid strengþe ȝif ȝe hine maȝen sturien
Wel wuste Merlin hu hit sculde iwurþen
Þa cnihtes tostepen mid muchelere strengþe
heo swunken ful swiþe ah næfden heo syȝe
þat heo auer æine stan sturien mahten
Merlin biheold Vther þe was þe kinges broþer
 and þas word sæide Merlin þe witeȝe
Vther tih þe aȝan and bonne þine cnihtes
 and stondeþ al abuten and ȝeorne bihaldeþ
 and beoþ alle stille þat na man þer ne sturie
ær ich sugge eou nu anan hu we scullen fon on
Vther droh hine abac and bonnede his cnihtes
þat ne bilafden þer nane aneoweste þan stane
al swa feor swa a mon mihte werpen ænne stan
 and Mærlin eode abuten and ȝeornen gon bihalden
þrie he eode abuten wiþinnen and wiþuten
 and sturede his tunge alse he bede sunge
þus Merlin dude þer þat cleopede he Vþær
Vther com swiþe and alle þine cnihtes mid þe
 and winneþ þas stanes alle ne scullen ȝe læuen nænne
for nu ȝe maȝen heom hebben swulche veþerene balles
 and swa ȝe sculleþ heom mid ræde to ure scipen lede
Þeos stanes heo ladden swa Merlin heom radde
 and duden heom in heore scipen and seileden uorþ to iwiten
 and swa heo gunnen wenden into þissen londe
 and ladden heom in ann velde þe is wunder ane brad 
he is brad and swiþe muri onuæst Ambresburie
þer Hengest biswæc Bruttes mid sæxen
Mærlin heom gon ræren alse heo stoden ærer
swa næuer nan oþer mon þene craft ne cuþe don
ne næuer ær þer biforen nes na mon swa wis iboren
þat cuþe þet weorc rihten and þa stanes dihten
þat tidende com to þan kinge i þan norþ ende
of Merlines fore and of Vthæres his broþer
þat heo weoren mid isunde icumen to þissen londe
 and þat þat worc wes al idiht and iset upriht
Þe king wes an breoste wunder ane bliþe
 and lette beode hustinge swa mid swa wes al his lond
þat al his folc swa swiþe muri come to Amberesburi
al his drihtliche uolc to Whitesunedæie
Þider com Aurilie þe king and al his folc mid him
a Whitensunendæie he þer wærf makede
alse ich þe wulle telle a þisse bocspelle
Weoren a þan walde teldes itælded
in þan brade uelde niȝe þusend teldes
Al þan Whitensunendæi þe king a þan uelde læi
hæt halȝien þe stude þe hæhte Stanhenge
Þreo dæies fulle wunede þe king stille
i þan þridde dæie heȝe wurþede his duȝeþe
he makede tweie biscopes wunder ane gode
Seint Dubriz to Kaerliun to Eouuerwic Seint Samson
beien heo iwurþen hali and mid Gode haȝe
I þan feorþe dæie duȝeþen todælden
and swa ane stunde hit stod a þan ilken
Þa ȝet þer wes a luþer gume Passent Vortigernes sune
wes þe ilke Passent into Wælisc londe iwent
and þer a þen ilke daȝen wes bicumen utlaȝe 
Ah ne durste he noht longe wunien þer for Aurilie and for Vther
ah he biȝet scipen gode and ferde bi sæflode
into Alemaine he uerde mid fif hundred monnen
 and þer he biwon muchel uolc and makeden scipferde
 and for swa longe þat he com to þisse londe
into þere Humbre þer he hærmes worhte
Ah ne durste he noht longe i þan ænde atstonde
Þe king ferde þiderward and Passent fleh aweiward
æfter sæ swa longe þat he com to Irlonde
Sone he þer funde þene king of þan londe
his heorte wes swiþe sær he grette þene king Gillomar
Hail seo þu Gillomar gumene ælder
ich æm to þe icume ich wes Vortigernes sune
mi fader wes Brutlondes king he luuede þe þurh alle þing
 and ȝif þu woldest toȝere beon þider min iuare
swa wit sculden ispæcken and minne fader wel wreken
 and wel wreken þi folc þat Vther her qualde
 and þi selcuþe wærc þat heo heonne droȝen
 and æc ich iherde suggen þer ic ferde inne sæ
þat þe king Aurilien seoc is iwurþen
 and liþ inne Winchæstre a bedde ful faste
Þu miht ileue me inoh for þis is witerliche soþ
Passent and Gillomar makeden heore forward þar
aþes heo sworen monie and unifohȝe
þat heo wolden al þis lond sætten on hæore tweire hond
þe aþes weoren isworene ah æft heo weoren forlorene
Þe king gaderede ferde wide ȝeond his ærde
to þere sæ beoþ iwende Gillomar and Passen
into þan scipen eoden and forþ heom letten gliden
Forþ heo wenden biliue þat heo comen to Meniue
þat wes a þan time tun swiþe hende
þat mon nu iwitterli clepeþ Seint Deouwi
Þer heo nomen hauene mid heȝere blisse
Scipen eoden a þat strond cnihtes eoden a þat lond
Þa sæide Passent touward Gillomar he went
Seie me king Gillomar nu we beoþ icumen her
Nu ich sette þe an hond halfendæl þis kinelond
for is of Winchastre icume to me anes cnihtes sune
 and sæiþ me swulne ræd þat Aurilie wule beon dæd
þat ufel is under his ribben þat ne mæi he noht libben
Her wit scullen wel wreken unker winemæies
biwinnen his wunseles swa us biþ alre selest
To þan kinge com þat word into Winchæstre
þat Passent and Gillomar weoren mid ferde icumen hær 
Þe king cleopede Vther þe wes his leoue broþer
Vther bed uerde ȝeond al þissen ærde
 and far to ure feonden and drif heom of ærde
oþer þu heom fusen oþer þu heom feolle
Ich wolde faren æc ȝif ich neore swa seoc
ah ȝif ich mai beon feore ich þe cumen after sone
Al dude Uþer swa þe king him sæide þer
 and Passen at Seint Deowi sorȝen iworhte þerbi
and þe king Gillomar muchel sorȝe he dude þær
Brutlond heo þurharnden hærȝede and barden
 and Vther i þissen ærde sumnede his ferde
 and hit wes longe uirst ær he mihte fusen ariht
 and Passent West Walisc lond set an his aȝere hond
Hit wes an ane dæie his duȝeþe weoren bliþe
þer com faren Appas feondes hine væreden
To Passent he quaþ þus Cum hidere to us
Ich þe wulle telle of ane wilspalle
Ich was at Winchæstre at þine wiþeriwinnen
þer liþ þe king seoc and sorhful an heorten
What scal beon mi mede ȝif ic þider ride
 and ich þe swa iqueme þat ich hine aquele
þa andswarede Passen and toward Appase went
Ich bihate þe todæi an hundred pund for ic mæi
ȝif þu me iquemest þat þu hine aquelle
Treoþen he plihten þesne swikedom to dihten
Appas eode to bure and þesne balu mæinde
he wes an hæþene gume ut of Saxlonde icume
Muneckes claþes he nom an he scar his crune ufenen
he nom him tweien iueren and forþ he gon fusen
 and wende anan rihte into Winchæstre
swulc hit weore an hali mon þe hæþene deouel
He wende to þan burhȝate þer þe king on bure lai
 and gratte þene dureward Godes grætinge
 and bad hine an hiȝinge gan in to þan kinge
 and suggen him to soþe þat Vther his broþer
hæfde him þider isend seolne læche
þene bezste læche þe wunede an æi londe
þe auerælcne sucne mon of ufele bringen con 
Þus læh þe laþe mon leodene kinge
for Uther wes ifaren forþ mid his ferde
no nauer Vther hine ne isæh ne þider hine isende
 and þe king wende þat hit weore soþ and ilefde him inoh
Wha wolde wene þat he swike weore
for an his bare liche he weorede ane burne
þerufenen he hæfde ane ladliche here
 and seoþþen ane cule of ane blake claþe
iblæcched he hæfede his licame swulc ismitte of cole
He cneolede to þan kingge his spæche wes ful milde
Hail seo þu Aurilien aþelest alre kingen
Hider me sende Vther þe is þin aȝen broþer
 and ich al for Godes luue æm to þe her icume
for ich þe wulle helen and al hal makien
for Cristes leofe Godes sune ne ræche ich nane garsume
no mede of londe no of seoluere no of golde
ah ælche seocken ich hit do for luue of mine Drihtene
Þis iherde þe king hit wes him swiþe iqueme
ah whar is æuere æi mon a þisse middelærde
þe þis wolde wenen þat he swiken weore
He nom his glæsfat anan and þe king mæh þeron
Anne while after þan þat glæsfat an honden nom
 and sceoweden hit forþrihttes biforen þas kinges cnihtes
 and þus sæide anan Appas þe haþene mon
Ȝif ȝe me wulleþ ileuen ær tomarwen eue
þes king scal beon al hal ihaled an his willen
Þa weoren bliþe alle þa weoren i bure
Appas eoden in ænne bur and þat balu mæinde
 and dude þerto atter þa scamoiene hatte
 and com ut forþrihtes imong þa burhcnihtes
 and þan kinge he gon dæle muchel canele
 and gingiuere and licoriz he hom lefliche ȝef
alle heo nomen þat lac and he heom alle biswac
Þeos swike feol a cneowe atforen þan leodkinge
 and þus saide him to Lauerd nu þu scalt afon
