of þissen drinchen ane dæle þat scal beon þin hale
 and þe king up drong and þer þat atter he dronc
Anan swa he hafde idrunke þe leche hine adun læide
Þus seide Appas to þan burcnihtes 
Wreoþ nu wel þene king þat he ligge a swæting
for ich sugge eou þurh alle þing al hal beoþ aure king
 and ich wulle to mine inne and speken wiþ mine monnen
 and to þere midnihte ich cume forþrihtes
mid oþer lachecrafte þa sculleþ beon him liþe
Forþ wende þe swike þe king læi on sweuete
Appas to his inne and spec wiþ his monnen
mid stilleliche rune bistal of þan tune
To þere midnihte þa sende þa burhcnihtes
sixe of heore monne to Appases inne
heo wenden hine to finden and longi hine to þan kinge
þa wes he ifloȝen and feondes hine uæreden
Þa men aȝein comen þer þe king wunede
 and cudden i þan bure of Appases fore
Þa mihte me iseon sorȝen inoȝe beon
cnihtes feollen adun and ȝirnden heore dæþes
Þer wes muchel waning heortne graning
þer wes moni reolic spel þer wes gumene iȝel
Heo leopen to þan bedde and þene king hedden
þa ȝet he lai on sweouete and on muchele swate
Þæ cnihtes mid weope þene king awehten
 and heo him to cleopeden mid mildere steuene
Lauerd hu mid þe hu beoþ þine beorste
For nu is ure læche ifaren buten laue
iliþen ut of hirede for hæne us bilæued
Þe king heom ȝaf andsware Al ic æm toswollen
 and þer nis nan oþer ræd nu nan ich wurþe dæd
 and ich bidde forþrihtes ȝe beoþ mine cnihtes
þat ȝe græten Vther þe is min aȝe broþer
 and biddeþ hine halden mi lond an onwalde
Godd seolf þurh alle þing lete hine beon god king
 and hateþ hine beon kene and æiwær riht deme
wærcche uolke for fæder hænen to frouere
þenne maie he halde lond an onwalde
 and nu todai þenne ich beo dæd nimeþ alle anne ræd
 and leteþ me ilenge riht to Stanhenge
þer liþ muchel of mine cunne þurh Sæxen aqualde
 and ofsendeþ biscopes and bocilarede men 
mi gold and mi seoluer deleþ for mire saule
 and leggeþ me an æst ænde inne Stanhenge
Næs þer nan oþer ræd þer iwarþ þe king dæd
 and al swa his men duden swa þe king demde
Inne Wæles wes Vther and herof næs naþing war
neuere þurh nare liste herof naþing nuste
naþeles he hafede mid him þene witeȝe Merlin
Aȝeineden þere uerde þe icumen wes to ærde
Vther lai inne Wales in anne wilderne
 and fundede to uarene wiþ Passent to fehten
Þa a þan auentime þe mone gon to scine
wel neh al swa brihte swa þe sunnelihte
Þa isehȝen heo feorre ænne selcuþe sterre
he wes brad he wes muchel he wes unimete
of him comen leomen igastliche scinen
þe steorre is ihate a Latin comete
Com of þan steore a leome swiþe sturne
at þeos leomen ende wes a drake hende
of þes draken muþe leomen comen inohȝe
Ah tweien þer weoren muchele þere oþere vnimete
þe an droh touward France þe oþer touward Irlonde
Þe leome þe toward France droh he wes briht vnifoh
to Munt Giu wæs iseȝen þa seolcuþe takne
þe leome þa strehte westriht a seouen bæmen wes idiht
Þis isah Vþer ah nas he noht herof war
sær him wes an heorte and seolliche auæred
swa wes al þat muchele folc þat wes in þere uerde
Vþer cleopede Merlin and bad hine cume to him
 and þus seide him to mid swiþe softe worden
Mærlin Merlin leoue freond fonde þiseoluen
 and sæie us of þan tacne þe we isæȝen habbeoþ
for nat ich on worlde riche to whan hit scal iwurþen
buten þu us raden aȝæn we moten riden
Mærlin sæt him stille longe ane stunde
swulc he mid sweuene swunke ful swiþe
Heo seiden þe hit iseȝen mid heore aȝen æȝen
þat ofte he hine wende swulc hit a wurem weore
Late he gon awakien þa gon he to quakien 
 and þas word seide Merlin þa witeȝe
Wæilawæi wæilawæi a þissere worlderiche
muchel is þa sorȝe þe isiȝen is to londe
Whær ært þu Vther Siten me biuoren her
 and ich þe wulle suggen of sorȝen inoȝen
Dæd is Aurilie kingene aþelest
swa is þe oþer Costanz þi broþer
þe Uortigerne biswac mid his swikedome
Nu haueþ Vortigernes cun Aurilien aquald
nu þu ært al ane of aþele þine cunne
Ah ne hope þu to ræde of heom þat liggeþ dede
ah þenc of þe seoluen seolþen þe beoþ ȝiueþe
for selde he aswint þe to himseolue þencheþ
þv scalt wurþen god king and gumenene lauerd
 and þu to þere midnihte wepne þine cnihtes
þat we i þan morȝenliht mæȝen come forþriht
forn at Meneue þer þu scalt fihten
ær þu þenne wende sclæht þu scalt makien
þu scalt beien slæ þer Passent and Gillomar
 and monie þusend of þan gumen þat beoþ mid heom hider icumen
Þat taken of þan steorre þe we isaȝen swa feorre
soþ hit is Uþer leof þat tacnede þines broþer dæd
Biuoren þa steorre wes þæ drake elcches wurmes vnimake
þat taken wes a þire half þat weore þu Uþer þiseolf
þu scalt habben þis lond and þin æie beon muchel and strong
Swulche toknen beoþ uncuþe of þas draken muþe
eoden tweien leomen wunder ane lihte
Þe an strehte feor soþ ut ouer France
þat is an æiȝesful sune þat of þine licame scal cume
þe scal moni kinelond mid compe biwinne
 and an ende he scal rede moniane þeode
Þe oþer leome þe strahte west wunder ane lihte
þat biþ a dohter þa þe biþ swiþe deore
Þe leome gon striden a ueire seoue strengen
þat beoþ seouen uæire sunen þe of þine dohter sculleþ cumen
þe scullen moni kinelond biȝiten to heore aȝere hond
heo sculleþ beon wel stronge a water and a londe
Nu þu hauest of me ihærde þe wule halpen
swiþe uorþrihtes far to þine fihte 
 and Merlin gon to slume swulc he wolde slæpen
Vp aras Vþer nu he wes wis and war
 and hæhte his cnihtes to horse forþrihtes
 and hæhte heom biliue faren to Meneue
 and alle heore fare græiþen alle heo scullen fehten
I þan flokke biforen he hafde cnihtes wel icoren
seouen þusend cnihte ohte men and wihte
Hafde he amidde cnihtes wel bihedde
oþer seoue þusend selere þeinen
Hæ hede bæfte ohtere cnihten
ahtene þusen ohtere kempen
 and of ganninde uolke swa feole þusend
þat a nane spelle ne mihte heom na mon tellen
Forþ heo wenden biliue þat heo comen to Meneue
Þer isah Gillomar whar him com Vther
 and hæhde his cnihtes to wepne forþrihtes
 and heo to biliue and gripen heore cniues
 and of mid here breches seolcuþe weoren heore leches
 and igripen an heore hond heore speren longe
hengen an heore æxle mucle wiæxe
Þa sæide Gillomar þe king a swiþe seollic þing 
Her cumeþ Vþer Aurilies broþer
he wule bidden mi griþ and noht fehten me wiþ
Þa formeste beoþ his sweines Faren we heom toȝeines
Ne þurfen ȝe nauere rehchen þah ȝe slæn þa wrecchen
For ȝif Vther Costantines sune wulle her mi mon bicume
 and Passente aȝeuen his fader richen
ich hine wullen griþien and latten hine liuien
 and inne fæire benden læden hine to mine londe
Þe king wordede þus þa while him alomp wurs
Weoren Vtheres cnihtes at þan tune forþrihtes
leiden fur a þene tun and fehten biliue
mid sweorden heom to rakeden and þa Irisce weoren nakede
Þa iseȝen Irisce men þat Brutten wes an eornest
feondliche heo fuhten and neoþeles heo feollen
heo cleopeden on heore king Whar ært þu niþing
whi nult þu hider wenden þu lezst us her scenden
and Passent þin ifere isih us fallen here
cumeþ us to halpe mid hahȝere strengþe
Þis iherde Gillomar þerforen wes his heorte sær
mid his Irisce cnihten he com to þan fihte
and Passend vorþ mid him beien heo weoren uæie
Þa iseh Vþer þat icumen wes þer Gillomar
to him he gon riden and smat hine i þere side
þat þat spere þurhrade and þa heorte toglad
Hiȝendliche he hine biwent and oftoc Passent
and þas word sæide Vther þe sele
Passent þu scalt abiden her cumeþ Vther riden
He smat hine uuenen þat hæued þat he adun halde
and þat sweord putte in his muþ swulc mete him wes uncuþ
þat þe ord of þan sworde wod in þere eorþe
Þa sæide Vther Passent liȝ nu þer
Nu þu hauest Brutlond al bitald to þire hond
Swa þe is nu iræd þeron þu ært ded
wikien ȝe scullen here þu and Gillomar þin ifere
 and brukeþ wel Brutlond for nu ic hit bitæche inc an hond
þat ȝit maȝen toȝere mid us wunien here
Ne þurue ȝe nauere adrede wha eou scullen feden
Þus sæide Vþer and seoþþe he arnde þer
and drof Irisce men ȝeond wateres and ȝeond fenes
and sloh al þa uerde þe mid Passent commen to ærde
Summe to þere sæ iwiten and leoppen in heore scipen
mid wederen and mid wateren þær heo forferden
Þus heo ispædden her Passent and Gillomar
Nu wes þis feht idon and Vther aȝen com
and forþrihtes wende into Winchæstre
In are brade strete he igon mete
þreo cnihtes and heore sweines cumen him toȝeines
Anan swa heo ine imette fæire heo hine igrætten
Hail seo þu Vther þeos æþeles beoþ þin æȝen
Ded is Aurilie kingene aþelest
he þe haueþ iset an hond al his kinewurþe lond
he bad þe beon a sele and þenchen on his saule
Þa weop Vþer wunder ane swiþe
Vþer wende forþriht into Winchæstre
þa weoren him biforen wiþuten þere burȝe
alle þa burhmen mid reouliche iberen 
Sone swa heo hine iseȝen heo him to sæiden
Vther þin are nu and æueremare
Ure king we habbeoþ ilore wa is us þerfore
Þu weore his broþer nafde he nænne oþer
no he nefde nenne sune þe mihte king bicumen
Ah nim þu þene kinehalm he is þe icunde
 and we þe wulleþ helpen and halden for lauerd
mid wapnen and mid æhten and al ure mihte
Þis iherde Vþer he wes wis and he wes war
þat þer næs cost nan oþer seoþþen dæd wes his broþer
He nom þenne kinehelm þe him bicom swiþe wel
and he wurþliche iwarþ him to kinge
 and heold gode laȝe and his folc lufede
Imong þat he king wæs and his wikenares chæs
Merlin him ætwende nuste he nauere whidere
no nauere a worlderiche to whan he bicome
Wa wes þan kinge swa wes al his duȝeþe
and alle his hirdmen þeruore murnende weoren
Þe king lette riden widen and siden
he bad gold and gersume ælche farinde gume
whaswa mihte finde Merlin an londe
þerto he læide muchel lof ah ne herde he him nawhit of
Þa biþohte Vther whæt Mærlin him sæide ær
in þan hereȝeonge inne Walisc londe
þer heo iseȝen þene drake ælches wurmes vnimake
and he þohte of þan tacnen þe Merlin him tahte
Þe king wes swiþe særi and sorhful an heorte
for ne les he næuere leouere mon seoþþen he wes an liuen
neouere nenne oþer ne Aurilie his broþer
Þe king lette wurchen tweien imaken tweien guldene draken
al for Mærlines luue swa swiþe he wilnede his cume
Þa þe draken ȝaru weoren þe oþer wes iuere
wharswa he an ærde ladde his ferde
he wes heremærke in auerælche happe
þene oþerne he wurþliche ȝæf into Winchæstre
into þan biscopstole þer he stude haldeþ
Þerto he ȝef his gode spere þermid me sculde þene drake bere
þenne me scolde halidom beren to processiun 
Þis iseȝen Bruttes þas draken þa weoren imaked þus
æuer seoþþen heo cleopeden Vther þe to hermærke þene drake bar
þene nome heo him laiden on þet wes Vþer Pendragon
Pendragun an Brutisc Drakenhefd an Englisc
Nu wes Vther god king ah of Merlin nefde he na þing
Þis word iherde Octa þer he norþ wunede
 and Ebissa his wedbroþer and Osa þe oþer
þa Aurilien sende þider and sette heom þer on his griþe
and bitahte heom an honde sixti hiden of londe
Octa iherden ful iwis al hu hit ifaren wes
of Aurilies dæþe and of Vtheres kinedome
Octa him to cleopede his cun þe wes aneoste
nomen heom to ræde of heore alde dede
þat heo wolden bi heore liue Cristindom bilaue
Heo heolden husting and hæþene bicomen
þa comen þer togadere of Hengestes cunne
fif and sixti hundred of heþene monnen
Sone wes þat word cuþ an ȝeond þan londe icud
þat Octa Hengestes sune wes hæþene bicume
 and þas ilke gumen alle þa Aurilien igriþed hæfuede
Octa sende his sonde into Walisce londe
after þan Irisce þe Vþer æturnen
and after þan Alemainen þe weoren awei idraȝene
þa weoren to wude iwende þe while men sloh Passent
and huden heom wel iwhar þe while men sloh Gillomar
Þat folc ut of wude teh and touward Scotlonde beh
Auer þer comen ma and ma and ferden toward Octa
þa heo tosomme weoren iwende þa weoren þer þritti þusend
wiþuten þa wifmen of Hengestes cunnen
Heo nomen heore uerde and gunnen to farene
 and setten al an heore hond biȝeonden þere Humbre lond
 and þat leoden þer heo gunnen liþen
ferde þer wes sellic and wenden riht to Eouerwic
and an ælche side þa burh gunnen biride
 and þa burh bilæien hæþene leoden
and nomen hit al to heore honde forþ into Scotlonde
al þat heo iseȝen heo talden heore aȝen
Ah Vþeres cnihtes þa weoren i þan castle 
wereden þene tun wiþinnen þat ne mihten heo næuere binnen
ne iherde mon in nane stude lute men þat swa wel duden
Swa sone swa Vþer of þissen þingen iwarþ war
færde he bad stronge ȝeond al his kinelonde
and he swiþe hiȝendliche ferde touward Eouerwic
ferde uorþriht anan þer him læi Octa
Octa and his ferde fusde heom toȝeines
wuruen heom togadere mid grimmere strengþe
heowen hardliche hælmes gullen
falewede feldes of fæie blode
 and þa heþene saulen helle isohten
Þa þes dæies ende bicom þa wes hit swa ufel idon
þat þat hæþene uolc þa ufere hond hafeden
 and mid muchelere strengþe sturmden þa Bruttes
and driuen heom to ane munte þæ wes unimete stor
 and Vþer mid his monnen teh to þan munte
and hæuede iloren in fihte leofe his cnihtes
fulle seouen hundred his hælp wes þa wurse
Þe munt hæhte Dunian þe Vther wes ufenan
wes þe munt þurhwexen mid ane wude feiren
Þe king wes þer wiþinnen mid swiþe feole monnen
 and Octa hine bilæi mid hæþene monnen niht and dæi
bilæi hine al abuten Wa wes þan Brutten
wa wes þan kinge Vþer þat he nes ær wær
þat he nefde an londe bet vnderstonde
Ofte heo eoden to ræde of swucchere neode
hu heo mihten ouercumen Octa Hengestes sune
Þer wes an eorl Gorlois ocht mon fuliwis
cniht he wes wel idon he wes Vþeres mon
eorl of Cornwaille cuþ he wes wide
he wes swiþe wis mon of alle þinge wel idon
To him saide Vþer særi an heorten
Hail seo þu Gorlois gumenene lauerd
Þu ært min aȝe mon and swiþe wel ich þe on
þu ært cniht wel idon muchel is þi wisdom
alle mine leoden ich don in þine ræden
 and alle we sculle wurchen after þine iwille
Þa heng his breowen adun þe king Vther Pendragun 
and stod him ful stille and bad Gorlois suggen his iwille
Þa andswarede Gorlois he wes hende ful iwis
Sæie me Vther Pendragun whi halst þu þin hafed adun
nast þu þat Godd ane is betere þene we al clæne
He mai whamswa he wule wurþcipe bitachen
Bihate we him on liue þat we him nulleþ liȝe
 and leten we us ræden of ure misdeden
Ælc mon forþriht af alle his sunen nimen scrift
ælc mon scriuen oþer swulc hit weoren his broþer
 and æuerælc god cniht nime on him muchel scrift
 and Godde we scullen bihaten ure sunnen to beten
 and to þere midnihte ȝarkien us to fihten
þeos hæþene hundes tælleþ us al ibunden
Octa Hengestes sunæ weneþ þat we beon alle inumen
heo liggeþ i þissen felden ihæled in heore telden
heo beoþ swiþe werie iboren heore wepnen
nu nan heo sculleþ slumen and seoþþen slæpen
of us nabbeoþ heo nane kare þat we aȝen heom wulleþ faren
To þere midnihte we sculleþ forþrihtes
swiþelicche stille adun of þissen hulle
na wurþe cniht swa god þat he scire æi word
ne nauer nan hæleþ þat he horn blawe
Ac we scullen steppen heom to swa we stelen wolden
ær heo wurþen iware we scullen heom amærre
we scullen heom to teon and tidende tellen
and æuerælc ocht mon sterkliche heom legge on
and swa we scullen of londe driuen vnicunde
and mid mihte of ure Drihten bitellen ure irihten
Al þas ferde idude swa Gorlois heom hauede ibede
Ælc mon forþrihte dude hine vnder scrifte
bihehten god to donne and þat ufel to forgonne
To þere midnihte wepnede heom cnihtes
and auoremeste uerde adun Vþer Pendragun
and his cnihtes alle swiþeliche stille
and smiten i þa waldes imong alle þa teldes
and sloȝen þa hæþene mid hæhȝere strenþe
fluȝen ȝeond þan feldes falewe lockes
Uolken hit wes ærmest heo droȝen heore þermes 
mid muchele vnisunde heo feollen to þan grunde
Þer wes forþriht inume Octa Hengestes sune
 and his wedbroþer Ebissa and his iuere Ossa
Þe king heom lette binden mid irene bænde
and bitahte heom sixti cnihten þe gode weoren to fihten
ufennen þan walden uaste to halden
 and he seolf draf him forþ and muchel dune makede
 and Gorlois þe hende uorþ an oþer ende
 and alle heore cnihtes æuere forþrihtes
adunrihtes sloȝen al þat heo neh comen
Summe heo crupen to þan wude an heore bare cneowen
heo weoren amærȝe volken alre ærmest
Octa wes ibunden and ilad to Lunden
and Ebissa and Ossa nes heom nauere al swa wa
Þis feht wes idon and þe king wende forþ
into Norþhumbre mid hæȝere blisse
 and seoþþen to Scotlonde and sette hit al his aȝere hond
He sette griþ he sette friþ þat ælc mon mihte faren wiþ
from londe to londe þeh he bere gold an honde
of griþ he dude swulc þing þat ne mihte næuer ær na king
from þan ilke time þat Bruttes comen her liþen
And seoþþen vmbe stunde he ferde to Lunden
he wes þere an Æstre mid aþele his uolke
bliþe wes þe Lundenes tun for Vthere Pendragun
He sende his sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde
he bæd þa eorles he bæd þa cheorles
he bæd þa biscopes þa bocilærede men
þat heo comen to Lunden to Vþer þan kingen
into Lundenes tun to Vþer Pendragun
Riche men sone to Lundene comen
heo brohten wif heo brohten child swa hehte Vther þe king
Mid muchele godnæsse þe king iherde mæsse 
 and Gorlois þe eorl of Cornwale and mid him cnihtes uale
muche blisse wes i þan tun mid Vþer kinge Pendragun
Þa þe mæsse wes isungen to halle heo þrungen
bemen heo bleowen bordes heo brædden
al þat folc æt and dronc and blisse heom wes imong
Þer sæt Vþer þe king an his hæh setle
forn aȝan him Gorlois hende cniht ful iwis
þe eorl of Cornwale mid aþele his wife
Þa heo weoren alle iseten eorles to heore mete
þe king sende his sonde to Igærne þere hende
Gorlois eorles wif wifmone alre hendest
Ofte he hire lokede on and leitede mid eȝene
ofte he his birles sende fron to hire borde
ofte he hire loh to and makede hire letes
and heo hine leofliche biheold ah inæt whær heo hine luuede
Næs þe king noht swa wis ne swa ȝærewitele
þat imong his duȝeþe his þoht cuþe dernen
Swa longe þe king þis him droh þat Gorlois iwærþ him wraþ
 and him gromede swiþe wiþ þene king for his wife
Þe eorl and his cnihtes arisen forþrihtes
 and forþ mid þan wife cnihtes swiþe whraþe
Vther king þis isah and herefore særi wes
 and nom him forþrihtes twælf wise cnihtes
 and sende after Gorlois gumenene ældere
and beden hine an hiȝinge cumen to þan kinge
 and don þan kinge god riht and beon icnowen of his pliht
þat he hafde þene king iscend and from his borde wes iwende
he and his cnihtes mid muchele vnrihte
for þe king him wæs glad wiþ and for he hailede in his wif
 and ȝif he nalde aȝein cumen and his gult beon icnawen
þe king him wold after and don al his mahten
binimen him al his lond and his seoluer and his gold
Þis iherde Gorlois gumenene lauerd
 and he andsware ȝaf eorlene wraþest
Næi swa me helpe Drihte þa iscop þas daȝes lihte
nulle ich nauere aȝæn cumen no his griþ ȝirnen
ne scal he neuere on liue me scende of mine wife
 and suggeþ Vþer kinge at Tintaieol he mai me finden
ȝif he þider wule ride þer ich him wulle abiden
and þer he scal habbe hærd gome and mucle weorldes scome
Forþ wende þe eorl ire on his mode
he wes wærþ wiþ þene king wunder ane swiþe
and þretede Vther þene king and alle his þeines mid him
ah he nuste whæt com seoþþe sone þeræfter
Þe eorl anan wende into Cornwaille 
he hafde þer tweie castles biclused swiþe uaste
þæ castles aþele weore of his eoldrene istreon
To Tintaieol he sende his leofmon þa wes hende
Ygerne ihaten wifene aþelest
and heo biclusde uæste inne þan castle
Ygerne wes særi and sorhful an heorte
þat swa moni mon for hire sculden habben þer lure
Þe eorl sende sonde ȝeond al Brutlonde
and bæd alcne ohte gome þat he him sculde to cume
for gold and for seolure and for oþere ȝiuen gode
þat heo ful sone to Tintaieole comen
 and his aȝene cnihtes comen forþrihtes
Þa heo togædere weoren sele þeines
þa hafde he fulle fiftene þusend
 and heo Tintaieol faste bitunden
Uppen þere sæstronde Tintaieol stondeþ
he is mid sæcliuen faste biclused
þat ne biþ he biwunne þurh nanes cunnes monnen
bute ȝif hunger cumen þer anvnder
Þe eorl uerde þenne mid seouen þusend monnen
 and wende to ane oþere castle and biclusde hine ful uæste
and bilefde his wif in Tintaieol mid ten þusend monnen
For ne þurue þa cnihtes dæies na nihtes
buten biwiten þat castelȝat and careles liggen slæpen
and þe eorl wuste þene oþer and mid him his aȝen broþer
Þis iherde Vther þe king wes swiþe steorc
þat Gorlois his eorl his ferde hafde igadered
and wolde halde weorre mid muchelere wraþþe
Þe king bad his ferde ȝeond al þissen ærde
 and ȝeond al þan londe þa stoden an his honde
monies kinnes leoden liþen heom togæderes
and comen to Lundene to þan leodkinge
Ut of Lundene tun ferde Vþer Pendragun
he and his cnihtes ferde uorþrihtes
swa longe þat heo comen into Cornwæille
 and ouer þat water heo tueoȝen þat hatten Tambreis
riht to þan castle þer heo Gorlois wusten 
Mid muchelere læþe þene castel heo bilæien
ofte heo toræsden mid ræȝere strengþe
tosomne heo leopen leoden þer feollen
Fulle seouen nihte þe king mid his cnihten
bilæi þene castel his men þer hafeden sorȝen
ne miste he of þan eorle naþing iwinnen
and alle þa seouen nihte ilaste þat selliche feoht
Þa iseh Vþer king þat him ne spedde naþing
ofte he hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
for Ygærne him wes swa leof æfne alse his aȝen lif
and Gorlois him wes on leoden monnen alre læþest
 and ælches weies him wes wa a þissere weorlderiche
for he ne mihte beon wurþe naþing of his wille
Þa wes mid þan kinge an ald mon swuþe hende
he wes a swiþe riche þein and ræh on ælche dome
he wes ihaten Vlfin muche wisdom wes mid him
Þe king bræid up his chin and bisah an Vlfin
swiþe he murnede his mod wes iderued
Þa quaþ Vþer Pendragun to Ulfin þan cnihte
Ulfin ræd me sumne ræd oþer ich beo ful raþe dæde
swa swiþe me longeþ þat ne mai i noht libben
after þere faire Ygærne Þis word halt me derne
for Ulfin þe leoue aþele þine lare
lude and stille don ich heom wulle
Þa andswarede Ulfin þan kinge þet spac wiþ him
Nu ihere ich muche seollic ænne king suggen
Þu luuest Ygærne and halst hit swa deorne
þe wifmon is þe to leof and hire lauerd al to laþ
his lond þu forbernest and hine blæþ wurchest
and þrattest hine to slænne and his cun to fordonne
Wenest þu mid swulche hærme to biȝeten Ygærne
þenne heo sculde don swa ne deþ na wifman
mid æie vnimete halden luue swete
Ah ȝif þu luuest Ygærne þu sculdest hit halden derne
and senden hire sone of seoluere and of golde
 and luuien hire mid liste and mid leofliche bihæste
Þa ȝet hit weore a wene whar þu heo mihtes aȝe
for Ygærne is wel idon a swiþe treowe wimmon
swa wes hire moder and ma of þan kunne
To soþe ich þe suggen leofest alre kinge 
þat oþere weies þu most aginnen ȝif þu hire wult awinnen
For ȝurstendæi me com to an æremite wel idon
 and swor bi his chinne þat he wuste Merlin
whar he ælche nihte resteþ vnder lufte
and ofte he him spæc wiþ and spelles him talde
 and ȝif we mihte Merlin mid liste biwinnen
þenne mihtest þu þine iwille allunge biwinne
Þa wes Vþer Pendragun þa softer an his mode
 and ȝaf andsware red Vlfin þu hauest wel isæd
Ich þe ȝiue an honde þritti solh of londe
þat þu Merlin biwinne and don mine iwille
Vlfin ȝeond þat folc wende and sohte al þa uerde
 and he vmbe stunde þene æremite funde
and an hiȝinge brohte hine to þan kinge
and þe king him sette an hond seouen sulȝene lond
ȝif he mihte bringen Merlin to þan kinge
Þe æremite gon wende in þene west ænde
to ane wilderne to ane wude muchele
þer he iwuned hafde wel feole wintre
and Merlin swiþe ofte þerinne sohte
Sone þe armite com in þa ifunde he Mærlin
vnder ane treo stonden and sære him gon longen
þene æremite he isæh cume alse while wes his iwune
he orn him toȝænes beiene heo uæineden þas
heo clupten heo custen and cuþliche speken
Þa sæide Merlin muchel wisdom wes mid him
Sæie þu mi leofe freond wi naldest þu me suggen
þurh nanes cunnes þinge þat þu wældest to þan kinge
Ah ful ȝare ich hit wuste anan swa ich þe miste
þat þu icumen weore to Vþere kinge
and what þe king þe wiþ spæc and of his londe þe bæd
þat þu me sculdest bringe to Vþer kinge
And Vlfin þe sohte and to þan kinge brohte
 and Vþer Pendragun forþrihtes anan
sette him an honde þritti solh of londe
 and he sætte þe an honde seoue sulhȝene lond
Vther is oflonged æfter Ygærne þere hende
wunder ane swiþe after Gorloises wiue 
Ah longe is æuere þat ne cummeþ nauere
þat he heo biwinne bute þurh mine ginne
for nis na wimmon treowere in þissere worlderiche
 and neoþeles he scal aȝe þa hende Ygærne
on hir he scal streonen þat scal wide sturien
he scal streonien hire on ænne swiþe sellichne mon
Longe beoþ æuere dæd ne biþ he næuere
þe wile þe þis world stænt ilæsten scal is worþmunt
and scal inne Rome walden þa þæines
Al him scal abuȝe þat wuneþ inne Bruttene
of him scullen gleomen godliche singen
of his breosten scullen æten aþele scopes
scullen of his blode beornes beon drunke
of his eȝene scullen fleon furene gleden
ælc finger an his hond scarp stelene brond
scullen stan walles biuoren him tofallen
beornes scullen rusien reosen heore mærken
Þus he scal wel longe liþen ȝeond londen
leoden biwinnen and his laȝen sette
Þis beoþ þa tacnen of þan sune þe cumeþ of Uþere Pendragune
and of Ygærne Þes speche is ful derne
for ȝet næt hit neoþer Ygærne no Uþer
þat of Vþere Pendragune scal arisen swilc a sune
for ȝet he beoþ unstreoned þa sturieþ al þa þeoden
Ah Lauerd quaþ Merlin nu hit is iwille þin
þat forþ I scal fusen to uerde þas kinges
þi word ich wulle heren and nu ich wulle wende
and faren ich wulle for þire lufe to Vthere Pendragune
and habben þu scalt þat lond þat he þe sette an hond
Þus heo þa ispecken þæ æremite gon to weopen
deorliche he hine custe þer heo gunnen dælen
Merlin ferde riht suþ þat lond him wæs ful cuþ
forþriht he fusde to þes kinges ferde
Sone swa Vþer hine isæh swa he him toȝeines bæh
 and þus quaþ Vþer Pendragune Mærlin þu ært wilcume
Her ich sette þe an honde al þene ræd of mine londe
and þat þu me ræde to muchere neode
Vther him talde al þat he walde 
 and hu Ygærne him wes on leoden wimmonnen leofest
and Gorlois hire lauerd monnenen alre laþest
 and buten ich habbe þinne ræd ful raþe þu isihst me dæad
Þa andswerede Merlin Let nu cume in Vlfin
 and bitæc him an honde þritti sulȝene lond
 and bitæc þan æremite þat þu him bihete
for nulle ich aȝæn na lond neouþer seoluer na gold
for ich am on rade rihchest alre monnen
 and ȝif ich wilne æhte þenne wursede ich on crafte
Ah al þin iwille wel scal iwurþen
for ich con swulcne lechecraft þe leof þe scal iwurþen
þat al scullen þine cheres iwurþen swulc þas eorles
þi speche þi dede imong þere duȝeþe
þine hors and þine iwede and al swa þu scalt ride
þenne Ygærne þe scal iseon a mode hire scal wel beon
heo liþ inne Tintaieol uaste bituned
Nis nan cniht swa wel iboren of nane londe icoren
þe mid strengþe of Tintaieol þe ȝeten mihten untunen
buten he weoren ibirsted mid hungere and mid þurste
Þat is þat soþe þat ich þe sugge wulle
þurh alle þinge þu scalt beon swulc þu eorl weore
 and ich wulle beon iwil del swulc him is Brutael
þat is a cniht swiþe herd he is þeos eorles stiward
Iurdan is his burcniht he is swiþe wel idiht
Ich wulle makien anan Ulfin swulc is Iurdan
Þenne bist þu lauerd and ich Brutael þi stiward
 and Ulfin Iurdan þi burcniht and we scullen faren nu toniht
faren þu scalt bi ræde wuderswa ich þe læde
Scullen nu tonihte half hundred cnihten
mid speren and mid scelden beon abuten þine telden
þat nauere nan quik mon ne cumen þer aneosten
 and ȝif þer aueræi mon cume þat his hæued him beon binumen
for þa cnihtes scullen suggen selen þine beornen
þat þu ært ilete blod and restest þe on bædde
Þas þingges forþrihte þus weoren idihte
Forþ ferde þe king næs hit cuþ naþing 
and ferden forþ mid him Vlfin and Merlin
he tuȝen riht þen wæi þa into Tintaieol læi
heo comen to þas castles ȝæte and cuþliche cleopeden
Vndo þis ȝætessel þe eorl is icumen here
Gorlois þe læuerd and Britael his stiward
and Iurdan þe burcniht we habbeoþ ifaren al niht
Þe ȝæteward hit cudde oueral and cnihtes urnen uppen wal
and speken wiþ Gorlois and hine icneowen mid iwis
Þa cnihtes weoren swiþe whæte and wefden up þa castles ȝæte
 and letten hine binnen fare þa læsse wes þa heore care
heo wenden mid iwisse to habben muchel blisse
Þa hædden heo mid ginne Merlin þer wiþinne
 and heolden Vþer þene king wiþinne heore walding
and ledde þer mid him his gode þein Ulfin
Þis tidinde com biliue in to þan wife
þæt hire læuerd wes icumen and mid him his þreo gumen
Vt com Ygærne forþ to þan eorle
and þas word seide mid wunsume wurde
Wilcume læuerd monne me leofest
 and wilcume Iurdan and Britael is alswa
Beo ȝe mid isunde todæled from þan kinge
Þa quæþ Vþer ful iwis swulc hit weore Gorlois
Muchel þat monkun þæt is mid Vther Pendragun
and ich æm bi nihte bistole from þan fihte
for æfter þe ic wes oflonged wifmonne þu ært me leofuest
Buþ into bure and let mi bed makien
and ich me wulle ræsten to þissere nihte uirste
 and alle dai tomærwe to blissien mire duȝeþe
Ygærne beh to bure and lætte bed him makien
wes þat kinewurþe bed al mid palle ouerbræd
Þe king hit wel bihedde and eode to his bedde
and Ygærne læi adun bi Uþere Pendragun
Nu wende Ygerne ful iwis þat hit weoren Gorlois
þurh neuere nænes cunnes þing no icneou heo Vþer þene king
Þe king hire wende to swa wapmon sculde to wimmon do
 and hæfde him to done wiþ leofuest wimmonne
 and he streonede hire on ænne selcuþne mon
kingen alre kenest þæ æuere com to monnen
 and he wes on ærde Ærþur ihaten 
Nuste noht Ygerne wha læie on hire ærme
for æuere heo wende ful iwis þat it weoren þe eorl Gorlois
Næs þer na mære uirst buten þat hit wes dæiliht
þer forþrihtes vnderȝeten þa cnihtes
þat þe king wes iuaren ut of þere uærde
Þa sæiden þa cnihtes soþ þæh hit neoren
þat þe king wes ifloȝen mid ærhþen afeolled
ah al hit wes lessinge þat heo seiden bi þan kinge
herof heo heolden muchel run uppen Vþer Pendragun
Þa seiden þa eorles and þa hæhste beornes
Nu þenne hit wat Gorlois hu hit iuaren is
þat ure king is ifaren and his ferde bilæiued
he wule forþrihtes wepni his cnihtes
and ut he wule to fihten and feollen us to grunden
mid woden his þeines muchel wæl makien
þenne weore us beteren þat we iboren neoren
Ah leten we blawen bemen and bonnien ure uerde
 and Cador þe kene scal beren þas kinges marke
hæbben haȝe þene drake biforen þissere duȝeþe
and faren to þan castle mid kene ure folke
and þe eorl Aldolf scal beon ure aldre
 and we him scullen here swulc hit þe king weoren
 and swa we scullen mid rihte wiþ Gorlois fihten
and ȝif he us wule speken wiþ and ȝernen þis kinges griþ
setten sæhtnusse mid æþen soþfæste
þenne maȝen we mid wurþscipen heonene iwenden
þenne nabbeoþ ure æfterlinges nane upbreidinges
þat we for ærhscipe heonene atærnden
Al þat leodliche folc bilufde þesne ilke ræd
Bemen heo bleowen bonneden uærden
up heo hafden þene drake ælches mærken vnimake
þer wes moni bald scalc þe sceld weiden on sculdre
moni þein kene and wenden to þan castle
Gorlois wes wiþinnen mid kene his monnen
he lette blawen beomen and bonnien his ferden
leopen an steden cnihtes gunnen riden
Þæs cnihtes weoren swiþe wate and wenden ut at þan ȝate
tosomne heo comen sone fastliche heo onsloȝen
feolle fæie men uolden isohten 
þer wes muche blodgute balu wes on folke
imong þan fihte ful iwis mon sloh þene eorl Gorlois
Þa gunnen his men fleon and þa oþere after teon
heo comen to þan castle and binnen heo þrasten
Sone hit comen binnen ba twa þa uerden
þer ileste þat fiht þurh þene dæiliht
ær þe dai weore al asceken wes þe castel biȝeten
næs þer nan swa wracche swein þat he nes a wel god þein
Comen þa tidinde into Tintageol an hiȝende
forþ into þan castle þer Vþer wes inne
þat islaȝen wes ful iwis þe eorl heore læuerd Gorlois
 and alle his heregumen and his castel inumen
Þis iherde þe king þer he læi an skentting
 and leop ut of bure swulc hit an liun weore
Þa quaþ þe king Vþer of þissen tiþende he wes wær
Beoþ stille beoþ stille cnihtes inne halle
here ich æm ful iwis eore læuerd Gorlois
and Iurdan mi burward and Brutael mi stiward
Ich and þas tweie cnihtes leopen ut of þan fihte
and hider in we beoþ idraȝen neore we noht þere islaȝen
Ah nu ich wulle fusen and sumnien mine ferde
and ich and mine cnihtes scullen al bi nihte
faren in ænne tun and imeten Vþer Pendragun
and buten he of sæhnesse speken ich wulle me wurþliche awrake
 and ȝe þesne castel bicluseþ swiþe uaste
and hateþ me Ygerne þat heo noht ne murne
Nu ich fare forþriht habbeoþ alle gode niht
Biforen ferde Merlin and þe þein Vlfin
 and seoþþen Uþer Pendragun ut of Tintageolestun
æuere heo uerden alle niht þat hit wes dæiliht
Þa com he to þan ærde þer læi his ferde
Merlin hafde a þene king his wlite iset þurh alle þing
þa icneowen cnihtes heore kinelauerd
þer wes moni oht Brut mid blissen afeolled
þa weoren inne Bruttene blissen inoȝe
hornes þer bleowen gleomen gunnen gleowen
glad æuerælch cniht al mid pælle biþæht
Þreo dæies wes þe king wuniende þere
 and þan feorþe dæie to Tintaieol he wende 
He sende to þan castle his selest þeines
 and grætte Ygærne wifuene aþelest
 and sende hire taken whæt heo i bedde speken
hehte heo þat heo aȝeuen þene castel biliue
þer nes nan oþer ræd for hire lauerd wes dæd
Ȝet wende Ygærne þat hit soþ weoren
þat þe dæde eorl isoht hafede his duȝeþe
and al heo ilæfde þat hit læs weore
þat þe king Vþer æuere weoren icumen her
Cnihtes eoden to ræde cnihtes eoden to rune
radden þat heo nalden þene castel lengere halden
heore brugge heo duden adun and bitahte hine Vþer Pendragun
Þa stod al þis kinelond æft an Vtheres hond
Þer Vþer þe king nom Ygærne to quene
Ygærne wes mid childe bi Vþer kinge
al þurh Merlines wiȝel ær heo biwedded weore
Þe time com þe wes icoren þa wes Arþur iboren
Sone swa he com an eorþe aluen hine iuengen
heo bigolen þat child mid galdere swiþe stronge
heo ȝeuen him mihte to beon bezst alre cnihten
heo ȝeuen him anoþer þing þat he scolde beon riche king
heo ȝiuen him þat þridde þat he scolde longe libben
heo ȝifen him þat kinebern custen swiþe gode
þat he wes metecusti of alle quike monnen
þis þe alue him ȝef and al swa þat child iþæh
Æfter Arþur wes iboren þeo ædie burde
heo wes ihaten Æne þat ædien maiden
 and seoþþen heo nom Loþ þe Leones ahte
heo wæs inne Loeneis leodene læfdi
Longe liuede Vþer mid muchelere blisse her
mid gode griþe mid gode friþe freo on kinedome
Þa þe he wes ald mon þa com him ufel on
þat vfel hine læide adun seoc wes Vþer Pendragun
swa he wes here seoc seoue ȝere
Þa iwurþen Bruttes swiþe unbalded
heo duden ofte unwræste al for æieleste
Þe ȝet læi ibunden in þe quarterne of Lunden
Octa Hengestes sune þa at Eouerwic wes inume 
and his iueren Ebissa and his oþer Ossa
Heom biuusten twælf cnihtes dæies and nihtes
þa weoren weri oflæien inne Lundenne
Octa iherde suggen of seocnesse þas kinges
 and spac wiþ þa wardesmen þe hine witen scolden
Hærcneþ me nu cnihtes þat ich eou wulle cuþen
We liggeþ here i Lundene uaste ibunden
and ȝe monienne longne dæi ouer us ilæien habbeoþ
Bettere us weoren to libben inne Sexlonde
mid muchele richedome þene þus reouliche here
 and ȝif ȝe wolden iwurþen and don mine iwille
ich eou wolden ȝiuen lond muchel seoluer and gold
þat a ȝe mihten riche rixlien in þan londe
and eoure lif libben swa eou biþ alre leofuest
For no biden ȝe nauere ȝiuen gode of Vþer kinge
for nu ful raþe he biþ dæd and his duȝeþen al bilæueþ
þenne nabben ȝe nouþer þat an no þat oþer
Ah biþenche eou ohte men and doþ us eoure mildze on
 and þencheþ whæt eou weoren leof ȝif ȝe þus ibunden leien
 and mihten in eouwer londe libben inne winne
Swiþe ofte Octa wiþ þæs cnihtes spac swa
Cnihtes gunnen runen cnihtes gunnen ræden
to Octa heo seiden ful stille We scullen don þine iwille
Aþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nalden
Hit wæs in ane nihte þat þe wind wende rihte
forþ iwenden cnihtes to þere midnihte
and ledden uorþ Octa and Ebissa and Ossa
after þere Temese tuhten forþ into þere sæ
forþ heo iwenden into Sæxlonden
Heore cun heom com aȝeines mid mucle flockes
heo liþen ȝeond þan leoden swa heom wes alre leofuest
me heom bitahte lond me ȝæf heom seoluer and gold
Octa hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
he þohten hider wenden and wræken his fader wunden
Ferden heo biȝæten of folke vnimete
to þere sa heo wenden mid muchele þrætte
to Scotlonde heo comen
sone heo fusden alond and mid fure hit igrætten 
Sæxes weoren ræie Scottes heo sloȝen
mid fure heo adun læiden þritti hundred tunes
Scottes heo sloȝen moni and unifoȝen
Comen þa tidende to Vþer kinge
Vþer wes swiþe wa and wunderliche ihærmed
and senden into Loæines to leofen his freonden
and grette Lot his aþum and hehte hine beon an sund
 and hahte hine nimen an his hond al his kinewurþe lond
chihtes and freomen and freoliche heom halden
 and leden heom to ferde swa laȝen beoþ an ærde
 and he hæhte his cnihtes leoue beon hærsume Loþe
mid leofliche læten swulc he weoren leodene king
For Lot wes swiþe god cniht, and hafde ihalden moni fiht
and he wes metecusti æueralche monne
he bitahten him þa warde of alle þissen ærde
Octa heold muche vnfriþ and Lot faht him ofte wiþ
 and ofte he ahte biȝæt and ofte he heom losede
Bruttes hafden muchel mode and vnimete prute
 and weoren æielese for þas kinges alde
and lætten swiþe hokerliche of Lote þan eorle
and duden swiþe vnwraste alle his haste
and weoren alle twiræde heore teone wes þa mare
Þis wes isæid sone seocken þan kinge
þat his hæȝe men Lot al forhoȝeden
Nu ich þe wulle tellen a þissen bocspællen
hv Vþer þe king uundede hine seolven
He sæide þat he wolde wende to his ferde
and mid his eȝene iseon wæ þer wolde wel don
He lette makien þere gode horsebere
 and letten beoden uerde ȝeond al his kineærde
þat ælc mon bi his liue comen to him swiþe
bi heore liue and bi heore leme to wræken þas kinges scome
 and ȝif þær is æi gume þæt nulle hiȝenliche cume
ich wulle hine hiȝenliche fordon oþer slæn oþer anhon
Alle ful sone to hirede heo comen
no durste þær bilæuen na þæ uatte no þe læne
Þe king forþrihtes nom alle his cnihtes
 and ferde him anan to þan tune of Verolam 
abuten Uerolames tun com him Vþer Pendragun
Octa wes wiþinnen mid alle his monnen
Þa wes Verolam a swiþe kinewurþe hom
Seint Alban wes þer islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
Þe burh wes seoþþe foruaren and muchel folc þer wes islæȝen
Vþer lai wiþuten and Octa wiþinnen
Vþeres ferde fusde to wale
ræsden to feondliche þeines riche
ne mihte heo of þan walle ænne stan falle
no mid nare strengþe þene wal amærre
Wælle bliþe wes þæ Hangestes sune Octa
þa he isæh Bruttes buȝen from walle
 and sorhful wenden aȝæin to heore telden
Þa sæide Octa to his iueren Ebissa
Her is icumen to Verolam Vþer þe lome mon
 and wulle wiþ us here fihten in his bære
he wænde mid his crucche us adun þrucche
Ah tomærȝe wæne hit dæi buþ duȝeþe scal arisen
 and oppenien ure castelȝæten þas riche we scullen al biȝeten
ne scullen we nauære here liggen for ane lomme monne
Ut we scullen riden uppen ure steden goden
and to Uþere fusen and his folc fællen
for alle heo beoþ fæie þat hider beoþ iridenen
and nimen þene lome mon and leggen in ure benden
and halden þene wræcche a þat he forwurþe
 and sa me scal lacnien his leomes þat beoþ sare
and his ban rihten mid bitere stelen
Þus him ispac Octa wiþ his iuere Ebissa
ah al hit iwraþ oþer þene heo iwenden
Amarȝe þa hit daȝede duren heo untunden
up aras Octa Ebissa and Ossa
and hehten heore cnihtes ȝarkien heom to fihte
vndon her brade ȝæten burȝen untunen
Octa him ut ræd and muche folc him after glæd
mid balden his beornen þer he bælu funden
Vþer him þis isæh þat Octa heom to bæh
 and þohten his ferde feolen to grunde 
Þa cleopede Uþer mid quickere stefene þer
Wær beo ȝe Bruttes balde mine þeines
Nu is icumen þe ilke dæi þe Drihten us helpen mai
þat Octa scal ifinden þat he þrættede me to binden
Iþencheþ on eoure aldren hu gode heo weoren to fehten
Iþencheþ þene wurþscipe þat ich eou habbe wel biwiten
ne læten ȝe næuere þas hæþene bruken eoure hames
þæs ilke awedde hundes walden eouwere londes
And ich wullen bidden Drihten þat scop þæs dæies lihten
 and alle þaie halȝen þa an hæfene hæhȝe sitteþ
þar ich on þissen felde mote beon ifroured
Nu fuseþ heom to swiþe fulste eou Drihten
þe alwaldinde God biwiten mine þeines
Cnihtes gunnen riden gæres gunnen gliden
breken bræde speren brusleden sceldes
helmes þer scenden scalkes feollen
Þe Bruttes weoren balde and bisie to fihten
 and þa hæþene hundes hælden to grunde
Þer wes islaȝen Octa Ebissa and Ossa
þer seouentene þusend siȝen into helle
feole þer atwenden touward þan norþ enden
Al þene dæilihte Vþeres cnihtes
sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen
þa hit wes eauen þa wes hit al biwunnen
Þa sunggen hiredmen mid hæȝere strengþe
 and þæs word sæiden inne murie heore songen
Her is Vþer Pendragun icume to Verolames tun
 and he hæfueþ idubbed swa Octa and Ebissa and Ossa
 and itah heom a londen laȝen swiþe stronge
þat men maȝen tellen heore cun to spelle
and þerof wurchen songes inne Sæxlonde
Þa wes Vþer bliþe and igladed swuþe
and spac wiþ his duȝeþe þe deore him wes an heorte
 and þas word sæide Vþer þe alde
Sexisce men me habbeoþ for hene ihalden
mine unhæle me atwiten mid heore hokerworden
for ich wes here ilad inne horsebere
 and sæiden þat ich wes ded and mi duȝeþe aswunden 
And nu is muchel sellic isiȝen to þissere riche
þat nu haueþ þeos dede king þas quiken aqualden
 and summe he heom flæmde uorþ mid þan wedere
Nu iwurþen herafter Drihttenes wille
Fluȝen Sæxisce men feondliche swiþe
þe weoren bihalues ihalden from þan fihte
forþ heo gunnen scriþen into Scotlonde
and nomen heom to kinge Colgrim þene hende
He wes Hængestes mæie and monnen him leofuest
and Octa hine lufede þæ while þe he leouede
Weoren þa Saxisce men swiþe iswunten
 and iscriþen heom tosomne into Scotlonde
 and Colgrim þene hende heo makeden to kinge
 and sumneden færde wide ȝeond þan ærde
and sæiden þat heo wolden mid heore wiþercraften
inne Winchastre tun quellen Vþer Pendragun
Wa la wa þat hit sculde iwurþen swa
Nu sæiden Saxisce men in heore somrunen
Nime we six cnihtes wise men and wihte
hæweres witere and senden we to hirede
læten heom uorþ liþen an almesmonnes wisen
 and wunien an hirede mid heȝe þan kinge
and æuerælche dæie þurhgon al þa duȝeþe
and gan to þas kinges dale swulc heo weoren vnhale
 and imong þan wracchen harcnien ȝeorne
ȝif mon mihte mid crafte a dæi oþer a nihte
inne Winchæstres tun cumen to Vþer Pendragun
 and mid morþspelle þene king aquellen
þenne weoren heore iwil allunge iwurden
þenne weoren heo carelæse of Costantines cunne
Nu wenden forþ þa cnihtes al bi dæies lihten
on ælmesmonnes claþes cnihtes forcuþest
to þas kinges hirede þer heo hærm wrohten
Heo eoden to þære dale swulc heo weoren unhale
 and hærcneden ȝeornen of þas kinges hærme
hu me þæne king mihte to dæþe idihte
Þa imetten heo enne cniht from þan kinge he com riht
he wes Vþeres mæi and monnen him leofuest
Þas swiken þer heo sæten onlongen þere streten 
cleopeden to þan cnihte mid cuþliche worden
Lauerd we beoþ wracche men a þissere weorlderiche
while we weoren on londe for gode men iholden
a þat Sæxisce men setten us adune
 and al biræiueden us and ure æhten binomen us
Nu we beden singeþ for Vþer kinge
ælche dæie on a mæl ure mete trukeþ
ne cumeþ nauere inne ure disc neoþer flæs ma no fisc
no nanes cunnes drænc buten water scenc
buten water clæne for þi we beoþ þus læne
Þis iherde þe cniht aȝæn he eode forþriht
 and com to þan kinge þer he lai on bure
 and seide to þan kinge Lauerd beo þu on sunde
herute sitteþ six men iliche on heouwen
alle heo beoþ iferen iscrudde mid heren
While heo weoren a þissere worlderichen
godfulle þeines mid goden afeolled
nu habbeoþ Sæxisce men isæt hom to grunden
þat heo beoþ on weorlde for wracchen ihalden
no raccheoþ heo to borde buten bræd ane
no to heore drencches bute water scenches
Þus heo leodeþ heore lif inne þire leode
 and heore beoden biddeþ þat Godd þe lete longe libben
Þa quaþ Vþer þe king Let heom cumen hider in
ich heom wulle scruden and ich heom wulle ueden
for mines Drihtenes lufe þa wille þa ich liuie
Comen into bure beornes þa swikele
þe king heom lette feden þæ king heom lette scruden
 and nihtes hom læiden ælc on his bedde
and ælc on his halue heoȝede ȝeorne
hu heo mihten þene king mid morþe aquellen
ah ne mihten heo þurh naþing aquellen Vþer þene king
ne þurh nane crafte cumen to him ne mahten
Þa iwærd hit in ane time þe ræin him gon rine
þa cleopede þer a læche þer he læi on bure
to ane burcnihte and hahte hine forþrihtes 
irne to þere welle þe wes onvæst þere halle
and setten þere ænne ohte swain to biwiten heo wiþ ræin
For þe king ne mai on duȝeþe bruken nanes drenches
buten cald welles stræm þat him is iqueme
þat is to his ufele aþelest alre drencche
Þas speche uorþrihtes iherden þas six cnihtes
to harme heo weoren wiþte and ut wenden bi nihte
forþ to þere welle þer ho hærm wrohten
Vt heo droȝen sone amppullen scone
ifulled mid attere weten alre bitterest
six amppullen fulle heo ȝeoten i þan welle
þa wes þa welle anan al mid attre bigon
Þa weoren ful bliþe þæ swiken on heore liue
 and forþ heo iwenden ne dursten heo þer bilæfen
Þa comen þer forþrihtes tweien burcnihtes
heo beren on heore honde twæie bollen of golde
Heo comen to þare welle and heore bollen feolde
aȝæin heo gunnen wende to Vþer þan kinge
forþ into þan bure þer he læi on bedde
Hail seo þu Vþer nu we beoþ icumen her
and we habbeoþ þe ibroht þat þu ær bedde
cæld welle water bruc hit on wunne
Vp aras þe seocke king and sat on his bedde
of þan watere he dronc and sone he gon sweten
his heorte gon to wakien his neb bigon to blakien
his wombe gon to swellen þe king gon to swelten
Næs þer nan oþer ræd þer wes Vþer king dæd
alle heo iwurþen dede þat drunken of þan watere
Þa þat hired isah þat sorhȝen of þan kinge
 and of þas kinges monnen þe mid attre weoren fordone
þa wenden to þere welle cnihtes þe weoren snælle
 and þa welle forduden mid derfulle swincche
mid eorþe and mid stanen stepne hul makeden
Þa nomen þa duȝeþe þene king dede
vnimete uolc and forþ hine uereden
stiþimodede men in to Stanhengen
 and hine þer bureden bi leofen his broþer
side bi side beiene heo þer liggeþ
Þa com hit al togadere þat hæhst wes on londe 
eorles and beornes and bocilarede men
heo comen to Lundene to muchelere hustinge
Nomen heom ro rade þeines riche
þat heo wolden ouer sæ senden sonde
into Bruttainne after bezst alre ȝeoȝeþe
þa a þissere weorldenriche a þan dæȝen weore
Ærþur ihaten bezst alre cnihten
and suggen þat he cumen sone to his kinedome
for dæd him wes Vþer alswa Aurilien wes ær
and Vþer Pendragune nefde nenne oþerne sune
þat mihte after his daȝen halden Bruttes to laȝe
mid wurþscipe halden and þisne kinedom walden
For ȝæt weoren in þissen londe Sæxes atstonden
Colgrim þe kene and moni þusend of his iueren
þa ofte ure Bruttes makeden hufele burstes
Bruttes ful sone þreo biscopes nomen
and ridæres seouene ræiȝe on wisdome
forþ heo gunnen buȝen into Bruttaine
 and heo ful sone to Ærþure comen
Hail seo þu Arþur aþelest cnihten
Vþer þe græten þa he sculde iwiten
 and bæd þat þu sculdest a Brutten þe seoluen
halden laȝen rihte and hælpen þine folke
and witen þisne kinedom swa god king sculden don
þine feond flæmen and driuen heom of londen
 and he bad þe to fultume þene milde Godes sune
þat þu mostes wel don and þat lond of Godde afon
for dæd is Vþer Pendragun and þu ært Ærþur his sune
 and dæd is þe oþer Aurilien his broþer
Þus heo gunnen tellen and Arþur sæt ful stille
ænne stunde he wes blac and on heuwe swiþe wak
ane while he wes reod and reousede on heorte
Þa hit alles up brac hit wes god þat he spac
þus him sæide þerriht Arþur þe aþele cniht
Lauerd Crist Godes sune beon us nu a fultume
þat ich mote on life Goddes laȝen halden
Fiftene ȝere wes Arþur ald þa þis tiþende him wes itald
 and alle heo weoren wel bitoȝen for he wes swiþe iþoȝe
Ærþur forþrihtes cleopede his cnihtes 
 and hæhte æuerælcne mon bonnien his weppnen
 and heore hors sadelie hiȝendliche swiþe
for he wolde buȝe to þissere Brutene
To þere sæ wenden sele þeines
at Mihæles Munte mid muchelere uerede
þa sæ heo sætten a þat strond at Suþhamtune heo comen alond
Forþ him gon ride Arþur þe riche
riht to Selechæstre þer him sel þuhte
þer wes Bruttene weored baldeliche isomned
Muchel wes þa blisse þa Arþur com to burhȝe
þer wes bemene blæst and swiþe glade beornes
þer heo houen to kinge Arþur þene ȝunge
Þa þe Arþur wes king hærne nu seollic þing
he wes metecusti ælche quike monne
cniht mid þan bezste wunder ane kene
he wes þan ȝungen for fader þan alden for frouer
and wiþ þan vnwise wunder ane sturnne
woh him wes wunder laþ and þat rihte a leof
Ælc of his birlen and of his burþæinen
 and his bercnihtes gold beren an honden
to ruggen and to bedde iscrud mid gode webbe,
Nefde he neuere nænne coc þat he nes keppe swiþe god
neuær nanes cnihtes swein þat he næs bald þein
Þe king heold al his hired mid hæȝere blise
 and mid swulche þinges he ouercom alle kinges
mid ræhȝere strengþe and mid richedome
swulche weoren his custes þat al uolc hit wuste
Nu wes Arþur god king his hired hine lufede
æc hit wes cuþ wide of his kinedome
Þe king huld i Lundene ane muchele hustinge
þerto weoren ilaþede his leondcnihtes alle
riche men and hæne to hæȝen þan king
Þa þe hit wes al icume uolc vnimete
vp aræs Arþur aþelest kingen
 and lette bringen him biforen halidomes wel icoren
þerto gon cneoli þe king sume þrie
nuste noht his duȝeþe what he deme wolde
Arþur heold up his riht hond ænne aþ he þer swor
þat næuere bi his liue for nanes monnes lære 
ne sculden inne Brutene Sæxes wurþen bliþe
londes beon wurþen no wurþscipe bruke
ah he heom wolde flemen for heo weoren iuæid wiþ him
sloȝen Vþer Pendragune þe wes Costances sune
swa heo duden þene oþer Aurilien his broþer
for þi heo weoren on londe laþest alre uolke
Arþur forþrihtes nom his wise cnihtes
weore heom lef weore heom laþ alle heo sworen þene aþ
trouliche þat heo wolden mid Arþure halden
 and wreken þene king Vþer þat Sæxes aqualden her
Arþur his writen sende wide ȝeond his londe
after alle þan cnihten þe he biȝiten mihte
þat heo ful sone to þan kinge comen
 and he heom wolde on londe leofliche athalden
scipien heom mid londe mid seoluere and mid golde
Forþ þe king ferde mid vnimete uerde
folc he ledde sællic and ferde riht to Eouerwic
Þer he læi ane niht amærwe he ferde forþriht
þer he wuste Colgrim and his iueren mid him
Seoþþen Octa wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
þe wes Hengestes sune vt of Sæxlonde icumen
Colgrim wes þe hæhst mon þat ut of Saxlonde com
after Hengeste and Horse his broþer
 and Octa and Ossa and heore iuere Ebissa
Heold a þan ilke dæȝen Colgrim Sæxes to laȝen
ladde and radde mid ræȝere strengþe
muchel wes þat moncun þat ferde mid Colgrim
Colgrim iherde tidende of Arþure þan kinge
þat he touward him com and wolde him vfel don
Colgrim hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
 and bonnede his uerde ȝeond al þan norþ ærde
Þer liþen tosomne alle Scotleode
Peohtes and Sæxes siȝen heom togæderes
 and moniennes cunnes men uuleden Colgrimen
Forþ he gon fusen mid vnimete verde
toȝaines Arþure aþelest kingen
he þohte to quellen þe king on his þeoden
 and his folc uallen uolden to grunden 
 and setten al þis kinelond an his aȝere hond
 and fallen to þan grunde Arþur þene ȝunge
Forþ wende Colgrim and his ferde mid him
 and wende mid his ferde þat he com to ane watere
þat water is ihaten Duglas duȝeþen hit aquelde
Þer com Arþur him aȝein ȝaru mid his fehte
in ane brade forde þa ferden heom imetten
fastliche onsloȝen snelle heore kempen
feollen þa uæie uolden to grunde
Þer wes muchel blodgute balu þer wes riue
brustlede scæftes beornes þer ueollen
Þat isæh Arþur on mode him wes unneþe
Arþur hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
 and teh hine abacward in enne uald brade
Þa wenden his feond þat he flæn walde
þa wes glad Colgrim and al his ferde mid him
heo wenden þat Arþur mid arhþe weore afallæd þere
 and tuȝen ouer þat water alse heo wode weoren
Þa Arþur þat isah þat Colgrim him wes swa neh
 and heo weoren beien bihalues þan wateren
þus seide Arþur aþelest kingen
Iseo ȝe mine Bruttes here us bihalfues
ure iuan uulle Crist heom aualle
Colgrim þene stronge ut of Sæxlonde
His cun i þisse londe ure ælderne aqualden
ah nu is þe dæi icumen þe Drihten haueþ idemed
þat he scal þat lif leosen and leosien his freonden
oþer we sculle dæde beon ne muȝe we hine quic iseon
Scullen Sæxisce men sorȝen ibiden
 and we wreken wurhliche ure winemaies
Vp bræid Arþur his sceld foren to his breosten
 and he gon to rusien swa þe runie wulf
þenne he cumeþ of holte bihonged mid snawe
and þencheþ to biten swulc deor swa him likeþ
Arþur þa cleopede to leofe his cnihten
Forþ we biliue þeines ohte
alle somed heom to alle we sculleþ wel don 
 and heo uorþ hælden swa þe hæȝe wude
þenne wind wode weieþ hine mid mæine
Fluȝen ouer þe woldes þritti þusend sceldes
 and smiten a Colgrimes cnihtes þat þa eorþe aȝæn quehte
Breken braden speren brustleden sceldes
feollen Sæxisce men folden to grunden
Þat isah Colgrim þeruore wa wes him
þe alre hendeste mon þe ut of Sexlonde com
Colgrim gon to flænne feondliche swiþe
 and his hors hine bar mid hæhȝere strengþe
ouer þat water deope and scelde hine wiþ dæþe
Saxes gunnen sinken sorȝe heom wes ȝiueþe
Arþur wende his speres ord and forstod heom þene uord
þer adruncke Sexes fulle seoue þusend
Summe heo gunnen wondrien swa doþ þe wilde cron
i þan moruenne þenne his floc is awemmed
 and him haldeþ after hauekes swifte
hundes in þan reode mid reouþe hine imeteþ
þenne nis him neouþer god no þat lond no þat flod
hauekes hine smiteþ hundes hine biteþ
þenne biþ þe kinewurþe foȝel fæie on his siþe
Colgrim ouer feldes flæh him biliues
þat he com to Eouerwic riden swiþe sellic
he wenden into burȝe and faste heo biclusde
hafuede he binnen ten þusend monnen
burhmen mid þa beztse þe him bihalues weoren
Arþur halde after mid þritti þusend cnihten
 and ferde riht to Eouerwic mid folke swiþe sellic 
and bilæi Colgrim þe weorrede aȝæin him
Seouen niht þer biuoren wes suþward ifaren
Baldolf þe hende broþer Colgrimes
and lai bi þare sæbrimme and abad Childrichen
Childric wes i þan daȝen cæiser of riche laȝen
inne Alemaine þat aþel wes his aȝene
Þa iherde Baldolf þer he bi sæ lai
þat Arþur hafde inne Eouerwic Colgrim biclused
Baldolf hæfde ibonned seouen þusend monnen
baldere beornnen þe bi sæ leien
heo nomen heom to ræden þat aȝæin heo wolden riden
and bilæuen Childric and faren into Eouerwic
 and fehten wiþ Arþure and aquellen al his duȝeþe
Baldolf swor on his grome þat he wolde beon Arþures bone
 and bruken al þas riche mid Colgrime his broþere
Nolde Baldolf abide þan keisere Childriche
ah þenne he ferde uorþ and droh him forþrihtes norþ
from dæie to dæie mid baldre duȝeþe
þat he com in ane wude in ane wilderne
from Arþures ferde fulle seoue milen
He hafde iþohte bi nihten mid seouen þusend cnihten
to riden uppen Arþur ær þe king wore war
and his folc afeollen and hine seolf aquelle
Ah al hit oþer iwarþ oþer he iwende
for Baldolf hafede on hirede ænne cniht Bruttiscne
he wes Arþures mæi Maurin ihaten
Maurin bihalues to þan wude halde
þurh wude and þurh feldes þat he com to Arþures teldes
and þus seide sone to Arþur kinge
Hail seo þu Arþur kingene aþelest
ich æm hidere icume ich æm of þine cunne
Her is Baldulf icumen mid swiþe hærde hæregumen
 and þencheþ in þissere nihte to slæn þe and þine cnihtes
to wracken his broþer þe swiþe is vnbalded
ah Godd him scal forwrænen þurh his muchele mihten
 and send nu uorþ Cador þene eorl of Cornwaile
and mid him ohte cnihtes gode and wihte
fulle seoue hundred selere þeines
 and ich heom wulle ræden and ich hom wulle leden
hu heo muwen Baldulf slæn alse enne wulf
Forþ ferde Cador and alle þas cnihtes
þat heo comen bihalues þer Baldulf lai on comele
heo him to helden on ælchere haluen
heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo aneh comen
þer weoren aqualde niȝen hundred alle italde
Baldulf wes bihalues igan him aburhȝen
 and þurh þa wilderne flæh feondliche swiþe
and hafde his men leofe mid reouþe bilæfued 
 and fleh him swa feor norþ þat he com swa uorþ
þer Arþur lai in uolde mid richen his ferde
al abuten Eouerwic king swiþe seollic
Colgrim wes wiþinnen mid Sæxisce monnen
Baldulf hine biþohte what he don mihte
mid wulches cunnes ginne he mihte cumen binnen
into þere burhȝe to Colgrime his broþere
þe wes him on liue leofest alre monne
Baldulf lette striken to þan bare lichen
his bærd and his chinne and makede hine to crosse
he lette sceren half his hæfd and nom him ane harpe an hond
He cuþen harpien wel an his childhaden
 and mid his harpe he ferde to þas kinges hirede
 and gon þær to gleowien and muche gome to makien
Ofte me hine smæt mid smærte ȝerden
ofte me hine culde swa me deþ crosce
ælc mon þe hine imette mid bismare hine igratte
swa nauere na mon nuste of Baldulfes custe
buten hit weore crosse icumen to þan hirede
Swa he eode longe upward swa longe he eode adunward
þæt heo weoren warre þe weoren þær wiþinnen
þæt hit wes Baldulf Colgrimes broþer
Heo wurpen ut enne rap and Baldulf hine faste igrap
and brudden up Baldolf þat he binnen com
mid swulches cunnes ginnes Baldulf com wiþinnen
Þa wes bliþen Colgrim and alle his cnihtes mid him
and swiþe heo gunnen þrattien Arþur þene king
Arþur bihalues wes and þis gomen isæh
and wraþde hine sulfne wunderliche swiþe
and hæhte anan wepnien al his wunliche uolc
he þohte þe burhȝe mid strengþe to biwinnen
Alse Arþur wolde to þan walle ræse
þa com þer riden Patric þe ricche mon
Þat wes a Scottisc þein scone an his londen
 and þus clupien agon to þan kinge anan
Hail seo þu Arþur aþelest Brutten 
Ich þe wulle tellen neouwe tidende
of þan kæisere Childriche þan wode and þan richen
þan strongen and þan balden He is inne Scottlonde
ihælde to are hafene and hames forberneþ
and waldeþ al ure lond after his ahȝere hond
He haueþ uerde wel idone al þa strengþe of Rome
he sæiþ mid his ȝelpe þenne me him win scenccheþ
þat þu ne dærst in nare stude his ræsses abiden
no on uelde no on wude no nauere nane stude
 and ȝif þu him abidest he þe wule binden
quellen þine leoden and þi lond aȝen
Ofte wes Arþure wa nauere wurse þene þa
and he droh hine abac bihalues þere burȝe
clupede to ræde cnihtes to neode
beornes and eorles and þa hali biscopes
 and bad þat heo him radden hu he mihte on richen
mid his monweorede his monscipe halden
 and fehten wiþ Childriche þan stronge and þan richen
þa hider wolde liþe to helpen Colgrime
Þa andswarede Bruttes þa þere weoren bihalues
Faren we riht to Lundene and lete hine liþen after
 and ȝif he cumeþ riden sorȝe he scal ibiden
he seolf and his ferde fæie scal iwurþen
Arþur al bilufeden þat radden his leoden
forþ he gon liþen þat he to Lundene com
Colgrim wes in Eouerwic and þær abad him Childric
Chilric gon wende ȝeon þan norþ ende
 and nom on honde muchæl dal of londe
Al Scotþeode he ȝaf his ane þeine
 and al Norþhumberlond he sette his broþer an hond
Galeweoie and Orcaneie he ȝaf his ane eorle
himseolf he nom from Humbre þat lond into Lundene
Ne þohte he naueremare of Arþur habben are
buten he wolden his mon bicume Arþur Vþeres sune
Arþur wes in Lundene mid alle Brutleoden
he bed his ferde ȝeond alle þissen ærde
þat æuerælc mon þe him god vþen
ræþe and ful sone to Lundene comen
Þa wes Ænglene lond mid ærmþe offulled
her wes wop and her wes rop and reouþen vniuoȝe 
muchel hunger and hæte at æuerælche monnes ȝete
Arþur sende ouer sæ sele tweie cnihtes
to Hoele his mæie þe wes him leofest monnen
þe ahte Bruttaine cniht mid þan bezste
and bad hine ful sone þat he hider come
liþen to londe leoden to helpen
for Chældrich hafde an honde muchel of þissen londe
and Colgrim and Baldulf him to iboȝen weoren
and þohten Arþur þene king driuen ut of cuþþen
binimen him his icunde and his kineriche
þenne were his cun iscend mid scomeliche witen
heore wurþscipe iloren a þissere worlderichen
þenne weoren þan kingge betere þat he iboren neore
Þis iherde Howel þa hahste of Brutaine
 and he cleopien agon his sele cnihtes anan
 and bæd heom to horse hiȝenliche swiþe
 and faren into France to þan freo cnihten
 and seide heom þat heo comen raþe and ful sone
to Mihæles Munte mid muchere strenþe
alle þa þe wolden of seoluere and of golde
wurhscipe iwinne a þissere weorlderichen
To Peito he sende sele his þeines
 and summe touward Flandres feondliche swiþe
and to Turuine tweie þer wenden
 and into Gascuinne cnihtes æc gode
 and hahten heom mid maine touward Mihhæles Munte
 and ær heo eoden to ulode heo sculden habbeon ȝiuen gode
þat heo mihte þa bliþere buȝen from heore ærde
 and mid Howele þan hende cumen to þissen londe
to helpen Arþure aþelest kingen
Þreottene dæies igon weoren seoþþen þa beoden commen þære
þa halden heo to sæ swa hahȝel deh from wolcne
twa hundred scipene þer weoren wel biwitene
me feolden heom mid folke and heo forþ wenden
wind stod and þat weder after heore wille
and heo at Hamtone halden to londe
Up leoppen of scipe wode scalkkes 
beren to londe halmes and burnen
mid spæres and mid sceldes heo wriȝen al þa feldes
Þer wes moni bald Brut þat beot wes aræred
heo beoteden swiþe bi heore quiken liue
þat heo wolden igræten Cheldric þene richen
þene balde kæisere mid muchele harme þere
And ȝif he nolde awæi fleon and touward Alemaine teon
and he wolde on londe mid fehte atstonden
mid balde his beornen beorkes abiden
here beo sculde bilauen þat heom weore alre leofest
hafden and heore honden and heore white halmes
 and swa heo scullen on londen losien heore freonden
hælden into hælle hæþene hundes
Arþur wes i Lundene aþelest kingen
 and iherde suggen suþere spellen
þat was icumen to londe Howel þe stronge
to Hamtune forþrihtes mid þritti þusen cnihten
 and mid vnimete uolke þat wolleȝede þan kinge
Arþur him toȝaines bah mid hæhȝere blisse
mid muchelere monweorede toȝæines his mæie
Tosomne heo comen blisse wes on hirede
custen and clupten and cuþliche speken
 and anan forþrihtes somneden heore cnihtes
Þa weoren þer tosomne sele twa ferden
Howel sculde dihten þritti þusend cnihten
 and Arþur hafde an londe feouwerti þusend an honde
Forþrihtes he wenden touward þan norþ ænde
toward Lincolne þe Cheldric þe kaisere bilai
Ah he heo þa ȝæte nefde noht biwunnen
for þer weoren wiþinnen seoue þusen monnen
ohte men and wihte dæies and nihtes
Arþur mid his ferde fusde touward burȝe
 and Arþur forbæd his cnihtes dæies and nihtes
þat heo liþen stille swulc heo stelen wolden
liþen ouer leoden and luden bilefden
hornes and bemen alle weoren bilafde
Arþur nom enne cniht þe wes oht mon and wiht
 and sende hine to Lincolne to leuen his monnen 
 and he heom to soþe sæide mid muþe
þat cumen wolde Arþur aþelest kingen
to þere middernihte and mid him moni god cniht
 and ȝe wiþinne þenne beoþ eou iwarre
þat þenne ȝe ihereþ þene dune þat ȝe ȝæten untunen
and fuseþ ut of burȝe and eoure feond felleþ
 and smiteþ a Cheldrichen þan strongen and þan richen
and we heom sculleþ tellen Bruttisse spelles
Hit was to þere middelniht þe mone scæn suþriht
Arþur mid his ferde fusde to burh
þat folc wes swa stille swa heo stelen wolden
forþ heo comen liþen þat heo iseiȝen Lincolne
Þus him cleopien agon Arþur þe kene mon
Whar beo ȝe mine cnihtes mine hærekemppen
Iseo ȝe þa teldes þer Childrich liþ i ueldes
Colgrim and Baldulf mid baldere strengþe
þat Alemainisce uolc þat us hæfeþ ihærmed
 and þat Sæxisce uolc þat sorȝen us bihateþ
þat alle habbeoþ aqualde þa hæhste of mine cunne
Constanz and Constantin and Vþer þe wes fader min
and Auriliæn Ambrosie mines fader broþer
 and moni þusend monnen of aþele mine cunne
Uten we heom to liþe and to grunde leggen
and wreken wruþliche ure cun and heore riche
and alle somed forþriht nu ride æueralc god cniht
Arþur gon to riden þa ferde gon gliden
swulc al þa eorþe wolde forbærnen
and smiten i þa ueldes imong Childriches teldes
Þæt wes þæ æreste mon þe þer cleopien agon
Arþur þe heȝe gume þe wes Vþeres sune
kenliche and lude swa bicumeþ kinge
Nu fulste us Marie Goddes milde moder
and ich ibidde hire sune þat he us beon a fultume
Æfne þan wordes turnden heo heore ordes
stikeden and sloȝen al þat heo neh comen
And cnihtes ut of burhȝe buȝen heom toȝæines
ȝif heo fluȝen to burȝen þer heo forwurden
ȝif heo floȝen to þa wude þer hi heom forduden 
comen þer heo comen æuere heo heom sloȝen
Nis hit a nare boc idiht þat æuere weore æi fiht
inne þissere Bruttene þat balu weore swa riue
for volken him wes ærmest þat æuere com to ærde
þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes on folke
dæþ þer wes rife þe eorþe þer dunede
Childrich þe kæisere hæfede ænne castel here
a Lincolnes felde þer he læi wiþinnen
þe wes neouwen iworht and swiþe wel biwust
 and þere weoren mid him Baldulf and Colgrim
and iseȝen þat heore uolc fæiesih worhten
 and heo forþriht anon on mid heore burnen
and fluȝen ut of castle kenscipe bidaled
and fluȝen forþriht anan to þe wude of Calidon
Heo hafden to iferen seouen þusend rideren
and ho bilafden ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
feowerti þusunde ifeolled to þan grunde
Alemainisce men mid ærmþe fordemed
and þa Sexisce men ibroht to þan grunden
Þa isæh Arþur aþelest kingen
þat Childrich wes ifloȝen into Calidonie itoȝen
and Colgrim and Baldulf mid him iboȝen weoren
into þan haȝe wude into þan hæȝe holme
 and Arþur bæh after mid sixti þusend cnihten
Bruttene leoden þene wude al bileien
and an are halfe hine feolden fulle seoue milen
treo uppen oþer treoliche faste
an oþer halue he hine bilai mid his leodferde
þreo daȝes and þreo niht þat wes heom muchel pliht
Þa isæh Colgrim alse he læi þerin
þat þer wes buten mete scarp hunger and hete
ne heom no heore horsen hælp nefde nenne
And þus cleopede Colgrim to þan kaisere
Sæie me lauerd Childric soþere worden
for whulches cunnes þinge ligge we þus here
Whi nulle we ut faren and bonnien ure ferden 
and biginnen fehtes wiþ Arþur and wiþ his cnihtes
for betere us is on londe mid monscipe to liggen
þene we þus here for hungere towurþen
iswencheþ us sære folke to scare
Oþer we sendeþ wiþ and wiþ and ȝeornen Arþures griþ
and bidden þus his milce and ȝisles him bitechen
 and wurchen freondscipe wiþ þan freo kinge
Þis iherde Childric þer he læi wiþinne dic
and he andswarede wiþ ærmliche stefene
Ȝif hit wulle Baldulf þe is þin aȝe broþer
and ma of ure iferen þe mid us sunden here
þat we bidden Arþures griþ and sahtnesse him wurchen wiþ
after æuwer wille don ich hit wulle
For Arþur is swiþe hæh mon ihalden on leoden
leof alle his monnen and of kinewurþe cunne
al of kingen icume he wes Vþeres sune
 and oft hit ilimpeþ a ueole cunne þeoden
þer gode cnihtes cumeþ to sturne fihte
þat heo ærest biȝiteþ after heo hit leoseþ
 and al swa us toȝere is ilumpen here
 and æft us bet ilimppeþ ȝif we moten liuien
Sone forþrihtes andswareden þa cnihtes
Alle us biluuieþ þisne ræd for þu hafest wel isæid
Heo nomen twælf cnihtes and senden forþrihtes
þer he wes on telde bi þas wudes ende
þe an cleopeden anan mid quickere stefne
Lauerd Arþur þi griþ we wolden speken þe wiþ
hider þe kaisere us sent Childric ihaten
 and Colgrim and Baldulf beien tosomne
Nu and æueremare heo biddeþ þine ære
þine men heo wulleþ bicumen and þine monscipe hæȝen
 and heo wulleþ ȝiuen þe ȝisles inowe
 and halden þe for lauerd swa þe beoþ alre leofest
ȝif heo moten liþe heonene mid liue
into heore leoden and laþspæl bringen
For her we habbeoþ ifunden feole cunne sorȝen
at Lincolne bilæued leofe ure mæies 
sixti þusend monnen þa þer beoþ ofslæȝene
 and ȝif hit þe weore wille an heorte
þat we mosten ouer sæ winden mid seile
nulle we naueremare æft cumen here
for her we habbeoþ forloren leoue ure mæies
swa longe swa biþ æuere her ne cume we næuere
Þa loh Arþur ludere stefene
Iþonked wurþe Drihtene þe alle domes waldeþ
þat Childric þe stronge is sad of mine londe
Mi lond he hafeþ todæled al his duȝeþe cnihtes
me seoluen he þohte driuen ut of mire leoden
halden me for hæne and habben mine riche
 and mi cun ai foruaren mi uolc al fordemed
Ah of him biþ iwurþen swa biþ of þan voxe
þenne he biþ baldest ufenan þan walde
 and hafeþ his fulle ploȝe and fuȝeles inoȝe
for wildscipe climbiþ and cluden isecheþ
i þan wilderne holȝes him wurcheþ
Faren whaswa auere fare naueþ he næuere nænne kare
he weneþ to beon of duȝeþe baldest alre deoren
Þenne siȝeþ him to segges vnder beorȝen
mid hornen mid hunden mid haȝere stefenen
hunten þar talieþ hundes þer galieþ
þene vox driueþ ȝeond dales and ȝeond dunes
he ulih to þan holme and his hol isecheþ
i þan uirste ænde i þan holle wendeþ
þenne is þe balde uox blissen al bideled
 and mon him todelueþ on ælchere heluen
þenne beoþ þer forcuþest deoren alre pruttest
Swa wes Childriche þan strongen and þan riche
he þohten al mi kinelond setten an his aȝere hond
ah nu ich habbe hine idriuen to þan bare dæþe
whæþerswa ich wulle don oþer slæn oþer ahon
Nu ich wulle ȝifen him griþ and leten hine me specken wiþ
nulle ich hine slæ no ahon ah his bode ich wulle fon
ȝisles ich wulle habben of hæxten his monnen
hors and heore wepnen ær heo heonne wenden
and swa heo scullen wræcchen to heoren scipen liþen 
sæilien ouer sæ to sele heore londe
 and þer wirþliche wunien on riche
and tellen tidende of Arþure kinge
hu ich heom habbe ifreoied for mines fader saule
 and for mine freodome ifrouered þa wræcchen
Her wes Arþur þe king aþelen bidæled
nes þer nan swa rehȝ mon þe him durste ræden
þet him ofþuhte sære sone þerafter
Childric com of comela to Arþure þan kinge
 and he his mon þer bicom mid his cnihten alle
Feouwer and twenti ȝisles Childric þer bitæhte
alle heo weoren icorene and hæhȝe men iborenne
heo bitahten heore hors and heore burnen
scaftes and sceldes and longe heore sweordes
al heo bilæfden þat heo þer hæfden
forþ heo gunnen siȝen þat heo to sæ comen
þer heore scipen gode bi þere sæ stoden
Wind stod on wille weder swiþe murie
he scufen from þan stronde scipen grete and longe
þat lond heo al bilæfden and liþen after vþen
þat nænne siht of londe iseon heo ne mahten
Þat water wes stille after heore iwille
heo letten tosomne sæiles gliden
bord wiþ borden beornes þer spileden
sæiden þat heo wolden eft to þissen londe
 and wreken wurþliche heore winemæies
 and westen Arþures lond and leoden aquellen
and castles biwinnen and wilgomen wurchen
Swa heo liþen after sæ efne al swa longe
þat heo commen bitwiȝe Ænglelonde and Normandie
heo wenden heore lofes and liþen toward londe
þat heo comen ful iwis to Dertemuþe at Totteneis
mid muchelere blisse heo buȝen to þan londe
Sone swa heo a lond comen þat folc heo asloȝen
þa cheorles heo uloȝen þa tileden þa eorþen
heo hengen þa cnihtes þa biwusten þa londes
alle þa gode wiues heo stikeden mid cnifes
alle þa maidene heo mid morþe aqualden 
and þaie ilærede men heo læiden on gleden
Alle þa heoredecnauen mid clibben heo aqualden
heo velledden þa castles þat lond heo awæsten
þa chirechen heo forbarnden baluw wes on folke
þa sukende children heo adrenten inne wateren
Þat orf þat heo nomen al heo sloȝen
to heore inne ladden and suden and bradden
al heo hit nomen þat heo neh comen
Alle dæi heo sungen of Arþure þan kinge
and sæiden þat heo haueden hames biwunnen
þæ scolden heom ihalden in heore onwalden
 and þer heo wolden wunien wintres and sumeres
and ȝif Arþur weoren swa kene þat he cumen wolde
to fihten wiþ Childrichen þan strongen and þan richen
heo wolden of his rugge makien ane brugge
and nimen þa ban alle of aþele þan kinge
and teien heom togadere mid guldene teȝen
and leggen i þare halledure þer æch mon sculde uorþ faren
to wurþscipe Childriche þan strongen and þan riche
Þis wes al heore gome for Arþures kinges sceome
ah al hit iwraþ on oþer sone þerafter
heore ȝelp and heore gome ilomp heomseoluen to scame
 and swa deþ wel iwære þe mon þe swa ibereþ
Childric þe kaisere biwon al þat he lokede on
he nom Sumersete and he nom Dorsete
and al Deuenescire þat volc al forferde
and he Wiltunscire mid wiþere igrætte
he nom alle þa londes into þære sæstronde
Þa æt þan laste þa lette heo blawen
hornes and bemen and bonnien his ferden
 and forþ he wolde buȝen and Baþen al biliggen
and æc Bristouwe abuten birouwen
Þis was heore ibeot ær heo to Baþe comen
To Baþe com þe kæisere and bilæi þene castel þere
 and þa men wiþinnen ohtliche agunnen
stepen uppen stanene wal wel iwepned oueral
 and wereden þa riche wiþ þan stronge Childriche
Þer lai þe kaisere and Colgrim his iuere 
 and Baldulf his broþer and moni anoþer
Arþur wes bi norþe and noht herof nuste
ferde ȝeond al Scotlond and sette hit an his aȝere hond
Orcaneie and Galeweie Man and Murene
and alle þa londes þe þerto læien
Arþur hit wende to iwislichen þinge
þat Childric iliþen weore to his aȝene londe
and þat he naueremære nolde cumen here
Þa comen þa tidende to Arthure kinge
þat Childric þa kæisere icumen wes to londen
and i þan suþ ende sorȝen þer worhten
þa Arþur seide aþelest kingen
Walawa walawa þat ich sparede mine iua
þat ich nauede on holte mid hungere hine adrefed
oþer mid sweorde al hine toswungen
Nu he me ȝilt mede for mire god dede
ah swa me hælpen Drihten þæ scop þæs dæies lihten
þerfore he scal ibiden bitterest alre baluwen
harde gomenes his bone ich wulle iwurþen
Colgrim and Baldulf beiene ich wulle aquellen
 and al heore duȝeþe dæþ scal iþolien
Ȝif hit wule ivnnen Waldende hæfnen
ich wulle wurþliche wreken alle his wiþerdeden
ȝif me mot ilasten þat lif a mire breosten
 and hit wulle me iunne þat iscop mone and sunne
ne scal nauere Childric æft me bicharren
Nu cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Whar beo ȝe mine cnihtes ohte men and wiþte
To horse to horse haleþes gode
and we sculleþ buȝen touward Baþe swiþe
Leteþ up fusen heȝe forken
 and bringeþ her þa ȝæsles biforen ure cnihtes
and heo scullen hongien on hæȝe treowen
Þer he lette fordon feouwer and twenti childerren
Alemainisce men of swiþe heȝe cunnen
Þa comen tidende to Arþure þan kinge
þat seoc wes Howel his mæi þerfore he wes sari 
i Clud ligginde and þer he hine bilæfde
Hiȝenliche swiþe forþ he gon liþe
þat he bihalues Baþe beh to ane uelde
þer he alihte and his cnihtes alle
and on mid heore burnen beornes sturne
 and he a fif dæle dælde his ferde
Þa he hafde al iset and al hit isemed
þa dude he on his burne ibroide of stele
þe makede on aluisc smiþ mid aþelen his crafte
he wes ihaten Wygar þe Witeȝe wurhte
His sconken he helede mid hosen of stele
Calibeorne his sweord he sweinde bi his side
hit wes iworht in Aualun mid wiȝelefulle craften
Halm he set on hafde hæh of stele
þeron wes moni ȝimston al mid golde bigon
he wes Vþeres þas aþelen kinges
he wes ihaten Goswhit ælchen oþere vnilic
He heng an his sweore ænne sceld deore
his nome wes on Bruttisc Pridwen ihaten
þer wes innen igrauen mid rede golde stauen
an onlicnes deore of Drihtenes moder
His spere he nom an honde þa Ron wes ihaten
Þa he hafden al his iweden þa leop he on his steden
Þa he mihte bihalden þa bihalues stoden
þene uæireste cniht þe verde scolde leden
ne isæh næuere na man selere cniht nenne
þene him wes Arþur aþelest cunnes
Þa cleopede Arþur ludere stæfne
Lou war her biforen us heþene hundes
þe sloȝen ure alderen mid luþere heore craften
and heo us beoþ on londe læþest alre þinge
Nu fusen we hom to and stærcliche heom leggen on
 and wræken wunderliche ure cun and ure riche
 and wreken þene muchele scome þat heo us iscend habbeoþ
þat heo ouer vþen comen to Dertemuþen
 and alle heo beoþ forsworene and alle heo beoþ forlorene
heo beoþ fordemed alle mid Drihttenes fulste 
Fuse we nu forþward uaste tosomne
æfne al swa softe swa we nan ufel ne þohten
and þenne we heom cumeþ to miseolf ic wullen onfon
an alre freomeste þat fiht ich wulle biginnen
Nu we scullen riden and ouer lond gliden
and na man bi his liue lude ne wurchen
ah faren fæstliche Drihten us fulsten
Þa riden agon Arþur þe riche mon
beh ouer wælde and Baþe wolde isechen
Þa tidende com to Childriche þan strongen and þan richen
þat Arþur mid ferde com al ȝaru to fihte
Childric and his ohte men leopen heom to horsen
igripen heore wepnen heo wusten heom ifæied
Þis isæh Arþur aþelest kinge
isæh he ænne hæþene eorl hælden him toȝeines
mid seouen hundred cnihten al ȝærewe to fihten
Þe orl himseolf ferde biforen al his genge
 and Arþur himseolf arnde biuoren al his ferde
Arþur þe ræie Ron nom an honde
he stræhte scaft stærcne stiþimoden king
his hors he lette irnen þat þa eorþe dunede
Sceld he braid on breosten þe king wes abolȝen
he smat Borel þene eorl þurhut þa breosten
þat þæ heorte tochan and þe king cleopede anan
Þe formeste is fæie nu fulsten us Drihte
and þa hefenliche quene þa Drihten akende
Þa cleopede Arþur aþelest kinge
Nu heom to nu heom to þat formest is wel idon
Bruttes hom leiden on swa me scal a luþere don
heo bittere swipen ȝefuen mid axes and mid sweordes
Þer feolle Cheldriches men fulle twa þusend
swa neuere Arþur ne les næuere ænne of his
þer weoren Sæxisce men folken alre ærmest
 and þa Alemainisce men ȝeomerest alre leoden
Arþur mid his sweorde fæiescipe wurhte
al þat he smat to hit wes sone fordon
Al wæs þe king abolȝen swa biþ þe wilde bar
þenne he i þan mæste monie swin imeteþ 
Þis isæh Childric and gon him to charren
 and beh him ouer Auene to burȝen himseoluen
and Arþur him læc to swa hit a liun weoren
 and fusde heom to flode monie þer weoren fæie
þer sunken to þan grunde fif and twenti hundred
þa al wes Auene stram mid stele ibrugged
Cheldric ouer þat water flæh mid fiftene hundred cnihten
þohte forþ siþen and ouer sæ liþen
Arþur isæh Colgrim climben to munten
buȝen to þan hulle þa ouer Baþen stondeþ
 and Baldulf beh him after mid seoue þusend cnihtes
heo þohten i þan hulle hæhliche atstonden
weorien heom mid wepnen and Arþur awæmmen
Þa isæh Arþur aþelest kingen
whar Colgrim atstod and æc stal wrohte
þa clupede þe king kenliche lude
Balde mine þeines buhȝeþ to þan hulles
For ȝerstendæi wes Colgrim monnen alre kennest
nu him is al swa þere gat þer he þene hul wat
hæh uppen hulle fehteþ mid hornen
þenne comeþ þe wlf wilde touward hire winden
Þeh þe wulf beon ane buten ælc imane
 and þer weoren in ane loken fif hundred gaten
þe wulf heom to iwiteþ and alle heom abiteþ
Swa ich wulle nu todæi Colgrim al fordemen
ich am wulf and he is gat þe gume scal beon fæie
Þa ȝet cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Ȝurstendæi wes Baldulf cnihten alre baldest
nu he stant on hulle and Auene bihaldeþ
hu ligeþ i þan stræme stelene fisces
mid sweorde bigeorede heore sund is awemmed
heore scalen wleoteþ swulc goldfaȝe sceldes
þer fleoteþ heore spiten swulc hit spæren weoren
Þis beoþ seolcuþe þing isiȝen to þissen londe
swulche deor an hulle swulche fisces in wælle
Ȝurstendæi wes þe kaisere kennest alre kingen
nu he is bicumen hunte and hornes him fulieþ 
flihþ ouer bradne wæld beorkeþ his hundes
he hafeþ bihalues Baþen his huntinge bilæfued
freom his deore he flicþ we hit scullen fallen
and his balde ibeot to nohte ibringen
and swa we scullen bruken rihte biȝæten
Efne þan worde þa þe king seide
he bræid hæȝe his sceld forn to his breosten
he igrap his spere longe his hors he gon spurie
Neh al swa swiþe swa þe fuȝel fliȝeþ
fuleden þan kinge fif and twenti þusend
whitere monnen wode under wepnen
hælden to hulle mid hæhȝere strengþe
and uppen Colgrime smiten mid swiþe smærte biten
And Colgrim heom þer hente and feolde þa Bruttes to grunde
i þan uormeste ræse fulle fif hundred
Þat isæh Arþur aþelest kingen
and wraþ him iwræþþed wunder ane swiþe
and þus cleopien agon Arþur þe hæhȝe man
War beo ȝe Bruttes balde mine beornes
Her stondeþ us biuoren vre ifan alle icoren
gumen mine gode legge we heom to grunde
Arþur igrap his sweord riht and he smat ænne Sexise cniht
þat þat sweord þat wes swa god æt þan toþen atstod
 and he smat enne oþer þat wes þas cnihtes broþer
þat his halm and his hæfd halden to grunde
þene þridde dunt he sone ȝaf and enne cniht atwa clæf
Þa weoren Bruttes swiþe ibalded
 and leiden o þan Sæxen læȝen swiþe stronge
mid heore speren longe and mid sweoreden swiþe stronge
Sexes þer uullen and fæiesih makeden
bi hundred bi hundred hælden to þan grunde
bi þusund and bi þusend þer feollen æuere in þene grund
Þa iseh Colgrim wær Arþur com touward him
ne mihte Colgrim for þan wæle fleon a nare side
þer fæht Baldulf bisiden his broþer
Þa cleopede Arþur ludere stefne
Her ich cume Colgrim to cuþþen wit scullen ræchen
nu wit scullen þis lond dalen swa þe biþ alre laþþest 
Æfne þan worde þa þe king sæide
his brode swærd he up ahof and hærdliche adun sloh
and smat Colgrimes hælm þat he amidde toclæf
and þere burne hod þat hit at þe breoste atstod
And he sweinde touward Baldulfe mid his swiþren honde
 and swipte þat hæfued of forþ mid þan helme
Þa loh Arþur þe aþele king
and þus ȝeddien agon mid gomenfulle worden
Lien nu þere Colgrim þu were iclumben haȝe
and Baldulf þi broþer liþ bi þire side
nu ich al þis kinelond sette an eower ahȝere hond
dales and dunes and al mi drihtliche uolc
Þu clumbe a þissen hulle wunder ane hæȝe
swulc þu woldest to hæuene nu þu scalt to hælle
þer þu miht kenne muche of þine cunne
