And gret þu þer Hengest þe cnihten wes faȝerest
Ebissa and Ossa Octa and of þine cunne ma
and bide heom þer wunie wintres and sumeres
 and we scullen on londe libben in blisse
bidden for eower saulen þat sel ne wurþen heom nauære
 and scullen her æuwer ban biside Baþe ligen
Arþur þe king cleopede Cador þene kene
of Cornwale he wes eorl þe cniht wes swiþe kene
Hercne me Cador þu ært min aȝe cun
Nu is Childric iuloȝen and awæiward itohȝen
he þencheþ mid isunde aȝen cumen liþen
Ah nim of mire uerde fif þusend monnen
 and fareþ forþrihtes bi dæie and bi nihte
þat þu cumme to þare sæ biforen Childriche
and al þat þu miht biwinnen bruc hit on wunnen
 and ȝif þu miht þene kaisere ufele aquellen þere
ich þe ȝifue to mede al Doresete
Al swa þe aþele king þas word hafede isæid
Cador sprong to horse swa spærc him doh of fure
fulle seoue þusend fuleden þan eorle
Cador þe kene and muchel of his cunne
wenden ouer woldes and ouer wildernes 
ouer dales and ouer dunes ouer deope wateres
Cador cuþe þene wæi þe toward his cunde læi
an oueste he wende fuliwis riht toward Toteneis
dæies and nihtes he com þere forþrihtes
swa neuere Childric nuste of his cume nane custe
Cador com to cuþþe biuoren Childriche
and lette him fusen biforen al þas londes folc
cheorles ful ȝepe mid clubben swiþe græte
mid spæren and mid græte waȝen to þan ane icoren
and duden heom alle clane into þan scipen grunde
 and hæhte heom þere lutie wel þat Childric of heom neore war
 and þenne his folc come and in wolden climben
heore botten igripen and ohtliche on smiten
mid heore waȝen and mid heore speren murþren Childriches heren
Al duden þa cheorles swa Cador heom tæhte
To þan scipen wenden wiþerfulle cheorles
in æuerælche scipe oþer half hundred
And Cador þe kene bæh in toward ane wude hæh
fif mile from þan stude þær stoden þa scipen
and hudde hine on wille wunder ane stille
Childric com sone ouer wald liþen
walde to þan scipen fleon and fusen of londen
Sone swa Cador isæh þat wes þe kene eorl
þat Childric wes an eorþen bitweonen him and þan cheorlen
þa clupede Cador ludere stefne
Wær beo ȝe cnihtes ohte men and wihte
Iþencheþ what Arþur þe is ure aþele king
at Baþen us bisohte ær we wenden from hirede
Leou war fuseþ Childric and fleon wule of londe
and þencheþ to Alemaine þer beoþ his ældren
and wule biȝiten ferde and æft cumen hidere
and wule faren hider in and þencheþ awræken Colgrim
and Baldulf his broþer þæ bi Baþen resteþ
Ah no abide he næuere þære dæȝen ne scal he no ȝif we maȝen
Æfne þere spæche þa spac þe eorl riche
and onuest he gon riden þe reh wes on moden 
halden ut of wudescaȝe scalkes swiþe kene
and after Cheldriche þan strongen and þan richen
Cheldriches cnihtes bisehȝen heom baften
isehȝen ouer wolden winden heoremærken
winnien ouer ueldes fif þusend sceldes
Þa iwærþ Childric chærful an heorten
and þas word sæide þe riche kaisere
Þis is Arþur þe king þe alle us wule aquellen
fleo we nu biliue and into scipen fusen
and liþen forþ mid watere ne recchen we nauere wudere
Þa Childric þe kaisere þas word hæuede isæid
þa gon he to fleonne feondliche swiþe
 and Cador þe kene com him after sone
Childric and his cnihtes to scipe comen forþrihtes
heo wenden þa scipen stronge to scuuen from þan londe
Þæ cheorles mid heore botten weoren þer wiþinnen
þa botten heo up heouen and adunriht sloȝen
þer wes sone islaȝen moni cniht mid heore wahȝen
wiþ heore picforcken heo ualden heom to grunden
Cador and his cnihtes sloȝen heom baften
Þa isah Childric þat heom ilomp liþerlic
þa al his folc mucle feol to þan grunde
Nu isæh he þer bihalues ænne swiþe mare hul
þat water tiþ þerunder þat Teine is ihaten
þa hulle ihaten Teinnewic þiderward flæh Childric
swa swiþe swa he mihte mid feouwer and twenti cnihten
Þa isæh Cador hu hit þa uerde þer
þat þe kaisere flæh and touwarde þæ hulle tæh
and Cador him after swa swiþe swa he mahte
and him to tuhte and hine oftoc sone
Þa saide Cador þe eorl swiþe kene
Abid abid Childric ich wulle þe ȝefen Teinewic
Cador his sweord anhof and he Childric ofsloh
Monie þe þer fluȝen to þan watere heo tuhȝen
inne Teine þan watere þer heo forwurþen
al Cador acwælde þat he quic funde
and summe heo crupen into þan wude and alle he heom þer fordude
Þa Cador heom haueden alle ouercumen and ælc al þat lond inumen 
he sette grit swiþe god þat þerafter longe stod
þeh ælc mon beere an honde behȝes of golde
ne durste nauere gume nan oþerne ufele igreten
Arþur wes forþ iwende into Scotlonden
for Howel lai inne Clud faste biclused
Hafden Scottes hine bilæien mid luþere heore craften
and ȝif Arþur neore þe raþer icumen þenne weoren Houwel inumen
and al his folc þer islaȝen and idon of lif daȝen
Ah Arþur com sone mid selere strengþe
and Scottes to fleonne feor of þan ærde
into Muræine mid mucle monweorede
And Cador com to Scotlonde þer he Arþur ifunde
Arþur and Cador into Clud ferden
 and funden þer Howel mid hahȝere blisse an sel
of his seocnesse isund wes iwurþen
muchel wes þa blisse þæ þa wes in burȝe
Scottes weoren inne Mureine and þer þeohten wunien
 and mid bolde heore worden heore beot makeden
and sæiden þat heo wolden þa riche walden
and Arþur þer abiden mid baldere strenþe
for ne durste nauere Arþur for his life come þer
Þa iherde Arþur ærhþen bidæled
whæt Scottes hafden isæid mid heore huxworden
þa sæide Arþur aþelest kingen
Whær ært þu Howel hæhst of mine cunne
and Cador þe kene ut of Cornwaile
Leteþ blæwen bemen and bonnien ure ferden
 and to þere midnihte we sculleþ faren forþriht
toward Mureine ure monscipe to bitellen
Ȝif hit wule Drihte þe scop þæs daȝes lihten
we heom sculle tellen sorhfulle spelles
heore ȝælp fellen and heomseolue aquellen
To þere midnihte Arþur aras forþriht
hornes me gon blawen mid hahȝere stafnen
cnihtes gunnen arisen and ræhȝe word speken
Mid muche monweorede into Mureine 
forþ gunnen wræsten þreottene þusend
a feormeste flocke feondliche kene men
Seoþþen com Cador þe eorl of Cornwæille
mid seouentene þusen selere þeinen
Seoþþen com Heowel mid his kemppen swiþe wel
mid an and twenti þusen mid aþelere kempen
Seoþþen com Arþur aþelest kingen
mid seouen and twenti þusend siȝen heom afterward
sceldes þer cliseden lihten hit gon dæȝen
Þat word com to Scotten þær þar heo wuneden
hu Arþur þe king com touward heore londe
feondliche swiþe mid vnimete folke
Þa weoren ærhest þat ær weoren baldest
and gunnen to fleonnen feondliche swiþe
into þan watere þer wunderes beoþ inoȝe
Þat is a seolcuþ mere iset a middelærde
mid fenne and mid ræode mid watere swiþe bræde
mid fiscen and mid feoȝelen mid uniuele þingen
Þat water is unimete brade nikeres þer baþieþ inne
þer is æluene ploȝe in atteliche pole
Sixti æitlondes beoþ i þan watere longe
in ælc of þan æitlonde is a clude hæh and strong
þer næstieþ arnes and oþere græte uoȝeles
Þe ærnes habbeoþ ane laȝe bi æuerælches kinges dahȝen
whænneswa æi ferde fundeþ to þan ærde
þeonne fleoþ þa fuȝeles feor i þan lufte
moni hundred þusen and muchel feoht makieþ
Þenne is þat folc buten wene þat reouþe heom is to cumene
of summes cunnes leoden þe þat lond wulleþ isechen
Tweien dæȝes oþer þreo þus scal þis taken heo
ær unkuþe men to þan londe liþen
Ȝet þer is sellic to suggen of þan watere
þer walleþ of þan mæren a moniare siden
of dalen and of dunen and of bæcchen deopen
sixti wateres alle þer isomned
swa neuere ut of þan mære na man no uindeþ
þat þer ut wenden buten an an ænde
an imetliche broc þe of þan mere ualleþ 
 and swiþe isemeliche into sæ wendeþ
Þa Scottes weoren todeled mid muclen vniselen
ȝeond þa monie munten þa i þan watere weoren
Arþur biseohte scipen and gon heom to wenden
 and sloh þer vniuoȝe moni and inoȝe
 and moni þusend þer wes dæd for heom trukede ælc bræd
Arþur þe aþele was an æst side
Howel þe sele wes a suþ halue
 and Cador þe kene bi norþen heom biwusten
and his smale uolc he setten alle bi weste siden
Þa weoren Scottes ihalden for sottes
þer heo leien ȝeond þa cliues faste biclused
þer weoren sixti þusend mid sorreȝe forfarene
Þa wes Irlondes king icume into hafene
twalf milen from Arþure þer he lai mid ferde
Scotten to hælpen Howel to forfarene
Þis iherden Arþur aþelest kinge
 and nom his ane ferde and þiderward fusden
 and funde þene king Gillomar þe icumen wes to londe þar
Arþur him faht wiþ and nolde him ȝiuen na griþ
and feolde Irisce men feondliche to grunden
And Gillomar mid twalf scipen teh from þan londe
 and ferde to Irlonde mid harme swiþe stronge
And Arþur a þan londe sloh al þat he uunde
and seoþþen he wende to þan mere þer he his mæi lette
Howel þene hende hahst of Brutlonde
wiþuten Arþure aþelest kingen
Arþur Howel uunde þer he wes bi hauene
bi þan mere brade þer he abiden hafde
Þa fainede swiþe folc an hirede
of Arþures cume and of aþele his dede
þer wes Arþur forþriht twei dæies and twa niht
Scottes leie ȝeond clude moni þusend dede
mid hungere foruarene folkene alre ærmest
I þan þridde dæiȝe faire hit gon daȝiȝen
þa tuȝen touward hirede alle þat weoren ihadded
 and þreo biscopes wise a boke wel ilæred 
preostes and muneckes vnimete monie
canones þer comen monie and wel idone
mid alle þan halidomen þa hahst an londe weoren
and ȝeornden Arþures griþ and his aþmeden
Þider þa wifes comen þa i þan londen wuneden
heo wæiden in hære ærmen heore children ærmen
heo weopen on Arþure wunder ane swiþe
and heore uæx fæire wælden to volde
curuen heore lockes and þer niþer læiden
to þas kinges foten biforen al his duȝeþen
nailes to heore nebbe þat æfter hit bledde
Neh þan alle clæne nakede heo weoren
sorhliche heo gunnen clupien to Arþure þan kinge
and summe þus iseiden þer heo on siþ weoren
King we beoþ on ærde ærmest alre uolke
we ȝeorneþ þine milzce þurh þæne milde Godd
Þu hauest a þisse londe ure leoden aslæȝen
mid hungere and mid hete mid feole cunne hærmen
mid wapnen mid wæteren mid feole wansiþen
vre children imaked faderlese and frofre bidæled
Þu ært Cristine mon and we alswa sunden
Sæxisce men beoþ hæþene hundes
Heo comen to þisse londe and þis folc here aqualden
ȝif we heom hereden þat was for ure hermen
for we nefden nænne mon þe us wiþ heom mihten griþien
Heo us duden swiþe wa and þu us dest al swa
þa heþene us hatieþ and þe Cristine us sari makieþ
Wær scullen we bicumen queþen þa wif to þan kinge
Aȝef us ȝet þa quicke men þa liggeþ ȝeond þas cluden
and ȝif þu ȝiuest milze þisse moncunnen
þi monscipe biþ þa mare nu and æueremære
Lauerd Arþur ure king leoþe vre benden
Þu hafust al þis lond inomen and al þis folc ouercumen
We beoþ under uote a þe is al þa bote
Þis iherde Arþur aþelest kingen
þesne wop and þesne rop and reouþen vniuoȝe
þa toc he to ræde and reosede on heorte
he uunde on his ræde to don þat heo hine beden 
he ȝæf heom lif he ȝef heom lumen and heore lond to halden
He lette blæwen bemen and þa Scottes bæcnien
 and heo ut of cluden to þan scipen comen
an auerælchen siden siȝen touward londe
Heo weoren swiþe iharmede mid scærpen þan hungre
aþes heo sworen swiken þat nalden
and heo þa iȝefuen ȝisles þan kingen
and alle ful sone þas kinges men bicomen
 and seoþþen heo gunnen fusen þat folc þer todelden
ælc mon to þan ende þer he wes wuniende
and Arþur þer griþ sette god mid þan bezste
Whær ært þu Howel mi mæi monne me leofest
isixst þu þisne muchelne mære þer Scottes beoþ amærred
isihst þu þas hæhȝe treon and sihst þu þas ærnes teon
Inne þisse uenne is fisc unimete
Isihst þu þas æitlondes þe ȝeond þas watere stondeþ
Seollic þuhte Howel of swulchere isihþe
and wonddrede wide bi þan watere flode
and þus þer cleopede Howel hæhes cunnes
Seoþþen ich wes mon iboren of mire moder bosme
no isah ich a none londe þus seolcuþe þinges
swa ich here biuoren me mid æȝenen bihælde
Wundreden Bruttes wunder ane swiþe
Þa cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Howel min aȝe mæi monnen me leofest
lust mire worden of mucle mære wunder
þat ic þe wulle tellen of soþe mine spellen
Bi þisse mære enden þer þis water wendeþ
is an lutel wiht mære monnen to wundre
He is endlonge feouwer and sixti munden
he is imeten a bræde fif and twenti foten
fif foten he is deop alfene hine dulfen
Feowernoked he is and þerinne is feower kunnes fisc
and ælc fisc an his ende þer he his cun findeþ
ne mai þer nan to oþere buten al swa tacheþ his icunde
Nes næuer nan mon iboren ne of swa wise crafte icoren
no libbe he swa longe þe maȝen hit vnderstonde
what letteþ þene fisc to uleoten to þan oþere
for nis þer noht bitwenen buten water clæne 
Þa ȝet cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Howel i þissen londes ænde neh þere sæstronde
is a mære swiþe muchel þat water is unfæle
and whænne þa sæ vledeþ swulc heo wulle aweden
and falleþ inne þene mære vnimete swiþe
no biþ næuere þæ mere on watere þa mare
Ah þenne þa sæ falleþ in and scen warþ þa uolden
and heo biþ al inne in alden hire denne
þenne swelleþ þe mære and swærkeþ þa vþen
vþen þer leppeoþ ut vnimete grete
fleoþ ut a þat lond þat leoden agriseþ an hond
Ȝif þer cumeþ æi mon þat noht ne cunne þeron
þat seollic to iseonne bi þere sæstronde
ȝif he his neb wendeþ touwærd þan mære
ne beo he noht swa loh iboren ful wel he beoþ iborȝen
þat water him glit bisiden and þe mon þer wuneþ softe
after his iwille he wuneþ þer uul stille
þat no biþ he for þan watere naþþing idracched
Þa sæide Howel hæh mon of Brutten
Nu ic ihere tellen seolcuþe spellen
 and seollic is þe lauerd þat al hit isette
Þa cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Blaweþ mine hornes mid hæhȝere stæfne
and suggeþ mine cnihtes þat ic fare forþrihte
Bemen þer blewen hornes þer stureden
blisse wes an hirede mid bisie þan kinge
for ælc wes ifreoured and ferde toward his ærd
And þe king forbæd heom bi heore bare liuen
þat na mon on worlde swa wod no iwurþe
no swa ærwitte gume þat his griþ bræke
and ȝif hit dude æi mon he sculden dom þolien
Æfne þan worde fusde þa uærde
þer sungen beornes seolcuþe leoþes
of Arþure þan kinge and of his hereþringen
and sæiden on songe to þisse worlde longe
neore neueremære swulc king ase Arþur þurh alle þing
king no kæisere in næuere nare kuþþe
Arþur forþ to Eouuerwic mid folke swiþe seollic
and wunede þer wiken sixe mid muchelere wunne 
Þa burhwalles weoren tobroken and tofallen
þat Childric al forbarnden and þa hallen alle clæne
Þa cleopede þe king Piram ænne preost mæren
he wes swiþe wis mon and witful on bocken
Piram þu ært min aȝe preost þe æþ þe scal iwurþen
Þe king nom ane rode hali and swiþe gode
and bitok Piram an hond and þermid swiþe muchel lond
and þene ærchebiscopes staf þer he Piram aȝaf
Ær wes Piram preost god nu he is ærchebiscop
Þa hæhte hine Arþur aþelest kingen
þat he rærde churechen and þa songes rihten
and Goddes folc biwusten and fæire heom dihtten
And he hæhte alle cnihtes demen rihte domes
and þa eorþetilien teon to heore cræften
 and æuerælcne gume oþerne igræten
 and wulc mon swa wurs dude þene þe king hafde iboden
he wolde hine ifusen to ane bare walme
 and ȝif hit weore læþ mon he sculde hongie for þon
Þa ȝet cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
hæhte þat alc mon þe his lond hafde forgan
mid wulches cunnes wite swa he biwæiued weore
þat he aȝain come ful raþe and ful sone
þe riche and þe laȝe and hefde æft his aȝen
bute he weore swa fule biwite þat he weore lauerdswike
oþer touward his lauerd manswore þene þe king demde forlore
Þer come þreo ibroþeren þe weore kiniborne
Lot and Angel and Vrien welle hwulche þreo men
Þeos hereþringes þreo comen to þan kinge
 and setten an heore cneowen biforen þan kæisere
Hal seo þu Arþur aþelest kingen
and þi duȝeþe mid þe a mote heo wel beo
We sundeþ þreo broþeren iboren of kingen
is al ure icunde lond igan ut of ure hond
for habbeoþ hæþene men us hene imakede
and iwæst us al Leonæis Scotlond and Muræf
 and we biddeþ þe for Godes luue þat þu us beo fultume
and for þire mucle wurþscipe þat þu us wurþe milde
aȝif us ure icunde lond and we þe sculleþ luuien 
hælden þe for lauerd an ælche leodwisen
Þis iherde Arþur aþelest king
hu þeos þreo cnihtes fæire hine bisohten
reousede on heorte and he reordien gan
and þas word sæide selest alre kinge
Vrien bicum mi mon þu scalt to Muræiue aȝæn
þerof þu scalt beon icleoped king of þan londe
 and hæh an mine hirede mid þine monweorede
And Angele ich sette an hond al togadere Scotlond
habbe hit an honde and beon king of þan londe
from þan fader to þan sune þerof þu scalt mi mon bicumen
And þu Lot mi leofe freond Godd þe wurþe liþe
þu hauest mine suster to wiue þæ bet þe scal iwurþe
Ich þe ȝifue Loenæis þat is a lond faier
and ich wulle leggen þerto londes swiþe gode
biside þere Humbre wurþ an hundred punden
For mi fader Vþer þe while þe he wes king here
lufede wel his dohter þe wes his bæd iþohte
 and heo is mi suster and haueþ sunen tweien
þeo me beoþ on londe children alre leofest
Þus spæc Arþur þe king þa wes Wolwain lute child
swa ves þe oþer Modræd his broþer
Wale þat Moddræd wes ibore muchel hærm com þerfore
Arþur for to Lundene and mid him his leoden
he heold inne londe ane muchele hustinge
and sette alle þa laȝen þat stoden bi his ælderne daȝen
alle þa laȝen gode þe her ær stoden
he sette griþ he sette friþ and alle freodomes
Þenene he for to Cornwale to Cadores riche
he funde þer a mæide vnimete fæier
Wes þas mæidenes moder of Romanisce mannen
Cadores maȝe and þat maide him bitahte
 and he heo fæire afeng and softe heo fedde
Heo wes of heȝe cunne of Romanisce monnen
næs in nane londe maide nan swa hende
of specche and of dede and of tuhtle swiþe gode 
heo wes ihaten Wenhauer wifmonne hendest
Arþur heo nom to wife and luuede heo wunder swiþe
þis maiden he gon wedde and nom heo to his bedde
Arþur wes i Cornwale al þene winter þere
and al for Wenhæuere lufe wimmonne him leofuest
Þa þe winter wes agan and sumer com þer anan
Arþur hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
þat his folc gode aswunden ne læie þere
He ferde to Æxchæstræn to þan midfesten
 and heold þer his hustinge of hehȝen his folke
 and seide þat he wolde into Irlonde
wenden al þat kinelond to his æhȝere hond
buten þe king Gillomar to him raþer come ær
and mid listen him speken wiþ and ȝirnde Arþures griþ
he wolde westen his lond and luþere him gon an hond
mid fure mid stele streit gomen wurchen
 and þat londfolc aslæn þe wolde stonden him aȝein
Æfne þan worde þa þe king sæide
þa andswarede þat folc fæire þan kinge
Lauuerd king hald þi word we beoþ alle ȝarewe
to ganne and to ride oueral to þire neode
Þer wes moni bald Brut þe hafde beres leches
heouen up heore bruwen iburst an heore þonke
Wenden touwarde innen cnihtes mid heore monnen
heo ruokeden burnen bonneden helmes
heo wipeden hors leoue mid linnene claþe
heo sceren heo scoiden scalkes balde weoren
sum scæft horn sum scaft ban sum ȝarked stelene flan
sum makde þwonges gode and swiþe strong
summe beoveden speren and beonneden sceldes
Arþur letten beoden ȝeond al his kineþeoden
þat æuerælc god cniht to him come forþriht
and euerælc oht mon comen forþriht anan
 and waswa bilæfden his leomen he sculde leosen
 and whaswa come gladliche he sculden wurþe riche
Seouen niht uppen Æstre þa men hafden iuast
þa comen alle þa cnihtes to scipen forþrihtes
wind heom stod an honde þe scaf heom to Irlonde 
Arþur a þet lond ferde and þa leoden amerden
muchel uolc he asloȝ orf he nom vniuoh
 and æuere he hæhte ælcne mon chirechegriþ halden
Þet tidinde com to þan kinge þe lauerd wes of þan londe
þat þer wes icumen Arþur and ærmþen iwrohte þer
He sumnede al his leoden ȝeond his kinelonde
and his Irisce uolc fusden to fehte
toȝæines Arþure þan aþele kinge
Arþur and his cnihtes heom wepnede forþrihtes
 and foren heom toȝeines folc vnimete
Arþures men weoren mid wepnen al biþehte
Þa Irisce men weoren nakede neh þan
mid speren and mid axen and mid swiþe scærpe sæxen
Arþures men letten fleon vnimete flan
and merden Irisc folc and hit swiþe ualden
ne mæhten heo iþolien þurh nanes cunnes þingen
ah fluȝen awai on siþe swiþe uæle þusend
and Gillomar þe king flah and awæwardes teh
and Arþur him after and þene king ikahte
he nom bi þan honde þene king of þan londe
Arþur þe hæȝe herbeorwe isohte
an his mode him wes þa æþe þat Gillomar him wes swa neh
Nu dude Arþur aþelest kingen
swiþe muche freondscipe atforen al his folke
he lette þene king scrude mid ælchere prude
and æc bi Arþure sat and æc mid himseolue æt
mid Arþure he win dronc þat him wes mucheles unþonc
Naþeles þa he isah þat Arþur wes swiþe glad
þa cleopede Gillomar an his horte him wes sær
Lauerd Arþur þi griþ ȝef me leomen and ȝif me lif
ich wulle þi mon bicumen and biteche þe mine þreo sunen
mine sunen deore to don al þine iwille
 and ȝet ich wulle mare ȝif þu me wult ȝefen ære
ich wulle þe bitache ȝisles swiþe rich
children sume sixti hæȝe and swiþe mæhti
Ȝet ich wulle mære ȝif þu me ȝifuest ære
ælche ȝere of mine londe seouen þusend punde 
 and senden heom to þine londe and sixti mark of golde
 and ȝet ich wulle mare ȝif þu wult me ȝifuen are
alle þa steden mid alle heore iweden
þa hæuekes and þa hundes and hehȝe mine mahmes
ich bitache þe to honde of al mine londe
And þenne þu hauest þis idon ich wulle nimen halidom
of seint Columkille þe dude Godes iwille
 and seint Brændenes hæfed þe Godd seolf haleȝede
 and seinte Bride riht fot þe hali is and swiþe god
 and halidomes inoȝe þe comen ut of Rome
 and swerien þe to soþe swiken þe þat ich nulle
ah ich þe wulle luuien and halden þe for lauerd
halden þe for hahne king and miseolf beon þin vnderling
Þis iherde Arþur aþelest king
 and he gan lihȝen luddere steftne
 and he gon andswerie mid ædmode worden
Beo nu glad Gillomar ne beo þin heorte noht sær
for þv ært a wis mon þa bet þe scal iwurþen
for æuere me æhte wisne mon wurþliche igreten
for þine wisdome no scal þe noht þa wurse
muchel þu me beodest þe scal beon þa betere
Her forþrihtes biforen al mine cnihtes
forȝiuen þe amare al þæ haluendæle
of golde and of gærsume ah þu scalt mi mon bicumen
and half þat gauel sende ælche ȝere to mine londe
Halfe þa steden and halfe þa iweden
halue þa hauekes and halue þa hundes
þæ þu me beodest ich wulle þe bilefen
ah ich wulle habben þire hæhre monne children
þeo heom beoþ alre leofuest ich heom mai þe bet ileouen
 and swa þu scalt wunien in wurþscipe þire
a þine kinedome i þine rihte icunden
 and ic þe wulle ȝeuen to þat ne scal þe king woh don
buten he hit abugge mid his bare rugge
Þeo hit sæide Arþur aþelest kingen
Þa hafden he an hond al tosomne Irlond
 and þe king his mon bicumen and bitæht him his þreo seonen
Þa spæc Ærþur to sele his cnihten
Faren to Hislond and nimen we hit to ure honde 
Ferde þer fusde and com to Islonde
Ælcus þe king wes ihaten hæh mon of þan ærd
he iherde þa tidende of Arþure þan kinge
he dude al so wis mon and wende toȝeines him anan
anan forþrihtes mid sixtene cnihtes
he bar on his honde ænne mucle ȝeord of golde
Sone swa he Arþur isæh swa he on his cneowen bæh
 and þas word him iquaþ þe king wes afæred
Wulcume sire Arþur wilcume lauerd
Her ich biteche þe an hond al togadere Islond
þu scal beon min hæhȝe king and ich wul beon þin underling
Ich þe wullen heren swa mon scal don his hærren
 and ich wulle þi mon bicumen and bitæche þe minne leofue sune
Esscol is ihaten and þu hine scalt iæþelien
to cnihte hine dubben alse þin aȝene mon
His moder ich habbe to wife þas kinges dohter of Rusie
And æc ælche ȝere ȝiuen þe wulle æhte
seoue þusend punde of seoluere and of golde
 and to æuerælche ræde beon ȝæru to þire neode
Þis ich wullen þe swerien uppen mine sweorden
þe halidom is a þere hilte þe hexste of þisse londe
likien swa ne liken nulle ich þe nauere swiken
Þis iherde Arþur aþlest kingen
Arþur wes wunsum þer he hafde his iwillen
 and he wes wod sturne wiþ his wiþeriwinnen
Arþur þa liþe word iherde of þan leodkinge
al þat he ȝirnde al he him ȝette
Ȝisles and aþes and alle his ibodes
Þa iherde suggen soþere worden
þe king of Orcaneie vnimete kene
Gonwais wes ihate haeþene kempe
þat Arþur king wolde cume to his londe
mid muchele scipferde fusen to leoden
Gonwais him uerde toȝæines mid wisen his þeines
and sette Arþure an hond al Orcaneies lond
and twa and þritti æitlond þe þider in liggeþ
and his monradene mid muchelere mensce 
And he him hafde a uoreward biforen al his duȝeþe
ælche ȝere to iwiten fulle sixti scipen
mid his aȝere costninge bringen heom to Londenne
ifulled to iwisse mid gode sæfisce
Þis forward he iuaste and ȝisles he funde
and aþes he swor gode swiken þat he nolde
 and seoþþen he lefe nom and forþ he gon liþen
Lauerd haue wel godne dæi ich wulle cumen wenne ich mai
for nu þu art mi lauerd leouest alre kingen
Þa Arþur hafde þis idon þa ȝet he wolde mare afon
he nom his writen gode and senden to Gutlonde
and grætte þe king Doldanim and hehte hine sone comen to him
 and himseolf his mon bicume and bringen him his tweien sunen
And ȝif þu þat nulle do þat þu wulle
Ich þe wulle sende sixtene þusend
heȝe herekempen to mucle þine harmen
scullen þi lond wasten and þiire leoden aslan
and þat lond setten swa heom bezst þincheþ
and þe seoluen binden and to me bringen
Þis iherde þe king þræt þas kaiseres
 and he on uaste iueng fæiere his iweden
hundes and hafekes and his gode horsses
muchel seoluer muchel gold his tweien sunen an his hond
And forþ he gon wenden to Arþure þan kingen
and þas word sæide Doldanim þe sele
Hail seo þu Arþur aþelest kingen
Her ich bringe tweiene mine sunen beiene
heore moder is kinges istreon quene heo is min aȝene
Ich tache þe mine leofen sunen miseolf ich wulle þi mon bicumen
ich heo biȝat mid ræflac ut of Rusie
And ic wulle sende gauel of mine londe
æuerælche ȝere to ȝiueles þingen
ich wulle senden þe into Lundene seouen þusend punden
Þat ic wulle swerien þat nulle ich næuere swiken
ah here ich wulle þi mon bicomen þi monscipe is þa mare 
swiken nulle ich nauere swa longe swa beoþ auere
Arþur nom his sonde and sende to Winentlonde
to Rumareþ þan kinge and hehte him cuþen an hiȝinge
þat he hæfde in his hond Brutlond and Scotlond
Gutlond and Irlond Orcaneie and Islond
He hæhte Rumareþ cumen and bringen him his ældeste sune
 and ȝif he þat nolde he wolde hine driuen of londe
and ȝif he mihte afon he wolde hine slæn oþer anhon
and his lond al fordon his leoden fordemen
Þis iherde Rumared þe riche king of Winete
swiþe he wes afered al swa þa oþere weoren arer
laþe him weoren þa tidende from Arþure þan kinge
Noþeles þe king Rumareþ hercnede rædes
he nom his ældeste sune and sele twælf eorles
 and ferde to Arþure þan kinge aþele
and set æt his foten and feire hine gon greten
Hail seo þu Arþur aþelest Brutten
Ich hatten Rumareþ þe king of Winetlonde
inoh ich habbe iherd kenne of kenscipe þine
þat þu ært widen icuþ kingen alre kennest
Þu hauest moni kinelond biȝiten al to þire hond
nis na king an londe þe þe maȝen stonde
king ne na kaisere in nauere nane compe
of al þat þu biȝinnest þu dest þine iwille
Her ich æm to þe icume and broht þe mine aldeste sune
her ich sette þe an hond me seoluen and mi kinelond
and minne sune leofe and mine leoden alle
wif and mine weden and alle mine wunnen
wiþ þat þu me griþie wiþ þine grim ræsen
And beo þu min hæhȝe king and ich wulle beon þin underling
and senden þe to honde fif hundred pund of golde
þas ȝeuen ich finde þe wulle æueralche ȝere
Al Arþur him ȝette þat þe king ȝirde
and seoþþen he heolde runen wiþ sele his þeinen
 and seide þat he wolde aȝæin to þisse londe
and iseon Wenhaiuer þe wuneliche quene
Bemen he lette blawen and bonnien his ferden
and to scipen wenden wunder bliþe þeines
Wind heom stod on willen weder alse heo wolden 
bliþe heo weoren alle for þi up heo comen at Grimesbi
Þat iherden sone þa hæhste of þissen londe
and to þære quene com tidende of Arþure þan kinge
þat he wes isund icumen and his folc on selen
Þa weoren inne Bruttene blissen inoȝe
Her wes fiþelinge and song her wes harpinge imong
pipen and bemen murie þer sungen
Scopes þer sungen of Arþure þan kingen
 and of þan muchele wurþscipe þe he iwunnen hafeden
folc com to hirede of feole cunne þeode
widen and siden folc wes on selen
Al þat Arþur isæh al hit him to bæh
riche men and pouere swa þe haȝel ualleþ
nes þer nan swa wræcche Brut þat he nes awælȝed
Her mon mai arede of Arþure þan king
hu he twelf ȝere seoþen wuneden here
inne griþe and inne friþe in alle uæȝernesse
Na man him ne faht wiþ no he ne makede nan unfriþ
ne mihte nauere nan man biþenchen of blissen
þat weoren in æi þeode mare þan i þisse
ne mihte nauere moncunne nan swa muchel wunne
swa wes mid Arþure and mid his folke here
Ich mai sugge hu hit iwarþ wunder þæh hit þunche
Hit wes in ane ȝeoldæie þat Arþur in Lundene lai
þa weoren him to icumen of alle his kinerichen
of Brutlonde of Scotlonde of Irlonde of Islonde
and of al þan londe þe Arþur hæfede an honde
alle þa hæxte þeines mid horsen and mid sweines
Þer weoren seouen kingene sunes mid seouen hundred cnihten icumen
wiþuten þan hired þe herede Arþure
Ælc hafede an heorte leches heȝe
and lette þat he weore betere þan his iuere
Þat folc wes of feole londe þer wes muchel onde
for þe an hine talde hæh þe oþer muche herre
Þa bleou mon þa bemen and þa bordes bradden
water me brohte an uloren mid guldene læflen
seoþþen claþes soften al of white seolke
Þa sat Arþur adun and bi him Wenhauer þa quene 
seoþþen sete þa eorles and þerafter þa beornes
seoþþen þa cnihtes al swa mon heom dihte
Þa heȝe iborne þene mete beoren
æfne forþrihten þa to þan cnihten
þa touward þan þæinen þa touward þan sweinen
þa touward þan bermonnen forþ at þan borden
Þa duȝeþe wærþ iwraþþed duntes þer weoren riue
ærest þa laues heo weorpen þa while þa heo ilæsten
and þa bollen seoluerne mid wine iuulled
 and seoþþen þa uustes uusden to sweoren
Þa leop þer forþ a ȝung mon þe ut of Winetlonde com
he wes iȝefen Arþure to halden to ȝisle
he wes Rumarettes sune þas kinges of Winette
Þus seide þe cniht þere to Arþure kinge
Lauerd Arþur buh raþe into þine bure
and þi quene mid þe and þine mæies cuþe
 and we þis comp scullen todelen wiþ þas uncuþe kempen
Æfne þan worde he leop to þan borde
þer leien þa cniues biforen þan leodkinge
þreo cnifes he igrap and mid þan anæ he smat
i þere swere þe cniht þe ærest bigon þat ilke fiht
þat his hefued i þene flor hælde to grunde
Sone he sloh ænne oþer þes ilke þeines broþer
ær þa sweordes comen seouene he afelde
Þer wes fæht swiþe græt ælc mon oþer smat
þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes an hirede
Þa com þe king buȝen ut of his buren
mid him an hundred beornen mid helmen and mid burnen
ælc bar an his riht hond whit stelene brond
Þa cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Sitteþ sitteþ swiþe elc mon bi his liue
and waswa þat nulle don he scal fordemed beon
Nimeþ me þene ilke mon þa þis feht ærst bigon
 and doþ wiþþe an his sweore and draȝeþ hine to ane more
 and doþ hine in an ley uen þer he scal liggen
and nimeþ al his nexte cun þa ȝe maȝen iuinden
and swengeþ of þa hafden mid breoden eouwer sweorden
Þa wifmen þa ȝe maȝen ifinden of his nexten cunden 
kerueþ of hire neose and heore wlite ga to lose
and swa ich wulle al fordon þat cun þat he of com
And ȝif ich aueremare seoþþen ihere
þat æi of mine hirede of heȝe na of loȝe
of þissen ilke slehte æft sake arere
ne sculde him neoþer gon fore gold ne na gærsume
hæh hors no hære scrud þat he ne sculde beon ded
oþer mid horsen todraȝen þat is elches swiken laȝen
Bringeþ þene halidom and ich wulle swerien þeron
swa ȝe scullen cnihtes þe weoren at þissen fihte
eorles and beornes þat ȝe hit breken nulleþ
Ærst sweor Arþur aþelest kingen
seoþþen sworen eorles seoþþen sweoren beornes
seoþþen sweoren þeines seoþþen sweoren sweines
þat heo naueremare þe sake nulde arere
Me nom alle þa dede and to leirstowe heom ladden
Seoþþen me bleou bemen mid swiþe murie dremen
weoren him leof weoren him læþ elc þer feng water and clæþ
 and seoþþen adun seten sæhte to borden
al for Arþure æiȝe aþelest kingen
Birles þer þurngen gleomen þer sungen
harpen gunnen dremen duȝeþe wes on selen
Þus fulle seoueniht wes þan hirede idiht
Seoþþen hit seiþ in þere tale þe king ferde to Cornwale
þer him com to anan þat wæs a crafti weorcmon
and þene king imette and feiere hine grætte
Hail seo þu Arþur aþelest kinge
Ich æm þin aȝe mon moni lond ich habbe þurhgan
ich con of treowrekes wunder feole craftes
Ich iherde suggen biȝeonde sæ neowe tidende
þat þine cnihtes at þine borde gunnen fihte
a midewinteres dæi moni þer feollen
for heore mucchele mode morþgomen wrohten
and for heore hehȝe cunne ælc wolde beon wiþinne
Ah ich þe wulle wurche a bord swiþe hende
þat þer maȝen sitten to sixtene hundred and ma
al turn abuten þat nan ne beon wiþuten
wiþuten and wiþinne mon toȝæines monne 
Whenne þu wult riden wiþ þe þu miht hit leden
and setten hit whar þu wulle after þine iwille
and ne dert þu nauere adrede to þere worlde longen
þat æuere ænie modi cniht at þine borde makie fiht
for þer scal þe hehȝe beon æfne þan loȝe
Timber me lete biwinnen and þat beord biginnen
to feouwer wikene uirste þat wrec wes iuorþed
To ane heȝe dæie þat hired wes isomned
and Arþur himseolf beh sone to þan borde
and hehte alle his cnihtes to þan borde forþrihtes
Þo alle weoren iseten cnihtes to heore mete
þa spæc ælc wiþ oþer alse hit weore his broþer
alle heo seten abuten nes þer nan wiþuten
Æuere ælches cunnes cniht þere wes swiþe wel idiht
alle heo weoren bi ane þa hehȝe and þa laȝe
ne mihten þer nan ȝelpen for oþere kunnes scenchen
oþer his iueren þe at þan beorde weoren
Þis wes þat ilke bord þat Bruttes of ȝelpeþ
and sugeþ feole cunne lesinge bi Arþure þan kinge
Swa deþ aueralc mon þe oþer luuien con
ȝif he is him to leof þenne wule he liȝen
and suggen on him wurþscipe mare þenne he beon wurþe
ne beo he no swa luþer mon þat his freond him wel ne on
Æft ȝif on uolke feondscipe arereþ
an æueræi time bitweone twon monnen
me con bi þan læþe lasinge suggen
þeh he weore þe bezste mon þe æuere æt at borde
þe mon þe him weore laþ him cuþe last finden
Ne al soh ne al les þat leodscopes singeþ
ah þis is þat soþþe bi Arþure þan kinge
Nes næuer ar swulc king swa duhti þurh alle þing
for þat soþe stod a þan writen hu hit is iwurþen

no mare no lasse buten alse his laȝen weoren
Ah Bruttes hine luueden swiþe and ofte him on liȝeþ
and suggeþ feole þinges bi Arþure þan kinge
þat næuere nes iwurþen a þissere weorlderichen 
inoh he mai suggen þe soþ wule uremmen
seolcuþe þinges bi Arþure kinge
Þa wes Arþur swiþe heh his hired swiþe hende
þat nas na cniht wel itald no of his tuhlen swiþe bald
inne Wales no in Ænglelond inne Scotlond no in Irlond
in Normandie no inne France inne Flandres no inne Denemarc
no in nauere none londe þe a þeos halfe Mungiu stondeþ
þet weoren ihalde god cniht no his deden itald oht
bute he cuþe of Arþure and of aþelen his hirede
his wepnen and his weden and his horsleden
suggen and singen of Arþure þan ginge
and of his hiredcnihten and of heȝe heore mihten
and of heore richedome and hu wel hit heom bicomen
Þenne weore he wilcume a þissere weorlderichen
come þer he come and þeh he weore i Rome
al þat iherde of Arþure telle
heom þuhte muchel seollic of selen þan kinge
And swa hit wes iuuren iboded ær he iboren weoren
swa him sæide Merlin þe witeȝe wes mære
þat a king sculde cume of Vþere Pendragune
þat gleomen sculden wurchen burd of þas kinges breosten
and þerto sitten scopes swiþe sele
and eten heore wullen ær heo þenne fusden
and winscenches ut teon of þeos kinges tungen
and drinken and dreomen daies and nihtes
þis gomen heom sculde ilasten to þere weorlde longe
And ȝet him seide Marlin mare þat wes to comene
þat al þat he lokede on to foten him sculde buȝen
Þa ȝet him sæide Mærlin a sellic þe wes mare
þat sculde beon unimete care of þas kinges forþfare
and of þas kinges ende nulle hit na Brut ileue
buten hit beon þe leste dæþ at þan muchele dome
þenne ure Drihte demeþ alle uolke
Ælles ne cunne we demen of Arþures deþen
for he seolf sæide to sele his Brutten
suþ inne Cornwale þer Walwain wes forfaren
and himseolf wes forwunded wunder ane swiþe 
þat he uaren wolde into Aualune
into þan æitlonde to Argante þere hende
for heo sculde mid haleweie helen his wunden
and þenne he weore al hal he wolde sone come heom
Þis ilefde Bruttes þet he wule cumen þus
 and lokieþ a whenne he cume to his londe
swa he heom bihahte ar he heonne wende
Arþur wes an weorlde wis king and riche
god mon and griþful his gumen hine luueden
Cnihtes he hafede prute and græte on heore mode
 and speken to þan kinge of seollichen þinge
and þus þat hired cleopede to heȝe þan kinge
Lauerd Arþur faren we to Francene riche
and iwinnen al þat lond to þire aȝere hond
flemen alle þa Freinscen heore king feollen
alle þa castles bonien and setten heom to mid Brutten
 and rixlien a þere riche mid rehȝere strengþe
Þa andswarede Arþur aþelest kingen
Eouwer wille ich wulle don ah ær ich wulle to Norweien
and ich wulle mid me leden Lot minne oþem
he is Wælwaynes fader þa ich wel luuie
For beoþ icumen of Norweiȝe niwe tidende
þat Sichelin king þer is ded his duȝeþen bileued
 and hæ hafeþ al his kineriche biqueþe her Loþþe
For þe king is al bidæled sune and eke dohteren
and Lot is his suster sune þe bet him scal iwurþe
for ich hine wulle in Norwæȝe neowe king makien
and hine wæl lere to witeȝen wel þa leoden
And þenne ich þus habbe idon ich wullen seoþþen cumen ham
and ȝarkien mine ferde and faren into France
and ȝif þe king me stont wiþ and nulle ȝeornen mi griþ
ich hine wulle mid fehte fallen to þan grunde
Arþur lette blawen hornes and bemen
and lette beoden to sæ Bruttes swiþe balde
Scipen he hæfde gode bi þere sæflode
fiftene hundred fusden from londe
and fluȝen after þere sæ swulc heo fluht hafden
 and buhȝen into Norwæȝen mid baldere strengþen
Sone swa heo comen hafne heo nomen 
mid muchelere strengþe stepen a þa riche
Arþur senden his sonde wide ȝeond þan londe
 and hæhte heom cumen sone and Lot habben to kinge
 and ȝif heo þat nolden alle heom he wolde aslan
Þa nomen heore sonden eorles Norenissce
and senden to þan kingen and hahten hine aȝain wenden
 and ȝif þu nult aȝæin faren sorhȝen þu scalt habben and kare
for longe biþ auere þat ne iwurþ næuere
þat we uncuþne mon to kinge scullen hæbben
For ȝif Sikelin is forþfaren her beoþ oþere icoren
þe we maȝen bi vre iwille hæbben to kinge
 and þis is þat soþe nis þer nan oþer
oþer far þe awæiward and wend þe riht hamward
oþer todæi a seoueniht þu scalt habben græt fiht
Þa eorles Norenissce nomen heom to ræde
þat king heo wolden habben of seoluen heore cunden
for al Sikelines quiden sotscipe heo heolden
And swa longe swa beoþ æuere ne scal hit stonde næuere
ah we scullen nimen Riculf þe is swiþe riche eorl
and hebben hine to kinge þis is us iqueme
and sumnen ure ferde ȝeond al þissen ærde
and faren to Arþure and flemmen hine mid fehte
 and Lot we scullen fusen and flemen of londen
oþer we mid fehten sculleþ hine fallen
Heo nome Riculfe þene eorl of Norene
and hefuen hine to kinge þeh hit neore him noht icunde
and sumneden uerde ȝeond Nornisce ærde
And Arþur an his ende ȝuond þat lond gon wende
þat londe he þurharnde burhȝes he uorbarnde
æhte he nom inoh muche moncun he þer ofsloh
And Riculf him gon riden toȝæines Arþure anan
togædere heo fusden and veht heo bigunnen
Bruttes buȝen heom to balu þer wes riue
Luken vt of scaþe sweordes longe
hefden fluȝen a þene uelde faluwede nebbes
beorn aȝein beorne scaft sette an breoste
burnen þer breken Bruttes bisie weoren
brustleden sceldes scalkes ueolen 
 and swa al þene dæiliht ilaste þis muchele fiht
ferden heo æst ferden heo west þer Noreine wes þa wurse
ferden heo suþ ferden heo norþ þe Norrene þer feollen
Bruttes weoren balde þa Noreine heo aqualden
Noreinisce men þer feollen fif and twenti þusend
and Riculf king þer wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
lutel þer eode to læue of þan leodfolke
wulcswa hafuede þat wracche lif ȝirde Arþures griþ
Arþur bisæh a Lot þe leof him wes swiþe
and þus him cleopien agon Arþur þe riche mon
Lot wend hider to me þu art mi wine deore
Her ich þe biteche al þas kineriche
of me þu scalt halden and habben me to munde
Þa wes Walwain þider icumen Lottes ældeste sune
of Rome from þan Pape þe Supplice wes ihate
þa longe him wes dihte and makede hine to cnihte
Wælle wel wes hit bitoȝen þat Walwain wes to monne iboren
for Walwæin wes ful aþelmod an ælche þeouwe he wes god
he wes metecusti and cniht mid þan bezste
Al Arþures hired wes swiþe ifurþed
for Walwaine þan kene þe icumen wes to hirede
and for his fader Lote þe iloten wes to kinge
Þa spac Arþur him wiþ and hehte hine halden god griþ
and hehte hine luuien his griþfulle leoden
 and þa griþ nolden halden fallen heom to grunde
Þa ȝet cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Whær beo ȝe mine Bruttes fareþ nu forþrihtes
ȝarkieþ bi þan flode mine scipen gode
Al duden þa cnihtes swa Arþur heom hæhte
Þa þa scipen weoren ȝaru Arþur gon to sæ faren
mid him he nom his cnihtes his Norenissce þeines
and balden his Bruttes and bah forþ mid vþes
and þe duhtie king com to Denemarke
he lette slæn teldes wide ȝeond þa feldes
bemen he lette blawen and his cume bodien
Þa wes inne Denemarke a king of mucle mæhte
Æscil wes ihate hext ouer Denene
he isah þat Arþur biwon al þat him wes on willen 
Æscil king hine biþohte whæt he don mahte
laþ him wes to leosen leouen his leoden
He isah þat mid strengþe stonden he ne mahte
aȝain Arþure mid nauere nane compe
He sende gretinge to Arþure kinge
hundes and hauekes and swiþe gode horsses
seoluer and ræd gold mid ræhfulle worden
 and ȝet dude mare Æscil þe mære
he sende to þan hæxten of Arþures hireden
and bad heom arndien him to hæhȝen þan kingen
þat he moste his mon bicumen and to ȝisle bitæchen his sune
and ælche ȝere him senden gauel of his londe
ænne bæt mid isunde from breorde to grunde
of golde and of gærsume and of godliche pallen
and seoþþen he wolde swerien swiken þat he nalden
Þis iherden Arþur aþelest kingen
þat Æscil Denene king wolde beon his vnderling
buten ælche fihte he and alle his cnihtes
Þa iwraþ iaþeled Arþur þe riche
and þus andswærede mid aþmode worden
Wel wurþe þan monne þe mid wisdome
biwineþ him griþ and friþ and freondscipe to halden
Þenne he isiht þet he biþ mid strengþe ibunden
iȝarked al to leosen leofue his richen
mid liste he mot leoþien luþe his bendes
Arþur hehte þene king cume and bringen his aldeste sune
and he swa dude sone þe king of Denemarke
Arþures iwille sone he gon fulle
tosomne heo comen and sæhten iwurþen
Þa ȝet cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Faren ich wulle to France mid muchele mire ferde
ich wulle habben of Noreweie niȝe þusend cnihtes
 and of Denemarke ich wulle leden niȝe þusend of þan leoden
and of Orkaneie enleuen hundred
and of Mureinen þreo þuseond monnen
and of Galeweien fif þusend of þan leoden
and of Irlonde elleuen þusend
and of Brutaine mine cnihtes balde 
scullen þræsten biforen me þritti þusunde
and of Gutlonde ich wulle leden ten þuseond of þan leoden
and of Frislonde fif þusend monnen
and of Brutaine Howel þene balde
and mid swulche uolke France ich wulle isechen
And swa ich ibiden Godes ære ȝet ich wulle haten mare
þat of alle þan londen þat stondeþ a mire honden
ich haten ælcne ohtne mon þe his wepnen beren con
alse he wule liuen and his lumen habben
þat he faren wiþ me to fehten wiþ Frolle
þat is Francene king fæie he scal iwurþe
He wes iboren i Rome of Romanisce cunne
Forþ ferde Arþur þat he com to Flandres
þat lond he gon biwinnen and sette hit mid his monnen
and seoþþe he beh þanene into Buluine
and al Buluines lond nom hit to his aȝere hond
and seoþþen he nom þene wæi þe in touward France læi
Þa bed he his bod allen his beornen
for þær heo uoren þat na wiht heo ne nomen
buten he mid rihte hit biȝiten mihte
mid rihte chepinge i þas kinges hirede
Þat iherde Frolle þer he wes inne France
of Arþures ispede and of alle his deden
and hu al biwonne þat he lokede on
and al hit him to beh þat he mid eȝene isah
þa wes þe king Frolle laþliche offered
A þere ilke worlde þa þis wes iwurþen
wes Francene lond Gualle ihaten
and Frolle wes from Rome ifaren into France
and ælche ȝere sende gauel of þan londe
ten hundred punde of seoluer and of golde
Nu iherde Frolle þe ældere wes of France
of þere londsorȝe þe Arþur dude an londe
Sonde he sende sone an uest touward Rome
and hehte Romanisce folc reden heom bitweonen
hu feole þusend cnihten heo þider wolden senden
þat he þa æþ mihte wiþ Arþure uihte
and ulemen of londe Arþur þene stronge 
Cnihtes gunnen riden vt of Romleoden
fif and twenti þusend ferden touward France
Þis iherde Frolle mid muchele his ferde
þat þe Romanisce uolc riden touward londe
Frolle and his ferde heom toȝeines ferde
þa heo comen tosomne kene men and wihte
of alle þan ærde vnimete uerde
Þæt iherde Arþur aþelest kingen
 and sumnede his ferde and heom toȝaines wende
Ah næs næuere king nan þa quic wes an eorþen
þa eouere ær an uolde swulc folc awalde
for of alle þan kinelonde þe Arþur hafuede an honde
forþ he ladde mid him alle þa kenneste men
þat nuste he neuere on weorlde hu feole þusend, þer weoren
Sone swa heo comen tosomne Arþur and Frolle
harliche heo igrætten al þat heo imette
Cnihtes swiþe stronge igripen speren longe
and ræsden heom togædere mid ræhȝere strengþe
Alle dæi þer weore duntes swiþe riue
folc feol to uolden and fæiesiþ worhten
græmende segges grasbæd isohten
gullen þa helmes ȝeoumereden eorles
sceldes þær scenden scalkes gunnen reosen
Þa cleopede Arþur aþelest kingen
Whar beo ȝe mine Bruttes balde mine þaines
Þe dæi him forþ ȝeongeþ þis folc us aȝein stondeþ
Lette we heom to gliden scærpe gares inoȝe
 and techen heom to riden þene wæi touward Romen
Æfne þan worde þe Arþur iseide
he sprong forþ an stede swa sparc deþ of fure
Him weore fuliende fifti þusende
hærde herekempen hælden to fihte
smiten uppen Frolle þær he wes on ulocke
and brohten hine of fleme mid muclen his folke
þer Arþur ofsloh muchel uolc and vniuoh
Þa fleh into Parise Frolle þe riche
and þa ȝeten tunden mid teonen inoȝe
and þa word seide sorhful an heorte 
Leouere me weore þat ich iboren neore
Þa weoren inne Paris plihtliche spelles ful iwis
sorhfulle iberen burhmen gunnen beouien
walles heo gunnen rihten þa ȝæten heo gunnen dihten
mete heo nomen al þat heo neh comen
an ælchere halue heo heolden to burȝe
heo uerden þider alle þe heolden mid Frolle
Þat iherde Arþur aþelest kingen
þat inne Paris wunede Frolle mid unimete uerde
and seiden þat he wolde wiþ Arþure stonden
To Paris ferde Arþur ærhþe bideled
and bilæi þa walles and arerde his teldes
a feower halue he heo bilai fouwer wiken and enne dæi
Auared weoren þa leden þa þere weoren wiþinnen
þa burh wes wiþinnen afulled mid monnen
and æten sone þene mete þe þer wes isomned
Þa feouwer wiken weoren aȝonged þa Arþur wes þær atstonden
þæ wes inne burȝe vnimete sorȝe
mid wræcche þan falke þe leie þer an hungre
þer wes wop þer wes rop and reouþen vniuohȝe
Heo cleopeden to Frolle and beden hine friþ wurchen
Arþures mon bicumen and his monscipe bruken
and þene kinedom halden of Arþure þan kenen
and no lete noht þat wræcche uolk uorfaren al mid hungre
Þa andswarede Frolle freo he wes an heorte
Nai swa me helpe God þæ alle domes awalt
ne scal ich nauere his mon bicume no he mi kinelauerd
miseolf ich wulle fihte a Gode is al þat rihte
Þa ȝet cleopede Frolle freo mon an heorte
Næi swa me helpe Drihten þe scop þas dæies lihten
nulle ic naueremare ȝirnen Arþures ære
ah fehten ich wulle buten ælche cnihte
licame wiþ licame biforen mine leoden
hond aȝain honde wiþ Arþure kinge
Whaþer unkere swa beoþ þere wakere sone he biþ þe laþere
wahþer vnkere swa þer ma luuien his freonden he biþ þe leouere
and whaþer unkere þe mæi of oþere þat betere biwinne 
habben al þis oþeres lond and sette hit an his aȝere hond
Þis ic wulle ȝirne ȝif Arþur hit wule ȝetten
and þis ich wulle swerien uppen mine sweorden
and ȝisles ich wulle finden þreo kingene sunen
þat ich þis forward wulle fastliche halden
þat nulle ich hit liȝen bi mine quike liuen
For leouere me is to liggen bifore mine leoden
þan ich iseo an uolde forfaren heom mid hungre
For we habbeoþ mid fehte ure cnihtes uorfarene
scalkes auælled fifti þusende
and moni ænne gode wifmon iwhorht to bleþere widewe
moni child faderlæs and frouere bidaled
and nu þis folc mid hungre wunderliche ihærmede
Forþi hit is betere bitwixen unke seoluen
todælen and todihten þis kinelond mid fihte
and habbe hit þa betere and bruken hit on wunne
Frolle nom twalf cnihtes mid þissen worden forþrihtes
and sende heom an sonde to Arþure kinge
 and iwuste ȝif he wolde þis forewarde halde
and mid his aȝere hond bitelen þat kinelond
oþer uoreliggen his leoden to harmen
and ȝif he hit bitalden hafde hit on an onwalde
Þat iherde Arþur aþelest kingen
næs he neuere swa bliþe ær an his liue
for him likede tidende from Frolle þan kinge
and þas word seide Arþur þe sele
Wel saiþ Frolle þe king is of France
betere is þat wit tweie bitelen þas riche
þene þer beon ofslaȝene ure þeines snelle
Þis foreward ich biluuie bifore mine leoden
to ane isette dæie to don þat he beodeþ
þat scal beon tomarȝen biforen unker monnen
þat fehten wit scullen unc seoluen and falle þe forcuþere
And whaþer unker þe geþ abake and þis feoht wulle forsake
beon he in ælche londe iqueþe for ane sconde
þenne mæie me singe of ane swulche kinge
þe his beot haueþ imaked and his cnihtscipe forsaken
Þæt iherde Frolle þe king wes of France 
þat Arþur fehten wolden himseolf buten cnihte
Strong mon wes Frolle and sterc mon on mode
and his beot imaked hafde biforen al his duȝeþe
and he ne mihte for scome muchelen scenden hine seoluen
bilæuen his balde ibeot þat he i burh hafde iseid
Sæide þat he sæide to soþe he hit wende
þat Arþur hit wolde forsaken and nawiht to þan fehte taken
for ȝif hit wuste Frolle þe king wes ane France
þat Arþur him ȝetten wolde þat he iȝirnd hafde
don he hit nolde for a scip ful of golde
Neoþeles wes Frolle to fihte swiþe kene
muche cniht and strong mon and modi on heorten
and sæide þat he wolde þene dæi halde
in þan æitlonde þe mid watere is biȝeonge
Þat æitlond stondeþ ful iwis inne þere burh of Paris
Þer ich wulle mid fehte bitele mine irihte
mid scelden and mid cnihtes iwede
nu tomarȝen biþ þe dæi habben þe hit biȝiten mæi
Comen þa tiþende to Arþure þan kinge
þat Frolle wolde mid fæhte France bitellen
næs he næuere swa bliþe ær an his liue
and he lehȝen agon ludere stæfnenen
and þas word seide Arþur þe kene
Nu ich wat þat Frolle wiþ me wulle fihte
tomarȝe in þan dæie alse he seolf demde
i þan aitlonde þat mid watere is bistonde
for hit bicumeþ kinge þat his word stonde
Leteþ blawen bemen and bodien mine monnen
þat æuerælc god mon toniht wakien for þon
and bidden ure Drihten þe alle domes awalt
þat he me iscilde wiþ Frolle þene wilde
and mid his riht honde witeȝe me wiþ sconde
And ȝif ich mæi þis kinelond biȝiten to mire aȝere hond
auereælche ærmen mon þe æþ scal iwurþen
and wurchen ic wulle muchel Godes wille
Nu me uulsten þerto þe alle þing mai wel idon
þe heȝe heueneliche king stonde me an helping
for ich hine luuien wulle þa while þe ich liuie
Þer wes al longe niht songes and candelliht 
hæhliche sungen clarckes hali Godes salmes
Þa hit dæi wes amarȝen duȝeþe gunne sturien
his wæpnen he nom an honden Arþur þe stronge
warp he an his rugge a ræf swiþe deore
ænne cheisil scurte and ænne pallene curtel
ænne burne swiþe deore ibroiden of stele
Sette he an hefde ænne helm godne
to his side he swende his sweorde Caliburne
his sconken he helede mid hosen of stele
and duden on his uoten spuren swiþe gode
Þe king mid his weden leop on his stede
me him to rehte anne scelde gode
he wes al clane of olifantes bane
Me salde him an honde enne scaft stronge
þer wes a þan ænde a spære swiþe hende
hit wes imaked i Kairmeþin bi a smiþ þe hehte Griffin
hit ahte Vþer þe wes ær king her
Þa þe iwepned wes þe rahȝe þa gon he to uarene
he mihte þa bihalde þe þer bihalfues weore
þene king richne rehliche riden
seoþþen þis weorlde wes astald nes hit nowhar itald
þat æuere ai mon swa hende wunden uppen horse
swa him wes Arþur sune Vþeres
Riden after þan kinge balde hereþringes
a þen feoremeste flocke feouwerti hundred
heȝe herekempen bihonged mid stelen
baldere Brutten bisie mid wepnen
After þan fusden fifti hundred
þeo Wælwain ladde þe wæs a wælkempe
Seoþþen þer gunnen ut siȝen sixti þusende
Bruttes swiþe balde þat wes þa bacwarde
Þer wes þe king Angel þer wes Lot and Urien
þer wes Vrienes sune Ywæin ihaten
þer wes Kæi and Beduer and biwusten þa uerde þer
þer wes þe king Howel hah mon of Brutlond
Cador þer wes æc þe kene wes on flocke
þer wes of Irlonde Gillomar þe strong
þer wes Gonwais þe king Orkaneies deorling 
þer wes Doldamin þe kene ut of Gutlonde
þer wes Escil þe king Denemarkes deorling
Folc þer wes afoten swa feole þusend monnen
þat nas nauere na swa witful mon a þissere weorlderichen
a nauere nane spelle þat mihte þa þusend telle
bute he hauede mid rihte wisdom of Drihtene
oþer he hafde mid him þat him hafde Mærlin
Arþur forþ gon liþe mid vnimete folke
þat he com fuliwis into þere burh of Paris
a west halue þan watere mid mucle his genge
An æst hælf wes Frolle mid mucchelere ferde
Ȝaru to þan fehte biforen his cnihtes alle
Arþur nom ænne bat godne and bæh þer an inne
mid scelde mid stede and mid alle his iwede
and he þat scip stronge scaf from þan londe
and stop uppen þat æitlond and ladde his stede an his hond
his men þe hine þer brohte alse þe king hehte
leten þene bat buȝen forþ mid þan vþen
Frolle into scipe ferde þe king wes unuele
þat he auere þohte wiþ Arþure to fehte
Ferde to þan æite mid aþele his wepnen
uppen þan æit he stop and his stede him after droh
þeo men þe hine þer brohten alse þe king hehte
lette þene bat fusen forþ mid þan vþen
and þa kinges tweien ane þer wuneden
Þa me mihte bihalden þe þer bihalues weoren
folc a þan uolde feondliche adredde
heo clumben uppen hallen heo clumben uppen wallen
heo clumben uppen bures heo clumben uppe tures
þat comp to bihalden of þan tweom kingen
Arþures men beden mid muchele æþmoden
Godd þene gode and þa hali his moder
þat heore lauerd þere siȝe moste habben
and þa oþere eke bede for heore kinge
Arþur stop a stel boȝe and leop an his blancke
and Frolle mid his iwede leop on his steden
þe an an his ænde a þan æitlonde 
and þæ oþer an his ænde i þan æitlonde
heo quehten heore scaftes kinewurþe cnihtes
heo græneden heore steden gode cnihtes heo weoren
Næs he næuere ifunde a næuere nane londe
nan swa wihtful mon þat hit wuste ær þan
whæþer of þan kingen ouercumen sculde liggen
for beien heo weoren cnihtes kene ohte men and wihte
muchele men on mihte and a maine swiþe stronge
Heo muneȝeden heore steden and tosomne gunnen riden
fusden feondliche þat fur him sprong after
Arþur smat Frolle mid feondstronge maine
uppen þene sceld hehȝe
and þe stede þe wes god leop ut i þe ulod
Arþur ut mid his sweorde balu wes a þan orde
and puinden uppen Frolle þer he wes an ulode
ær heore comp weore icumen to þan ænde
Ah Frolle mid honde igræp his spere longe
and kept Arþur anan alse he aneoust com
and þene stede balde smat i þere breoste
þat þat spere þurh raf and Arþur adun draf
Þa aras þe mondrem þat þe uolde dunede aȝen
aqueþen þa weolcne for reme of þan uolke
Þær Bruttes wolden ouer water buȝen
ȝif Arþur up ne sturte stercliche sone
and igræp his sceld godne ileired mid golde
and toȝaines Frolle mid feondliche lechen
breid biforen breosten godne sceld brade
And Frolle him to fusden mid his feondræse
and his sweord up ahof and adunriht sloh
and smat an Arþures sceld þat he wond a þene feld
þe helm an his hæuede and his hereburne
gon to falsie foren an his hafde
 and he wunde afeng feouwer unchene long
heo ne þuhte him noht sær for heo næs na mare
þat blod orn adun ouer al his breoste
Arþur wes abolȝe swiþe an his heorte
and his sweord Caliburne swipte mid maine
and smat Frolle uppen þæne hælm þat he atwa helden 
þurhut þere burne hod þat hit at his breoste atstod
Þa feol Frolle folde to grunde
uppen þan grasbedde his gost he bilæfde
Þa Bruttes lohȝen ludere stefuene
and leoden to fleonen feondliche swiþe
Arþur þe riche wende to londe
and þus cleopien agon aþelest kingen
Whær ært þu Walwain monne me leofest
Heot þas Romwæren alle mid griþen liþen heonne
ælc mon bruke his ham swulc Godd hit him on
hat ælcne mon halde griþ uppen leome and uppen lif
and ich hit wulle dihten todæi a seouennihte
hat þis folc þenne liþen al tosomne
and cumen to me seoluen þæ bet heom scal iwurþen
Heo scullen me monradene mid monscipe fremmen
and ich heom wulle holden a mine onwolden
and setten i leode laȝen swiþe gode
For nu scullen Romanisce laȝen to þan grunde reosen
þa iuurn here stoden mid Frolle
þe liþ on æite ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
Herafter ful sone scal his cun of Rome
heren tidinge of Arþure þan kinge
for ich heom wulle wiþ speken and Rome walles tobreken
 and munegie heom hu king Belin Bruttes ladde þider in
and iwon him þa londes alle þat stondeþ into Rome
Arþur beh to þan ȝæte forn at þere burȝe
comen witfulle men þe þa burh biwusten
and Arþur letten binnen mid alle his monnen
bitahten him halles bitahten him castles
bitahten him ful iwis al þa burh of Paris
þer wes muchel blissce mid Brutisce uolke
Þe dæi sæh to burhȝe þe Arþur iset hafde
com al þa monweorede and his men bicomen
Arþur nom his duȝeþe and atwa heom todalde
and þa haluendæle Howele bitætte
and hehte hine uaren sone mid muchele þere uerde
mid Brutisce monnen londes iwinnen
Howel dude al swa alse Arþur hine hehte
he biwon Barri and alle þa londes þerbi 
Angou and Turuine Aluerne and Gascunne
and þa hafuenes alle þe herden to þan londes
Guitard þe duc hæhte þe Peytouwe ahte
he nolde buȝen Howele ah heold toȝæines him æuere
nolde he ȝirnen na griþ ah Howel him faht wiþ
ofte he uolc ualde and ofte he ulem makede
Howel al þat lond weste and ofsloh þa leode
Þa isæh Guitard þe i Peitou wes lauerd
þat alle his leoden him to lose eoden
wiþ Howele he griþ makede mid al his monweorede
and bicom Arþures mon þas aþele kingen
Arþur him warþ liþe and luuede hine swiþe
 and hehte hine his lond bruken for he him bæh to foten
þa hafde Howel hæhliche agunnen
Arþur hafde France and freoliche heo sette
he nom þa his ferde and wende ȝeond þan ærde
to Burguine he wende and sette hit an his honde
and seoþþen he gon liþen into Loherne
and alle þa londes sette himseolue an honde
al þat Arþur isæh al hit him to bæh
and seoþþen he wende ful iwis aȝain ham to Paris
Þa hafde Arþur France mid gode griþe astalde
iset and isemed þat sel was an þeoden
þa hehte he þa cnihtes alden þa he hafde ȝare athalden
þat heo to þan kinge comen and heore læn afængen
for heo feole ȝeren hafden ibon his iueren
Summen he ȝæf lond summen seoluer and gold
summen he ȝæf castles summen he ȝaf claþes
hehte heom uaren an wunne and beten heore sunnen
forbed heom to berne wapnen for ælde heom eode ouenan
and hehte heom luuien swiþe Godd in þissen liue
þat he an ende ful iwis ȝefen heom his paradis
þæt heo mosten bruken blisse mid ænglen
Alle þa cnihtes alde foren to heore londe
and þa ȝunge bilæfden mid leouen heore kingen
Alle þa niȝen ȝere Arþur wuneden þere
niȝen ȝere he heold France freoliche on honde
and seoþþen na lengere þat lond he ne walde 
Ah þa while þe þat kinelond stod an Arþures hond
þinges seolcuþe siȝen to þere þeode
monienne modfulne mon Arþur makede milde
and monienne hehne mon he helde to his foten
Hit wes an ane Æsttere þat men hafden iuaste
þat Arþur an Æstere dæi hafde his aþele men atsomne
al þat hæhste moncun þat herden into Francen
 and of alle þan londen þe þider in læien
Þer he ȝette his cnihten alle heore irihten
elc ane he ȝef æhte alse he iærned hafde
Þus him iquaþ Arþur aþelest kingen
Kæi bisih þe hiderward þu ært min haxte stiward
her ich Angou ȝiue þe for þire weldede
and alle þa irihte þe þider in beoþ idihte
Cneole me to Beduer þu art min hexte birle her
þa while þa ich beo an liue luuien ich þe wulle
her ich ȝiue þe Neustrie aneuste mire riche
Þa hehte Neustrie þat nu hatte Normandie
Þe ilke tweien eorles weoren Arþures deore men
at rede and at rune an æuerælche tune
Þa ȝet him seide Arþur aþelest kingen
Wend þe hider Howeldin þu ært mi mon and mi cun
haue þu Bulune and bruc his on wunne
Cumme ner Borel þu art cniht wis and war
her ich þene Mans þe mid monscipe bitæche
and bruc þu his on wunne for þire weldede
Þus Arþur þe king delde his drihtliche londes
after heore iwurhte for he heom þuhte wurþe
Þa weoren bliþe spelles in Arþures hallen
þer wes harepinge and song þer weoren blissen imong
Þa Æstre wes aȝonge and Aueril eode of tune
and þat gras was riue and þat water wes liþe
and men gunnen spilien þat wes Mæi at tune
Arþur nom his folc feire and to þere sæ uerde
and lette bonien his scipen wel mid þan bezsten
 and ferde to þissen londe and up com at Londen
up he com at Lundene leoden to blissen 
Al hit wes bliþe þat hine isæh mid eȝen
sone heo gunnen singe of Arþure þan kinge
and of þere wurþscipe muchele þe he iwunne hafde
Þer custe uader þene sune and seide to him welcume
dohter þa moder broþer þene oþer
suster custe suster þa softere heom wes an heorten
A monie hundred studen stoden bi þan weie
folc fraininge of feole cunne þingen
and cnihtes heom talden of heore onwalden
and heore ȝeolp makeden of muchele biȝeten
Ne mihte na mon suggen nære he na swa hende mon
of halue þan blissen þa weoren mid þan Brutten
Ælc ferde an his neode ȝeond þas kineþeode
from burhȝe to burhȝe mid blissen uniuoȝe
and þus hit ane stunde stod a þan ilke
blisse wes on Brutene mid balde þan kinge
Þa Æstre wes aȝeonge and sumer com to londe
þa nom Arþur his red wiþ riche his monnen
þat he wolde inne Karliun bere his crune him on
and a Whitesunedæi his folc þer isomnie
A þen ilke daȝen men gunnen demen
þat nes i nane londe burh nan swa hende
na swa wide cuþ swa Karliun bi Uske
buten hit weoren þa burh riche þe Rome is ihaten
Þa ȝet wes mid þan kinge moni mon an londe
þat quidde þa burh of Karlion ricchere þene Rome
and þat Uske weore selest alre wateren
Medewes þer weoren brade bihalues þere burhȝe
þer wes fisc þer wes fuȝel and fæiernesse inoȝe
þer wes wude and wilde deor wunder ane monie
þer wes al þa murhþe þe æi mon mihte of þenche
Ah nauer seoþþen Arþur þider bæh þa burh seoþþe no iþæh
no nauere ne mæi bitwene þis and Domesdæi
Summe bokes suggeþ to iwisse þat þa burh wes biwucched
and þæt is wel isene soþ þat hit sunde
I þære burh weoren twa munstres swiþe mære
þat an munstre wes of Seint Aaron þerinne wes muchel halidom
þat oþer of þan martir Seint Iuliæn þe heh is mid Drihten 
þer weoren nunnen wel idon moni heh iboren wifmon
Þe biscopstole wes at Seint Aaron per wes moni sel mon
canunes þer weoren þe cuþ weoren widen
þer wes moni god clarc þe wel cuþe a leore
muchel heo ferden mid þan crafte to lokien in þan leofte
to lokien i þan steorren nehȝe and feorren
þe craft is ihate Astronomie
Wel ofte heo þan kinge seide of feole þinge
heo cudden him on leoden what him sculde ilimpen
Swulc wes þe burh of Karliun þer wes muchel ricchedom
þer wes muchel blisse mid bisie þan kinge
Þe king nom his sonde and sende ȝeond his londe
hæhte cumen eorles hehte cumen beornes
hehte cumen kinges and æc hereþringes
hehte cumen biscoppes hehte cumen cnihtes
hahte alle þa freomen þa euere weoren an londe
bi heore life hehte heom beon a Whitesunedæi at Kærleon
Cnihtes gunnen riden vnimete whiden
riden touward Kairliun of feole cunne londen
To þan Whitesunedæie þer com þe king Angel
king of Scotlonde mid sceone his folke
moni wes þe faire mon þe folȝede þan kingen
Of Mureiue king Vrien and his fæire sune Ywæin
Stater king of Suþ Wales and Cadwaþlan king of Norþ Wales
Cador eorl of Cornwale þa þe king luuede
Moruiþ of Glouchæstre Maurin of Winchastre
Gurguint eorl of Herford and Beof eorl of Oxeuord
Gursal þe balde from Baþe þer com ride
Vrgent of Chastre Ionatus of Dorchestre
Ærnald of Salesburi and Kinmarc of Cantuareburi
Balien of Silechæstre Wigein of Leirchæstre
Argal eorl of Warwic mid folk swiþe sellic
Dunwale Apries sune and Kegein Elauþes sune
Kineus þer wes Coittes sune and Cradoc Catelles sune
Ædlein Cledaukes sune Grimarc Kinmarkes sune
Run Margoitt and Netan Clofard Kincar and Aikan 
Kerin Neton and Peredur Madoc Traher and Elidur
Þis weoren Arþures aþele eorles
and þa haxte þeines ohte of alle þissere þeode
wiþuten þan beornen of Arþures borden
þa na man ne mihte ikennen ne al þat folc inemnen
Þa weoren ærchebiscopes þreo inne þissere þeode
inne Lunden and in Eouuerwic and inne Karliun Seint Dubric
he wes swiþe hali mon þurh alle þinge wel idon
To Lundene læi þe ærchebiscopstol þe to Cantwareburi wes seoþþe idon
seoþþe Engliscemen þis lond heom iwunnen
To tellen þat folc of Kairliun ne mihte hit na mon idon
Þer wes Gillomar þe king Irisce monnen deorling
Maluerus king of Islonde Doldanet king of Gutlonde
King Kailin of Frislonde Æscil king of Denelonde
Þer wes Loþ þe kene þe king wes bi Norþe
and Gonwæis Orcaneie king utlaȝen deorling
Þider com þe wilde þe eorl of Builuine
Læȝer wes ihaten and his leoden mid him
of Flandres þe eorl Howeldin of Chærtres þe eorl Cherin
Þeos ferede mid him al þat Frensce moncun
twalf eorles swiþe ræihe þe rixleden ouer France
Guitart eorl of Peiters Kæi þe eorl of Angers
Beduwear eorl of Normandie þat lond hehte þa Neustrie
of þe Mans com þe eorl Borel of Brutaine þe eorl Howel
Howel eorl wes freo mon and faire weoren his iwede
and al þat folc Frensce bihongen weoren feire
iwepned wel alle and hors ho hafden uatte
Þer weoren bisides fiftene biscopes
Nes na cniht ne na swein ne oht mon þat weore þein
from þa porz of Spaine to þan tune of Alemaine
þat þider icomen nere ȝif he iboden weore
al for Arþures æie aþeles cunnes
Þa al þis hired wes icumen ælc king mid his folke
þer me mihte bihalde þe þer bihalues weore 
moni seolcuþne mon þe isiȝen wes to burhȝen
and feole cunne tiþende mid Arþure þan kinge
Þer wes moni sellic claþ þer wes moni cniht wraþ
þer weoren herberȝe hæhliche awurþe
þer þa innes weoren mid strengþe biwunnen
þer weoren on uelden moni þusend telden
þer com spic and water and aten vnimete
ne mai hit na mon suggen on his tale of þan win and of þan ale
þer com hey þer com gras þer com al þat god was
Þa al þis folc isomned was at sele þan kingge
þa com þe Whitesunedæi alse Drihten hine sende
þa comen þa biscopes alle biuoren heore kinge
and þa ærchebiscopes þreo biuoren Arþure
and þene kinehelm nome þa him wes icunde
and setten uppen his hafde mid heȝere blisse
swa heo hine gunnen lede al mid Godes rede
Seint Dubris eoden biuoren he wes Criste icoren
þe ærchebiscop of Lundene eode an his riht honden
and bi his luft side þe ilke of Eouerwike
Fiftene biscopes biuoren of feole londen icoren
heo weoren bihangen alle mid palle swiþe balde
þe weoren alle ibrusted mid barninge golde
Þer feouwer kinges eoden biuoren þan kaiseren
heo weȝeden on heore honde feouwer sweord of golde
Þus hehte þa an þe wes a swiþe duhti mon
þat wes Cador þe king Arþures deorling
þe oþer of Scotlonde sweord he weide an honde
 and þe king of Norþ Walles and þe king of Suþ Wales
and þus heo gunnen leden þe king to chirechen
þeo biscopes gunnen singe biuoren þan leodkinge
bemen þer bleowen bellen þer ringeden
cnihtes gunnen riden wifmen forþ gliden
To iwissen hit is isaid and soþ hit is ifunden
þat no isah no mon nauer ær mid eorþliche monne her
half swa hahne ricchedom a nauer nane hepen
swa mid Arþure was aþeles cunnes
Into chirchen bicom Arþur þe riche mon 
Dubriz þe archebiscop Drihten him wes ful god
of Rome he wes legat and of þan hirede prelat
he song þa hali masse biuoren þan leodkinge
Comen mid þere quene wifmen wel idone
þere richchere monne wif alle þe wunede on londe
and þere hehere monnen dohtere þa quene hafden isohte
al swa þa quene hafde ihate bi hire fulle wite
I þere chireche i þere suþ halue sat Arþur þe king himseolf
bi pere norþ side Wenhæiuer þa quene
Þer comen hire biforen feouwer quenen icoren
ælc bar on luft honde enne beh of rede gold
 and þreo snauwhite culueren setten an heore sculderen
þæt weoren þa feouwer quenen þere cnihte wifen
þa beren an heore heonden þe feouwer sweordes of golde
biuoren Arþure aþelest kingen
Moni mæide child wes þere mid mære þere quene
þær wes moni pal hende on faire þan uolke
of monies cunnes londe þer wes muchel onde
for ælc wende to beon betere þene oþer
Feole cnihtes anan comen to þere chirechen
summe for guþinge summe for þan kinge
summe to bihalden þa wifmen þat weoren balde
Songes þer weoren murie þa ilaste swiþe longe
ich weone ȝif hit weore ilast seoue ȝere
þa ȝet heo weolden mare þe þerat weoren
Þa þe masse wes isungen of chircchen heo þrunge
þe king mid his folke to his mete uerde
mid mucle his duȝeþe drem wes on hirede
Þa quene an oþer halue hire hereberwe isohte
heo hafde of wifmonne wunder ane monien
Þa þe king wes isete mid his monnen to his mete
to þan kinge com þæ biscop Seind Dubriz þe wes swa god
and nom of his hafde his kinehælm hæhne
for þan mucle golde þe king hine beren nalde
 and dude enne lasse crune on þas kinges hafde
and seoþþen he gon do a þere quene al swo
Inne Troie þis wes laȝe bi heore ælderne daȝe 
þa Bruttes of come þe weoren wel idone
alle þa wepmen at heore mete seten
sundi bi heomseoluen þat heom þuhte wel idon
and al swa þa wifmen heore iwune hafden
Þa þe king wes isete mid alle his duȝeþe to his mete
eorles and beornes at borde þas kinges
þe stiward com steppen pe Kæy wes ihaten
hæxt cniht on londe vnder þan kinge
of alle þan hæpe of Arþures hirede
Kay hehte him biuoren moni hæh mon icoren
þer weoren a þusend cnihtes bald wunder wel italde
þat þeineden þan kingen and his hereþringen
ælc cniht hafde pal on and mid golde bigon
and alle heore uingeres iriuen mid gold ringes
Þas beorn þa sunde from kuchene to þan kinge
An oþer half wes Beduer þas kinges hæȝe birle
mid him weoren eorlene sunen of aþele cunne iboren
and þere hehȝe cnihtene sunen þa þider weoren icumen
seouen kingene sunen þat mid him quehten
Bedeuer auormest eode mid guldene bolle
after him a þusend þrasten to hirede
mid alle þas cunnes drenche þe me cuþe on biþenche
And þa quene an hire ende wifmen swiþe hende
a þusend hire eode biuoren riche men and wel icoren
to þæinen þere quene and þai þat mid hire weoren
Nes he næuere iboren of nane cnihte icoren
ilæred no læwed a nauere nare leode
þe cuþe him itelle an æies cunnes spelle
of halue þan richedome þe wes inne Kairliune
of seoluere and of golde and gode iweden
of hehȝe iborene monnen þa inne hirede wuneden
of horsen and of hafueken of hunden to deoren
and of riche iweden þa a þan hirede weoren
 and of alle þan folke þe wuneden þer on folde
wes þisses londes folk leodene hendest itald
 and al swa þa wimmen wunliche on heowen
and hahlukest iscrudde and alre bezst itoȝene
For heo hafden on iqueþen alle bi heore quike liue 
þat heo wolden of ane heowen heore claþes habben
Sum hafde whit sum hafden ræd sum hafde god grene æc
and alches cunnes fah claþ heom wes wunder ane laþ
 and elche untuhtle heo talden vnwurþe
Þa hafde Ænglene ard þat alre bezste hereword
and þis leodisce uolc æc leofuest þan kinge
Þa wifmen hehȝe iborene þa wuneden a þissen londe
hafden iqueþen alle on heore quides soþe
þat nan lauerd taken nolde inne þissere leode
næuer nænne cniht neore he noht swa wel idiht
bute he icostned weoren þrie inne compe
 and his ohtscipen icudde and ifonded hine seolue
baldeliche he mitte þenne ȝirnen him brude
For þere ilke tuhtle cnihtes weoren ohte
þa wifmen wel idone and þa betere biwitene
þa weoren i Brutene blissen inoȝe
Þa þe king iȝeten hafde and al his monweorede
þa buȝen of burhȝe þeines swiþe balde
alle þa kinges and heore hereþringes
alle þa biscopes and alle þa clærckes
alle þa eorles and alle þa beornes
alle þa þeines alle þa sweines
feire iscrudde helde ȝeond felde
Summe heo gunnen ærnen summe heo gunnen urnen
summe heo gunnen lepen summe heo gunnen sceoten
summe heo wræstleden and wiþergome makeden
summe heo on uelde pleouweden vnder scelde
summe heo driuen balles wide ȝeond þa feldes
Monianes kunnes gomen þer heo gunnen driuen
 and whaswa mihte iwinne wurþsciþe of his gomene
hine me ladde mid songe atforen þan leodkinge
and þe king for his gomene ȝæf him ȝeuen gode
Alle þa quene þe icumen weoren þere
and alle þa lafdies leoneden ȝeond walles
to bihalden þa duȝeþen and þat folc plæie
Þis ilæste þreo dæȝes swulc gomes and swulc plæȝes
Þa a þan ueorþe dæie þe king gon to spekene
and aȝæf his gode cnihten al heore rihten
he ȝef seoluer he ȝæf gold he ȝef hors he ȝef lond
castles and claþes eke his monnen he iquemde 
þer wes moni bald Brut biuoren Arþure
Nu comen to þan kinge neouwe tidinde
Arþur þe balde king sat at ane borde
biuoren him seten kinges and feole hereþringes
biscopes and clærekes and swiþe ohte cnihtes
Þer comen into halle spelles seolcuþe
þer comen twalf þeines ohte mid palle biþehte
hæȝe herekempen hehȝe men on wepne
ælc hafde on heonde grætne ring of golde
and mid æne bende of golde ælc hafde his hæfd biuonge
Æuer tweie and tweie tuhte tosomne
ælc mid his honde heold his iuere
and gliden ouer ulore biuoren Arþure
swa longe þat heo comen biuoren Arþure þan leodkinge
Heo grætten Arþur anan mid aþelen heore worden
Hal seo þu Arþur king Bruttene deorling
and hal seo þi duȝeþe and al þi drihtliche uolc
We sunden twælf cnihtes icumen her forþrihtes
riche and wel idone we sundeþ of Rome
Hider we sunden icumene from ure kaisere
Luces is ihaten þe waldoþ Romeleoden
he hahte us hider wende to Arþure þan kinge
and þe hat græten mid his grim worden
 and sæiþ þat he awundred is wunder ane swiþe
whar þu þat mod nime a þisse middenerde
þat þu derst of Rome wiþsuggen æi dome
oþer hebben up þin eȝen aȝein ure ældren
and wha hit þe durre ræden þat þu swa reh ært iwurþen
þat þu þrattien darst domes walden
Luces þene kaisere hexst of quicke monnen
Þu haldest al þi kinelond a þire aȝere hond
and nult noht þene kaisere of londe ihere
of þan ilke londe þe Iulius hafde an honde
þa inne iuurn daȝæn biwon hit mid fehten
and þu hit hauest atholde a þire anwolde
mid balden þine cnihten binimest us ure irihten
Ah sæi us Arþur sone and word send to Rome
we sculleþ bere þin ærde to Luces ure kaisere
ȝif þu wult icnawen þat he is king ouer þe 
and þu his mon bicumen wulle and hine for lauerd icnawen
and don riht þan kaisere of Frolle þan kinge
þat þu mid woȝe at Paris asloȝe
 and nu haldest al his lond mid unrihte a þire hond
Ȝif þu i þissen twælf wiken temest to þan rihten
and þu wult of Rome þolien æi dome
þenne miht þu libben imong þine leoden
And ȝif þu swa nult don þu scalt wursen vnderfon
þe kaisere wule her cumen swa king scal to his aȝen
king swiþe kene and nimen þe mid strengþe
ibunden þe lede biuoren Romleoden
þenne most þu þolien þat þu ærst forhoȝedest
Æfne þisse worden Bruttes buȝen from borden
þer wes Arþures hird hehliche awraþþed
and muchene aþ sworen uppen mære ure Drihten
þat alle heo dede weoren þa þeos arunde beden
mid horsen al todraȝene dæþ heo sculden þolie
Þer heo buȝen to Bruttes swiþe wraþe
luken heom bi uaxe and laiden heom to grunde
þer weoren men Romanisce reouliche atoȝene
ȝif Arþur ne leope to swulc hit a liun weore
and þas word seide wisest alre Brutten
Bilæueþ bilaueþ swiþe þas cnihtes on liue
ne sceollen heo on mine hirede nenne harm þolien
heo beoþ hider iriden ut of Romleoden
swa heore lauerd heom hehte Luces is ihaten
Ælc mon mot liþen þer his lauerd hine hateþ gan
nah na man demen erendesmon to dæþen
bute he weoren swa ufele biwiten þet he weore lauerdswike
Ah sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle
and ich me biræde wulle of swulchere neode
wulc word heo scullen aȝen beren to Luces þan kaiseren
Þa seten adun alle þa duȝeþe on heore benche
and þa luding alæid biuoren þan leodkinge
Þa stod Arþur him up aþelest kingen
and he cleopede him to seouen sune kinges
eorles and beornes and þa þe weoren baldest
and alle þa wiseste men þa wuneden a þen folke 
wenden into ane huse þe wes biclused faste
an ald stanene weorc stiþe men hit wurhten
þer men gunnen rune his redȝeuen wise
wulc andswere he ȝiuen wolde Luces þan kaisere
Þa iboȝen weoren alle beornes to benche
þa wes hit al stille þat wuneden inne halle
þer wes vnimete æie mid mære þan kinge
ne durste þer na man speken leste þe king hit wolde awreken
Þa stod þer up Cador þe eorl swiþe riche ær
and þas word sæide bifore þan riche kinge
Ich þonkie mine Drihte þat scop þes dæies lihte
þisses dæies ibiden þa to hirede is iboȝen
and þissere tidinge þe icumen is to ure kinge
þat we ne þuruen na mare aswunden liggen here
For idelnesse is luþer on ælchere þeode
for idelnesse makeþ mon his monscipe leose
ydelnesse makeþ cnihte forleosen his irihte
idelnesse græiþeþ feole uuele craften
idelnesse makeþ leosen feole þusend monnen
þurh eþeliche dede lute men wel spedeþ
For ȝare we habbeoþ stille ileien ure wurþscipe is þa lasse
ah nu ic þonkie Drihtne þæ scop þas daȝes lihte
þat Romanisce leoden sunden swa ræie
 and heore beot makieþ to cumen ure burhȝes
ure king binden and to Rome hine bringen
Ah ȝif hit is soþ þat men saiþ alse segges hit telleþ
þat Romanisce leoden sunden swa ræȝe
and sunden swa balde and swa balufulle
þat heo wulleþ nu liþen into ure londen
we heom scullen ȝarekien ȝeomere spelles
heore ræhscipe scal heomseoluen to reouþe iwurþen
For nauere ne lufede ich longe griþ inne mine londe
for þurh griþe we beoþ ibunden and wel neh al aswunden
Þat iherde Walwain þe wes Arþures mæi
and wraþþede hine wiþ Cador swiþe þa þas word kende
and þus andswærede Walwain þe sele
Cador þu ært a riche mon þine ræddes ne beoþ noht idon
for god is griþ and god is friþ þe freoliche þer haldeþ wiþ 
and Godd sulf hit makede þurh his Goddcunde
for griþ makeþ godne mon gode workes wurchen
for alle monnen biþ þa bet þat lond biþ þa murgre
Þa iherde Arþur þat flit of þissen eorlen
and þus spac þe riche wiþ raȝen his folke
Sitte adun swiþe mine cnihte alle
and ælc bi his lifen luste mine worden
Al hit wes stille þat wunede inne halle
Þa spak þe king balde to riche his folke
Mine eorles mine beornes balde mine þeines
mine duhti men mine freond deoren
þurh eou ich habbe biwunnen vnder þere sunnen
þat ich æm swiþe riche mon reh wiþ mine feonden
gold ich habbe and gærsume gumenen ich æm ælder
no biwan ich hit noht ane ah dude we alle clæne
To moni feohte ich habbe eou ilad and æuere ȝet weoren wel irad
swa þat feole kinelondes stondeþ a mine honde
ȝe beoþ gode cnihtes ohte men and wihte
þat ich habbe iuonded i wel feole londen
Þa ȝet him spac Arþur aþelest kingen
Nu ȝe habbeoþ iherd hæȝe mine þeines
what Romanisce men redeþ heom bitwenen
and wulc word heo sendeþ us here into ure londe
mid write and mid worde wiþ grætere wræþþe
Nu we mote biþenchen hu we ure þeoden
and ure muchele wurþscipe mid rihte maȝen biwiteȝen
wiþ þis riche moncun wiþ þas Romeleoden
and andsware heom senden mid aþelen ure worden
mid mucle wisdome vre writ senden to Rome
 and iwiten at þan kæisere for whan he us ofcunnen
for whan he us mid þrætte and mid hokere igræteþ
Swiþe sære me gromeþ and vnimete me scomeþ
þat he atwit us ure luren þat we ifeorn habbeoþ forloren
Heo suggeþ þat Iulius Cesar hit biwon mid compe i fehten
Mid strengþe and mid fehte me deþ feole vnrihte
for Cesar isohte Bruttene mid baldere strengþe
no mihte Bruttes wiþ him heore lond werien
ah mid strenþe heo eoden an hond and bitahten him al heore lond 
and þerafter sone alle his men bicome
Sum ure cun heo hadden islaȝen and sum mid horsen todraȝen
summe heo ladde ibunden ut of þissen londen
and þis lond biwunne mid unrihte and mid sunnen
 and nu axeþ mid icunde gauel of þissen londe
Al swa we maȝen don ȝef we hit don wulleþ
þurh rihte icunde of Beline kinge
and of Brennen his broþer þan duc of Burgunne
Þeos weoren ure ældre þa we beoþ of icumene
þeos bilæie Rome and þa riche al biwunnen
 and biuoren Rome þere stronge heore ȝisles anhenge
and seoþþen heo nomen al þat lond and setten hit an heore aȝere hond
and þus we mid rihte ahten Rome us biriden
Nu ich wulle leten Belin and Brenne bilæuen
and speken of þan kaisere Costantin þan stronge
he wes Helene sune al of Brutten icume
he biwon Rome and þa riche awelde
Lete we nu of Costantin þe Rome iwon al to him
and speken of Maximiæn þat was a swiþe strong mon
he wes king of Brutene he biwon France
Maximien þe stronge Rome he nom an honde
and Alemaine he biwon eke mid wunder muchele strengþe
and al from Romayne into Normandie
And þeos weoren mine ælderen mine aþþele uoregenglen
and ahten alle þa leoden þa into Rome leien
and þurh swuche dome ich ahte to biȝeten Rome
Heo ȝirneþ me an honde gauel of mine londe
al swa ic wille of Rome ȝif ich ræd habbe
Ich wilnie a mine þonke to walden al Rome
and he wilneþ me in Brutene to binde swiþe uaste
and slæn mine Bruttes mid his balureses
Ah ȝif hit on mi Drihten þe scop dæiȝes and nihtten
he scal his balde ibeot sære abuggen
 and his Romleoden þerfore scullen reosen
