and ic wulle ræh beon þer he nu rixleþ on
Wunieþ nu stille alle ic wulle suggen mine iwille
ne scal hit na man oþer idon ah hit scal stonden þeron 
He wilneþ al and ich wilni al þæt wit beiene aȝæþ
habben hit nu and aȝe þe hit æþ mæȝen iwinne
for nu we scullen cunne wham hit Godd unne
Þus spac þe balde þe Brutene hafde an onwalde
þat wes Arþur þe king Bruttene deorling
Setten his kempen and his quides lusten
summe heo sæten stille mucle ane stunde
summe heo muche runen ræhten heom bitweonen
summe hit þuhte heom god summe hit mengden heore mod
Þa heo hafden longe ilustned þan kinge
þa spac Howel þe hende hah mon of Brutene
and his quides ræhte biuoren raien þan kinge
Lauerd king hercne me alse ich ær dude þe
Þu hafest isæid word soþe selehþe þe beoþ ȝifþe
Hit wes ȝare iqueþen þat we nu sculleþ cuþen
i þan iuurn ȝere þat nu is ifunden here
Sibeli hit sæide hire quides weoren soþe
and sette hit on bocke uolke to bisne
þat þreo kinges sculden buȝen ut of Brutlonde
þa biwinnen sculden Rome and al þa riche
and alle þa londes þe þerto liggeþ
Þe uorme wes Belin þat wes a Brittisc king
þe oþer wes Costantin þe king wes on Brutene
þu scalt beon þe þridde þe Rome scal habben
And ȝif þu wult biginnen þu hit scalt biwinnen
and ich wulle þerto helpe mid haȝere strenþe
ich wulle ouer sæ sende to selen mine þeinen
to balden mine Brutten þa bet we scullen fusen
Ich wulle haten alle þa aþele of Bruttainne
bi leomen and bi heore liue ȝeond alle mine londe
þat heo beon ȝarewe sone mid þe uaren to Rome
Mi lond ich wulle sette to wedde for seoluere
and alle þe æhten of mine londe for seoluere and for golde
and swa we scullen uaren to Rome and slan Luces þene kaisere
 and bitellen þine irihten I þe lede ten þusend cnihtes
Þus Howel spilede hext of Brutaine
Þa þe Howel iseid hafde þat him sel þuhte
þa spæc Angel þe king Scotlondes deorling
and stod uppen ane boncke and beien his broþeren 
þat was Lot and Vrien tweie swiþe aþele men
Þus Angel þe king seide to Arþure þan kene
Læuerd Arþur ich sugge þe þurh soþe quides mine
þat ilke þat Howel hafeþ ispeken ne scal hit na man awreken
ah we hit scullen ilæsten bi ure quicke liuen
And lauerd Arþur þe hæhȝe lust me ane stunde
cleope þe to ræde þine eorles riche
and alle þa hæxte þa beoþ in þine hirede
 and bide heom þe suggen mid soþen heore worden
whæt heo þe wulleþ fulste þine iuan to fordonne
Ich þe leden wulle cnihtes of mire leode
þreo þusend kempen ohte alle icorene
ten þusend men auote to uehte swiþe gode
and fare we to Rome and iwinnen þa riche
Ful swiþe us mæi scomien and ful swiþe us mai gromien
þat heo sculle senden sonden after gauele to ure londe
Ah swa us helpe Drihte þæ scop þas daȝes lihte
heo hit scullen abugge mid heore bare liue
For þenne we habbeoþ Rome and alle þa riche
we scullen nimen þa londes þa þerto liggeþ
Peoile and Alemaine Lumbardie and Brutaine
France and Normandie þa hit hæhte Neustrie
and swa we sculleþ meþegie heore mod vnimete
Þa þe king isaid hafde þa andswarede alle
Iniþered wurþe þe ilke mon þe þerto nule helpen
mid ahten and mid wepnen and mid alle his imihten
Þa wes Arþures hired sturneliche awraþþed
cnihtes anburste weoren þat alle heo gunnen biuien
Þa Arþur iherd hafde his hired iberen
þa cleopien agon þe king wes abolȝen
Sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle
and ich eou wulle telle what ich don wulle
Mine writen ich wulle maken þa wel beon idihte
and sende þan kæisere modes sorȝe and muchel kare
and ich wulle ful sone faren into Rome
Nulle ich þider na gauel bringe ah þane kaiser ich wulle binden
and seoþþen ich wullen hine anhon and al þat lond ich wulle uordon 
and foruaren þa cnihtes alle þe aȝein me stondeþ i fehte
Arþur his writ nom an honden mid wiþerfulle worden
and þan beornen hit bitahte þæ þa ærnde hafde ibrohte
and seoþþe he lette heom scruden mid ælchere pruden
mid þan hæxte scrude þa he hafde on bure
and hehte heom faren sone to Luces of Rome
and he cumen after wolde swa raþe swa he mihte
Þas twælfe heore wai ferden touward heore londen
mid seolure and mid golde
cnihtes swa iscrudde no þurh al swa wel idihte
þus Arþur heom dihte al for heore worde
Þas twalf cnihtes foren þat heo to Rome comen
heo gretten heore kaisere heore kinelauerd
Hail seo þu Luces þu art hæxt ouer us
We woren at þan raȝe at Arþure þan kinge
we habbeoþ writen ibroht þe word swiþe grate
Arþur is þe kenneste mon þat we æuere lokeden on
and he is wunder riche and his þeines beoþ balde
þer is æuerælc swein swulc he cniht weore
þer is æuerælc swein swulc he weore riche þein
þer beoþ þa cnihtes swulc hit weoren kinges
mete þer is vnimete and men swiþe balde
and þa ueieȝereste wifmen þa wunieþ on liuen
and himseolf Arþur þe balde uæiȝerest ouer alle
Bi us he sende word þe þat he wule to þisse londe
na gauel he nule bringen ah þe seoluen he wule binden
and seoþþ he wule þe anhon and þis lond al fordon
and Alemaine Lunbardie Burguine France and Normandie
Frolle he sloh is iua swa he wulle us alle do
and ahnien him ane þa we aȝen alle clane
Herto he wule leden kinges eorles and hereþringes
And her we habbeoþ an honden writen þat he sende
þe þe quiddieþ what he wule don þenne he cumeþ hider on
Þa þæ ærnde wes iseid þæ kaisere wes ful særi mon
 and astured weoren Romweren alle mid sterclichere wræþþe
Ofte heo eoden to ræde ofte heo heolden rune
ær heom mihte iwurþen waht heo don wolde 
Noþeles a þan ende enne ræd heo ifunden
þat was þurh þa senaturs þa þet sinaþ heolden
þan kaisere heo radden þat he write runen
and sende his sonde ȝeond feole kinelonde
and hehte heom cume sone alle to Rome
of euerælche londe þe heom oht lufeden
and alle þa wulleþ mid fehte biȝiten lond oþer ahte
Folc þer com sone to þere burh of Rome
swa muchel swa þer neuere ærer na mon no isumnede
Heo seiden þat heo wolden ouer Munt Giu iwenden
and wiþ Arþure fehten wharswa heo hine ifunden
and Arþur slæn oþer anhon and his hired al fordon
and ahnien þan kaisere Arþures riche
Þe æreste king þe þer com he wes swiþe kene mon
Epistrod king of Grece Ethion duc of Boece
per com mid mucle wiȝe Irtac king of Turckie
Pandras king of Egipte of Crete þe king Ipolitte
of Syrie þe king Euander of Frigie þe duc Teucer
of Babilone Mæptisas of Spaine þe kaisere Meodras
of Medie þe king Boccus of Libie þe king Sexstorius
of Bittunie Pollidices of Iturie þe king Sexes
Ofustesar king of Aufrike nes þer na king his ilike
mid him com moni Aufrican of Ethiope he brohte þa bleomen
Þa seolue Romleoden liþen heom tosomne
þat weoren at nexte of Rome þa hexte
Marces Lucas and Catel Cocta Gaius and Metel
þis weoren þa sixe þe þat senaht al biwusten
Þa þis folc isomned wes of feole cunne londes
þa sette þe kaisere arimen al þæne here
Þa weoren þer riht italde to fihte swiþe balde
feouwer hundred þusende cnihtes a þan hæpe
mid wepnen and mid horsen swa bihoueþ to cnihten
Nes he neuere iboren i nauere nane burȝe
þat mihte þat folc tellen þat þer eoden auoten
Auormest heruestes dæie uorþ heo gunnen sturien
auer riht þene wæi þet touward Munt Giu lai
Lete we nu ane while þeos ferde bilæue
and speke we of Arþure aþelest kinge 
þa þe he bisoht hafde his þeines sele
and ælc wes ham iuare þer he lond hafde
And raþe aȝæin comen cnihtes to hireden
mid wepnen wel idihten þurh allen heore mihte
of Scotlond of Irlond of Gutlond of Islond
of Noreine of Denene of Orcaneie of Maneie
of þan ilke londen beoþ an hundred þusende
iwepnede þeines ohte on heore londes wise
Neoren hit noht cnihtes no þes wæies idihte
ah hit weoren men þa kenlukeste þa æi mon ikende
mid mucle wiaxen mid longe saxen
Of Normandie of Angou of Brutaine of Peitou
of Flandres of Bulunne of Loherne of Luueine
comen an hundred þusende to þas kinges hirede
cnihtes mid þan bezsten þurhcostned mid wepnen
Þer comen þa twalf iueren þa France sculden heren
twelf þusend cnihtes heo brohten forþrihtes
and of þissen londe Arþur nom an honde
fifti þusend cnihtes kene and ohte men to fihte
Howel of Brutaine cnihtes mid þan bezste
ten þusend ladde of his leodfolke
Of ganninde monnen þa heo forþ wenden
þurh nane cunnes spelle ne cuþe heom na mon telle
Arþur þa hehte aþelest kinge
to ane isette time þat folc isomnien
bi heore bare lifen at Barbefleote
 and þer he wolde gædere sele his þede
Þis lond he bitahte ane selcuþe cnihte
he wes Walwainnes broþer næs þer nan oþer
Moddred wes ihaten forcuþest monnen
treouþe nefde he nane to nauer nane monne
he wes Arþures mæi of aþelen his cunne
ah cniht he wes wunder god and he hafde swiþe muchel mod
Arþures suster sune to þere quene wes his iwune
þat wæs ufele idon his æme he dude swikedom
Ah al hit wes stille in hirede and in halle
for na man hit ne wende þat hit sculde iwurþe 
ah men to soþe iwenden for Walwain wes his broþer
þe alre treoweste gume þe tuhte to þan hirede
þurh Walwain wes Modræd monnen þa leouere
and Arþur þe kene ful wel him iquemde
He nom al his kinelond and sette hit Moddræd an hond
and Wenhauer his quene wurþlukest wiuen
þa þe in þissere leode wunede an londe
Arþur bitahte al þat he ahte
Moddrade and þere quene þat heom was iqueme
Þat was ufele idon þat heo iboren weoren
þis lond heo forradden mid ræuþen uniuoȝen
and a þan ænden heomseoluen þe Wurse gon iscenden
þat heo þer forleoseden lif and heore saulen
and æuer seoþþe laþen in auerælche londe
þat nauer na man nalde sel bede beoden for heore saule
for þan swikedome þat he dude Arþure his æme
Al þat Arþur ahte he Moddrede bitahte
lond and his leoden and leofen his quene
and seþþen he nom his ferde of folken swiþe hende
and ferde ful sone touward Suþhamtune
Þer comen seilien sone ȝeond þa sæ wide
scipes uniuoȝe to þas kinges folke
þe king þat folc beide ȝeond þa scipen longe
bi þusend and bi þusend to þan scipen þrasten
þe uader weop a þene sune suster a þene broþer
moder a þa dohter þa þa duȝeþe sturede
Weder stod on wille wind wex an honde
ankeres heo up droȝen drem wes on uolken
Wunden into widen sæ þeines wunder bliþe
scipen þer forþ þrungen gleomen þer sungen
seiles þer tuhten rapes þer rehtten
wederen alre selest and þa sæ sweuede
For þere softnesse Arþur gon to slæpen
Alse þe king slepte a sweuen him imette
feorlic wes þat sweouen þene king hit auerde
þa þe king him awoc swiþe he wes idræcched
and granen agon ludere stefenen
Næs þer nan swa þriste cniht under Criste 
þat durste þene king fræine of his farecoste
ær þe king himseolf speke and spilede wiþ his beornen þere
and þus Arþur him seide þa he awoc of slæpe
Lauerd Drihten Crist domes waldende
midelarde mund monnen froure
þurh þine aþmode wil walden ænglen
let þu mi sweuen to selþen iturnen
Þa spac Angel þe king Scottene deorling
Lauerd sæi us þi sweuen seleȝehþe us beo ȝeueþe
Bluþeliche quaþ þe king to blisse hit iwurþe
Þer ich lai a sweuete agan ich forto slepe
me þuhte þat in þere weolcne com an wunderlic deor
æst in þan leofte ladlic an sehte
wiþ leite mid storme sturnliche wende
nis in nare leode nan swa ladlic beore
Þa com þer westene winden mid þan weolcnen
a berninge drake burhȝes he suelde
mid his feure he lihte al þis londriche
me þuhte a mire sihȝeþe þat þa sæ gon to berne
of leite and of fure þa þe drake ferede
Þes drake and beore beien tosomne
radliche sone togadere heo come
heo smiten heom togaderen mid feondliche ræsen
floȝen of heore hæȝene swulc furburondes
Ofte wes þe drake buuen and eft seoþþen bineoþen
neoþeles a þan ænde heȝen he gon wende
and he flah dunrihte mid feondliche ræsen
and þene beore he ismat þat he to þere eorþe iwhat
and he þer þene beore ofsloh and hine limmele todroh
Þa þat feht wes ido þe drake aȝen wende
Þis sweuen me imette þer ich lai and slapte
Biscopes þis iherden and bocilærede men
þis iheorden eorles þis iherden beornes
ælc bi his witte wisdom sæiden
þis sweuen aræhten
Ne durste þer na cniht to ufele ræcchen na wiht
leoste he sculden leosen his leomen þat weoren him deore 
Forþ heo gunnen liþen an eouste bilife
wind heom stod on wille selest alre wedere
heo hæfden al þat heom wes neod to londen heo comen at Barbefleot
To Barbefleot at Costentin þer com muchel moncun in
of alle þan londe þa Arþur hafde an honde
Swa sone swa heo mihten ut of scipe heom rehten
þe king his folc hehte herberwe isechen
an badien þe king wolde þat his folc come
Nes he þere buten ane niht þa com him to an hende cniht
he talde tidinge Arþure þan kinge
he seide þat þer wes icumen a scaþe liþe
of westward Spaine wel dreori feond
and inne Brutaine bisi wes to harme
bi þere sæside þet lond he weste wide
nu hit hatte Munt Seint Michel þat lond ewelde iwidel
Lauerd king queþ þe cniht to soþe ich þe cuþe herriht
he hafueþ inome þine maȝe mid hahliche strenþe
heȝe wimmon iboren Howeles dohter icoren
Eleine wes ihaten aþelest maidenen
To þan munte he heo uerede aþelest maidene
nu fulle feowertene niht þe feond heo hafueþ ihalden þerriht
nute we on liue þeh he heo nabbe to wife
Alle he makeþ him to mete þa men þa he igripeþ
ruþeren hors and þa scep gæt and þa swin eke
al þis lond he wule forfare buten þu afeollen ure kare
lond and þas leode a þe is ure neode
Ȝet þe cniht seide to þan uolckinge
Isihst þu lauerd þe munt and þene wude muchele
þer wuneþ þe scaþe inne þa scendeþ þas leode
We habbeþ wiþ him iuohten wel feole siþen
bi sæ and bi londe þes leoden he amærde
ure scipen he aseingde þat folc he al adrente
þeo þat feuhten a þan londe þeo he adun leide
we habbeoþ idriuen þat swa longe þat we hine læteþ ane
faren heu swa he wule after iwille him
þis londcnihtes ne durren wiþ him mare na fehten
Arþur þis iherde aþelest alre kinge 
he cleopede him to þene eorl Kæi þe wes his stiward and his mæi
Beduer eke to him he cleopede he wes þes kinges birle
He hæhte heom forþriht beon al war to midderniht
mid alle heore wepne to wenden wiþ þan kinge
þat na mon under Criste of heore uare nuste
buten Arþur þe king and þa tweien cnihtes mid him
and heore sweines sixe ohte men and wihte
and þe cniht þe radde hit þan king heom ladde
To þere midnihte þa men weoren aslepe
Arþur forþ him wende aþelest alre kinge
Biforen rad heore londcniht þat hit was dæiliht
heo lihten of heore steden and rihten heore iweden
Þa iseȝen heo nawiht feorren a muchel fur smokien
uppen ane hulle mid sæulode biuallen
and anoþer hul þer wes swiþe heh þæ sæ hine bifledde ful neh
þeruuenon heo iseȝen a fur þat wes muchel and swiþe stor
Þæ cnihtes þa tweoneden to whaþere heo faren mihten
þet þe eotend war neore of þeos kinges fore
Þa nom him to rede Arþur þe ræȝe
þat heo sculden somed faren aneosten þan ane furen
and ȝif hine þer funden aquellen hine to deþen
Forþ þe king wende þat he com aneuste
noht he þer ne funde bute a muchel fur þer berninde
Arþur eode abute and his cnihtes bi his siden
na whit heo ne funden quikes uppen wolden
buten þat fur muchele and ban vnimete
bi atlinge heom þuhte þritti uoþere
Arþur þa nuste nenne red godne
 and bigon him to spekene to Beduer his eorle
Beduer far biliue adun of þissen hulle
and wend þe ouer þat water deope mid allen þine iwede
and mid wisdome wend to þan fure
and bihalues þe iga and bihald ȝeorne
ȝif þu miht afinden oht of þan feonden
And ȝif þu hine miht ofȝiten on aiȝes cunnes wisen
wend adun stille þat cume to þan watere
 and seien me þer sone what þu iseȝen habbe
and ȝif hit ilimpeþ swa þat þu liþen to þan fure 
 and þe feond þe ofȝite and þu to fuse
hafe mine godne horn þe al mid golde is ibon
and blawe hine mid maine swa mon scal for neode
and fus þe to þan feonde and bigin to fihten
 and we þe scullen fusen to swa we hit swiþest maȝen don
And ȝif þu hine ifindest aneouste þan fure
and þu al unaȝeten aȝein miht iwende
þenne forbeode ich þe bi þine bare life
þat þu nauere wiþ þene scucke feht no biginne
Beduer iherde what his lauerd him seide
his wepnen he on him dude and forþ him iwende
and up astæh þene munt þe is unimete
He bar an his honde ænne gære swiþe stronge
ænne sceld an his rugge irust al mid golde
hælm an his hafde hehne of stele
his bodi wes bifeong mid fæire are burne
he hafde bi his side enne brond al of stele
and forþ he gon steppen stiþ imainede eorl
þat he com fusen an neouste þan furen
and he under ane treo gon him atstonden
Þa iherde he wepen wunder ane swiþen
wepen and weinen and wanliche iberen
Þa þe cniht wende þat hit þe eotend weoren
and he anbursten agon swulc weore a wilde bar
and forȝæt sone þat his lauerd him sæide
His sceld he bræid on breoste his spere he igrap faste
and an neoste gon fuse touward þan fure
he wende to finden þene feond sturne
þat he fehten mihte and fondien hine seolue
Þa fond he þer ane quene quecchen mid hafde
heorlockede wif weop for hire weisiþ
wanede hire siþes þat heo wæs on liues
þat set bi þan fure mid reolichen ibere
 and sæt and biheold æuere ænne burinæsse
and hire ȝeddes sæide ȝeomere stefne
Wale Eleine wale deore maide 
wale þat ich þe uedde þat ich þe uostredde
wale þat þæ waldscaþe here þe haueþ þus foruare
wale þat ich wes iboren mine leomen he haueþ tobroken
Þa bisæh þat wif abuten whar þe eotend come buȝen
biseh a þene eorl Beduer þa icumen wes þer
Þa sæide þat wif here þer heo sæt bi fure
Whæt ært þu fære whit eært þu angel eært cniht
beoþ þine feþerheomen ihaneked mid golden
Ȝif þu ært of heuene þu miht isund faren heonene
and ȝif þu ært eorþlic cniht ærm þu iwurþest forþriht
For nu anan cumeþ þe scaþe þe alle þine leomen wule todraȝen
þeh þu weore stel al he þe awalt iwildel
He uerde to Brutaine to aþelest alre bolde
to Howeles castle hæh mon inne Brutene
þa ȝaten alle he tobrac and binnen he gon wende
He nom þare halle wah and helden hine to grunde
þæs bures dure he warp adun þat heo tobarst a uiuen
he funde i þan buren fæirest alre bruden
Eleinen wes ihaten aþelest kunnen
Howeles dohter hæh mon of Brutene
Arþures maȝe of swiþe heȝe cunne
Ich wes hire uostermoder and feire heo uostredde
Þer þe eotend unc ifeng forþ mid himseoluen
fiftene mile
into þisse wilde wude hider to þissen ilke stude
þus he us diste todæi a seouen nihte
Sone swa he hider com swa he þat maide inom
he wolde monradene habben wiþ þan maidene
Ælde næfde heo na mare buten fihtene ȝere
ne mihte þat maiden his mone iþolien
anan swa he lai hire mide hire lif heo losede sone
 and her he heo biburede burden alre hendest
Eleine min aȝen uoster Howelles dohter
Þa he hafde þis idon swa me seoluen inom
a uolden he me laiden and lai mid me seoluen
nu hafeþ he mine ban alle ladliche abrokene
mine leomen al toleþed mi lif me is alaþed
Nu ich habbe þe itald hu we beoþ her ihæd
flih nu swiþe lest he þe ifinde
for ȝif he cumeþ abolȝen mid his baluræsen 
nes he neuere iboren þe maȝen stonden þe biuoren
Efne þissen worden þa þat wif seide
Beduer heo gon hirten mid hendeliche worden
Leofe moder ich æm mon and cniht æm wel idon
and ich þe wule suggen þurh soþe mine worden
næs nan kempen iboren of nauer nare burden
þat mon ne mæi mid strenþe stupen hine to grunde
 and hire þe ane alde wifmon swiþe lutle beoþ þine mæhten
Ah hafuen nu swiþe godne dæi and ich wulle faren minne wæi
Adun him ferde Beduer to his duȝeþekinge
and talde him hu he hafde kare and hu he hafde al ifare
and what þat wif alde of þan maidene him talde
and hu þe eotend ælche dæi bi þan alde wiue lai
Þer heo heom bitwenen heolden heore runen
hu heo mihten taken on þat þe scucke weore fordon
Þeo while com þe eotende faren and fusden to his fure
he bar uppen his rugge burþene grete
þat weore twælf swine iteied tosomne
mid wiþen swiþe grete, ywriþen al togadere
Adun he warp þa dede swin and himseolf sæt þerbi
his fur he beten agon and muchele treowen læiden on
þa six swin he todroh and euere he to þan wiue loh
 and sone umbe while he lai bi þan wife
ah he nuste noht þan tidende þat comen to his wifeþinge
He droh ut his gleden his flæsce he gon breden
and þa six swin he gon æten alle ær he arise of selde
al biwaled on axen wanliche weoren þa sonden
and seoþþen he gon ræmien and raxlede swiþe
 and adun lai bi þan fure and his leomen strahte
Lete we nu þene eotend bilafuen and atlien to þan kinge
Arþur at þan watere his wapnen nom an honde
 and þe eorl Beduer god cniht wis and war
and þe þridde wes Kæi þes kinges stiward and his mæi
Ouer þan watere heo comen iwepned mid þan bezsten
 and stiȝen up þan hulle mid allen heore maine
þat heo comen fusen aneuste þan furen 
þer þe eotende lai and slæp and þa quene sæt and weop
Arþur hine teh bisiden his iferen
forbad heom bi heore leomen and bi heore bare liuen
þat nan neoren swa kene þat heom neh comen
buten he iseȝen þat hit ned weoren
Beduer atstod him þere and Kæi his iuere
Arþur gon stepe vorþ stiþimoded kempe
þat he com to þan ulette þer þe feond lai and slæpte
Æuere wes Arþur ærhþe bideled
þet wes sutel þeron sellic þah hit þunche
for Arþur mihte þere þene eotende al tohæuwe
slan þene scucke þer he lai and slapte
Þa nolde Arþur on slepen na wiht hine areppen
leste he an uferre daȝe upbræid iherde
Þa cleopede Arþur anan aþelest kingen
Aris aris feondscaþe to þine fæiesiþe
nu wit scullen delen þene dæd of mire maȝen
Ær þe king hæfde þæs ful isæide
þe eotend up asturte and igrap his mucle clubbe
and wende mid þan dunten Arþur al todriuen
ah Arþur bræid heȝe his sceld buuen his hælme
and þe eotend smat þeranouenan þat al he gon toscenen
And Arþur him swende to an hiȝende mid his sweorde
and þen chin him ofswipte mid alle þan cheuele
and sturte him biaften ane treo þe þer stod aneouste
and þe eotend smat after biliue and noht hine ne hutte
ah he þat treo smat þat al his clubbe todraf
And Arþur aneouste þat treo bieorn abute
and swa Arþur and þe scucke biurnen hit þreie abuten
Þa wes þe eotend heui swiþe and Arþur wes swiftre
 and oftoc þene eotend and up ahof his gode brond
and þat þih him ofsmat and eotend adun wæt
And Arþur atstod and biheold þa gon to spekene þe ueond
Lauerd lauerd ȝef me griþ wha is þat me fihteþ wiþ
Ne wende ich þat na man a þissere weorlderichen
me mihte þus lehtliche aleggen mid fehte
bute hit Arþur weore aþelest alre Brutte 
and neoþeles næs ich nauere of Arþure afæred sære
Þa him sæide Arþur aþelest kingen
Ich æm Arþur þe king Bruttene deorling
Tel me of þine cunne and whar beo heore beonste
and wha þe weore on uolde fader oþer moder ihalde
and of wulche londe þu art iliþen hidere
and whi þu mine maȝe aualled hafuest mid morþe
Þa andswarede þe feond þer he læi and biheold
Al þis ich wulle don and þine treoþe underfon
wiþ þat þu me lete liuien and mine leomen hælen
Arþur hine iwræþþede wunder ane swiþe
and he Beduer cleopede balde his kempe
Ga aneouste Beduer and hefd him binim her
 and fere hit forþ mid þe adun of þisse munte
Beduer aneouste com and his hæfued him binom
 and swa heo þeonene ferden adun to heore iferen
Þa sat þe king adun and hine gon to resten
and þas word seide Arþur þe sele
No uæht ich nauere ueht non uppen þissere uolden
buten þa ich sloh þene king Riun uppen þan munte of Rauinite
Seoþþen heo uorþ wenden and to þere uerde comen
þa þe þat hafd iseȝe sellic heom þuhte
whar weore under heuene swulc hafed ikenned
Howel of Brutaine beh to þan kinge
and þe king him seide al of þan maidene
Þa wes Howel sari and sorhful an heorte forþi
and nom al his feren and ferde to þan munte
þer þat Brutisce maide bibured læi on eorþe
He lette þer areren sone ane chireche swiþe faire
a Seinte Marie nomen Drihtenes moder
 and seoþþen he ȝæf nome þan hulle ær he þonne wende
and hehte hine Æleine Tunbel nu hit hæhte Munt Seint Myhhel
Þa wes Arþures hired sellich isomned
of Irlonde and of Scotlonde þider weoren iscriþene
Þa lette þe king blauwen bemen an hireden
 and wenden of Brutaine bisie men and kene
þurhut Normandie þæ hehte þa Neustrie 
heo uerden þurhut France and folc heom after ferde
heo buȝen ut of France into Burguine
His hauwæres þer comen and heolden his iferen
 and cudde þan kinge þer i þare cuþþe
þat Luces þe kaisere and al his Romanisce here
þiderward heo comen fromward heore þeoden
 and swa heo wolden fusen in touwward France
and al þat biwinnen and seoþþen wenden hidere
 and Bruttes alle aquellen quicke þer heo heom funde
and Arþur þene kene ibunde lede to Rome
Þa wes abolȝen baldest alre kingen
and hehte a þan feldes slen alle his teldes
and þer he wikien wolde þat he þat soþe wuste
whær he minte þene kæisere iwisliche kepen
Þat water hehte Albe þer lai þe king balde
An wis cniht þer com ride to þas kinges uerde
þe wes al forwunded and his folc afelled swiþe
hafden Romanisce men al his lond biræiued him
He talde þan kinge neouwe tiþende
whar lai þe kaisere and al his Romanisce here
 and whær he hine mihte iwinde ȝif he hine wolde wiþ him fihten
oþer griþ makien wiþ Romanisce monnen
Ah lauerd Arþur quaþ þe cniht ich þe wulle cuþen herriht
þat betere þe is freondscipe to habben þene for to fihten
for aȝan þine tweie heo habbeoþ twælue
swa feole kinges swa feole heredringes
Nis he in nare kuþþe þe hit þe maȝe icuþþe
for alle þan uolke þe uulieþ þan kinge
wiþuten þan Romleoden of his aȝere þeoden
and wiþute þan uolke þe ȝirneþ þas kinges are
Þa þe talen weoren alle italde and Arþur heo hafden understonde
þa cleopede þe king forþrihtes his deoreste cnihtes
 and radden heom bitwenen enne castel to areren
onuast þan wateren þe Albe wes ihaten
On ane swiþe feiere stude itimbred he wes ful sone
þer feng moni hond to an hiȝende he wes ido
for ȝif Arþur misferde þenne he come to fihte
oþer his uolc ueolle oþer setten to fleonne 
þenne þohte he to atstonden at þan castle stronge
Þa cleopede he eorles tweie aþele men and wise
heȝe men icunned þan kinge swiþe deore
þæ an wes of Chartres and hehte Gerin muchel wisdom wunede mid him
þe oþer hehte Beof of Oxeneuord welle wide sprong þas eorles word
Þe ȝet þe king cleopede Walwæin þe wes his deoreste mæi
for Walwain cuþe Romanisc Walwain cuþe Bruttisc
he wes iued inne Rome wel feole wintre
Þe king nom þas þreo cnihtes hende and to þan kaisere heom sende
and hehte hine mid his ferde faren aȝæin to Rome
 and þat he næuere into France his ferde no ladde
And ȝif þu þider wendest and þine ferde ledest
þu scalt beon underuonge to þine uæiesiþe
For France is min aȝen and ich heo mid fehte biwon
and ȝif þu nult bilauen þat þider nult liþen
fare wit to uihte and falle þe uorcuþere
and lete we þat folc wræcche wunien an ære
While Romleoden iwunnen þa þeoden
and seoþþen heo þa þeoden mid fehte forloseden
and ich heo mid feohte biwon and mid fehte wule halden
Forþ þa cnihtes wenden godliche kempen
þat weoren Gerin and Beof þe hende and Walwain þe balde
iburned and ihelmed an hæȝen heore steden
and ælc weiede an sculdre sceld swiþe godne
heo beren on heore honde gares swiþe stronge
Forþ heo gunnen ride riche men from hirede
muchel of þere duȝeþe þe mid Arþure wunede
mid Walwaine eoden and æþmodliche hine beden
þat he wiþ Romleode summe sake arerde
þat we maȝen mid fehte fondien us seolue
for hit is feole ȝere þat heore þrættes comen here
and heore beot makieþ þat heo us wulle bihafdi
Nu is hit muchel leodscome ȝif hit scal þus aligge
bute þer sum sake beo ær we iwurþe sæhte
scaftes tobrokene brunies totorne
sceldes toscened scalkes toheouwen
sweordes ibaþede i blode þan rede 
Forþ þa eorles wenden þurh æne wude muchelen
and mærcoden enne wæi þe ouer anne munte læi
þat heo bicomen sone to þan uolke of Rome
wurþliche iwepned wunden an horsen
Þer me mihte bihalden þe mon þe bihalues weore
moni þusenden þrasten ut of telden
al to bihalden þeos þreo cnihtes balde
and biheolden heore steden and biheolden heore iweden
 and hercnede tidende from Arþure þan kinge
and aneouste forþrihtes fræinede þa cnihtes
and ȝif þe king heom isend hæfde to þan kaisere
to speken þan kæisere wiþ and to ȝirnen his griþ
Ah for nauer nare speche þas þreo eorles riche
nolden abiden ær heo comen riden
forn to þas teldes deoren þerinne wes þe kaisere
Adun heo gunnen lihten and bitahten hore steden
and swa heo iwepned mid alle wenden into telde
forn to þan kaisere þe Luces wes ihate
Þer he sæt an his bedde heore ærnde heo him cudde
ælc his saȝe sæide swa him sel þuhte
 and hehten hine wenden aȝæin to his londen
þat he nauere mid unfriþe France no isohte
Þa while þa þeos eorles þreo seiden heore erende
aset þe kaisere swulc he akimed weore
and andsware nauer nan no aȝæf þissen eorlen
ah he lustnede ȝeorne luþer on his þohte
Þa anbælh Walwain swulc an iburst þein
and þas word sæide Walwain þe kene
Luces þe riche þu ært kæisere of Rome
we beoþ Arþures men aþelest Brutten
He sent þe his sonde wiþuten gretinge
he hat þe faren to Rome þa riche is þin aȝen
let hine halden France þe he biwon mid fehte
and hald þu richen and þine Romleoden
While þine aldren France ieoden
mid fehte heo þer biwunnen unimete wunnen
swa ane while heo þer liueden and seoþen heo hit leoseden 
mid fehte Arþur hit biwon and he hit wule walden
He is ure lauerd we beoþ his leodkempen
He us hæhte suggen soþ to þe seoluen
ȝif þu nult aȝen buȝen þi bone he wule iwurþen
and ȝif þu nult aȝen wenden ah iwurþien þin iwillen
and þu wult þat kinelond bitellen to þire hond
nu tomorȝen is þe dæi haue ȝif þu biȝete mæi
Þæ andswarede þe kaisere mid grættere wræþþe
Nulle ich noht aȝæin faren ah France ich wulle bitellen
mine ældren hit heolden and ich hit wulle habben
Ah ȝif he wolde bicumen mi mon and for lauerd me icnawen
 and treouliche me heren and me for hærre halden
griþien ich him wulle and his gumen alle
and lete halde Brutlond þæ Iulius hafde in his hond
 and oþere londes monie þe Iulius hafde an honde
þat he naueþ nane rihte to þæ riche þæh he walde
þa he scal alle leose buten he leoþ makie
Þa andswarede Walwain þæ wes Arþures mæi
Belin and Brenne beiȝene þa ibroþere
Brutlond heo ahten and France heo biwunnen
and seoþþen heo uerden sone and biȝeten Rome
and þer heo wuneden seoþþe wel feole ȝere
Þa þis wes al iuare þa wes Brennes kæisere
and walde Romleoden and alle þa þeoden
And Rome is ure icunde þa þu haldest an honde
and ȝif we mote libben we hit wulleþ habben
beute ȝif þu wulle icnawen beo þat Arþur is king ouer þe
and ælche ȝere him senden gæuel of þine londen
and ȝif gæst him a leoþ þu miht libben þa eþ
Þa sæt bi þan kaisere a cniht of his cunne
Quencelin ihaten hæh mon inne Rome
Þes cniht andswarede biuoren þan kaisere
 and þus him seide þe cniht was unisele
Cnihtes fareþ eou aȝæin and cuþeþ eower kinge
Bruttes beoþ bolde ac heo beoþ unwræste italde
for æuere heo ȝelp makieþ heore monscipe is luttel
Mare he þohte to suggen þa Walwain bræid to sweorden
and smat hine ufenen þat hafde þat he atweo hælde 
 and he hiȝenliche anan heolde to his horsen
and heo up leopen mid grimliche lechen
and þas word seide Walwain þe sele
Swa me helpe þe ilke lauerd þe scop þes daȝes lihte
ȝif æueræie is swa kene of eouwer moncunne
þat us after kenne ich hine wulle aquelle
he scal beo toswungen mid brade mine sweorden
Efne þare ilke tale þa cleopede þe kaisere
Haldeþ heom haldeþ alle heo sculleþ heongien
heȝe uppen treouwe oþer mid horsen beon todraȝene
Efne þissere sæȝe þa þe kaisere seide
þe eorles gunnen riden and spureden heore steden
heo scæken on heore honden speren swiþe stronge
beren biforen breosten brade heore sceldes
Aneouste gunnen ride eorles ræȝe
and æuere þæ kaisere lude gon cleopie
Nimeþ heom slæh heom iscend heo us habbeoþ
Þer me mihte ihere þe þer bihalues weore
clupien þusende of þan þeodfolke
Hider hider wepnen Wende we heom æfter
Hider ure sceldes þe scalkes atwendeþ
Sone heom after wenden iwepnede kempen
þer sixe þer seouene þer æhte þer niȝene
And æuere þa eorles arnde biliues
and æuere umbe stunde biseȝen heom bihinde
and euere þa cnihtes of Rome after biliue come
And þer com aneouste alre swiþest ærne
 and euere cleopede kenlich swiþe
Wendeþ aȝæin cnihtes and werieþ eo mid fihtes
Hit is eo muchel scome þat ȝe wulleþ atsceken
Walwain icneo þene reme of þan Romanisce men
he wende his stede and to him gon ride
 and smat hine þurh mid þan spere swa he ispited weore
 and bræid to him þat spere þe gume iwat sone
 and þæs word kende Walwain þe kene
Cniht þu ride to swiþe betere þe weore at Rome
Marcel hehte þe cniht heȝere monnen
Þa Walwain isæh þat he to grunde bæh 
sone his sweord he ut abræid smat of Marcele þat hefd
and þas word sæide Walwain þe sele
Marcel far to helle and tel heom þer spelles
and wune þer toȝere mid Quencelien þin ifere
and haldeþ þer unker rune betere inc weoren inne Rome
for þus we eou scullen techen ure Bruttisce speche
Gerin isæh hu hit ferde hu þe Romanisce lai þer dune
and his hors muneȝede and ænne oþerne imette
and smat hine þurhut mid his spere and þas word spilede
Rid nu swa Romain and reos þe to hellen
and þus we scullen grundien ȝif Godd us wule fulsten
Nis noht wurþ þratte buten þer beo dede æc
Bos isæh þe ohte mon hu his iueren hafden idon
 and his hors wende wunder ane swiþe
and mid alle his mitte teh to ane cnihte
 and smat hine buuen þan scelde þat tobarst his gode burne
 and þurhut þene sweore þe swælt ful sone
And þus þe eorl cleopien agon kenliche on his feren
Bruttes us wulleþ scenden ȝif we heonne wendeþ
bute we bet aginnen ær we heonene iwenden
Efne þere speche þe þe eorl kende
heo biwenden heom sone wunder ane swiþe
and ælc his sweord swiþe adroh and ælc his Rumain ofsloh
 and seoþþen heore hors wenden and heore wæi heolden
And þæ Romanisce men riden eouere after heom
ofte heo heom on smiten ofte heo heom atwiten
ofte heo sæiden heom to Abuggen ȝe scullen þa dede
ah ne mihten heo þurh nane þinge heore nenne adun bringe
no nenne hærm þer don heom i þan wiþerhappen
Ah æuere umbe whilen þe eorles aȝain wenden
and ær heo totwemden þe wurse wes Romleoden
Þus heo iuerden fiftene milen
þat heo comen to ane stude vnder ane ueire wude
onuast þan castle þer Arþur lei uaste
Þreo milen þerfrom to þan wuden þrungen
niȝe þusende þe Arþur þider senden
baldere Brutten þe bezst þat lond cneowen
heo wolden wite þat soþe of Walwain þan kene 
and of his iueren hu heo iuaren weoren
whaþer heo liue weoren þa heo bi wæie læien
Þæs cnihtes siȝen þurh þene wude wunder ane softe
uppen ane hullen and ȝeorne biheolden
Heo letten alle þa horsmen i þan wude alihten
and rihten heore iwepnen and alle heore iweden
buten an hundred monnen þe þer sculden bihalden
ȝif heo onȝiten mihten þurh æies cunnes þingen
Þa iseȝen heo feorren in ane uelde muchelen
þreo cnihtes ærnen mid allen heore mainen
After þan þreom cnihten þritti þer comen
after þan þrittie heo iseȝen þreo þusende
þerafter comen þrasten þritti þusen anan
Romanisce leoden mid ræue bihonged
And þa eorles biuoren heom aneuste atarnden
euere þene rihte wæi þe touward þan wude lai
þer heore iueren wel ihudde weoren
Þa eorles ærden to þan wuden þa Romanisce after riden
þa Bruttes toræsden on heore iræste steden
and smiten to auorenon and feollen an hundred anan
Þa wenden Romleoden þat Arþur come riden
and weoren afered feondliche swiþe and Bruttes after heom
and sloȝen of þan folke fiften hundred
Þa com heom to fulste of heore aȝe uolke
þa Arþur þider hafde isend sixtene þusund
baldere Brutten mid burnen bihonged
Þa com þer ride þat wes an eorl riche
Petreius ihate heh of Rome
mid six þusend kempen þan Romanisce to helpen
 and mid muchelere strengþe leopen to þan Brutten
and lut þerof nomen ah monie heo ofsloȝen
Bruttes to wude hælden þe oþere after wenden
and þa Bruttes auoten uaste aȝæin stoden
and þa Romanisce men fuhten ridende
and Bruttes heom to heolden and heore hors sloȝen
 and moni þer nomen and in þene wude droȝen 
Þa iwarþ Petreius wraþ þat his wes þa wurse þer
and he mid his uerde from þan wude wende
and Bruttes heom to buȝen and biæften heom sloȝen
Þa Bruttes weoren ut of wude iȝein to þan felde
þa atstoden Romleoden mid ræȝe strenȝe
Þa bigon þat muchele fiht þer ueollen eorlles and moni god cniht
þer ueollen a dæi fiften þusend
aþelere monnen ær hit weore æfen
Þer he finden mihte þe his main wolde fondien
hond aȝan honde strongne aȝein stronge
sceld aȝein scelde scalkes þer ueollen
Vrnen þa streten mid blodestræmen
leien ȝeond þan ueldes goldfaȝe sceldes
al þene dæi longe heo heolden þat feht stronge
Petreius an his halue his folc heold tosomne
þa iwræþ sone þat Bruttes hafden þat wurse
Þat isæh þe eorl heȝe of Oxeneuorde
Beof wæs ihæten hæh Bruttisc mon
þat a nare wisen ne mihte hit iwurþen
þat Bruttes ne mosten reosen buten heo ræd haueden
Þa eorl þa cleopede cnihtes aþele
of þan alre bezsten of alle þan Brutten
and of þan kennesten þe þer quike weoren
and tuhte hine ut a þan felde aneouste þere ferde
and þus him iseide an heorte him wes unneþe
Cnihtes hercnieþ nu to me Drihten us helpe
we beoþ hidere icumen and þis feht habbeoþ undernumen
buten Arþures rede þe is ure hexte
ȝif us oht ilimpeþ we him þa bet likieþ
and ȝif us ilimpeþ uuelen he us wule hatien
Ah ȝif ȝe wulleþ minne ræd þenne ride we al glad
We beoþ þreo hundred cnihtes ihelmede þeines 
ohte men and kene aþele iborene
Cuþeþ eouwer cnihtscipe we beoþ of are cuþþe
Rideþ þenne ich ride and fulieþ mine rede
Alle haldeþ him to to þan cnihte þa ich do
ne nime ȝe nenne stede no nanes cnihtes iwede
ah æuerælc god cniht slæn æuere adunriht
Æfne þan worde þe þe cniht sæide of Oxeneuorde
to his iueren bisiden þe gon he to riden
æfne al swa swiþe swa hund þene heort driueþ
and his iueren after mid allen heore mahten
þurhut þene muchele uehte al þa cnihtweorede
fluen an heore steden uolc heo þere aqualden
Wo wæs heom iboren þa i þan weie heom weoren biuoren
for alle heo hit totreden mid horsen and mid steden
and swa aneouste heo iwenden and Petreium iuengen
Beof him biarnde and mid ærmen biclupte
 and bræid hine of his stede and to eorþe hine istræhte
he wuste him bihalues balde his cnihte
Bruttes adun sloȝen Petreius heo droȝen
and þa Romleoden ræhliche fuhten
and a þan laste ne mihte mon wite wha oþerne smite
þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes on compe
Þa isæh Walwain þer he wes bihaluen
mid seouen hundred cnihten þider he gon hælden
in his wæiȝe þat he funde al he hit aqualde
and ridende igrap Petreiun on richen his steden
and ladde uorþ Petreiun læþ þeh hit weore him
þat heo to þan wude comen þer heo wel wusten
sikerliche to halden þene riche mon of Rome
and æft ut a þene ueld wenden and bigonnen to fehten
Þer me iseon mihte sorȝen inoȝe
sceldes scenen scalkes fallen
halmes tohælden hæhȝe men toswelten
blodie ueldes falewede nebbes
Bruttes heom toræsden þa fluȝen Romleoden
Bruttes heom sloȝen and monie heo quic nomen
and þe dæiende þæ wa wes Romleoden þa
Þa bond men uaste kempen Romanisce
and lædden heom to þan wude biuoren Walwaine 
heom biwakeden a þere nihte twenti hundred cnihten
Þa hit dai wes amarȝen duȝeþe gon sturie
forþ heo gunnen liþe to heore kinelauerde
and swulc lac him brohte þat leof him wes to habben
Þa spac Arþur him þus Wulcume Petreius
Nu ic þe wulle teche Bruttisce spæche
Þu ȝulpe biforen þan kaisere þat þu me woldest aquellen
Nimen mine castles alle and mine kineriche
and muchel þe sæl iwurþen of þat þu wilnedest to habben
Ich wulle bitachen þe ful iwis minne castel inne Paris
and þer þu scalt wunien swa þe beoþ alre leoþest
ne scalt þu nauere mare þi lif þenne lede
Arþur þa cnihtes nom þe þer iuongen weoren
þreo hundred rideres he nom eke anan
þe alle weoren iueren
cnihtes swiþe ohte and kene men to uihte
and hæhte heom amorȝen monliche arisen
binden Romanisce men mid stronge raketehȝen
and lede Petreius to þere borh of Paris
Feouwer eorles he hæhte forþ heom ibringen
Cador Borel Beduer and Richer
he hehte heom beon iueren þat heo siker weoren
and cumen aȝain sone to heore kinelauerde
Þis wes al þus ispeken ah hit wes sone underȝeten
Hæwæres foren ȝeond þas kinges ferden
 and iherden suggen soþere worden
wuder Arþur wolde senden þæ cnihtes þe he hafde i benden
and þa hauweres forþrihte wenden uorþ bi nihte
þat heo comen sone to þan kaisere of Rome
and talden al heore tale hu þas feouwer eorles sculden uare
and forþ lede Petreius to þære burh of Paris
and al heo talden þene wæi þe intowardes Parise læi
and whar me heom kepen mihte in ane slade deopen
and biraiuien of heom Petreiun þene riche mon
 and þa feouwer eorles ileggen and fasten heom binden
Luces þis iherden þe kaiser of Rome 
and he leopt to wepne swulc hit a liun weore
and ten þusend hehte kempen iþoȝene
to horse and to wepnen aneouste foren wenden
He cleopede Sextorius of Libie he wes king of Turkie dux
he sende after Euander þe of Babiloine wes icumen þer
he cleopede to þan senaturs Bal Catel Carrius
þeos weoren alle kineborne and þeos weoren alle icoren
aneouste to riden and Petreium aredden
Anan swa hit was euen forþ heo iwenden
heom ladden twelue of þan leodfolke
þa swiþe warre weoren and þa weiȝes cuþen
Þa riden Romleoden riseden burnen
quahten on hafden helmes heȝen
seldes on rugge ræȝe Romleoden
Heo ferden alle nihte neodliche swiþe
þet heo comen in þe wai þa into Parise lei
þa weoren heo biuoren and Bruttes biaften
Ah wale þat hit nuste Cador þe kene
þat þa Romleoden heom forriden hafueden
Heo comen in ænne wude on ænne swiþe faire stude
in ane dale deope diȝelen bihælues
sweoren heom bitwænen þat þer heo wolden kepen
Þer heo leien stille ane lutle stunde
 and hit agon daiȝen and deor gunnen waȝeȝen
Þa comen Arþures men quecchen after streten
riht þene ilke wæi þer þe oþer uerde læi
heo riden singinge segges weoren bliþe
Neoþeles Cador wes þer swiþe wis and swiþe war
he and Borel þe eorl riche buȝen heom togæderes
 and nomen heom bitweonen fif hundred cnihtes
and biuoren wenden iwepnede kempen
Richer and Beduer wenden heom bafte þer
and þa cnihtes fereden þa heo iuongen hafden
Petreium and his iueren þa iwunne weoren
Þa heo comen riden uppen Romleoden
 and Romleoden ræsden to mid ræȝere strengþen
and smiten a þan Brutten mid swiþe bitere duntes 
breken Bruttene trume balu wes on folke
þe wude brastlien gon beornes þer feollen
Bruttes heom wiþstoden and stærcliche heom weoreden
Þat iherde Richer and þe eorl Beduer
hu heore iueren heom biuoren fuhten
Petreiun heo nomen and heore inume allen
and mid þreo hundred sweinen into wude senden
And heomseolue fusden toward heore ifæren
and smiten a Romleoden mid raȝere strengþen
þer wes moni dunt iȝeuen and moni mon þer wes islaȝen
Þa underȝæt Euander þe heþene king wes swiþe war
þat heore uolc gon waxen and Bruttes gunnen wonien
and buȝen heom tosomne his cnihtes seleste
and uuenon þan Brutten swulc heo heom wolden abiten
Bruttes wokeden þa and heore wes þat wurse
heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo neh comen
Wa wes Brutten þere buten Arþure
heore helþ wes to lutel þere at heȝere neode
Þer wes Borel ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
Euander king hine aqualde mid luþere his crafte
and þreo Bruttes eke heȝe men iborene
Þer islaȝen weoren þreo hundred of heore iueren
and monie quike nomen and narwe heom ibunden
þa nusten heo godne ræd nanne for alle heo wenden beon dede
neoþeles heo fuhten swa ohtliche swa heo mahte
Þa wes ut ifaren from Arþures ferden
þæ king of Peytouwe har mon iblowen
Guitard he hehte Gascunne he ahte
he hæfde to iueren fif hundred rideren
þreo hundred scuhten kene men to uehten
and seouen hundred auoten þa fuse weoren to harmen
Heo weoren ifaren into þan londe fodder to biwinnen
æiþer uodder and mete to læden to heore ferde
Þa luden heo iherden of þan Romleoden
heore deden heo bilafden and þiderward gunnen liþen
stiþimodede men and swifte slauþe bidæled
þat heo comen sone anneouste þan fehte 
Guitard and his cnihtes þerriht forþrihtes
igrippen heore sceldes swiþe balde cnihtes
and alle þa scutten scuuen heom bisides
and þa men auoten to gunnen fusen
and alle somed smiten on mid smarten heore dunten
At þan uorme smællen Romaniscen veollen
fiftene hundred folden to grunden
þer wes islæȝen Euander þe king wes ful sturne ær
Catellus of Rome forȝæt his domes þære
Þæ astalden þer flem þat ær staþel heolden
þa rugges towenden and fluȝen Romleoden
Bruttes heom after buȝen and mid baluwe heom igrætten
and swa monie heo þer nomen and swa monie heo þer sloȝen
þat no mihte Bruttene uerde biueolen namare
And þa Romanisce men þe þer atfaren mihten
atarnede ful sone to þan kaisere
and talden him tidende of Arþure þan kinge
for heo wenden to soþe þat Arþur þider comen
þer wes auared swiþe þe kaisere and his ferde
þe Bruttes islaȝen hafden þat heom sel þuhten
aȝeinward heo buȝen þa mid baldere biȝete
and to þan stude wenden aȝæin þer þat feht hafde ibeon
and bureden þa deden and þa quike gunnen forþ leden
And senden after Petreiun þæ heo ær nomen
 and after his iueren þæ ær inumen weoren
and senden heom alle fuliwis into þære burȝe of Paris
and þreo castles fulden and faste heom biclusden
after Arþures heste aþelest kingen
Alle Brutleoden luueden Arþuren
alle heom stod him æie to þat wuneden a þan ærde
swa dude þan kaisere of Ærþure he hafde muchele kare
and alle Romleoden of Arþure weoren afærde
Þa wæs mid soþe ifunde þat Mærlin sæide whilen
þat sculden for Arþure Rome ifullen afure
and þa wal of stanen quakien and fallen
Þas ilke tacninge sculde beon of Luces þan kæiseren 
 and of þan senature þa mid him come of Rome
and of þan seoluen wisen þæ þer gunnen resen
þat Merlin i furndaȝen seide al heo hit funden þere
swa heo duden ære and seoþþen wel iwhare
ær Arþur iboren weore Merlin al hit bodede
Þe kaisere iherde suggen soþere worden
hu his men weoren inumen and hu his folc æc ofslaȝen
Þa weoren inne his ferde feolevalde sorȝe
summe mænden heore freond summe þrætteden heore ueond
summe bonneden wepnen balu heom wes ȝeueþe
Þa iseh Luces þat luþere him ilimped wæs
for ælche dæi he losede of his leodfolke
ah he herm iuredde his heȝe men he losede
He iwærþ afered þa wunder ane swiþe
and nom him to ræde and to somrune
þat he wolde to Æust mid alle his iuerde
forþ bi Lengres he wolde uare of Arþure he hafde muchele kare
Arþur hafde his hauwares an hirede þas kaiseres
and sone duden him to witen whuder he wolde wenden
Arþur lette sone somnien his ferde
stilleliche bi nihte his cnihtes seleste
and forþ þe king wende mid sele his folke
An his riht honde he lette Lengres stonde
and i þæne wæi biforen ferde þe Luces faren wolde
Þa he com in ane dale vnder ane dune
þer he gon atstonden kennest alre kingen
þat dale is mid soþe Sosie ihaten
Arþur þer adun lihte and hæhte al his duȝeþe
græþien heom to fihte swa scolden cnihtes ohte
þat whenne Romleoden þer comen riden
þat heo uengen heom on swa ohte cnihtes sculden don
Alle þa sweines and þa unwræste þeines
 and of þan smale uolke feole þusunde
þe king heom sette in ane hulle mid feole heremarken
þat he dude for ȝepscipe þerof he ȝelpen þohte
al swa hit iwarþ seoþþe þerafter ful sone 
Arþur ten þusend nom of aþelen his cnihten
sende a riht honde mid raue bihonge
he lette oþere ten þusende an his lift honde
ten þusend biuoren ten þusend biæften
mid heomseoluen heo heolden sixtene þusund
bihalues he sende into ane wude hende
seouentene þusend selere cnihten
wel iwepnede men þene wude to biwitteȝen
þat heo mihte þider uare ȝif him neod weore
Þa wes inne Gloucestre an eorl mid þan bezste
Moruiþ wes ihate mon swiþe kene
him he bitahte þene wude and þa ferde
And ȝif hit ilimpeþ swa wule þe liuiende Godd
þat heo ouercumen beon and biginnen to fleon
setteþ heom after mid allen æouwer mahten
and al þat ȝe oftake maȝen doh hit of lifdaȝen
þa uatte and þa lene þa riche and þa hene
For no beo in nauer nare leode no in none leode
cnihtes al swa sele swa beoþ mid me seolue
cnihtes al swa ræȝe cnihtes al swa riche
cnihtes al swa stronge in nauer ane londe
Ȝe beoþ under Criste cnihten alre kennest
and ich æm rihchest alre kinge vnder Gode seolue
do we wel þas dede Godd us wel spede
Cnihtes þa andswarede stilleliche under lufte
Alle we scullen wel don and alle we scullen touon
Niþing wurþe þe cniht þe ne cuþe his mahten herriht
Þa sænde heo a ba siden al þa men auoten
þa lette he sette up þene drake heremærken unimake
bitæhte hine ane kinge þe wel hine cuþe halde
Angel kinge of Scotlonde þa uormeste uerde heold an honde
Cador þe eorl of Cornwaille þa uerde heold baften
Bof hafde ane þe eorl of Oxenuorde
Þe eorl of Chæstre Gerin þa ueorþe uerde heold mid him
Þa uerden uppen þere dune heold Escil king þe Denisce
Lot heold þa ane þe leof was þan kinge
Howel of Brutaine heold ane oþere 
Walwain þe kene wes bi þan kinge
Kai wuste ane stiward wæs þas kinges
Beduer ane oþer þe wes þes kinges birle
Þe eorl of Flandres Howeldin ane uerde hefde mid him
Ane muchele uerde hefde Guitard þe king of Gascunnes ærd
Wigein eorl of Leicestre and Ionatan eorl of Dorchestre
heo wusten þa twa uerden þe þer weoren auoten
Þe eorl of Chastre Curselein and eorl of Baþe þe hehte Urgein
ho biwusten ba þa uerden þa weoren þær auoten
þeos sculden a twa haluen halden to þan uehte
to þissen twam eorlen þa ohte cnihtes weoren
hafden Arþur treouþe þe eorles weoren treowe
þa weoren alle þa uerden isette alse Arþur sel þuhte
þa cleopede him to þe king of Brutaine
his redȝiuen alle þa ræiȝest weoren to dome
 and þus seide Arþur anan to aþelen his monnen
Hercneþ nu touwardes me mine wines deore
iræsed ȝe habbeoþ tweien to Romanis monnen
and twien heo beoþ ouercumen and islaȝen and inumen
for heo al mid wronge wilneden of ure londe
and min heorte seiþ me þurh ure Drihten hehne
þat ȝet heo scullen beon ouercumen baþe islæȝen and inumen
Ȝe habbeoþ ouercumen Noreine ȝe habbeoþ ouercume Denene
Scotlond and Irlond al iwunen to eouwer heond
Normandie and France biwunnen mid fehte
Þreo and þritti kinelond ich halde a mire aȝere hond
þæ ȝe hit under sunnen habbeoþ me biwunnen
And þis beoþ þa forcuþeste men of alle quike monnen
hæþene leode Godd heo seondeþ laþe
ure Drihten heo bilæueþ and to Mahune heo tuhteþ
 and Luces þe kæisere of Godd seolf naueþ nane care
þat hafueþ to iueren haþene hundes
Goddes wiþeriwinnen we heom scullen awelden
leggen heom to grunde and us seoluen beon isunde
mid Drihtenes willen þe waldeþ alle deden
Þa andswarede eorles þare Alle we beoþ ȝarewe
to libben and to liggen mid leouen vre kingen
Þa þas ferde wes al idiht þa wes hit dailiht
Luces at Lengeres boȝede and al his Romleode 
he hehte his men blawen his guldene bemen
bonnien his ferden forþ he wolde riden
from Lengres to Auste swa læi his weie rihte
Forþ gunnen riden Romanisce leoden
þat heo ane mile comen neh Arþure
Þa iherde Romleoden ræȝe tiþenden
iseȝen alle þa dales alle þa dunes
alle þa hulles mid helmes biþahte
heȝe haremarken hæleþes heom heolden
sixti þusende þrauwen mid winde
sceldes blikien burnen scinen
palles goldfaȝe gumen swiþe sturne
steden lepen sturede þa eorþe
Þe keiser isah þæne king fare þer he was bi wudescaȝe
he Luces þa sæide þæ lauerd of Rome
 and spac wiþ his monnen ludere stefnen
What beoþ þeos utlaȝen þa þisne wei us habbeoþ foruaren
Nime we ure wepnen and heom to wenden
heo sculleþ beon islaȝene and summe quic iulaȝene
alle heo sculle beon dede mid wite fordemde
Efne þan worden heo iuengen heore wepnen
Þa heo igæred weoren mid gode heore wepnen
þa spac Luces sone þæ lauerd of Rome
Biliue we heom to alle we scullen wel do
Þer weoren icumen mid him fif and twenti kingen
heþene uolc alle þa heolden of Rome
eorles and dukes eke of æstene weorlde
Lauerdinges quæd Luces þa Mahun eou beo liþe
Ȝe beoþ kinges riche and hereþ into Rome
Rome is mi rihte rihcchest alre burȝe
and ich ah hæxst to beon of alle quike monnen
Ȝe iseoþ her on uolden þa ure ifan sunden
heo þencheþ to rixlien heȝe ouer ure riche
halden us for hænen heomseoluen riche iwurþen
Ah we heom scullen forbeoden mid baldere strengþen
for ure cun hæxst was of alle quike monnen
and alle þa lond biwinnen þa heo on lokeden
and into Brutlonde ferde Iulius þe stronge
and biwon him to hondes feole kinelondes 
Nu wolden ure underlingges beon ouer us kingges
ah heo hit scullen abuggen mid heore bare ruggen
no scullen heo nauere liþen aȝæin to Brutaine
Æfne þan worde þa sturede þa uerde
bi þusend and bi þusende heo þrunggen tosomne
ælc king of his folke ȝarkede ferde
Þa hit al was iset and ferden isemed
þa weoren þarriht italde fulle fiftene ferden
twein kinges þere æuere weoren ifere
feouwer eorles and a duc dihten heom togadere
and þe kæisere himseolf mid ten þusend kempen
Þa gon þat folc sturien þa eorþen gon to dunien
bemen þer bleowen bonneden ferden
hornes þer aqueþen mid hæhȝere stefnen
sixti þusende bleowen tosomne
Ma þer aqueþen of Arþures iueren
þene sixti þusende segges mid horne
þa wolcne gon to dunien þa eorþe gon to biuien
Tosomne heo heolden swulc heouene wolde uallen
ærst heo lette fleon to feondliche swiþe
flan al swa þicke swa þe snau adun ualleþ
stanes heo letten seoþþen sturnliche winden
seoþþen speren chrakeden sceldes brastleden
helmes tohelden heȝe men uellen
burnen tobreken blod ut ȝeoten
ueldes falewe wurþen feollen heremærken
Wondrede ȝeond þat wald iwundede cnihtes oueral
sixti hundred þar weoren totredene mid horsen
beornes þer swelten blodes aturnen
stræhten after stretes blodie stremes
balu wes on uolke þe burst wes vnimete
Swa al swa suggeþ writen þæ witeȝen idihten
þat wes þat þridde mæste uiht þe auere wes here idiht
þeo at þan laste nuste nan kempe
whæm he sculde slæn on and wham he sculde sparien
for no icneou na man oþer þere for vnimete blode 
Þa hæf þat fiht of þan studen þer heo ær fuhten
and bigunnen arumþe ræsen tosomne
and neouwe ueht bigunnen narewe iþrungen
þer weoren Romleoden reouliche iladde
Þa comen þer kinges þreo of hæþene londe
of Ethiope wes þe an þe oþer wes an Aufrican
þe þridde wes of Libie of hæþene leode
Heo comen to þere uerde a þere æst ænde
 and þene sceldtrume breken þe Bruttes þer heolden
and anan fælden fiftene hundred
baldere þeinen of Arþures þeoden
þa wenden Bruttes sone to þa rugges
Þa comen þer riden tweien eorles kene
þat was Beduer and Kæi Arþures birle and his mæi
heore Bruttes heo isehȝen mid bronden tohawen
Þer iwurþen tobursten eorles swiþe balden
mid ten þusend cnihten hælden to þan uihten
amidden þan þrunge þer heo þihkest weoren
and sloȝen Romleoden reouliche swiþen
 and ȝeond þan uehte wenden after heore iwillen
Þa weoren heo to þriste and to ufele heom biwusten
wala wa wala wa þat heo neoren war þa
þat heo ne cuþen biwiten heom wiþ heore wiþeriwinnen
for heo weoren to kene and to ærwene
and to swiþe fuhten and to ueor wenden
and spradden to wide ȝeond þat feht brade
Þa com þe king of Mede þe muchele and þe brade
heþene hereþrihng þer he hærm wrohte
he ladde to iueren twenti þusend rideren
he heold on his honde ænne gare swiþe stronge
Þene gare he uorþ strahte mid strongen his maine
and smat þene eorl Beduer forn a þan breoste
þat þa burne tobarst sone biuoren and bihinde
anopened wes his breoste þa blod com forþ luke
Þer feol Beduer anan ded uppen uolden
þer wes sarinesse sorreȝen inoȝe
Þer Kai funde Beduer ded liggen him þer 
 and Kai þat lich wolde leden mid himseolue
mid twenti hundred cnihten he hælde þer abuten
and feondliche feuhten and falden Romleoden
 and of Medie þer sloȝen moni hundred monnen
þat ueht wes strong swiþe and heo weoren þer to longe
Þa com þer liþen a swiþe ladlic king an
mid sixti þusend monnen sele of his londen
Setor þe kene þe com him from Libie
Þer þe king stronge wiþ Kæi him gon fehte
and forwundede Kai swiþe inne strongen þan fehte
to þan bare deþe reoulich wes þa dede
His cnihtes þerrihte hine ladden of þan uihte
mid muchelere strengþe þurh þat feht stræhten
Wa wes Arþure kinge for þa tidinge
Þæt iseh þe riche þein Ridwaþelan wes ihaten
Beduerres suster sune of heȝe Bruttes he wes icume
þat Boccus mid his spere stronge Bedver hafde istunge
Wa wæs him on liue þa his æm wes an deþe
for he of alle monnen mæst hine lufede
He cleopede of his cunne cnihtes swiþe gode
 and of þan alre leofeste þe he on liue wuste
fif hundred bi tale fusden tosomne
Riwaþþlan þa sæide riche mon of Bruttene
Cnihtes ȝe beoþ of mine cunne cumeþ hidere to me
and wreke we Beduer min æm þa bezst wes of ure cunne
þa Buccus hafd ofstungen mid his spere strongen
Fuse we alle tosomne and ure ifan feollen
Æfne þan worde forþ he iwende
and alle mid him anan aþele his iueren
and Buccus þene king icneowen þer he was i compen
mid his spere and mid his scelde monine king he aqualde
Riwadþlan braid ut his sweord sone and him to sweinde
and smat þane king a þene helm þat he a twa toueol
and æc þere burne hod þat hit at þe toþen atstod
and þe heþene king hælde to grunde
 and his fule saule sæh into helle
Riwærdþlan þa seide ræh he was on mode 
Boccus nu þu hafst aboht Beduer þu sloȝe
and þi saule scal toȝere beon þas wurse iuere
Æfne þan worde swulc hit þe wind weore
he þraste to þan fihte swa þode doþ on felde
þenne he þat dust heȝe aȝiueþ from þere eorþe
al swa Riwadþlan ræsde to his feonden
Al heo hit sloȝen þat heo aneh comen
þe while þe heo mihte walden heoren kinewurþe wepnen
neouren in al þan fihte cnihtes nane betere
þe while þat heom ilaste þat lif on heore breoste
Boccus þene king heo ofsloȝen and a þusend of his cnihten
Þa wes Beduer awræken wel mid þan bezsten
Þer wes an oht eorl aþeles cunnes
Leir wes ihaten lauerd of Buluine
he isæh i þan fihte enne ueond fusen
þat on admirail of Babiloine he wes ældere
muchel uolc he aualde uolde to grunde
And þe eorl þat bihædde an heorte him was unneþe
he bræid an his breoste ænne sceld bradne
and he igrap an his hond a sper þat wes swiþe strong
 and his hors muneȝeden mid alle his imaine
and þene admiral hitte mid smærten ane dunte
vnder þere breoste þat þa burne gon to berste
þat him þer bæfte þat sper þurhræhte
fulle ane ueþme þe ueond feol to grunde
Þat isah sone þeos admirale sone
Gecron is ihate and his spere grap anan
and smat Leir þene eorl sære a þa lift side
þurhut þa heorte þe eorl adun halde
Walwain þat bihedde þer he wes on uehte
and he hine iwraþede wunder ane swiþe
þat isæh Howel hæh mon of Brutten
and he þider halde mid fiftene hundred monnen
herde herekempen mid Howele fusden
and Walwain heom uuenon swiþe stiþimoded mon
he hefde to iferen fif and twenti hundred 
baldere Brutten þa bigunnen heo to fehten
Þer weoren Romleoden reouliche iledde
Howel heom kepte Walwain heom imette
þer wes wunderlic grure þa welcnen aqueþen
þa eorþe gunnen to buuien stanes þer bursten
urnen stremes of blode of ærmen þan folke
þat wel wes unimete þa weoren Bruttes werie
Kinard þe eorle of Strugul bilefde þene king Howel
 and inom mid him Labius Rimarc and Boclouius
Þis weoren þa keneste men þat æi king ahte
þeos weoren on moncunne eorles main stronge
Heo nalden for heore mucle mode fulien Howele þan gode
ah bi heomseoluen heo sloȝen alle þe heo neh come
Þat isæh a riche mon of þan Romleoden
hu Kinard þe kene heore uolc þer aqualde
and þe cniht gon him alihten of leofuen his steden
and nom him on his honde a spere imaked of stele
 and biwalede hine a blode and bihalues him eode
þat he com a þan ende þer fæht Kinard þe stronge
Kinardes burne he up ahof and he þene eorl þer ofsloh
Þa ȝeiden lude alle Romleode
and buȝen to þan Brutten and heore trume breken
 and feollen heremarken uolc adun helden
sceldes þer scenden scalkes þer feollen
þer ueollen to grunde fiftene þusende
baldere Brutten balu þer wes riue
Swa ilaste longe þat uiht swiþe stronge
Walwain gon ȝeonge ȝeond þat wæl muchele
and somnede his cnihtes alle þer he heom funde i fihte
Aneouste þer com ride Howel þe riche
heo somneden heore beire uolc anon and forþ heo gunnen fusen
and riden to Romleoden mid raȝere wraþþen
 and fastliche heom to buȝen and breken þere Freinsce trumen
And Walwain forþrihte þer he ifunde
Luces þene kaiser leouien under scelde
 and Walwain him to sweinde mid þe stelene sweorde
and þe kaisere hine þat gome wes swiþe sturne 
sceld aȝein scelden sciuren þer wunden
sweord aȝein sweorde sweinde wel ilome
fur fleh of þe stelen þa ueond weoren abolȝen
Þer wes viht swiþe strong stureden al þa ferden
þe kaisere wende Walwain to scende
þat he miht an uuere daȝe ȝelpen uor þere deden
Ah Bruttes him þrungen to þræfliche swiþe
 and þa Romanisce men arudden heore kæiseren
and heo tosomne heolde swulc heouene wolde ualle
Alle þene dailiht heo heolden seoþþen þat fiht
ane lutle stunde ær þe sunne eode to grunde
Arþur þa cleopede aþelest alre kinge
Nu we heom to alle mine cnihtes ohte
 and Godd seolf us fulste ure feond to afallene
Æfne þan worden þa bleou men þa bemen
fiftene þusend anan þraste to blauwen
hornes and bemen þa eorþe gon beouien
for þan vnimete blase for þan mucle ibeote
Romleoden wenden rug to þan feohten
feollen heremarken heȝe men swulten
fluȝen þa þe mihten þa ueie þær feollen
Muchel monslæht wes þere ne mihte hit na man tellen
hu feole hundred monnen toheouwen þer weoren
i þan mucle þrunge i þan monslæhte
Wes þe kaisere ofslæȝen a seolcuþe wisen
þat nuste hit nauer seoþen na mon to sugen
of nauer nare cuþþe wha þene kaisere qualde
Bute þa þet feht was al idon and þat folc wes al iblissed
þa funde men þene kaisere ofstungen mid ane spere
Word com to Arþure þer he wes on telde
þat þe kaisere wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
Arþur lette slæn an teld amidden ænne bradne ueld
 and þider iberen lette Luces þene kaisere
and lette hine bitillen mid goldfaȝe pallen
and biwiten hine þer lette þreo daȝes fulle
þe while he wurchen lette an werc swiþeriche 
ane cheste longe and wreon heo al mid golde
And lette leggen þerinne Luces of Rome
þat wes a swiþe duhti mon þa while his daȝes ilasten
Þa ȝet dude Arþur mære aþelest alre Brutte
Arþur asechen lette alle þa riche
kinges and eorles and þa riccheste beornes
þa i þan fehte weoren islaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen
he lette heom burien mid baldere pruten
Buten þreo kinges he beren lette Luces þan kaisere
and lette makien beren riche and swiþe maren
and lette heom sone senden to Rome
and grette Romweren alle mid græten ane huxe
and seide þat he heom sende þat gauel of his londe
and efte wold heom alswa senden heom gretinge ma
ȝif heo ȝirnen wolden of Arþures golden
and þerafter wulle sone riden into Rome
and tellen heom tiþinge of Brutlondes kinge
and Rome walles rihten þe ȝare weoren tofallen
And swa ich wulle awelden þe wode Romleoden
Al þis ȝelp wes idel ido for eoþer weis hit eode
al oþer hit itidde þe leoden he bilæfden
al þurh Modred is mæin forcuþest alle monnen
A þan muchele fihte Arþur of his cnihtes losede
fif and twenti þusend a uolden tohavwen
of Brutten swiþe balde biræued at liue
Kæi wes forwunded seore wunder a swiþe
to Kinun he wes ilad and sone þerafter he wes ded
bibured he wes þere bihalue þan castle
imong heremiten þat wæs þe riche mon
Kæi hehte þe eorl Kinun þe castel
Arþur ȝæf him þene tun and he þerto tumde
and sette þer þene nome after himseoluen
for Keises dæþe Kain he hit hehte
nu and auere mare swa hit hehte þere
Seoþþen Beþuer wes islæȝen and idon of lifdahȝen
Arþur hine beren lette to Bæios his castle
and biburied he wes þere inne þere burȝe 
wiþuten þan suþ ȝæte in eorþe me hine sette
Howeldin iulut wes forþ into Flandres
and alle his bezste cnihtes þer flutten uorþrihtes
into þan eorldomen þenne heo þer comen
and alle þa dede in eorþe me heom leide
inne Teruane heo liggeoþ alle clane
Leir þene eorl me ladde into Buluine
 and Arþur þeræfter seoþþe wunede in ane londe
inne Burguine þer him bezst þuhte
Þat lond he al biwuste and alle þe castles sette
and seide þat he wolde himseolue þat lond holde
And seoþþen he his beot makede a sumere þat he wolde
faren into Rome and ahnien al þa riche
and beon himseolf kaisere þe Luces wuneden ære
And monie of Romleoden wolden þat hit swa eoden
for heo weoren adradde to heore bare deþe
þat monie þer awæi fluȝen and heore castles bibuȝen
and monie sende sonde to Arþure þan stronge
and monie him speken wiþ and ȝirnden Arþures griþ
and summe heo wolde aȝein Arþure halden
and halden wiþ him Rome and weren þa leode
And neoþeles heo auered weoren for heore uæiesiþen
þat nusten heo under Criste nenne ræd godne
Þa wes hit itimed þere þat Merlin saide while
þat Romwalles sculden aȝein Arþure touallen
þat was agan þære bi þan kaisere
þa ueol þerinne fehte mid fifti þusund monne
ruren þer to grunde riche Romleoden
Þa Arþur wende to soþe to aȝen al Rome
 and wunede inne Burguine richest alre king
Þa com þer in are tiden an oht mon riden
and brohte tidinge Arþure þan kinge
from Moddrede his suster sune Arþure he wes wilcume
for he wende þat he brohte boden swiþe gode
Arþur lai alle longe niht and spac wiþ þene ȝeonge cniht
swa nauer nulde he him sugge soþ hu hit ferde
Þa hit wes dæi a marȝen and duȝeþe gon sturien 
Arþur þa up aras and strehte his ærmes
he aras up and adun sat swulc he weore swiþe seoc
Þa axede hine an uæir cniht Lauerd hu hauest þu iuaren toniht
Arþur þa andswarede a mode him wes uneþe
Toniht a mine slepe þer ich læi on bure
me imætte a sweuen þeruore ich ful sari æm
Me imette þat mon me hof uppen are halle
þa halle ich gon bistriden swulc ich wolde riden
alle þa lond þa ich ah alle ich þer ouer sah
and Walwain sat biuoren me mi sweord he bar an honde
þa com Moddred faren þere mid unimete uolke
he bar an his honde ane wiax stronge
he bigon to hewene hardliche swiþe
and þa postes forheou alle þa heolden up þa halle
Þer ich iseh Wenheuer eke wimmonnen leofuest me
al þere muche halle rof mid hire honden heo todroh
Þa halle gon to hælden and ich hæld to grunden
þat mi riht ærm tobrac þa seide Modred Haue þat
Adun ueol þa halle and Walwain gon to ualle
and feol a þere eorþe his ærmes brekeen beine
 and ich igrap mi sweord leofe mid mire leoft honde
and smæt of Modred is hafd þat hit wond a þene ueld
And þa quene ich al tosnaþde mid deore mine sweorede
and seoþþen ich heo adun sette in ane swarte putte
and al mi uolc riche sette to fleme
þat nuste ich under Criste whar heo bicumen weoren
Buten miseolf ich gon atstonden uppen ane wolden
 and ich þer wondrien agon wide ȝeond þan moren
þer ich isah gripes and grisliche fuȝeles
Þa com an guldene leo liþen ouer dune
deoren swiþe hende þa ure Drihten makede
Þa leo me orn foren to and iueng me bi þan midle
 and forþ hire gun ȝeongen and to þere sæ wende
And ich isæh þæ vþen i þere sæ driuen
and þe leo i þan ulode iwende wiþ me seolue
Þa wit i sæ comen þa vþen me hire binomen 
com þer an fisc liþe and fereden me to londe
þa wes ich al wet and weri of sorȝen and seoc
þa gon ich iwakien swiþe ich gon to quakien
Þa gon ich to biuien swulc ich al fur burne
And swa ich habbe al niht of mine sweuene swiþe iþoht
for ich what to iwisse agan is al mi blisse
for a to mine liue sorȝen ich mot driȝe
wale þat ich nabbe here Wenhauer mine quene
Þa andswarede þe cniht Lauerd þu hauest unriht
ne sculde me nauere sweuen mid sorȝen arecchen
þu ært þe riccheste mon þa rixleoþ on londen
and þe alre wiseste þe wuneþ under weolcne
Ȝif hit weore ilumpe swa nulle hit ure Drihte
þat Modred þire suster sune hafde þine quene inume
and al þi kineliche lond isæt an his aȝere hond
þe þu him bitahtest þa þu to Rome þohtest
and he hafde al þus ido mid his swikedome
þe ȝet þu mihtest þe awreken wurþliche mid wepnen
 and æft þi lond halden and walden þine leoden
and þine feond fallen þe þe ufel unnen
and slæn heom alle clane þet þer no bilauen nane
Arþur þa andswarede aþelest alre kinge
Longe biþ æuere þat no wene ich nauere
þat æuere Moddred mi mæi
wolde me biswiken for alle mine richen
no Wenhauer mi quene wakien on þonke
nulleþ hit biginne for nane weorldmonne
Æfne þan worde forþriht þa andswarede þe cniht
Ich sugge þe soþ leofe king for ich æm þin vnderling
þus hafeþ Modred idon þine quene he hafeþ ifon
and þi wunliche lond isæt an his aȝere hond
he is king and heo is quene of þine kume nis na wene
for no weneþ heo nauere to soþe þat þu cumen aȝain from Rome
Ich æm þin aȝen mon and iseh þisne swikedom
and ich æm icumen to þe seoluen soþ þe to suggen
Min hafued beo to wedde þat isæid ich þe habbe
soþ buten lese of leofen þire quene
 and of Modrede þire suster sune hu he hafueþ Brutlond þe binume, 
Þa sæt hit al stille in Arþures halle
þa wes þer særinæsse mid sele þan kinge
þa weoren Bruttisce men swiþe vnbalde uor þæn
Þa umbe stunde stefne þer sturede
wide me mihte iheren Brutten iberen
and gunne to tellen a feole cunne spellen
hu heo wolden fordeme Modred and þa quene
and al þat moncun fordon þe mid Modred heolden
Arþur þa cleopede hendest alre Brutte
Sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle
and ich eou telle wulle spelles vncuþe
Nu tomærȝe þenne hit dæi biþ and Drihten hine sende
forþ ich wulle buȝe in toward Bruttaine
and Moddred ich wulle slan and þa quen forberne
and alle ich wulle fordon þa biluueden þen swikedom
And her ich bileofuen wulle me leofuest monne
Howel minne leofue mæi hexst of mine cunne
and half mine uerde ich bilæfuen a þissen ærde
to halden al þis kinelond þa ich habbe a mire hond
 and þenne þas þing beoþ alle idone aȝan ich wulle to Rome
 and mi wunliche lond bitæche Walwaine mine mæie
and iuorþe mi beot seoþþe bi mine bare life
Scullen alle mine feond wæisiþ makeȝe
Þa stod him up Walwain þat wes Arþures mæi
and þas word saide þe eorl wes abolȝe
Ældrihten Godd domes waldend
al middelærdes mund whi is hit iwurþen
þat mi broþer Modred þis morþ hafueþ itimbred
Ah todæi ich atsake hine here biuoren þissere duȝeþe
and ich hine fordemen wulle mid Drihtenes wille
miseolf ich wulle hine anhon haxst alre warien
þa quene ich wulle mid Goddes laȝe al mid horsen todraȝe
For ne beo ich nauere bliþe þa wile a beoþ aliue
and þat ich habbe minne æm awræke mid þan bezste
Bruttes þa andswarede mid baldere stefne
Al ure wepnen sunden ȝarewe nu tomarȝen we scullen uaren
A marȝen þat hit dæi wes and Drihten hine senden
Arþur uorþ him wende mid aþelen his folke 
half he hit bilæfde and half hit forþ ladde
Forþ he wende þurh þat lond þat he com to Whitsond
scipen he hæfde sone monie and wel idone
ah feowertene niht fulle þere læi þa uerde
þeos wederes abiden windes bidelde
Nu was sum forcuþ kempe in Arþures ferde
anæn swa he demen iherde of Modredes deþe
he nom his swein aneouste and sende to þissen londe
and sende word Wenhaueren heou hit was iwurþen
and hu Arþur wes on uore mid muclere ferde
and hu he wolde taken on and al hu he wolde don
Þa quene com to Modred þat wæs hire leofuest monnes
and talde him tidende of Arþure þan kinge
hu he wolde taken an and al hu he wolde don
Modræd nom his sonde and sende to Sexlond
after Childriche þe king wes swiþe riche
and bæd hine cume to Brutaine þerof he bruke sculde
Modræd bad Childriche þene stronge and þene riche
wide senden sonde a feouwer half Sexlonde
and beoden þa cnihtes alle þat heo biȝeten mihte
þat heo comen sone to þissen kinedome
and he wolde Childriche ȝeouen of his riche
al biȝeonde þere Humbre for he him scolde helpe
to fihten wiþ his æme Arþuren kinge
Childrich beh sone into Brutlonde
Þa Modred hafde his ferde isomned of monnen
þa weoren þere italde sixti þusende
herekempen harde of heþene uolke
þa heo weoren icumen hidere for Arþures hærme
Modred to helpen forcuþest monnen
Þa þe uerde wes isome of ælche moncunne
þa heo weoren þer on hepe an hunddred þusende
heþene and cristene mid Modrede kinge
Arþur lai at Whitsond feouwertene niht him þuhte to long
and al Modred wuste wat Arþur þær wolde
ælche dai him comen sonde from þas kinges hirede 
Þa ilomp hit an one time muchel rein him gon rine
 and þæ wind him gon wende and stod of þan æst ende
and Arþur to scipe fusde mid alle his uerde
and hehte þat his scipmen brohten hine to Romerel
þer he þohte up wende into þissen londe
Þæ he to þere hauene com Moddred him wes auornon
ase þe dæi gon lihte heo bigunnen to fihten
alle þene longe dæi moni mon þer ded læi
summe hi fuhten a londe summe bi þan stronde
summe heo letten ut of scipen scerpe garen scriþen
Walwain biforen wende and þene wæi rumde
 and sloh þer aneuste þeines elleouene
he sloh Childriches sune þe was þer mid his fader icume
To reste eode þa sunne wæ wes þa monnen
þer wes Walwain aslæȝe and idon of lifdaȝe
þurh an eorl Sexisne særi wurþe his saule
Þa wes Arþur særi and sorhful an heorte forþi
 and þas word bodede ricchest alre Brutte
Nu ich ileosed habbe mine sweines leofe
Ich wuste bi mine sweuene whæt sorȝen me weoren ȝeueþe
islaȝen is Angel þe king þe wes min aȝen deorling
 and Walwaine mi suster sune wa is me þat ich was mon iboren
Up nu of scipen biliue mine beornes ohte
Æfne þan worde wenden to fihte
sixti þusend anon selere kempen
and breken Modredes trume and wel neh himseolue wes inome
Modred bigon to fleon and his folc after teon
fluȝen ueondliche feldes beoueden eke
ȝurren þa stanes mid þan blodstremes
Þer weore al þat fiht idon ah þat niht to raþe com
ȝif þa niht neore islaȝen hi weoren alle
Þe niht heom todelde ȝeond slades and ȝeon dunen
and Modred swa vorþ com þat he wes at Lundene
Iherden þa burhweren hu hit was il ifaren
and warnden him inȝeong and alle his folke
Modred þeone wende toward Winchastre
and heo hine underuengen mid alle his monnen
And Arþur after wende mid alle his mahte 
þat he com to Winchestre mid muchelere uerde
 and þa burh al biræd and Modred þerinne abeod
Þa Modred isæh þat Arþur him wes swa neh
ofte he hine biþohte wæt he don mahte
Þa a þere ilke niht he hehte his cnihtes alle
mid alle heore iwepnen ut of burhȝe wenden
and sæide þat he weolde mid fihte þer atstonden
He bihehte þere burȝewere auermare freo laȝe
wiþ þan þa heo him heolpen at heȝere neoden
Þa hit wes dæiliht ȝaru þa wes heore fiht
Arþur þat bihedde þe king wes abolȝe
he lette bemen blawen and beonnen men to fihten
he hehte alle his þeines and aþele his cnihte
fon somed to fihten and his ueond auallen
and þe burh alle fordon and þat burhfolc ahon
Heo togadere stopen and sturnliche fuhten
Modred þa þohte what he don mihte
 and he dude þere alse he dude elleswhare
swikedom mid þan mæste for auere he dude unwraste
he biswac his iueren biuoren Winchestren
and lette him to cleopien his leofeste cnihtes anan
and his leoueste freond alle of allen his folke
and bistal from þan fihte þe feond hine aȝe
and þat folc gode lette al þer forwurþe
Fuhten alle dæi wenden þat heore lauerd þer læi
and weore heom aneouste at muchelere neode
Þa heold he þene wai þat touward Hamtone lai
and heolde touward hauene forcuþest hæleþe
and nom alle þa scipen þa þer oht weore
and þa steormen alle to þan scipen neodde
and ferden into Cornwalen forcuþest kingen a þan daȝen
And Arþur Winchestre þa burh bilai wel faste
 and al þat moncun ofsloh þer wes sorȝen inoh
þa ȝeonge and þa alde alle he aqualde
Þa þat folc wes al ded þa burh al forswelde
þa lette he mid alle tobreken þa walles alle
Þa wes hit itimed þere þat Merlin seide while 
Ærm wurþest þu Winchæstre þæ eorþe þe scal forswalȝe
swa Merlin sæide þe witeȝe wes mære
Þa quene læi inne Eouwerwic næs heo næuere swa sarlic
þat wes Wenhauer þa quene særȝest wimmonne
Heo iherde suggen soþþere worden
hu ofte Modred flah and hu Arþur hine bibah
Wa wes hire þere while þat heo wes on life
Ut of Eouerwike bi nihte heo iwende
 and touward Karliun tuhte swa swiþe swa heo mahte
þider heo brohten bi nihte of hire cnihten tweiȝe
and me hire hafd biwefde mid ane hali rifte
and heo wes þer munechene karefullest wife
Þa nusten men of þere quene war heo bicumen weore
no feole ȝere seoþþe nuste hit mon to soþe
whaþer heo weore on deþe
þa heo hireseolf weore isunken in þe watere
Modred wes i Cornwale and somnede cnihtes feole
to Irlonde he sende aneoste his sonde
to Sexlonde he sende aneouste his sonde
to Scotlonde he sende aneouste his sonde
he hehten heom to cume alle anan þat wolde lond habben
oþer seoluer oþer gold oþer ahte oþer lond
on ælchere wisen he warnede hine seoluen
swa deþ ælc witer mon þa neode cumeþ uuenan
Arþur þat iherde wraþest kinge
þat Modred wæs i Cornwale mid muchele monweorede
 and þer wolde abiden þat Arþur come riden
Arþur sende sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde
and to cumen alle hehte þat quic wes on londe
þa to uihte oht weoren wepnen to beren
and whaswa hit forsete þat þe king hete
þe king hine wolde a folden quic al forbernen
Hit læc toward hirede folc vnimete
ridinde and ganninde swa þe rim falleþ adune 
Arþur for to Cornwale mid unimete ferde
Modred þat iherde and him toȝeines heolde
mid vnimete folke þer weore monie uæie
Uppen þere Tambre heo tuhten togadere
þe stude hatte Camelford euermare ilast þat ilke weorde
And at Camelforde wes isomned sixti þusend
 and ma þusend þerto Modred wes heore ælder
Þa þiderward gon ride Arþur þe riche
mid unimete folke uæie þah hit weore
Uppe þere Tambre heo tuhte tosomne
heuen heremarken halden togadere
luken sweord longe leiden o þe helmen
fur ut sprengen speren brastlien
sceldes gonnen scanen scaftes tobreken
þer faht al tosomne folc vnimete
Tambre wes on flode mid vnimete blode
mon i þan fihte non þer ne mihte ikenne nenne kempe
no wha dude wurse no wha bet swa þat wiþe wes imenged
for ælc sloh adunriht weore he swein weore he cniht
Þer wes Modred ofslaȝe and idon of lifdaȝe
in þan fihte
Þer weoren ofslaȝe alle þa snelle
Arþures heredmen heȝe and lowe
and þa Bruttes alle of Arþures borde
and alle his fosterlinges of feole kineriches
And Arþur forwunded mid walspere brade
fiftene he hafde feondliche wunden
mon mihte i þare laste twa glouen iþraste
Þa nas þer namare i þan fehte to laue
of twa hundred þusend monnen þa þer leien tohauwen
buten Arþur þe king ane and of his cnihtes tweien
Arþur wes forwunded wunder ane swiþe
þer to him com a cnaue þe wes of his cunne
he wes Cadores sune þe eorles of Corwaile
Constantin hehte þe cnaue he wes þan kinge deore
Arþur him lokede on þer he lai on folden
and þas word seide mid sorhfulle heorte 
Costæntin þu art wilcume þu weore Cadores sone
Ich þe bitache here mine kineriche
and wite mine Bruttes a to þines lifes
and hald heom alle þa laȝen þa habbeoþ istonden a mine daȝen
and alle þa laȝen gode þa bi Vþeres daȝen stode
And ich wulle uaren to Aualun to uairest alre maidene
to Argante þere quene aluen swiþe sceone
 and heo scal mine wunden makien alle isunde
al hal me makien mid haleweiȝe drenchen
And seoþe ich cumen wulle to mine kineriche
and wunien mid Brutten mid muchelere wunne
Æfne þan worden þer com of se wenden
þat wes an sceort bat liþen sceouen mid vþen
and twa wimmen þerinne wunderliche idihte
and heo nomen Arþur anan and aneouste hine uereden
and softe hine adun leiden and forþ gunnen liþen
Þa wes hit iwurþen þat Merlin seide whilen
þat weore unimete care of Arþures forþfare
Bruttes ileueþ ȝete þat he bon on liue
and wunnien in Aualun mid fairest alre aluen
and lokieþ euere Bruttes ȝete whan Arþur cumen liþe
Nis nauer þe mon iboren of nauer nane burde icoren
þe cunne of þan soþe of Arþure sugen mare
Bute while wes an witeȝe Mærlin ihate
he bodede mid worde his quiþes weoren soþe
þat an Arþur sculde ȝete cum Anglen to fulste
Costantin þus leouede on londe and Bruttes hine lufede
and swiþe deore heom he wes and wrþeliche heo hine heolden
Nu hæfuede Modred sunen tweie an maine swiþe stronge
hei iseȝen hu hit ferde here of Arþure þan kaisere
and hu heore fader wes ofslaȝe and idon of lifdaȝen
 and hu Bruttes todreued weoren mid feole cunne bursten
Þa ilke tweie broþeren speken heom bitweohnen
and somneden þa cnihtes alle selest þa heom þuhte
þa weoren wide tofloȝen ut of þan wiþeruehte
and somneden uerde wide ȝeond þan arde 
and þuhten to slan Costantin and al his lond binimen him
Þat iherde sugge Costantin þe king wes abolȝen
and sende his sonde wide ȝeond his londe
and hirede hehte cume þan kingge to helpe
Siȝen toward hirede ȝeonglinges snelle
þritti þusend anan somned comen þrasten
and þe king forþrihtes makeden hom cnihtes
Þa oþere cnihtes þer comen þa at þan fehte ar weoren
þa hafde he tosomne sixti þusende
Þat iherde bodien beien Moddredes sunen
and nomen heom to rade and to somrune
þat þe an liþen wolde into Lundene
and þe oþer liþen wolde into Winchastre
and þer heo wolden abiden þat þe king comen riden
and wolden wiþ him fehten mid allen heore mehten
Ah þæ hit com to neode oþer weis hit eode
Costantin gon liþe touward Lundenne
Þat iherden bodien þeo þa burh biwusten
hælden tosomne to heore hustinge
heo nomen heom to rade and to somrune
þat heo wolden halden alle mid Costantin þan kinge
and forsaken Modredes sune þæ þat morþ wrohte
Modredes sune flah and into ane munestere teh
And Constantin him after wende and þer hine icæhte
þe king mid his sweorde þat hefd him ofswipte
And þus þe king wordede wræþ on his þonke
Liȝe þer þu laþe mon leof þu beo þan Sucke
slæþ heom aneouste al þat ȝe findeþ þere
mine wiþeriwinnen weorpeþ heom to grunden
Þis slaht wes sone idon for moni mon þer wenden to
Seoþen lette Costantin þe king wes on londe
blawen his bemen and bonnien his ferden
and wende riht þene wai þe touward Winchæstre lai
and forþ ladde mid him þa Bruttes of Lundene
and to Winchæstre comen and aneouste binnen wenden
Þat isæh Meleou þe wes Modredes sone 
and from his iueren cherde and fleh to are chirche
and forþriht anan wende forn to ane wefde
Costantin braid ut his sweorde and þat hafde him ofswipte
þat seint Anfibales weofd iwraþ þerof a blode
