and seoþen he lette slen alle Melaeoues men
Þeo wes Costantin king here of þessere kineriche
þa bigunnen blissen in Brutene to wunien
her wæs griþ her wes friþ and freoȝ laȝen mid folke
and ful wel heolden þa ilke laȝen þat stoden on Arþures daȝen
Ah þat ilke ilaste to lutele while
for no ilast he buten feouwer ȝer his feond hine aqualde
and his folc hine uerede into Stanhenge
and þer hine leide bi leofen his aldren
Seoþþen wes Conan ihouen her to kinge
þat wes þe forcuþeste mon þet sunne here scean on
Costantines suster sune his æm he biswac to deþe
for he hefde rihte to þissere kineriche
Conan mid attere his æmes sune aqualde
He bigon unfriþ is men him fuhten wiþ
and he gon sechien to his twam susteren
alc burh i þan londe ferde al to sconde
astured wes al þas þeode strongliche swiþe
Six ȝere ilaste þas særinesse on londe
þa veol þe king of horse and fæisiþ makede
wel wes al þis folke for his fæiesiþe
Þa þis wes al ido þus þa iwarþ king Uortiporus
Þeo comen Sexisce men seilen to londe
and muchelne harm wrohten biȝeonde þere Hunbren
sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen
And Uortiporus þe hende sende after genge
and ferede heom ouenon and feolde Sexisce men
and monie þusend sente to þare segrunde
and þus he heom aferde and flemde of londe
þat næuer seoþþen bi his daȝen ne lusten heom hider uaren 
His daȝes ilaste seuen ȝere and seoþþen he deiȝede
And seoþþen nom þas riche Malgus þe reȝe
þat was þe faireste mon wiþuten Adam and Absolon
swa alse þe boc us suggeþ þa æuere iboren weore
Þes lette his hired dihte al wiþ ohte cnihten
þuhten alle þes sweines swulche heo weoren þeines
haueden alle his hiredcnafe ælches godes sweines laȝe
Ne durste nauere nan vnhende mon þas kinges hus isechen
He biwun þa londes alle þa stoden him an honde
Þa wes al þas Bruttene afeolled mid blisse
þa bleden uorþ comen ȝeond al þis kinedomen
Þe king ne rohte of æhte ah al he hit ȝaf his cnihten
no mihte no mon sugge of wundere namare
þene wes mid þan kinge buten of ane þinge
He luuede þane sunne þe laþ is ure Drihtene
þa wifmen heo forsoken to mare sunne heo token
wapmon luuede wapmon wifmen heom laþe weoren
swa þat monie þusende wenden of þissen lond
wifmen swiþe feire ferden to oþere þeoden
for mucchel scome heom þuhte þat wepmen heom ne rohte
Þurhut alle cunnes þinge þis ilke wes a god kinge
buten of þere sunne þat ich iseid habbe
Þa com an of his cunne Carric wes ihaten
and nom þisne kinedom and mid seorȝen wunede þeron
snel cniht wes Carric ah he nes noht iseli
þat wes for unleoden spilden al his þeoden
Þeos king wes aþel Bruttisc mon hux and hoker me warp him on
he forlætte Carriches and Kinric hine cleopede
and ȝet on feole bocken his nome me swa writeþ
Folc hine gunnen hænen folc hine gunne hatien
and hoker loþ sungen bi laþen þan kingen
Þa bigon weorre ouer al þissen arde
and Sexisce men sone seileden to londe
and herberȝe token aneouweste biȝeonde þere Humbre
and þe king wæilien agon wide ȝeon þas þeoden
læþ he wes al folke þa him on lokede 
Þa wes in Aufrike a king swiþe riche
he wes an Aufrican Anster ihaten
he hafde sonen tweien snelle cnihtes beien
Gurmund hehte þe eldere and Gerion hehte þe ȝeongere
Þe alde king deȝede his daȝes weoren aȝeongen
he bitahte his sune Gurmunde selen his riche
Ah Gurmund hit forhoȝede and habbe he heo nolde
and þohte al oþer and ȝef heo his broþer
and seiden þat he nolde aȝen nane riche
bute he heo biwunne mid wepnen and mid monnen
ah mid compe he wolde aȝen kineriche
oþer nauermare nolde he habbe nane
Gurmund was kempe icostned on mæine
and he wes þe strongeste mon þæ æi mon lokede on
He bigon to sende ȝeond al þan londe
into Babilonie into Macedonie
in Turkie into Persie
into Nubie into Arrabie
 and bad alle þe ȝeonglinges ȝeond þa hæþene londes
þat heo heom biȝeten wurþliche wepnen
and he heom forþrihtes wolden makien cnihtes
and seoþþen mid heom wenden and fonden whar he mihten
mid strongen kempen biwinnen kineriche
Hit halde touward Aufrike of feole kuneriche
monies riches monnes sune monie haþene gume
comen to Gurmunde þan hæþene þringe
Þa þis ferde wes isomned and his folc arimed
þa weoren þer italde cnihtes swiþe balde
an hundred and sixti þusend freoliche iwapned
wiþuten heore scutten þa biuoren scolden scuuen
wiþuten þan craftmonnen þe comen to Gurmunde
Forþ heo iuusden vnimete uerden
to þare se wenden þa heo wind hafden
into scipe halden haþene kempen
Seouentene þer foren þat kinges sunen weoren
þer weoren twenti and æhten of eorlene streone 
suipten from londe seouen hundred scipene
a formeste flocke wiþuten þa feoliende
Forþ flet mid vþe folc vnimete
þa æitlondes allen þa heo biforen funden
alle heo eoden an honde þan kinge Gurmunde
moniane kinge he faht wiþ and alle heo ȝirnden his griþ
 and alle þe londes he biwon þat he lokede on
And þa a þan ende he com to Irlonde
and þat lond he al biwon and aqualden þa leoden
and wes icleoped king þere of þan kinelonde
 and seoþþen he gon wende into þissen londe
seil heo droȝen to hune and comen to Suþhamtune
Þa wunede biȝeonde þere Hunbre of Hengestes cunne
in þan norþ ende drenches sume sixe
heo iherden tiþinde of Gurmund þan kinge
ofte heo heom biþohte what heo don mihten
hu heo mihten biswiken Karic of his richen
and Bruttes alle aquellen mid luþeren heore craften
Sexisce men senden sonde to Karic þan king
and seiden þat heo wolden wiþ hine griþ iwurchen
leofere heom weore to here Karic
þene Gurmunde þan vncuþe kinge
ȝef he heom wolde griþien þat heo mosten liuien
 and aȝeuen heom þat lond þat while Uortigerne þe king
Hengeste bitahte þa he nom his dohter leoue
and heo him wolden senden gauel of þan londe
halden hine for hehne king Karic heore deorling
 and þis heo him toȝeornden mid ȝislen to isoþien
And Karic heom ilefde al heore leosinge
and þis griþ ȝette and dai heom sette
Þa wes Karic biswiken al mid heore craften
Karic auer seoþen Kineric he hehten
al mid hokerworden þe king heo forhusten
Karic ileouede to soþe Sexisce monne lare
Vnder þan worden heo letten writ makien
 and senden heore sonden to Gurmunt þen kinge 
and þus þa word seiden þa a þan writ stoden
Hail seo þu Gurgmund hal seo þu heþene king
heil seo þi duȝeþe hail þine drihtliche men
We sunden men Sexisce selest of þan kunne
þa Hengest of Sexlonde hider mid him brohte
wunieþ inne Brutaine bi norþe þere Humbre
þu art heþene king we heþene kempen
Karic is Cristine mon he is us laþ forþan
and ȝif þu wult al þis lond nimen to þire aȝere hond
we wulleþ mid þe uehten mid fullere strenþen
and Caric ofslæn and alle his cnihtes flan
 and setten al þis kinelond a þire aȝere hond
ȝif þu hit wult us aȝiuen we þe wulleþ ȝelden
sixti hundred punden to alches ȝeres firsten
 and we wulleþ þine men bicumen to ȝislen sullen þe ure sunen
And ȝif hit þi wille weore þat þu hider woldest wende
þas forwarde makien and þas spechen uæstnien
we wulleþ oueral atlien to þe seluen
a watere and a londe halden þe uor kinge
Þa bigon to spekene Gurmund þe kene
Ȝarkieþ mine scipen biliue forþ ic wulle liþe
Seiles heo up droȝen forþ heo gunnen siȝen
luken rapes longe liþen forþ mid uþen
and swa heo gunnen wenden to Norþhumbrelonde
and speken wiþ Sexisce men and sæhte iwurþen
and sworen þat heo wolden heore forward halden
Þa weoren heo al an Gurmund and Sexesce men
þa somneden heo uerde vnimete an ærde
 and ferde touward Karriche þan kinge of þissere riche
and æuere heo sungen mid hokere of Kinriche þan kinge
Caric his Bruttes gaderede and beide heom tosomne
and him to wende al þat was on londe
for rihtere neode nusten heo red betere
Caric muchel folc hafde and ferde vnimete
 and ofte he com to compe to Gurmunde kinge
and ofte he him faht wiþ and neuere no ȝirde his griþ
and for heo hokerede him on he iwarþ swiþe kene mon
 and ȝif he hafde genge efne wiþ Gurmunde
Gurmund weore sone islaȝen his folc idon of lifdaȝen
Ah æuere a þan ende wæx Gurmundes genge
and æuere a þan ende feol Carriches genge
Gurmund draf Carriche wide ȝeond þas riche 
and Carric at Cherinchestre biclusde hine ful faste
and moni dæi þer biuoren he lette þider fusen
al þat he hafde ihalden þat corn of þissen londe
and þa walles fastnede wunder ane stronge
Gurmund þet iherde and þider he gon ride
and bilæi Chirenchestre wiþutene swiþe faste
And Gurmund al þis kinelond walde to his aȝere hond
burȝes he forbarnde tunes he forswelde
Bruttes he aqualde balu wes on londe
munekes he forpinede on mani are wise
þa riche wif he lette his hiredmen makien to horen
preostes he alle ofslæh alle þa chirchen he todroh
clærkes he aqualde alle þa he funde
eche child he lette seoþe  
alle þa cnihtes he lette hon forþrihtes
al þis lond forferde a ueole cunne wise
Wulc wræcche folc swa mihte fleh ut of þeode
sum to Wales wende sum to Cornwale
sum into Neustrie þe hatte nu Normandie
sum fleh biȝeonden sæ into Bruttaine
and gunnen wunien seoþþe æn þet lond heht Armoriche
 and summe heo fluȝen to Irlonde for þan æie of Gurmunde
and þer wuneden þeouwe inne þraldome
heo and al heore cun and her ne come nauere aȝen
And þus losede Bruttes al þas kinelondes
And Gurmund bilæi Chirenchestre abuten swiþe uaste
and Caric wes wiþinnen and moni of his monnen
wa wæs þan leoden þe þa weoren on liuen
Hit was in ane dæie þat Gurmund mid his duȝeþe
dringes heþene riden a slatinge
Þa com þer an gume riden to Gurmunde kingen
he wes ihaten Isemberd inne France wes his ærd
he wes Louweises sune þas kinges of þere þeode
his fader hine hafuede ut idriuen of al his kinerichen
þat no moste he neouwar wunie on al his onwalde
and he fleh to þissen londe to Gurmunde kinge
he hafde to iueren twa þusend rideren
and Gurmunddes mon he bicom ne mihte he na wurse don
for Crist seolue he forsoc and to þan Wursen he tohc
and þer forlete he Cristindom and heþescipe nom him on
And swa heo uoren beien mid mucle heore uerde
and bileien Chirenchestre an elche halue wel faste
Wel ofte Kariches men comen ut of burhȝen
and ræsden an Gurmunde mid ræȝere strenþe
and sloȝen of his folke feole þusende
 and senden heom to helle heþene hundes alle
Karic wes swiþe goud cniht and swiþe wel he heold his fiht
and faste he heold Chirchestre mid strengþe þan mæste
þat ne mihte Gurmund næuere mæren his ferde
ar he lette heom mid ginnen biswiken wiþinnen
Gurmund castles makede abuten Chirenchestre
þreo he bitahte þreom heþene cnihte
himseoluen he heold þat ane Isembard þat oþer
Gurmund makede ænne tur þerinne he bulde ænne bur
þerinne he pleoȝede his plaȝen þa me luuede a þeon daȝen
þerinne he hafde his maumet þa he heold for his god
Hit ilomp on ane dæiȝe þat Gurmund mid his duȝeþe
weoren swiþe bliþe and druncken of wine
Þa com þer an heþene mon awaried wurþen he forþan
and askede tidende Gurmunde þe kinge
Seie me lauerd Gurmund þu art swiþe riche king
heou longe wult þu beoȝie abuten þissere burȝe
what wult þu ȝiuen me ȝif ich þe burh ȝiuen þe
and al þat is wiþinne to don þine iwille
þat noht no biþ to leue al þu hit slat aȝe
Þa andswarede Gurmund þe riche heþene king
Ich ȝiue þe ane eorldom auere to aȝe
wiþ þat þu aneoste þe burh me bitache
Þis forward wes imaked anan lut men hit wuste
Þa þes heþene cniht up aras forþrit
 and nettes bisohte ibroiden swiþe narewe
and þa tolen þerto and cuht heom swiþe narewe
þer biforen he gon ȝeoten draf and chaf and aten 
Þus he hit gon dihten and sparewen þerto liht
and he a þan uorme drahte swiþe monie he ilahte
and he from þan grunde nom heom mid isunde
þat alle heore whingen noht awemmed neoren
Þa bisohte he nutescalen and lette þe curneles ut draȝen
 and tinder nom and lette i þan scalen don
 and foren to þære nihte fur þeron brohte
and to þan sparewen uoten uaste heom icnutten
Þeos he lette forþ wenden swiþe ueole sparewen
þa sparwen heore flut nomen and fluȝen to heore innen
ȝeond þare burȝen þær heo ar wuneȝende weoren
i þan eouesen he grupen swa heo duden in þen muȝen
Anan swa þet fur wes hat swa þe sparewe innere crap
þe wind com mid þere nihte and þat fur awehte
and þa burh a feole studen gon hure to bernen
an æst halue an west halue wa wes Brutten þere
þenne heo wenden beon sikere and fluȝen in ane ende
þenne aras þat fur anan biuoren and bihinden
Gurmund lette blawen hornes and bemen
fiften þusende þarsten to blase
Bruttes forburnen Bruttes gunnen irnen
heo leopen ut of walle and me heom sloh alle
Nes hit nohwhar iseid no a bocken irad
þat æi folc swa feire swa forfare weore
swa wes Caric and his genge þe king wes of Bruttene
Þa burh born alle niht þe brune wes vnimete
þat feht wes sone idon þat fur heom eoden ouenon
And Carrich king him isah þat he ouercume wæs
þe king him gon crepen an heonden and a futen
swulc he mid unsunde al uorwunded weore
and swa he swiþe stille bistal from his duȝeþe
and west him gon wenden into þe Walsce londen
 and þas waiȝes he wende ut of þisse londe
and nuste nauere na man whar Karic him bicom
buten ænes an ane tide an cniht þer com ride
 and seide Gurmunde of Kariche tidende
þat he in Irlonde somnede genge
and wolde mid fehte æft faren hidere
Ah nuste nauere na man to whan þe þret him bicom
And þus wes Chirenchestre and his londes aweste
and Gurmund ihouen to kinge of al þisse kinelonde
for þenne þe burh wes biwunnen mid swulcches cunnes ginnen
mid sparewen þat beren þat fur and sparewen heo forbarnden
And feole wintere seoþþen þat folc þa þer wunede
cleopeden heo Sparewenchestre in heore leodspellen
and ȝet hit dude summe men to imuȝen þe alde deden
And þus wes þa riche burh mid reouþen fordemed
and Gurmund wes on londe iheouen her to kinge
and Gurmund wes an heþene mon and fordude þane Cristindom
Þa þis wes al þus ifare þæ wes her sorȝe and muchel care
Gurmund falde þa munstres and anheng alle þa munkes
of cnihten he carf þe lippes of madenen þa tittes
preostes he blende al þis folc he scende
ælcne bilefued mon he lette bilimien
and þus he gon to taken on and fordude al þisne Cristindom
And seoþþen he uor to Lundene to ane muchele hustinge
þider gunnen siȝe alle Sexleode
þa wuneden i þissen londe mid Gurmunde kinge
and his men bicome monie and vniuoȝe
heom heold forward and aȝef heom sone al þis ærd
of him to heoldenne and habben hine for kinge
And þe king hehte al þat hine lufede
þat wharswa heo mihten finde Bruttes i þissen londe
þat hine anan sloȝen oþer mid horsen todroȝen
buten he libben wolden his lif in þraldome
and forsaken Godes mæsse and luuien hæþenesse
þenne moste he libben þeou a þisse londe
Bisiden Allemaine is a lond Angles ihaten 
þer weoren iborne þa ilke þe weorn icorne
þa Gurmund an hond bitahte al þis kinelond
alse he heom a forward hædde ȝif he hit biwunne
Al his biheste he heom bilaste
Of Englen heo comen and þerof heo nomen nomen
and letten heom cleopien ful iwis þat folc þat wes Ænglis
 and þis lond heo cleopeden Ænglelond for hit wes al on heore honde
Seoþþe ærest Bruttes bæhȝen to þissen londe
Brutaine hit wes ihaten of Brutten nom taken
a þat þis folc com þa þisne nome him binom
And moniee of þan burȝen and monie of þan tunen
and monie of þan londen and of þan hamen
heo binomen heore namen al for Bruttene sceome
and nomen al þis lond and setten hit al an heore hond
for Gurmund hit heom al ȝette and himseolf aȝein wende
Þa comen heo to Lundene to þan muchele hustinge
and wolden ane king makien to þissere kineriche
Þa ne mihtte heom iwurþe wha þis lond scolde aȝen
and towende mid alle a muchelere wraþþe
and fif kinges aneouste heo makeden in þisse londe
And ælc nom of oþere al þat heo mihten
ane while unsome and an oþere while isahte
and þus heo wuneden here an hundred and fif ȝere
þat neuere com here Cristindom icud i þissen londe
no belle irungen no masse isunge
na chirche þer nes ihaleȝed no child þer nes ifuleȝed
Þa wes inne Rome a pape of Godes dome
Gregori wes ihate Godd seolf hine lufede
Þa wes hit in ane stunden þat þe pape wolde wenden
þat he wolde speden an ane of his neoden
Þa com he in are strete þat strahte to Rome
þa isah he leden of Englisce leoden
þreo swiþe fæire men faste ibunden 
heo scolden beon iseolde and þa paneȝes weoren italde
Þa fræinede þa pape anan of feiȝere þan monnen
whonnene heo weoren and hu heo þare comen
and of wulche stronde heo istroned weoren
Þæ andswarede þe an þat wes a swiþe fair mon
We beoþ heþene men and hider beoþ iladde
and we weoren ut isalde of Anglene londe
and fulluht we to þe ȝeorneþ ȝef þu us wult ifreoiȝen
Þat seiden men Anglisce aþele iborene
Þa reousede Gregori Godd hine luuede
and þas andsware saide þe pape wes isele
Iwis ȝe beoþ Ænglisce englen ilicchest
of alle þan folke þa wunieþ uppen uolde
eouwer cun is feȝerest of alle quike monnen
Þe pape heom freinede of feole tidinde
of laȝen and of londen and of þissere leodene kinge
and heo him al seiden soþ þat heo wusten
and he heom ureoiȝen lette and fulluht on sette
and charde aȝein sone eft into Rome
Anne cardinal cleopede icoren of his uolke
Austin wes ihotæn aþelest clærken
þe pape him seide in his somrune
Austin þu scalt wende mid soþfæste þonke
into Englelonde to Æþelberte kinge
 and beode þer Godes goddspel þe scal spede ful wel
And ich þe feouwerti bitæche wel gode clærkes
Nu tomarȝen biþ þe dæi þa þu scalt do þe i þene wæi
Forþ ferde Austin and his clærkes mid him
þat him wes ful iwil at Tanette he com hider in
 and swa he up is iwend þat he com into Kent
Swa he uorþ to Cantuareburi þer him þuhte swiþe muri
þer he funde Aþelbert þat king wes a þan ærd
Aþelberde he talde tidende of þan heoueneliche kinge
he seide him þat goddspel and þe king him luste swiþe wel
wel he þat larspel undernom aneouste he ȝirnde Cristindom,
Iuulȝed iwarþ Aþelberd king and al his duȝeþe mid him, 
and anan he gon to wurche ane swiþe feire chirche
a seinte Trinetþes nome wel wes þan kinge þeruore
Þa iwende seint Austin vorþ æst and west and suþ and norþ
and seoþþe þurhut Englelond and turnde hit to Godes hond
clærkes he lerde chirreches he arerde
seoke men he helde þur Halindes mihte
And swa he droh suþward þat he com to Dorchestre
þer he funde þa wurste men þa on londe wuneden
he talde heom Godes leore and duden him to scare
he tahten heom Cristindom and heo grenneden him hon
Þer stod seint Austin and his clærkes mid him
and speken of Crist Godes sune al swa wes ær heore iwune
þer heo iwurþen to to wraþere hele
and nomen tailes of rehȝen
and hangede on his cape an elchere halue
and bihalues urnen and wurpen hine mid banen
and seoþþe ȝeiden him on mid ȝeomerliche stanen
 and swa heo hine gunnen sende an driuen hine ut of þan ende
Seint Austin heo weoren laþ and he iwraþ swiþe wraþ
and he fif milen iwende from Dorchestre
and com to ane munte þe muchel wes and hende
þer he lai on cneowe ibede and cleopede auere touward Gode
þat he hine awreke a þan awarriede uolke
þa hine isend hafden mid heore scaþe deden
Vre Drihte hine iherde into þere heouene
and his wreche sende an wræstliche þan folke
þa þe rihȝen tailes hangede a þan clarkes
Þa tailes heom comen on þeruoren heo maȝen iteled beon
Iscend wes þat moncun muggles heo hafden
and inne hirede ælches men cleopeþ heom muglinges
and euerelc freo mon ful telleþ heom on
 and Englisce freomen in uncuþe londen
for þan ilke dede heo habbeoþ neb rede
and monies godes monnes sune in vncuþe londe
þe nauere ne com þer neh is icleoped cued
Austin him wunede vnder ane munede
and his clarkes mid him eke þeo comen of Rome 
cleopede to Drihtene þe scop daȝes lihte
særimod and sorhfulle heom sceomeden wel sære
þat þat vniwraste moncun heom iscend hafden
Þa wolde he þerafter sone wenden to Rome
and menen to Gregorie þan holi appostolie
hu Dorchestreseten hine gunnen greten
Al swa he wes al ȝareou and wolde his wei uaren
a þere ilke nihte þa ateoden him ure Drihte
and nemnede him his rihte nome welle uain wes he þeruore
Whæt þenchest þu Austin what þenchest þu leof min
Woldest þu þus sone faren aȝein to Rome
No scalt þu noht ȝete fusen of londe
þu ært swiþe leof me and ich wulle wunien mid þe
and þu scalt irædliche into hefneriche
heofne is þe al ȝaru þider scal þi saulen uaren
Þus spac ure Drihten wiþ Austin his cnihten
Þa þe Austin underȝæt whæt ure Drihten hæden isæid
and he isah ure Drihte þe þus him bihehte
and ure Drihten waht to heofene and Austin a cneowe heolde
adun to þere uolde þer he iseh ure Drihten stonde
weopende he cleopede to heuenliche kinge
ȝeorne he bad are to þan almihtie Gode
ær he mid alle ueolle adun to þere uolde
A þan ilke stude þer stod ure Drihten
þer he pihte his stæf himseolf he cneoulede þer neh
and his iueren he seide larspel and hit likede him ful wel
Þa he isaid hauede þa sæȝen of ure Drihten
his staf he nom an honde and wolde to his inne ȝeonge
Up he læc þene staf þat water þerafter leop
Þe ueȝereste welles stræm þe irneþ on uolden
Ær nes þer na tun no wunende na man
Sone uolc gaderede to Austin þan gode
and al bi his læuen þider gunnen liþen
and bigunnen þer to bulden bi þan watere þa was hende
Moni mon þer uætte hele þene stude he cleopede Cernele
cerno cernis þat is Latin ful iwis
cerno an Englisc leoden ich iseo swa hit is iqueþen
el is Ebreowisc þat is Godd ful iwis 
þene tun he cleopede Cernel ich iseo Drihten iwildel
to þissere weorlde longe þe nome þer scal stonde
alse hit is iqueþen after Godes leoden
þene stude to iwurþien þer stod ure Drihten
and his engles mid him þa he spac wiþ Austin
Austin wende wide ȝeond Englene londe
he fullehtede kingge and heore heredringes
he fullehtede eorles he fullehtede beornes
he fullehtede Englisce men he fullehtede Sexisce men
and sette an Godes honde al þat was on londe
Þa wes he ful bliþemod þat folc he hafde iblissed
Norþ in Englelonde Bruttes hæfden an honde
muchel del of londe and castles swiþe stronge
Þa Bruttes nalden þan Enlisce buȝen
imong heom munekes weoren muchelere weorede
Seint Austin funde inne þisse londe
seouen biscopes to iwisse singende masse
and enne ærchebiscop þe at Karliun atstod
and at Bangor wes a munecclif mid muneken uniuoȝe
Dionot hæhte heore abbeod he wes of heȝe monnen
he hæfden on seuen hepen sixtene hundred muneken
and ȝet ma þerto munekes swiþe balde
and of Bruttisce streonen stiþe imodede men
Writen sende Austin to þan seouen biscopen
and hehte heom comen sone and speken wiþ himseolue
 and don him hersumnesse and þurh him singen masse
for he hauede an honde þa hehnesse of þissen londe
he was icleopped legat of þissen londe he wæs primat
 and þas þinges weoren idone þurh þene pape of Rome
Þas biscopes reiȝe weoren and andswere aȝeuen
Ne beo we nawit under him þe is ihaten Austin
ah we beo on londe heȝe men and stronge
and habbeoþ ure irihte of ure archebiscpe
þe wuneþ inne Karliun godd clarc and wel idon
þa haueþ his cantelcape on of Gregorie þan pape
and mid wurþscipe mucle haldeþ his wike
For no scal hit nauere iwurþen a þissere worlderichen
þat we auere buȝen Austine þan uncuþen 
for he is ure fulle ifa and his iferen alswa
For Austin is iboȝen hidere into þissen londe
and haueþ ifulleȝed þene king Cantuaren aþeling
Aþelbert ihaten heh inne Anglene
and he hafueþ ifunden here hundes heþene
þa comen of Sexlonde mid Gurmunde þan kinge
þeo he alle fullehteþ and to Gode fuseoþ
þeo haldeoþ ure kinelond mid unrihte on heore hond
Cristine we beoþ alle and of Cristine cunne
and ure elderne swa weoren agan is þreo hundred ȝeren
 and heo beoþ neowene icumen and Cristindom habbeoþ undernumen
and Austin heom fullehteþ and to Gode fuseoþ
For þan we hine hatiȝen uulleþ and heren hine nulleþ
nauere to ure liue no scullen we him wurþen liþe
Þæs tiþende come to Austine sone
hu þe biscopes hine scenden and wulc andsweore him senden
and hu Bruttisce clerekes him seiden hokeres
Þa wes he sarimod and sorhful an heorten
and fuse him gon sone and ferde to þan kinge
and mænde to Aþelberte þan kinge of ÆstAngle
hu Bruttisce biscopes hine grætte mid huxes
and hu heo uorhoȝeden to halden hine for herre
Þe king hine iwraþede wunder ane sweþe
and saide þat he wolde aquellen heom a londe
and swe he dude seoþþe þerafter ful sone
Aþelbert wes inne Kintte king of þan londe
þa hafde he enne mæi Æluric wes ihaten
inne Norþhumberlonde furcuþest alre kinge
he radde al þa redes þat dede weoren þa biscopes
þat heo weoren alle ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
Nu nuste noht Bruttes þere þat balu heom wes ȝiueþe
Aþelbert sende sonde wide ȝeond his londe
Æluric sende sonde ȝeond Norhhumberlonde
heo somneden uerde mucle on arde
 and wolden þa Bruttes al fordon þa clærkes fordemen
heo uoren to Leirchæstre and þa burh bileien uaste 
heo wusten þerinne Brochinal þat wæs a Bruttisc eorl
cniht mid þan bezsten wunede inne Leirchastre
Bruchinal ut wende and ȝarewede his ferde
and wende him ut to uihtes wiþ Aþelbertes cnihtes
and sone wes him ouercumen and alle his Bruttes weoren inumen
 and swa heo gunnen þrasten into Leirchæstren
sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen
and seiden þat heo wolden into Wales wenden
 and slæn al þa Bruttes þa þer weoren bihalues
Æluric luuede murie inne Leirchastre
Vnder þan ilke þinge comen to Æluric þan kinge
munekes and eremite and canunes white
biscopes and clærckes and preostes mid Godes mærkes
and feolen to his foten and his griþ ȝeornden
and beden hine for Godes leoue leten heom beon on londe
and ho him wolden foren bidden to þan heȝen kingen
Þa andswarede forcuþest kinge
Lusteþ nuþe alle whæt ich sugge wulle
wendeþ ut a þan felde mid eower monwerede
and ich eou wulle word senden hu hit scal iwurþen
and mine rædȝiuen reden me wulleþ
Vt wenden munekes and þa massepreostes
vt wenden clærkes vt wenden canones
alle ut wenden þa þer icumen weoren
þes kinges griþ to wilnien for lufe of Godd seolfne
Wiþuten þere burȝe an ane uelde brade
wes isomned þat folc sone sorȝe heom wes ȝefþe
Aluric nom to rede þeh na man hine ne bede
þat he al þas wolde feollen to þan grunde
He sende forþrihtes fif hundred cnihtes
and niȝen hundred mid heom balde men afoten
mid mucle wiaxen a þene ueld wenden
and mid unrihtes sloȝen al þat heo neh comen
Heo ualden to grunde fiftene hundred
and fife and sixti anan selere monnen
bocilerede men balu wes on uolken 
Þis sone wes itald wide and side
Þa weoren on londe þreo heȝe men italde
and al þa Bruttes anan halden to þan ilken
Baldric þe kene eorl of Cornwale
swa hehte þe an heh mon on londen
he heold Deuenescire al an his honde
alse þet water Desse wendeþ into þere sæ
Bruttes þat lond heolden wel swiþe longe
a þat Aþestan þe stronge þe king of þissen londe
heom binom þas londes alle and drof heom ouer Tambre
þat nauere heo þas kineþeode seoþþen no walde
Inne Norþ Wales wes a king Cadwan þe kene
of Suþ Wales Margadud monnen alre uæȝerest
al þat lond sele into Sæuerne
from þan ufere ende þat wendeþ into þare sæi
Inne Maluerne aneouste Seuarne
Margadud king wunede mid swiþe mucle uolke
and Aþelstan him laþ to þe king of þissere leode
and heom heold swa harde and mid hærme heom igrette
and dreof heom mid his wepnen ut ouer Weȝen
and þat lond binom heom þat liþ þer bitwixen
Seuerne and Weȝe no walden heo hit seoþþen
Margadud and Baldric and Cadwan þe balde
somneden ferde of folke unimete
and foren uppen Aluriche þan kinge of Norþhumbre
and hardliche wiþ him fuhten and his ferde felden
Þer iwarþ sone forwunded ful sære
þe king of Norþhumbre þat comp wes vnimete
þer wes Baldric eorl anan mid bronden toheouwen
i þan compe þer ueollen ten þusend cnihten
þurh steles biten baldere Brutten
Anglisce and Sexisce seouentene þusend
mid machen weoren toheowen þa hep wes þa lassen
Æluric him uorþ heolde into Norþhumbre
forwunded swiþe sare sorhful wes his duȝeþe
Comen i þissen londe to ane hustinge 
Cadwan and Margadud and heore monweorede
buȝen uorh mid heom al Brutleoden
to Leirchestre foren and þa burh nomen
Þa hehten heo an hiȝinge cumen to hustinge
al þat wolde libben inne þissere leoden
Þer comen Ænglisce þer comen Sexise
þer heo makeden to kinge Cadwan þene kene
al hit him aloþede þat he on lokede
þa weoren Æluriches wunden inne Norhhumbre
alle iheled ah þe helþe was neoþered
for lurre of his monnen and for his leoden uallen
Æluric iherde from þes kinges hirede
feole tidende of Cadwane kinge
þrattes unimete of alre laþest monne
Æluric sende sonde into Scotlonde
and into Norþ londe þer he cnihtes mihte uinden
and after al þan uolke þe þer cumen mihte
and bad heom heore helpes to heȝere neodes
Cadwan gaderede uerde ȝeond alle þissen ærde
and al of Wælisce londe comen to his honden
and heolde hine forþ seoþþen toward Norþhumbren
Aluric þis iherden and him toȝæines wenden
þat nas heom bitweounen buten bare twa milen
fusden þa uerden swulc heo wolden uehten
Þa isæȝen eorles þa iseȝen beornes
biscopes þa iseȝen and bocilarede men
ȝif heo togadere comen and mid wepnen onsloȝen
þat þær sculde ualle moni beorn fæie
Ofte heo biþohten what heo don mahten
heo setten griþ heo sette friþ to anes dæiȝes firste
heo speken heom tosomne and spileden bitweonen
þat heo wolden alle þa kinges sehtnie
Þer iwurþen sahte þa kinges beie tweien
sæhte and some heo custen wel ilome
þas kinges wel ilomen mid luue heom icusten
eorl custe oþer swulc hit weore his broþer
sweines þer ploȝeden blisse wes mid þeinen
Æluric wes king on londe bi norþen þere Humbre
and Cadwan wes king sele a suþ half þere Humbre
blisse wes on hireden mid balden þat kingen
Næs hit isæid næuere an sæȝe no on leoþe
þat mare luue weore ifunden bitweone twei kingen
for þat þe an hafden þat heo hafden beien
þe an heold þene oþer deorluker þene broþer
Beien heo wifes nomen ofte heo togadere comen
þa þe wifes iwedded weoren on ane time to bedde heo eoden
æiþer mid his lufe wende toward heore wife
he streoneden tweien sunen beien an ane timen
beien an ane dæie heo weoren afte iborne
togadere heo weoren ibredde togadere heo weoren iuedde
Þa children wuxen and wel iþoȝen
wel wes heore aldren
For to uæstnen þa luuen of leofuen heore uæderen
tosomne me heom tahte tosomne me heom tuhte
beien heo wereden anes kunnes iweden
al swa duden þa children swa ær duden þa aldren
swa mouchel luue heolden þat sellic þuhte monnen
And þus heo wuneden here wel feole ȝere
þat þæ children weoren muchele iwaxen
riden uppen steden and luueden cnihtes iweden
heore maines heo uondeden wel ueole siþen
heore armes weore stronge heo breken scaftes longe
mid longe sweorden heo smitten þa ȝifen smærte biten
Heore uaderes þa comen mid mucle faȝernessen
inne Bruttaine mid muclere blisse
þa ȝet þat londriche hehte Armoriche
þa ȝunge men me dubbede beiȝene to cnihte
Wiþ an luttel ȝeren þa uaderes dede weoren
and þa twa children weoren ihouen to kingen
æiþer heold his icunden swa duden ær heore ældren
Þæ wes inne Cantwareburi þa burh wes þa swiþe muri
an ærchebiscop þe wes mon swiþe god 
he forbad þan kingen kinehelm to nimene
a þat hinseolf comen and setten hine an heore hafden
Þat bod wes ihalden a þas ærchebiscopes onwalden
and Cadwadþal his lond haueden a þis hælue þere Humbre
and Edwine al biȝeonde touward þan norþ ende
kinges heo weoren ihouene and kinges isworene
ah forbode wes þa crune an ure Drihtenes nome
Cadwalan þohte þe wes Cadwanes sune
ofte he hine biþohte what he don mahte
seoþþen heore faderes beiene forþ weoren ifarene
Næfde þa sehtnesse ilast buten seouen ȝere urist
Cadwalan hefde castles swiþe monieȝe
and þe richedom stod mære on Cadþwalanes hond
Cadwaþlan gon liþe into Londene
he sende men gode after þan erchebiscope
and hehte ful sone þat he to Lundene come
Þa he to Lundene com iqueme hit wes þan kingen
þe king auoten eode toȝeines þan erchebiscope
wiþuten his halle dure and sæide Þu art wilcume
 and leofliche hine bihedde and lauerd hine cleopede
He aȝaf ure Drihten ælchere irihten
he spac of feire lære and al of Godes are
his spechen weoren gode wiþ þan ærchebiscope
Þe king hine biþohte feire and swiþe ofte
þat he on his icunde king hine makede
To ane isette dæiȝe þat folc þær isomnede
þer mæ Cadwaþlan sone makede to kinge
muchel wes þa blisse þat wæs in þære burȝe
Of þisse uarecoste Adwine naþing nuste
ah sone swa he hit wiste wraþ he wes an heorte
and seide auere wiþ and wiþ Ich wulle makien unfriþ
and al ic wulle aquellen þat ich quike uinde
of Cadwaþlanes uolke ualsest alre monne
Uerde he gon gaderen of feole þusend monnen
he hehde ituht to herie a þas half þære Humbre
Eoden heom to ræde cnihtes swiþe gode
alle þa wiseste men þa weore inne londe
heo lerden Edwine king þe wes heore lauerd 
þat he sende his sonde to Cadwaþlane kinge
 and bisohte hine uæire alse his leofe broþer
and for þere muchele luue þa heolde heore aldren
þat hine letten king beon and his kinehalm avon
and he wolde aȝein wenden heom to his folke
ouer þere Humbre and griþ þær halden
and ner æft aȝen teon wiþ þan he moste king beon
ihouen and ihalden þurh þene heȝe Godd
and he wolden bi his liuen Cadwalain luuien
and beon ȝaru to his neode an ælchere þeode
Þis iherde Cadwalan þe king wes bi suþþen
and he andswerede mid aþelere speche
Nu ich iherd habbe wordes wise
of Edwine his bisocne þe is mi broþer deore
ich me biræde wulle of swulchere neode
and after ane lutel daȝen him andsware ȝeuen
whaþer he hit wolde iunne oþer him forbeode
hu swa his riche men ræden him wolden
Þe dæi wes isæt ah lutel mon wes þe bet
Þa þis al wes iwurþen þa comen heo to ane uorde
Duglas þa water wes ihaten þer heo touwenden
þer wes þa motinge bituxe þan twam kinge
Ædwine bisohte mid alle þat he mahte
þat Cadwalan him þolede kinehelm to beberene
and he hine wolde luuien a to his liuen
Riche men eoden to ræde of swulchere neode
summe hit gonnen ræden summe to forbeoden
summe þer heolden wel to summe nolden hit no
Þa while þa cnihtes wise þa spechen sculden rihte
þe king in are medewe alihte of his stede
þan kinge luste slepe þa riche weoren at rede
Com þer a burcniht
he wes þes kinges suster sune Brien hehte his nome
he nom his lauerdes hefd þe leof him wes on uolke
in his bærm he hit læide and his lockes he toscædde
Þe king him gon to slæpen and Brien gon to wepen 
urnen þa teres uppen þes kinges leores
and þe king awoc of slepen wete weoren his wongen
he grapede an his nebbe he wende þat hit bledde
and bisæh uppen Brien mid braden his lechen
Þa isah he of Brien his teres ut luken
sære gon þe kempe wepen ouer kinge
Þa axede þe king anan Cadwalan ihaten
Whæt is þe leofe mæi þat þu swa wepest todæi
þu ært ihalden kene gume hauest þu nu quene þeouwes inume
Sæiȝe me biliue hu þe beon on siþe
Brien þa andswerede cniht mid þan bezste
Nu we maȝen wepen mid wanliche iberen
halden us for hæne þer we weoren heȝe
Nu þu wult underuon þat nauer ær nes idon
tweien kinges halden kinehelmes on londen
Nuþe we scullen wepen þæ ær richen weoren
for wurþscipe ualleþ adune þer wes ær wunne
Cadwadlan þis iherde þe king wes on londe
and iwærþ him abolȝe bitter ane swiþe
and aneouste sende sonde to Edwine kinge
and hehte hine hihȝenliche uaren of his riche
For ne scal he nauere bi mine quiken liuen kinehelm broken
and ȝif he hit wul auon ich hit wulle wernen
and ic hine biræuien wulle at his baren liue
 and nimen al Norþhumberlond to mire aȝære hond
and walden al his riche and he scal wurþen hene
Þas tidende me brohten to Adwine kinge
 and he iwræþ abolȝen wunder ane swiþe
swa biþ a bar wilde
þenne he biþ in holte bistonden mid hunden
and þas andsware kende wraþest alre kingen
Swa me helpen Drihten þa scop þas dæiȝes lihten
and þa halidomes alle þa wunieþ inne Rome
kinehelm ich wulle bruke and he hit scal abugge
and þeruore ibiden bitterest alre balewen
he scal habben paþes weste and wildernesse inoȝe
and moni modsorhȝe his monscipe scal ualle
Al swa hit ilomp suþþe þæræfter ful sone
Æiþer þratte oþer swiþe and þruste mid worde 
 and swa heo todelden dæd heo bihehten
Ædwine wes kempe his men weoren kene
Cadwaþlan wes cniht god and he hafde muchel mod
Edwine wende ouer Humbre and Cadwaþlan to Lundene
þas kinges weoren wraþe þa aræs þa weore
Heo riden and heo arnden heo herȝede and heo barnde
heo sloȝen and heo nomen al þat heo neh comen
wa wes þan beondes þa on londe wuneden
Cadwalan wes inne Lundene and somnede his leoden
wide he sende sonde ȝeond feole kinelonde
he hafde on his ferde fifti þusende
herekempen heȝe to hermen swiþe kene
Adwine bi norþe his writen nom aneouste
and sende in to Denene
to Galwaþe and to Scotlond þat stod on Edwines hond
he somnede uerde ȝeond alle his ærde
þat he isomned hafde sixti þusende
cnihtes swiþe kene wode to uihte
Cadwaþlan gon liþe ut of Lundenne
touward Norþhumbre hærmes he wrohte
he for ouer Humbre hiȝenliche swiþe
and bigon to westen þat lond þat stod on Edwines hond
Þa wes Edwine king ærhþen bideled
and he forþrihtes spac wiþ his cnihtes
Wurþe for niþing þe mon þe nule hine sturien
habben bares heorte and remes brede
cuþen þan kinge þat we quiken sunde
He lette blawen bemen and bonnien his uerden
forþ he gon wende þat he com to þan ende
þer þe king Cadwaþlan wunede on cumelan
Togadere gunnen resen þeines riche
breken speren longe sceldes brastleden an honde
heouwen heȝe helmes scænden þa brunies
feollen ærm kempes æmteden sadeles
drem wes on uolcke þa eorþe gon to dunien
urnen þa brockes of reden blodes
feollen þa folckes falewede nebbes
Bruttes gunnen breoþen balu wes on uolken 
Þus heo gunnen delen þene dæi longe
riht to þan euening þa fleh Cadwalan þe king
and Edwine him after gende mid allen his imihten
Alle niht Cadwalan flah mid his cnihten
nefden he of his ferde buten fif hundred cnihten
heo fluȝen to Scotlonde sorhen heom com on honde
And Edwine after annon mid fiftene þusend monnen
baldere þeines heore beot wes iuorþed
Fulede þere uerde folc unimete
from dæiȝe to daȝe þene king heo gunnen driuen
soþ is on þan spellen heo þohten hine aquellen
Cadwaddlan flæh to þere sæ scipen he þer funde
þa scipen heo gunnen hure mid ahten swiþe deore
into Irlonde þa scipen gunnen wende
hauene heo þer nomen isund þa scipen comen
Þa ahte Irlond a king þat wes swiþe strong
he hehte Gille Patric god king i þan rich
he underfeng Cadwalan faire nid his cossen
and ȝaf him wickinge ȝeond Irlonde
Lette we nu beon Cadwaþlan and ga we to Edwine aȝan
Edwine in þissen londe amarden þas leoden
burȝes he barnde castles he ualde
his here wrohte on londe harmes vniuoȝe
al Cadwaþlanes lond he walde to his aȝere hond
Þa comen hauweres to hirede þas kinges
and seiden tidende Edwine kinge
wa wrþe heom for þon þat heo iboren weore
saȝen heo him sæiden of ane mæidenne
þat wes Briennes suster hende ueirest wifmonne
heo wunede i Winchæstre inne þan castle
And Edwine mid his ferde þiderward wende
sone swa he þider com mid strenþe he heo nom
ladden heo to Eouuerwic anan cnihtes swiþe wel idon
to bure me ladde to þas kinges bedde
Þe king dude vnwisdom þat he þat ilke maide nom
for þe wifmon a wes þes ilke kinges iua
Þa wunede i þan hirede an clarc þe com from Spaine 
Pelluz wes ihaten of heȝere laren
feole craftes he cuþe þa he isah in þan lufte
on sterren and on sunne and on þare sæ brade
insiht he cuþe a winde and a mone
of þan uisce þer he wlæt and of wurmen þer heo crepe
Cadwaþlan in Irlonde gaderede genge
and to scipe flutte mid muchelre uerde
Pelluz swiþe ueorre isah on þan sterre
þat ferde cumen wolde uppen Ædwine kinge
and Pelluz hine lerde
hu he þas leoden mihtte alre bezst biwiten
Ba bi londen and bi scipen Cadwaþlan and his men
ofte gunnen fusen to cumen to þissen londen
biuoren wes æuere Edwine and þa hafne heom forwarnde
þurh Pelluces lare ne mihten heo cumen here
Wa wes Cadwalan þat he wes on liuen
for he bigon þene swikedom uppen his sweordbroþeren
and þeruore himself hafde hærm þene meste
Cadwalan him to cleopede his bezste cnihtes alle
and seide þat he wolde wende to Brutaine
and þene king iseon þe Salemon wes ihaten
an heorte him weore þe selere for heo weoren isibbe
heo weoren of ane cunne þa kinges beiȝe tweien
Bruttes heo weoren beine ah swiþe heo weoren unbalde
Cadwaþlan to scipen com and seh forþ mid uþen
and seilede after vþe unsel him wes on mode
to ane æitlonde heo bicomen þat stondeþ bi Gernemuþe
likede swa heom likede þer heo gunnen wikie
þer heo abiden wederes for þe wind heom stod toȝæines
Þa iwarþ þe king þere isæcled ful swiþe
and hafde þat uuel hate binumen him wes þa hele
Þa niȝen dæȝes weoren aȝeong þe king wes swiþe unstrong
þa wes he wræccheliche oflust after deores flæsce
Brien his mæi he cleopede and sone hit him cudde
þat buten he hafde deores flasc anan dæd he moste þolien
Ofte wes Briene wa and neouuere wurse þene þa 
hundes nom Brien and hiredmen wel idon
ȝeond wudes and ȝeond feldes heo uerden bilifes
þurh nanes cunnes ginne no mihten heo deor iwinne
nouþer heort no hinde no mihte heo nauere ifinde
Þe king sende his sonde after Brien þa wes to longe
Leof was þe king Briene wa wes him on liue
Ofte he hine biþohte what he don mahte
and biþohten him enne ræd seoþþen he þohten him swiþe god
he igrap a nailsax selliche kene and wel iwhæt
and feng himseolue swa neh þat he nom his aȝe þeh
for unimete neode þerof he makede brede
he bredde heo an hiȝinge and brohte heo þan kinge
Hail seo þu Cadwaþlan þu ært mi kinelauerd
ich habbe þe here ibroht breden alre deorest
þat ich auere an æi borde beren biuoren kinge
held me to and æt herof sone þin hele heo scal iwurþen
Þe king sæt on his bedde his beornes hine biheolde
of þere brede he æt sone þerafter him wes þæ bet
Þe king him gon to sweten þat ufel hine gon forleten
wiþinnen þan fif niht þe king iwræþ fere forþriht
swa næuer þe king nuste whæt he inoted hafde
Þe king iwræþ al uere his folc iwarþ bliþe
wind heom com on wille heo wunden up seiles to coppe
scipen gunnen liþen leodscopes sungen
Ba weoren sehte sæ and þa sunne
wind and þa wide se ba eke isome
flod ferede þa scipen scopes þer sungen
At Ridelæt he com alond þer wes blisse and muche song
bitwixe Dinan and þere sæ ȝet hit is isene
Sone swa he þer com feire he wes underuon
þa kinges weoren bliþe beiene togaderes
þer wunede þe king al þene winter a skenting
þerafter com leinten and dæȝes gunnen longen
þer heo gunnen somnien scipen uniuoȝen
folc unimete grunden an uolde
Þus dude Cadwalan and Peluz hit wuste anan
þurh his dweomercræften þe wunede in þan lufte 
and al þat he auunde in þan lufte and bi þan grunde
þurh ælches cunnes þing he warnede æuere Ædwine king
and dude him al to witen of þare uerde and of þan scipen
Cadwaþlan wes in Brutaine mid Salemone þan kinge
þe wes his moddrie sune and muchel hine lufede
 and þat iherde suggen wel feole siþen
þat Pelluz þe hende þe com ut of Spaine
warnede Edwine þene king æuer þurh alle þing
of feole cunne þinge þat him weoren to cumene
Caþwaþlan þan gode wa wes on mode
and ofte spæc wiþ Brien þe wes his deoreste mon
and nomen heom to rede and to somrune
þat alle þa while þe Pelluz weore alife
no mihte Cadwaþlan comen to þissen londe
mid nauer nare lisse þat Edwine hit nuste
Brien bonnede his fare Brien hafde mucle care
nom him an honde of seoluer and o golde
maþmes unimete moniare cunne
nom he tunnen gode and þa æhte dude þerinne
To þære sæ he wende and seilede mid vþe
he hafde on his uore wintunnen inoȝe
on sæ and on londe his win he lette fonden
and on alle wissen he toc him on swulc he weore a chepmon
In he wende at Barbefleot and at Suþhamtune up aleop
þer he ut draȝen lette win of his tunne
and hendeliche hit delde alle þare duȝeþe
þa him abuten weore riche and henen
and alle luuede þene chapmon þa him lokede on
Vmbe seouennihten he spac wiþ his cnihten
alle weoren his iueren swulc heo chapmen weoren
and eorþhus heo hureden stiþ biwaled on eorþen
heo cluseden þer wiþinnen alle heore wintunnen
heo scupten heore lauerde ænne nome neowe
heo hahten hine Kinebord ut of Spainisce ard
He saiden þat he wenden wolde wide ȝeond þissen londe
 and fondien wher he mihte his win sullen on wille
Forþ he wende bi nihte mid one of his cnihte 
forþ he gon liþe into Lundene
and aneouste gunnen wende onfast Westmustre
and fraineden tiþinde of Edwine kinge
Sone men him talde soþ þat heo funde
þat þe king in Eouerwic wnede mid allen his folke
mid muchere blisse men he hafde inoȝe
Brien gon to farene uorþ mid ane iuere
ut of Lundene derneliche he liþede
þene wæi touward Eouuerwike wraþ on his mode
Þa he iuaren hafde fulle seouen nihte
þa imette he enne pilegrim pic bar an honde
hiȝendliche þe com from þas kingges hirede
Brien hine gon fræine of his farecoste
þe pillegrim him talde al þat he wolde
Wiþ him warfte Brien al his iweden
and æiþer gon liþe þider him to luste
Brien enne smiþ funde þe wel cuþe smiþie
and saide þat he wes pelegrim ah pic nefden he nan mid him
þene þridde dæi þer bifore at his inne he wes forlore
His foreward he makede þe smiþ gon to smiþeȝe
ane pic swiþe long swiþe muchel an swiþe strong
swiþe scarp wes þe pic þe staf wes swiþe sellic
Þene staf he nom an honde and ferde ouer þan londe
þat he com sone liþe to þas kinges hirede
Brien eode upward Brian eode dunward
ne mihte he iheren word of his suster nan
no he uraini ne durste for þes kinges folke
Þa hit wes dai amarȝe þat Drihten hine sende
þe king lette feden alle þa neode hafden
alle þe blæþe þe wuneden on þe burȝe
me heom hehtte onneouste cume to þan castele
bi þusend and bi þusunde þræsten gunnen binward
Brien wenden binne mid oþer wrecche monnen
his lætes weoren alle swulc he lome weore
alle his hateren weoren totoren nas he noht to þan iboren
Þe an hine putte hiderward and þe oþer hine putte ȝeondward
uncuþ him wes swiþe swulc craft on folcke
his pic he heold bisiden and sat imong þan oþeren 
Þe king him gon to þeinen mid alle his herecnihten
þæ quene bar to drinken and alle hire burlutlen
Þa ilomp hit seoþþe þerafter ful sone
þat Galarne þat maiden com hire ȝeongen
bolle heo hafde an honden þermide heo bar to dringen
þa isæh heo Brien þer deore hire broþer
on wræcches monnes liche þeh he weoren riche
Anan swa þat maiden hine isæh sone heo him to bæh
and droh of hire uingre an of hire ringe
and salde him an honde ænne ring of rede golde
and þus sæide Galerne þat godfulle maide
Haue þis gold wræcche Godd þe wurþe milde
and buȝe þe þermide hateren þat wiþ chele þe maȝen werien
Þa wuste he to soþe þat his suster icneou hine
 and þas word seide Brien þe sele
Forȝelde hit þe Drihten þe sop þas daȝes lihten
þat þu þissen lome monne ȝiue of þine golde
Ymong þan wrecche uolke þat maiden heo hudde
bitwxen twam windewen þat maiden iwarþ an selden
and spæc wiþ hire broþren þa bet hire wes on heorten
and talden him tiþende al of þas kinges hirede
and heo him tahte Pelluz þene clarc þe com from Spæine
and he lokien agon in læþest alre monne
Þa heo togadere hafden ispeken sone heo gunen todelen
for nauer neoþer nalde for his æfne wiht of golde
þat þe king hit wusten þat heo togaderen weoren
for sone heo weoren fordon ba oþer ofslaȝen oþer anhon
Þat folc hafden alle iȝeten and arisen from heore seten
dremeden drunkene men dune wes on folke
Pelluz wes aneoste and ȝemde þene nap
Brien him atlede to for he hafde him ful wa ido
his pic he nom an honden and helede hine under capen
swa longe he gon atlen þat he com him baften
and imong al þan þrunge þærsten him i þan ruge
þat he brac ut biforen under his breosten
And forþ he biwafde þene pic he bilæfde 
and forþ imong þan uolke þa wes he al fere
and wende him aneoste of þas kinges hirede
æuere forþ þene wæi suþriht alse he læi
Þa he þus hafde idon to Axcetre he bicom
þer he funde forþrihtes monie of his cnihtes
and freineden ȝeorne of his leodkinge
And Brien heom gon tellen þat wilspelles weoren
and seiden þat Cadwaþlan cumen wolde anan
mid swa muchele uerde of feole cunne ærde
þat ne durste Edwine king cumen toȝæines him naþing
no in nauer nare burȝe ne durste he him ibide
Þat iherde Deuene and þa men of Deorchestre
and þan Cornwælscen wel heom wes on liuen
Brien sende his sonde ouer sæ to Brutlonde
and dude þan kinge to witen aiþer bi worden and bi writen
of alle his deden and þat Pelluz wes on deþen
and bad hine an hihȝende comen to þissen londe
 and þe king duden swa swa swiþe swa he mæhte
And Brien sende sonde into Suþhamtune
and longien him to lette his maþmes leoue
 and alle þa beornes anan þe buȝen him to wolden
comen aneouste into Exchæstre
and stiþimodede men þa burh gunnen walden
Cadwalan þat iherde þe king wes ful bliþe
and inne Brutaine bonnede ferde
þat he þreo hundred hauede hæȝere scipene
and al he hafden þerto þat heom bihouede
And þe king Salomon wide gon sende
and forþ he gon liþen mid his Brutleoden
þat is to iwitene mid twa hundred scipene
to helpen his cunne Cadwaþlan kinge
Weder stod an wille wind mid þan bezste
heo rihten heore loues and up droȝen seiles
liþen ouer sæstræm swa sel þuhte heom
Þa comen he to Tottenes beien þa kinges
Selemon þe sele and Cadwalan þæ kene
þat londfolc wes bliþe for heore leodkinge 
Þa wes in Æstlonde a king þe hehte Penda
he biwuste a þan daȝen þat folc of Merchene laȝen
and he lufde Edwine Edwine lufde hine
and euere he wolde reden Edwine to his neoden
And Penda iherde suggen soþere worden
þat Brien heold Exchestre biclused wiþinnen faste
and þe king Penda wide gon sende þa
and sumede uerde and forþ him fusen
 and wenden to Exchastre mid vnimete genge
and bilæi uul faste þa burh of Exchestre
Brien þe wihte mid twa hundred cnihte
wes þer wiþinnen and þa burh wereden
Sone þa tidende icumen wes to þære hauene of Totenes
to Caþwalane kinge hu Brien wes biþrungen
he lette blawen bemen and bonnien his ferden
 and ferde æuere þene wæi þæ touward Exchestre lai
and delde a þreo ulockes his duhtie cnihtes
and þus cleopien agon þe king wes abolȝen
Æuerælc god cniht faren heom to forþriht
for we beoþ cnihtes gode mid wepnen wel idihte
arude we Brien þe is min ibore mon
For ȝif heo nimeþ Brien heo hine wulleþ aquelen
and seoþþen heo wulleþ hine ahon and alle his iferen fordon
 and us þerafter sone mid alle heore imæhte
To heo gunnen riden gæres heo letten gliden
breken bræde weiȝes brustleden scaftes
golduaȝe sceldes scanden bilifes
feollen þa cnihtes faleweden nebbes
ȝeond þan feldes wide swulten men uæiȝe
blod orn in þe weiȝe strames swiþe brade
þer neoren eorles no wurþer þene cheorles
Þer weoren þa ofslæȝene seouen þusend fulle
Marcchisce monnen þa þer icumen weoren
þa falden heo adune heremarken uaȝe 
heo wurpen sceldes sone dunede þa eorþe
Þa sette to fleme alre ȝeomerest folke
and Cadwalan after heom mid allen his imahten
 and mid his aȝene honden nom þene king Pendan
he wes Mærwales fader Mildburȝe aldeuader
Pendan heo nomen and duden hine i benden
wiþinnen Excestre and biwusten hine wel faste
Swa sellic hit ferde in alle þan uahte
þat nas Pendan þe king amarred nanes kunnes þing
and Cadwalan hine biwuste wel þurh alle custe
and fæire heo hine uedde and faire he eode to bedde
Þa weoren agan seouen niht þa nom Pendan enne cniht
þe wes swiþe wis mon and wel cuþe speken
and cleopede hine to rade and seide him of his neode
and ȝeorne hine bisohte for lufe of ure Drihte
þat he speke wiþ Cadwalan þe wes his kinelauerd
þat he hine griþede þurh þene Godd heȝe
and he wolde bicumen his mon his monscipe hæhȝen
dæiȝes and nihtes he and al his cnihtes
Þe cniht him forþ wende to Cadwalane kinge
þer he hine imette and fæire hine igrette
and dude alse god mon sel him wurþe for þan
for a is treowe monnen treouþe ihalden
Hal seo þu Cadwalan þu art mi kinelauerd
Þe ibundene king Penda hider me gon sende
 and ȝerneþ þine ære nu and aueremære
and he wulle þi mon bicume and to ȝisle seollen þe his sune
and of þe his kinelond halden and for lauerd þe ikenne
 and on ælchere þeode beon ȝaru to þine neode
he wule beon þi mon icoren aȝein ælcne mon iboren
Þa andswærien agon mid aþelen his worden
Cadwalan þe kene þe king of Suþlonde
Ȝif Penda wolde halde þat he me bihateþ to don
and bitechen me his sune his gold and his gærsume
 and treouwe mon auere beon and neouwar min herm iseon
 and likede swa him likede næuere me biswike
ich me biræden wolde of swulchere neode
Þer anan forþriht andswarede þe gode cniht 
La swa ic auere mote iþeon ich wulle his an barh beon
and habbeon to iueren an hondret rideren
uppen alle ure londe uppen seoluer and uppen golde
And swa ich bide are ȝet he wulle mare
ane suster he haueþ hende in þan æst ende
nis nan feirure wifmon þa whit sunne scineþ on
þe king of France Leouwis ȝirneþ hire ful iwis
and he wulle hire to morȝeue þene Mans bitæchen
and habben heo to quene þat mæiden Helene
And ich suggen þe to soþe þæh ich þi broþer weore
æuere þe is selere þisulf þat þu heo habbe
þurh hire þu miht biwinnen lufe of hire cunnen
and iwinnen al þi kinelond to þire aȝere hond
and wunien on londe and walde þine riche
Þa andswarede Cadwalan þe king wes on londen
Hit is on mine rede to don þat þu bede
Ȝif þu miht under Criste þis forward me ileste
ich þe ȝeuen to hure al Deuenescire
al for Heleine lufe hiȝendliche let heo cume
Þe cniht him gon wende mid muchelere genge
to þan castle of Deoure on þere sæ oure
he nom þer Helene wunderliche and fæire
and forþ he heo ladde into Winchæstre
þer wes muchel blisse burhmen weoren bliþe
Þer þe king Cadwalan com him toȝeines heom
he weddede þat mæiden and nom heo to his bedden
þer wes wifþing riche and vnimete blisse
Þa hit wes dæi amarȝen and duȝeþe gunnen sturien
 and þe king iuæstned hafde alle his forwarde
þa nom he muchele genge and after Penda sende
þer he wes ful faste in þan castle of Æxchæstre
and mid muche lufe hine hehte cumen to Lundenne
Penda to Lundene com he wes ahtliche underuon
and Cadwalan þe kene mid lufe hine custe
and Penda bicom his mon þer his monscipe wes þe mare
þa weoren Lundenisce men bliþest arle leoden 
Þa wes hit seoþþe þerafter noht longe
Cadwalan gan liþe wide ȝeond þis londe
alle þa hine lufeden he heom gon griþien
alle þa him heolden wiþ he binom heore lif
and heore leoden and al þat heo leof hafden
and hiȝendliche gon wende touward þere Humbre
and gon þat lond westen mid hærmen þan mæsten
Þat iherde Edwine and alle þat luueden hine
swiþe heo gunnen dreden of Cadwalanes deden
Edwine nom his sonde and senden to Sexlonde
he sende into Denene he sende into Noreine
into Wellisce londe into Scotlonde
into Orcaneiȝe into Galwaiȝe
into Islonde into Frislonde
into Gutlonde þer gumen weoren kene
he bed heom cumen sone mid wepnen wel idone
to driuen ut þa Bruttes þe bisie weoren to harmes
and þenne he Bruttes hæfden mid bronden tohæuwen
he wolde al þis kinelond setten an heore hond
bute þat he icleoped weore king of þan londe
he wolde þere duȝeþen þis lond al todalen
Ah he ful lutel wuste what ilomp seoþþe
Comen touward londe touward Edwine kinge
bi sæ and bi londe feole cunne leoden
þer comen seouen kinges and six sunen kinges
seouentene eorles and sixti þusend beornnes
Næs he boren nauere in nauer nare burhȝe
þe mihte in æi spelle þat oþer uolc telle
nas hit nauere isæid no on bocken irad
þat æuer ær weore æi swa muchel ferde
æuere in Ængelonde þurh ænie king togadere
Edwine gon to uarene mid mucle his ferde
and Cadwalan after wende mid unimete folke
Þe stude hehte Hædfeld þer heo atstoden under scelde
twelf milen is þe wald þe is ihaten Heþfeld
Edwine an his ende his teldes alle sette
his marken and his mare and eke his monweorede
and Cadwalan þe kene him com toȝaines sone 
þer fusden tosomne uerden unimete
Heo fuhten feondliche feollen þa uaiȝe
brokes þer urnen mid unimete stremen
of bloden þan ræde þe balu wes unimete
Helmes þer gullen beornes þer ueollen
sceldes gunnen scenen scalkes gunnen swelten
at þan forme rese fifti þusende
baldere beornen heore beot wes þæ lasse
Þer wes Edwines ferde ȝeoumerest alre uolke
 and Edwine himseolf anan ærmest alre kingen
þer wes Edwine ofslaȝen and his sunen tweien
þer feollen seouen kinges and six sunen kinges
his eorles his beornes his cnihtes his cheorles
þer wes þe swein and þe cnaue beinen of are laȝe
nefden heo nane are of þan lasse no of þan mare
ah al þa ferde wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
Of þan fehte fleh a gume Edwines ȝungeste sune
wellen henden wes þe mon Osric ihaten
nefde he to iueren buten an hundred rideren
Þeos to wuden wenden and þer gunnen wunien
and barnden Cadwalanes lond and eoden him luþere an hond
 and his folc sloȝen a feole cunnes wissen
Þat iherde Cadwalan þe king wes on londen
hu Osric Edwines sune dude utlaȝen wune
Cadwalan muchel uolc nom and lette heom to wuden gan
and Osric heo funden and wiþ him fehten
þer heo Osric sloȝen and alle his iueren
Nu wes þe king Cadwalan bliþest alre kempen
nu wes icleoped Cadwalan king ouer Anglen
Penda wes king under him and ma þa iqueme weoren him
Cadwalan aquald hefde of Edwines cunne
al þat þer wes hende wiþuten ane monne
he wes ihaten Oswald under Drihtene bald
he wes of Edwines cunne and him leofuest monne
 and he wes hex monnen of Edwines cunnen
Oswald nom on his hond al togadere Edwines lond
eorles and kempen his men al bicomen
me heold hine king hæhne biȝeonde þere Humbre
þat iherde Cadwalan and þus quaþ to his eorlen 
Somnie we nu ferde ȝeond alle mine ærde
nu ich mi lond habben bitald nu hauiþ hit Oswald
ah þeruore him scal ileoten bitterest alre baluwen
For þan kinelond ich hine aqualle wulle
and al his ferde fallen to grunde
and al þat he of com ich hit wulle fordon
and swa me scal him tache to walden kineriche
Aleggen ich wulle his muchele mod monnen he is me laþest
Cadwalan somnede uerde mucle in þissen ærde
 and ferde touward þere Humbre ȝaru al to fehte
Oswald þis iherde þas heȝes Godes icorne
and nom him al his ferde þa hafde in his ærde
and forsoc þat feht sone forsaken him weoren laþe
and ferde æuere forþward
 and Cadwalan him after wende ah oftaken he hine ne mahte
Þa wes Cadwalan adred for wiþ Scotten he wes iuæid
for he þat norþerne uolc hæuede ineouþered ful swiþe
 and nom him to rede of swulchere neode
þat he aȝain wolde for þer he kare hafde
and biteche Penda þe wes his underkinge
folc and his ferde to flemen of arde
Edwines mæi Oswald and driuen hine of londe
And al Cadwalan spede swa he ispeken hafde
aȝæn he gon wende into þisse londe
and in þan norþ ende sette þene king Penda
to fleomen Oswalde ut of þissen londe
Oswald þat iherde þat Cadwalan chærde
and þer wunede Penda to driuen hine of londe
þa was þæ king Oswald an his þonke swiþe bald
and aȝæin him gon wende muchele his ferde
toȝeines þan kinge Penda to fleomen hine þenne
Penda hine biþohte swiken hu he mahte
he sende to Oswalde þen norþerne kinge
 and seide þat he wolde sahtnesse wurche
and timliche him speken wiþ and makeȝen sehtnesse and griþ
and beon saht and some swulc heo weoren broþeren
and faren of þan ende to Cadwalane kinge
and leten þene king Oswald habben his riche and his lond
Þene dæi and þe stude heo setten sæhnesse to makien
and þerafter ful sone heo cumen tosomne
Oswald com muchel biforen he wes to Godes hond icoren
þe studen hehte Houenfeld þer Oswald sette his teld
he lette sone arere a muchel cros and mare
and hehten al his ferde fallen on heore cneowen
and bidden þane almihti Godd þurh his milde mihti mod
þat he heom ȝiue mildze of heore misdede
and ȝif Penda þat griþ breke þat ure Drihten hit awreke
Þa weren iended þas beden þa com him Penda riden
and word seide swikelest alre kinge
Oswald þu art wilcume wunne þe is ȝeueþe
hafue þu al þi kinelond ah nim þi seoluer and þi gold
nim an hundred hunden nim an hundred haueken
nim an hundred steden nim goldfah iwede
and send þas gretinge to Cadwaþlan kinge
and þus þu maht him wiþ makien þe sahtnesse and griþ
 and ich wulle a þine stude beon þat þa lufe scal wel iþeon
 and ȝet ich þe suggen wulle ane sunder rune
hu þu mihte fon on þat hit ne buþ nauere undon
and cleope mid þe tweien þat þine treowe men beon beien
 and ich wulle tweien to me þa wel scullen reden
Þa rad forþ a þan felde falsest alre kinge
and Oswald rad a þene feld næfde he sper ne nænne sceld
Penda his sweord ut adroh and he Oswald ofsloh
þis wes Seint Oswald þe amurþered wes aquald
and Penda gon to fleonne mid alle his ferde
þat isehȝen forþrihtes Oswaldes cnihtes
and after heom setten mid allen heore mihten
mucchel del heo sloȝen of þan monweorede
and þe king Penda uneþe gon awende
and neoþeles he atræd þe Seint Oswald biswac
Penda com to þissen londe to Cadwaþlan kinge 
and talde al þan kinge hu he iuaren hafden
Hit likede wel þan kinge buten for ane þinge
hit ofþuhte him ful sone for þan swikedome
Nu hafde Oswald þe a morþe wes aquald
ænne ælpine broþer nes þer nan oþer
he wes icleoped Oswi þe wes a swiþe duhti mon
þa þringes norþerne makeden hine to kinge
for wa wes heom on life for heore lauerdes deþe
Oswi nom to his hond al his broþer kinelond
Oswi hafde emes sunen þe weoren swiþe prute gumen
and ma of his cunne þa weoren modfulle
heo hafden muchele onde to þan kinelonde
and makeden mucchel unfriþ and ofte fuhten him wiþ
and þohten hine aquellen for his kinelonden
Ah Oswi wes cniht sturne þat he þer cudde
alle þa him beren onde he draf of þan londe
hiȝendliche he heom quehte ouer þere Humbre
þat nes þer nan to laue of þan þe him weoren laþe
And heo gunnen wenden to þan kinge Pendan
and menden heom to Pendan of Oswy þan kinge
þat he heom idriuen ut hafde of al heore icunde
and heo bisohten Penda þene king of Æstlonde
þat heom fulste Oswy to foruarne
and heo wolden bicumen his men and his monscipe heȝen
ȝif he wolde Oswy fordon oþer slæn oþer ahon
Þa andswerede Penda þe king of Æstlonde
At me nabbe ȝe nenne ræde for ich æm wiþ Oswi iuæid
for ich Oswald aqualde wihteste alre kinge
and Oswy his broþer is oht cniht and arþ heorte nawiht
ȝif he me mihte cacchen he me wolde quellen
Ah fareþ to Cadwalane þe king is on londe
and ȝif he me wulle sende þat folc of his londe
vt of Corwale cnihtes icudde
and of Walisce londe mid seolure and mid golde
þenne wlle ich Oswy anan mid ærmþen igreten
driuen hine of londe leoden to sconde
oþer slan hine mid egge laþest alle ginge 
Þas cnihtes gunnen wende to Cadwaþlane kinge
To Cadwaþlane heo come mid falsæn dome
þan kingen heo tolden al þat heo wolden
Hit ilomp an ane time to þan Whitesunetide
þat þe king hehte of londen comen al to Lunden
alle þe wolden his griþ and wiþ þan kinge habben friþ
Þider comen kinges and æc hereþringes
þider comen eorles þider comen beornes
biscpes þider comen and bocilerede men
riche and hene þider heo comen alle
alches cunnes leoden þa þene king lufeden
 and þe king a þan daiȝe his crune bar an hæfde
þer wes muchel blisse mid balde þan kinge
for þe king wes swiþe treowe mon his treouþe wel he iheold
Þa þas leoden alle iliþen weoren tosomne
þa stod him up Penda biuore Cadwaþlane kinge
and þus he gon tellen on false his spellen
Lauerd we beoþ icumen alse þu hafdest iqueþen
alle þine men iborne Englisce and Bruttisce
eorles and beornes cnihtes and clærckes
and we þine kinges þa beoþ þine underlinges
Ah Oswy seide æuere þat nulle he come nauere
no þine heste iuorþen ah bihateþ hærm to don
Nert þu noht swa modi swa him is Oswy
he forhoȝeþ ful iwis to isechen þine hiredes
Ah ȝif þu wult me lenen and þine læue iunnen
and þu me wulle fulsten and ferde bitæchen
and swa muchel of þine garsume god swa þe þunche
ich wulle uorþ aneouste and faren ouer Humbre
 and Oswy þer makien ærmest alre kingen
no scal he mid strenþe þene stude uinde
þat ich hine nulle þe an hond sulle
oþer quic oþer ded þat me þuncheþ god ræd
 and ȝif þu þis nult don þu scalt wurse underfon
for Oswy is a swulc mon þine scome he wulle don
Þa andswarede Cadwalan þe kene
Penda ich hit þe sugge oueral Oswy haueþ forwal
oþer he liþ ibedde ibunden mid ufele
oþer uncuþe leoden icumen beoþ to his þeoden 
for nulle he nauere icnawen þat he nolde him to cumen
þa ich hehte alle cumen mid griþe mid friþe and mid lufe
Ah Penda ga þider ut anan ich wulle wiþ mine eorlen
mine rune halden and minne red finden
wheþer ich þe ȝetten wullen þa þing þe þu bede
and ich wulle after Oswine senden aþele mine sonde
and haten hine hiȝindliche cumen to mine riche
Þider ut eode Penda an eorl wes his iuere
and Cadwaþlan wes þerinne mid swiþe feole monne
Þus him spac Cadwaþlan þe king wes of Englen
Ȝe beoþ mine men alle þa beoþ a þisse mote
and ȝe habbeoþ alle iherd whæt Penda king hafueþ iseid
and hu he wulle taken on and Oswi king al fordon
ȝif ic him lenen wulle mine leoden to vulste
and ic wulle þat ȝe me reden of wlchere deden
þa ich lete Oswi fordo þa ich lete hine cumen me to
 and ȝif he for mire sonde forsakeþ hider to cumene
mine here ich lete seoþþen hine hene makien
Þa iwærþ abolȝen a Welisc king in þe hepen
he wes ihaten Margadud monnen wurþe him ȝeomerist
for æuere he Ænglisce men bihehte hærm þene meste
Þus seide Mærgadud of Suþ Wales he wes duc
Her nu me Cadwaþlan whæt ich þe wulle cuþe
Þu hauest þine willen iseid ah þis nis noht god red
Hit is swiþe ȝare þat Bruttes comen here
and mid him ure ældre þe Bruttes weoren aþele
and þis lond ieoden Bruttisce leoden
and longe hit walden after heore willen
þa while þa hit wes on heore hond hit wes ihaten Brutlond
Nu nabbe we of þan londe buten þene west ende
þa Bruttes hafden iwuned here wel feole wintre
Þa comen Englisce men mid heore ufele craften
heo weore wiȝelfulle and þis lond al biwunne
and biswiken heore lauerd sonen and alle his leoden
 and ȝiuenen heore kinge ane heþene quene
þa comen of Sexlonde þa leoden us beoþ laþe 
þurh þere quene ure cun aqualden here
and swa habbeoþ Englisce men ure icunden atheolden
þet we nauere seoþþen bisechen hit no mihten
Penda king is Englisc and Oswy alswa ful iwis
Let þu þa hundes hannen togaderes
eiþer freten oþer swa hund deþ his broþer
and leten heore whelpes whæruen heom bisides
elc oþer quelle þat þer nan quic no leue
And ȝif Oswy cumeþ bufen and þat feht maȝen ouercumen
we him sculleþ to luken and neouþer hine aleggen
lond and his leoden and his laȝen uallen
and ȝif Penda biþ buuen and þat comp maȝen ouercumen
þin aȝe mon is Penda mid alle his kinelonda
Þenne hauest þu Englisc lond to þire aȝere hond
and alle þine wurþscipe þus þu miht biwinnen
 and libben a þin lif swa þe arle leofest biþ
No findest þu nauermare mon þa þe durre haten on
Þa andswarede a mon þe bald wes on hireden
Lust nu me Cadwaþlan lust me ane stunden
Nis þar nan betere red þene Margadud haueþ ised
 and ȝif þat nult don þu scalt wurse afon
 and alle þine leoden þa later þu hafuest to neoden
Efne þissere saȝe þa þe Brut sæide
þa wes icleoped Penda and com into hirede
and Cadwaþlan him ȝette al þat he wolde
Þa wes Penda bliþe and igladed swiþe
Penda and his cnihtes to horsen forþrihtes
and aneousten gunnen wenden toward Norhhumberlonden
 and Oswi iherden suggen þat Penda hine sohte
 and ȝarecode his ferden and fusde toȝæines Pendan
faht heo bigunnen ræȝe heo weoren beien
feondliche heo fuhten uæiden heo weoren
vnimete feollen fæie men on folden
Þa hit wes uppen non þa sunne gon to nipen
þer wes Oswy ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen
 and his sune and his æm and eorles sume uiuen
þer weoren niȝe þusunde þringes norþerne
islaȝen i þan dæiȝe þa duȝeþe wes þa lasse
 and þe king Penda sære wes iwunded þa
 and þonene gon wende æst to his londe
Oswy hæfden ænne sune Osric wes his nome
he wes ane stunde mid Cadwaþlane kinge
in his hirede iued and deorliche ifostred
Osric bisohte Cadwalan swa mon scal his lauerde don
þat he moste beon his mon and his fader lond habbeon
Cadwaþlan him ȝet al þat he ȝirde
he bitahte him an hond al his fader kinelond
hehte hine hit habben and halde mid wunne
God king wes Cadwaþlan swa him wes icunden
he wes king hire seouen and feouwerti ȝere
Þa uerde he to Lunden to gladien þa leoden
and heold ane metsunge mid þan uolke of Lundene
he æt of ane uisce uretliche swiþe
ær þe uisc ieten weore iuueled was þe king
seouen niht and enne dæi þe king a þan ufele læi
nes þer nan oþer red seoþþen wes þe king ded
heo bureden hine in Lunden særi weoren þa leoden
Enne sune hafde Cadwaþlan Cadwalader ihaten
he wes Penda suster sune al of kingen icume
þeos feng to his riche after his fader daiȝe
Swiþe leoflic wes þe mon his leoden hine luueden
he wes swiþe god cniht and swiþe sturne inne fiht
æh an his daȝen ilompen reoþen on leoden
Ærst aswond þat corn here ȝeond al þas kineriche
þerafter hit wes swa deore and al folc gon to deȝen
swa þat þu mihtes fare fulle seouen nihte
þat no mihtest þu þurh nene chep finde neouwer na bred
an burȝe and on londe leoden weoren ȝeoumere
no nan uolc on londe þat offingred nes sære
Þa þat wes idriuuen longe ȝeond þas leoden
þa com þer anoþer sorȝe þerafter ful sone
þat quale com on orue vnimete swiþe
þer cheorl draf his sulȝe ioxned swiþe fæire
oþer while he brohte ham halue his oxen 
oþer brohte enne þe oþer no brohte nenne
and swa hit on leode ilaste wel longe
Þerafter sone sorȝen vnimete
comen to folke ȝeond al þas kineþeode
uppen þan monen morþ wes iwurþen
quelen þa eorles quelen þa beornes
quelen þa þeines quelen þa sweines
quelen þa lareden quelen þa leouweden
quelan þa ældren quelen þa ȝeongeren
quelæn þa wifmen quelen þa wanclen
þat no mihte on þan ende þat folc on þan londe
burien þa dede swiþe heo gunnen deȝe
þat ofte in þan putte þer me þene dede isette
þer deiȝede þe quike uppen þen dede
And swa hit ilomp wide ȝeond Ænglene þeode
þat folc ut of londe flah on ælche ænde
monie hundred tunen bilæued weoren of monnen
þat lut me uinde mihte men uaren ȝeond londe
Wa wæs Cadwalader þe king wes on londe
for scome he ne mihte fleon no for hærme her beon
Neoþeles he hine biþohte hu he faren mahte
he nom his maþmes alle and his men deore
 and bah suþ ouer sæ into Brutaine
and nom þer wickinge mid Alaine þan kinge
þe wæs sune Salemonnes þas sele kinges
þe swiþe lufede Cadwaþlan þe while his daiȝes ilaste
Þær Alæin þe king Cadwalader underueng
 and funde him in þan londe al þat he wolde
þurh elleouen ȝere þe king wunede þere
 and elleouen ȝere þe sorhȝe wunede here
þat wes hunger and hette nefede þat folc nenne mete
 and þe qualm muchele þe wes on moncunne
Þat folc flah into wuden and wuneden in þe cluden
leien in þa stangraffen and liueden bi deoren
heo liueden bi wuden heo lifeden bi wurten
bi moren and bi rote nas þer nan oþer boten
Þa elleue ȝer weoren on fast aȝeongen
þa sunne gon to scine þe rein bigon to rine 
þe qualm gon to stunte men gunnen to sturien
ut of wude heo droȝen and wuneden in tunen
Heo speken tosomne and spileden bitweonen
and nomen heore sonde and sende into Sexlonde
and cudden heore cunne of heore qualesiþe
 and hu heo ifaren hafden elleue ȝeren
 and hu þat ufel wes atstunt and hu þa tunes ibuld
and hu þer wes fæiȝer lond inoh seoluer and gold
 and beden heom cumen swiþe hider to heore icunde
for þa Bruttes þa ær weoren here æuere heo weren fleme
no durste heo næuere mængen imong Englisce monnen
no nawhit heo nusten of heore uarecosten
þat weoren heore sonden isend to Sexlonden
Þa heȝe Sexisce men iherden þas sonden
þa fusden touward sæ fifti þusende
baldere beornen mid scelden and mid burnen
mid wifen and mid children to þissen londe wenden
Mid þan formeste swipen her comen þreo hundred scipen
siȝen after seoþþe sixti tosomne
bi sixe bi seouene bi tene bi eolleue
bi twelue bi twenti bi þritti bi feowerti
Mid heom com Æþelstan þe æþele ut of Sexen
inne Lundene hine cruneden and houen hine to kingen
Edward þe king þesne biȝat on are chiuese
þis wes þe formeste Englisce mon þe al Ænglelond biwon
he wes icruned and ieled þis lond wes al his aȝen
and seoþþen he wuneden here sixtene ȝere
Hit ilomp inne frimdæȝen feor her biæften
þat her wes an heh mon Inne wes ihaten
Þe king wende to Rome to þan heȝe dome
and he Peteres weofed þere wunliche isohte
brohte þer to lake his maþmes leofe
Þa ȝet he dude mare to Peteres are 
of æuerelche huse þat husbonde wunede
 and his biweddede wif weore on þere ilke wike
þe king enne peni ȝette to Peteres huse
Inne wes þe uormeste mon þe Peteres peni bigon
Þa Inne king wes him ded and his laȝen weoren aleid
þa afeol þat feoh here fif and sixti ȝere
a þet Aþelstan com liþen into þissen londen
 and hafden iwuned here fulle fiftene ȝere
Þe king his fet custe and faire hine igrette
 and eft þat ilke feoh ȝete þat Inne king dude ære
 and swa hit hafeþ ist onde æuer seoþþe a þisse londe
Drihten wat hu longe þeo laȝen scullen ilæste
þa tiden comen sone to Cadwaþlader kinge
into Brutaine þer þar he wunede
mid Alaine kinge þe wes of his cunne
me dude him to understonde of al þisse londe
hu Aþelstan her com liþen ut of Sexlonden
and hu he al Anglelond sette on his aȝere hond
and hu he sette moting and hu he sette husting
and hu he sette sciren and makede friþ of deoren
 and hu he sette halimot and hu he sette hundred
and þa nomen of þan tunen on Sexisce runen
 and ȝilden he gon rere mucle and swiþe mære
 and þa chirchen he gon dihten after Sexisce irihten
and Sexis he gan kennen þa nomen of þan monnen
and al me him talde þe tiden of þisse londe
Wa wes Cadwaledere þat he wes on liue
leofere him weore on deþe þeone quic on life
særi wes his heorte and sorhful wes his duȝeþe
Wiþ his freond he spac ofte
hu he faren mihte and iwinnen his rihte
and wulchere wise he mihte wiþ Aþelstane fihte
 and iwinnen his cunde æft to his honde
þa Aþestan and his cnihtes eke heolde mid unrihte
Sume him radde to uehten summe wriþ to wurchen 
þat he mosten of Aþelstan halden his lond and beon his mon
Vnder þissen uarecoste he sumnede ferde
of alle þane monne þat he biȝeten mihte
 and somnede alle þa scipen þa bi þare sæ fluten
and þohte mid strengþe steppen to londe
Þa þe ȝaru wes þa uerde and þas scipen ibone
com þe wind suþerne þa sæt an heore wille
Þa sæide þe king Nu to scipe an hiȝing
And þe king into chirche gon wenden Godes werk to worchen
and masse þer iherden of mære ane preoste
Þe king læi on cneouwen and cleopede to Criste
 and bed ure Drihten þe walt alle deden
þat he from himselue taken him sende
ȝif hit weore iqueme þan heouenliche Deme
wheþer he scolde liþen þe he scolde bilauen
Þe while þe he spac touward Goden þa gon he to slepen
þa gon he to slumme selehþe him wes ȝiueþe
of seoluen ure Drihten þe scop þis dæȝes lihte
Þenne þe king imætte a cneouwen he slepte
þat him com biforen gon a wunder ane fair mon
 and þas word kende to Bruttene kinge
Awake Cadwalader Crist þe haueþ deore
and ȝarke þine uore and far swiþe to Rome
þu uindest ænne pape preost mid þan bezste
he þe scal scriuen of þine weorldlifen
þat hine sunen alle scullen þe from falle
and þu scalt wurþe clene al þurh Godes dome
of alle þine misdede þurh mihte of ure Drihte
And seoþþen þu scalt iwiten and faren to heofnerichen
for no most þu naueremære Ænglelond aȝe
ah Alemainisce men Ænglen scullen aȝen
and næuermære Bruttisce men bruken hit ne moten
ær cume þe time þe iqueþen wes while
þat Merlin þe witeȝe bodede mid worde
Þenne sculle Bruttes sone buȝen to Rome
and draȝen ut þine banes alle of þene marmestane
and mid blissen heom uerien uorþ mid heomseoluen 
in seoluere and in golde into Brutlonde
Þenne sculle Bruttes anan balde iwurþen
al þat heo biginneþ to done iwurþeþ after heore wille
þenne scullen i Bruttene blissen wurþen riue
wastmes and wederes sele after heore iwille
Þa awoc Cadwalader wunder him þuhte
strongliche he wes auæred ladliche offurhte
to wulche þinge hit iteon wolde þat him wes itacned þere
Ofte he lette runen ofte he lette ræde
and seowede hit þan kinge þe wunede in þan londe
þe inemned wes Alain Cadwalader nexte mæi
Þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al his londe
and lette beoden alle þa bocares wise
and talden heom þa tacninge of Cadwalader kinge
Þær heo gunnen ræde þer heo gunnen rune
 and radden him to taken on al swa Godd him hafde itakned to don
Þer he bilafde his scipen and his leode
his wæi and his iwille He cleopede heom to stille
Yuni and Iuore beiȝen heo weoren him deore
Yuor wes his stepsune and Yuni his suster sune
beien heo weoren him leofe beine heo weoren him deore
heo weoren cnihtes beien and swiþe wel idihte
Þus spac Cadwalader þe king wes of Bruttene
Yuor and Yuni beiene ȝet senden of mine leode
hercnieþ mine lare no scal hit eou reouwe nauere
Of heouene me beoþ icume hiȝe Godes tacne
þat ich scal faren to Rome to þan pape wel idone
Þe pape hatte Sergius he weteþ Peteres hus
me and mine wiue he scal bletseiȝen and scriue
 and þer we scullen ure daȝes ba driuen to þan ende
longe biþ auer no iseo ȝe me æft næuere
Ah here ich bitache inc Walisc lond þat ȝet stond a mire hond
and nimeþ þas muchele uerde and fareþ to þan londe
and haldeþ hit on wunne þa wile ȝe maȝen hit werie
and ich inc halsi beien þurh þan heouen kinge
þat unker æiþer oþer luuie swa his broþer 
and habbeoþ þat lond auermære tou æure liues ende
 and brukeþ hit on wunne and eouwer bernen alle
Yuni hit wes itacned me alse ȝe scullen nu iseo
for Merlin þe wise hit seide mid worde
al of mine forþfare and of mire unimete care
and Sibillie þa wise a bocken hit isette
þat ich scal iuullen mines Drihtes wille
Alc faren nu his wæi and habbeoþ alle godne dæi
Cadwalader fusde þat he com to Rome
þer he Sergius funde þene iselie pape
he scraf Cadwalader þe king wes of Bruttenne
Ne wunede þe king þer bute uifte half ȝere
þa com him ufel on swa Godd hit wolde habben idon
elleoue daȝes biforen Maiȝe he ferde of þisse liue
and his saule sende to þan heouenlicche kinge
His ban beoþ iloken faste i guldene cheste
and þer heo scullen wunie þat þa daȝes beon icumene
þa Merlin ine iuurn daȝen vastnede mid worden
Ga we nu to Yuni aȝan and to Iuore his weddebroþere
Heo somneden ferde wide ȝeond þan ærde
forþ heo gunnen fusen mid fif hundred scipenen
nes hit nawit longe þat heo ne comen to Walisce londe
Al þas Bruttes weoren todriuen ȝeond cludes and ȝeond cliuenen
ȝeond chirchen and ȝeond muneccliuen ȝeond wudes and ȝeond liþen
Sone me heom saiden þat isiȝen weoren to londe
mid Iuore and Yuni ten siþen fifti
scipen bradefulle of Brutten swiþe balde
Þæs Bruttes on ælc ende foren to Walisce londe
and heore laȝen leofeden and heore leodene þæuwen
and ȝet wunieþ þære swa heo doþ aueremære
 and Ænglisce kinges walden þas londes
 and Bruttes hit loseden þis lond and þas leoden
þat næuere seoþþen mære kinges neoren here
Þa ȝet ne com þæs ilke dæi beo heonneuorþ alse hit mæi
iwurþe þet iwurþe iwurþe Godes wille
